MAT 1:1 Dawite na, Abrame na gidida Yesus Kristosa yeletetha zarkey hayssappe kaalizayssa
MAT 1:2 Abiramey Yisaqa yelides. Yisaqay Yaqoobe yelides. Yaqobey Yudane iza ishata yelides.
MAT 1:3 Yuday Timarippe Faresane Zara yelides. Faresy Asrome yelides. Asromey Arame yelides.
MAT 1:4 Aramey Aminadabe yelides. Aminadabey Ne7asone Yelides. Ne7asoney Selimone yelides.
MAT 1:5 Selimoney Bo7eze Ere7abippe yelides. Bo7ezey Urutippe Iyobede yelides. Iyobedey Iseye yelides.
MAT 1:6 Iseyey kawo Dawite yelides. Dawitey Oriyo machcheyfe Solomone yelides.
MAT 1:7 Solomoney Robi7ame yelides. Robi7amey Aabbiya yelides. Aabbiyaykka Aasafe yelides.
MAT 1:8 Asafey Yosafaxxe yelides. Yosafaxxey Iyorame yelides. Iyoramey Oziyane yelides.
MAT 1:9 Oziyaney Iyoatamme yelides, Iyoatamey Akaze yelides, Akazey Hizqassa yelides.
MAT 1:10 Hizqassay Minasse yelides, Minassey Ammoxe yelides, Amoxxeykka Yosiyasa yelides.
MAT 1:11 Yosiyasay Babiloone di7o layth Ikoniyanene iza ishata yelides.
MAT 1:12 Babiloone di7oppe guye Ikkoniyaney Salatiyale yelides, Salatiyaleykka Zarubabele yelides,
MAT 1:13 Zerubabeley Abiyodde yelides, Abiyodey Eliyaqqemme yelides, Eliyaqqemmey Azare yelides.
MAT 1:14 Azarey Sadeqqe yelides, Sadoqqey Akimme yelides, Akimeykka Eliyodde yelides,
MAT 1:15 Eliyodey Alazare Yelidess, Alazarey Matane yelides, Mataney Yaqqobbe yelides.
MAT 1:16 Yaqoobeykka Kirstosa getetidaysa Yesusa yelida Maramo ekana gigisida Yosefo yelides.
MAT 1:17 Hesa gish Abirameppe yidi Dawite gakanas tamane oydu yeleteth, qasse Dawiteppe Babiloone di7o wode gakanas taammane oydu yeleteth, Babiloone di7oppe Kirstossa yeleteth gakanas tamane oydu yeleteth gidana.
MAT 1:18 Yesus Kirstosa yeletetha tarikey hessa mala; iza ayeya Marama Yosefos gigista utada dishin izi izira gagonta dishin Xillo Ayanan qanthatada bistadus.
MAT 1:19 Izo gigisida Yosefoy xillo asa gidida gish Maramo asa sinthan qonce kesonta qotara aganas ba wozinara qachidess.
MAT 1:20 Haysa izi qopishin Xossa kitanchay agumora izas qoncidi “Dawite na Yossefo ne gigisida Marama qanthatiday Xillo Ayanan gidida gish izo ne so efanas baboppa,
MAT 1:21 Iza adde na yelana, izi asa nagarappe ashanade gidida gish iza sunth ne Yesusa ga sunthana” gidess.
MAT 1:22 Godday nabe Isayasa dunan “hekko gela7oya qanthatana, atumanakka yelana, naza sunthaykka Amanu7ele getistana, hessa birshechikka <Xossi nunara> gusa getetidi xafetidaysi polistana mala haysi wurikka hanidess.”
MAT 1:24 Yossefoykka dhiskkoppe begidi Goodda kitanchay iza azazida mala Maramo ba so efidess.
MAT 1:25 Gido atin bada iza koyro naza yelana gakanas izo ekibeyna. Yeletida gutha naza suntha Yesusa gidess.
MAT 2:1 Kawo Herodosa wode Yesusay Bistaleme Yihudan yelettidappe guye away mokiza bagappe erata/eranchati Yerusalame yidi
MAT 2:2 “Yeletida Ayhude kawoy awan dize? away mokiza bagara iza xolinteza beyidi izas goynana yidos” gidi oychida.
MAT 2:3 kawo Herodosay hessa siyidi dagamidess, Yerusalamen diza asay wuri izara dagamidess.
MAT 2:4 izika qesista halaqatane woga tamarsizayta kumeth shishidi “Kirstosay awan yeletane” gidi oychidess.
MAT 2:5 istikka izas “nabey ‘Yuda bitan dizare hane Bistaleme ta dere Isra7eele nagizadey neppe kezana gish hanko Yuda harizaytappe azanikka guxakka’ gidi xafida gish izi Bistaleme Yudan yeletana” gidi yotida.
MAT 2:7 Hesafe guye Herodosay he erata/ eranchata/era asata geemara xeygisidine ista hasa7isidi xolintezi istas betida likke wode eridess.
MAT 2:8 Erata Bistaleme yedidi “bidi gutha naza koyte takka bada izas goynana mala demida mala ha taakko simidi izi awan dizakkon tas yotite” gidess.
MAT 2:9 Eratikka/eranchatikka kawoy istas gidaysa siydappe guye bida. Away mokida bagara istas betida xolintey ista kalethidi gutha nazi dizaso gathidess.
MAT 2:10 isti xolinteza be7ida wode daro ufa7etida.
MAT 2:11 Keth gelidi gutha naza iza ayeyra Maramira demidine gulbatidi izas goynida. Be saxine saxine doyidi worqqa, ixanene, karbe giza miish izas imida.
MAT 2:12 Isti Herodosakko simononta mala agumon kehi nagistana mala getetida gish hara ogera ba dere simida. Gibxe gango
MAT 2:13 Era asati/erati/eranchati/ bidappe guye Goda kitanchay Yosefos agumora betidi “Herodosay gutha naza wodhana koyiza gish ne simana wode ta nena erisana gakanas dendada gutha naza ayeyra ekada duge Gibxe biitta baqatada hen dasha” gidess.
MAT 2:14 Hesa gish Yosefoy dendidi ayiyo nazara ekidi gidothara duge Gibxe bidess.
MAT 2:15 Herodosay hayqana gakanas hen de7idess. “Ta naza ta Gibxe bitappe xeygadis” gidi Goday kasse nabe dunan hasa7idays hayssan poletidess.
MAT 2:16 Eranchati/erati/ era asati iza balethidaysa erida wode Herodosay kehi hanqetidess. Eranchati izas kasse yotida wode mala ba assi kitidi namm7u laythane namm7u laythappe garsata Bistalemenine Bistaleme yushon diza gutha atuma nayta wursi wodhisidess.
MAT 2:17 Hesan “Yeehoyne gita waaso girthay Raman siyetidess, Era7ela ba naytas yekadus, nayti wuri wurida gish minanas danda7onta ixadus” getetidi nabe Ermasan yotetidaysi poletidess. Gibxeppe Nazrete simo
MAT 2:19 Herodosay hayqidappe guye Goda kitanchay agumora Yosofos Gibxe biittan betidi
MAT 2:20 “Dendada gutha nazane iza ayiyo ekada Isra7eele biitta sima, naza wodhana koyizayti hayqida” gidess.
MAT 2:21 Yosefoy dendidi naza ayeyra ekidi Isirae7el biitta simidess.
MAT 2:22 Gido atin Arkela7osay ba awa Herodosa ola Yuhudan kawotidaysa siydine he banas babidesss. Goday agumora izi he bonta mala yotida gish Galila awuraja bidess.
MAT 2:23 Nazrete getetiza kaatammayo bidi hen dus oykidess. Kasse nabetan “Nazrawe getistana” getetidi kassetidi sinthafes hasa7etidaysi kumidess.
MAT 3:1 He wode xaammqiza Yaanisay asas “salo kawotethi matida gish inte nagarappe simite” gi sabakishe Yihuda bazo biittara yidess.
MAT 3:3 “Goda ogge othite, wogga oggezakka lo7othite gishe bazo biittan wasiza qaala” getetidi kasse nabe Isayasan yotetidaysi Yaanisa gishasa.
MAT 3:4 Yanisay gamela ithikkeppe othetida mayo mayess, ba xesikka dafora gixess, izi miza qummay degera essanne bole.
MAT 3:5 Yerusalameppe, kumetha Yiudappene Yordanosse shahaaththaa matan diza dere wursoppe asay wuri Yaanisakko woodhdhidi
MAT 3:6 ba nagarakka izas paxxishe Yordanosse shaafan iza kushen xaamaqetidess.
MAT 3:7 Daro farsawetinne saduqaweti izi xamaqizaso yishin beydi Yaanisay “inteno shoshato iintte sinthara diza hanqoppe atana mala intena oni beside?”
MAT 3:8 Iintte iintte nagrappe simidaysa besiza otho othitte.
MAT 3:9 ‘Nu away Abiramey nus dess’ gizaysan interkka intena balethopitte, ta intess Xoossi hayta shuchatappe Abirames na othi denthanas danda7es gays.
MAT 3:10 Hekko beeyxxey qanxxanas miththata garsan gigeti utidess. Hesa gish Lo7o ayfe ayfonta mithi wuri qanxxistanane taman yegistana.
MAT 3:11 tani marotethas hathan xamaqays haray ato shin ta iza caama tokanas besontadey, tappe adhiza minoy guyera yana, izikka Xillo Ayananine tamn intena xxamaqqana.
MAT 3:12 kath suragiza layday iza kushen dess, izikka ba kaththa baleza piti geeshana, ba gistezakka kaththa di7en qolana, happa gidikko to7onta taman xxugana.” gidess.
MAT 3:13 He wode Yesusay Yanisan xamaqistanas Galilappe Yordanose shaafa bidess.
MAT 3:14 Gido atin Yanisay “haysi hanena tani nenan xamaqistana besishin neni waanada taakko yayi?” gidi izara eqetidess.
MAT 3:15 Yesuusaykka “aykkoyka ba ero garki! hayssa othidi nuni xilloteth wursi polans nus beses” gidess. Yansaykka iza qofa ero gi ekidess.
MAT 3:16 Yesusay xamqetidi hathappe kezida mala herakka saloy doyetin Xossa ayany woolle kafo milatidi iza bolla wodhishin beyidess.
MAT 3:17 Saloppekka “tani izan ufa7etiza nazine ta siqiza ta nazi hayssakko” giza qalay siyetidess.
MAT 4:1 Hessappe guye Xillo Ayanay Xala7en pacistana mala Yesusa duge bazo bita efidess.
MAT 4:2 Oydu tammu galasine oydu tammu qama xoomidappe guye Yesuusay gafidess.
MAT 4:3 Pacizaysi Yesusakko shiqidi “ne Xoossa na gidikko ane hayta shuchata uketh gidana mala azaza” gidess.
MAT 4:4 Yesusaykka “ ‘assi Xoossa dunappe keziza qalanppe atin kaththan xala deenna’ getti xafetidess” gidi izas zaridess.
MAT 4:5 Kalethidikka Xala7ey yesusa gesha katamayo efidi meqidese ketha quste bola kesidi
MAT 4:6 “Ne Xoossa na gidikko ane hayssappe duge guppa, ays gikko ‘ne toy suchan dhuphetonta mala kitanchati ba kushra nena denthana mala ne gish Xoossi ba kitancha kiitana’ geteti xafetidess” gidess.
MAT 4:7 Yesusaykka “qasse maxafatan ‘ne Xoossa Godda paaccoppa’ geteti xafetidess” gidi zaridess.
MAT 4:8 Qasekka Xala7ey Yesusa kehi dhoqqa zuma bola kesidi salo gufanthon diza kawotetha iza bonchora wursi ehi besidi
MAT 4:9 “ne kundada tas goynikko hayssa ubbaa ta neess iimana” gides.
MAT 4:10 Yesuusay hayso “Xala7e ta sintahppe hakka neni ne Godas Xossas goyna, izas Xalala goyna getetidi xafetidess” gidess.
MAT 4:11 Hesappe Xala7ey iza agidi bidess, kiitanchatikka yiidi iza madida.
MAT 4:12 Yesusay Yansay qachetidaysa siyidi gede Galila simmidess.
MAT 4:13 Nazirete katama agidi Zabilone Niftaleme heran aba matan diza Qifirnahome kataman duus oykidess.
MAT 4:14 Hesan Zabilonenine Niftaleme bitan, Yordanoseppe he pinthan aabba gaxxara ehaaththaiza ogge matan diza ayhuda gidonta Galila dere asay, dhuuman diza derey wolqama po7o be7idess, Hyqo kuwa garsan diza deress po7oy po7idess' getetidi nabe Isayasa dunan kasetidi hasa7etidaysi poletidess.
MAT 4:17 Yesuusay he wodeppe domidi “Salo kawotethi matidess marota gelitte” gidi sabakko oykidess.
MAT 4:18 Yesuusay Galila aabba achara adhishe nam7u ishantata, heytikka Phixxirosa getetiza Simonane iza isha Indirasa be7idess. Istika mole oykizayta gidida gish mole oykiza gite aban yegishe detess.
MAT 4:19 Yesusay ista “ha yite tana kalite, ta intena asa oykiza as othana” gidess.
MAT 4:20 Isti herakka mole oykiza giteza yegidi yesusa kalida.
MAT 4:21 Guth sinthe bishe hara nam7u ishantata Zabdosa na nam7ata Yaqobene Yanisa be7idess. Istika ba awa Zabdosara wogolo gidon mole gite lo7othetes, Yesusaykka ista xeygin
MAT 4:22 isti herakka wogolozane ba awa agidi kalida.
MAT 4:23 Yesusay ista mukuraben asa tamarsishene kawotetha mishiracho qaala sabakishe qasse dere garsan ay hargey sakizaytakka pathishe kumetha Galila yuydess.
MAT 4:24 Hesa gedon lo7o nashoy kumetha Soore biittan siyetidess. Dereykka dumma dumma sakon daro wayzaytane daydanthi istan gelidaytane, bolappe biittan yegiza hargey dizayta, silidayta izakko ehin wursikka pathidees.
MAT 4:25 Hesafe dendidaysan Galilappe, tamu katamappe, Yerusalameppene, Yihudappe, Yordanose shaafa pinthappe yida daro asay iza kalidess.
MAT 5:1 Daro derey shiiqidaysa beyida wode Yesusay pude zuma bolla kezidi utides, iza kaalizaytika izakko yida.
MAT 5:2 Izikka ista hizigidi tamarso oykides.
MAT 5:3 ayanan bena kawushizayti anjetidayta ays gikko salo kawothi istasa.
MAT 5:4 qadhetizayti anjetidayta ays gikko isti ministana.
MAT 5:5 ashketi anjetidayta ays gikko isti biitta latana.
MAT 5:6 xiloteth gafetizaytine saamotizayti anjetidayta ays gikko isti kalana.
MAT 5:7 asas lo7o othizayti anjetidayta ays gikko istikka lo7oy othistana. ????
MAT 5:8 wozana xilloti anjtidayta ays gikko isti Xoos beyana.
MAT 5:9 saroteth oothizayti anjetidayta ays gikko isti xoosa nayta geeteti xeygistana.
MAT 5:10 xillotetha gish goodetizayti anjetidayta ays gikko salo kawotethi istasa.
MAT 5:11 Ta gedon asay intena cayikko, goodikonne iita yo wordora inte bolla haasa7ikko inte anjetidayta.
MAT 5:12 Inte salon demana waagay keehi gita gidida gish ufaysan guppitte. Ays gikko intefe kase nabetakka hessaththo gooddida.
MAT 5:13 inte ha biita asas maxine mala. Maxiney ba mal7otetha yediza gidiko zaridi demanas danda7ize? gede kare yegetidi yedheteespe atin.
MAT 5:14 Inte deres po7o. Zuma bola diza katamaya qotistanas danda7uku.
MAT 5:15 Asi xoomppe oythidi kethan diza asa wursos po7ana mala dhoqason wothetes atin gema son wothi eretena.
MAT 5:16 Hesathokka asay inte lo7o otho beydi inte salon diza inte aawa bonchana mala inte po7oy asa sinthan po7o.
MAT 5:17 Tani Musse wogane nabeta qaala sharana yida intes milatopo; polanas yadis atin sharanas yabeykke.
MAT 5:18 Ta intess tumu gays, saloyne bitay adhana gakanas Musse wogay wuri polistana atin wogappe isi pidaleykka woykko issi qerinakka shaaretuku.
MAT 5:19 Hessa gish onikka ha azazoyntafe guxizaro gidikokka othonta yegi adhikko, hankoytakka yedhi adhana mala tamarsikko salo kawotethan he uray guth geteti xeygistana. Gido atin hayta azazota othi polishe hankoyta polana mala tamarsikko izi salo kawotethan gta getistana.
MAT 5:20 Ta intes gays, inte xillotethi Parsawistapene Musse woga tamarsizayta xillotethafe aadhonta agikko salo kawoteth gelana danda7ekista.
MAT 5:21 Kasse asatas wodhopa, wodhida ura bolla pirdistana getetidaysa inte siydista.
MAT 5:22 Ta qasse intes gizay ba isha bolla wogay baynda hanqetiza ura bolla pirdistana, onikka ba isha napay gizadey dere dulata sinthan oychistana, eya giza ura ganame tama pirday naages.
MAT 5:23 Hessa gish neni yarsho shishizason Xoossas yarshana gishin ne ishay ne bolla michetidazi nes qofetikko,
MAT 5:24 ne yarshizaysa hen yarshoson aga gada koyro bada ne ishara giga, hessafe guye simada ne yarshoza Xoossas shisha.
MAT 5:25 nena kasasida ne morkey ne bolla pirdsonta mala pirdiza danay qachizaysas nena athi imonta mala qasho kethan ne wodhontamala buro ogge bolla dashe ne morkke urara elela giga gida.
MAT 5:26 Ta nes tumu gays izi pirdisi wursida gidikko wusetha isi santimiyo qanxana gakans qashoppe birshistakka.
MAT 5:27 laymatoppa gizaysa inte siydista
MAT 5:28 Tani gidikko intena hiz gays macasha amo ayferra xelida uray wuri ba wozinan izira laymatadess.
MAT 5:29 Nagara othans ne oshacha ayfey nes gaso gidiko neppe kessa wora yega, ne asatethay kumeth gede ganame taman yegistanape ne asatethafe isay pacikko lo7o.
MAT 5:30 Ne oshacha kushey nagara othos gaso gidiko neppe qanxa diga ne asatethay kumeth ganamen yegistanaysafe ne asatethafe issi bilitey ness pace gidiko lo7o.
MAT 5:31 machcho anjizadey anjida firma waraqata izis imana beses getetidees.
MAT 5:32 Tani qasse intena hizgays hara urara laymatishin beyonta dishe ba maco anjizadey wuri iza laymatana mala othes. Hesathokka anjetizaro ekizadeykka laymatida mala qodetes.
MAT 5:33 kasse asatas wordo caqofa; Xoossa sinthan ne caqidaysa naga getetidaysa inte siyidista.
MAT 5:34 Ta qass intena aykkokka caqofite gays saloy Xoossa wonbara gidida gish salon caqofite.
MAT 5:35 Bitay Xoossa soy shempizaso gidida gish bitankka caqopite woga kawo katama gidida gish Yerusalamenkka caqopite.
MAT 5:36 Inte hu7enikka caqopite inte hu7e iskistappe issineyokka bothu woykko kareth histanas danda7ekista.
MAT 5:37 hessa gish inte inte garsan hasa7etishin inte hasa7ay E ganaz E gite akkay ganas akkay gite, hessappe kare gididay wuri ita urappe yizaza.
MAT 5:38 Ayfe gishas ayfe acha gishas acha getetidaysa inte siyidista
MAT 5:39 Ta kass intes gizay ita othida urara eqetofite gido attin nes oshacha shagala baqizades hankoysakka yusha bessa.
MAT 5:40 Issi uray ne garsara maydaysa neppe ekkanas nena motikko bolara maydaysakka gujada izas imma
MAT 5:41 Issi ass nena issi sate ooge ne bana mala wolqathikko issippe nam7u dakko gidana ogge iza bays.
MAT 5:42 Nena wosizades imma, neppe tal7e ekkanas koyzades zokko zaroppa.
MAT 5:43 Ne lagge siqa, ne morke siqa getetidaysa siyidista
MAT 5:44 Ta qass intena inte morketa dosite, intena godizaytas wosite gays.
MAT 5:45 Inte hessaththo othikko inte salo awas nayta gidana. Izi awa arshe itatasine lo7otas issi bola omo imess irakka xilotasine nagaranchatas issi bola bukises.
MAT 5:46 Intena dosizayta xalala inte dosikko intes aza wagay dize? Qaraxa ekizayti hessaththo othetene?
MAT 5:47 Inte ishata xala inte sarothikko hankoytappe azan lo7eti? amnontaytikka hessaththo othetes.
MAT 5:48 hessa gish inte salo away wothoy bayndade gidida mala intekka wothoy bayndade gidite.
MAT 6:1 Assi intena beyana mala asa sinthan lo7o othonta mala nagetite, hessaotho othiko inte salo awappe waga demekista.
MAT 6:2 Inte manqotas mado immiza wode assi tana beyo gidi asa sinthan bonchetanas ogenine mukuraben xurumba punisiza qodheppe qomon hanizaytatho othofite. Ta intes tumu gays isti ba waga wursi han ekki gidida.
MAT 6:3 Inte manqotas imishin oshacha kushey othiza hadirsa kushey eroppo.
MAT 6:4 inte immoy geman gido qotan othetidaysa beyiza inte awaykka inte waga intes immana.
MAT 6:5 Inte wosishe qodheppe qomon hanizayta mala hanopite isti assi beyana mala mukurabistanine oydu ogge bola eqidi wosanas dosetes. Ta intes tumu gays isti kumetha waga ekichida
MAT 6:6 Ne wosana wosiza ne kifile gela kare ne bolla gordada geman diza ne awakko wossa. Geman othetidaysa beyza ne away ne waga nes immana.
MAT 6:7 Amanonta asay issi qaala zari zari wosiko istas siyetiza milatin isti zari zari gizaysatho intekka wosishe issi qaala zari zari gopitte.
MAT 6:8 Gido atin inte away inte wosanappe kasetidi intes azi koshizakone eriza gish inte ista milatopitte.
MAT 6:9 Inte wosishe hizgi woossite “salon diza nu Aawo ne sunththi anjjetto,
MAT 6:10 Ne kawotethi ha yo; Ne sheney salon gidida mala bitankka hano.
MAT 6:11 Hachchis gidiza kath nuus hach imma.
MAT 6:12 Nu nuna qohidaytas atto giza mala nekka nu qoho nuus atto ga.
MAT 6:13 Iittappe nuna asha attin nuna paacen gelthofa; Bonchoy medhippe medhina gakkanaas neyssakko; amin77i”
MAT 6:14 Inte intena qohidaytas ato gikko inte salo away intes ato gana.
MAT 6:15 Qasse inte asa nagara ato gonta ixikko inte awaykka inte nagra ato gana.
MAT 6:16 Inte xoomma xoomishe qodheppe qommora xoommizaytatho shulupitte. Isti ba xoommizaysa assi erana mala ba ayfeso isetes. Ta tumu gays hessaththo othizayti ba wagga kummeth ekki gidida.
MAT 6:17 Neni xoomma xoomikko ne ayfeso mecista, ne hu7e tiyista.
MAT 6:18 Hessatho ne xoommikko geman diza ne away xalala erizazine assi onikka eronta qotan gidana. Qotan othetidaysa beyza ne awaykka ne wagga ness immana.
MAT 6:19 Bil7ay mizason buqidine shiydi moretizason kaysoy bokidi kaysanas danda7izason ha bitta bola intes mishe shishopette.
MAT 6:20 Gido atin bilay manas, buqidi woykko shiyidi moretonta kaysoy bokki ekkana danda7ontason hen salon intes mishe shishite.
MAT 6:21 Ne mishay dizason ne wozanay hen dess.
MAT 6:22 Ayfey asatethas po7o hessa gish ne ayfey paxa gidikko ne kumetha asatetethay po7o gidana.
MAT 6:23 Ne ayfey hargancha gidikko ne kumetha asatethay dhumma xala gidana, histikko nenan diza po7oy dhumma gidikko qasse dhummay wanida gird gida dhumma gidande?
MAT 6:24 Issi uray nam7u godas othana danda7ena. Issa ixidi nam7anthoza dossana, woykko issa bonchidi nam7antha leqana Xoossasine mishas nam7atas gathi othanas danda7etena.
MAT 6:25 Hessa gish ta intena inte dussa gish ay mino? ay uyino? ay mayino? gidi hirgopitte gays. Shempoy qumappe ashoy mayoppe adhene?
MAT 6:26 Anne salo kafota xelite zeretena maxetena di7en qoletena shin inte salo away ista muzes. Inte istafe kehi adheketi?
MAT 6:27 Ane intefe daro wayetidi bes immetida laytha bola hara issi galas gujana danda7iza asi dize?
MAT 6:28 Qsse mayo gish aazas hirgeti? anne co denban diza cishata xelite, daburetena woykko suqetena.
MAT 6:29 Hessa gish ta intena gizay haray ato shin kawo Solomonaykka ba bonchora ha cishatappe isiney mala lo7o maybeyna.
MAT 6:30 Inteno pace amanoy dizayto hachi asa ayfen betidi wonto taman wodhana mata hayssatho mayziza xoossay intena hessafe lo7othi athi mizanas danda7ene?
MAT 6:31 Hessa gish nu ay mane, ay uyane, ay mayne gidi hirgopitte.
MAT 6:32 Hankko ammanonta asay hayssa demans daro qopes. Haysi wuri intes koshizaysa inte salo away eres.
MAT 6:33 Hara wursoppe sinthatidi Xoossa kawotetha xilloteth koyte hayti wuri intes gujistana.
MAT 6:34 Hesa gish wontos keezi qopopitte, wonto metoy wontos aqo. Issi issi galasay bess gidiza metora dess.
MAT 7:1 Inte bola pirdetonta mala hara asa bolla pirdofitte.
MAT 7:2 Inte pirdida mala inte bola pirdistana. Inte makkida mishara intes makistana.
MAT 7:3 Ne ayfen diza gita miththa beyonta dashe ne isha ayfen diza qeri bura aazas xelay?
MAT 7:4 Ne ayfen gita mith dishin ne isha “ane ta ne ayfeppe qeri buuryo kesays” ganas wana danda7ay?
MAT 7:5 Neno qodheppe qommon hanizayso kasistada ne ayfen diza gita miththa kesa gida hessafe kalada ne isha ayfen diza bura kesanas lo7otha xelandasa.
MAT 7:6 Be ton yedhonta malane simidi intena saxi dakerethonta mala anjetidaysa kanata sinthanine Worqa gudunthata sinthan yegopitte.
MAT 7:7 wosite intes imistana, koyte inte demana kare qoxitte intes doyistana.
MAT 7:8 Wosidades wursos imistana koyza uray demana qoxizades karey doyistana.
MAT 7:9 inte gidoppe isadenay uketh wosikko shuchu immiza aaway dandde?
MAT 7:10 woykko mole wosikko shoshu imizadey dande?
MAT 7:11 Histin inte itata gidi utidi inte naytas lo7o miish immo erizayta gidikko inte salo away iza wosizaytas waanidi adhiza lo7o miish imane?
MAT 7:12 Hessa gish hara assi intes othana mala inte koyzaysa mala intekka haratas othite. Musse wogayne nabeti hayssan kuuyetes.
MAT 7:13 Xuntha pengera gelitte, dhaysana efiza oggey gita, pengeykka aho, daro asay he pengezara geles.
MAT 7:14 deyos gathiza ogey gidiko xuntha, pengeykka xuntha, gelanaytikka guuthata xalala.
MAT 7:15 istas garssa bagay *sudhume /kana suyqqe/ mala* giidi utidine dorssa ite mayidi inte gido gelid garssara oothiza wordo nabetappe naagetite.
MAT 7:16 inte ista ista oothon erandista. Aguntha worappe woyney, qum7ude agunthafe etha ayfey maxetizee?
MAT 7:17 Hessathokka lo7o mithi wuri lo7o ayfes iita mithika iita ayfe ayfees.
MAT 7:18 lo7o mithi iita ayfe ayfanas danda7ontaysa mala iita mithi lo7o ayfe ayfanas danda7ena.
MAT 7:19 lo7o ayfe ayfonta mithi wurikka qannxxistanane taman yegistana.
MAT 7:20 hesssa gish inte ista ista ayfen erana.
MAT 7:21 salon diza ta aawa shene polonta dishe tana ‘godo godo’ gizay wuri salo kawotethi gelena.
MAT 7:22 he gelas daroti “godo godo nuni ne sunthan buro hananaysa yootibeykoni? ne sunthan daydanthi kesibeykoni? ne sunthan daro malata oothibeykoni?” gaana shin
MAT 7:23 he wode ta istas “ta intena mulekka erabeykke inte iitati taape haakite” gaada qoncera ta istas yootana.
MAT 7:24 histikko hayssa ta qaala siyidi oothon peyshizadey ba keeth zaala bolla keexizade milatees.
MAT 7:25 Handzidze iray bukin haroykka gogides carkoyka carkides, keethaka sugides, shin zaala bolla keexetida gish kundibena.
MAT 7:26 Haysa ta qaala siyidi oothonta uray gidiko ba keeth ace bolla keexxida eeya ura mala.
MAT 7:27 Handzidze iray bukin haroyka harotides, carkoyka carkides, he keethaka sugides keethayka iita kundethi kundides.
MAT 7:28 Yesuusay tamarsi wursin asay iza timirtezan malaletides.
MAT 7:29 Gasoyka Musse wogga tamarsizayta mala gidonta izi godatethi diza asa mala tamarsida gishasa.
MAT 8:1 Yesuusay zuma bolafe wodhin daro derey iza kaalides.
MAT 8:2 Isi inchiracha hargey dizadey yesuusakko shiiqidi iza sinthan gulbatidi “Godo ne koykotana pathanas dandayasa” gides.
MAT 8:3 Yesuusay ba kushe yedidi “ta dosadis paxa” gin adezi he hargezappe heerakka paxides.
MAT 8:4 Qasseka Yesuusay adeza “ne paxidaysa oonasika yootopa, gido attin baada nena qeeses beessa. Musey azazida yarshoza gaatha, hesika istas markka gidana” gides.
MAT 8:5 Yesuusay qifirnahome gakidda mala xeetu wotadaratas halaqay izako shiiqidi iza hizgi woosides.
MAT 8:6 Godo ta ashkaras asatethay oothonta ixin daro saketidi keeththan zin7on dees gides.
MAT 8:7 Yesuusaykka izas ta baada pathana gides.
MAT 8:8 Xeetu wotadarata halaqay izas zaaridi “ta neena ta keeth gelithanas besizade gidike, gido attin ne haan daada issi qaala xala giiko ta ashikaray paxana.
MAT 8:9 Taasikka tana azaziza halaqati taape bollara deetes, qassekka taas azazetiza wotadarati taape garssara deetes istafe isa ba giiko bees qase isa haaya giikko yees ta ashikara ‘hessa ootha’ giiko oothees” gidess.
MAT 8:10 Yesuusay iza zaarozan malaletidi bena kaalizayts “ta intes tumu gaysi haray atoshin Isira7eelista garsan hayssa mala amanoy dizade isadeka demabeykke.
MAT 8:11 Ta intes yootays daroti away mokiza bagafene wuliza bagafe yana salo kawotetha madan Abramentara Yisaqantaranne YaaqobEntara issipe utana.
MAT 8:12 Salo kawotethi istas gidana besiza asati heen kare duman yegistan heenka yehoyne acha garceth gidana” gidess.
MAT 8:13 Yesuusaykka xeetu wotadarata halaqas “ne ba ne amano mala nees hano” gides; ashikarazi heraka paxides.
MAT 8:14 Yesusay buro Pixirosa keth gelishin Pixirosa bolotiya micha harge sakistada zin7idaro be7idess.
MAT 8:15 Izi kushe Yesusay bochin michay agin dendada Yesusa mokadus
MAT 8:16 He galasa omars daydanthi oykida daro asata Yesusako ehida. Izikka tuna ayanata ba qalara istafe kesidess, harganchatakka wursi pathidess.
MAT 8:17 Isayasay “izi nu harge ekidess nu sakokka tokidess” gida qalay hayssan poletidess.
MAT 8:18 Daro asay iza yuyi adhidaysa beydi Yesusay asa abafe he finth pinana mala azazidess.
MAT 8:19 Hesa wode issi ayhude amano tamarsizadey izakko shiqidi “tamarsizayso ne biza wursoso takka nena kalana” gidess.
MAT 8:20 Yesusaykka izas zaridi “workenats oolay dess, salo kafotas kafo kethi dess, tas asa nas gidikko hu7e gelithizasoykka bawa” gidess.
MAT 8:21 Iza kaliza issi hara uray qasse “Goddo koyro bada ta aawa moogo?” gidess.
MAT 8:22 Izi qasse “hayqidayti ba hayqeth moogeto; neni gidikko tana kaalla” gidess.
MAT 8:23 Hesafe guye Yesusay wogolon gelin iza kalizaytikka wogolon kali gelin issippe bida.
MAT 8:24 Qopponta aba gidon danbalay dendidi wogoloyo mitana gakkanaas ista waysidess. Hessi wuri hanishin yesusay dhiskidess.
MAT 8:25 Iza kalizayti iza begothidi “Godo nu dhayos nuna asha” gida
MAT 8:26 Yesusaykka ista “inteno amanoy pacidayto aazas hayssa mala babeti?” gidess. Hessappe dendidi carkozane abba danbala izi hanqin herakka sirph gidess.
MAT 8:27 Istika “Haysi abayne carkoykka izas azazetizadey izi wanidade” gidi malaletida.
MAT 8:28 Izi aba pinidi Gergesenone giza dere gakida mala daydanthi oykida nam7u asi dayti ba diza dufope kezidi iza gagida. Assi he ogezara adhanas danda7etonta mala asas daro kehi meto gidi detes.
MAT 8:29 Istika “Xoossano ness nunara aza gogotethi dize? Nu wodey gakkonta dishin nuna xugana yadi” gidi wasida.
MAT 8:30 Hen istafe guth hakidi daro guduntha wudey issi bola hemetes.
MAT 8:31 Daydanthati Yesusa “ne nuna kessana gidikko haytan daro gudunthatan nu gelana mala nus fiqadde imma” gidi wosida.
MAT 8:32 Yesusakka ista “bitte” gides. Daydanthatikka istafe kezidi gudunthatan gelida. Gudunthati wurikka ba dizaso afora bezumishe aban gelidi hathan mitetidi hayqida.
MAT 8:33 Guduntha hemizayti elelidi katamay dizaso bidi gudunthay hanoysane daydanthi ista oykida asata bola hanidaysa wursi asas yotida.
MAT 8:34 Katama asay wuri Yesusara gaganas kezidess. Yesusay beydine ista dere yedi banamala iza wosida.
MAT 9:1 Hesafe guye Yesusay aba bola wogolora pinidi kasse ba diza katama yidess
MAT 9:2 Hen issi gunda ura asay zaphara tokidi Yesusakko ehidess. Yesusaykka ista amano beydi gunda ura “aykoy ba hayso nazo ne nagaray ato getetidess” gidess.
MAT 9:3 He wode woga tamarsizayti “haysi Xoossa casha giidi ba ulora gugimida.”
MAT 9:4 Yesusay ista qohaaththaa eridi “inte wozinan iita yo aazas qopeti?
MAT 9:5 Ne nagaray ato getetidess gusapene dendada ba gusafe awaysi kawushe?
MAT 9:6 Gido atin asa nas biita bola asa nagarappe maranas sheney dizaysa eranamalasa giidi gunda adeza” denda ne zapha ekada gede neso ba” gidess.
MAT 9:7 gunda adezikka dendidi beso bidess.
MAT 9:8 Dereykka hessa beydi malaletethanine babon kumidi hayssa sire godatethi asas immida Xoossa galatidess.
MAT 9:9 Yesusay heppe dendidi bishe issi Maatosa gizadey qaraxa qanxisizason utidaysa beydi tana kala gin dendidi iza kalidess.
MAT 9:10 Yesusay Maatosa son maada bola dishin daro qaraxxa shishizaytine nagranchati izakko yidi izarane iza kalizaytara issippe manas utida.
MAT 9:11 Parsaweti hessa beyidi Yesusa kalizayta “intena tamarsizaysi qaraxxa shishizaytarane nagranchatara wosti istara issippe kath mize? gi oychida.
MAT 9:12 Yesusaykka isti gizaysa siyidi ista” aakkimey koshizay saketidaytas atin saketonta paxatas gidena.
MAT 9:13 Hessa gish inte biidi “yarsho gidonta maroteth dosays giza qaala birshech tamaritte. Nagaranchata xeygana yadis atin xilota xeyganas yabeyke” gidess.
MAT 9:14 Xamaqiza Yanisa kalizayti Yesusakko yidi “nunine parsaweti xoomishin nena kalizayti aazas xoometene” gi oychida.
MAT 9:15 Yesusay istas “mishira lageti mishiraz istara dishin mozistana danda7izo? mishiray istafe ekistana wodey yana, isti he wode xoomana gidess.
MAT 9:16 Gal7a mayo bola oratha qanxeth wothi sikiza asi dena. Gal7a bola orath wothi sikiko orathazi galaza pedherethidi ha das darsana.
MAT 9:17 Oonikka oratha woyne caje gal7a ogoron gujenna. Gujiza gidikko ogorozi dhuqana, woyne cajezikka gukkana, ogorozikka go7ay bayndaz gidana. Gido atin oratha woyne cajey oratha ogoron gujetes, hessa malara woyne cajezine ogorozi lo7o nagetidi gam7ana. FFFFFF needs foot note.
MAT 9:18 Yesusay asa hasa7ison dishin issi shuumey iza sinthan kundidi “tas na dara hayqana gaysu iza paxa dana mala yada ne kushe izi bola wotharki” gin
MAT 9:19 Yesusay dendidi izara bidess, iza kalizaytikka izara bida.
MAT 9:20 Tamane nam7u layth kumeth izippe suthi gukiza issi macashi Yesusape guyera yada iza afala macara bochadus.
MAT 9:21 Iza hessa othiday haray atiko iza afala xera bochizakko ta faxana giza amanoy izi wozanan diza gish bochadus.
MAT 9:22 Yesusaykka guye simi xelidi macashayo “aykkoy ba ta naye nena ne aamanoy pathidess” giin maccashaya herakka paxxa agadus.
MAT 9:23 Yesusay shuumeza kethako gakishin derey zayeranne dinkera wasishe yeekizaysa be7idi
MAT 9:24 Kichite naya dhiskadus atin hayqqabeyku giin isti iza bolla miicida.
MAT 9:25 Derey wuri keethafe kezin izi keeth gelidi nay kushe oykides; nayaka denda eqadus.
MAT 9:26 Wooreykka dizason dizason laaletides.
MAT 9:27 Yesusay heepe bishin nam77u qooqeti “Dawite no nuna maarariki” giidi waasishe iza geedo kaalida.
MAT 9:28 qooqetika yesuusay gelida keeththa iza kaalidi gelida. yesuusaykka ista “ta inte ayfe pathana dandda7izaysa amaneeti?” giidi oychides. istikka ee godo gida.
MAT 9:29 hessafe guye yesuusay ista ayfe bochidi “inte amano mala intes hano” gidees.
MAT 9:30 Isita ayfeykka xeelides yesuousaykkaoonikka hayssa eronta mala” giidi minthi yootides.
MAT 9:31 Gido atin isti kezidi heera wurisoson yesuusa gish woresida.
MAT 9:32 Isiti heepe kezishin daydanthi oykida isi duuna muume ura yesuusako ehida.
MAT 9:33 Daydanthazi kezidape guye he duuna muume adezi hasa7a oykidess; derezikka malaletidi “hayssa mala hanoy Isra7eele biitan haniin nu beyi erokko” giida.
MAT 9:34 Gido atin parsawista zaaridi iza “daydanthi kesizay daydanthata halaqana” gida.
MAT 9:35 Yesuusay ista mukuraben tamarisishene xoosa kawotetha mishiracho yootishe qasekka harge wursoppe asa pathishe katamanine mandaratan yuuyides.
MAT 9:36 Asay wuri heemizadey baynda dorssa mala keehi metotetidi xeelizay bayndade gididaysa be7ida wode istas daro michetides.
MAT 9:37 Bena kaalizaytikka “maxa gakida kaththay daro shin maxi shiishizayti guuthata.
MAT 9:38 Hesa gish kaththa goday kaththakko oothanchata yedana mala woosite gides.”
MAT 10:1 Yesuusay bena kaaliza tamane nam77u
MAT 10:2 Tamane namm7u hawarista sunthay hayssafe kalizaysa; koyro Pixerosa getetiza Simona, Iza isha Indirasa Zabdosa na Yaqobene iza isha Yanisa
MAT 10:3 Filiphosane Bertelemosa, Tomassane qaraxa shishiza Maatosa, Ilfosa na Yaqobene Tadosa,
MAT 10:4 Be bagas zili7etiza Simonane guyeppe Yesusa hayqos athi immida Asqoroto Yuda
MAT 10:5 Hayta tamane namm7ata wurssi gede amanonta dereta gath bopitte Samariya asa katamma gelopite
MAT 10:6 atin Isra7ele keth gidida dhayda dorsatakko bite.
MAT 10:7 Bidine salo kawoteth matidess gidi sabakite.
MAT 10:8 Harganchata pathitte, hayqidayta hayqoppe denthite, inchiracha hargizayta geshite, daydanthata kesite inte mela ekidaysa mela immite
MAT 10:9 Worqa, bira woykko xarqimala gidin inte kissen oykofite.
MAT 10:10 Othnchas hachis hachis gidizazi koshiza gish inte oges giidi shinqqe, koshonta mayo, caamma woykko gufe eki bopitte.
MAT 10:11 Issi katama woykko issi mandara inte geliza wode intena mokkanade koyi demidi iza kethan shempitte heppe kezana gakanas hen takitte.
MAT 10:12 Inte onna kethekka gelishe saro gite.
MAT 10:13 He kethay sarotay besiza keth gidiko inte sarotay he kethas gido, sorotay besonta keth gidikko inte sarotay agidi intes simmo.
MAT 10:14 Ay assikka intena mokki ekkanasine inte giza siyanas koyontade gidikko he ura kethappe woykko he katamaappe kezishe issta bolla yiza gomeppe inte atidaysas markka gidana mala inte to bolla diza guddula pitidi kezitte.
MAT 10:15 Ta intess tummu gays pirda galas he katmay bolla gakkana pirday Soodomma bolane Gamora bolla gakkida pirdappe deexo gidana.
MAT 10:16 Ta intena dorssa mala sudhumista gidora kitays. Hessa gish shosha mala cincatane wole mala ashikkista gidite.
MAT 10:17 Assay intena oykkidi pirdiza dulatas shishana, ba mukuraben intena garafana, hessa gish istafe nagetite.
MAT 10:18 Ta gedon dere harizaytakkone kawotakko intena efana. Ista sinthenine amanonta asata sinthan inte markka gidana.
MAT 10:19 Intena isti oykkiza wode nu ay gi hasa7ino, woz gi mal/th/s/e immino gi hirgoppitte. He wode inte gaanazi intes immistana.
MAT 10:20 Intenan hasa7anay inte aawa ayanappe atin intena gidekista.
MAT 10:21 Ishay ba isha hayqos aathi imana, aaway ba na bolla, nayti bena yelidayita bolla dendidi hamakal7anane hara asa wodhisana.
MAT 10:22 Ta gish asi wurikka intena ixxana. Gido atin wurseth gakkanaas mini eqiday izi atana.
MAT 10:23 Asay intena inte diza heerape gooddikko haraso kichite. Ta intes tumu gaysi inte isra7eele katama wursi gakkonta dishin ta asa nayi yaana.
MAT 10:24 Ashkaray godappe woykko kaalizadey kalethizadefe aadhena.
MAT 10:25 Tamarey bena tamarisizayssa mala woykko ashikaray goda mala gidikko hesi izas gidana. Keetha aawa be7el zebula giikko so asa ays hessafe iita geetene?
MAT 10:26 Hesa gish istas babopite; geemetiday qonconta qotetiday geeshi kezonta atena.
MAT 10:27 Ta intes dhumara yootidaysa poo7on haasa7ite haythan siyidayssa qonchen haasa7ite.
MAT 10:28 Asho wodhikofe atinshempppo wodhanas danda7ontaytas babopite hessafe ashone shemppone gaaname taman dhaysanas danda7izaysas babite.
MAT 10:29 Issi santen bayzetiza nam77u gashe kafotappe isiniyakka inte salo aawa sheney baynda co kunda atiku.
MAT 10:30 haray ato shin inte hu7e iskeykka taybon dees.
MAT 10:31 hessa gisha babopite daro gashe kafotape inte waagay aadhi bonchetidaza.
MAT 10:32 asa sinthan taas markatizades taaka salon diza ta aawa sinthan izades mrkatana.
MAT 10:33 qase asa sinthan tana kadhidhade taka salon diza ta aawa sinthan iza kadhana.
MAT 10:34 Ta biita bolla saroteth ehanas yida intes milatopo; maasha ehanas atin saroteth ehanas yabeyke.
MAT 10:35 Tani yiday na aawappe, maca na aayipe, machcho bolotippe shaakanasa.
MAT 10:36 Asas morkey so asa gidana.
MAT 10:37 Taape aathidi ba aawa woykko ba aayo siiqizadey taas gidanas besena. Taape aathidi ba atuma na woykko, meeca na siiqiza uray taas gidanas besena.
MAT 10:38 Mesqele tookidi tana kaalonta uray taas gidanas bessenna.
MAT 10:39 Be shemppo aashshanas koyza uray dhayses; ba shemppo ta gish aathi imizadey aashes.
MAT 10:40 Intena moki ekizadey tanakka moki ekes. Tana mokki ekizadey tana kitidadekka moki ekess.
MAT 10:41 Issi nabe nabetethan moki ekizadey he nabeza waga demana. Xillo ura iza xillotetha gish mokki ekkiko he xilloza waga ekkana.
MAT 10:42 Hessa gish ta intess tummu gays onikka hayta guthatappe tana kalizade gidida gish issi xu7a irxa hath ushikko hiniskka wagay dhayena.
MAT 11:1 Yesusay bena kaliza tamane nam7u asatas azazo immi wursidappe guye tamarsanasne sabakanas Galilan diza katamta bidess.
MAT 11:2 Yanisay qasho kethan dishe kirstosay othiza hanota siyidi bena kalizayta izakko yedidi ass ashizadey yana getetiday nene ye hara nagino gidi oychidess.
MAT 11:4 Yesusaykka zaridi “biidi inte sidaysane inte beyidaysa Yanisas yotite.
MAT 11:5 Qoqeti xeletess wobeti hamutetes inchracha hargizayti geyetes tuuleti siyetes hayqidayti hayqoppe paxi dendetes manqotas mishracho qalay yotetes.
MAT 11:6 Tanan dhuphetontadey anjetidade.
MAT 11:7 Yanisa kalizayti bidappe guye Yesusay asas Yanisa gish hizgidess “azi beyanas duge bazo bideti carkoy qathiza shombaqo beyanas yideti?
MAT 11:8 Woykko az beyanas kezideti? Lo7o mayo mayidi lo7i utidade beyana yideti? Lo7o mayo mayidi lo7izayti kawota kethan deteess.
MAT 11:9 Histin az beyana kezideti? nabe beyana kezideti? Ee ta intes gays nabeppe adhizaysa beyanasa.
MAT 11:10 “Ne bana ogee neess gigisanade neppe sinthara kalethada ta ness kitana getetidi iza gish kasse xafetida uray izakko” gidees.
MAT 11:11 Ta intess tumu gays maccashappe yelettida asappe xamaqiza Yanisa milatiza uray biita bolla dendibeyna. Gidikkokka Xoossa kawotethan asa wursoppe lafa uray Yanisappe aadhana.
MAT 11:12 Xamaqiza Yaanisa wodeppe ha simmin ha7i gakanas salo kawotethi daro bagara sugetees. Izzo demanayti mino asata xala.
MAT 11:13 Nabetikka Musse wogaykka wuri Yaanisa wode gakkanaas buroppe hananaysa yotida.
MAT 11:14 Histikko inte ekkana koykko izi yana getetida Elasay izakko.
MAT 11:15 Siyiza haythi diza uray siyo.
MAT 11:16 Haysa ha wode asa azan lemusso? Giyan uttidi ba lagista “Nu intess dith dixin inte duribeykkista yeho zilalith zilalin yekibeykista giza nayta milatetes.
MAT 11:18 Yaanisay musafene ushafe naagetidi yida gish daydanthara dess gida.
MAT 11:19 Ta asa nay mashene uyashe yiin haysi midi kalonta asa, ushanchane qaraxa shishizaytasine nagaranchatas lage gida. Gido attin Xoossa eratethi ba othon xiladus.
MAT 11:20 Hessappe guye Yesusay izi malatata othida katama asay marotethan gelonta agida gish “Kurazinene Betesayda intena aye inte bolla othetida malatay Xirosa bolane Sidona bolla othetidakko isti maqa maydinne bidinthan utidi beni beni marotethan geli gidanashin.
MAT 11:22 Hessa gish tani intes gizay firda galas inteppe adhidi Xiirosasine Sidonas qixaatey kawuyana.
MAT 11:23 Hanne Qifirnahome pudde salo dhoqu dhoqu ganas koyadi? Gido atin neni duge si7ole wodhandasa, ne bolla othetida malatay Sodomen othetidakko Soodomey hach gakanas daanakoshin.
MAT 11:24 Hessa gish ta nena gizay pirda galas qixatey neppe Soddomas kawuyana. /s Kirstosay immiza shemppo
MAT 11:25 Hessa wode Yesusay hizgidi wosidess. “Salo bitta Godo, ta awo, hayssa daro eranchatappene cinccatappe qotada qeri naytas ne qoncisida gish ta nena galatays.
MAT 11:26 Aabo Ee haysi ne sinthan lo7o ne shene gididi betidess.
MAT 11:27 Wurikka ta aawappe tass imetidess, aawappe atin naza gish eriza uray bawa, qasse nazappene nazi ba shenen qoncisida urappe haray aawa eriza uray ba.
MAT 11:28 inteno, tokkoy dexidaytine daburidayti wurikka taakko ha yitte, takka intess shemppo immana.
MAT 11:29 Ta qambara tokitte tappekka tamaritte tani ta wozinan aadane ashke inte shemppos inte shemppo demana.
MAT 11:30 Ta qambaray shaykone ta tohoy kawushe.
MAT 12:1 Hesappe guye Yesusay sambata galas kaththa gidora adhi bidess. Iza kalizaytikka gafida gish tiya duthidi shigechi muus oykidda.
MAT 12:2 Parisaweti hessa beyidi Yesusa “hekko nena kalizayti sambata galas oothistanas besontaysa oothetess gidda.”
MAT 12:3 Izikka istas zaridi “Dawiteyinne izara diza asati gafida wode izi ay othidakkone nababibeyketi?
MAT 12:4 Xoossa keth gelidi qesistappe attin Dawiteyne izara dizayti bochanas besonta dumma uketh midess.
MAT 12:5 Woykko qeseti sambata sharidi meqidess gidon otho othikko moro gidontaysa ooritte wogappe nababibeyketi?
MAT 12:6 Gidikkokka ta intess gizay meqdeseppe adhizadey han dess.
MAT 12:7 “Yarsho gidonta ta maroteth dosays” giza qaalay ay gusukunne inte erizakko xillota bolla pirdekistakkoshin
MAT 12:8 asa nay sanbatas godda” gidees.
MAT 12:9 Heppe izi gede adhishe ista mukurabe gelidess.
MAT 12:10 Henikka issi kushe silidadey dess. Yesuusa kasasanas gasso koyidi “sambata galas pathanas besize?” gidi iza oychidess.
MAT 12:11 Izikka ista “inteppe isadde dorsi sambata galas olan gilikko ba dorssa izi gelidi ollafe gochi kessi erene?
MAT 12:12 Histikko assi dorssappe kehi adhene? hessa gish sambata galas lo7o oothoy digetena” gidess.
MAT 12:13 Addeza “ne kushe pidisa” gidess, addezikka ba kushe pidisin hinkko kusheza mala paxa gididees.
MAT 12:14 Giddo atin parsaweti heppe kezidine Yesuusa wosti oyki wodhanakone ba garsan zoretidda.
MAT 12:15 Yesusay ista qohaaththaa eridi heppe haraso deesh gidess. Daro derey iza kalidess harganchatakka wursi pathidess.
MAT 12:16 Izi onakone asas yotonta mala ista azazidess.
MAT 12:17 Hesikka haniday nabe Isayasan “Ta doridayne ta izan ufa7etiza ta nay haysich; ta ayanappe ta iza bolla wothana, izikka amanonta deretas tumu pirda awajana, oyetena, woykko wassena. Izas qalaykka karen siyetena, Tuma pirda xonos gathana gakanas tinceti utida shomboqokka menthenane cuwatiza muqadakka toysena, amanonta dereti iza ufaysan nagana” getetidi yotetida tinbite qalay polistana.
MAT 12:22 Hessappe guye daydanthi oykin xelanasine hasa7anas dayda7onta issi ura Yesusakko ekki yida. Yesusaykka iza pathin addezi xelanassine hasa7anas dandaydess.
MAT 12:23 Assay wurikka malaletidi “haysi addezi Dawite nasha?” gidess.
MAT 12:24 Giddo atin parsaweti hessa siyda wode “Haysi addezi daydanth kesizay daydantha halaqa bi7el zebula wolqan xala gidanas besses” gida.
MAT 12:25 Yesusay ista qofa eridi “ba garsan isay issappe shaketiza kawotethi wurikka kundana, ba garsan shaketiza katamay woykko ketha assi minena.
MAT 12:26 Xala7ey Xala7e kesiza gidkko Xala7ey ba garasan shaketidess gusa. Hessatho hanikko iza kawotethi wani minana danda7ize?
MAT 12:27 Tani bi7el zebula wolqan kesiza gidikko inte nayti aza woliqan kesane? Hessa gish inte nayti inte bolla pirdana.
MAT 12:28 Gido atin tani daydanth kesizay Xoossa ayanan gidikko Xoossa kawotethi intekko yidess gussa.
MAT 12:29 Woykko issi uray wolqara dizade keth gelidi mishe bonqana koyikko kasetidi he wolqara dizadeza oyki qashonta wosti bonqane? Qachidappe guye bonqana dandayes.
MAT 12:30 Tanara gidontadey tanara eqetes, tanara issippe shishonta uray wurikka lales.
MAT 12:31 Hessa gish ta intess tumu gays nagara othoyne cashi wuri asas ato getistana shin Xillo ayana cayida uray maretena.
MAT 12:32 Ay assikka asa na bolla hasa7iza iitta qaalay maristana shin Xillo Ayana bolla hasa7iza iita qaalay gidikko hayssa ha woden gidin woykko buro yana woden gidin maroy deena.
MAT 12:33 Mithi wuri ayfen eretizaysa mala inte lo7o ayfe demana mala intes lo7o mithi deyo, intes iita mithi diza gidikko inte ita ayfe ekkana.
MAT 12:34 Inteno marzera diza shoshato inteni iitata gidi utidi wosti lo7o hasa7anas dandayeti? Ulo garsan kumidazi dunara hasa7etess.
MAT 12:35 Lo7o assi ba wozinan kunthi wothida lo7o yooppe lo7o hasa7es, iitta assikka ba wozinan kunthi wothidda itatethappe iitta yo kesses.
MAT 12:36 Gido atin ta intess gizay asay ba hasa7ida hada qaala wurso gish pirda galas wurikka oychistana.
MAT 12:37 Gassoykka ne qalappe dendidaysan ne xilada atanane ne qalappe dendidaysan ne bolla pirdistana
MAT 12:38 Hessappe guye issi issi Musse woga tamarsizaytine parsaweti Yesusa “astamare, nu neppe malalsiza malata beyanas koyos” gida.
MAT 12:39 Izi istass zaridi “ha iitane layma yeletay malata oyches gido attin nabbe Yoonasa malatappe atin hara malatay imetena” gidess.
MAT 12:40 Yoonasay gita mole ulo giidon heedzdzu qamane hezu galas gami7ida mala asa nay hezu galasine hezu qamma bitta ulon gam7ana.
MAT 12:41 Nanawe asay pirda galas hayssa ha yeletara dendidi ha yeleta bolla pirdana; gasoykka Nanawe asay Yoonaasa markatethan maroteth gelida gishasa. Hekko Yoonaasappe adhizadey han dees.
MAT 12:42 Dugge baga dere kawoya Solomoone erateth siyanas bitta gaxappe dendada yidda gish pirda galas iza hayssa yeletethara dendada ha yeletetha bolla pirdana. Hekko Solomooneppe adhizadey hayssan dess.
MAT 12:43 Tuna ayanay asappe kezidi sheemppo demanas hathi baynda mela bitan dabures, gido attin ba koyiza shemppo demena.
MAT 12:44 Hessappe qasse kasse ta dizaso siimma bana gidi beniso izi simishin kasse izi dizasoy aykoyne baynda mela keth gididi geyidine gigeti dizaysa deemess.
MAT 12:45 Hessafe bidi hara beppe itiza lapun iitta ayanata benara ekidi yeess. Istika he uran gelidi deyana. He uras kasse dusafe guye dusay iita gidana. Haysa iitta yeletethaskka hessa mala hanana.
MAT 12:46 Yesusay asas yotishin iza ayiyane ishati iza yochana koyidi karen eeqidashe;
MAT 12:47 Issi uray hekko ne ayane ne ishati nena hasa7isanas karen eeqidi nena koyetes gidess.
MAT 12:48 Yesusaykka ta aya oone? ta ishatich isti oonante? gidess.
MAT 12:49 Be kushera bena kalizaytakko malatidi, ta ayane ta ishati haytanta.
MAT 12:50 Salon diza ta aawa shene othizayti wurikka tass isha michchonne ayo gidess.
MAT 13:1 He galaskka Yesusay kethafe kare kezidi abba achan utidess.
MAT 13:2 Daro derey iza yuyi adhidi gidothida gish asa aba gaxan agidi wogolo gido geli utidi,
MAT 13:3 Daro yo lemusora hizgi yotidess “issi goshanchay zereth zeranas kezidess
MAT 13:4 Izi zerishin issi issi zerethi ooge achan wodhiin kafoti yidi maxi mida.
MAT 13:5 Issi issi zerethi melane shuchatiza bitta bolla wodhin bittay mela bitta gidida gish elele caarides.
MAT 13:6 Gido atin away awin shulidine xapho yedonta agida gish melidess.
MAT 13:7 Issi issi zerethay aguntha gidon wodhidess, agunthaykka dicidi carecha culidess.
MAT 13:8 Hara zerethikka loo7o orde bittan wodhidi ayfekka ayfidess, issay xetu, issay usupun tamu issay hezu tamu ayfe immidess.
MAT 13:9 Siyiza haythi diza uray siyo.
MAT 13:10 Hessafe iza kalizayti izakko shiqidi aazas lemusora yotay gida.
MAT 13:11 Izikka istas hizgidees “Salo kawotetha xuuray intes imitidess istas gidikko immetibeyna.
MAT 13:12 Dizades dizaysa bolla gujistanane darana shin bayndadafe hina dizarakka ekista gidana.
MAT 13:13 Ta hayssatho lemusora yotizay isti siyshe ezigonta gishine xeelishe deemonta gishasa.
MAT 13:14 Isayasay “Inte sisa siyanashin yushi qopekista, xeelo xeelana shin wozinan wothekista, dereza wozinay mumides, ista haythaykka siyena, xelonta mala ba ayfe qili7imida, hesi bayndakko issti ba ayfera beydine ba haythara siyidi ba wozinan yushi qopidi taakko ha simin ta issta pathana shin” gida tinbite qalay istan poletidess.
MAT 13:16 Inte ayfey xeliza gishine inte haythati siyiza gish inte anjetidayta.
MAT 13:17 Ta intes tumu gays daro nabetine daro xillo asati ha7i inte beyzaysa beyanasine ha7i inte siyzaysa siyanas amotida shin istas hanibeyna.
MAT 13:18 Histikko ha7i zeretha lemusoza birshech siyite
MAT 13:19 Kawotetha qaala siyidi yushi qoponta ay asa wozinappekka Xla7ey yiidi zaretida zeretha bogi ekki gidana. Hessikka ogge bolla wodhida zeretha.
MAT 13:20 Shucha bolla zaretidaysi qaala siyda mala ufaysan siyidi herakka ufaysan ekizade milates.
MAT 13:21 Gido atin xapho yedanas danda7onta agida gish daro gam7onta qaalla gedon metoyne godetethi yiza wode eleli dhuphetes.
MAT 13:22 Aguntha gidon zaretida zerethay qaala siyidi hayssa ha alamezas daro metotethane duretetha qofan baletidine culetidi ayfe immonta asa mala.
MAT 13:23 Lo7o bitan zaretida zerethay qasse qaala siyidi yushi qopizade milates tuma ayfe ayfes, isay xetu issay usupun tamu issay hezu tamu ayfe imidess.
MAT 13:24 Yesusay hara lemiso istas hizgi yotidess; salo kawotethi ba gosha bittan lo7o zereth zeridade milates.
MAT 13:25 Gido atin assi wuri zin7ida wode iza morkey yidi gisteza gidon lesho zeridi bidess.
MAT 13:26 Gisitezi dicidi ayfe ayfiza wode leshoykka izara issippe betidess.
MAT 13:27 kaththa goda ashikarati godakko shiqidi “godo, ne goshan lo7o zereth zerabeykki? Haysi leshoy awappe yide. gida.
MAT 13:28 Izikka istas hessa morkey othidess gidess. Ashikatatikka nu bidi leshoza harumana mala koyiza gi oychida.
MAT 13:29 Izikka istas, akay hanena gasoykka inte leshoza harumishe gistezara gathi shodana,
MAT 13:30 aagite maxa wodey gakanas issippe dico. He wode maxizayti leshoza kasetidi qori maxidi taman xuganas miirqen miirqen qachite, gisteza qasse shishidi gotaran/ pedhen/ gelthite gada ta intes yotan gidess.
MAT 13:31 Hara lemuso istas hizgides “salo kawotethi issi uray ba gade gidon zerida etha ayfe mala.
MAT 13:32 Etha ayfey hara miththa ayfe wursoppe daro lafa gidikkokka dicada miththa wursoppe gitta gidaysu. Salo kafotikka izi hange bolla keexidi deyana gakanas gita mith gidaysu.
MAT 13:33 Ha7ikka hara lemuso istas hiz gi yotides salo kawotethi macashi liixxey dendanamala liixxe gidon gujida gutha irsho milataysu.
MAT 13:34 Yesusay hayssa wursi asas lemusora yotidess. Lemusoy baynda issinokka yotibeyna.
MAT 13:35 Hessankka kasse nabe donan “ta duna ta lemuson doyana; alamey medhetosoppe ha simin qotetidaysa ta hasa7ana” geteti yotetidaysi poletidess.
MAT 13:36 Hessappe asa agidi keth gelidess. Iza kalizayti izakko shiqidi kaththa gidon diza leshoza gish ne yotida lemusoza birshech nus yota dida.
MAT 13:37 Izikka istas zaridi lo7o zereth zeriday asa na
MAT 13:38 Gosahy hayssa alameza, lo7o zerethay kawotetha nayta gididaysa besess, leshoy qasse Xal7e nayta.
MAT 13:39 Leshoza zeridi bida morkey dabilosa. Maxxa wodey alame wursethi gidishin maxxizayti Xoossa kiitanchata.
MAT 13:40 Leshoy qoretidi taman xugetizaysa mala alame wursethan hessaththo hanana.
MAT 13:41 Asa nay ba kitanchata kittana istikka nagaras gaso gididaytane iita ochizayta iza kawotetha garsappe wursi qori kessana.
MAT 13:42 Yeehoy dizasone ache garcizaso daro wolqamma taman ista yegana.
MAT 13:43 Hessa wode xilloti ba aawa kawotethan awa arshe mala po7ana. Siyiza haythi diza uray siyo.
MAT 13:44 Salo kawotethi gade gidon qotetida mishe milates. Issi uray he mishiyo demidi zari qotidess. Ufaysafe dendidaysan bidi bess dizaz wursi bayzidi he mishiya diza biitta shamidees.
MAT 13:45 Hessathokka salo kawotethi al7o worqa koyza zal7ancha milatess.
MAT 13:46 Daro al7o gidida inqo giza shucha demida mala bidi bess dizaz wursi bayzidi shamidess.
MAT 13:47 Qassekka salo kawotethi abba gidon yegetidi dumma dumma mole oykidda mole gitte milates.
MAT 13:48 mole oykizayti gittey kumiza wode gochidi abba mata kessida. Hen utidi lo7o lo7o mole qoridi keechen gujida. Iitta molista wora yegida.
MAT 13:49 Alame wursethan hessaththo hanana. kitanchati yidi nagaranchata xilotappe shakidi yekizasone ache garcizaso gede to7onta taman yegana.
MAT 13:51 Yesuay ista haysi wuri intess gelide? gidess. Istika E gida.
MAT 13:52 Izikka zaridi “hessa gish salo kawotetha xuuray gelida Musse woga tamarsizadey oonikka izas miniji wothida al7o mishappe oorathane kasse ceega miish kessizade milates” gidess.
MAT 13:53 Yesusay hayssa lemusota yoti wursidi heppe haraso bidess.
MAT 13:54 Gede ba dere biidi ista mukuraben asa tamarso oykidess. Istika malaletidi haysi adezi hayssa eratethane hayta maalatata oothana wolqa awappe demide?
MAT 13:55 Haysi anaxeza na dene? iza ayeyi sunthi Maramo dene? Iza ishati Yaqobene Yosefone Simonane Yihuda gidetene?
MAT 13:56 Micheti nunara dizayta gidetene? Histin haysi adezi hayssa wursi awappe ekide? gida.
MAT 13:57 Hesa gish isti izi gizaysa ekkibeytena. Yesusay istas “nabey ba derenine ba kethan bonchetena atin harason bonchetes” gidess.
MAT 13:58 Isti amanonta agida gish daro malatata hen othibeyna.
MAT 14:1 He wode Galila dere hariza Herdosay asay Yesusa nashizaysa siydess.
MAT 14:2 Herdosay ba ashikaratas “Hessa gidikko xamaqiza Yanisay hayqoppe dendidi yidess gusakka! Haysi wuri gitta malatay iza kushen othetizay hessasa” gidess.
MAT 14:3 Herdosay ba isha Piliposa machcho Herodiyada gason Yanisa oythidi qasho keth (woynene) yegidess.
MAT 14:4 Gaasoykka Yanisay Herodossa ne izo ekkana mala wogga gidena gida gishasa. Footnote- Pilip is stil alive
MAT 14:5 Heredosaykka yanisa wodhanas koyshin asay Yanisa nabe mala xeliza gish babidess.
MAT 14:6 Herodosay ba yeletetha galas Herodiyada naya yethan iza ufaysida gish naya iza oychidaz wursi imanas izis caqidess.
MAT 14:8 Nayakka ayeyi zoren xamaqiza Yanisa hu7ey keren wothada ah7i hanini tas imma gadus.
MAT 14:9 He wode kawoy michetidess. Gido atin caaqida gishine izara diza imathata gish giidi nay oychoy polistanamala azazidess.
MAT 14:10 Kiitidine Yanisay woyne kethan dishin qoodhdhe qanxisidess.
MAT 14:11 Qanxetida hu7eza keren wothidi nays imida. Nayakka ekkada ba ayeys immadus.
MAT 14:12 Yanisa kalizayti iza aha ekidi moogidine hanidaysa wursi Yesusas yotida.
MAT 14:13 Hessa siyida mala Yesusay kasse ba dizaso agidine wogolon gelidi berkka hara poqethaso bidess. Dereykka hessa siydi katamay dizasoppe tohora iza kaalidess.
MAT 14:14 Yesusay wogolozappe wodhishe daro asa beydi asas michetidess. Saketizaytakka pathidess.
MAT 14:15 Galasaykka qammi qammi bizaysa beyidi iza kalizayti izako shiqidi haysi nu dizasoy bazokko, gadeykka qami qami biza gish gede mandara bidi bes manaz shamana mala asa yeda gida.
MAT 14:16 Gido atin Yesusay ista “inte asas manaz imite atin asay banas koshena gidess.
MAT 14:17 Istika istas zaridi “hayssan nus ichachu ukethine nam7u molistappe atin haray bawa” gida.
MAT 14:18 Izikka ista ane he dizayta ha tass ekki yite gidess.
MAT 14:19 Qassekka asay maata bola utana mala azazides ichachu ukethane nam7u molista ba kushen oykidi ba ayfe pude salo doqu histidi galatidi uketha menthidi bena kalizaytas imidess. Istika asaas imidda.
MAT 14:20 Asay wurikka midi kalidess. Hessappe guye iza kalizayti asappe mishin atidaysa tamane nam7u masobe kumeth shishida.
MAT 14:21 Mida asay macashane gutha nayti gujetonta atumasi xalala ichachu shi gidana.
MAT 14:22 Herakka iza kalizayti wogolon gelidi gede he pinth izappe kasetidi pinana mala azazidi asa moyzanas bess guye atidess.
MAT 14:23 Dereza moyzidape guye wosa wossanas berkka zumma bolla kezidess. Gadey dhuminkka hen zumma bolla berkka dess.
MAT 14:24 Hessa wode wogoloya abba kantha bishin bulahey dendidi daro metotho oyqidess.
MAT 14:25 Qaamappe koyro kutoy zamare baqishin (uushin) Yesusay abba bollara hamutidi iza kalizayti dizaso yidess.
MAT 14:26 Yesusa kalizaytikka izi abba bollara hamuti yishin beydi babidi iza moytil7e gidine babidi wasida.
MAT 14:27 Yesusaykka herakka aykkoy ba tanakko babofite gidess.
MAT 14:28 Pexirosay Godo, nena gidikko ta abba bollara hamutada neekko bana mala tana azaza gidess.
MAT 14:29 izikka iza haya gidess. Pexirosaykka wogolozappe wodhidi hatha bolara hamutidi Yesusakko yidess.
MAT 14:30 Gido atin carkoza wolqa beyidi babida gish hathan miteteth oyqidi “Godo tana asha gidi waasidess.”
MAT 14:31 Yesusay herakka ba kushe yedi oykidi “neno amanoy pacidayso aazas sidhadi?” gidess.
MAT 14:32 Pexirosayne Yesusay wogolozan gelida mala carkoy sirphi gidess.
MAT 14:33 Hessappe guye wogolon dizayti “Neni tumu Xoossa na” giidi izas goynida.
MAT 14:34 Aaba pinidi Genserexe gizaso gakida.
MAT 14:35 Hen dizayti Yesusa gididaysa erida wode he heran yuyi adhanas diza asas kiita yedida. Asaykka harganchata wursikka Yesusakko ehidess.
MAT 14:36 Harganchati iza afala xera xala bochana mala Yesusa wosida. Bochidayti wurikka paxida.
MAT 15:1 Qassekka Yerusalemeppe yida farsawetine Musse wogga tamarsizayti Yesusako shiqidi
MAT 15:2 nena kalizayti kasse nu awata wogga aazas dhaysizo? Qumma manas kushe ecetetena gida.
MAT 15:3 Yesusaykka istas “Inte inte wogas gidi Xoossa azazo ays shareti?
MAT 15:4 Xoossi ne ayiyone ne awa boncha; ba awa bolla woykko ba aye bolla iita qaala hasa7idadey hayqo gi azazishin
MAT 15:5 inte gidikko ay asikka ba awa woykko ba ayo ta intes othanas besizaz ay mishekka Xoossas yasho atha shishadasa gikko
MAT 15:6 issi uray hessa othikko ba awa woykko ba ayo bonchontadess gista hessa gish inte wogas gidi Xoossa qaala sharista.
MAT 15:7 Inteno qodheppe qomon hanizayto Isayasay inte gish yotishe “Haysi derey tana dunan xala bonches wozinay gidikko tappe hakidees meda hada tana goyness; ista timirteykka assi wothida wogga gidi sinthappe hananaysa yotidaysi tumakko.
MAT 15:10 Yesusay asa bekko xeygidi siyite wozinan wothite
MAT 15:11 asa tunisizay awa dunara pude kezizazippe atin dunara duge gelizay tunisena” gidees.
MAT 15:12 Qasse iza kalizayti izakko shiqidi “farisaweti ne gidaysa siyidi hanqettidaysa eradi? gida.
MAT 15:13 Izi istas ta awa saloysi tokonta mithi wurikka dhoqistana
MAT 15:14 Ista agagite isti qoqeti kalethiza qoqista gidida gish qoqeti qoqe kalethikko nam7ay isay isara oyketidi afon wulana
MAT 15:15 Pexirosay Yesusa ne yotida lemusoza nuss birsha gidess.
MAT 15:16 Izikka “Inte ha7i gakanasikka eri beykista gusse? gidess.
MAT 15:17 Dunara gelizay wuri duge qanthe kanthidi gede kare kezizaysa ereketi?
MAT 15:18 Dunara kezizay gidkko wozinappe pultees; asa tunisizay hessa.
MAT 15:19 Itta qofay shemppo wodoy; laymay; laymatanas qaqatoy; kaysoy wordo markatethine asa sunthi moroy wuri wozinappe pultess.
MAT 15:20 Assa tunisizay haytantappe atin kushe mecetonta musi ass tunisena.
MAT 15:21 Yesusay heppe kezidi gede Xirosane Sidona giza dere bidees.
MAT 15:22 Issi Kanaane macashi dizara he herappe kezada Yesusakko yada “Godo Dawite no tas michista ta naya tuna ayanay oykkin keha wayaysu gada wasadus.
MAT 15:23 Gido atin izi isi qalakka izis zaribeyna. Histin hessa wode iza kalizayti izakko shiqidi “nuna kala kala waysiza gish ne izo moyzikoch? gidi iza oychida.
MAT 15:24 Izikka istas tani Isra7ele kethappe dhayda dorsatakko xala kitistadis gidess.
MAT 15:25 Macashayakka Yesusa to bolla kundada “Godo tana madariki!” gadus.
MAT 15:26 Izikka izis zaridi nayta kath ekidi kana butalatas kanas yeganas besena gidees.
MAT 15:27 Izakka E Godo butalatikka ba goda madafe gaden wodhida kath maxi metes gadus.
MAT 15:28 Hizgin Yesusay macasheyo Hane macashaye ne amanoy gita, ne koyda mala ness hano gidees; macashayi naykka herakka paxidees.
MAT 15:29 Yesusay heppe dendidi Galila Aba ach bidi hen diza issi zumma bolla kezi utidees.
MAT 15:30 Qodan daro derey wobista qoqistanne, silata, hasa7onta mumista haratakka daro harganchata ehidi iza to achan wothida; izikka ista pathidees.
MAT 15:31 Mumey hasa7ishin to silay lo7ishin wobey sit gidi hamutishin qoqey xelishin beyidi asay malaletidees; Isra7ele Godakka galatidees.
MAT 15:32 Yesusay bena kalizayta xeygidi asay tanara hezu galas gam7ida gishine mana kathi baynda gish asay tana michees. Oge bollan gafan daburidi kundonta mala mela ulora yedanas koyke” gidees.
MAT 15:33 Iza kalizaytikka hayssan aykoykka baynda bazo bitan hayssa sire dere muzanas gidiza qumma nu awappe demane? gida.
MAT 15:34 Yesusaykka ista intes appun ukethi dize? gi oychin istikka lapun ukethine qi gutha moleti deetes gidees.
MAT 15:35 Izikka derey bitta bolla utana mala azazidees.
MAT 15:36 Lappun ukethine moleza ba kushen oykidi; galatidaysappe guye menthidi bena kalizaytas imidees; istikka deras gishida.
MAT 15:37 Asay wurikka midi kalidees, Yesusa kalizayti asappe atidaysa lappun masobe kumeth shishida.
MAT 15:38 Midaytikka naytine macashay baynda adeti xala oydu shi gidida.
MAT 15:39 Yesusay dereza moyzidappe guye wogolon gelidi Megidole getetizaso gidees.
MAT 16:1 Parsawetinne Saduqawe getetizayti Yesusakko shiqidi iza pacanas saloppe malata bessa gidi oychida.
MAT 16:2 Izikka istas hizgidees “omarsa wode saloy zo7ikko gadey awana gista
MAT 16:3 wonta bolla saloy dexidi dexidees hach iray bukkana gista. Salo mala xelidi shakista shin ta yana wode malata shakanas danda7ekista.
MAT 16:4 Haysi itane laymma yeletay malata koyes gido attin yonasa malatappe hara mlatatay izas immetena. Yesusay ista hen agagidi hraso bidees.
MAT 16:5 Abba pinida mala yesusa kalizayti qumma oykanaysa baletida.
MAT 16:6 Yesusaykka qoppitte Paraawista irshopene Saduqawista irshoppe nagetite gidees.
MAT 16:7 Isti qasse ba gidon nun kath oykkonta gish hessa gidees gidi isay isara hasa7etida.
MAT 16:8 Yesusaykka ista qofa eridi inteno amanoy pacidayto “kath oykkonta gish aazas isay isara hasa7eteti? gidees.
MAT 16:9 Ichachu ukethi ichachu shi asas gidid apun masobey tiripin inte dendiakkone yushi qopekketi?
MAT 16:10 Hesathokka lappun budenay oydu shi asas gididi appun masobey tirpin inte denthidakone wozinan wothibeykista guussa
MAT 16:11 Histin ta intes yotiday kaththa gish gidontaysa wanidi yushi qopeketi? Ha7ikka parsawista irshoppenne saduqawista irshoppe nagetitte.
MAT 16:12 Ha7i izi ista qofisizay bukko denathanas gujiza irsho gish gidonta Parsawistane Saduqawista timirteppe nagistana mala gididaysi istas gelidees.
MAT 16:13 Yesusay Piliphos Qisariya getetiza bitta gakida wode bena kalizayta asay tana asa na oona gizze giddi oychidees.
MAT 16:14 Istika issi issi asay xamaqiza Yanisa ges baga asay Elasa gess bagay Ermassa woykko nabetappe issadde gidonta agena gess gidees.
MAT 16:15 Izikka ista intechi tanna onna getii gidees.
MAT 16:16 Simmona getetiza Phixirosay “neni Kirstosa deyo Xoossa na gidikki” giddi zaridees.
MAT 16:17 Yesusay “Yona na Simona neni anjetidade ness hayssa qincisiday salon diza ta awappe atin ashoynne suthi gidena gidees.
MAT 16:18 Neni Phixirosa (zala), hayssa zala bolla tani ta wossa keth kexxana ganame pengetikka izo xonetena.
MAT 16:19 Salo kawotetha qulfista ta ness immana, neni bitta bolla hanno gizay wuri salonkka hannana. Bitta bolla ne hanoppo gidaysi wurikka salonkka hanena.
MAT 16:20 Kalethidikka izi Kirstosa (Xoossappe tiyetidade) gididaysa isti onasikka yotonta mala mala bena kalizaytas lo7othi yotidees.
MAT 16:21 Hessappe ha simin Yesusay Yerusalame banasne hen dere cimatanine qesista halaqatan Musse woga tamarsizayta kushen waye ekanasne hayqanas hezantho galas hayqoppe dendanas bena kalizaytas qoncisidi yotidees.
MAT 16:22 Phixirosaykka gede issi baga gochi zaridi godo haysi ne bolla gakofo gidi hanqidees.
MAT 16:23 Yesusaykka Phixirosakko shiqidi “Hayso xala7ey hayssappe kicha neni asazappe atin Xoossa yoyi ne wozinan garsan baynda gish ne tas dhuphe gidadasa gidees.
MAT 16:24 Qassekka Yesusay bena kalizaytas “tana kalanas dosiza uray bena kado ba masqale (ba meto) tokidi tana kalo” gidees.
MAT 16:25 Be shempo ashana koyzadey wuri dhaysana, gido attin ba shempo ta gish dhaysizadey ashana.
MAT 16:26 Assi alamme kumeth harikoka shempos pacikko iza ayi madane? woykko assi ba shempo gish qanxana danda7izazi aze?
MAT 16:27 Assa nay ba awa bonchoranne salo kitanchantara yana issi issi uras iza otho mala iza waga immana.
MAT 16:28 Ta intess tumu gays hayssan eqida asata garsafe asa nay ba kawotethara yshin beyana gakanas hayqoy ista bochonta asati detees.
MAT 17:1 Usupun galasappe guye Yesusay Phixirosane Yaqobe qassekka Yaqobe isha Yanisa benara ekidi istara xala issi dhoqa zumma bolla kezidees.
MAT 17:2 Isti hen dishin Yesusa medhay lametidees, iza ayfezoy awa arshe mala po7idees iza mayoykka po7omala xolqidees.
MAT 17:3 Herakka Museynne Elasay Yesusara hasa7ishe istas bertidees.
MAT 17:4 Phixirosay Yesusa “Godo nu hanini dizakko nuss lo7okko, ne shene gidikko issi dasse ness issi dasse Musses issi dasse Elasas hezu dase otho” gidees.
MAT 17:5 Izi buro hasa7an dishin po7iza sharay ista kamidees, shara gathara, tani izan ufa7etiza ta dosiza ta nay hayssakko izi giza siyitte giza qaala girethi siyetidees.
MAT 17:6 Iza kalizaytakka hessa siyidi dayamidi ba hu7en bita bolla kundida.
MAT 17:7 Yesusay istakkidi shiqidi ista bochidi dendite babofite gidees.
MAT 17:8 Isti dhoqi gi xelishin Yesusappe atin izara hara ura onaka beybetena.
MAT 17:9 Isti zumma bollafe wodhishin Yesusay asa nay (tani) hayqoppe dendana gakkanaas inte beyonysa onasikka yotonta mala gi azazidees.
MAT 17:10 Yesusa kalizaytikka “Histin Musse woga tamarsizayti Elasay kasetidi yanas bess aazas gizo gidi oychidees.
MAT 17:11 Izikka istas Elasay tumu yidi wursikka gigisana gidi zaridees.
MAT 17:12 Gido atin ta intes gizay Elasay yidees gidikkoka asay ba koyda mala iza bolla othidees atin iza eribeyna hessathokka asa nay (tani) isata kushen waye beyana.
MAT 17:13 Hessa wode Yesusa kalizayti Yesusay isatas yotizaysi xamaqiza Yanisa gish gididays erida.
MAT 17:14 Ista garsan diza asakko simida mala issi uray Yesusakko shiqidi iza sinthan gulbatidi Godo ta na daysa bolafe yegiza hargey daro waysiza gish tas marariki daro wode taman kundedees hatha gidonkka geles.
MAT 17:16 Tani naza nena kalizaytakko ehadis shin isti iza pathana danda7ibeytena gidees.
MAT 17:17 Yesusaykka neno amanonta gela yeletazo ayde gakanas ta intenara dane? Qasse ayde gakanas ta intena danda7ane? ane naza ha taakko ehitte gidees.
MAT 17:18 Hessafe Yesusay daydantha seridi nazappe kesidees, Nazikka hini satteppe simidi paxidees.
MAT 17:19 Yesusa kalizayti xalala izakko shiqidi nuni daydantha kesanas aazas danda7ibeykoni? gidi oychida.
MAT 17:20 Izikka istas intes amanoy pace gidida gish danda7ibeykista ta intes tumu gays qeri gashe ayfe sire amanoy inte bolla dizakone hayssa zuma hayssafe dendada gede ba inte gidakko izi intess bana intena xonanay dena gidees.
MAT 17:21 Haysa malay gidikko xomanine wosan atin haran kezena
MAT 17:22 Isti Gelilan issippe dishin Yesusay ista tana asa na asas athi immna
MAT 17:23 istikka iza wodhana izikka hezantho galas dendana gin iza kalizayti kehi michetida.
MAT 17:24 Yesusayne iza kalizayti Qifirnahome getetiza so gakidappe guye maqidasse gira ekizayti Phixirosakko shiqidi inte astemarey maqidasse gira nam7u dinareza ays qanxene? gida. (issi diranrey he wode issi uras nam7u galasa damoza lagge)
MAT 17:25 Izikka istas qanxees gidees. Phixirsay keth gelida mala Yesusay kasetidi “Simona dere kawoti gira gidin woykko qaraxa gidin ba naytappe ekizoye haratappe ekiza milatize? gidees.
MAT 17:26 Phixirosaykka haratappe eketes gides. Yesusaykka histikko nayta bolla acoy ba gidees.
MAT 17:27 Histikkokka ista nu michisontamala ne mole oykiza yarda ekka bada abana yega, koyro oykkida moleza duna ne poqa demiza issi istatre ekada ta suntharane ne sunthara gira qanxa gidees. (istaterey he wode misha)
MAT 18:1 He wode Yesusa kalizayti izakko shiqidi salo kawotethan nu garasan wusofe adhanadey oone gi oychida.
MAT 18:2 Yesusay issi na xeygi ehidi ista gidon essidi “ta intess tummu gays inte simonta ixxikkone gutha nayta mala hannonta ixikko mulekka salo kawoteth gelekista gidees.
MAT 18:4 Hesa gish ha naza mala bena ziqisizadey salo kawotethan wursofe adhana.
MAT 18:5 Haysamala gutha na ta sunthan ekizadey tana ekess.
MAT 18:6 Giddo atin tana amaniza guthatappe isade dhupiza uray dexo woxa shuchu ba qodhen qachetidi aba cimana yegetidi mitetikko izas lo7o gidana.
MAT 18:7 Hana alameya asse dhuphana gasso gidida gish izis ay! dhuphey yuss agena shin dhuphezas gasso gidizades aye!
MAT 18:8 Ne kushey woykko ne toy nena dhuphanas gaso gidikko neppe qanxa diga ne nam7u keshena woykko nam7u tohora gede medhina taman yegistanappe wobe woykko to sila gidada he gede deyoy dizaso geloy ness lo7ana.
MAT 18:9 Hessathokka ne ayfey nes dhuphe gidikko neppe kessa yega, nam7u ayfera gede ganame taman ne yegistanaysappe issi ayfera deyo dizaso ne gelizaysi ness lo7o.
MAT 18:10 Hayta gutha gidoppe issiniyokka inte kadhonta mala nagetite! ta intess tumu gays salon diza ista kitanchati salon ta awa ayfeso wurso galas xeletes.
MAT 18:11 Asa nay dhaydayta ashans yidees.
MAT 18:12 Ane tass yotitte isi uras xetu dorssi dikko qass istafe issina dhaykko hankko udufun tamane udufuna zumma bolla yegidi dhaydaro koyana bi erene?
MAT 18:13 Ta intess tumu gays hanqon dhayonta udufun tamane udufun dorsistappe athidi betida dorsayn ufa7etess.
MAT 18:14 Hessathokka ha guthata garsafe issay dhayana mala salon diza inte awa shene gidana.
MAT 18:15 Ne isay nena qohikko izakko bada iza xala nenara ekada iza moro izas yota izi ne giza siyikko ne isha ne ass othasa.
MAT 18:16 izi ne giza siyonta ixikko yoyi wuri nam7u markan woykko hezu markan shatimetiza gish isade woykko nam7u ass nenara ekka bada iza hasa7isa.
MAT 18:17 Izi istakka siyonta ixikko wosa kethas yota, wosa kistahkka siyonta ixxikko izade ne amamontademe qaraxa shishizade mala qoda.
MAT 18:18 Ta intess tumu gays inte bita bolla qachiday wurikka salonkka qachetida gidana inte bitta bolla birshiday salonkka birshetida gidana.
MAT 18:19 Qassekka ta intess tumu gays inte bita bolla nam7u gididi ay gishikka ero ero gidi inte oychikko salon diza ta away intess immana.
MAT 18:20 Nam7u woykko hezu gidid ta sunthan inte shizason hen inte gidon ta dana.
MAT 18:21 Hessa wode Phixirosay Yesusakko shiqidi “Godo ta ishay tana qohikko ta izas appun to ato go? lapun to ato go? gidess.
MAT 18:22 Yesusaykka izas zaridi lappun tamu to lapun atin lapun to xala ga gike gidees.
MAT 18:23 Hessa gish salo kawotethi ashikara bolla diza mishe shishana koyda kawo milataysu.
MAT 18:24 Misha qoda oykidamala iza ashikaratappe daro milione bira achoy iza bolla dizade ekki yida.
MAT 18:25 Ashikaraykka iza bolla diza acoza qanxoy xonxa gish izikka iza machiyakka iza naytinne izas dizaz wuri bayzetidi mishay qanxistana mala iza goday azazidees.
MAT 18:26 He wode ashikarazi godaza to bolla kundidi tani ta bolla diza acoza ubbaa ness qanxana gakanas tass gutha wode imarkki gidi wosidees.
MAT 18:27 Iza godaykka izas michetidi iza galeza wirsi maridi yedidees.
MAT 18:28 He ashikarykka ba goda achappe kezidamala gutha bira (acoy) iza bolla diza ba lage demidine ne bolla diza ta mishayo ha7i hanini qanxa gidi culi oykidees.
MAT 18:29 He iza lagge ashikary tass gutha wode imarki ta ness qanxana gidi iza to bolla kundidi wosidees.
MAT 18:30 Gido atin izas gutha wode imanas koyonta ixidi iza laggezi ba bolla diza aco qanxana gakanas woynen yegidees.
MAT 18:31 Hessa izi othishin be7ida asayne hanko iza lagge ashikarati daro cichetida. Bidikka hanidaysa wursi ba godas yotida.
MAT 18:32 He wode godaz he ashikkara xeygisi ehidi hayso neno itazo ne tana wosin ne bola diza acoza ta ness agadisshin ta nena marida mala nekka ne lageza maranas besne?
MAT 18:34 Gidi iza bolla diza acoza izi wursi qanxanas gakanas qachana mala qachizaytas athi imidees.
MAT 18:35 Hesa gish inte issay issa wozinappe maronta agikko salon diza ta awaykka intena marena.
MAT 19:1 Yesusay hasa7i wursidappe guye Galila agidi Yordanose pinthan diza Yihuda awuraja bidees.
MAT 19:2 Daro derey iza hen kalin izikka harganchata pathidees.
MAT 19:3 Parsaweti iza pacanas izakko shiqidi ay gasonkka assi ba machcho anjana besize? gidi oychida.
MAT 19:4 Izikka istas Xoossi koyroppe macane adene medhidaysa nababibeyketi? gidess.
MAT 19:5 Qassekka assi awane ayo agidi ba machchira issippe gidees, nam7anykka issi asho gidetes getetidaysi hayssa gedon gidene? gidess.
MAT 19:6 Nam7ay issi asho atin sinthafe namyu gidetena. Hessa gish Xoossi gathi waxidaysa assi shakofo.
MAT 19:7 Istika izas histin Musey assi ba machcho anjidi anjo waraqata izis immidi yedo gidi aazas azazide? gida.
MAT 19:8 Yesusaykka istas Musey inte wozina mumeteth beydi machcheta inte anjana mla fiqde intes imides atin koyroppe hessamala gidena gidees.
MAT 19:9 Ta intess tummu gays ba azinappe hara urara laymatonta dishin ba machcho anjidi hararo machcho ekizadey wuri laymates izikka gidees, anjetidarokka ekizadey izira laymates.
MAT 19:10 Yesusa kalizayti izas machi wogayne azina wogay hayssamala gidikko machcho ekonta agoy lo7o gida.
MAT 19:11 Gido atin Yesusay istas issi issi istas imetida asatappe atin hayssa timirteza onikka ekkanas danda7ena gidees.
MAT 19:12 Gasoykka issi issi asay ba ayi uloppe yeletishe guddula gididi yeletes, issi issi asay asa kushen qaeatetidi gundilees, issi issi asay salo kawotethas gidi bena berka gudila othiza asikka dees. Haysa ekanas danda7izdey eekoo.
MAT 19:13 Qassekka yesusay ista bolla ba kushe wothidi wosana mala gutha nayta izakko ekki ehida gido attin iza kalizayti nayta ehida asata bolla hanqettida.
MAT 19:14 Yesusay nayta ha taakko yero digofitee, salo kawotethi haytanta malasa gidees.
MAT 19:15 Be kushe nayta bolla wothidi anjidappe guye heppe denddi bidees.
MAT 19:16 Hessappe qasse issi uray Yesusakko shiqidi “tamarsizayso medhina de7o demanas demans ta lo7o otho ayi otho? gidi oychidees.
MAT 19:17 Yesusaykka tana aazas lo7o gish oychazi? Lo7oy isade xala, gede de7oy dizaso ne gelana koykko azazota naga gidees.
MAT 19:18 Adezikka azazoti awayte? gidi oychidees. Yesusaykka zaridi “assi wodhoppa laymatoppa kaysotoppa wordo markatoppa ne awane ne ayo boncha ne shoro ne mala siqa gidees.
MAT 19:20 Wodalazikka zaridi hayssa ubbaa ta nagadis haray azi tas pacide? gidees.
MAT 19:21 Yesusaykka zaridi ne mule xilanakoykko bada ne haridaz ubbaa bayzada misha wursi manqotas imma neni salon mishe demandasa hessappe guye simma yada tana kala gidees.
MAT 19:22 Addezikka hessa siyidi izas daro mishi diza gish kehippe mishetishe bidees.
MAT 19:23 Yesusaykka bena kalizata ta intes tumu gays dureti salo kawoteth gelaysi daro meto gidees.
MAT 19:24 Qassekka ta intes gizay durey salo kawoteth gelanaysappe gamelay narfe lukora adhethi kawusha gida gidees.
MAT 19:25 Hessa siyida iza kalizayti dar qopidi histin oni atana danda7ize gidi Yesusa oychida.
MAT 19:26 Yesusaykka ista xelidi “haysi asa achan dandaetena Xoossa achan gidikko wurikka danda7etes gidees.
MAT 19:27 Phixirosaykka izas zaridi “nu nursikka agidi nena kalidos histin ha7i nu ayi demanesha gidees.
MAT 19:28 Yesusaykka istas ta intess tumu gays asa nay buro yana oratha alamen ba boncho zupane bola utiza wode inte tan lakidayti tamane nam7u zupanne bola utidi tamane nam7u Isra7ele nayta bolla pirdana.
MAT 19:29 Ta suntha gish gidi ba keth, ba ishata ba michista ba awane ba ayo ba nayta woykko ba bitta agiza assi wuri xetu kushe dikko ekkana medhina deyo latana.
MAT 19:30 gido attin daro snthe gidida asati guye gidana, daro guyen diza asati sinthana.
MAT 20:1 Salo kawotethi ba woyne atakiltte gidon othan othanchata qaxaranas maladora kezida issi akakilitey diza gadadade milataysu.
MAT 20:2 Issi galasa damuza gidizaz hasa7etidi gigidappe guye othanchata woyne akakilte otho oythidees.
MAT 20:3 Malado hezu saten kezidi othoy baynda mela giyay eqizason eqida hara asata demidees.
MAT 20:4 Inte bidi ta woyne gidon othite ta intes besiza mishe immana gidees.
MAT 20:5 Istika bida. Qassekka galasappe usuppun satenine udufun sate bolla kezidi hara othanchata othon gelithidees.
MAT 20:6 Omarsa wode tamane issi sate gidiza wode kezidi coo eqidayta harata demidi inte kumetha galas othoy baynda aazas hayssan eqeti gidi oychidees.
MAT 20:7 Istika nuna othisiza asi dhayda gish eqidos gida. Izikka ista intekka bidi ta woyne akakilte gidon othite gidees.
MAT 20:8 Gadey qamishin woyneza akakilteza goday othancha halafezas guyfe yidaytappe oykkada koyro yidayta gakans diza othnchata wurso xeygada ista otho waga qanxa gidees.
MAT 20:9 Tamane isintha sate bolla othon gelidayti yidi isay isay kumetha galasa waga ekkida.
MAT 20:10 Koyro othon gelidayti yishe ba wozinara hinkoytappe bollara daro demmna gi qopishin istasikka hinkoytara gina imidees.
MAT 20:11 Misha ekishe qanxizade bolla hayti wursethan othon gelidi issi sate xala othidayti kumetha galasa othon daburidine awan xugetidi pe7ida nusara wosta istas issi gina qanxay gida.
MAT 20:13 Izikka istafe issi ade ta jalaw nena qohabeykke issi galasas gidiza damuzen othanas tanara gigabeyki? ha7i he7i ne gisha ekada ba, ness imidaysa sire wursethan yidaysasikka ta immana koyays.
MAT 20:15 Histin ta mishan ta dosidaz othanas danda7ikina? woykko ta kiya gididaysi nena miqaynsize? gidees.
MAT 20:16 Hessa gish guyen dizayti sinthe, sinthen dizayti guye adhana.
MAT 20:17 Yesusay Yeruslame bishe bena kaliza tamane nm7ata duma ekidi hiz gidees.
MAT 20:18 Hi7a nuni Yerusalame bana gos asa nay qesista halaqasine Muse woga tamarsizaytas adhi immistana istikka izi hayqana mala iza bolla pirdana.
MAT 20:19 Iza bolla qidhi ka7anasine garafana mala wodhana malakka deretas athi immana hezantho galas izikka hayqoppe dendana.
MAT 20:20 Hessappekka Zabidosa nayta aya ba naytara Yesusakko shiqada iza sinthan gulbatada izi izis issi miish othana mala wosadus.
MAT 20:21 Izikka izo ay koyazi gidees, izakka hayti ta na nam7ati ne kawotethan isay ne oshachara issay ne hadirsara utana mala otharki gadus.
MAT 20:22 Yesusaykka zaridi inte wosizaz erekista tani uyiza xu7a inte uyana danda7ane? gidees. Istika E danda7os gida.
MAT 20:23 Izikka ta xu7appe tummu inte uyanashin ta ushachanine ta hadirsan utethi ta away gigisidadentas atin tani imizaz dena gidees.
MAT 20:24 Tamati hessa siyidi nam7u ishata bolla hanqettida.
MAT 20:25 Yesusay ista issi bolla xeygidi dere harizayti ba hariza dere bolla godatizaysamala godatethi dizayti wolqara harizaysa inte ereta gidees.
MAT 20:26 Inte garsan hessa mala hananas besena intefe gita gidana koyzadey intes othizade gido.
MAT 20:27 Intefe bolla gidanas koyzadey intefe garse gido.
MAT 20:28 Asa nay asay izas othana mala gidonta asas othanasine ba shemppo darota gish athi immanas yidees.
MAT 20:29 Yesusay bena kalizatara Yarikofe kezidi bishin daro derey iza kalidees.
MAT 20:30 Hen ayfey qoqida nam7u asati oge dunad utidi detees. Yesusay adhizaysa siyidi Godo Dawite no nuna mara gidi wasida.
MAT 20:31 Derey hayzite gidi hanqidees, gido attin isti camo waso wasishe Godo Dawite no nuna mara gida.
MAT 20:32 Yesusaykka eqidi ista xeygidi ta intes ay othana mala koyeti? gidees.
MAT 20:33 Istika nu ayfey xelanamala koyos gida.
MAT 20:34 Yesusaykka istas michetidi ista ayfetakka ba kushera bochechin herakka xelidi iza kalida.
MAT 21:1 Isti Yerusalame matan Debirezayte zuma bolla diza Betefage getetizaso gakidamala Yesusay bena kalizaytappe nam7ata kitidees.
MAT 21:2 Hano inte matan diza mandarayo bidi inte he gakida mala issi hare dizara ba guteyra qachista dishin inte demana. Birshidi ha taakko ekki yite.
MAT 21:3 Onikka intena aysi hayssatho otheti gikko Goday ista koyes gite, intena oychizadey herakka yedana.
MAT 21:4 Haysikka hanizay kase naben na Xiyonis hizgite “Hekko ne kawoy ashikke gididi hareyone hareyo guteyo togidi neekko yana getetidaysi polistanasa” gidees.
MAT 21:6 Iza kalizayti Yesusay istas yotida mala othida.
MAT 21:7 Hareyo izi guteyra ehidi ba mayo ista bolla wothin izikka harista togidees.
MAT 21:8 Derappe dariza bagay ba mayo ogge bolla micidees, baga asay miththa bonco duthi duthi ogge bolla athi athi yegidees.
MAT 21:9 Izappe sinthara biza dereyne guyera kaliza dereykka ba qaala dhuqu histidi Dawite nay galateto! Goda sunthan yiday anjetidade! Xoossi galateto! gida.
MAT 21:10 Izi Yerusalame gelida wode katama asay wuri haysi oone? gidi yark yarkidees.
MAT 21:11 Iza kalidi yida dereykka hasi Galila garsan diza Nazireteppe yida Nabe Yesusa gidene gidees.
MAT 21:12 Hessappe Yesusay maqidasse gelidi maqidasse lasah gathan bayzizaytane shamizayta godidees. Misha lamizayta xaraphezaka haraphe bayzizayta oyde shiri shiri yegidi ta kethay wosa keth getetes getetidi xafetidees inte qas bonqizayta aqoso histidista gidees.
MAT 21:14 Ayfe qoqistane toy silida asata Yesusakko maqidase ehida. Izikka ista pathidees.
MAT 21:15 Gido atin qesista halaqatine Muse woga tamarsizayti izi othida malalatane woze kawo galatay dawute nas giddo gidi wasiza gutha nayta beyidi daro hanqetidees.
MAT 21:16 Istika Yesusa hayti nayti gizaysa siyay? gida Yesusaykka istas E siyadis, Nayta dunappene dhamiza qeri nayta dunan ta galata gigisadis gizaso mulerakka nababi ereketi? gidees.
MAT 21:17 Ista yegi agidi he katamappe kezidi bitanya gizaso bidi hen eqidees.
MAT 21:18 Yesusay wontetha galas malado guye katama simishin iza gafisidees.
MAT 21:19 Oge matan issi balase giza mith beydi gede izikko shiqishin haythe xalafe atin ayfey bayndaysa beydi “Hi7appe ne bolla ayfey doppo gin balase miththay herakka meladus.
MAT 21:20 Yesusa kalizayti hessa byidine malaletidi hana balaseya wanada heraka melade gida.
MAT 21:21 Yesusaykka ista ta intes tumu gays intes amanoy dikone inte sidhonta agikko balase miththay bolla hanidaysa mala xala gidonta hayssa zumma hayssafe dhoqalistada duge aban gela inte gidakoka izi gelana gidees.
MAT 21:22 intess amanoy dikko inte wosan oychida miish wursikka ekana.
MAT 21:23 Yesusay maqidasse gelidi tamarsishin qesista halaqatine dere cimati izako shiqidi hayssa wursi ona shenen otahzi? hayssa otahanas shene ness oni imide? gidi iza oychida.
MAT 21:24 Yesusaykka istas zaridi takka intena issino oychays inte tass zariko takka ha ta othizayta ona shenen othizakone takka intess yotana
MAT 21:25 Yanisa xinqatey awappe yide? Saloppe yideye asappe? gidees. Istika nu saloppe yidees gikko histin aazas amanibeyketi? gana gidi ba garsan issay issara zoretida.
MAT 21:26 Qasse nu asappe gikko asay wurikka Yanisa nabe gidi amaniza gish nu babos.
MAT 21:27 Hessa gish Yesusas nu eroko gidi zarida izikka istas hayta ta othizata onna shenen othizakone takka intes yotikke gidees.
