MAT 21:28 Yesusay ista hiz gidees intes ay milatiz namm7u atumma nay diza issadey des izikka koyro nazakko bidi ta nazo hach gede woyne miththaso bada otha gidees.
MAT 21:29 Nazi qasse bikke gidine guyeppe muzetidi bidees.
MAT 21:30 Namm7antho nazakka kaseysathokka ba gin nazi ero gidi bonta aga gidees.
MAT 21:31 Hayta namm7atappe awwa shene poliday awaysse? Isstikka koyro naza gida. Yesusaykka istass ta intess tummu gays qaraxa shishizaytane laymatizayti salo kawotethi intefe sinte gelana.
MAT 21:32 Xamaqiza Yanisay intena xilotetha ogge besanas intekko yidess shin inte izi giza amanibeykkista gido attin qaraxa shishizaytine layamatizati gidikko amanida izi hanidazi inte beyi simidikka marotethan gelidi amanibeykkista.
MAT 21:33 Hara lemusokka siyitte woyne mith tokizasoy dizadey he woynezas birda yushi athidi woyneza ayfe gum7anas olla bokkidees. Woyneza naganas miththa bolla shakko gigisidees. Hessappe guye bita woyne miththara goyzaytas kira immidi hara dere bidees.
MAT 21:34 Boney gakishin woyneza ayfe ekanas ba ashikarata bitta goyzaytakko yedidees.
MAT 21:35 Bitta goyzayti ashikarata oykidi issa wodhida issa qasse shuchan cadida.
MAT 21:36 Gada goday kaseytappe adhiza hara ashikarata yedidees. Goyzayti ha7ikka kaseyta bolla othidaysamalakka ista bollakka polida.
MAT 21:37 Wursethan oni eri isti izas babanakone gidi ba na athi yedidees.
MAT 21:38 Gido atin bita goyzayti naza be7idamala “Haysi iza latanaysakko, ane ha yite iza wodhidi bitta latos gida.
MAT 21:39 Naza oykidi woyney toketidasoppe gede kare kessidi wodhida.
MAT 21:40 Ero woyneza goday yiza wode he bitta goyiza asata itess wositana milati?
MAT 21:41 Istika heytanta itata daro waysi wodhidi woyney toketiza gadappe besiza woyne ayfe wodera izas immiza hara gade goyzaytass kirasana gidi izas zarida.
MAT 21:42 Yesusaykka istas “Gesha maxafan gimbe kexizayti iita gidi wora yegida shuchay kethas wana hu7e gidees, Xoossi hayssa othidees, iza othoykka nu ayfes malalisizaz, geteti xafetidaysa nababibeyketi? gidees.
MAT 21:43 Hessa gish ta intess Xoossa kawotethi intefe ekistada ayfe ayfiza deretass immistana gidees.
MAT 21:44 Haysa shucha bolla kundizay meqana shuchaykka iza bolla wodhizadeykka liqana.
MAT 21:45 Qessista halaqatine Parisaweti iza lemuso lemusoy ista gish gididaysa erida.
MAT 21:46 Gido atin isti iza oyki qaphonta mala asay Yesusa nabe mala xelizagish babidees.
MAT 22:1 Qassekka Yesusay hara lemuso hizgidi yotidees.
MAT 22:2 Salo kawotethi ba nas sarge gigisida issi kawo milataysu.
MAT 22:3 Kawoykka digisas yotidayta xeyganas ba ashikarata yedidees, xegetidaytikka nu bokko gida.
MAT 22:4 Qassekka hara ashikarata kasse istas yotidayta hekko ta sanga boratanne handaida mehista shukada digisa gigisadis, wurikka gigetida gish sargeso hayitte gidi yotite.
MAT 22:5 Xeygetidayti gidikko iza xeysa wudan yegonta agidi issay ba goshaso issay ba zal7eso bidees.
MAT 22:6 Hankko atidayti ashikarat oykidi daro waysidi wodhida.
MAT 22:7 Kawoykka hanqetidi olizayta yedidi ashikara wodhidayta dhaysidees, issta katama xugidees.
MAT 22:8 Be ashkaratakka “Sargeza digisay gigidees, gido attin sargezaso xeygetidayti sarges besizayta gidibeytena.
MAT 22:9 Gede ogge bolla kezidi inte demida assi wursi ha sargge digisas xeygitte.
MAT 22:10 Ashkaratikka ogge bolla kezidi ba demidayta lo7otakka itatakka wurssi shishidi sargeza keth imath kunthida.
MAT 22:11 Kawoykka xeygetida imatha beyanas keth geliza wode sarge mayo mayonta ura demidees.
MAT 22:12 Yalo sarge moyo mayonta wanada hayssa gelanas danda7adi gi oychin adezas zarana qalay dhaydees.
MAT 22:13 Kawoykka ba ashkarata hayssa adeza tone kushe shishi qachidi hen karen diza dhumana kessi olitte hen yehoynne acha garcechi gidana gidees.
MAT 22:14 Xeygetidayti darota doretidayti gidikko guthata.
MAT 22:15 Hessappe guye Parisaweti kezi bishe iza dunappe bala qaala wosti demi oykino gidi zoretida.
MAT 22:16 Bena kalizayti Herodosa asatara izakko izakko “astamare neni tumanchane Xoossa ogge tumappe tamarsizade gididaysane onasikka dumma mado othonta wursiqa issi mala ne xelizaysa nu eros” gidees.
MAT 22:17 Ness ay misatizakkone ane nus yota qesares gira qanxanas besize? nesene?
MAT 22:18 Yesusaykka ista gene qofa eridi “inteno qodheppe qomoto tana yon balethi oykanas aazas koyeti? gidees.
MAT 22:19 Inte gira qanxiza misha anne tana besite gin istikka issi dinare giza miish izas ehida.
MAT 22:20 Izikka hayssa misha bolla diza misiley onayse? xafey onayse gidees.
MAT 22:21 Istika izas qesareysa gida. Izikka istas zaridi qesareysa qesares Xoossisa Xoossas imite gidees.
MAT 22:22 Hessa siyida wode malaletidine iza agagidi bida.
MAT 22:23 Hayqidaytas dendoy bawa gidi amaniza saduqaweti he galas Yesusakko shqidi hizgi oychida.
MAT 22:24 Tamarsizaso Mussey issi uray machcho ekidi na yelonta hayqikko iza ishay hayqidaysa machcho ekidi ba isha latiza na yelo gidees.
MAT 22:25 Nu achan lappun ishati detes shin koyro ishay machcho ekidi na yelonta hayqida gish kaallo ishay iza machchiyo ekidees.
MAT 22:26 Namm7antho ishaykka hayqida ishatho na yelonta hayqidees, hessathokka hanishin macashaya lappuntha isha geladus.
MAT 22:27 Wursethan macashaya hayqadus.
MAT 22:28 Hessa gish lappunati wurikka izo ekkida shin hayqoppe dentha galas macashaya lappuntappe awaysa machcho gidane?
MAT 22:29 Yesusaykka istas zaridi “Gesha maxafatanne Xoossa wolqa inte eronta gish inte baletista” gidees.
MAT 22:30 Hayqoppe dendidappe guye asay sallo kitanchata mala gidana atin eketenane geletena.
MAT 22:31 Hayqidayta dentha gish gidikko Xoossi tani Abrame Xoossa Yisaqa Xoossa Yaqobe Xoossa gidi intes yotoysa nababibeyketi? Xoossi paxata Xoossa atin hayqethata Xoossu gidena.
MAT 22:33 Derykka hessa siyidi iza timirtezan malaletidees.
MAT 22:34 Yesusay Saduqawista co7u hisitidaysa siyidi Parsaweti issi bola shiqetida
MAT 22:35 Ista garsafe issi Musse woga lo7ethi erizadey Yesusa pacanas koydi “astamare Musse wogata garsan wurosoppe adhizay awaysse? gidi oychidees.
MAT 22:37 Izikka zaridi ne Godaa Xoossa ne kumetha wozanappe, ne kumetha shempefe, ne kumetha qofappe dossa.
MAT 22:38 Haysi koyronne wursoppe adhiza azazo.
MAT 22:39 Namm7anthoykka iza milates, hesikka ne shoro ne hu7e mala dossa gizaysa.
MAT 22:40 Musse wogayne nabeta timirtey wurikka hayata namm7u azazotan qachetes.
MAT 22:41 Parsaweti issi bolla shiqeti dishin Yesusay ista
MAT 22:42 Kirstosa gish intess ay geti? Izi nona na? gi oychidees, istikka izas zaridi izi Dawite na gida.
MAT 22:43 Izikka istas “histin Dawitey Xillo ayana wolqan “Xoossau ta Godda ta ne morketa ne to garsan gulbatisana gakanas ne ta oshachan uta aazas gidde?
MAT 22:45 Hessa gish Dawitey iza ta Goda gidi xegikko wanidi izas na gidana danda7ize?
MAT 22:46 Izas issi qaala zarana danda7ida uray woykko he galassappe simiin iza oycho oychana xalida uray onikka betibeynna.
MAT 23:1 Qassekka Yesusay derezasine bena kalizatas hiz gidees;
MAT 23:2 Musse woga tamarsizaytinne Parsaweti Musse wonbara bolla utida
MAT 23:3 Hessa gish isti intess yotizaysa wursi othitene nagite gido attin isti dunan hasa7izaysa mala othon besonta gish inte ista otho kalofite.
MAT 23:4 Hessathokka assi tookanas danda7onta dexo toho qachidi asa hashe bolla wothetes shin bess gidkko biradhe xerankka bochetena.
MAT 23:5 Ista otho wursi assi beyana mala othetes, ba ashenkintabe (maxafa garsappe xafi ekida issi issi xiqisista kitabe sikidi liphe bolla woykko kushen qachizaz) oothetees. Be mayo macara adusetees.
MAT 23:6 Gibizay dizason boncho so mukurabenkka sinthara utana dosetes.
MAT 23:7 Hesathokka giya gidon saro getistanasine asay issta astamarento gana mala koyetees.
MAT 23:8 Inte gidikko astamare geteti xegetoppitte, inte astamarey issa xala gidishin inte wurikka issay issas ishnta.
MAT 23:9 Salon intess aaaway xala diza gish bitta bolla onakka awa gidi xegoppitte.
MAT 23:10 Inte astemarey issi kirstosa xala gidida gish inte “astemarento” getopitte.
MAT 23:11 Inte garsan wursoppe adhizadey intess othizade gidana.
MAT 23:12 Bena dhoqisizadey kawuyana, bena kawushizadey bonchetana.
MAT 23:13 Inteno qodheppe qomoto Musse woga tamarsizayte, inteno Parsaweto asay Xoossa kawoteth gelonta mala asa bolla inte penge gordiza gish intena aye? Inte intes gelekistane gelanas koyzaytakka gelthekista.
MAT 23:14 Inteno qodheppe qomoto Musse woga tamarsizayto qassekka Parsaweto intena aye! azinay baynda macashata ketha kalosishe asa ayfe sinthan adusa wossa inte wosiza gish inte iita pirda pirdistana.
MAT 23:15 Inteno qodheppe qomoto (dunan cimzayto) Musse woga tamarsizayto qasseka Parsaweto issi ura ayhude amanon gelthanas abba bollarane bitta bollara yuyi daburdine amanthida asa intefe nam7u kushe athidi ganame na inte kesiza gish intena aye.
MAT 23:16 Inteno intees qoqi utidi harata kalethizayto intena aye! Onikka maqidassen caqiko aykoy ba gido attin maqidasse gido diza worqan caqiko caqo gomey gakana gista.
MAT 23:17 Inteno qoqidayto baletidayto worqafene worqa dumathida awaysi adhize?
MAT 23:18 Hesathokka onikka yarsho yarshizaso bolla caqiko aykoy ba shin yarshizaso diza yarsho bolla caqikko caqoy gomes gista.
MAT 23:19 Inteno qoqeto yarshoppene yarsho shishizasoppe awaysse adhizay?
MAT 23:20 Hessa gish yarsho shishizaso bolla caqizadey yarsho soza bollane yarshizaso bolla diza miish wurson caqess.
MAT 23:21 Hessathokka maqidasseza bolla caqiday maqidasanine iza gidon aqizaysan
MAT 23:22 Salon caqizadeykka Xoossa alganine algga bolla utidaysan caqees.
MAT 23:23 Inteno qodheppe qomoto Musse woga tamarsizayto Parsaweto intena aye! Assotappene anugappe katkal7appe tamappe issino immista shin wogatappe wanatizayta heytikka tuma firda, marotethine ammaneteth gidikko kadhidista. Heyta agonta dishe haytanta inte othanas intes besess shin agidista.
MAT 23:24 Inteno qoqe kalethoto u7e gaccidi uyista shin gamela mume mitista.
MAT 23:25 Inteno qodheppe qomon hanizayto Musse woga tamarsizaytone Parsaweto intena aye! Xu7asine keres bolla baga qucista shin iza gidon dizaysa inte bonqanine uzetethan shisidista.
MAT 23:26 Neno qoqe Parsawezo koyrotada xu7asine keres garsa baga gesha, hessappe guye kare bagay kesh gidana.
MAT 23:27 Inteno qodheppe qomoto Musse woga tamarsizayto qasse Parsaweto bolla baga norara meshetidi lo7izayti gidoy gidikko hayqidayta meqethine daro tunanetethan kumida dufota milatiza gish intena aye!
MAT 23:28 Intekka bolla bagara asaas xilo asata milatista, inte gidoy gidikko dumma cimonine itatethan kumidess.
MAT 23:29 Inteno dunan cimizayto Musse woga astemareto qsekka Parsaweto inetena aye! Nabista dufo lo7othizayto xillo asata dufo hawultera gigisizato,
MAT 23:30 Nu awati nagista wodhiza wode nu dizakko istara zuppetokoko shin,
MAT 23:31 Inte nabeta wodhida asata nayta gididaysa inte dunara interka inte inte bolla markatista.
MAT 23:32 Histikko othetishe poletonta ogge bolla diza inte aawata otho politte,
MAT 23:33 Inteno dukiza ita shosha nayto ganame tamma pirdappe inte wani atane?
MAT 23:34 Hessa gish nabetane eranchata astamaristakka ta intess yedana, inte ista garsappe issi issi asata wodhana, bagayta inte kaqana, bagyta inte mukuraben garafanane ha katamappe hara inte godana.
MAT 23:35 Hessa gish xillo Abele suthafe ha simin maqidasenine yarsho so gidon inte wodhida Barakiyo na Zakarasa sutha gakanas bitta bolla gukida xillota sutha wursos inte oychistana.
MAT 23:36 Ta intess tumu gays kasse adhida yo wursos haysi ha yeletay oychistana.
MAT 23:37 Hane Yursalame nabeta wodhizare neekko kitetidayta shuchara cadizare cadizare hanne Yurusalemekuto aya ba ciyista ba qefe gido shishiza mala ta ne nayta shishanas apun wode koyadina shin inte gidikko koybeykista.
MAT 23:38 Hekko inte kethi kays gidi atana.
MAT 23:39 Ta intess tumu gays inte Goda sunthan yizadey anjetidade gana wodey gakanas nmm7antho tana beyekista.
MAT 24:1 Yesusay maqidasse kezi bishin iza kalizayti maqidase shucha ketha iza bessana koyidi izakko shiqida.
MAT 24:2 Izikka istas hayasa wursi xeletti? Ta intess tumu gays haysi inte beyza isay issa bola diza shuchay laletonta issi shchikka hayssatho deyena gidees.
MAT 24:3 Izi Dabirazayte getetiza zumma bolla uti dishin iza kalizayti xala izakko shiqidi ane nus yota haysi ne gizaysi ayde hanane? Ne yusasine wode wursethas malatay aze gi oychida.
MAT 24:4 Yesusaykka zaridi oikka intena balethonta mala nagetite.
MAT 24:5 Buro daroti ta kirstosa gishe ta sunthan yana, darotakka balethana.
MAT 24:6 Ollane olla gish carkotiza worekka inte siyana. Ha yoti wurikka wolqara polistana shin wursethi buro gidida gish inte hayssan dagamonta mala nagetite.
MAT 24:7 Derey dere bolla kawoy kawo bolla dendana, dumma dumma deren koshayne bitta qathi hanana.
MAT 24:8 Hessi wurikka mixas lesso mala.
MAT 24:9 He wode intena wayes athi immana, intena wodhana, ta suntah gedon dere wurson inte ixetidayta gidan.
MAT 24:10 He wode daro asay dhuphistana, issay issa athi athi immanane ba garsan ixistana.
MAT 24:11 Daro wordo nabeti dendanane darota balethana
MAT 24:12 Itatethi dariza gish darotappe siqoy irxana.
MAT 24:13 Wurseth gakanas minida uray atana.
MAT 24:14 Dere wursos marka gidana mala haysi kawotetha wungilay kumetha alamen yotistana, hessappe guye wursethi yana.
MAT 24:15 Hessa gish nabe Danelan yotetidaysa mala “dhayso tunatethi anjetidason” eqidaysa inte beyza wode (nababizadey wozinan wotho).
MAT 24:16 He wode Yihudan dizayti pude zumma bolla gangeto.
MAT 24:17 Ketha kara bolla dizadey onikka ba miish kethafe kessana gidi duge wodhofo.
MAT 24:18 Gade gidon dizadey onikka ba mayo ekka gidi so simofo.
MAT 24:19 He galasatan qanthara diza macashatasine na dhanthiza ayistas aye!
MAT 24:20 Hessa gish inte gangoy balgo woykko sanbata galas gidonta mala wositte.
MAT 24:21 He wode alamey medhetosoppe hachi gakanas hani eronta mishi sinthafekka iza milatizay baynda wolqama metoy hanana.
MAT 24:22 He galasti qamontakko asho mayida assi wuri atenashin doretidayta gish he galasati qamana.
MAT 24:23 He wode onikka hekko kirstosi hayssan dess, woykko hessan dess giza ura amanopitte.
MAT 24:24 Wordo kirstosayne wordo nabeti buro denda istas danda7etikko doretidayta balethans gidi wolqama malatatane kasse otheti eronta miish othana.
MAT 24:25 Hekko hayssa intes kasista yotays.
MAT 24:26 Hessa gish hekko hirki bazon dess gidi intess yotikko he kezobitte, hekko ilppinen dess gikko amanoppitte.
MAT 24:27 Wolqanthi away mokizasora wolqamidi away wulizaso gakanas po7izaysa mala asa na yusaykka hessaththo hanana.
MAT 24:28 Ahay dizaso anko kafoy shiqees.
MAT 24:29 Herakka he ita meto galasatappe guye awa arshey dhumana, aginay ba po7o digana, xolinteti saloppe qoqefistana, salo wolqamatikka qaxana.
MAT 24:30 He wode asa na malatay salo bolla bistana, bitta bolla diza derey wuri yekkana, asa naykka salo shara bolla daro wolqarane gita bonchora yishin asay beyna.
MAT 24:31 Kitanchatakka daro wolqama xurumba girethara yedana. Istika doretidayta oydu mezanappe salo gaxa issafe hara issi baga gaxa shishana.
MAT 24:32 Balase giza miththafe hayssa tamaritte, balase miththays unquloy cililiza wode iza haythe kesishin hessa wode boney matidaysa inte ereta.
MAT 24:33 Hesatho hayta inte beyza wode izi pengen matidaysa inte erana.
MAT 24:34 Ta tumu gays haysi wuri polistana gakanas ha yeletay adhena.
MAT 24:35 Saloy bittay adhana shin ta qalay gidikko mulekka adhena.
MAT 24:36 He galasyone he sateyo aawappe atin salo kitanchata gidinkka naza gidinkka oonikka erena.
MAT 24:37 Nohe wode handaysa mala asa na yussi hessa mala gidana.
MAT 24:38 Dhaysa hathafe kasse Nohey markaben geliza galas gakanas asay mishene uyishe, ekishene gelishe gam7idees.
MAT 24:39 He wodey gakanas azzi hananakone asay erontane hasa7ay baynda basha hathay yidi mitidaysa mala ta asanay yiza wodeykka hessaththo hanana.
MAT 24:40 He wode nam77u asati issippe goshan pey7ana shin istafe issadey ekistana, issadey atana,
MAT 24:41 Namm7u macashati woxan issippe gacana shin istafe issiniya ekkistana issiniya attana.
MAT 24:42 Histikko inte Goday yana galasa inte eronta gish begidi nagite.
MAT 24:43 Haysa wozinan wothite, kaysoy qamappe appuntha sate bolla yanakone erizakko iza miish kaysoy ekonta mala ketha aaway begidi nagana.
MAT 24:44 Assa naykka inteqopponta sate bolla yana intekka hessaththo gigetidayta gidite.
MAT 24:45 Wodera so asa qumma mizana mala goday ba ketha asa bolla shuumida amanetiza cinca oothanchay one?
MAT 24:46 Kethaaway simidi yiza wode izas immida hadara othipolishe betida oothanchay anjetidaysa.
MAT 24:47 Ta intess tummu gays Goday iza ba harida wurso bolla shuumes,
MAT 24:48 Gido atin he othanchay iita gididi ta goday gam7idi yana gidi
MAT 24:49 dendidi hankko othanchata wadha oykidi mathotizaytara mikkone uykko
MAT 24:50 izi qopponta qopponta saten iza Goday yidi
MAT 24:51 iza qanxethi ka7ana, iza exxa qodheppe qomora othizaytara othana. Henikka yehoyne acha garcethi hanana.
MAT 25:1 He wode salo kawotethi mishira mokanas xomppe oykidi kezida tammu gellaota milataysu.
MAT 25:2 He tammatappe ichachu gela7oti eyata, hankko ichachati qasse eraata.
MAT 25:3 Eyati kuraze xomppe oykida shin wurikko qolana hara nagge lamba oykibeytena.
MAT 25:4 Erati gidkko ba kurazezara wurikko gujana lagge lammba hara xarmusen oykidda.
MAT 25:5 Machiyo ekkana mishiray yonta gam7in dhiskoy dexin asay wurikka dhiskidees.
MAT 25:6 Gidi gidoth gidishin mishrazi yes kezidi moki ekitte giza xeyssa qalay siyetidees.
MAT 25:7 Hessa wode gela7oti wurikka dendidi ba xomppe xomppe oythethone gigeteth oykida.
MAT 25:8 Dogati erata nu xomppey to7ana giza gish inte lambappe nus immitte gida.
MAT 25:9 Era gela7oti istas zaridi nuss diza lambay nusara intessaranne intesara gidonta gish bidi lamba bayzizaytappe intess shamitte gida.
MAT 25:10 Isti lamba shamna bida wode mishrazi gakiwodhidees. Kasse gigeti utidda gela7oti bulacha so izara gelida, kareykka gordetidees.
MAT 25:11 Guth gam7ishe hakko gela7oti yidi “Godo Godo kare nuss doy7a” gida.
MAT 25:12 Izikka zaridi “ta intess tumu gays ta intena erikke” gidees.
MAT 25:13 Hessa gish yana galasa woykko sateza inte eronta gish gigetidi nagite.
MAT 25:14 Xoossa kawotethi bess dizaz wursi ba ashikaratas hadara immidi hara dere bana dendida issi ass milatees.
MAT 25:15 ashikaratas isas issas istta wolqama mala gigisidi issas ichachu shi birra, issas namm7u shi bira, hankoysas qasse issi shi birra immidi bidees.
MAT 25:16 Ichachu shi birra ekida adezi herakka mishan zal7e oykidi hara ichachu shi birra tirpisidees.
MAT 25:17 Qssekka namm7u shi birra ekidaysi hara namm7u shi birra wodhisidees.
MAT 25:18 Issi shi birra ekidaysi ba goda bira bitan magidi qotidees.
MAT 25:19 Ashikarata goday ba bidason daro wode gamm7i simidi misha istara shalagetidees.
MAT 25:20 Ichachu shi birra ekida ashikaray hara ichachu shi birra wodhsidaysa ekki yidi godo ne tass ichachu shi birra imadasa shin hekko hayssa ta harra ichachu shi bira wodhisadis gidees.
MAT 25:21 Iza godaykka lo7o othadasa neno lo7o ammanetida ashikarazo ne gutha mishan amanetida ass gidida gish ta nena daro misha bolla shuumana, gede ne goda ufaysaso gela gidees.
MAT 25:22 Hessathokka namm7u shi birra ekkidaysi godazakko shiqidi godo ne tass namm7u shi birra immadasa shin hekko hara namm7u shi birra wodhisadis gidees.
MAT 25:23 Godazikka lo7ethadasa hayso loo7one tass ammanetida ashikarazo neni guthan amanetidade gidida gish ta nena daro misha bolla shuumays, gede ne goda ufaysaso gela gidees.
MAT 25:24 Issi shi birra ekkida ashikaray sniqidi godo neni zeronta soppe maxizadene lalonta soppe shishiza minxe iita ass gididaysa ta erays.
MAT 25:25 Hessa gish ta babada bitta bokkada ne birra bokkida ollan mogada qotadis, ne miish nesssa beya he7i gidees
MAT 25:26 Iza goday zaridi hayso iita azala ashikarazo tani zerontasoppe maxizade lalontasoppe shishizade gididaysa ne eray?
MAT 25:27 Histin ta simma yiza wode ta misha yelora ta ekkana mala tirpisi zal7iza asas ne immanas besseseshin gidees.
MAT 25:28 Ane ha7i iza shi birra ekidi tammu shi biray dizadess immitte.
MAT 25:29 Dizades gujistanane dari dari bana bayndadeppe he diza guthayiyakka izappe ekista gidana.
MAT 25:30 Haysa go7ay baynda ashikara gede yekizasone achey garcetizaso heni karen diza dhumman kesi yegitte gidees.
MAT 25:31 Assa nay ba kitanchata wursora bonchon yiza wode ba boncho zuppane bolla utana.
MAT 25:32 Derey wuri iza sinthi shiqana izikka mehe hemiza uray desh dorsappe qori shkiza mala asa issa issape qori shakana.
MAT 25:33 Dorsata izas oshacha bagara deshata hadirsa bagara essana.
MAT 25:34 He wode kawoy oshacha bagara dizayta “inte ta aaway intena anjidayti ha yite, alamey medhetosoppe intes gigetida kawotetha latitte gana.
MAT 25:35 Gasoykka tani gafin tana muzidista, ta sametin tana ushidista, ta immatha gidada yin tana moki ekidista.
MAT 25:36 Ta kalotin tana mayzidista, ta saketin tana hargisidista, ta qashetin tana oychidista.
MAT 25:37 Xillotikka zaridi “Godo ne gafin nena ayde muzidoni?, woykko ne samotin ayde beydi nena ushidoni?
MAT 25:38 Nu ayde nena beydi immathateth mokidoni? woykko ayde ne kalotin beydi nena mayzidoni?
MAT 25:39 Hessathokka ne saketin woykko qachetin ayde beydi nena oychidoni gana.
MAT 25:40 Kawoykka zaridi ta intes tumu gays hayta lafa gidida ta ishatappe isades inte tass othida mala gana.
MAT 25:41 Qassekka hadirsa bagara dizaytas inteno qangetidayto tappe shaketidi Dabulosasine iza kitanchatas gigetida medhina taman bitte gana.
MAT 25:42 Gasoykka ta gafin tana muzibeykkista, ta samotin tana ushibeykista,
MAT 25:43 tana immathateth mokibeykista. ta kalotin tana mayzibeyketta, ta saketinine qashetin tana oychibeyketta.
MAT 25:44 Istika zaridi godo ne gafin woykko ne samotin woykko ne immath gidin woykko ne kalotinine ne sakketin woykko ne qachetin nu nenna beydi ayde ness gakibeykoni? gana.
MAT 25:45 He wode izikka istas zaridi ta intees tumu gays haninta lafa ta ishatappe issadees inte othonta agidaysi tass inte othonta agida mala gana.
MAT 25:46 Heyti gede medhina pirdan bana xilota gidikko medhina deyokko bana.
MAT 26:1 Yesusay hessa hasa7i wursidappe guye bena kalizaytas namm7u galasappe guye paziga gididaysa ereti? Assa nay kaqistanas adhi immistana gidees.
MAT 26:3 Hessappe guye qesista halaqatinne dere cimmati Qayafa getetiza qessista halaqa gibe gidon shiqidi hiillara Yesusa oythidi wodhisanas maqetida.
MAT 26:5 Gido atin asa garsan oshi dendontamala ba7ale galas gidoppo gidi qachida.
MAT 26:6 Yesusay Bitaniyan inchiracha hargera diza Simona getetizade son dishin
MAT 26:7 Issi macashi dizara wagay kezi al7o gidida albasxirose getetiza shito issi bilqaxe kumeth oykkada Yesusakko shiqada izi madan utidishin iza hu7e bolla shitoza gusadus.
MAT 26:8 Iza kalizayti hessa beydi haysi aazas mela moretize?
MAT 26:9 Shitozi daro wagas bayzetidi mishay manqotas imetizakoch? gida.
MAT 26:10 Yesusay hessa eridi hano macashayo aazas wayseti? iza tass lo7o othadus.
MAT 26:11 Manqoti wurso wode intenara detees, ta gidikko wurso wode intenara dikke gidees.
MAT 26:12 Iza shitoza ta bolla gusidaysi tana mogos gigidanasa.
MAT 26:13 Ta intess tumu gays haysi wongelay sabaketiza alame yushon awnkka iza othidaysi izo qopisizaz gididi hasa7istana.
MAT 26:14 Hessappe guye tammane namm7atappe issay Asqorotu Yihuda getetizaysi qesista halaqatakko bidi
MAT 26:15 ta intees iza atha immikko inte tass ay immane? gidees. Istika izas hezu tammu birra iza kushen taybi immida.
MAT 26:16 He galasappe simidi Yihiday Yesusa istas athi immanas giga wode nagishe gam7idees.
MAT 26:17 Uketha ba7ale giza ba7ale galas iza kalizayti Yesusakko shiqidi ne paziga manaso awan gigisana mala koyay? gida.
MAT 26:18 Izikka istas zaridi gede katamma bidi ebelo getetiza ass asstamarey ta wodey matida gish tana kalizaytara paziga ta ne kethan bochana gidees gidi yotite gidees.
MAT 26:19 Iza kalizaytikka Yesusay ista azazida mala paziga kawo gigisida.
MAT 26:20 Gadey omarsishin Yesusay tammane nam7atara madan utidees.
MAT 26:21 Isti musan dishin izi istas ta tumu gays intefe issay athi immana gidees.
MAT 26:22 Istika kehi muzetidi taran taran Godo tanesha gida.
MAT 26:23 Izikka zaridi tana athi immanadey keren tanara kushe yedizadekko gidees.
MAT 26:24 Iza gish kasse xafetidaysa mala asa nay baana, gido attin asa na athi immizadees aye anna! he uray yeletonta atidakko izas lo7okoshin
MAT 26:25 Iza athi immana Yihuday “tamarsizayso tanesha?” gides. Izikka Ee ne gida mala, gidees.
MAT 26:26 Isti musan dishin Yesusay miza qummappe ekkidi anjidees. Menthidine bena kalizaytas immidi he7itte miitte, haysi ta ashokko gidees.
MAT 26:27 Qassekka usha denthidi galatidinne bena kalizaytas immidi “wurkka hayssappe uyitte.”
MAT 26:28 Daro asa nagarappe marana gukiza ta oratha caqo suthay hayssa.
MAT 26:29 Ta intess gizay ta aawa kawotethan ta intenara oratha wogan uyana gakanas hayssappe sinthan hayssa woynne ayfe intenara uykke gidees.
MAT 26:30 Mazimure yexidappe guye pudde dabrazayte giza zumma bolla kezida.
MAT 26:31 Yesusay istas inte wuri hach ommars tanan dhuphetidi tana yegi bana, hemizaysa ta shcana mehetinne lalistana getetidi kasse xafetidees gidees.
MAT 26:32 Gido atin tani dendaysafe guye intefe sinthatada gede Galila bana gidees.
MAT 26:33 Phixirosay zaridi hankoyti wuri ne gedon dhuphetikokka tani mulekka dhuphetikke gidees.
MAT 26:34 Yesusaykka izas zaridi “tumu gays hach qamma kuntoy uuonta kassistada hezu to ne tana kadana gidees.
MAT 26:35 Phixirosay qasse nenara ta hayqana koyshikokka mulekka ta nena kadikke gidees. Yesusa kaliza hankoytikka kumeth izaysathokka gida.
MAT 26:36 Hessappe guye Yesusay bena kalizaytara gede getesemane getetizaso bidees. Istakka he bada ta wosishin inte hayssan utishite gidees.
MAT 26:37 Phixirosarane Zabidossa nayta namm7ata benara ekki bishe ogge bolla muzetethine daro qoppo oykidees.
MAT 26:38 Hessapeka ta shempiya hayqana gakanas daro muzistadus tanara minidi hanini takitte gidees.
MAT 26:39 Istappe guth gede adhidi sintha bolla kundidi “ta aawaw ness danda7etikko haysi metoy tappe adho gido attin tani koydama mala gidonta neni koyda mala hano gi wosidees.
MAT 26:40 Hessappe simidi bena kalizaytakko yidi isti dhiskishin demidees. Phixirossakka hayto asato inte tanara issi satekkone minanas xonide?
MAT 26:41 Pacen inte gelonta mala minidi wositte, ayanani gigetidees shin ashoy gidikko daburancha gidees.
MAT 26:42 Qassekka nammanthao bidi ta aawaw hayssa uyanasi tass atonta miish gidikko ne sheney poleto gidi wosidees.
MAT 26:43 Qassekka izi yishin ista ayfe dhiskoy kumida gish zin7idayta beydees.
MAT 26:44 Ista agagidi qassekka bidi hezantho kasse wodida qaala zari wosidees.
MAT 26:45 Hessappe bena kalizaytakko simidi ha7ikka shempidi dhiskideti? heko ha7i satey matidees asa nay nagaranchata kushen adhi immistana gidees.
MAT 26:46 Dendite ane boss tana athi immizadey yussa bolla dees.
MAT 26:47 Izi hasa7ishin tamane namm7atappe issay Yihiday yidees. Qessista halaqatine dere cimati yedida daro asay torane duqa oykidi Yudara issi dees.
MAT 26:48 Yudaykka ta yerizadey iza gidida gish oykite gidi kasse yoti wothidees.
MAT 26:49 Siti gi Yesusakko bidi tamarsizayso saro gishe Yesusa yeridees.
MAT 26:50 Yesusaykka ta lagge ne yida qohaaththaa polla gidees. Herakka asay shiqetidi Yesusa oykidi qachidees.
MAT 26:51 Yesusara dizaytappe issay githa mash shodidi qesista halaqaza ashikara hayth qanxidees.
MAT 26:52 Yesusaykka anne ne mash kohon zara geltha masha shodizayti mashan dhayana.
MAT 26:53 koshikko ta ta aawa oychizakko daro shiyan qodetiza izi tass yedonta agana milatize?
MAT 26:54 Hessatho othikko qasse gesha maxafatan hanana getetidaysi wani polistane gidees.
MAT 26:55 He wode Yesusay asa wonbade oykiza asatho mashne durqa ekidi tana oykana yideti? Wontin wontin maqidasen utada ta tamarsishin kasse oykibeykista shin.
MAT 26:56 Gido atin haysi wurikka hanidaysi kasse nabeti gesha maxafatan yotidaysi polistanasa. Hessa wode Yesusa kalizayti iza yegidi dhayida.
MAT 26:57 He wode Yesusa oykidi asati Muse woga astematetine dere cimati issippe shiqidason qesista halaqa Qayafakko ehaaththaida.
MAT 26:58 Gido atin Phixirosay qesista halaqa gibe gakanas hahora Yesusa kalidees. Gibe gido gelidi haizaysa wurseth beyanas gibe nagizaytara utidees.
MAT 26:59 He wode qesista halaqatine Ayhudata dulatay kumeth Yesusa wodhisanas wordo marka koydees.
MAT 26:60 Wordo markati daroti shiqikokka besiza markateth demibeytena, gido attin guyeppe namm7u ass dayti shiqidi haysi adezi ta Xoossa maqidasse lalada hezu galasara zarada kexana danda7ays gidees gidi markatida.
MAT 26:62 Hessa siyida qesista halaqay utethafe dendi eqidi hayti asati ne bolla markatizaysas aykoka zarikki gidees.
MAT 26:63 Yesusaykka co7u gidees, qesista halaqay ta nena de7o Xoossa sunthan oychays neni Kirstosa, Xoossa na gidikko tass yota gidees.
MAT 26:64 Yesusaykka ne goysokka mala gido attin intess wursos ta yotizay sinthappe asa nay wolqama ushichan utidi salo sharara yiza wode inte beyana gidees.
MAT 26:65 He wode qesista halaqay ba mayo dakidi Xoossa bolla xasha qaala hasa7idees, nus hayssafe adhiza hara azza markka koshze Xoossa bolla casha qaala izi hasa7ishin inte inte haythara siyidista.
MAT 26:66 Intes ay milatize? gidees. Istika zaridi izas hayqoy beses gida.
MAT 26:67 He wode Yesusa ayfeson cutishe icida, bagayti baqishe.
MAT 26:68 Kirstosa, ne nena nabe gasashin nena baqiday oonakkone ane nus yota gida.
MAT 26:69 Hessafe guye Phixirosay qessista halaqa gibe gido uti dishin issi ketha gidon othiza macash dizara izakko shiqada nenikka Galila Yesusara dizde gadus.
MAT 26:70 Izi qasse ne ay gizakone ta erikke gidi wurso asa sinthan kadidees.
MAT 26:71 Gibezappe keziza penge izi bishin issi hara othanchiya iza xelada hen gadan dizaytas haysi adezi Nazirete Yesusara dizadekko gadus.
MAT 26:72 Izikka ta iza erikke gidi namm7antho kadidees.
MAT 26:73 Guthu gamm7ishin hen eqida asati shiqidi Phixirossa ne hasa7ay ne haytara dizaysa qoncisees, tummappe ne ista baga asa gida.
MAT 26:74 Izikka caqishene ammatishe hessa adeza ta erikke gidees. Herakka kuutoy uu7ides.
MAT 26:75 Hessa wode Yesusay kasse Phixirosas kuutoy wasanas ne tana hezu to kaadana gidi yotida qalay qofetin Phixirosay kare kezidi cammo yeho yekidees.
MAT 27:1 Malado wontara qessista halaqatine dere cimati wurikka Yesusa wodhana ogge zoretida.
MAT 27:2 Yesusa qachi efidi gazhe Philaxossas athi immida.
MAT 27:3 Iza athi immida Yudaykka Yesusa bolla pirdetidaysa beydi atha immonta agarkina gidi ba ekida hezu tammu birra qessista halaqatisine dere cimatas zari immidi xillo asa atha immida gish ta moradis gidees. Istika histin nus ay meto ne era ekka gida.
MAT 27:5 Hessa gish Yuday birra ehaaththaidi maqidasse gidon yegidi kezi bidi kaqeti hayqidees.
MAT 27:6 Qessista halaqati birra denthidi “sutha waga gidida gish maqidasse mishan gujanas bessena” gida.
MAT 27:7 Be garasan zoretidi imath gidida asatas dufo gidana mala issi mana (urqa miish medhizadeza) gade shamida.
MAT 27:8 Hesa gish he gadey hach gakanas sutha gade getetess.
MAT 27:9 Izas waga gidana mala Isra7ele nayti heregida hezu tammu birra qori ekida. Xoossi tana azazida mala urqa othancha gades immida getetidi nabe Ermasa dunan yotetidaysi poletidees.
MAT 27:11 He wode Yesusay dere harizaysa sinth shiqidees. Dere harizaysikka “Neni Ayhuda kawo?” gidi oychidees. Yesusaykka ne gida mala gido gidees.
MAT 27:12 Qessista halaqatine dere cimati iza kasasishin Yesusay istas ayne zaribeyna.
MAT 27:13 He wode Philaxosay Yesusa apun yon nena motizakone siyikki gidees.
MAT 27:14 Dere harizaysi kehi malalistana gakanas Yesusay issi qalaka zaribeyna.
MAT 27:15 Dere harizaysas ba7ale galas derey qasho asappe ebeloy nus birsheto gi oychikko issi ura birshiza wogay dees.
MAT 27:16 He wode gene othon erettida Yesusa getetiza Barbane getetiza issi qasho assi dees.
MAT 27:17 Derey shiqida mala Pilaxosay Barbaneppene Kirstosa getetiza Yesusappe ta intess oona birshana mala koyeti? gidees.
MAT 27:18 Philaxosay issti coo qanates athi immidaysa erishe oychidees.
MAT 27:19 Izi pirda zuppane bolla uti dishin iza machiya iza gedeon hach tani agumora darometotistadis, hessa xillo addeza bolla ne oothonta mala giza kitta Philaxosas yedadus.
MAT 27:20 Gido atin qessista halaqatinne cimati istas Barbaney birshistana malane qass Yesusa wodhana mala wossanas dereza qalay gagana mala othida.
MAT 27:21 Dere harizasi namm7atappe oona birshana mala koyeti? gi oychin issti Barbane birsha gida.
MAT 27:22 Philaxosaykka histakko Kirstosa getetiza Yesusa wosto gidees. Wurkka kaqeto gida.
MAT 27:23 Philaxosaykka aysi? ay iita othide? gidi sista oychidees. Issitkka qasse kehi wasidi qacheto gida.
MAT 27:24 Philaxossay hanizaysi wurikka asay ba garasan mulaketethafe atin hara ay go7ay bayndasa yushi xelidi “Haysa adeza sutha gommppe ta gesha, hayssafe guye inte shene gidi hathi ehisidi dereza sinthan ba kushe mecetidees.
MAT 27:25 Derey wuri iza suthi nu bollane nu nayta bolla gakko gidi zaridees.
MAT 27:26 He wodde Barbane isstas birshidi Yesusa garafisdappe guye kaqana mala athi immidees.
MAT 27:27 Hessappe wotadarti Yesusa gede dere harizaysa gibe eeki bidi wuri shiqidi Yesusa gido athida.
MAT 27:28 Iza mayo qaridi hara ewidi zo7o mayo mayzida.
MAT 27:29 Aguntha akilile xaxidi gigisida, iza hu7e bolla gufanthida shambeqo gufe oshacha kushen oythidinne iza sinthan gulbatidi “Ayhuda kawo intees too” gidi iza qidhida.
MAT 27:30 Iza bolla cutida, shomboqo gufeza iza kusheppe ekkidi Yesusa hu7en zari zaridi shocida.
MAT 27:31 Iza bolla qidhi ka7idaysappe guye qassekka zo7o may7oza qari ekkidine kasse iza mayoza zari mayzidi kaqanaso ekki bida.
MAT 27:32 Issti ekki bishin Qarna gizasoppe yida Simona getetizade demidi masqalezakka iza wolqara tosida.
MAT 27:33 Birshechaykka hu7e guge getetiza Golgotta getetizso gakishin ciyera walaketida woyne caje uya gidi immida, gido attin izi ganxi ekkidi uyana koybeyna.
MAT 27:35 Iza kaqidappe guyen iza mayoza bolla sama yegidi gishetida.
MAT 27:36 Hen utidi iza nagida.
MAT 27:37 Haysi Ayhuda kawo Yesusa giza moto qaala iza hu7eppe bollara wothida.
MAT 27:38 Nam7u wombadistappe issay Yesusappe oshacha bagara issay hadirsa bagra issi kaqetida.
MAT 27:39 Oggera adhi biza asay cayshene hu7e qathishe “maqidasse lalada hezu galasan othizayso, anne nena asha, ne Xoossa na gidikko anne masqale bollappe wodha” gida.
MAT 27:41 Qessista halaqati dere cimatara gididi iza bolla qidhishe hiz gida
MAT 27:42 Hara asa ashidees shin bena ashanas danda7ibeyna izi Isra7ele kawo gidikko ane ha7i masqale bollafe wodho, nukka iza ammanana.
MAT 27:43 Xoossan ammanetidees, bena Xoossa na gidamala Xoosi iza dosiza gidikko anne ha7i iza asho.
MAT 27:44 Izra issippe kaqetida wonbadetikka hessathokka casha qaala iza bolla qoqofida.
MAT 27:45 Galasappe usuppun sateppe bidi uduppun sate gakanas kumetha bittay dhumidees.
MAT 27:46 Udufun sate gidishin Yesusay qaala dhoqu histidi “Elohe elohe lama sebeqitani gidi wasidees. Hessa gussas birshechay “ta Xoosso ta Xoosso tana aysi agadi” gussa.
MAT 27:47 Hen gadan eqida asatappe issi issi asati iza wasoza siyidi Elasa xeygeskko gida.
MAT 27:48 Isstappe issadey woxi bidi utha shedho woykko zanza milatizazi ekkidi calida woyne caje yegi caphisidine shomboqo getetiza miththa xeran qaphidi uyana mala Yesusa dunakko shishidees.
MAT 27:49 Hankko asay qasse agagitte ane Elasay yidi iza ashin beyana gida.
MAT 27:50 Yesusay qassekka dhoqa qalan wasidi shomppo kezidees.
MAT 27:51 He wode maqidasse magalashy bolla hu7era duge simmi daketidi nam7u kezidees bitaykka qaxidees zalatikka za7ida.
MAT 27:52 Dufotikka doyetida, kasse hayqida Xoossa asappe daro bagay dendidees.
MAT 27:53 Dufoppe kezidi Yesusa denthappe guye gede gesha katama gelidi darota ayfen betida.
MAT 27:54 Xetu wotadarata halaqayne izara issippe Yesusa nagizayti bitta qathanne hanidaysa wursi beydi daro babida. Qasse haysi tummappe Xoossa nakoshin gida.
MAT 27:55 Galilappe yidi Yesusa koshizazan othi madanas kaliza daro macashati hanizaysa wursikka hahora xelishe hen detees.
MAT 27:56 Issta gidon magideleppe yida Maramirane, Yaqobene Yossa ayo Maramira, qassekka Zabidossa nayta ayeyira issippe detees.
MAT 27:57 Gaddey ommarsishin Yosefo getetiza issi dure adde daysi Armatiyasa getetizasoppe yidees. Izikka ba bagara Yesusa kalizade.
MAT 27:58 Izi Philaxossa sinthi shiqidi Philaxossay Yesusa anha izas immana mala wosin Philaxosaykka izas immana mala azazidees.
MAT 27:59 Yosefoy anh7a ekkidi gesha mogo afalan xaxidees.
MAT 27:60 Shuchu wocidi bees gigisida dufon ehaaththai wothidi gita shuchu gendersidi dufoza gordidees.
MAT 27:61 Hessa wode Magidale Maramiranne hara Maramira dufoza ginan utida.
MAT 27:62 Sambatas gigetiza wontetha galas qessista halaqatine Pharsaweti Philaxossa sinth shiqidi hiz gida.
MAT 27:63 Godo he wordoy kasse paxa dishe hezu galasappe guye ta dendana gida qalay nu wozinan turchu gidees.
MAT 27:64 Hessa gish iza kalizayti iza anha kaysoti ekkidi deres izi hayqoppe dendidees gidi weresonta mala hezantho galas gakanas dufoy nagistana mala azaza, akkay gikko kaseysappe guye balay adheth gidana gida.
MAT 27:65 Philaxosaykka istas nagizayti detees bididnne intess erettida mala nagisitte gidees.
MAT 27:66 Isstikka bidi dufoza dunna mataman gordidi nagana zabe essida.
MAT 28:1 Sambatay adhidappe guye samintappe koyro galas buro saloy zo7ishin Magidale Marama hara Maramakka dufoza beyana bida.
MAT 28:2 Qopponta dishin gitta bitta qathi hanidees, Godda gitanchaykka salloppe wodhi dufakko bidi shucha gendesidi iza bolla utidees.
MAT 28:3 Kitanchas medhay wolqantha po7o mala, mayoykka shacha mala bo7otu.
MAT 28:4 Dufo nagizayti kitanchazas babidi kokoridinne hayqeth milatida.
MAT 28:5 Kitanachay macashata baboppite inte kaqetida Yesusa koyzasa ta erays izi ha7i han bawa, izi kasse yotida mala hayqoppe dendidees ha yidi izi zin7idaso beyte gidees.
MAT 28:7 Ha7ikka eleli bidi iza kalizaytas hayqoppe dendidees intefe kasetidi Galila bees, inte iza hen demana gidi yotite hi7a ta intes yotidas.
MAT 28:8 Macashatikka babonine ufaysan kumidi iza kalizaytas yotanas elelidi wothan dufoy dizaso yegi agidi bida.
MAT 28:9 Herakka Yesusay ista demidi hayto saro gidees. Istika Yesusakko shiqidine iza to oykidi izas goynida.
MAT 28:10 Yesusay ista babofite bidine isti Galila banal mala ta ishatas yotite. Istti tana hen beyana gidees.
MAT 28:11 Macashati buro ogge bolla dishin nagizaytappe gutha bagati katama bidi hanidaysa wursi qesista halaqatas yotida.
MAT 28:12 Qessista halaqatikka dere cimatara shiqetidi zoretida, wotadaratas gidiza miish immidi nuni zin7on dishin iza kalizayti qammara yidi kaysi efida gite gida.
MAT 28:14 Haysi worey dere harizaysa matan siyetikokka nuni izas lo7othi yotana, aykko itaykka inte bolla gakkonta mala nu ootha gida.
MAT 28:15 Wotadaratikka misha ekkidi isti gida mala oothida, haysi yozi hach gakanas Ayhudata achan daro son yotetishe dees.
MAT 28:16 Hessappekka Yesusa kaliza tamane issineti Yesusay issta besida Galilan diza zumma bolla kezida.
MAT 28:17 Yesusa be7idamala izas goynida, ista grasappe guxiza batati sidhida.
MAT 28:18 Yesusaykka bena kalizaytakko shiqidi salonine bitta bollan godatethi tass immetidees. Hessa gish bidi dere wursos Aawa Na7azane Xillo Ayana suthan xamaqishe tana kalizayta oothite, ta intena azazidaysa wursi nagana mala tamarsitte takka alame wurseth gakanas ta intenara daysi gidees.
MAR 1:1 Xoossa na Yesus Kirstosa koyro mishirachoy hayssa.
MAR 1:2 Nabe Isayasa bagara “Hekko ness ogge lo7othanade ta kitana urra ta neeppe sinthara yedana
MAR 1:3 Godas ogge gigisite izi baana ogge sit histi othite, gishe bazo bitan wasiza gireth” geteti xafetides.
MAR 1:4 Hesathokka xamaqiza Yanisay asa xaamaqishenne “inte nagarappe simmidi xammaqettitte, Xoossi inte nagara atto gaana” gi elishe bazora kezi wodhides.
MAR 1:5 Yihuda derey kumeth Yerusalame asay wuri Yanisakko bi bidi ba nagara nagara paaxxi paaxxi Yordanose shaafan Yanisa kushen xammaqetidees.
MAR 1:6 He wode Yanisay mayzay gamela ithikkeppe othetida mayo, dabba dafora dances, miza qummay bollene degera eessa.
MAR 1:7 Izi “tani hokkada iza camma qasho birshanas besontadey tappe adhizadey tappe guyera yana.
MAR 1:8 Tani intena hathan xammaqays izi gidikko intena Xillo Ayanan xammaqana gidi sabakidees.
MAR 1:9 He wode yesusay Galila garsan diza Nazrete getetiza katamayppe Yordanose shaafa yidi Yanisa kushen xamaqetidees
MAR 1:10 Yesusay xamaqetidi Hathafe kezida mala saloy doyetin Xillo Ayanay izza bolla wolle kafo milatidi wodhishin beyidees.
MAR 1:11 Qassekka ta dosiza nay nena; nenan ta ufayistays giza qaala girethi pude salora setetidees.
MAR 1:12 Herakka Xillo Ayanay izza duge bazo kalethidi efidees.
MAR 1:13 Hen banzonkka oyduu tammu galas gakanas Xal7aera pacetishe gam7idees. Do7atara issippe deyidees, kitanchatikka iza madida.
MAR 1:14 Yansay qasho keth gelidaysappe guye Yesusay Xoossa mishiracho qaala sabakishe gede Galila biidi “Wodey gakidess; Xoossa kawoteth matides; nagarape simitte, mishracho qalan amanite” giidi sabakidees.
MAR 1:16 Yesusay Galila abba achara adhishin Simonayne iza isha Indirasay mole oykizayta gidida gish isti mole oykiza gite aban yegishin be7ides.
MAR 1:17 Yesusay ista hayte tana kalitte inte mole oykii shisiza mala ass oykizayta histana gides.
MAR 1:18 Isti herakka mole giteza yegi agidi Yesusa kaallida.
MAR 1:19 Guthu gede sinthe adhidi Zabidosa naa Yaqobene iza isha Yanisay wogolon utidi mole gite gigisishin beydine herakka ista xeygidees.
MAR 1:20 Istika ba aawa Zabidosas qaxaretidi othiza asatara issippe wogoloza gidon agidi Yesusa kaallidi bida.
MAR 1:21 Heppekka Qifirnahomme bida. Herakka Yesusay Ayhudata sanbata galas Ayhudata wossa keth gelidi tamarso oykidees.
MAR 1:22 Xafista mala gidonta godatethara diza asa mala izi tamarasin asay wuri iza timirtezan malaletidees.
MAR 1:23 He wode Ayhudata wosa keeththan diza tuna ayanay iza bolla diza issi adey
MAR 1:24 “Nazirete Yesusa ne nuppe azi koyay? Nuna dhaysana yadi? Ne oonakone ta nena erays, neni Xoossa gesha” gidi wasidees.
MAR 1:25 Yesuasakka tunna ayanaza “co7u gada izappe keza” giidi hanqidees.
MAR 1:26 Tuna ayanay addeza gendersidi izi qaketishin izappe wasishe kezidees.
MAR 1:27 Derey wuri “asso haysi aza pala? Haysi godatethara diza oratha timirtekko! Tunna ayanatakka azazes istikka izas azazetetes” gi malaletishe asay ba garsan issay issa oychecho oykides.
MAR 1:28 Herakka iza otho worey kumeth Galila yushon diza dere wuruson siyetidees.
MAR 1:29 Ayhudata wossa kethafe kezida mala Yaqoberanne Yanisara issippe gede Simonasone Indiriyasaso gelida.
MAR 1:30 He gelidamalakka Simona bolotiya micha harge sakistada zini7idaysa izas yotida.
MAR 1:31 Hessa gish Yesusay izikko shiqidi izi kushe oykidi denthidees. Michay agin iza dendada ista mokkadus.
MAR 1:32 Away wuldappe guye gadey dhumishin asay harganchatane daydanthi oykida asa wursi Yesusakko ekki yidees.
MAR 1:33 He katamayn diza asay wuri keeththa karen shiqides.
MAR 1:34 Izikka dumma dumma hargen saketidayta darota pathidees. Daro daydanthatakka kesidees. Gido atin daydanthati Yesusay oonakone eriza gish daydanthati hasa7ana mala Yesusay koybeyna.
MAR 1:35 Sosey zon7onta malado wontara Yesusay dendidi issi pashka so biidi hen wossa oykidees.
MAR 1:36 Simonayne izara dizayti Yeusa koyana kezi bida.
MAR 1:37 Isti iza demidi assi wuri nena koshan dees gida.
MAR 1:38 Yesusaykka “ta yiday tamarsanas gidida gish anne mishracho qaala yootanas matan diza gutata boss” gidees.
MAR 1:39 Hesa gish Ayhudata wossa keeththan geli geli sabakishene daydanth kesishe Galila kumethan yuyidees.
MAR 1:40 Issi inchiracha hargizadey Yesusakko shiqidine iza sinthan gulbatidi “koykko ne tana pathana danda7asa” gi wossidees.
MAR 1:41 Yesusaykka adezas michetidi ba kushe yedi iza bochidine “ta ne paxanamala koyays paxa” gidees.
MAR 1:42 Herakka adeza inchiracha hargey agin, adezi paxidees.
MAR 1:43 Yesuaykka addezas “onaskka hayssa ne hasa7onta mala nagista, giddo atin bada qesses nena bessa, derezas markka gidana mala ne paxidaysas Mussey azazida yarshoza shisha” gidi kehi minth yotidees.
MAR 1:45 Gido atin adezi kezi biidi ba bida wurso son wore darsi dharcidees. Hessa gedon Yesusay awa katamankka qoncera gelanas danda7ibeyna. Hessafe dendidaysan katamappe karera assi baynda son dusu oykidees. Assay gidikko awappe awappekka izakko yidees.
MAR 2:1 Gutha galasafe guye “Yesusay guye Qifirnahome simidi soon dees” giza wore asay siyidees.
MAR 2:2 Hessa gish kethara karera utizasoy dhayana gakanas daro derey shiqidees. Izikka Xoossa qaala asas sabakidees.
MAR 2:3 Oydu ass dayti issi toy silida ass tokidi izakko ehida.
MAR 2:4 Assa darotethafe dendidaysan Yesusay dizaso gathanas danda7onta gish Yesusay diza ginara kaara lukidi harganchaza izi zin7ida zaphara Yesusa sinth duge wothida.
MAR 2:5 Yesusay asata amano beydi toy silida adeza “hayso ne nagaray maretidees” gides.
MAR 2:6 Hen gadan utida issi issi Musse woga Xahaaththaeti ba wozinara haysi addezi wosti hayssatho gizee? Xoossa bolla casha qaala hasa7eskko! issi Xoossafe atin nagara marana danda7izay onne gidi qopida.
MAR 2:8 Yesusay herakka isti ba wozinan qopidaysa ba ayanan eridi “inte wositi hayssatho qoppetii?
MAR 2:9 Toy silidadeza ne nagaray maretidees gusafenne dendada ne zapha tokkada ba gusafe aways kawushee?
MAR 2:10 Gido atin asa nass bitta bollan agara marana godatethi dizaysa inte erana mala” gidi to silla addeza
MAR 2:11 “dendada ne tokkista yida zaphe tokkada ne soo ba” gidees.
MAR 2:12 Izikka dendidi asay wuri beyshin zapha tokidi bidees. Hen gadan diza asay wurii hanozan malaletidi “Haysa malay hanini beybekko” gidi Xooss galatidees.
MAR 2:13 Qasekka Yesusay Galila abba lanqe yides. Daro dereykka izakko yin izikka yida asa tamarsides.
MAR 2:14 Izi oogera adhi bishin Elifiyosa na Leewy qaraxa shishizason utidaysa beydine “haya tana kaalla” gidees, izkka dendidi Yesusa kalidees.
MAR 2:15 Hesafe guye leewe son kaththa madan uti dishin qaraxa shishiza daro asatinne nagaranchati izara kali yida gish issti Yesusaranne iza kalizaytara issife kaththa madan utida.
MAR 2:16 Parsawista bagafe gidida Musse woga tamarsizayti Yesusay nagaranchataranne qaraxa shishizaytara mishin beydi iza kalizayta “Qaraxxa shishizaytaranne nagaranchatara aazas mizee?” giidi oychida.
MAR 2:17 Yesusaykka isti gizaysa siyidi “Akimmey harganchatas koshes atin hargontaytas gidena. Takka nagaranchata xeyganas yadis attin xillota xeyganas yabeykke gides.
MAR 2:18 Yanisa kalizatinne Parsaweti xomma xommetes. Issi issi asati Yesusakko yidi Yanisa kalizaytinne Parsawista kalizayti xommetees. Nena kalizayti azass xommetene gi oychida.
MAR 2:19 Yesusaykka istas mishiray istara dishin mishira lageti xommi erizo? Mishiray istara dishin xommi eretena.
MAR 2:20 Mishiray isstappe ekistana wodey yana he wode issti xommana.
MAR 2:21 Gal7a mayo bolla oratha curqa wothi sikizadey onnikka deenna, hessaththo othikko orathazi gal7a dakki dakki yeges; dakethaykka kassefe gede adhi ites.
MAR 2:22 Hessathokka oratha woyne caje gal7a ogoron wothizadey denna. Wothiza gidikko woynne cajezi gal7a ogoroza dhuses, woynne cajezine ogorazi namm7ay moretetes. Hessa gish oratha woynne cajey danas besizay oratha oogorana” gidees.
MAR 2:23 Yesusay Ayhudata sanbata galas gistte tiya gidora adhishin iza kalizayti izara issippe bishe tiya xupho oykkida.
MAR 2:24 Parsaweti “Nena kalizayti sanbata galas digetida miish aazas othizo? gidi Yesusa oychida.
MAR 2:25 Izikka istas “Dawitey gafidi mizaz koyda wode izara issippe dizaytara izi othidaysa nababibeyketii? gidees.
MAR 2:26 Abiyatarey qessista halaqatethan dishin izi Xoossa keth gelidi qeseti xalala manas besiza dumma kaththa bess midine benara dizaytas immidees.
MAR 2:27 Qassekka sambaytas asas medhetidees atin assi sanbatas medhetibeyna.
MAR 2:28 Hessa gish ta asa nay sambata goda. gides.
MAR 3:1 Hara galas Mukurabe gelidees, henikka kushey silida uray dees.
MAR 3:2 Iza motanas gasso koyza asati izi Ayhudata sambata galas pathankkonne gidi pathishin beyana koyda.
MAR 3:3 Izikka ha kushey silida addeza “shiqi utidda asa sinthan denda eqqa” gidees.
MAR 3:4 Hessafe guye Yesusay asa “sambata galas besizay lo7o othoye ita othoo? Assa shemmpo aashoye woykko shemppo wodho? gidi oychidees. Isstikka coo7u gida.
MAR 3:5 Istta wozina shuchatethan michetidi izza giddothidi yuyi adhi eqida asa hanqora eqidi addeza “Ne kushe pidisa” gidees. Addezikka ba kushe pidisin kushezi mulera pathidees.
MAR 3:6 Parsaweti kezi bidi iza wosti dhaysanakkone Herdossa baga gidida asatara zoretida.
MAR 3:7 Yesusay bena kalizata abbako bidees. Galilappenne Yudappe yida daro derey iza kalidees.
MAR 3:8 Izi othizaysa siyidi asay Yudapppe, Yerusalemppe, Edomasappe, Yordanose pinthan diza dereyppe qasse Xirosappene Siddona herappe izakko yidees.
MAR 3:9 Asay darida gish iza kun7isonta mala gutha wogolo issti gigisana mala bena kalizayta azazidees.
MAR 3:10 Izi darota harganchata pathida gish sakkoy waysizayti wurii iza ba kushera bochanas dafetidees.
MAR 3:11 Tuna ayanatikka iza be7ida mala iza sinthan kundidi “Neni Xoossa na” gishe wasida.
MAR 3:12 Gido atin izi oonakone tuna ayanati qoncisontamala kehippe hanqidees.
MAR 3:13 Yeusay pudde zumma bolla kezidi ba koyzayta bekko yana mala xeygidees, isttikka izakko yida.
MAR 3:14 Izara issippe gidana malanne sabakanas yedana mala tamane namm7ata Hawarista gis sunthidees.
MAR 3:15 Assappe daydanthata kessana mala istasi godateth imidees.
MAR 3:16 Izi sunthida tammane nam7ata sunthi hayssappe kalizaysa; Phixirosa getetida Simmona,
MAR 3:17 Bo7ornegesse woykko dada nayta getetida Zabidossa nayta Yaqobene Yanisa,
MAR 3:18 Indirasa, Philiphosa, Bertelemossa, Mattossa, Tommasa, Ilposa na Yaqobbe, Tadossa, ba bittas zil7etiza Simmona,
MAR 3:19 Yesusa athi immida Asqorotu Yudda.
MAR 3:20 Hessappe guye Yesusay issi so gelidees. Izine iza kalizayti kath mana wodey istas dhayana gakanas derey qassekka dari shiqidees.
MAR 3:21 Iza hanota siyida iza daboti gooyonta agena gidi benara ekki banas izi dizaso gakida.
MAR 3:22 Yerusalameppe Yida Xafetikka Bi7el zebula betetiza daydanthata halaqay iza bolla dees, izi daydanthata kesizay daydanthata halaqa wolqana gida.
MAR 3:23 Izikka ista xeygidi lemusora, “Xala7y asappe Xal7e wosti kesanne?” gidees.
MAR 3:24 Be garsan shakkoy diza kawotethi minanas danda7ena.
MAR 3:25 Issi ketha assikka ba garasan shaketikko eqanas danda7ena.
MAR 3:26 Hessathokka Xala7ey ba garasan issay issara shaketikkonne eqanas shakkoy dikko mini eqanas danda7ena, hesikka izas wurseth gidees.
MAR 3:27 Hessa gason issi uray koyrotidi wolqamara ura qashonta dishe wolqamazaso gelanasine iza mishe bonqanas danda7ena, Ketha mishe bonqanas danda7etizay wolqama ura qachikko xala.
MAR 3:28 Ta intess tumu gays asa naytas nagaraynne cashi wuri matistana,
MAR 3:29 gido attin Xillo ayana bolla casha qaala hasa7iza asa wursoso medhinas nagara aco gidana atin medhinaskka maristana.
MAR 3:30 Hessa izi giday isstti iza “Ne bolla tunna ayanay dees” gidaysa gishasa.
MAR 3:31 Hessappe guye iza ayiyanne iza ishati yidinne karen eqidi asse izakko kitidi xeygisida.
MAR 3:32 Iza yuyi adhi utidda daro asay “Hekko ne ayiyanne ne ishati karen eqidi nena koyetees” gida.
MAR 3:33 Izikka zaridi ta aya onne? ta ishatichi onanitte? gidees.
MAR 3:34 Iza yui utidda asakko xelidi “ta ayanne ta ishati haytantakko” gidees.
MAR 3:35 Xoossa shene othizay wuri izi ta isha, ta michchone, ta ayo” gidees.
MAR 4:1 Hara wode qasse abba achan tamarso oykidees, izakko daro derey shiqidees.
MAR 4:2 Izikka daro yota lemuson hizgi tamarsidees.
MAR 4:3 Siyitte issadey kath zeranas kezidees.
MAR 4:4 Izi zershin issi issi zerethi oogge bolla wodhidees. Oogge bolla wodhida zeretha kafoti maxi mida.
MAR 4:5 Baggay lo7o biittay baynda mela biittan wodhides shin bittay mela gidida gish herakka caridees.
MAR 4:6 Gido atin away kezida mala shulidees. Xapho yedonta gish melidees.
MAR 4:7 Qasse issi zerethi handay aguntha gidon wodhidees agunthaykka dicidi culida gish ayfibeyna.
MAR 4:8 Hara zerethi qasse lo7o orde biitta bolla wodhidagish caridi dicidees ayfekka ayfidees; issa hezu tammu, issay qasse usuppun tammu, hara issay qasse xettu ayfidees.
MAR 4:9 Yesusay qassekka siyiza haythi diza uray siyo gidees.
MAR 4:10 Izi berkka dishin tammane namm7atinne kasse izara diza asay izi yotida lemusoza gish iza zari oychida.
MAR 4:11 Izikka istas intes Xoossa kawotetha xuray gelidees shin karen dizaytas gidikko yoyi wuri lemusora yotetees.
MAR 4:12 Hessikka kasse “istti beydi be7idaysa akekontamalanne istti simontamala, qassekka ista nagaray maretonta malasa gedees.
MAR 4:13 Qssekka Yesusay hiz gidees “Haysi lemusoy intess gelibeyne? Histin hara lemuso inte wosti eranne?
MAR 4:14 Zeretha zeriday qaala zeres
MAR 4:15 Issi issi asati ogge bolla wodhida zeretha mala, issti qaala siyiza wode Xala7ey yidi herakka istti siyida qaala issta wozinappe ekki gidees.
MAR 4:16 Hessakko harati mela biitta bolla wodhida zeretha milatetees. Istti qaka siyidi ufaysara eketess.
MAR 4:17 Gido attin issti xappo yedonta gish gutha wode gam7ishin qaala gedon metoy woykko godistay asata bolla yiza wode herakka dhuphetetees.
MAR 4:18 Harati qasse aguntha gidon wodhida zeretha milatetees, issti qalla sisi siyetees.
MAR 4:19 Gido atin ha biitta metoynne misha pacehnne hara amoy issiti siyida qaala culidi ayfe ayfonta mala digees.
MAR 4:20 Hankoyta lo7o biittan zaretidda zeretha milatetees, heytikka qaala siyidi ekizadene hezu tammu, ayfe usuppun tammu ayfene xetu ayfe ayfizayta.
MAR 4:21 Qassekka hizgdeess “Xomppe oythidi gemason woykko arssa garsan wothi ereti? Po7ana mala qonceson wothista giddene?
MAR 4:22 Hessa gish qotetidi qoncen kezontay po7on kezonta gemman attanay bawa.
MAR 4:23 Hessa gish siyiza haythi dizadey siyo.
MAR 4:24 Gujidikka inte siyizaysa wozinan wothite inte maqiza mishara intess makkistana hessappe daroy gujettana.
MAR 4:25 Dizades gujistanashin bayndadefe izas dizarakka ekkistana gidana gidees.
MAR 4:26 Qssekka hizgidees “Xoossa kawotethi zereth zeriza issi ura milataysu.
MAR 4:27 Zeridadey ommars zin7es wontishin dendees, gido attin izi eronta dishin zaretida kaththay mokidi culidees.
MAR 4:28 Gadeyka koyro carecha kalethada buxxa buxxappe kalethada buxxa bolla lo7o ayfe immadus.
MAR 4:29 Kathay kaxidappe guye boney gakin ketha aaway herakka matha oykkes.
MAR 4:30 Qassekka hiz gidees “Xoossa kawoteth nu azara ginisi beyane? azara lemusane?
MAR 4:31 Biitta bolla wursofe lafa gidida sanafice ayfe milataysu.
MAR 4:32 Zeristada dicidappe guye qass akakiltista wursofe adhiza gish kafoti yidi he akakiltey hangista kuwa gidon shempetees.
MAR 4:33 Yesusaykka asay ekanas danda7izaysa kena hayta milatiza hara daro lemusora istas yotides.
MAR 4:34 Aymish gidikkokka asas lemusoy baynda yoti erena. Izinne iza kalizayti xala dizawode gidikko wurssi birsh yootes.
MAR 4:35 He galas gadey qamishin bena kalizayta “anne gede he pinth piinos” gides.
MAR 4:36 Issti asa hen agagidi izi uti diza wogolozara Yeussa ekki bidda. Hara wogolotikka istara isife detes.
MAR 4:37 He wode wolqama bulahey abba bolla dendidi wogoloza hathi kummana gakanas bulahey shocechidees.
MAR 4:38 Gido atin Yesusay borkoth borkotidi wogolozas guye bagan zin7idees. Isstikka iza denthidi “astamare nuni wurshin nena metene” gida.
MAR 4:39 Izikka dendidid carkoza “Coo7u ga”, abbakka “woppu ga” gides, carkoykka co7u sirphi gidees, mullekka co7udees.
MAR 4:40 Bena kalizaytakka “Haysatho aazas babideti? hayssa gakanas intess ammanoy bayee?” gidees.
MAR 4:41 Issttikka kehi babidi ba garsan issay issara “caarkkoynne abbay izass azazetizay haysi onnee?” getetida.
MAR 5:1 Abba pinidi gede Gergesene getetizaso bida
MAR 5:2 Yesusay wogoloyppe wodhida mala tunna ayanay izza bolla dizadey dufosoppe kezidi Yesusara gagana izako yides.
MAR 5:3 Haysi adezi dufoson dizadene oonikka iza haray atoshin sansalatara qachanas danda7ibeyna.
MAR 5:4 Daro wode to birataranne sansalatara qachetees. Gido atin kushe sansalata duthethi yeges, too biratakka mentherethi yeges, oonikka iza oykidi teqanas danda7ibeyna.
MAR 5:5 Galasine qamma dufota gidoninne zummata bolla yuyi yuyi wasishe ba bolla shuchara qanxerethes.
MAR 5:6 Izikka Yesusa hahon be7idamala wothan izakko yidi iza sinthan gulbatidi goynidees.
MAR 5:7 Kehi wassidi “Hayso woogga Xoossa na Yesusa nees tanara azi dizee? Xoossa sunthan ta nena wosays tana waysoppa gidees.
MAR 5:8 Izi hessa giday Yesusay kasse neni tunna ayanay hayssafe keza gida gishasa.
MAR 5:9 Hessafe qasse Yesusay iza ne sunthi oone gidi oychidees. Izikka nuni darota gidida gish ta sunthi Legewone getetes gidees.
MAR 5:10 He dereppe kessi yedonta mala Yesusa kehi wosidees.
MAR 5:11 Hen matan zumma bolla daro gudunthi heemetes.
MAR 5:12 Tunna ayanati nu gudunthatan gelanamala nuss ero garkki gidi Yesusa wosida.
MAR 5:13 Izikka istas ero gidees. Tunna ayanatikka adezappe kezidi gudunthatan gelida. Namm7u shi gidida gudunthay wurii aafozara dugetha gendereti wodhidi wurikka abban mitettidees.
MAR 5:14 Guduntha hemizayti baqatidi hanidaysa katamaninne dere garsan yotida. Dereykka hanidaysa beyanas ba dizasoppe dizasoppe kezidees.
MAR 5:15 Yesusaykka yidi daro daydanth iza bolla dizadez wozinay izas simin mayo maydinne woggara utidaysa yida asay beydi babidees.
MAR 5:16 Haysa be7ida asay daydanthi iza bolla dizadeza gishinne gudinthati hanoysa derezas yotida.
MAR 5:17 Hessafe guye he dere asay Yesusay ista dere yedidi bana mala wossidees.
MAR 5:18 Yesusay wogolon gelishin daydanthati izappe kezida uray Yesusara danas wosidees.
MAR 5:19 Yesusay qasse izi oychidaysa akkayo gidine “Neni gede ne so ba, Goday ness ay mala gita miish othidakkonne izi ness othida marotetha ne soo asas yota” gides.
MAR 5:20 Adezikka ba so biidi Yesuusay izas othida gita miish wursi tammu katamma getetiza deren yotin siyiday wurikka malaletidees.
MAR 5:21 Yesusay qassekka wogolon gelidi gede pinth pinidi abba achan dishin daro asay iza ach shiqidinne iza gidothides.
MAR 5:22 Mukirabe halaqatappe issay Iya7irosa getetizaysi izi dizaso bidi Yesusa demida mala iza to bolla kundidi
MAR 5:23 Tass gutha naa dizara hayqana gaysu iza hayqonta paxa dana mala ne ha yada ne kushe izi bolla wotharki gidi kehi wosides.
MAR 5:24 Yesusaykka izara issippe bidess. Daro asay iza kun7ana gakanas kaalidees.
MAR 5:25 Tammane nam7u layth kumethi suthi izi bollafe gukiza macasha dizara hen asara daysu.
MAR 5:26 Iza bess diza miish ubbaa wursana gakanas akimeppe akime lamon daro daburadus. Gido atin sakoy izis gede daridees atin ayinne keybeynna.
MAR 5:27 Iza Yesusa gish siyidamala asa gidora Yesusa guyera kalada iza mayo bochaduss.
MAR 5:28 Gassoykka ta ay hanadakka iza mayo kushera bocho bochizakkokka ta paxana gada qopida gishasa.
MAR 5:29 Gukiza suthay herakka eqi agidees, izakka paxidaysa ba asatethan eradus.
MAR 5:30 Beppe wolqay kezidaysa Yesusay eriidi gede asakko simidi “Ta mayo oone bochiday?” gides.
MAR 5:31 Iza kalizayti qasse haysi derey kun7etidi sugetishin beyashe wanada <tana bochiday oonne?> gay gida.
MAR 5:32 Yesusay hessa othiday oonakkone beyanas yushi xelidees.
MAR 5:33 Macashayakka bess azi wanidakkone erada babashene kokorashe yada Yesusa sinthan gufanada hanida tumma wurssa izas yotaduss.
MAR 5:34 Izikka “ta naaye ne amonoy nena ashides Saron ba, ne wayeppe paxa” gidees.
MAR 5:35 Yesusay buro hasa7a bolla dishin mukurabe halaqa Iya7irosa soppe yidi Iya7irosas “ne naaya hayqaduss, Goda mela aazas dabursaz?” gida.
MAR 5:36 Gidikkokka Yesusay issta hasa7a lepp histidi mukurabe halaqaza “Ne amano xala ammana atin baboppa” gidees.
MAR 5:37 Pixirosa Yaqoberane Yaqobe isha Yanisappe atin haray oonikka iza kalana mala koybeyna.
MAR 5:38 Gede mukurabe halaqa keth gakidamala asay wasishe cammo yeho yekizaysa beyidees.
MAR 5:39 So gelidi haysi wuri aza wasonne aaza yeho? Naya dhiskadus atin hayqabeyku gidees.
MAR 5:40 Qassse asay wuri iza bolla bicidees asa wursikka kethappe kesidi nayi aawane nayi ayiyo qassekka izara issippe yidayta iza kalizayta xala kalethidi naya diza so gelidees.
MAR 5:41 Nayi kushekka ooykidi “Xaalita kum!” gidees. “Xaalita kum” gusas birshechi hane naye denda guussa.
MAR 5:42 Nayakka herkka denda eeqadus, hene hane hamutaduss. Iziskka laythay tammanne namm7u laytha; asaykka he hanozan daro malaletides.
MAR 5:43 Yesusay hayssa oonikka eronta mala kehi minthi yotidees; “nays mana qumma immitte” gides.
MAR 6:1 Hessafe guye Yesusay heppe dendidi gede ba dere bidees. Iza kalizaytikka izara bida.
MAR 6:2 Ayhudata sambatay gakin Ayhudata wossa keth gelidi tamarsishin siyida asay malaletishe hiz gidees “Hayssi adezi hayssa wursi aawappe eekidee? haysi izas immetida eratethay aze? qasse hayti izi othiza malatati wani iza kushen hanizo?
MAR 6:3 Haysi anaxeza gidenee? Marami na Yaqobenta Yosofonta, Yihudantane Simonanta isha gidene? Iza micheti nunara han nu matan dizayta detene? Giidi hessafe dendidaysan izan ufa7etibetena.
MAR 6:4 Yesusaykka isstas “Nabey bonchetontay ba deren ba dabota gidonine ba so asa achan xala” gidees.
MAR 6:5 Hen gutha harganchata bolla kushe wothi pathorippe attin hara aykko malatakka oothanas danda7ibeynna.
MAR 6:6 Isstas ammanoy bayndaysa beyidi malaletidees. Hessafekka Yesusay mandarappe mandaran yuyi yuyi tamarsides.
MAR 6:7 Tammane namm7ata beekko xeygidi namm7u namm7u histi kitishe tunna ayanata bolla isstas godateth immidees.
MAR 6:8 Izi “ogges gidiza gufe attin oogge shinqe woykko qaraxite woykko mishshe oykoppitte.
MAR 6:9 Caamma athitte gido attin lammana mayo oykopitte.
MAR 6:10 Issi keth inte gelikko he katammappe inte kezana gakanas he kethan diitte.
MAR 6:11 Awankka oonikka intena mokki eekonta ixxikko heppe kezishe he dereta bolla marka gidanamala inte to bolla diza gudula qoqofitte” gidi azazides.
MAR 6:12 Isstikka heeppe kezidi derey marotethan gelana maal sabakida.
MAR 6:13 Daro daydanthata kesida daro harganchata zayte tiyi tiyidi pathida.
MAR 6:14 Yesusa sunthi kassefe ereti ereti bishin kawo Herodossay hessa siyidees. Issi issi asati “hayssa mala malatata othiza Xamqiza Yanisay hayqoppe dendina” gida.
MAR 6:15 Bagayti “Elasakko gida” baga asay qasse “kasse nabetappe issa mala” gida.
MAR 6:16 Herodosay yoza siyidi “ta iza qodhe qanxisida Yanisay hayqoppe paxxi dendidees” gidees.
MAR 6:17 Herodossay ba isha Pilipossa machcho Herodiyado ekkida gedon oyketidi qacheelotana mala azazidi yanisa qasho keth gelithidees.
MAR 6:18 Yanisay Herodosa “ne isha machcho ne ekontamala wogay nena diges” gida gish qachides.
MAR 6:19 Herodiyaday hessa gish holotada iza wodhisanas koyadus shin danda7abeykku.
MAR 6:20 Gasoykka Yanisay xillo ass gididaysa Herodosay eriza gish Yanisas babesine iza naages. Yansay yotizaysa Herodosay siydi hirgizagidikokka izzi yotizaysa wozinappe siyes.
MAR 6:21 Herodosa yeleta galas bonchanas dhoqa shuumistas olla wotadarata azaziza wanatasine Galila biittan kehi eretiza gitta asatas gibira kesidees, hesikka Herodiyadis gigga galas gididees.
MAR 6:22 Herodiyadi maca naaya gelada asa sinthan yeth yexin Herodosane izi xeygida asa izi yethay ufaysidees. Kawoykka nayo “ne koyiza miish ubbaa tana oycha ta ness immana” gides.
MAR 6:23 Qassekka ta kawotetha baga gididakkokka ne oychikko wurssa taa neess immana gidi iziss caqidees.
MAR 6:24 Nayakka elela kezada ba ayeyo “kawo azi oychchoo?” gadus. Ayiyakka “Xammaqiza Yanisa hu7e qanxada imma ga” gadus.
MAR 6:25 Nayakka elela kezada kawozakko gelada “xamaqiza Yanisa hu7e keren wothada ne tass immana mala koyayis” ga oychadus.
MAR 6:26 Kawoy he yozan daro handatidees, gido attin xeygetida immatha gishine caqida qalla gish iziss akaye ganas koybeyna.
MAR 6:27 Hessa gish wotadaratappe issa eesson kitidi Yansa qodhe qanxidi iza hu7e eki yana mala azazidees, izikka biidi qasho ketha gidon Yanisa qodhe qanxides.
MAR 6:28 Hu7eza sanera ehidi nayes immidees, naykka ba ayeyis immadus.
MAR 6:29 Yanisa kalizaytikka hessa siyida mala yidi Yanisa anha ekki efidi mogida.
MAR 6:30 Hesafe guye kitetidayti simidi Yesusa achan yuyi adhidi ba othidaysanne ba tamarsidaysa wursi izas yotida.
MAR 6:31 Daro asay yishenne bishe giza gish qumma miza wodeykka deybeyna, “Anne inte xala tanara poqethaso anne boss guthu shemppi ekkitte” gidees.
MAR 6:32 Hessa gish istti berkka wogolon gelidi issi poqethaso bidda.
MAR 6:33 Issti bishin daroti beyidi tora wothan issttappe sinthe adhida.
MAR 6:34 Yesusay wogoloyppe wodhiza wode daro derey shiqi utidaysa be7ides. Hemizadey baynda mehe mala gidida gish asas qadhetides. Daro yokkka tamarso oykidees.
MAR 6:35 He wode gadey qami qammi biza gish iza kalizayti izakko shiqidi hizgida “Haysi nu dizasoy baazokko gaddey qamides.
MAR 6:36 Haysa heran assi dizaso biidi assy bess miza kath shamidi mana mala asa yeda gida.
MAR 6:37 Izi istas zaridi “asas mizaz inte immitte” gidees. Isttikka malaletidi “nuni bidi namm7u xetu dinarera kath shamidi hayssa asas immizakko gidandee?” gida.
MAR 6:38 Izikka istas “intes ay lage ukethi dizakonne anne bidi xelitte” gin istti bi xelidi “ichachu ukethine namm7u moley des” gida.
MAR 6:39 Hessafe kalidi asa cilila maatta bolla oydan oydan utisana mala azazidees.
MAR 6:40 Assaykka xetu xetunne ichachu tammu ichachu tamm gididi oydan utidees.
MAR 6:41 Izikka ichachu okethane namm7u molista ba kushen oykidi pudde sallo xelidi anjidinne uketha menthi menthi asas gishana mala bena kalizaytas immidees, namm7u molistakka wurso asas shakerethidees.
MAR 6:42 Assay wurikka midi kalides.
MAR 6:43 Yesusa kalizayti asssay kali min atidaysa tammane namm7u pitha kumeth oydappe shishida.
MAR 6:44 Kathi mida asappe atummasay xala ichachu shiye.
MAR 6:45 Herakka izzi asa moyzishe izza kalizayti sinthatidi gede pinth Betesayda getetizso pinana mala azazides.
MAR 6:46 Heppekka ista agagidi wosanas pude zumma bolla kezides.
MAR 6:47 Gaddey qamin wogoloy abba gidon dishin izi berkka biitta bolla dees.
MAR 6:48 Abba bolla carkoy keezi metida gish izza kalizayti abba shri shiri wogolo lagiza mishara baxetishin Yesusay beydees. Wontta bolla istakko yidees, Yidene ista achara adhi banadan hanidees.
MAR 6:49 Gido atin adhi bana hanishin iza byda mala moytil7e be7ida milatin wurikka wassida.
MAR 6:50 Wurikka iza beydi dagamida, izkka herakka issta yochidinne aykoy ba; tanakko dagamofitte gides.
MAR 6:51 Izikka wogolon isstakko gelin carkkoy co7u gidees, isstikka daro malaletida.
MAR 6:52 Kase izi ukethan othida malata birshech isti eronta gish ista wozinay docides.
MAR 6:53 Abba pinidi Gensarexe getetizaso gakidi wogolappe wodhidi wogoloza hen qachidi aggi bida.
MAR 6:54 Issti wogoloppe wodhida mala asay Yesusa erides.
MAR 6:55 Wurikka ba dizaso dizaso woxeretidi harganchata zaphan tooki tooki ekidi Yesusay dizaso ehida.
MAR 6:56 Izi gakida gutan woykko katamma gidon woykko dere garsan gidin harganchati izi adhishin izza wosidine iza mayo bochidi paxanamala shishi shishi dubbushay dizson wotnida. Izi adhishin iza mayo bochidayti wuri paxida.
MAR 7:1 Hessafe guye Parsawetinne Yerusalameppe yida issi issi Xafeteti Yesusa gaxa yuyi adhidi
MAR 7:2 Yesusa kalizaytappe bagayti mecetonta qita kushera kath mishin be7ida.
MAR 7:3 Parsawetinne kasse cimma Aydude asati kasse dere woga naganas kushe lo7othi mecetonta kath mi eretena.
MAR 7:4 Giya bi simikkokka bolla meceti geyonta dishe kath mi eretena. Hesathokka wancakka, ottokka, sanekka, zin7iza hithekka mecha malata hara wogatakka naagetes.
MAR 7:5 Parsawetinne Xafeti Yesusa “nena kalizayti kasse awata wogamala duss agidi aazas kushe mecetonta kath mizo?” gidi oychidees.
MAR 7:6 Izikka istas “Isayasay qodheppe qomo bagan haniza inte gish <haysi derey ba metershan tana bonches woznay gidikko tappe hakidees.
MAR 7:7 Tas mela hada goynytes; issta timirteykka assi wothida woga xala> gidi yotida tuma.” gidees.
MAR 7:8 Xoossa woga agidi assi wothida woga nagetees.
MAR 7:9 Qassekka “inte wogas giidi Xoossa woga inte agagiza cincatetha ooggey intes dees.
MAR 7:10 Ays gikko Musey ne ayone ne aawa boncha; ba ayone ba aawa cayizadey mulekka hayqo gides.
MAR 7:11 Shin inte qasse issi uray ba aawa woykko ba ayyo inte tappe demmanas koshiza mado ta Xoossas immadis gikko
MAR 7:12 inte qasse hayssaddey ba aawaskka ba ayyeys hara aykokka othana mala koyekista.
MAR 7:13 Hessa gish inte woga nagana gidi Xoossa qaala lamista. Hesantakka milatiza darota othista.” gides.
MAR 7:14 Qassekka Yesusay asa beekko xeygidi “wurikka ta giza siyitene wozinan wothitte.
MAR 7:15 Kareppe ulo gido gelidi ass tunisiza issi miishika deena. Harappekka asse tunisizay kethawappe gede kare keziza misha.
MAR 7:16 Siyiza haythi dizay siyo” gidees.
MAR 7:17 Izi asa karen agidi keth gelin iza kalizayti izi yotida lemusoza birshech Yesusa oychida.
MAR 7:18 Izikka ista intesikka yoy gellene? Kareppe gelidi asse tunisiza mishi azikka deena.
MAR 7:19 Kareppe gelizay gede wozinan gidonta; dugge qantha gido geles qasse heppe izade asatethappe gede kare kezes.” Yesusay hessa giday assi miza kathi wurikka gesh gididaysa qoncisanasa.
MAR 7:20 Kalethidikka “asappe kezizazi asse tunises.
MAR 7:21 Assa wozina gidoppe kezizay iita qofata laymma ammone, kaysotethi, asse wodho laymeteth,
MAR 7:22 yiqeteth, itateth, baletho, laymma kasse, qanateteth, asa sunth moro, otorotethinne, azala.
MAR 7:23 Hayti iitta hanoti wuri asappe kezetesinne asse tunisetes” gides.
MAR 7:24 Heeppe kezidi Xirosa giza dere bidees, hen issade keth gelidi izi hen dizaysa assi erontamala koydees. Gido atin izi hen iza dusay qotistanas danda7etibeyna.
MAR 7:25 Herakka issi tuna ayanay oykida qi na dizari aya Yesusay hen diza siyada izakko yada iza too bolla kundadus.
MAR 7:26 Macashaya Ayhude gidonta Girike qaala hasa7iza macashi shin izi yeleta gadey Sirofinqe getetes. Izakka yesusay izi nayeppe tuna ayna kesana mala wosadus.
MAR 7:27 Izikka zaridi izis “nayta qumma ekki kanas yeganas besonta gish koyro nayti mi kaleto” gides.
MAR 7:28 Izakka zarada “E Godo kanatikka madda matan de7idi nayta kusheppe gaden wodhidaysa meteskko” gadus.
MAR 7:29 Izikka “histiko neni hessa gida gish ba daydanthay ne nayeppe kezidees” gidees.
MAR 7:30 Iza simadda so bishin naya daydanthay yedin paxada hixan zin7idaro demadus.
MAR 7:31 Hesafe Yesusay Xirosa bitappe dendidi Sidona gizasora adhidi Tammu katama gizasora kanthidi gede Galila abbakko gakidees.
MAR 7:32 Assay issi haytha tulene ayfe qoqe assi izakko he ekiyidi Yesusay iza bolla ba kushe wothanan mala wosida.
MAR 7:33 Yesusaykka iza asappe shakki ekki bidi ba kushe biradhista adeza haythan gelithidees, qassekka cuchu cutidi addeza inxarsa bochidees.
MAR 7:34 Pudde salo xelidine tokki shempidi “Efata” gides. Hesikka “Pogetta” gussa.
MAR 7:35 Herakka addeza haythati pogetida, inxarsaykka birshetin geshi hasa7idees.
MAR 7:36 Yesusay hayssa be7idayti onaskka yotonta mala azaziddes, gido attin asay izi azazizdaysafe bollara kehi gujidi yotida.
MAR 7:37 Derezikka woggappe athi malaletidi “Izi othidaysi wuri lo7o; tuleti siyanamala, mumeti hasa7anamala othides” gida.
MAR 8:1 He wode qasse daro assi shiqides, shiqida asas miza kathi baynda gish Yesusay bena kalizayta xeygidi hizgidees;
MAR 8:2 Hayti asati tanara heedzdzu galas gakanas gam7ida gishinne qassekka istas miza kathi baynda gish tana miichetes.
MAR 8:3 Istappe issi issi asati hahoppe yida gish hayssa gafara ta ista so yedikko daburidi ogge bolla kundana.
MAR 8:4 Iza kalizaytikka zaridi “hayssa bazon hayssa mala dere muzana qumma awappe demmane?” gida.
MAR 8:5 Izikka ista intekkon appun ukethi dize? gi oychidees. Isttkka “lappun ukethi dees” gida.
MAR 8:6 Izikka asay gadde bolla utana mala azazides; lappun uketha ba kushen oykidi galtidinne menthidi asas gishechanamala bena kalizaytas immin istika derezas gishida.
MAR 8:7 Qassekka hen diza qeri molista gish Xoossu galatidi asas gishistanamala bena kalizayta azazidees.
MAR 8:8 Dereukk midi kalidees. Hessappekka iza kalizayti madappe tirfida kath lappun pitha kummeth denthida.
MAR 8:9 Hessa mida asay oydu shiye gidana. He asa moyzidi bena kalizatara wogolon gelidi gede Dalmanuta getetizaso bidees.
MAR 8:11 Parsaweti yidi Yesusara palameteth oykida. Iza paacanas koydi bena saloppe malata besana mala oychida.
MAR 8:12 Izikka tooki shmepidi “Haysi yeletazi aazas malata koyizee? Ta intes tummu gays hayssa yelets issi malataykka immetena gidees.
MAR 8:13 Ista hen agidinne wogolon gelidi he pinth piniddees.
MAR 8:14 Izza kalizayti kath oykonta baletida gish issi uketh atin wogolo gidon hara ay kathikka deena.
MAR 8:15 Yesusay ista “Parsawista isrshppenne Herodosa irshoppe nagetitte gidi azazidees.
MAR 8:16 Issti qasse ba garsan issay issara “izi nuna hayssa gizay nuss kath baynda gishasakko” gi yotetida.
MAR 8:17 Qasse Yesusay issta qofa eridi <Nuss kathi baynda gish gasa> gidi inte garsan aazas hasa7eteti? Ha7ikka yushi qopeketi? Wozinanka wotheketi? woykko inte wozinay mumidee?
MAR 8:18 Intees ayfey dees shin xeleketi? Haythi dees shin siyeketi? Akekeketi?
MAR 8:19 Ichachu uketha ichachu shiye asas ta mentha immin appun pitha kumeth kath denthideti?” gides. Isstika zaridi “tamanne namm7u” gida.
MAR 8:20 Izikka “Lappun uketha oydu shiye asas ta mentha immin appun pitha kumetha kathi denthideti” gi oychin isstika “lappun” gida.
MAR 8:21 Izikka istta histin “Ha7i gakanas yushi qopibeykistaka” gidees.
MAR 8:22 Hessfe gede Betesayda gizaso bida. Gutha asatikka issi ayfe qoqe assi Yesusakko ehidi Yesusay iza bochanamala wosida.
MAR 8:23 Izikka he qoqeza kushe oyki gochidi asssi dizasoppe gede kare kesidi addeza ayfen cutidinne ba kushe iza bolla wothidi ha7i ness azi betize? gi oychidees.
MAR 8:24 Izikka dhoqu gi xelidi “asay mith milatidi qaxetishe betes” gidees.
MAR 8:25 Qassekka Yesusay ba kushista iza ayfeta bolla wothidees, herakka iza ayfeti xelida, kasse po7oykka izas simmin wursikka geshi xelidees.
MAR 8:26 Qasse “ha gutata gido geloppanne oonasikka yotoppa” gidi iza gede izaso yedidees.
MAR 8:27 Yesusay bena kalizaytara Pilipos Qisariya achan diza gutata bidees, Issti oogge bolla dishin benna kalizayta “tana asay oona gize?” gidi oychidees.
MAR 8:28 Issttikka zaridi nena “Xammaqiza Yanisa gizaytikka deetes, bagayti qasse Elasa getees, harati qass Nabistappe issade getees gidi yotida.
MAR 8:29 Kalethidikka Intech tana oona geti? gidi oychidees. Pixirosay “Neni Kirstosa (Xoossappe kitetidade) gidees.
MAR 8:30 Yesusaykka ba gish oonasika istti yotontamala minthi yotides.
MAR 8:31 Hessafe Yesusay bena kalizayta “asa nay daro waye beyanaysane dere cimmatan, qesista halaqanine, xafistan kadhistanaysa asa kushen hayqanaysa, hayqoppe hezantho galas dendanas besizaysa tamarso oykidees.
MAR 8:32 Izikka hessa istas qoncisi yotidees, Pixirosaykka iza dumma shaki efidi hessaththo goppa gidi hanqidees.
MAR 8:33 Yesusay qass bena kalizayta yushi xelishe Pixirosa “Xal7e ne tappe gede guye ba, neni asazappe atin Xoossaz qopakka” gidi hanqidees.
MAR 8:34 Hessafe guye asa bena kalizaytara issippe bekko xeygidi “tana kalanas dosizadey dikko bena kado ba masqale tokidi tana kalo” gidees.
MAR 8:35 Be shemppo ashana dosizadey dhaysana shin ta gishine ta mishiracho qaala gish ba shemppo dhaysizadey wurikka ashana.
MAR 8:36 Assi alame kumeth harikkone ba shempofe mela atikko iza ay go7anne?
MAR 8:37 Ero assi ba shemppo gish lame ekanay azi dize?
MAR 8:38 Hayssa laymane nagarncha yeleta gidon dishe tananine ta qalan yelatiza assi wuri ta asa nay taa aawa bonchoranne gesha kitanchatara yiza wode issstan yelatana.” gides.
MAR 9:1 Kalethidikka Yesusay “ta intes tummu gays ha eqida asafe Xoossa kawotethi wolqara yishin beyana gakanas hayqonta issi issi asati detess” gidess.
MAR 9:2 Usupun galassafe guye Yesusay Phixirosa Yaqobbene Yanisa benara kalethi ekkidi issi giitta zumma bolla kezidees. Issti berkka dishin issta sinthan iza medhay lammeti wodhides.
MAR 9:3 Izi mayda mayoy bitta bolla onikka mayo mecidi hessa mala bothanas danda7onta bothu botides.
MAR 9:4 He wode Elasaynne Mussey Yesusara hasa7etishe istas betida.
MAR 9:5 Phixirosay Yesusa “Asatemare nuni han hayssan dizakko nus lo7oko; nes issi dasse, Musses issi dasse, qasse Elassas issi dasse, hezu daassista nu othikoch? gidees.
MAR 9:6 Daro babida gish Phixirosay ba gizaysa eridi gibeyna.
MAR 9:7 Heerakka sharay ista kamin shara gidora “Haysi ta dosiza ta naza izi giza siyitte” giza qaala girethi yides.
MAR 9:8 Herakka issti yushi xelin Yesusappe atin oonikka hara uray istara dena.
MAR 9:9 Issti zumma bollappe duge wodhishin asa nay hayqofe dendana gakanas hayssa isti be7idaysa oonaskka yotonta mala azazidees.
MAR 9:10 Istika bes yotida qaala ba wozinan oykida shin “Hayqoppe dendo gussi ay gusakkonne” gidi ba garasan hasa7etida.
MAR 9:11 Qasse issti Musse woga tamarsizayti kasetidi Elasay yana koshes aazas gizo? gidi iza oychida.
MAR 9:12 Yesusay istas “Tumukka Elasay kassetidi yidi wursikka kasse mala oothana. Histinikka asa nay daro waye eekanasinne kadhistanas beses geteti xafetidaysi intes ay milatize?
MAR 9:13 Gido atin ta intess gizay Eelasay gidikko yidess shin asaykka iza gish xafetida mala bena koshida mala iza bolla othides.” gides.
MAR 9:14 Dugge garsan atida Yesusa kalizaytakko issti simi yishin daro asay issta gidothin Musse woga tamarsizayti istara palametizaysa beyida.
MAR 9:15 Derey iza demida mala malaletidi sarotana izakko woxidees.
MAR 9:16 Izikka ista “Inte istara aza gish palameteti?” gidi oychidees.
MAR 9:17 Assa garsafe issadey “Astemare tuna ayanay izan gelin duna mumida ta na daysa ta neekko eekka yadis,
MAR 9:18 Ayanazi dendiza wode bollafe yegess; dunara goponto kessi kessi yegesss; achekka garcess; asatethakka zodisses. Tunna ayana keseto gada nena kalizayta ta oychin istikka danda7ibeytena.
MAR 9:19 Yesusaykka istatas zaridi “Inteno amanonta yeletato, ayde gakanas ta intenara danne? Qasse ayde gakanas ta intena danda7ane? Aane naza ha ehitte” gidees.
MAR 9:20 Assaykka naza izakko ehidees, tunna ayanay Yesusa be7ida mala naza herakka biitta bolla gendersidi kokorsidinne dunnara goponto coopu histides.
MAR 9:21 Yesusay naza aawa “Haysi hargey izza oykin woqqa wodde? gidees. Naza aawaykka “natethafe domidi” gides.
MAR 9:22 Iza wodhanas koydi daro wode tamankka hathankka yegess, ness danda7etikko nuss michistanne nunna madda gidees.
MAR 9:23 Yesusay qasse “Ness danda7etikko gay? Aamanizadees wurikka danda7etess” gidees.
MAR 9:24 Naza aaway herakka “Ta ammanays shin ta amanoy lafa, tanna madarikki” giidi wassidees.
MAR 9:25 Assay wocamishe bureti eekidi izakko yizaysa Yesusay beydi “Hayso tulene mume ayanazo hayssa nazappe keza, ne qasse simada gelonta mala ta nena azazays” gidi tuna ayana seridees.
MAR 9:26 Tunna ayanazika kehi wasidees, nazikka kehi qaketidappe guye nazappe kezidees. Daroti hayqidees gana gakanas nazi an7ah milatidees.
MAR 9:27 Gido atin Yesusay naza kushe oyki denthidees. Nazikka dendi eeqidees.
MAR 9:28 Yesusay so gelidappe guye iza kalizayti “Nu izappe tunna ayana kessanas aazas danda7ibeykoni?” giidi iza oychida.
MAR 9:29 Izikka istas “hayssa malay kezana danda7izay wosaninne xoomman xallala” gidees
MAR 9:30 Heppe dendi Galila bagara adhi bida. Yesusay ba dizso oonikka eeranamala koybeyna.
MAR 9:31 Gassoykka Yesusay bena kalizaytas “Assa nay asa kushen adhi immistana istikka iza wodhana, hezantho galasafe guye izi dendana” giidi issta tamarsiza gishasa.
MAR 9:32 Gido atin izi gizaysi isstas gelibeyna; iza ooychanasikka babida.
MAR 9:33 Hessafe guye Qifirnahomme bidda. Izi keth gelidi “Inte ooge bolla aza gish palametideti” gi oychidees.
MAR 9:34 Isstti qass ooge bolla “Nu garssan nuppe wursoppe adhizay oone?” gidi palametida gish wurikka co7u gida.
MAR 9:35 Izi utidappe guye tammane namm7ata xeygidi “Koyro gidana koyizadey wursoppe wursethinne wursotas ashkara gido” gidees.
MAR 9:36 Qii gutha na ehidi ista gidon esidinne idimmidi
MAR 9:37 Hayta gutha anaytappe issade ta sunthan mokki ekkizadey tannakka mokki ekes. Tana mokki ekizadey wuri tana xalala gidonta tana kitidaysakka mokki ekkes” gidees.
MAR 9:38 Yanisaykka “Astemare, issadey ne sunthan daydanth kesishin nu beydos. Izi nuna kalonta gish kesonta mala digidos” gidees.
MAR 9:39 Yesusay qasse “digopitte oonikka ta sunthan malata oothidi esotidi ta bolla iitta hasa7anas danda7ena” gidees.
MAR 9:40 Nunara eeqetontay wuri nunara dees.
MAR 9:41 Ta intes tumu gays inte tiyetida Kirstosas gidida gish ta sunthan issi qulle hath intena ushidadey wuri ba oothoysi waga dhayena.
MAR 9:42 Hayta tana amaniza ha guthatappe issade dhuphizay wuri dexo woxa shuchi iza qodhen qashetin duge abba gido ooletidakko izas keya gidana.
MAR 9:43 Hessa gish ne kushey nena balethikko neppe qanxa yegga namm7u kushera gede ganamme tamman ne banaysafe kushe duxa gidada gede de7on geloy ness lo7o gidana.
MAR 9:44 Ganamen guxuneyne hayqena, tamaynne to7ena.
