MAR 9:45 Nena ne toy balethikko neppe qanxa diga namm7u tora gede ganame taman yegistanappe ne wobbe gidada gede deyoso geloy ness lo7o.
MAR 9:46 Ganamen guxuneyne hayqena, tamaynne to7ena.
MAR 9:47 Nena ne ayfey balethikko woca kessada neppe diga, namm7u ayfera gede ganamen yegistanappe issi ayfera gede Xoossa kawoteth geloy ness lo7o.
MAR 9:48 Ganamen guxuneyne hayqena tamaynne to7ena.
MAR 9:49 Burro assi wuri tamman pacistana (metora adhana woykko xillo tamay geshana)
MAR 9:50 Maxinney lo7o, gido attin maxinney ba maxineteth yedikko inte wosti iza mal7o eranne? Inte asatethan maxinney do inte inte garsan dosetitte.
MAR 10:1 Yesusay heppe dendidi gede Yuda giza derene Yordanose shaafappe pinthan diza dere bidees. Dereykka qasse iza yuyi adhin izi kasse ba oothiza mala asa tamarsides.
MAR 10:2 Issi issi Parsaweti izakko yiidi “Assi ba machcho anjanas besize?” gidi iza pace oycho ooychida.
MAR 10:3 Izikka istas “Mussey intena ay gi azazide?” gidi zari oychidees.
MAR 10:4 Isstikka izas “Mussey ta izo anjadis giza waraqata xafi immidi anjo gidees” gida.
MAR 10:5 Yesusaykka zaridi istta “Mussey hayssa mala woga xafidaysi inte wozinay minida gishasa” gidees.
MAR 10:6 Gido attin Koyro Xoossi medhishe macanne adde oothi medhidees.
MAR 10:7 Hessa gish assi ba aawane ba ayo agidi ba machchira waxetess.
MAR 10:8 Namm7ay issi asho gidetes, hessa gish istti namm7ay issinoppe atin namm7u detena.
MAR 10:9 Hesa gish Xoossi gathi waxidayta assi shakofo.
MAR 10:10 Qassekka issti so gelin iza kalizayti he yoza gish zari iza oychida.
MAR 10:11 Izi istas “Oonikka ba machcho anjidi hara macash ekiko he macashay bolla laymma oothes.
MAR 10:12 Macashayakka ba azina agada hara ade gelikko izakka laymataysu” gidees.
MAR 10:13 Yesusay bocherechana mala asay nayta izakko ehidees. Iza kalizayti qassse ehida asa bolla hanqettida.
MAR 10:14 Yesusay hessa bey hanqetidi “Nayti taakko yeto digofitte, Xoossa kawotethi haytanta malasa.
MAR 10:15 Ta intes tumu gays Xoossa kawoteth hayssa gutha nayta mala ekontadey izin mulekka gelena.” gides.
MAR 10:16 Nayta idimidi ista bollla ba kushe wothidi anjides.
MAR 10:17 Heeppe buro oge kezishin issi uray wooxishe izakko gakidinne iza sinthan gulbatidi “Lo7o astemare tani medhina deyo demana mala ay oothana tass besize?” gi ooychidees.
MAR 10:18 Yesusaykka “Azas tana Lo7o gay? Issi Xoossafe atin kiyay ba” gides.
MAR 10:19 “Neni azazota eray? Wodhoppa laymatoppa kaysotoppa wordo markatofa asse balethoppa ne aawane ne ayo boncha gizayta” gidees.
MAR 10:20 Adezikka zaridi “Astamare ta hayta wurssa natethafe ooykkada nagadis” gidees.
MAR 10:21 Yesusay iza xelidinne dosidi “Histikko ha7i ness issi miish paces badanne ness diza ubbaa bayza, miisha manqotas imma, neni salon shiqida miish demandasa, histadane haaya tana kala” gidees.
MAR 10:22 Adezikka hessa siyidi daro muzotidees. Izas daro haroy diza gish muzotishe bidees.
MAR 10:23 Yesusay yushi athi xelidi bena kalizayta “duristas Xoossa kawoteth geloy ay mala dexo!” gides.
MAR 10:24 Iza kalizaytikka iza hasa7an malaletida. Yesusay qasse zaridi “nayto, Xoossa kawoteth geloy ay mala dexo miishe!
MAR 10:25 Durey Xoossa kawoteth gelanaysafe gamelay narfe lukkora adhanaysi kawuyana!” gides.
MAR 10:26 Iza kalizaytikka darsi malaletidi ba garsan issay issa “Histin ooni attana danda7ize?” gida.
MAR 10:27 Yesusay ista xelidine “Haysi asas danda7etena, Xoossa matan gidikko hessamala gidena. Xoossas wurikka danda7etees” gidees.
MAR 10:28 Phixirossay qasse “Hekko nuni wursikka agidi nena kalidos” gidees.
MAR 10:29 Yesusaykka zaridi “Ta intes tumu gays ta gishinne mishiracho qaala gish gidi ba keth woykko ba ishata woykko ba michista woykko ba aayo woykko ba aawwa ba nayta woykko ba gade agida uray wuri
MAR 10:30 hayssa ha wodezan ha7i goodetethara kethata, ishata, michista, aayeta, naytanne gadekka xeetu kushe athi ekontaynne burro yana alamezanikka medhina deyo latontadey deena.
MAR 10:31 Gido atin daro sinthatidayti guyista, guyetidayti sinthata.” gides.
MAR 10:32 Issti Yerusalame efiza ooge bolla dishin Yesusay istafe sinthe sinthe bess. Iza kalizayti iza bussan malaletida. Hankko iza gedon diza asay qass izas babidees. Qassekka tammane namm7ata derezappe dumma shakidi ba bolla azi gakanakonne istas hiz gi yotidees;
MAR 10:33 “Nuni Yerusalame kezana, asa nay qesista halaqatassine Muse woga tamarsizaytas adhi immistana, istikka iza bolla hayqo pirda pirdanane dere asas athi immana.
MAR 10:34 Iza bolla qidhi ka7ana, iza bolla cutana, izakka garafanane wodhana shin izi hezu galasafe guyen hayqoppe dendana.”
MAR 10:35 Qasse Zabbidossa nayti Yaqobeyne Yanisay izakko shiqidi “Astamare nuni nena wosidaza ne nus ubbaa oothanamala nu koyos” gida.
MAR 10:36 Izikka istas “ta intees ay oothana mala koyeti?” gidees.
MAR 10:37 Istika “Neni ne boncho son nuppe issadey ne oshachan issadey ne hadirsan utnamala nus ero garki” gida.
MAR 10:38 Yesusaykka “Inte oychizaysa erekista, tanni uyana usha uyanasine tani xamaqetiza xinqata xamaqistanas danda7andeti?” gidees.
MAR 10:39 Isttika zaridi “Ee danda7os” gida. Yesusaykka “ta uyza usha inte uyanane ta xamaqetiza xinqata inte xamaqistana.
MAR 10:40 Shin ta oshachara woykko ta hadirsara utethi istas gigidaytasa attin ta iimmana miish gidena” gidees.
MAR 10:41 Tammanti hessa siyidi Yaqobene Yanisa bolla hanqettida.
MAR 10:42 Yesusaykka issi bolla shishidi “Dere halaqa getetizayti dere harizaysa mala istta shuumeti ista bolla ba godateth besizaysa inte ereta.
MAR 10:43 Gido atin inte garsan gitta gidana koyzadey wuri ashikara gido.
MAR 10:44 Sinthe adhana koyzay wuri wursos ayle gido.
MAR 10:45 Asa nay gidikko asas oothansine ba shemppo darota gish athi immans yades atin ase othisanas yibeyna.” gides.
MAR 10:46 Heppe gede Yarkko bida. Yesusaynne iza kalizayti hara daro asatara Yarkofe kezishin Xemosa naa Berxemossa getetiza ayfe qoqey ooge bolla utidi woses.
MAR 10:47 Izikka yizay Nazirete Yesusa gididaysa siyidi “Dawite na Yesusa tana mara” gidi kehi wasidees.
MAR 10:48 Daroti izi co7u gana mala hanqida, gido attin izi “Dawiteno tana mara” gidi kehi wassidees.
MAR 10:49 Yesusaykka eqidi “iza ha xeygitte” gidees. Istika qoqeza “Aykoy ba denda nena xeyges” gida.
MAR 10:50 Izikka ba mayo qari yegidi puthuku gi dendi eqidi Yesusakko yides.
MAR 10:51 Yesusaykka “Ta ness ay oothanamala koyaz” gidees. Qoqezikka “Aastamare ta xelanas koyays” gidees.
MAR 10:52 Yesusaykka zaridi “Ba nena ne aamanoy pathidees” gidees. Herakka iza ayfey xelidees. Izikka yesusa kali bides.
MAR 11:1 Isti gede Yerusalame Dabirazayte giza zumma achan diza Betefagenne Bitaniya gizaso matida wode Yesuay bena kalizaytappe namm7ata hizgi kitidi;
MAR 11:2 “Gede inte sinthan diza gutayo bitte, inte he gelida mala hen assi iza togi eronta qashon diza harre gutte inte demmana; birshidi iza ha ekiyitte.
MAR 11:3 Onikka intena hayssa ays ootheti? gikko Godas koshesn gidi yotite, izikka intes eeson zari yedana” gidees.
MAR 11:4 Isstikka bidi issi ketha karen oge bolla qachetti diza hare gutte demidi birshida.
MAR 11:5 Hen eqida issi issi asati “Hare guteza aazas birsheti” gi oychida.
MAR 11:6 Yesusa kalizayti Yesusay istas gidamala asatas yotin eero eki biite gida.
MAR 11:7 Gutezakka Yesusakko ehidi ba mayo iza zokko bolla yegin Yesusay iza togidees.
MAR 11:8 Daro asay ba mayo kessi kessi ogge bolla micidees. Baga asay cilila mihta hathi qanxi qanxidi ogge bolla lalidees.
MAR 11:9 Yesusappe sintharanne guyera diza asay qaala dhoqu hisitidi “Hossana Goda sinthan yizadey anjetidade.
MAR 11:10 Hanna yizara nu aawa Dawite kawotehaya anjetidaro, hosana bolla salon Xoossi boncheto” gishe wassidees.
MAR 11:11 Yesusay Yerusalame gakidi hessapekka maqidasse gelidees. He heran dizaysa wursi xelidi gadey qamida gish tamane namm7atara gede Bittanya kezides.
MAR 11:12 Wontetha galas issti Bittanyappe kezi bishin Yesusay gafides.
MAR 11:13 Izi issi haythi cililida balase getetiza mith hahon beydi ayfey danakonne gidi izikko yidees. Giddo atin balase mith ayfonta wode gidida gish boncofe atin issi ayfeykka izippe demibeynna.
MAR 11:14 Hessa gish mithiyo “Hanife guye medhinas onikka neppe ayfe moppo” gidees. Iza kalizaytikka izzi gizaysa siyida.
MAR 11:15 Gede Yerusalame bida heppeka gede maqidase gelidi hen bayzizaytanne shamizayta kessi godo oykidees. Mishe lamizayta xaraphezane wolle bayzizayta oyddee gufanthi gufanthi yegidees.
MAR 11:16 Onnikka ay miish tokidi maqidees gibe gidora adhonta mala digidees.
MAR 11:17 Istakka tamarsishe “Ta kethi dere wursos Woossa keth gidana geteti xafetibeyne? Gido atin inte qasse kaysonta gongolo kesidista” gidees.
MAR 11:18 Qessista halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti hessa siyidi iza wosti dhaysanakkone oogge koshu oykida. Giko atin dereykka iza timirttezan malaletida gish izas babida.
MAR 11:19 Istika gadey qamin katamayppe kezi bida.
MAR 11:20 Wontetha galas malado isti oggera adhi bishin balasse miththaya xaphoppe melidaro be7ida.
MAR 11:21 Yozi iza wozanan akeketin Phixirosay Yesusa “Astammare hekko hanna ne qangida balaseya meladus” gidees.
MAR 11:22 Izikka zarid “Xossu ammanitte.
MAR 11:23 Ta intes tummu gays <Oonikka hayssa zummaza ne dhoqalistada gede abban gela> gizakkone hessakka wozanan sidhonta ammanidakko izadees hanana.
MAR 11:24 Hessa gish inte wossan oychidaz wursi eekida mala ammanikko intes hanana.
MAR 11:25 Hessathokka inte wosas eqiza wode inte sallo aaway inte nagara atto gana mala intekka intena qohidayta nagarawursi atto gitte.
MAR 11:26 Inte atto gonta ixikko inte sallo aawaykka inte nagara atto gena.” gides.
MAR 11:27 Qassekka Yerusalamme yida. Yesusay maqidasse kare gidon gedene hanne yuyetishin qessista halaqati Muse woga tamarsizaytinne dere cimmati izakko shiqidi
MAR 11:28 “Haysa ne oothizay ay godatethara? Hayta ne oothana mala hayssamala godateth ness ooni immide?” gida.
MAR 11:29 Yesusaykka istas zaridi “Aanne takka intena issi oycho ooychaysi intekka tass zarikko takka ha yotta ay godatethara oothizakkonne intes yotana.
MAR 11:30 Yanisa xinqatey Xoossafe ye asappe? anne tass zaritte” gidees.
MAR 11:31 Isstikka ba garsan issay issara “Nu saloppe gikko izi nuna histin aazas iza ammanibeyketi? gana.
MAR 11:32 Nu asappekko gikko Yanisay tummu nabbe gididaysa derey wuri ammaniza gish hessaththo gana babida.
MAR 11:33 Hessa gish nu eerokko gidi Yesusas zarida. Yesusaykka “Histikko ta hayta aza godatethara oothizakkonne takka intes yotikke” gidees.
MAR 12:1 Qasse istas lemusora yotishe hizgidees “Isadey ba woyne mith tokides. Birda yushi athides; woyne miththa ayfe gum7ana olla bokidees nago kethekka kexides. Hesafe goshanchatas kira imidi hara dere bides.
MAR 12:2 Mithay ayfizawode woyne miththa ayfe eeka ya gidi ashikaratappe isade goshanchatakko yedidees.
MAR 12:3 Goshanchati ashikaraza oykidi wadhidi mela kushe yedida.
MAR 12:4 Namm7anthokka hara ashikara yedidees. Goshanchatti ha7ikka ashikara oykki hu7istara bo7idinne kawushidi zari yedida.
MAR 12:5 Ha7ikka zaridi hara ahshikara yedidees. He yedoysakka wodhida; hara darota gidofe issi issi asata qoxida; bagayta wodhida.
MAR 12:6 Ha7ikkka kitanas haray dees; izikka aaway dosiza iza naaza. Ta naza isti bossana gi qopidi wursethan ba naza yeddides.
MAR 12:7 Goshancahti qass ba garsan “Haysi wana iza latana nazakko ha yitte nu iza wodhikko bittay nuss gidana” gidda.
MAR 12:8 Hessa gish hen oyki wodhidi woynne miththaya dizasoppe haraso kessi yegida.
MAR 12:9 Histin woynne miththa goday intes ay oothana milatize? Izi yana, goshanchatakka wodhana, woynne miththa haratas immana.
MAR 12:10 Maxxafan “Shucha keth kexizayti hanena giidi wora yegida shuchay ketha ma7izenes bolla hu7e gididees hessakka Goday othidees. Hessikka nu ayfes malalizaz” getetidi xafetidaysa nababibeyketi?
MAR 12:12 Izi istas lemusoza yotiday ista gish gididaysa Ayhude halaqati erida gish iza oykanas koyda. Gido atin asas babida gish yegidi bida.
MAR 12:13 Iza yon qaxxana mala Parsawistappene Herodosa bagatappe qorerethidi issi issi ass izakko yedida.
MAR 12:14 Istika izakko yidi “Astemare neni moroy baynda ass gididaysa nu eros; ne oonaskka babada wordo madakka; Xoossa oogge xalala tummu tamarsasa. Oromme kawo qesares gira qanxanas besizeye besene? Nu qanxinoye qanxofino?
MAR 12:15 Yesusaykka ista oychoy qodheppe qommo gididaysa eridi <Azas tana qaxana koyeti?> Anne issi dinare hamite ta beyays gidees.
MAR 12:16 Isstikka misha ehin “Haysi iza bolla dizay oona misilenne misille bolla xafetidaysi oona gize? gidees. Istika qesareysakko gida.
MAR 12:17 Yesusaykka “Qessareysa qessares, Xoossisa Xoossas immitte” gidees. Isstikka iza zaron malaletida.
MAR 12:18 Hessappe guye hayqidaytas hayqoppe denthi bawa giza saduqaweti izakko yidi iza hizgi oychida.
MAR 12:19 Astamare issades machcho ekidi na yelonta hayqikko hayqidaysa ishay iza machcheyo ekkidi izas lata na yelana mala kasse Mussey nus xafidees.
MAR 12:20 Gido attin lapun ishanti detees; istafe bayray machcho ekkidi na yelonta hayqidees.
MAR 12:21 Kalozi he macashayo ekidi ha7ikka na yelonta hayqidees. Hezanthoykka yelonta hayqidees.
MAR 12:22 Lappunatikka he macashayo ekkidi latta yelibeyttena wursethan macashayakka hayqadus.
MAR 12:23 Histin lappunatikka izo ekkidashin hayqoppe dendoy diza gidikko ha macashaya istafe onna machcho gidane?” gida.
MAR 12:24 Yesusaykka istas hiz gidees “Inte baletizay gesha maxafatane Xoossa wolqa erontagishaskko.
MAR 12:25 Hayqidayti dendiza wode salo kiitanchata mala gidana atin ekketenane geletena.
MAR 12:26 Hayqidayta dentha gishas gidikko Musse maxafan hesikka qeeri wora gidon eexiza tama gidofe Xoossi “Tanni Aabiramme Xoossa; Yisaqe Xoossa; Yaqoobe Xoossa gididaysa nababibeyketi?
MAR 12:27 Xoossi paxata Xoossu atin hayqethata Xoossu gidena. Hessa gish inte daro baletidetta.” gides.
MAR 12:28 Isstii palamman dishi n Xafistappe issadey ista palamma siyidinne Yesusay oychetidaysas lo7othi zaridaysa akkekidi “Eero azazotappe wursooppe adhizay awayse?” gidi oychidees.
MAR 12:29 Yeususay izas hiz gidees “Wursooppe adhizay hayssa <Isra7ele siya Gosa Xoossi issi Goda,
MAR 12:30 nekka Goda ne Xoossa ne kumetha wozinappe, ne kumetha shempofe, ne kumetha qofappe, ne kumetha woqappe dossa.
MAR 12:31 Namm7anthoykka ne lagge ne hu7e mala dossa.” ha namm7atappe adhiza azazoy bawa.”
MAR 12:32 Xaafezikka “Aastamare lo7o gadasa Xoossi issino gididaysanne izappe haray bayndaysa ne yotidaysi like.
MAR 12:33 Iza ne kummetha wozinnappe ne kummetha qofappe ne kumetha wolqappe dossoy Qassekka ne lagge ne hu7e mala dossoy Xugetiza yarshopene hara yarsho wursoppe adhes” gidees.
MAR 12:34 Yesusayka adezi yushi qoppidi zaridaysa beydi “Neni Xoossa kawotethappe hahondakka.” gidees. Hessappe guye iza ooychanas xalida uray betibeynna.
MAR 12:35 Yesuaya maqidase gathan tamarsishe Muse woga tamarsizayti aazas Kirstosay Dawite na gizo?
MAR 12:36 Dawitey Xiillo Aayanan hasa7ishe “Goday ta Goda ne morketa ta ne too gars athana gakanas ta ushchan uta gidees” gess.
MAR 12:37 Histin Dawitey ba dunara iza Goda gikko wanidi simmi izas na gidane? gidees. Daro dereykka izgizaysa ufaysara siyidees.
MAR 12:38 Izi tamarsishe hiz gidees “Muse woga tamarsizaytappe nagetite, gaderea gochetiza adussa mayo mayidi yush yuyana dosetees; awankka adhi adhi ass istas boncho sarotta immana mala koyettees.
MAR 12:39 Ayhudata wossa kethan dhoqaso, digisasonkka/gibirasonkka/ bonchoso koyetes.
MAR 12:40 Isti azinay baynda macasha keeth kalosetees, qasskka bena besanas adusa wossa wossetes. Haytanti iitta pirda pirdistana.
MAR 12:41 Yesusaykka asay muxuwata yegizason utidi daro asati immizayssa maqidasse misha shishiza saxinen yegizaysa xelidees. Daro dureti daro miish yegida.
MAR 12:42 Issi azinay baynda amm7o dizara issi sikkinappe daronta xarqumala biratappe othetida namm7u miish yegadus.
MAR 12:43 Yesusay bena kalizayta xeygidi ta intes tumu gays “Saxinezan yegida wursoppe hana manqo am7eya adheth yegadus.
MAR 12:44 Hayti wuri ba diza tirppa mishappe yegidashin hana qasse ba manqotetha wolqara bess dizaysa sinthafe izo koshizaysara ubbaa immadus” gides.
MAR 13:1 Izi maqidaseppe kezishin iza kalizaytappe issay astemare haysi kethaynne kethay kexetida shuchay ay mala lo7izakkone hayssa beyay? gidees.
MAR 13:2 Yeusayakka zaridi “hayta giitta kethata xelay? shucahti issay issa bolla diza mala detena, wurikka lalistana” gidees.
MAR 13:3 Yeususay maqidaseza ginara Dabirazayte zumma bolla utidishin Phixirosay, Yaqobey, Yanisaynne Indirasay xalla izakko shiqidi
MAR 13:4 “Haysi ayde hananakkone nus yot. Haysi wursethan polistanas malatay aze? gi oychida.
MAR 13:5 Yesusaykka istas hizgidees “Oonikka intena balethonta mala nagetite.
MAR 13:6 Buro daroti <Ta Kirstosa> gishe ta sunthan yana, darotakka balethana.
MAR 13:7 Inte olanne olla wore siyiza wode dagamopitte. Hessi hananaysi attena. wursethi gidikko burona.
MAR 13:8 Derey dere bolla kawoy kawo bolla dendana, daroson bitta qathinne qoshay hanana, heyti wuri mixas leeso malla.
MAR 13:9 Inte intes nagetite. Buro intena dere dulatan athi immana. Isti intena Ayhudata wossa kethan garafana. Inte ta markata gidana mala ta gish dere dananata sinthaninne kawota sinthan eeqana.
MAR 13:10 Kyoyrotidi mishiracho qalay dere wursos sabakistana beses.
MAR 13:11 Inte oyketidi pirdas shiqiza wode hino he sateyin intes immetizaro hasa7ite atin bidi nu ay gino gidi kaseti hirgopitte. Hasa7anay Xiillo Ayanappe atin intena gideketta.
MAR 13:12 Ishay isha aaway ba na hayqos athi immana. Nayti bena yelidayta bolla makal7ananne wodhana.
MAR 13:13 Ta gedon inte asa wurson ixetidayta gidana. Wurseth gakanas mini eeqidadey gidikko atana.”
MAR 13:14 Inte, dhaysana tunatethi izas besontason eeqidashe beykko nababizadey wozinan wotho, Yudan dizayti pude zumma bolla gangeto.
MAR 13:15 Ketha karen dizadey so gelofo ba miish kesana gidi kethe geloppo.
MAR 13:16 Goshason dizadey ba mayo ekanas guye simoppo.
MAR 13:17 He galasatan qanthera diza macashatasine na dhanthizaytas aye ana!
MAR 13:18 Hessikka balgon gidonta mala Xoossu wositte.
MAR 13:19 Koyro Xoossi medhetetha wursi medhosoppe ha7i gakanas woykko hayssappe guye izara lemusotizay baynda gitta metoy hanana.
MAR 13:20 Goday he galasata qanthotakkao oonikka atena shin bess doretidayta gish he galasata qanthides.
MAR 13:21 He wode oonikka hekko kirstosay hayssan dees, gikko woykko hekko hen dees gikko amanopitte.
MAR 13:22 Wordo kirstosatinne wordo nabeti buro dendidi malatatane kasse hani eeronta palamish oothon istas danda7etikko haray ato shin doretidaytakka balethana.
MAR 13:23 Hessa gish nagetite, he wodey gakonta dishin haara hayssa ubbaa ta intes yotadis.
MAR 13:24 He wode he metozappe kalidi awa arshey dhummana aginaykka po7uku.
MAR 13:25 Xoolinteti saloppe qoqofistana, salon diza wolaqamati qaaxana.
MAR 13:26 He wode asa nay gitta wolqarane bonchora salo sharara yishin asay iza beyana.
MAR 13:27 Izikka kiitanchata yedidi oydu bagafe/mizaneppe/ biitta gaxappe salo gaxa gakanas diza bess doretidayta shishana.
MAR 13:28 Lumusoza balase miththafe tamaritte. Unquloy cililiza wode haythe kesishin bonney matidaysa inte ereista.
MAR 13:29 Hesathokka hayti ta gidayti poletishin inte beykko wodey mati yidi penge gakidayssa erite.
MAR 13:30 Ta intes tumu gays ha yoti polistana gakanas haysi ha yeletay adhena.
MAR 13:31 Saloynne haysi biittay adhana shin ta qalay gidikko adhena.
MAR 13:32 Qasse he glasay gish woykko he satey gish ta aawappe atin salo kitanchata gidinkka naza gidnkka onikka erena.
MAR 13:33 Hessa gish wodey aydekkone inte eronta gish nagetite, minitene wositte.
MAR 13:34 Haysikka ba keth ashikaratas agidi; ashskarata issa issa iza iza ootho oythidi penge nagizaysi begidi nagana mala azazidi bida asa milates.
MAR 13:35 Histikko ketha aaway wode yanakone woykko qama gidi gidoth yanakone woykko kutoy wasishin yanakone woykko wonta bolla sosey zo7ishin yanakko inte erontagish begidi nagitte.
MAR 13:36 Izi yishin inte qopponta zin7idashe izi intena demofo.
MAR 13:37 Ta intes yotizaysa asa wursos yotays, minidi nagite> gays.”
MAR 14:1 Pazigane uketh muussa ba7ale galasay bonchetanas namm7u galasi atishin qesista halaqatine Muse woga tamarsizayti Yesusa balethi oykidi wodhdana ogge koyida.
MAR 14:2 Gido atin asay meto medhonta mala ha bocho ba7ale galasatan gidoppo gida.
MAR 14:3 Izi Biittaniya giza son issi kasse inchiracha hargi paxida Simona getetizaysa son quumma bolla dishin waagay daro al7o gidida nadorse getetiza shitoy kummi utida philqaxe ooykida issi macashaya philqaxeza menthada shitoza Yesusa hu7e bolla gusadus.
MAR 14:4 Hen gadan diza asatappe issi issi asati “haysi shitozi aazas wogay baynda gukize?” gidi ba garsan hanqettida.
MAR 14:5 Shitozi bayzo bayzidakko heedzdzu xeetu dinareppe bollara bayzetidi manqotas immistanashin, giidi macashiyokka kadhida.
MAR 14:6 Gido atin Yesusay istas hizgidees “agitte hano macashayo aazas wayseti? Iza tass lo7o miish oothadus.
MAR 14:7 Manqoti ay wodekka intenara detees. Inte koyda wode aydekka ista madanas danda7ista shin ta gidikko wursso wode intenara dikke.
MAR 14:8 Hanna ba oothanas danda7izari keena oothadus. Tass mogos gidana mala ta asho kasista tiyadus.
MAR 14:9 Ta intes tummu gays haysi mishiracho qalay alame kumethan sabaketizason awankka iza othidaysi izo hassa7isizaz gididi hasa7istana.
MAR 14:10 Hessappe guye tamane namm7atappe issay Asqoroto Yuday Yesusa athi immans qesista halaqatakko bidess.
MAR 14:11 Istika hessa siyidi ufa7etida, izas mishe immans izara gigida. Hessa gish Yesusa athi immanas giga wode nagishe gamm7idees.
MAR 14:12 Paziga dorssi shuketiza uuketha mussa bonchiza koyro galas Yesusa kalizayti Yesusakko shiqidi “Paziga ka7o manaso awan gigisana mala koyaz?” gi oychida.
MAR 14:13 Izikka bena kalizaytappe namm7ata hizgi kitides “Gede katama biitte, inte bishin issi hath otora tokidadaey intenara gagana.
MAR 14:14 Izi bidi gelizaso gakanas iza kalitte. Keethadezas “Astamarey nena, tana kalizaytara paziga ka7o manas tas gidiza immatha shemposoy awayse gidees” giitte.
MAR 14:15 Izikka bolla poqe bolla diza gigi utida aaho so intena bessana, hen izan gigisitte.”
MAR 14:16 Iza kalizaytikka kezidi gede katama bida. Wurikka Yesusay gida mala gidi beetides, pazigakka hen gigisida.
MAR 14:17 Gadey qamishin Yesusay bena kaiza tammane namm7atara gakidees.
MAR 14:18 Issti madan dishin ta intess tummu gays inte gidoppe issay izikka tanara issippe mizaysi tana athi immana” gidees.
MAR 14:19 Istika muzotidi “Tanesha? tanesha? gidi issay issay Yesusa” ooychida.
MAR 14:20 Izikka istas “Tamane namm7atappe issay tanara ba kushe keren yedizadekko.
MAR 14:21 Kasse xafetida mala asa nay iza gish hayqana shin asa na athi immizades aye! He uray kasse yeletonta agidakko izas lo7okoshin!” gides.
MAR 14:22 Issti mishin uketha eeki anjidinne menthidi bena kalizaytas hayssa ta asho heyte gi imidees.
MAR 14:23 Ushakka denthi galatidi istas imin isti wurikka uyida.
MAR 14:24 Qasse “Haysi darotta gish gukkana ta ooratha caqo suutha.
MAR 14:25 Ta intes tummu gays ooratha woyneppe gigida usha Xoossa kawotethan ta uyana galasiyo gakanas namm7antho hayssa uyikke.” gides.
MAR 14:26 Hessafe guye mazmure issippe yexidi pude Dabirazaytte zumma bolla kezida.
MAR 14:27 Yesusay “Ta hemizaysa shocana he wode iza dorssati laletna geteti xafetidaysa mala inte wurikka tanan duphistana.
MAR 14:28 Ta dendidaysappe guye gidikko ta inteppe kasistada Galila bana.” gides.
MAR 14:29 Phixirosaykka “asay wuri dhuphetikkokka tani dhuphetikke!” gides.
MAR 14:30 Yesusaykka “Ta ness tumu gays hach qama kutoy namm7u to wasana gakanas neni tana heedzdzu to kadana” gidees.
MAR 14:31 Phixirosay qass “ta nenara hayqizakkokka mulekka nena kadikke” gidi kehi minthi yotidees. Hankoytikka wuri izaysatho gida.
MAR 14:32 Hessappe guye Getesemane getetizaso bida Yesusaykka bena kalizayta “Tanni wosishin inte hayssan gamm7isitte” gidees.
MAR 14:33 Phixirosa, Yaqobene Yanisa benara eeki bidees. Kehi muzotideesne hirgidees.
MAR 14:34 Qassekka isttas “Ta shempiya daro muzotadus inte han dishittene dhiskonta nagitte” gidees.
MAR 14:35 Istta achappe guthu gede paqidi biitta bolla gufanidi hanikko he sateya izappe adhana mala wosidees.
MAR 14:36 “Abba aabbo, ness wuri danda7etees, hayssa waye xu7a tappe hasa. Gido attin ne sheneppe atin ta sheney hanoppo” gides.
MAR 14:37 Izi heppe simi yishin iza kalizayti dhisikidayta beyidees. Phixirsokka “Simona dhiskadi? Haray ato shin issi satekka sura utada nagoy nena xonide?
MAR 14:38 Inte pacen gelonta mala begidi wositene minite. Shempoy gigeti utidees shin ashoy gidikko daburancha.” gides.
MAR 14:39 Qassekka bidi koyro wosoysathokka wosides.
MAR 14:40 Izi namm7antho simi yishin issta ayfen dhiskoy dexxin dhiskidayta demides, shin issti izas ay zaranakonne eribeytena.
MAR 14:41 Hezantho yidi “Ha7ikka inte zin7idi shempeti? Ha7i gidana, sateyakka gakkadus hekko asa nay nagaranchata kushen adhi immistana.
MAR 14:42 Ane eqitte boss, tana athi immandey yidees.” gides.
MAR 14:43 Izi buro hasa7an dishin tamane namm7atappe issay Yuday yidees. Izara issippe qesse halaqatapene Muse woga tamarsizaytappe kitetida daro asay githa mashanne durqa oykidi yidees.
MAR 14:44 Iza athi immana Yuday istas “asa gidoppe ta yerizadey iza gidida gishas oykidi lo7ethi nagi efiite” gidi kaseti malata immi wothides.
MAR 14:45 Gakida malara Yuday Yesusakko shiqidi “Astamare” gidi yeridees.
MAR 14:46 Assatikka Yesusa oykida.
MAR 14:47 Iza achan eqida issay masha shohoppe shodidi qessista halaqa ashkara hayth qanxidees.
MAR 14:48 Yesusaykka istas “Panga mala tana oykkana mashane durqa oykidi yeti?
MAR 14:49 Wontin wontin maqidassen tamarsashe ta intenara dishin oykibeykista shin kasse xafetidaysi polistan mala haysi hanidees.” gides.
MAR 14:50 Hessa wode iza kalizayti wuri iza yegi agi bida.
MAR 14:51 Be kaloteth qeeri naxalan kamida issi nay Yesusa kalishin asssay iza oykin
MAR 14:52 nazi naxala yegidi kallo kichidees.
MAR 14:53 Yesusakka gede qessista halaqakko efida. Qessista halaqati dere cimatine Muse woga tamarsizayti hen issippe wuri shiqida.
MAR 14:54 Phixirosaykka Yesusa hahora kalishe qessista halaqa gibe gakanas bidees. Izi hen utidi hara asatara tamma ho7ishin
MAR 14:55 qessista halaqatinne dere cimmati wuri Yesusa wodhanas markatana ass koyida shin demanas danda7ibeytena.
MAR 14:56 Daroti iza bolla wordora markatikkokka markata qalay oyketibeynna.
MAR 14:57 Issi issi markati;
MAR 14:58 “Haysi adezi <Ta asa kushen kexetida maqidasse lalada asa kushey bochontaz hara maqidasse heedzdzu galasara ta kexana> gishin nu siyidos” gi markatida.
MAR 14:59 Gidikokka ista markatethi issi bolla woodhibeyna.
MAR 14:60 Qessista halaqaykka ista sinthan dendidi eqqi “Hayti ne bolla markatizaysi aze? Ne aazas duuna zariki?” gidi Yesusa oychidees.
MAR 14:61 Gido atin Yesusay isstas aykokka zaronta coo7u gidees. Qessista halaqay qassekka “Anjetida Xoossa nay kirstosay nene?” gi oychidees.
MAR 14:62 Yesusaykka zaridi “Ee tanank, asa nay woqama Xoossa ushachana utishininne salo sharara yishin inte iza beyana” gides.
MAR 14:63 Qessista halaqay ba mayo dakidi “Nuss hara aza marka koshize?
MAR 14:64 Izi casha qaala Xoossa bolla hasa7ishin inte siyidista ha7ich intes ay milatizee?” gides. Istika izas hayqoy beses giidi wurikka issi qalan pirdida.
MAR 14:65 Hessa wode issi issi asati iza bolla cuchu cutida, iza ayfe goozi oykidi icishe “anne buro hananaysa yoota” gida. Bagayti qasse shagalan baqishe efida.
MAR 14:66 Phixirosay duge bagara hen gibbe gidon dishin qesista halaqa garadistappe issiniya yadaus.
MAR 14:67 Phixirosay tama ho7ishin tish hista xeladane “Neni Nazirete Yesusara dasa gidikki?” gadus.
MAR 14:68 Izi qass “Ne gizaysade ta erikke, ne gizays tass gelena” gidi kadidees. Hessafe gede penge poqi eeqi dishin herakka kutoy wasidees.
MAR 14:69 He garadeya iza be7idamala hen eeqida asatas “Haysi adezi izara diza asatappe issadekko!” gada qassekka hasa7adus.
MAR 14:70 Izi qassekka kadides. Gutha wode gamm7ishin hen eqida asati Phixirossa “Neni Galila asa, hessa gish tummappe ne isstappe issade” gida.
MAR 14:71 Gido atin izi qass “inte gizade ta erikke” gishe caqonne bena qangeth oykidees.
MAR 14:72 Herakka kutoy namm7antho wasidees. Phixirosaykka “kutoy namm7a wasanas ne tana hedza kadana” gida Yesusa qalay izas qopetin hiqumidi yekides.
MAR 15:1 Malado wontara qessista halaqti dere cimatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti kummetha shango alafistara issippe zoretidi Yesusa qachi ekki efidi Philaxosas athi immida.
MAR 15:2 Philaxosaykka Yesusa “Ne Ayhudata kawo?” gi ooychidees. Yesusakka “Ee ne gida mala” gidi izas zaridees.
MAR 15:3 Qessista halaqatikka daro yoho iza bolla shisi motida.
MAR 15:4 Philaxosay qass “Ne aazas malthe immikki? Hekko nena daro yon motetes” giidi qassekka oychidees.
MAR 15:5 Gido atin Yesusay ha7ikka izas aykkoka malthe imonta gish Pilaxosaykka malaletides.
MAR 15:6 Paziga ba7ale galas Pilaxosay derey birshana mala oychidade birshi yediza wogay kasse dees.
MAR 15:7 Itta oothon dere bolla dendidi shemppo wodhida asatara issippe qashetida barbane getetiza issadey dees.
MAR 15:8 Dereykka yidi kasse dosse gididaysa izi oothana mala Philaxosa wosidees.
MAR 15:9 Pilaxosaykka istas “Ta intes Ayhude kawo birshana mala koyetii? gi ooychidees.
MAR 15:10 Philaxosay hessaththo ooychiday kasse qessista halaqati Yesusa qanaten athi immidaysa eriza gishasa.
MAR 15:11 Qessista halaqati qass iza olla Barbaney birsheto gi oychana mala dereza denthethida.
MAR 15:12 Philaxosay “Histikko inte Ayhuda kawo giza adeza wostana mala koyeti” gides.
MAR 15:13 Issti qassekka “Kaqa kaqa” gi wasida.
MAR 15:14 Philaxosaykka “Ay iita oothide?” gi istta oychidees. Istti qass “Kaqa kaqa” gidi kasseppe athi wasida.
MAR 15:15 Philaxosaykka dereza ufaysana gidi Barbane istas birshides. Yesusa garafidi kaqanas athi immidees.
MAR 15:16 Wotadarati Yesusa dere harizaysa gibe ekki bidi atida wotadarata wursi shishida.
MAR 15:17 Yesusa waga la7o gidida zo7o mayo mayzida; aguntha akilile xaxidi iza hu7en wothida.
MAR 15:18 Hessappekka “Aayhuda kawo saroy ness gido!” gishe iza sarothida.
MAR 15:19 Iza hu7e gufera shocida; iza bollakka cutida gulbatidi izas goynida.
MAR 15:20 Iza bolla qidhi ka7idappe guye kasse mayzida zo7o mayoza qari ekidi kase iza mayoza zari mayzidi kaqanaso eki bida.
MAR 15:21 Alakisandrosanne Rufosa aawa Simmona getetiza issi qarena dere assi dereppe katama yizaysa Yesusa masqale wolqara ooyki tosida.
MAR 15:22 Hessafe Yesusa izas birshechay “asa hu7e guge” Golgothu getetizaso efida.
MAR 15:23 Karbe getetiza dhalera walaketida woynne caje uuyana mala izas immin izi ekonta ixidees.
MAR 15:24 Hessafe guye iza kaqida, iza mayo issade issade awaysa gakanakone gidi sama yegidi gishetida.
MAR 15:25 Issti iza kaqishin wonappe hezu saatte gididees.
MAR 15:26 Isstti masqale bolla xafi shishida moto qalay “Aayhude kawo” giza qaala.
MAR 15:27 Izara issippe namm7u pangata issa izappe ushachara issa hadirsara kaqida.
MAR 15:28 Heesankka kasse maxafay “Ittatara issippe taybetidees” gida tinbite qalay poletidees.
MAR 15:29 Ooggera adhi bizaytikka ba hu7e qathishe “Oy! oy! maqidasse lalada hezu galasan kexanay nene?” gidi pala cashe cayishe;
MAR 15:30 “Anne ha7i masqale bollappe wodhada nena asha” gida.
MAR 15:31 Hesathokka Qessista halaqatinne Muse woga tamarsizayti ba garsan issay issas “harata ashidees shin bena ashana danda7ibeyna” gidi iza qidhida.
MAR 15:32 “Nu iza beydi amanana mala anne haysi kirsotosay Isra7elista kawoy ha7i masqaleppe wodho” gida. Izara kaqetidaytikka iza bolla cashe korida.
MAR 15:33 Usuppun satteppe oykidi uudufun sate gakaans biittay wuri dhumidees.
MAR 15:34 Uddufun satte bolla Yesusay “Eelohe eelohe lama sabaqitani?” gidi qaala dhoqu histidi wasidees. Hessas birshechay “Ta Xoosso Xoosso ne tana aazas agadi” gussa.
MAR 15:35 Hen gadan eqida asappe issi issi asati hessa siyidi “Eelasa xeygesikko” gida.
MAR 15:36 Hesappe issi uray eleli bidi calida woynne caje isponje mala mishan gelithi kessidi miththa xeran qaphidi uuyana mala Yesusas shishidees. Hessafe qasse “Anne agagitte Elasay yidi iza kaqoppe wothishin nu beynna” gidees.
MAR 15:37 Hessafe Yesusay qaala dhoqu histi wasidi shempo kezides.
MAR 15:38 Meqidase magalasha pude hu7era duge namm7u kezi daketidees.
MAR 15:39 Yesusa ginara eqida issi xeetu wotadara halaqay Yesusay hessaththo gita qalara wasidi shemppo kezishi beydi “Haysadey tummu Xoossa nakoshin” gidees.
MAR 15:40 Hessa wode macashati hanizaysa hahon didi xeleida. Issta gidoppe Magidaleppe yida Maramane natiza Yaqobene Yossa aayo Maramira qassekka Solomira issippe deetes.
MAR 15:41 Heyti macashati Galilan Yesusa kalishene izas othishe gamm7idayta. Istarakka issippe hara daro macashati Yerusalame bida.
MAR 15:42 Wodey qami qami bishin Sanbatas gigetiza galasi gakidees.
MAR 15:43 Dere cimata garsan bonchetida issi Armata ass Yosefo getetizaysi Xoossa kawoteth nagishe dizadey babonta Philaxossakko bidi Yesusa anha wosidees.
MAR 15:44 Philaxosaykka izi hini wode elera hayqidaysa siyidi malaletidees. Xeetu wotadarata halaqa xeygidi izi hayqin woqa wodekkonne ooychidees.
MAR 15:45 Izi hayqidaysa xeetu wotadarata halaqay geshi eridappe guye Yesusa anha Yosefos immidees.
MAR 15:46 Yosefoykka mogo mayo shamidi anha masqaleppe wothidi mogo mayon xaxidi shuchappe wocetida dufon wothidees. Duhaaththaa dunna shuchara tucidees.
MAR 15:47 Magidaleppe yida Maramirane Yossa ayo Maramra Yesusa anha awan mogidakkon beyida.
MAR 16:1 Sanbatay adhidappe guye Magidale Marama Yaqobe aayo Maramira Salomira issippe bidi Yesusa anha tiyanas shito shamida.
MAR 16:2 Samintafe koyro galas malado wontara buro awa arshey kezida mala Yesusa dufokk buro bishin
MAR 16:3 “Dufoza dunappe shucha nuss ooni gendersanee?” gidi ba garsan hasa7etida.
MAR 16:4 Issti dhoqu gi xelishin daro gitta shuchay dufoza dunappe genderidaysa beyida.
MAR 16:5 Gede dufoza giddo gelida mala issi botha mayo mayida panthi ushacha bagara utidaysa beyidi dagamida.
MAR 16:6 Izi qass istas “Dagamopitte inte kaqetida Nazirete Yesusa koyista, izi dendidees han deena, issti iza wothidaso hayssa beyte” gidees.
MAR 16:7 Gido atin inte biidi iza kalizaytasine Phixirosas kasse intes yotida mala inteppe kasetidi izi Galila bana. Inte iza hen demana gidi istas yotitte gidees.
MAR 16:8 Macashatikka malaletishene kokorishe dufappe kezi baqatida. Babida gish oonasikka aykkokka qatibeytena.
MAR 16:9 Samintappe koyro galas Wogga wonta maladora izi hayqoppe dendidappe guye Yesusay izippe lappun daydanth kesida Magidale Maramis koyro betides.
MAR 16:10 Izakka bada kasse izara dizayti muzotishenne yekishe dishin demada yotadus.
MAR 16:11 Isti Yesusay paxa dizaysanne iza ta iza beyadis gidaysa siyidi amanibeytena.
MAR 16:12 Hessappe guye iza kalizaytappe namm7ati gede dere gars bishin Yesusay isstas hara ass milati betidees.
MAR 16:13 Isstikka simidi hessa iza kalizaytappe atidaytas yotida. Gido atin iza kalizyti siyidi amaibeytena.
MAR 16:14 Hessappe guye tammane issineti kaththa madan dishin Yesusay istas qoncidees. Izi hayqoppe dendin iza beyida asati isstas yotin siyidi ammanonita agida gish isstas ammanoy bayndaysanne issta wozina mumetetha gish issta borides.
MAR 16:15 Isstaskka hizgidees “Gede alame wursoso biite, mishracho qaala medhetetha wursoso sabakitte.”
MAR 16:16 Aamanidayne xamaqetiday atana. Amanontay gidikko pirdistana.
MAR 16:17 Tana amanizayta hayti malatati kalana. Isti ta sunthan daydanthata kesana, ooratha qalankka hasa7ana.
MAR 16:18 Issti shoshata ba kushera oykkana, wodhiza marzekka uyikoka issta qohena. Be kushe harganchata bolla wothi wossikko haraganchati paxana.
MAR 16:19 Goda Yesusay hessa yotidappe gueye pudde salo dendidi bidi Xoossa ushacan utidees.
MAR 16:20 Iza kalizayti hessappe kezidi wursoson adhi adhi sabakida. Godaykka isstara oothidees. Issta timirteza ekidi oothizaytas ba yotida qalakka malata othi othi minthidees.
LUK 1:1 Boncho Toofilosa nu achchan hanida yota gish daro asati bees hanida mala xaafida.
LUK 1:2 He taarikkezikka koyroppe denthidi ba ayfera be7ida markattine Xoossa qaala yoottidayti nuus aathiddayssa.
LUK 1:3 Taka ta baggara xaphoppe denthada keeha naagistadanne paaca xeellada taarikkeza wursa sinthe xaafistanaas bessizaysa sinthasada kaallidi xaafistanaas bessizaysa kaalethada naagettada nees xaafana mala taas lo7o gidi beettides.
LUK 1:4 Haysa wurssa ta oothizay ne tamaaridaysi tuma gididayssa nena ero guussassa.
LUK 1:5 Herdossay Yuda biittan kawottida wode Aabiya geettetiza qeessista halaqqa bagafe qeessetetha ootho taray iza gakida Zakarassa geetettiza issi qeessey dees. Iza machcheyaka Elsabeexxo geetetaysu, izaka Aaronne bagga asa. Nam7atika Goda azazonne iza woga wothoy bayndda naagidi dizaytanne Xoossa sinthan xillo asa.
LUK 1:7 Gido attin Elsabeexxa na yelonta makkara gidida gish istas nay baa, nam77atika wodey sugetida asa.
LUK 1:8 Zakarassay Xoossa sinthan qeessetetha ootho taray iza gakin izi oothishin
LUK 1:9 qeessistas diza woga mala Xoossa keeththan gelidi exxaane cuwassana mala exay iza gakkidees.
LUK 1:10 Exxaaney cuwattishshin asay wurikka karen diidi woosses.
LUK 1:11 Goda kiitanchay exxaaney cuwatiza sooppe oshacha baggara eqqidi Zakarasas beettides.
LUK 1:12 Zakarasaykka iza beyidi keehi dagammidi babbides.
LUK 1:13 Kiitanchay Zakarasas babbofa ne woossay setettides, ne machcheya Elssabeexxa nees attumma na yelana iza sunthaka ne Yanisa gaada sunthanna.
LUK 1:14 Iza yellistan neni daro ufa7istana, daro asaykka ufa7istana.
LUK 1:15 Goda sinthan izi gita gidana. woyneppe oothetida cajje gidinkka hara mathosiza usha gidinkka izi uyenna, izi buro ba aayye qanthen dishe xillo ayanan kumana.
LUK 1:16 Isra7eele asappe darota ista Xoossako zarana.
LUK 1:17 Aawata wozina ista naytaakko, azazettontaytikka gede xillota cincatethakko zaarana malanne Godas bessiza dere giigissana mala Elaasa ayananne iza wolqan Godappe sinthara izi baanna.
LUK 1:18 Zakarassay kiitanchas, tani cima ta machcheyakka cimadus tani hayssa aazan eranee? giidi oychchides.
LUK 1:19 Kiitanchaykka zaaridi tani Xoossa sinthan eqqiza Gabrelle. Tanika ha miishrachchoza nees gathanas kiitistada yadis.
LUK 1:20 Heko neni ba woden polistana ta qaala amanontta ixxida gish ne duunay muummaana, nenikka haasa7ana dandda7akka gides.
LUK 1:21 He wode derey Zakarassay Xoossa keethafe kezonta aazas gam77idakkonne giidi handadhettishe naagides.
LUK 1:22 Izi Xoossa keethafe kezidi asa haasa7isanas danda7ibeynna. malati malati bessoppe attin haasa7anas danda7onta aggin asay izi Xoossa keeththan Xoossafe ooratha miish beyddaysa erides.
LUK 1:23 Zakarasaykka ba ootho taray polettidappe guyyen ba so simmides.
LUK 1:24 Hessafe kaallin iza machcheya Elsabeexxa na qanthatadus, ichachchantho aginnay gakanas asi bena beyontta mala qotistadus.
LUK 1:25 Izaka Goday ba maarotan ta kadhetetha asa giddofe digganas ha wodezan hayssa taas oothides gadus.
LUK 1:26 Elsabeexxa qanthatidda usuppuntha aginan, Xoossi ba kiitancha Gabrelle, Galila biittan diza, Naazirete giza katama yeddides.
LUK 1:27 Izikka kawo Daawutte zereth gidida Yosefo geettetiza asas giiga utida Maaramo geetettiza geela7oyko kiitettides.
LUK 1:28 Yiidine iza dizaaso gelidi “hanne Xoossi nena anjjidare saro Xoossi Goday nenara dees nenika anjettidaro” gides.
LUK 1:29 Maarama kiitancha haasa7ani keha dagamada, haysi ay giza sarota gaada yoza keha qoppadus.
LUK 1:30 Kiitanchaykka Maaramo “Xoossi nenan ufa7etiza gish babbofa,
LUK 1:31 neni qanthatana, attumma naaka yelana, sunthakka Yesussa gaada sunthanna,
LUK 1:32 Izika gita gidana, wursofe bolla Xoossa na geetettana, Godaa Xoossay iza aawa Daawutte kawotetha izas immana.
LUK 1:33 Izi Isra7eelle nayta bollan medhinas kawotana, iza kawotethaskka wurisethi deenna.”
LUK 1:34 Maaramaka kiitanchas “tani adde gelabeyke, shin haysi waani hananee?” gaada oychchadus.
LUK 1:35 Kiitanchayka Maaramis “xillo ayaanaay ne bolla wodhana wursofe bolla Xoossa wolqay ne bolla kuwasa na hessa gish yellistana naazi geeshsha Xoossa na geetettana.
LUK 1:36 Asi yeluku iza makkara giidi haasa7iza ne dabboya Elsabeexxa cimatethan attumma na qanthatada yelanaas usupuntho aginna oykadus.
LUK 1:37 Xoossassi hanonta miishi baa.”
LUK 1:38 Maaramakka zaaradda hekko tani Xoossa aylle diikkina ne gida mala taas hano giin kiitanchay izippe shaakettidi biddes. Maarama Elsabeexxo beyana badus.
LUK 1:39 Maaramakka he wode matara eesota denddada pude geze deren diza issi Yuda katama badus.
LUK 1:40 Zakarassa keethe geladakka Elsabeexxo sarotadus.
LUK 1:41 Elsabeexxa Maarami sarotha siyida mala qanthan diza naazi izi qanthan guppides, Elsabeexxinkka xillo ayaanaay kumides.
LUK 1:42 Izaka ba qaala dhoqqu oothada hiz gadus “maccassa wursofe ne anjettidaro, ne qanthen diza naazikka anjetidaysa.
LUK 1:43 Ta Goda aaya taako yada tana oychanas tani oonee?
LUK 1:44 Ne sarotho qaala ta siyida mala ta ulo giddon diza nay ufaysan guppides.
LUK 1:45 Polistana giidi Goday izis yoottidaysa amaniddara iza anjjetidaro.”
LUK 1:46 Maaramakka izi ba aylleyi kawushshatetha xellida gish ta shemppiya Goda dhoqqu oothada bonchaysu. Ta ayanaykka tana ashshizza ta Xoossan ufa7istaysu. Wolqqama Goday taas giita miishshe oothida gish hachchife sinthan asi wuri tana anjjettidaro gaana. Iza sunthaykka geeshsha.
LUK 1:50 Iza maaretethay izas babizayttas na na gakanas daana.
LUK 1:51 Be wolqan daro mino ootho oothides ba wozina qofan otoretizayta laalides.
LUK 1:52 Kawota kawotethafe wothides, ashketta qasse dhoqqu dhoqqu histtides.
LUK 1:53 Gafidayta lo7o miishshan kalthides durista gidikko mela kushe yeddides.
LUK 1:54 Kase nu aawatas Abramesinne iza qommotas gida qaala naaganas ba maaretetha yushi qoppidi ba aylle Isra7eele maaddides gadus.
LUK 1:56 Maaramakka Elsabeexxi achchan heezzu agina sire gam7ada ba so simadus.
LUK 1:57 Elsabeexxis yelo gallassay gakin attumma na yeladus.
LUK 1:58 Izi guttattinne dabbottikka Goday izis gita maaretetha oothidaysa siyidi izira issife ufa7ettida.
LUK 1:59 Yellettida osppuntha gallas qaxaras yida. aaza aawa sunthan Zakarasa giidi sunthana koyida.
LUK 1:60 Gido attin aaya hanena, iza sunthi Yanisa geetetto gadus.
LUK 1:61 Istika izis ne dabbotappe Yanisa geetettidi xeysettida asi oonikka baawa gida.
LUK 1:62 Aaway Zakarassay naaza oona giidi sunthana koyidakonne malaatan oychchida.
LUK 1:63 Zakarasaykka xaafiza miishshe izas immana mala oychchi ekkidi sunthay “Yanisa” giidi xaafin asay wurikka malalettides.
LUK 1:64 Heeraka Zakarassa duunay pogettidi inxarssay birshettin Xoossa galata oykides.
LUK 1:65 Iza guttati wuri daro babbidda. Haysi wurikka dhoqqa geze biittan Yuda dereni, wurso son haasa7ettides.
LUK 1:66 Haysaka siyida asi wurikka ha guutha nay ay hananeeshsha? giidi hanoza wursika ba wozinan oykkides. Goda kushey tumappe izara issife dees.
LUK 1:67 Naaza aaway, Zakarassay xillo ayaanan kumidi tinbbite haasa7ishe
LUK 1:68 yiidi ba asa ashshidda gish Isra7eele Xoossi galatetto gides.
LUK 1:69 Beni wode ba geeshsha nabeta duunan haasa7ettidayssa mala ba aylle Daawute keeththan ashshizza woliqqa nuus denthides.
LUK 1:71 Izi nuna nu morketappene, nuna ixxizayta kusheppe ashshees.
LUK 1:72 Haysa izi oothiday nu aawatas ba maaretetha bessanassa, ba geeshsha caaqqoza yushi qoppanaasa.
LUK 1:73 Kase nu aawa Abrames caaqqidayssa qopana malane, nu morketa kusheppe izi nuna kessin nuni izas babboy baayndda oothanasinne, nu diza wode wurson ba sinthan nuna geeshshatethanne xillotethan essanassa.
LUK 1:76 Goda oge giigissanas ne izappe sinthara biza gish ta naazo neni woga Xoossa nabe geetetana.
LUK 1:77 Assay ba nagarappe maaretida gish deres attotetha erateth ne immana mala
LUK 1:78 nu Xoossa lo7o maaretethafe denddidayssan saloppe nuus away kezides.
LUK 1:79 Hessikka dhuman dizaytasne hayqqo kuwa garsan dizaytaskka po7isana malane nu tohotakka sarotetha oge kalethannassa.
LUK 1:80 Guutha naazikka diccides ayananka minnidees. Isra7eele asas qonccen beettanna gakkanaas bazo biittan deyides.
LUK 2:1 He wode biitta bollan diza asi wurikka taybeettidi xafistana mala orome kawo Awuggisxxossafe awajjay kezides:
LUK 2:2 Hessikka Qerenewoossa geetettizaysi Soore giza dere haariza wode hannida koyro dere taybo.
LUK 2:3 Hessa gish asi wuri xafistanaas ba dere biddes.
LUK 2:4 Yosefoykka asho dabbotethan Daawute bagafe gididda gish Galila awurajja garssan diza Naazirete katamappe Yuda awurajja Beettaleme geetettiza Daawute katamappe yidees.
LUK 2:5 Izi xafistana bishin izas giigistada yelana matida Maaramira biddes.
LUK 2:6 Izetikka heen dishin izis yelo wodey gakkides.
LUK 2:7 Izaka koyro attumma na yeliddaysafe guye imathi aqqizza keeththan aqqizza soy bayndda gish naaza carqqara xaaxadda miiza gaaxotan zin7adus.
LUK 2:8 Beettaleme achchan dorssa heemiza asati dorssa naagishe qammaara karen aqqizzayti deetees.
LUK 2:9 Goda kiitanchaykka istako yides, Goda boncho poo7oykka ista lanqqen yuuyi aadhdhannas po7ides. Istika keehi dagammida gish,
LUK 2:10 kiitanchay ista “babofite, wurso asas gidiza gita ufaysa miishshrachcho ekka yadis.
LUK 2:11 Hach kawo Daawute katama Beettalemen shemppo dhaley yellettidees. Izikka Goda kirstosa geetettees.
LUK 2:12 Cariqqara xaxeti zin7ida gaccino na demmanddista hessikka intes malaata gido gides.”
LUK 2:13 Izarakka hara daro salo kiitanchati beettidda. Xoossa galatishe,
LUK 2:14 bolla salon Xoossassi bonchoy gido sarotethaykka biitta bollan izi dosiza asas wursos gido gida.
LUK 2:15 Kiitanchati istafe shaakkettidi salo simmin dorsse heemizayti ba garsan issay issa “ane ha yite Goday nuus qonccisidaysanne haanddayssa Beistalame katama biiddi beyos” gida.
LUK 2:16 Istika elelli biiddi Maaramira, Yosefora mehe kath muziza gonggen zin7ida naara demmida.
LUK 2:17 Beyddaysafe guyyen Goda kiitanchay naaza gish istas yoottidayssa wursi zari yottida.
LUK 2:18 Heemizayti yoottidayssa siyida asay wuri keehi malalettides.
LUK 2:19 Gido attin Maarama yoza wurssa ba wozinan wotha dentha qoppashe gam7adus.
LUK 2:20 Heemizaytika handdays wurikka kiitanchay istas yoottida mala gididi beettidda gish siyidaysassine beyddayssas wursos Xoossa galatishenne bonchishshe simmida.
LUK 2:21 naazi yelettin osppuntha gallassan qaxaretiza wodey gakin aayeya iza qanthatanappe kase kiitanchay gida mala Yesussa geetettidi suummidees.
LUK 2:22 Muse woga mala isti geeyiza wodey wurini Yosefoyne Maarama guutha na Yesussa Godaa Xoossa sinthe shiishanas ekkidi Yerusaleme kezida. Hessika Goda wogan koyro yelettiza addey wuri Godas dumma gidana geetettidi Xafetidayssa polanaasinne,
LUK 2:24 qassekka Goda wogan nam77u wole kafotanne woykko nam77u wole kafo ciyista geetettiddayssa mala yarsho shiishanaassa.
LUK 2:25 He wode Yerusaleme kataman xilloonne Xoossa babbiza issi Simona geetettiza asi dees, izikka Isra7eele nayta attotetha naagiza asane xillo ayyaanany iza bolla shemppida asa.
LUK 2:26 Qassekka kirstossa beyontta dishe hayqqonta mala xillo ayyaanany izas qonccides.
LUK 2:27 Izika he wode xillo ayyaanany kaalethin maqqdase lasha gaath gelidees. Naaza aayeyiranne aawara Muse wogan bessizayssa polanaas guutha na Yesussa ekkidi gelida wode,
LUK 2:28 Simonay naaza ekki idimmidi Xoossa galatishe,
LUK 2:29 “Godo, ne caaqqida qaala mala ha7i tani ne ayylleya ne ashshizzayssa ta ayfera beyidda gish hi7a tana saron ekka, asa wurso sinthan ne giigisida attotetha ha7i ta ta ayfera beyadis.
LUK 2:32 Haysika wurso deres geemmettidayssa qoncisiza poo7o, ne dere Isra7eleska boncho” gides.
LUK 2:33 Aawaynne aaya iza gish haasa7etida yozan malaletida.
LUK 2:34 Simonaykka ista anjjidees, Maaramokka “daro asa wozina qofay qonccana mala haysi Isra7eelen diza darotas dhayosinne atethas, iza ixxizaytas qasse malaata gidana mala doorettides” gides.
LUK 2:35 Qassekka darota wozina qofay qonccana mala naaza michay qara mashsha mala ne wozina phaliqqana.
LUK 2:36 Qassekka Aasseere bagafe Fanu7eele na Haana geetettiza cimmida nabey daysu, izaka ba koyro azinara laappun layth kumeth deyadus.
LUK 2:37 Laythay izis osppun tammanne oydu layth gidana gakkanaas qammane gallas xoomashene woossashe maqqdaseppe shaakketonta am77etethan gam77adus.
LUK 2:38 He wodekka shiiqqada Xoossa galatadus. Yerusaleme wozetethi naagishe dizaytas wursos guutha naaza gish yootadus.
LUK 2:39 Yoseforane Maaramira Goda wogan azazettidayssa polidi Galila awurajjan diza ba so Naazirete katama simmida.
LUK 2:40 Guutha naazikka diccidi minni minni biddes, eratethankka kumides, Xoossa aaro keyatethaykka iza bolla dees.
LUK 2:41 Aawaynne aaya laythan laythan faaziga bonchannas Yerusaleme beettes.
LUK 2:42 Naazas laythay tammanne nam77u layth kumida wode kase dose gididayssa mala faaziga bonchanna kezida.
LUK 2:43 Faziga baaleza wursidi ba so simmishn guutha naazi, Yesussay Yerusalemen attides. Yelidaytikka izi attiddayssa eribeeyttenna.
LUK 2:44 Benara issife biza oge asara dees gishe issi gallassa oge bida. Gido attin izi istara baynddaysa eridi ba dabbota achchanne laggeta achchan dizakkonne giidi koyida.
LUK 2:45 Koyi koyidi beettontta ixiin Yerusaleme simmida.
LUK 2:46 Heezzu gallassafe guye maqqdasen tamarisizayta giddon uttidi siyishenne asata oychchishenne ista oychcha zarishe maqqdasen dishin demmida.
LUK 2:47 Siyidayti wuri Yesussa akekkaninne iza zarozan daro malaalettida.
LUK 2:48 Yosefoyne Maarama iza beyida wode malaaletida. Maaramaka ta nazo ays hayssa mala oothadi? ne aawaynne taninne nena koyishe keehi metottettidos gadus.
LUK 2:49 Izikka zaaridi tana ays koydettii? Tani ta aawa keeththan daanas bessizaysa eribeykketi gides.
LUK 2:50 Gido attin istas izi yoottidayssi gelibeynna.
LUK 2:51 Heeppe simmin istara issife Naazirete wodhidi istas azazettishe deyidees. Aaya Maaramaka he haanida miishsha wurssa ba wozinan naagashe gam7adus.
LUK 2:52 Yesussay cincatethan, geesaninne saban Xoossa sinthanne asa sinthan diccides.
LUK 3:1 Xiibaros geetettiza qeesarey kawottida tammanne ichachchantho laythan Phanxoossa Philaxosa gizays Yuda biitta haariza wode, Herdossay Galila biitta haariza wode, iza ishay piliphoossay, Ixuriyasanne Xirakkondose biitta haariza wode, Lisannyossay Sabilane biitta haariza wode,
LUK 3:2 Haanaynne Qayafay waana qeeseta gidida wode Xoossa qaalay baazo biittan diza Zakarassa na Yanisakko yides.
LUK 3:3 Yaanisay Yordanose shoore achchan diza dereta wurson “inte nagara atto gaanas nagarappe simmidi xamaqqetite” gidi yoottides.
LUK 3:4 Hessika qasse nabe Isayaasay bazon hizgidi wassiza asa koshinch “Godas oge giigissite baassidikka lo7ethite.
LUK 3:5 Shoobba biittay wuri kumana guutha zumayne gita zumay wuri ziq gaana geella ogey sitta moorettida ogey lo7o gidana.
LUK 3:6 Asa zerethi wuri ashshizza Xoossa woliqqa beyana giidi bazon wassiza asa qaala giireth” giidi ba maxaafan xaafida mala.
LUK 3:7 Yanisaykka iza kushen xamaqqistana yiza asas “inteno ha shoosha nayto yaana diza Xoossa hanqqofe haakkana mala ooni intena zoridee?
LUK 3:8 Inte naggara oothoppe simmidayssa erisiza ootho oothite <Abramey nu aaway nuus dees> gusi aggitte gides. Xoossi bees giikko ha shuchchatappe Abrames na oothi denthaanas dandda7izayssa erite”
LUK 3:9 Beyxxey mith qanxanas miththa xaphon dees. Lo7o ayfe ayfontta iita mithi wuri qanxettidi taman yegistana.
LUK 3:10 Asaykka “histtini ay oothooni” giidi oychchides.
LUK 3:11 Yanisaykka asas “nam77u mayoy diza issi mayoy bayndda asas imo qassekka qumay dizaykka shaakkidi immo” gides.
LUK 3:12 Qaraxa shiishizayttikka xamaqqistanaas yiidi “tamarisizayso nu ay oothino?” gida.
LUK 3:13 Izikka “inte azazettidayssafe bollara qaraxa shiishoppite” gides.
LUK 3:14 Wotadarattikka “nuni qasse ay oothino” giidi oychchida. izikka “oona miishshakka gidin dafi ekkofite qassekka oonane wordon mootopite inte damozay intes giddana” gides.
LUK 3:15 Asay Yanisa beyidi haysi kirstossa? giidi ba wozinan sidhides.
LUK 3:16 Yanisaykka wursos “tani intena haathan xamaqays gido attin ta iza caamma birshaanas besoontta tappe aadhdhizaddey yaana. izi intena Xillo Ayaananne taman xamaqqana.
LUK 3:17 Kath suragiza layiday iza kushen dees. Balezza kumetha geeshshanna gistteza qasse di7en qollana gafezakka to7onta taman xuugana” gides.
LUK 3:18 Yanissay asa hara dumma dumma zore qaalara minnithethi zorishe mishrachcho qaala yoottides.
LUK 3:19 Gido attin Galila biitta haariza Herdoosay ba isha machcho Herooddiyaado ekkida gishine hara daro iita oothida gish Yanisay iza hanqqida gish
LUK 3:20 kase mooro bolla hara gujjidi Herdossay Yaanisa woyne keeththan yegides.
LUK 3:21 Asay xamaqqettidappe guyyen Yesussaykka xamaqqetides, izi woosishin saloy doyettides.
LUK 3:22 Xillo Ayyaanaykka wole milattida iza bolla wodhides. “saloppe ta dosiza nay nena nenan tani ufa7istays” giza qaalay yides.
LUK 3:23 Yesussay Xoossa ootho oykkishn laythay izas heezu tamu laytha mala gidana. Asaykka izi Yosefo na, Eelle na,
LUK 3:24 Maati na, Lewe na, Milki na, Yuda na, Yosefo na,
LUK 3:25 Matattiyu na, Amoxxe na, Nahome na, Isilime na, Naage na,
LUK 3:26 Maate na, Matatiyo na, Semeye na, Yosefo na, Yuda na,
LUK 3:27 Yoonane na, Reese na, zerubbaabeele na, Selatiyale na, Nere na,
LUK 3:28 Milki na, hadi na, Yosa na, Qoosame na, Elimodamme na,
LUK 3:29 Yose na, Elazare na, Yorame na, Maaxate na, Eelle na,
LUK 3:30 Simoona na, Yuda na, Yosefo na, Yooname na, Eliyaqqeeme na,
LUK 3:31 Meliya na, Maaxate na, Naatane na, Daawute na,
LUK 3:32 Iseeye na, Iyobede na, Bo7eeze na, Selimoona na, Ne7asoone na,
LUK 3:33 Amnaddabe na, Aarame na, Aaronne na, Esrome na, Faareesse na, Yuda na,
LUK 3:34 Yaqoobe na, Yisaqqa na, Abrame na, tara na, Nakore na,
LUK 3:35 Seerohe na, Raggawe na, Faaleeqqe na, Aabere na, Saala na,
LUK 3:36 Qayneme na, Aarfakkisidde na, Seeme na, Nohe na, Lamehe na,
LUK 3:37 Matosala na, Henokke na, Yarede na, Malali7eele na, Qaynane na,
LUK 3:38 Henosse na Seete na Addamme na, Xoossa na, milatides.
LUK 4:1 Yesussay Xillo Ayyaanaan kumidi Yordanose shooreppe simmida mala Xillo Ayyaanaany iza kaalethidi bazzo biitta efides.
LUK 4:2 Heenkka xala7en oydu tamu gallassa paacetides. He paacetiza galassatan aykkokka monta gish wursethan gafides.
LUK 4:3 Xala7eykka Yesussa ne Xoossa na gidikko ane hayssa shuchchay kath gidana mala azaza gides.
LUK 4:4 Yesussaykka zaaridi asi kaththan xalla deenna geetettidi xafettides, giidi xala7es zaarides.
LUK 4:5 Hessafe kaallidi xala7ey Yesussa issi dhoqqa zuma bolla kessidi salo gufanthon diza kawotetha qiphphida ayfey xeelanas beesdine,
LUK 4:6 haysi ne beyizza biitta kawotetha duretethay wurikka taas imetides taka ta dosizaddes immanas dandda77iza gish, neeska immana gides.
LUK 4:7 Hesa gish ne kunddada taas goynnikko haysi wurikka nees gidana gides.
LUK 4:8 Yesussaykka zaaridi ne Godaa Xoossaassi kunddada iza xalla woosa geettetidi xaafettides gides.
LUK 4:9 Hessafekka Yesussa Yerusalemeni maqqdase xeera kessi essidi Xoossa maxaafan “nena naagana mala Xoossi ne gish ba kiitancha azazanna, ne toy shuuchchan qoxetonta mala kiitanchati ba kushera nena dhoqqu histi oykkana” geetettidi xaafettida gish ne Xoossa na gikikko ane hayssafe duge kundda gides.
LUK 4:12 Yesussaykka “ne Godaa Xoossa paacofa” geetettides giidi zaarides.
LUK 4:13 Xala7eykka ba paacanayisa wursidappe guyyen hara bees giiga wodey beettanashshe Yesussappe shaakkettides.
LUK 4:14 Yesussaykka Xillo Ayyaanaan wolqan Galila simmides. Iza lo7o nashoy Galila achchan diza deretan wurson siyettides.
LUK 4:15 Izikka mukkuraben tamaarisishin iza timirttey lo7in asay wurikka iza galatides.
LUK 4:16 Heeppe ba yellettida katama Naazirete yiidi kase sanbbata gallas mukurabe geliza mala mukurabe gelidi Xoossa maxaafa nabbabanaas dendi eqqides.
LUK 4:17 Nabe Isayasa maxaafay izas imetin maxaafa doyida mala
LUK 4:18 “Goda ayyaanaany ta bollan dees, manqotas mishrachcho qaala yootana mala tana tiyides, qachchetidaytas birsheteth, qooqqeti xeellana oge ta awajjana mala, metotettidayta aashsha na mala, dossettida Goda laytha awajja ta yootana mala tana kiittides” giza so demmida nabbabidinne,
LUK 4:20 maxaafa gordidi mukurabe naagizayssas zaari immidi uttides. Mukuraben dizayti wurikka iza tishsh oothi xeellida.
LUK 4:21 Izikka istas “haysi inte inte haythara siiyida maxaafa qaalay hach poletides” gides.
LUK 4:22 Asay wurikka iza gish lo7o xallala haasa7eetes. Qassekka iza duunappe keziza lo7o qaalappe denddidaysani malalettidi haysi Yosefo na gidennee? gida.
LUK 4:23 Izikka dhale Godo nerka nena patha. Qifirnahomen neni oothishin nu siyidaysa hayssan ne katamankka ootha giza leemuso inte ta bolla malaatanayisas sidhey baa giidi istas yoottides.
LUK 4:24 Qassekka ta intes tuma gays nabey ba yellettida deren bonchetti erenna gides.
LUK 4:25 Gidoattin ta intes tuma gays heezu laythinne baga gakanas saloy gordettin wolqama koshay biitta bolla hannida Elassa wode he laythatan daro azinay bayndda maccassati Isra7eele biittan deettes shin Elassay istafe isineykoka kiitetibeyna. Gidoattin Sidona giza biittan Serappta geetettiza kataman diza issi azinay bayndda maccaseyko kiitettides.
LUK 4:27 Nabe Elsa7e wode Isra7eele deren daro inchiracho harggizayti deetes shin Sooriya biitta asa gidida Ni7imaneppe attin he darotappe oonikka inchiracho harggefe paxibeyyna.
LUK 4:28 Mukuraben dizayti wurikka hessa siiyidi daro hanqqettida.
LUK 4:29 Be utidasooppe dendi eqqidi Yesussa katamappe kare kessidi duge zaari yedanaas ista katamaya oothettida dhoqqa zuma xeera ekki efida.
LUK 4:30 Gido attin izi ista giddon shaakki yegidi aadhdhi biddes.
LUK 4:31 Heeppekka Galila awurajjan diza Qifirnahome geetettiza katama wodhides. Heenkka sanbbata gallas daro asa tamarso oykides.
LUK 4:32 Izi Godatethara haasa7iza gish iza timirttan malalettida.
LUK 4:33 Mukuraben tuna ayyaanaany oykida addey dees. Izikka ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi
LUK 4:34 “Naazirete Yesussa ha7i ta waano? Nenara tana aazze gathidee? Ne yiday nuna dhaysanasee? Ne oonnakkoone ta erays ne Xoossa xillo gidikii?” giidi wassides.
LUK 4:35 Yesussaykka tuna ayyaanaan ha addezappe co7u gaada keza giidi seerides tuna ayyaanaaykka daro asa sinthan addezza boollafe yegidi issi qohokka gathonta yedidi kezides.
LUK 4:36 Asay wurikka malalettidi ba garsan issay issara aso haysi ay giza timirttee? Godatetharane wolqara iita ayyaanaan azazes istikka kezeetes giidi haasa7ettida.
LUK 4:37 Yesussa lo7o nashoyka wursoso gakides.
LUK 4:38 Hessafe guye Yesussay mukurabeppe kezidi Simoona keeth gelides. Simoona bolottiya wolqama micha harggey oykin sakistada dishin Yesussa izo patharki giidi woossida.
LUK 4:39 Izika iziko shiiqqidi hokidi micha harggeza seerides. Micha harggeyka yedin heeraka denda eqqada imathata mokadus.
LUK 4:40 Away wulana gishin dumma dumma harggey oykida asa wursi izako ekki yida. Izikka hargiza asata wurso bolla ba kushe wothidi pathides.
LUK 4:41 Tuna ayyaanaanti qassekka Yesussa “neni Xoossa na” gishenne waasishe daro asatappe kezida, gido attin izi ista seerides, tuna ayyaanaanti izi kirstosa gididayssa eriza gish isti isinoka haasa7ana mala koybeyna.
LUK 4:42 Gadey woonitishn Yesussay issi poqqetha so biddes. Daro asaykka iza koyishe izi diza so gakides. Izi istafe shaakettidi bontta mala digganas koyida.
LUK 4:43 Gido attin istas gede hara katama baada Xoossa kawotetha mishrachcho qaala yootanas taas besses, tani kiitettida gita qofay hessa gides.
LUK 4:44 Izika Yihuda mukurabistan qaala guji yoottides.
LUK 5:1 Yesussay Gensereexxe abba lanqqen eqqidi Xoossa qaala tamaarisishin siiyiza asay iza kuni7isides.
LUK 5:2 He wode nam77u wogoloti abba achchan dishin Yesussay be7ides. mole oykizayti wogolotappe wodhdhidi mole gitista meeceetes.
LUK 5:3 Yesussay wogolotappe Simoona wogolon gelidi biittafe gede abba gido shishanna mala oychidinne wogolo giddon uttidi asa tamaarsides.
LUK 5:4 Tamaarsidi wursidape guye Simoona abbay ciimmatizaso shiiqqa mole oykanas inte giteza abba gido yegite gides.
LUK 5:5 Simoonay Yesussas zaaridi Godo qamma kumeth daaburi aqqiddi issinokka oykibeyko, gidoattin ne qaalan giteza yegana gides.
LUK 5:6 Yegida wode daro mole oykida. Giteyka daakettides.
LUK 5:7 Hara wogolon dizayti yiidi ista maaddana mala kushera wuti xeygida. Istika yiidi nam77u wogolota mole kunthida. Wogolotika duge miteteth oykida.
LUK 5:8 Simoona geettetiza Phexiroossay hessa beyidi Yesussa gulbate bolla kundidi Godo ta nagarancha gidida gish ta achchafe kichcha gides.
LUK 5:9 Izi hessa giday izine izara dizayti oykida daro molezan malalettida gishassa.
LUK 5:10 Qassekka Simoona laggeti zabidoosa nayti Yaqobeyne Yanisayka wuri malalettida. Yesussaykka Simoona babofa hayssafe guye ne asa oykizadde gidana gides.
LUK 5:11 Istika wogolota biittako shiishshidi wursikka yegi7agidi Yesussa kaallida.
LUK 5:12 Yesussay katamatappe issineyin dishin inchirachcha harggey bolla wursi oykida issi asi he kataman dees. He urayka Yesussa beyidi iza sinthan kundidi “Godo ne koyko tana pathana danda7asa” giidi woossides.
LUK 5:13 Yesussay ba kushe yedi bochchidi “ta dossadis paxa” gides. inchirachchay heeraka dhaydes.
LUK 5:14 Yesussay izas “hayssa oonaskka yootoppa, gido attin baada nena qeese halaqas bessa istas marka gidana mala ne geeyidayssas Musey azazida yarshoza shiishsha” giidi azazides.
LUK 5:15 Gido attin iza gish asay haasa7iza worey kaseppe aakki aakki biddes. Keehi daro asay iza haasa7a siyanasinne bena sakiza harggefe paxanas izako shiiqidees.
LUK 5:16 Yesussay daro wode asi bayndda poqqethaso biidi woossides.
LUK 5:17 Yesussay tamaarsishin asay Galilappenne Yihudappe qassekka Yerusalemeppe yida Farsawetinne woga tamaarisizayti heen uttida. Izi pathana mala Goda wolqay izara dees.
LUK 5:18 He wode asay issi kumetha bollay silidi qaaxonta harggancha zaphara tooki ekki yiidi keethe gelthidi Yesussa sinthan wothanas paacida.
LUK 5:19 Asa darotethafe dendidaysani keethe gelthanas xoonetida gish pude keeththa kaara bolla kezidinne kaara lukidi harggancha zaphara tooki ehidi asa giddora Yesussa sinthan wothida.
LUK 5:20 Yesussay ista amano beyidi hayso ne ne nagarappe maaristadasa gides.
LUK 5:21 Muse woga xaafizaytine Farsaweti haysi Xoossa bolla xallatethan hayssatho haasa7izay izi oonee? Issi Xoossafe attin nagara maaranaas ooni danda7ize giidi qoppida.
LUK 5:22 Yesussay ista qofa erida gish “inte inte wozinan ays hessaththo qoppeti?” gides.
LUK 5:23 Neni nagarappe maaristadasa gusafenne dendada ba gusafe awayssi kawishee?
LUK 5:24 Gido attin ta hayssa giday asa naas biitta bolla asa nagarappe maaranaas Godatethi dizaysa inte erana mala. Qassekka he sila ura “nena gays! eqqa dendada ne zapha tookada baa” gides.
LUK 5:25 Izi heeraka ista sinthan dendi eqqides. Kase ba zin7ida zapha tookidi Xoossa galatishe beso bides.
LUK 5:26 He wode asi wuri malalettides. Xoossa galatishe hach malalisizaz be7ides giidi daro babida.
LUK 5:27 Hessafe guye Yesussay heeppe kezi bides. Lewe giza issi qaraxa qanxisizaysi qaraxa qanxizason uttidaysa beyidi tana kaalla gides.
LUK 5:28 Izika wursi aggidi iza kaallides.
LUK 5:29 Leweyka Yesussassi ba keeththan gita diggisa diggisides. Qaraxa shiishiza daro asattinne hara asatikka istara issife maaddan uttida.
LUK 5:30 Farsawetinne ista Xaafeti qaraxa shiishshizaytarane nagaranchatara issife aazas meeti giidi Yesussa kaallizayta bolla zigirettida.
LUK 5:31 Yesussaykka istas hargganchatas attin paxa asas aakkime koshshenna gides.
LUK 5:32 Taka nagaranchata maaretethako zaranaas attin xillota xeyganas yabeykke gides.
LUK 5:33 Istika zaaridi Yanisa kaallizayti daro wode xoometesinne woosetes Farsawista kaallizaytikka izathokka oothetes. Nena kaallizayti gidikko wurso wode meettesinne uyettes gida.
LUK 5:34 Yesussaykka istas zaaridi mishray issife dishin diggissasi xeeysettidayta xoomisanaas bessizze? gides.
LUK 5:35 Gido attin mishray istafe shaakistana wodey yaana isti he wode xoomana.
LUK 5:36 Istas oorath mayoppe qanxi ekkidi gal77a mayo bolla wothi sikizaaddey deenna wothi sikkikko oorathazi gal77ara gaaggonta gish gal77aza daakkana gides.
LUK 5:37 Woyneppe othetida oorath cajje gal77a ogoron kunthidi wothiza asi oonikka baawa wothiza gidikko woyneppe oothettida ooratha cajjey gal77aza daakana. Woyne cajjezikka biittan gukkana gal7a ogoroy sinthafe go7ontaz gidana.
LUK 5:38 Hessa gish ooratha woyne ushy ooratha ogoron gujjistanas besses.
LUK 5:39 Histikko caalla woyne ush uyidaappe guye caalontazi uyana koyizay ooninne deenna gaasoyka caallay lo7o giza gish.
LUK 6:1 Issi sanbbata gallas Yesussay kaththa giddora aadhdhi bishin iza kaallizayti tiya xuphi ekkidi ba kushen shigechchi mishni,
LUK 6:2 Farsawistappe issi issi asati sanbbata gallas oothanas besoonttaysa ays oothetii? gida.
LUK 6:3 Yesussaykka istas Daawuttey izara diza asati gafida wode Daawutey oothidaysa nabbabibeyketii? giidi zaarides.
LUK 6:4 Izi Xoossa keeth gelidi qeeseti xalla maana mala azazettida dumma ukeetha bees miidi benara dizaytas immides.
LUK 6:5 Qassekka Yesussay asa nay sanbbata Goda giidi istas yoottides.
LUK 6:6 Yesussaykka hara sanbbata gallas mukurabe gelidi tamarisishin oshacha kushey silida issi assi heen dees.
LUK 6:7 Muse woga tamaarisizaytine Farsaweti Yesussa mootanas gaasso koyidi ane izi sanbbata gallassan addeza pathiko beyana giidi naagishe gam77ida.
LUK 6:8 Yesussaykka ista wozana qofa eridi kushey silida addeza wurso sinthan denda eqqa gides. addezzika dendi eqqides.
LUK 6:9 Yesussaykka ista ta intena issi miish ane oychchays sanbbata gallas oothanas bessizay lo7o ootho woykko iita oothoo? Shemppo asho woykko dhaysoo? giidi oychchides.
LUK 6:10 Qassekka Yesussay ba yuushon diza wursi yuushi xellidape guyyen addeza ne kushe piddisa gides. Addezzika Yesussay gida mala oothides. Iza kusheykka paxides.
LUK 6:11 Gido attin asati hanqettida, Yesussa bollankka ay oothanas koshizakonne ba giddon zorettida.
LUK 6:12 He gallassatappe issi gallas Yesussay woosanaas zuma bolla kezidi qamma kumeth Xoossa woosishe aqides.
LUK 6:13 Gadey wonitishin bena kaallizayta xeeygidi istafe tammanne nam77anta doorides. Istaka hawarista giidi sunthidees.
LUK 6:14 Istika Phexirosa giidi sunthida Simoonane iza isha Indirassa, Yaqobe, Yanisa, Pilphosa, Barttalemossa,
LUK 6:15 Matosa, Toomassa, Ilfiyosa na Yaqobe, ba deres olatana giigetiza Simoona,
LUK 6:16 Yaqobe na Yudane Yesussa aathi immida asqqoroto Yuda.
LUK 6:17 Yesussaykka istara issife zuma bollafe duge wodhdhidi denba son eqqides. Iza kaallizaytappe daro asay heen dees, Yihudappene Yerusalemeppe, qassekka Xirosappenne Sidona abba achchafe yida keehi daro asaykka heen dees.
LUK 6:18 Istika yiday Yesussay gizaysa siyanasinne harggefe paxannasa. tuna ayaanaykka wayssizayti wuri paxida.
LUK 6:19 Wolqqayka izappe kezidi darota pathiza gish asay wuri iza bochchannas yides. ufaysanne gaasota
LUK 6:20 Yesussaykka bena kaallizaytas hiz gides Xoossa kawotethay intes gidida gish inteno manqqoto inte anjettidayta,
LUK 6:21 Inte guyyeppe kaallanna gish ha7i gafizayto inte anjettidayta, inte guyyeppe miicana gish inteno ha7i yekkizayto inte anjettidayta,
LUK 6:22 asay ta gish intena ixxishin, ba giddofe shaakkishin, borishin intena iita sunthara xeygishn inte anjettidayta,
LUK 6:23 Intes salon gita woytoy diza gish he wode ufaysan guppite, ays giiko ista aawati nabeta bolla hessaththo oothida.
LUK 6:24 Gido attin inteno dureto inte ha7i ufa77ettida gish intena ayye,
LUK 6:25 inteno ha7i kalidayto intena ayye inte guyyeppe yeekkana, inte guyyeppe michistanasinne yeekkana gish inteno ha7i miicizayto intes ayye inte guyyepe yekana,
LUK 6:26 asi wuri inte gish lo7o haasa7iza wode intena ayye ana, ays giiko ista aawati wordo nabetas hessa mala oothida.
LUK 6:27 Gido attin ta yootizaysa siyizayto tani intes yootizay inte morketa siiqite, intena ixxizaytas lo7o oothite,
LUK 6:28 intena qanggizayta anjite, intena qohizaytas woosite,
LUK 6:29 issi shagalan baqqikko, nam77antho shagala gujja bessa, oonine ne bollara mayidaysa qaari ekkikko gaathara mayidaysakka diggofa.
LUK 6:30 Nena woosiza wursos imma, ne miishsha ekkida assi zars immana mala oychchofa.
LUK 6:31 asi intes oothanna mala inte koyizaysatho intekka hara asas oothite.
LUK 6:32 Nagaranchattikka bena siiqizayta siiqiza gish inte intena siiqizayta xalla siiqikko intes ay dumma anjjoy dizee?
LUK 6:33 Inte intes lo7o oothizaytas xalla lo7o oothikko intes ay dumma anjjoy dizee? Ays giikko nagaranchattikka hessaththo oothiza.
LUK 6:34 Tal7e ekkidi zaarana danda7etes gizaytas xalla inte tal7ikko inte hara ay dumma anjjo demmanee? Ays giiko nagaranchatika isti tal7idaysa sire zaaridi ekkanas nagaranchatas tal7etesi.
LUK 6:35 Gido attin Xoossi bena galatontaytasinne iitatas keeha gidida mala inte morketa siiqite, lo7o oothite, guyyepe zaaridi ekkanas qoponta dishe tal7e immite, hessanika intes kushe zaaroy gita gidana, qassekka inte woga Xoossa na gidana.
LUK 6:36 Inte aaway keha gidida mala intekka kiyata gidite.
LUK 6:37 Inte harata bolla pirdoppite inte bollakka pirdetena, inte bolla firday darontta mala harata bolla firda darssoppite, asas atto gite inteskka atto geetetana.
LUK 6:38 Immite inteskka imettana, intes inte makkida miishshan simmidi makkistana gish naaqi baqqettiddi, yigettidi, kumidi woran gukanashe lo7o makkiza miishshan makettidi inte ki7on idiman imistana.
LUK 6:39 Qassekka Yesussay istas leemuso hiz gidi yoottides “qooqqey qooqe kaalethanas danda7izee? kaalethikkokka nam77ati issay issara oykettidi ollan gelettennee?
LUK 6:40 Tamaarey bena tamaarisizaddeppe aadhdhenna, gido attin lo7ethi tamaarida asi wuri ba astaamare mala gides.
LUK 6:41 Ne ayfe giddon diza tuussa xeellonta dashe ne isha ayfe giddon diza buura ays xellayii?
LUK 6:42 Ne ayfen diza tuussa beyontta ne isha tani ne ayfen diza buura ane kessays gaanas wosta danda7ayii? Neno milatisizayso koyrotada ne ayfen diza tuussa kessa, hessafe guye ne isha ayfen diza buura kessanas lo7etha xeellandasa.”
LUK 6:43 Lo77o mithi iita ayfe ayfenna, qassekka iita mithi lo7o ayfe ayfenna.
LUK 6:44 Mithi wurikka ba ayfe ayfen ereetes, agunthafe balase geettetiza miththa ayfey maaxettenna, laadeppe woyne ayfey qanxxettenna.
LUK 6:45 Lo77o asi ba wezina kumida lo7o miish kesses, iita asikka ba wezina kumida iita miishshafe iita kesses, asi wurikka ba wezina kumi palahidaysa ba duunan hassa7ees.
LUK 6:46 Tani gizaysa oothekista shin ays tana “Godo Godo” geetii?
LUK 6:47 Taako yiidine ta qaala siyyidi polizay wuri oonna milatizakkonne ta intena bessana, keethe keexanas ziq oothi bookkiddi shuchcha bollan ba keeth keexida asa milates. Haro haathi yiidi he keeththa suggides, gido attin minni keexetida gish qaathanas dandd7ibeynna.
LUK 6:49 Gido attin ta qaala siiyidi polonta asi ba keeth lo77ethi bassonttanne garssan shuchcha yegontta keexida asa milates, haroykka keeththa sugin keethay heeraka kundidi iita lalethi laletides.
LUK 7:1 Yesussay hessa wursikka dere sinthan yooti wursidaysafe guye Qifirnahome gizaso bi gelides.
LUK 7:2 Heen Qifirnahomen xeetu wotaddarata halaqqay dees he addezas izi siiqiza ashkkaaraay harggidi hayqqos shemppo bolla dees.
LUK 7:3 Izikka Yesussa gish siiyidi ba ashkaara pathana mala Yesussa wooserkketi giidi issi issi Ayhudde bagga asatappe cimata Yesussakko yeddides.
LUK 7:4 Kiitettidi bida asati Yesussako yiidi hayssa ashkaara addeza gish ne pathana besses giidi minnithi woosida.
LUK 7:5 Ays giiko haysi addezi nu asa daro dosees, nuusikka mukurabe keexisiday iza.
LUK 7:6 Yesussayksa izistara bides. Yesussay addeza keethako matiza wode addezi ba laggeta Yesussakko yedidi “Godo ne ta keeth gelanaas beessenna taka nena ta keethe gelthanas bessiza asi gidonta gish haa yashe daaburoppa” gides.
LUK 7:7 Tani ne sinthan beettanas bessontta asa gidida gish neekko babbeykke, hessa gish neni heen daadda qaala xalla giiko ta ashkkaaray paxana.
LUK 7:8 taaskka tana azaziza asi tappe bollara dees. Tappe garssara tani azaziza wotaddarati deetes. Issa haaya giiko yes issa he ba giiko bees ashkkaaraykka hessa ootha giiko azazettidayssa oothes.
LUK 7:9 Yesussaykka ha addey gidayssa siiyidi addeza hanotethan malalettides. Guyye simmidi bena kaalliza deras ta intes gizay hayssa mala gita amano haray atoshin Isra7eele nayta garsankka demmabeykke gides.
LUK 7:10 Yesussakko kiitettida asati guye kiittida halaqqa so simmida wode ashkkaaray paxidaysa beydda.
LUK 7:11 hessafe guyyen Yesussay gam7ontadishe Nayne giza katama bena kaallizaytarane daro derera issife bides.
LUK 7:12 Izi biiddi katama geliza miixxa gakishin he katamayppe daro asay anha tooki ekkidi keziwodhdhides. Hayqqidays ba aayeys izi izaka. aayeyskka azinay baa, katamappe daro asay izira issife dees.
LUK 7:13 Godaykka izo beydda wode izis michettidi aykkoy baa yekofa gides.
LUK 7:14 Shiiqidine anha tookkida zapha bochchin anha tookidayti sit gi eqqida. Yesussaykka hayso nazo nena gays denda gides.
LUK 7:15 hayqqida naazikka suuri uttidi haasa7a oykkides. Yesussaykka naaza aayeys efi immides.
LUK 7:16 asay wurikka keehi babbiddi Xoossa galatishe “gita nabey nu giddofe dendidees, Xoossikka hayssa dereza yiidi be7ides” gides.
LUK 7:17 haysi Yesussa gish haasa7etiza lo7o haasa7ay kumetha Yihudanine Yihuda yushon diza deretan wurson kezides.
LUK 7:18 xamaqiza Yanisa kaallizaytikka hayssa wursi Yanisassi yoottida. Yanisaykka ista garsafe nam77anta xeeygidi,
LUK 7:19 izi yaana geetettidi haasa7etizays neneyee? hara ura naagino gi oychchite giidi Godakko yeddides.
LUK 7:20 bida asati Yesussakko gakkidi xamaqqiza Yanisay izi yaana geetettidi haasa7etizays neneyee hara ura naagino giidi neeko nuna yeddides gida.
LUK 7:21 he wode Yesussay daro asa waayepe harggefene tuna ayananatappe pathides. daro qooqqista ayfeykka xeellides.
LUK 7:22 Yanisay kiittin izakko yidayta biiddi inte inte ayfera beyddaysanne siiyidaysa Yanisassi yoottite. Ayfe qooqqeti xeelletesi toho wobeti suure hamuttetes inchirachcho harggizayti paxida tulleti siiyida hayqqidayti hayqqoppee dendida manqqotas mishrachcho qaalay yootettes.
LUK 7:23 Tanani dhuphetonta asi wurikka anjetidaysa gides.
LUK 7:24 Yanisay kiitida asati Yesussa achchafe bidaysafe guye Yesussay daro asas Yanisa gish hizggi yoottides “inte ay beyanas bazo kezidetii? carkoy heene hanne qathethiza shomboqo beyanassee?
LUK 7:25 ay beyanas kezidetii? lo7iza mayo mayida ura beyana kezidetii? lo7o mayo mayidi warix gizayti ishalo duusa dizayti kawo keeththan deetes.
LUK 7:26 histikko ay beyanas kezidetii? nabe beyanasee? Ee ta intes tuma gays inte keziday nabeppe aadhdhizadde beyanassa.
LUK 7:27 Xoossa qaalan <ne baanna oge nees baassi lo7ethanna kiitettida ura ta neppe sinthara yedana> geetettidi iza gish Xaafetidays izakko.
LUK 7:28 tani intes gizay maccasafe yellettida asa garsan Yanisappe aadhdhiza uray oonikka deenna, Xoossa kawotethan gidikko asa wursofe guuthu geetettida asi Yanisappe aadhdhanna.”
LUK 7:29 qaraxa shiishizayttikka attontta hayssa Yesussa qaala siyidayti wurikka Yanisa kushen xamaqqettidi Xoossassi bessiza boncho immida.
LUK 7:30 Farsawetinne Muse woga eranchati Yanisa kushen xamaqqetonta gish Xoossi izistas waana qofa oothidi shiishidaysa hiraysida.
LUK 7:31 qassekka Yesussay zaaridi histtikko ha7i yellista asa aazan leemusoo? isti ay milatizo? gides.
LUK 7:32 giyan uttidi ba garsan issay issara xeygettidi “intes nuni diith diixxidos shin duribeykkista zilalis zilalidosishin yekkibeykkista giza nayta milateetes gides.
LUK 7:33 ays giiko xamaqqiza Yanisay kath montanne woyneppe oothettida cajje uyonta yin dayiddanthi iza bolla dees gidista.
LUK 7:34 asa nay qasse miishshenne uyishe yin ganjamanne ushancha qaraxa shiishizaytarane nagaranchatara laggetees gidista.
LUK 7:35 hessa gish eratetha tumatethay izi nayta wursota achchan amanettides.
LUK 7:36 hessafe guye Farsawistappe issi uray Yesussa quma maanaas ba keethe xeygin Yesussay xeeyigida Farsawe keeththa biiddi uttides.
LUK 7:37 he kataman diza issi nagarancha maccash dizara Yesussay Farsawe keeththan quma maada bollan dizayssa siyada issi albbasxxirosse bilqqaxxe shitto ekka yadus.
LUK 7:38 yaadane Yesussappe guyyera iza toho achchan eqqada yekashenne ba afunthan iza toho caphisadda ba huu7e ithikera quccashenne yerashe shitto tiyadus.
LUK 7:39 Yesussa qumas xeeysida Farsaweykka hessa beyidi haysi addezi nabe gididakko hanna iza bochchida maccashiyaiza oonakkoone ay oothiza asakonne eranakko shin, iza nagaranchakko shin giidi ba wozinan qoppides.
LUK 7:40 Yesussaykka Simoona “nees ta yootanazi dees” gides. Simoonaykka tamaarisizayso ero yoota gides.
LUK 7:41 Yesussaykka zaaridi issi miishshe tal7e immizaddefe tal7e ekkida nam77u asati deetes, istafe issa bolla ichachu xeet dinnarey dees, nam77anthoza bolla ichachu tamu dinnarey dees.
LUK 7:42 istas qanxiza miishi dhayn tal7e immidaysi nam77anta acoza wursikka maarides. histtikko ha nam77antappe ha tal7e immidaysa darssi dosanay awayssee? gides.
LUK 7:43 Simoonaykka zaaridi “daro acoy maarettidaysa gaada qoppays” gides. Yesussaykka “tumu firdadassa” gides.
LUK 7:44 he maccashaykko yuuyiidi Simoona hano maccashiyo xeellay? ta ne keeth gelin ne ta tohos haathe shishabeykka shin iza gakides ta to ba afunthan caphisada ba huu7e ithikera quccadus.
LUK 7:45 neni aynne tana yerabeykkashin iza gakides ta gelosooppe oykkada ta toho yero aggabeykku.
LUK 7:46 ne ta huu7e zayite tiyabeykka shin iza gidikko ta toho shitto tiyadus.
LUK 7:47 hessa gish ta nena gizay iza tana keeha dosida gish iza ba daro nagarappe maaristadus, guuthara maaretiza ura siiqoykka guutha.
LUK 7:48 Yesussay maccashiyo ne nagarappe maaristadasa gides.
LUK 7:49 izara issife maaddan uttida imathatikka haysi nagara maarizay izi oonee? giidi ba wozinara qoppida.
LUK 7:50 Yesussaykka maccashiyo nena ne amanoy ashshides saron baa gides.
LUK 8:1 Hessafe guye Yesussay Xoossa kawotetha mishrachcho sabbakishe dumma dumma katamata giddorane dere gaathara aadhdhidees. Aadhdhidi biza wode iza kaalliza tammanne nam77ati izara deetes.
LUK 8:2 Qassekka tuna ayaanaappenne iita harggefe paxida issi issi maccashati izara deetes. Istika laappun tuna ayaanaany izippe kezida Magidele giza dereppe yida Maaramo,
LUK 8:3 kawo Herodosason oothiza kuza machcho Yohano qassekka Sosinonne hara daro maccashati deetes. Istika bees dizamiishshaara Yesussas oothizayta.
LUK 8:4 Daro derey issife shiiqidi dishin qassekka asay dumma dumma katamappe izakko wodhiza wode Yesussay leemusora tamaarisishe hizgides
LUK 8:5 issi goshshanchay zerethi zeranas kezides, zerishinkka bagazi ogen wodhin asa toon yedhettides, salo kafotikka yiidi maxi mida,
LUK 8:6 issi zerethay shuuchcha gadeni wodhidi heerakka caarides gadezzikka mela gade gidida gish elle meli kichchides.
LUK 8:7 Qassekka hara zerethi aguntha giddon wodhides agunthaykka izara issife diccidi caarechchaykka dicconta mala cuullides.
LUK 8:8 Qassekka hara zerethay lo7o aradda gadeni wodhides caaridda wodekka xeetu kushe ayfides. Yesussay haasa7a wursidi qaala dhoqqu histidi “siyiza haythi diza asi siyo” gides.
LUK 8:9 Yesussa kaallizayti zeretha leemusozas birsheth imma giidi oychchin,
LUK 8:10 izikka hizgiidi zarides Xoossa kawotetha xuura eroy intes imettides haratas gidikko leemusora yootays qassekka harati beyidi wozinan wothontamalanne siiyidi yuushi qopponta mala hannidees.
LUK 8:11 Zeretha leemusoykka hayssa, zeretha geettetidays Xoossa qaala,
LUK 8:12 oge lanqqen wodhidays qaala siyizayta giddo attin isti amanidi attontta mala xalla7ey yiidi qaala ista wozinappe eekkigidizayta.
LUK 8:13 Shuuchcha bolla wodhidaytikka qaala siiyidi ufaysara ekkizayta, istikka ha7is amanetes attin metoy ista bolla gakkiza wode xapho yedonta gish ellera amano kaddizayta.
LUK 8:14 Aguntha giddon wodhidayti qaala siiyizayta, heytikka aqqipey7iddi biitta bolla duussas qofaninne duretethan duusa lo7otethan culetidi lo7ethi ayfe imetena.
LUK 8:15 Aradda biittan wodhidays qaala suureninne lo7o wozinan siiyidi naaggizaytane danda7an minnidi ayfe ayfizzaytta.
LUK 8:16 Poo7o po7isidi baatha giddon woykko arssa garssan wothiza asi baawa, gido attin keethe geliza asas poo7ana mala qoncceson wothetees.
LUK 8:17 Qotettidi qoncce kezontay poo7o kezidi eretonta qotan attanna miishshi deenna.
LUK 8:18 Hessa gish inte siiyizaysa naageti siiyite, diza uras gujjistana baynddadees wursofe izas diza milatizarakka ekettakkichchanna.
LUK 8:19 Hessafe guye Yesussa aayanne ishati Yesussakko yida. Shin asa darotethafe denddidaysani izako shiiqqanas dandd7ibbeyitenna.
LUK 8:20 He wode asay Yesussas ne aayanne ne ishati nena beyanas koyidi karen eqqida giidi yoottidees.
LUK 8:21 Yesussaykka zaaridi ta aayanne ta ishati Xoossa qaala siiyidi naagizayta gides.
LUK 8:22 Issi gallas Yesussay bena kaallizaytara wogolo giiddo gelidi abbafe he pinith pinnos gides.
LUK 8:23 Istika pinishin abba bolla gote carkkoy dendidi waayssiza wode Yesussay dhiskkides. Haathayka wogoloza giddo gelin asay daro metotettides.
