LUK 8:24 Yesussa kaallizayti izakko shiiqqidi “Godo, Godo nu wurana hanos” giidi Yesussa dhiskofe denthida. Izikka beeggiddi carkozane abba danbbala seerin carkoyne abba danbbalay coo77u gides.
LUK 8:25 Izika bena kaallizayta inte amanoy awa bidde gides. Istika ba garssan babishshenne malaletishe carkonne haathenne azazizay, isttikka izas azazettizay izi oonee gida.
LUK 8:26 Izappe guye Galilape he pinithan diza Gergesenonne giza dere wogolora pinida.
LUK 8:27 Yesussay wogolozappe gadeni wodhida wode dayiddanthi iza bolla diza issi asi katamappe kezidi iza demmides, he uray daro wode mayo mayonta kallo keeththan aqontta duufo bees aqoso oothida asa.
LUK 8:28 Yesussa beydda wode wassishe Yesussa sinthan kunddides, qaala dhoqqu histidi “boncho Xoossa na Yesussa taasnne nees ay gaytotethi dizee? Ne tana waaysonta mala nena woosays” gides.
LUK 8:29 Tuna ayaanaay hessa gaanas danda7iday addezappe kezana mala Yesussay azazida gishassa. Tuna ayaanaanazikka woden woden denddiza gish addezzi sanithalataninne birattan toho qachi naaginkka qachettida sanithalata duuthethidi iza bolla diza dayiiddanthay iza duge bazo zaari efees.
LUK 8:30 Yesussay ne sunthi oonee giidi oychchides, izikka daro dayiiddanthati iza bolla gelidi diza gish ta sunthi “leegoone” gides.
LUK 8:31 Dayiiddanthatika wursethi baayndda cima oilan bena yegonta mala minnthidi woossida.
LUK 8:32 Henka zuma bolla daro gudunthi heemetes, dayiiddanthatakka gudduntha wudezan gelite giidi azazana mala woossida, Yesussaykka ero gides.
LUK 8:33 Dayiiddanthatika addezappe kezidi guddunthatan gelida, guddunthatikka aafozza dugunthara bichcharishshe biiddi abban gelidi abban mitettida.
LUK 8:34 Heemizayti handdaysa beydda wode beezhumi biiddi katama asasne dere asas yoottida.
LUK 8:35 Handdayssa beyana giidi asay ba dizasooppe Yesussakko yides, dayiiddanthay izappe kezida addezzika wozinay kanay simmini afala mayidi Yesussa toho garsan utidaysa beyidi babida.
LUK 8:36 Dayiiddanthan oyketida addezzi paxishin beyddayti izi waani paxidakkonne derezas yootida.
LUK 8:37 Gergesenonne matan diza asay keehi babbda gish Yesussa hayssafe kichch giidi woossida, izikka wogolozan gelidi simmi bides.
LUK 8:38 Dayiiddanthay izappe kezida addezzi Yesussara issife daanna mala woossides,
LUK 8:39 Gido attin ne so simadda Xoossi nees oothida gita miish yoota giidi moyzides. Addezzikka Yesussay izas oothida gita miish ba kataman diza asas wursos qonccen yootishe biddees. Ya7irosa naanne Yesussa mayo bochchidda maccassa
LUK 8:40 Assay wuri Yesussa yuusa naagishe gam77ida gish izi simmishni ufaysan mokki ekkida.
LUK 8:41 He wode Iya7irossa geetettiza mukurabe halaqqay yiidi Yesussa toho bolla kundidi Yesussa iza so baanna mala woossides.
LUK 8:42 Izi hessaththo oychchiday izas tammanne nam77u laytha kumida issi macca nay sakistada shemppo bolla diza gish. Izi he buussan dishin derey daridi ba garsan sugetidi iza keehi un7isides.
LUK 8:43 Tammanne nam77u laythi suuthi izippe gukishin diza issi maccashiya bees diza miishsha ubbaa dhale eriza asatas imma wursini izo pathanaas danda7ida uraykka isoykka baa.
LUK 8:44 Izakka guyyera shiiqqada Yesussa afala maccarata bochchadus, gukkiza
LUK 8:45 Yesussaykka “tana bochchidday oone?” gides. Wurika nuni bochchibeykko gi kadida wode phixrossay zaaridi Godo asi wuri yuuyi aadhdhidi nena suggerethidi un7ises gides.
LUK 8:46 Gido attin Yesussay asi tana bochchides, wolqay tappe kezidaysa ta erays gides.
LUK 8:47 Maccashiya eretonta qotistada baannaas danda7ontaysa erida wode kokorashe yaada Yesussa sinthan kunddadus. Izakka Yesussa waana bochchidakkonne qassekka ellera waana paxidakko wurso asa sinthan yootadus.
LUK 8:48 Izikka ta nayee ne amanoy nena pathides, saron ba gides.
LUK 8:49 Yesussay buro maccasheys haasa7a bolla dishin mukurabe halaqqa Iya7irosa keethafe issi asi Iya7irosas ne naya hayqqadus hessa gish hayssappe guye astamaareza mela daabursofa gides.
LUK 8:50 Yesussay hessa siiyidi Iya7irosa aykkoy ba baboofa amanna attin ne naya paxana gides.
LUK 8:51 Yesussay Iya7irosa keeth geliza wode Phexirosa, Yanisane Yaqobe qassekka nay aawappenne aayeyippe attin haray oonikka izara gelana mala koybeyna.
LUK 8:52 He wode asay wuri nayis wuwu gi wassi yekkishin Yesussay yeekofite iza zin77adus attin hayqqabeykku gides.
LUK 8:53 Asaykka naya hayqqidaysa eriza gish Yesussa bolla miicides.
LUK 8:54 Gido attin izi nay kushe oykkidi ta nayee denda gides.
LUK 8:55 Nayis shempoyka simmides. Heerakka denda eqqadus, Yesussaykka izis miza miish immana mala azazides.
LUK 8:56 Nka yelidaytika malaletida. Gido attin izi handdayssa oonaaskka yotonta mala azaziddes.
LUK 9:1 Yesussaykka tammanne nam77u hawarista issife xeeygidi dayiddanthata kessana malane harggefe pathana mala istas wolqanne Godatethi immides:
LUK 9:2 qassekka Xoossa kawotetha yootanasinne harggizayta pathanas ista kiittidees.
LUK 9:3 istaskka “oge bishe guufe woykko, qaraxite woykko, quma woykko miishshe woykko nam77u mayo aykkokka oykki baannas koshshenna.” gides.
LUK 9:4 intekka he katamayppe kezana gakanas koyro gelida oona keeththanka gidin heen gam7ite.
LUK 9:5 katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixxikko he katamayppe kezidi intena mokkontaytas markka gidana mala inte tohon diza gudula pittidi kezite gides.
LUK 9:6 istikka Goday gida mala kezidi miishrachcho qaala yootishene hargganchata pathishe dere wurson guttappe gutta yuuyiida.
LUK 9:7 he wode issi issi asati Yanisay hayqqoppe denddides, baggati Elasay kezidi beettides, qasse bagati beni nabetappe issay hayqqoppe dendidees giidi haasa7etiza gish Yuda biitta haariza Herdoossay hessa siyidi hanza miishshan ba wozinan metotettides.
LUK 9:9 Herdoossaykka tani iza qoodhe qanxida xamaqiza Yanisay hayqqides, histin iza gish hayssa mala haasa7etishn ta siyizays izi oonee? giidi iza ba ayfera beyana koydees.
LUK 9:10 hawarettikka simmidi isti oothidaysa wursi Yesussassi yoottida. izikka ista xalla benara ekkidi Beettesaydda geetettiza poqqethan diza katama bides.
LUK 9:11 gido attin daro asay hessa eridi ista kaallides. izikka ista mokki ekkidi Xoossa kawotetha gish yoottides. qassekka harggefe pathanas bessizayta pathides.
LUK 9:12 gadey lem7ishin tamman nam77u hawareti izakko shiiqqidi “nuni dizay baazo biittan gidida gish asay biiddi bees aqana sonne miza miish koyana mala asa moyiza” gida.
LUK 9:13 gido attin izi istas zaaridi “mizaz inte istas immite” gides. istikka nuus ichachu ukeethafenne nam77u moleppe haray ba. ha asas gidiza kath koshikko shamanas besses gida.
LUK 9:14 Yesussaykka bena kaallizayta “asa ichachu tamu ichachu tamu histi shaakki shaakki utisite” gides. heenkka ichachu shi gidana attumma asay dees.
LUK 9:15 Yesussa kaallizaytika Yesussay azazida mala asa wursi utisida.
LUK 9:16 Yesussaykka ichachu ukeeththanne nam77u molista oykidi pude salo xeellidi Xoossa galatides. izikka ukeetha menithidi asa gathana mala bena kaallizaytas immides.
LUK 9:17 asay wurikka miidi kaallides. Yesussa kaallizaytika asappe atidda tammanne nam77u masobe kumeth maaddafe denthida.
LUK 9:18 issi gallas Yesussay berkka woossishin iza kaallizayti izara deetes. izikka ista “asay tana oona gizee?” giidi oychchides.
LUK 9:19 istikka izas “issi issi asay xamaqqiza Yanisa bagayti Elasa harati qasse beni nabetappe issay hayqoppe denddidees geetes” gida.
LUK 9:20 izikka ista “intech tana oona geetii?” giidi oychchides. Phexirosaykka “neni Xoossafe kiittetida kirstoosa” giidi zaaridees.
LUK 9:21 Yesussaykka ista hayssa oonaskka yootoppite giidi minnithi yoottidi
LUK 9:22 qassekka asa nay daro waayye ekkanas besses, dere cimatan qeese halaqqataninne Muse woga xaafizaytan ixistanane ista kushen hayqqanasinne hezantho gallassan hayqqpope dendana gides.
LUK 9:23 qassekka wursosi “ba shemppo ashshana giza asi wuri dhaysana, shin ba shempota gish giidi dhaysiza asi ashshana. hessa gish tana kaalana koyiza asi diikko bena kaddo, wurso gallas ba masqqale tookkidi tana kaalo” gides.
LUK 9:25 asi alame mule wodhisidi ba shemppo dhaysiko aaza go7ay dizee?
LUK 9:26 oonikka tananinne ta qaalan yeelatikko asa nay ba bonchora, aawa bonchoranne geeshsha kiitanchata bonchora yiza wode tani izan yeelatana.
LUK 9:27 ta intes tumu gays hayssan eqqida asappe hayqqanappe sinthan Xoossa kawotethi beyana bagga asati deetes.
LUK 9:28 Yesussay hessa gida osppun gallassa malappe guye woossanas zuma bolla kezides. bishe benara Phexirosa, Yanisanne Yaqobe ekki bides.
LUK 9:29 izi woosishin iza ayfesoy lametides. iza medhaykka wolqantha mala xoliqidi booxxidees.
LUK 9:30 nam77u asati Museynne Elasay izara haasa7ettida.
LUK 9:31 istikka bonchora qonccidi Yerusalemeni polistana diza Yesussa hayqqo gish haasa7ettida.
LUK 9:32 Phexirosane izara dizayta deexo dhiskkoy oykkides. istikka dhiskofe beeggidi Yesussa bonchonne nam77u asi izara eqqidayta beydda.
LUK 9:33 he nam77u asati Yesussappe shaakketi bishin Phexirosay Yesussa “Godo issi daasse nees, issi daasse Muses issi daasse Elasas oothidi haan dizaakko nuus lo7oshin” gides. gido attin Phexirosay ba gizaysa eronta gides.
LUK 9:34 izi hessa haasa7ishin shaaray yiidi ista genthides. shaara giddo gelidi babida.
LUK 9:35 shaara giddofekka “tani doorida nay hayssa iza siyite” giza qaalay setettides.
LUK 9:36 qaalay setettida wode Yesussay xalla beettides. Yesussa kaallizayttikka hanidda miishsha wursi ba wozinan oykkida attin oonaaskka yoottibeyitena.
LUK 9:37 wontetha gallas isti zuma bolla wodhin daro asay yiidi Yesussara gaagidees.
LUK 9:38 he wode asa giddofe issi uray qaala dhoqqu histidi “tamaarisizayso taas issi nay xalla diza gish iza ne xeellana mala ta nena woosays.
LUK 9:39 iza iita ayaanaay oykishin haasa7ay bayndda wasses, qakketishe duunara goppontto kesses, qoho gathidappe guye daro waayisdi agges.
LUK 9:40 nena kaallizayti nazappe kessana mala ista ta woosadisi, gido attin kessana dandda7ibeyitenna” gides.
LUK 9:41 Yesussaykka istas zaaridi “amanontta ha wode wobe asato tani intenara aydde gakkanaas daanee? intenakka aydde gakanas dandda7anee? naaza ane ha eha!” gides.
LUK 9:42 naazi yishin iita ayaanaay iza boollafe yegin qakkettides. Yesussaykka iita ayaanan seeridi naaza pathidi naaza aawas immides.
LUK 9:43 asaykka wuri Xoossa gitatethan malaletides. izi oothidaysan asay wuri malaletishn Yesussay bena kaallizayta
LUK 9:44 “asa nay asa kushen aadhdhidi imistana, intekka ha yoza baloppitte” gides.
LUK 9:45 gido attin izi gizaysi istas gelibeyna. ays giiko isti akekkontta mala yozi istafe geemettides, zaaridikka oychchonta mala babida.
LUK 9:46 iza kaallizayti ooni oonappe aadhizakkone ba garsan palametida.
LUK 9:47 Yesussaykka ista wozina qofa eridi guutha na ekki yiidi ba matan esidi
LUK 9:48 “ha guutha na ta sunthan ekkizaddey oonikka diikko tana ekkees, tana ekkizaddeyka tana kiitiddaysa ekkees. inte wursofe guutha uray izi wursofe aadhdhes” gides.
LUK 9:49 Yanisaykka “Godo issi uray ne sunthan dayiddanth kesishin beydos. gido attin izi nunara kaalonta gish digganas koydos” gides.
LUK 9:50 “intena ixonta asi wuri inte baga gidida gish diggopite” gides.
LUK 9:51 Yesussay salo biza wodey matida gish Yerusaleme baanas denddidees.
LUK 9:52 izikka sinthethidi ase kiittides. istikka koshiza miish giigissanappe kasetidi Samarya biittan diza issi guta bida.
LUK 9:53 gido attin derey izi Yerusaleme bizayssa erida gish mokki ekkibeyitenna.
LUK 9:54 iza kaallizaytappe Yaqobeyne Yanisay hanzaysa beyidi “Godo Elasay oothoysatho tamay saloppe wodhidi ista dhayso” giidi azazana mala koyay? gida.
LUK 9:55 gido attin Yesussay istakko yuuyiidi “intes ay mala ayaanaay dizakkon erekketii? asa nay yiday asa shemppo ashshanas attin dhaysanas gideenna” giidi ista seerides.
LUK 9:56 isti wurikka hara guta bida.
LUK 9:57 istikka birshin issi asi istakko shiiqidi “tani neni biza wursoso nena ta kaalana” gides.
LUK 9:58 Yesussaykka “worikenatas aqqizza olay, kafotas qasse aqqizza kafo keethi dees gido attin asa nas ba hu7e ayssiza soykka baawa” gides.
LUK 9:59 Yesussaykka hinkoysa “tana kaala” gides. he uraykka “Godo ta kasista baada ta aawa moogoo?” gides.
LUK 9:60 Yesussaykka “aggagga hayqidayti hayqidayta moogetto, neni gidikko baada Xoossa kawotethaa asas yoota” gides.
LUK 9:61 qassekka hara uray “Godo ta nena kaalana shin koyro so baada ta keeththa asa saro gaada yoo?” gides.
LUK 9:62 gido attin Yesussay “boora kaso oykkidi goyishe guye zaari xellizaddey oonikka Xoossa kawotethas beesena” gides.
LUK 10:1 Hessafe guye Goday hara laappun tammanne nam77u asa dooridi sunthidees. Istaka nam77u nam77u histtidi izi baanna sootane katamata wursika izeti kasettidi baanamala kiittides.
LUK 10:2 Maxa gakkida kaththay daro kaththa maxi shiishizayti guuthata hessagish kaththa Goday kaththa maxxidi shiishizayta kaththay dizaso yeddanamala woosite gides.
LUK 10:3 Hessa gish biite dorssati sudhume giddora biza mala ta intena yedays.
LUK 10:4 Korojo woykko qaraxite woykko caamma ekkofite, oge bolla oonakka saro gooppite.
LUK 10:5 Oona keethekka geliza gidikko koyrotidi “keeththa aso saro” giite.
LUK 10:6 He keeththan saro dosiza asi diikko inte sarotay hekeeththan shemppana, saro dosiza asi donta agikko inte sarotay intes simana.
LUK 10:7 Intes maana shiishida kath wursi miishshenne uyishe he inte gelida keeththan utite, oothiza uras ba woliqa wagga ekkanas izas besses. Ha keethafe he keeth yuuyoppite.
LUK 10:8 Inte ay katamakka gakkiza wode asay intena mokki ekkiko isti intes aathida quma miite.
LUK 10:9 He kataman diza hargganchata pathidi Xoossa kawotethi intekko matides giidi yoottite.
LUK 10:10 Gido attin inte biiddi issi katama gelishin he katama asay intena mokki ekkonta ixxikko he katama asay shiiqiza dubbusha kezidi
LUK 10:11 “nu to bolla diza inte katama gudula intes marka gidanamala nu toho boollafe pittos shin Xoossa kawotethay intekko matidaysa erite” giite.
LUK 10:12 Ta intes yootays firda gallas he katama firdappe Soddome katama firday shaykko gidana.
LUK 10:13 Kurazine nena ayye, Beette sayida nena ayye intenan oothetida malaatati Xirosaninne Sidonani oothetidakko istikka mayo mayidinne biiddinith gorppettidi he wode beni maaristanashin.
LUK 10:14 Gido attin firda wode intefe Xirosasinne Sidonaas shaykkana.
LUK 10:15 Hanne Qifirnahome pude salo dhoqqu dhoqqu gadii? Neni duge si7ole wodhana,
LUK 10:16 Inte gizaa siiyiza uray tana siiyes intena ekkonta uray tanakka eekkenna tana ekkontaykka tana kiitidayssa eekkenna.
LUK 10:17 Laappun tammanne nam77atikka ufa7etishe simmidi “Godo haray atoshin dayiddanthatikka ne sunthan nuus haaretida” giidi yootida.
LUK 10:18 Izika istas “xalla7ey wolqantha mala saloppe kundishin ta beyadis” gides.
LUK 10:19 Histikko shooshshanne masmasonne inte yedhana mala morkke woliqqa wurso bolla intes Godatethi immadis intena qohiza issi miishshkka deenna.
LUK 10:20 Inte sunthay salon Xafetida gish ufa7etite attin tuna ayaanaanti intes haaretida gish ufa7etofite
LUK 10:21 He wode Yesussay Xillo Ayaanaan ufa7etidi hizgides “salos biittas Goda gidida aabbo hayssa wursaka cincatappenne eratappe qotada guutha duudde naytas ne qonccisida gish tani nena galatays Ee aabbo haysi ne lo7o sheney hanidees.
LUK 10:22 Wuri ta aawa matappe taas imetides qassekka iza nay oonakkoone aawappe attin eriza uray baawa aaway oonakoone naazappe attin woykko naazi izas qonccisanas dosida urappe attin eriza uray baa”
LUK 10:23 Bena kaallizaytakko simmidi istas dumma “inte beyizzaysa beyiza ayfeti anjjettidayta.
LUK 10:24 Ta intes tuma gays daro nabetinne kawoti inte ha7i beyizzaysa beyanas koyidi beybeyttenna inte ha7i siiyizaysaka siiyanaas koyidi siybeyitenna.”
LUK 10:25 Issi gallas Muse woga tamaarisiza issi uray Yesussa paacanaas koyidi “tamaarisizayso tani medhina deyo laattanas ay oothoo?” gidi oychchides.
LUK 10:26 Yesussaykka zaaridi woga maxaafan ay geeteti Xafettidee? izape nees geliday aazee? giidi oychchides.
LUK 10:27 Uray zaaridi “ne Godaa Xoossa ne kumetha wozinappe, ne kumetha shemppofe, ne kumetha woliqqafene, ne kumetha qofappe siiqa, ne laggekka ne hu7e mala siiqa gees” giidi zaarides.
LUK 10:28 Yesussaykka lo7o zaaradasa nenikka hinnidan oothikko medhina deyo demmna gides.
LUK 10:29 Uray bena xilisanaas koyidi “histini ta laggey oonee?” giidi Yesussa oychchides
LUK 10:30 Yesussaykka zaaridi issi uray Yerusalemeppe Iyarko wodhishin panggati demmida iza mayo qaari ekkida, keehi qoxerethidi hayqqoppenne paxappe giddon yeggi aggi bida.
LUK 10:31 Issi qeesey he ogera bees duge wodhishe aamunthontta he qoxettida ura demmida pooqethara yegi aadhdhidees.
LUK 10:32 Qassekka issi Lewe baga asappe issi uray he ogera aadhdhishe qoxettida ura beyidi ha7ikka pooqidi aadhdhidees.
LUK 10:33 Issi Samaarya biitta asi he ogera aadhdhi bishe qoxettida ura bolla gakki wodhides, ura beyidinne keehi michchetides.
LUK 10:34 Urako shiiqidine maduntha dhaallana mala woyra zayitene woyneppe cajje maduntha bolla gusidi qachchides, ura ba hare togisidi imathi shemppizaso efidi lo7ethi xellides.
LUK 10:35 Wontetha gallas imathi shemppiza keeththa Godas nam77u dinnare immidinne nena hara miishsha kessisikko ta simashe nees immana neppe kessada lo7etha naaga gides.
LUK 10:36 Histiko ha heezu asatappe pangatan qoxetidi hayqqoppenne paxappe giddon yegettida uras keehi mata laggey nees awayssa milatizee?
LUK 10:37 Muse woga tamaarisizayskka michettidaysako! gides. Yesussaykka izas nekka baada izaysatho ootha gides.
LUK 10:38 Yesussayne iza kaallizayti oge bishin Yesussay issi guta gelides, Marta geetettiza issi maccashiya ba son Yesussa moka ekkadus.
LUK 10:39 Izis Maaramo geetettiza issi michchiya daysu. Maaramakka izappe qaala siyashe Goda toho garsan uttadus.
LUK 10:40 Shin martay ootho daroppe dendidaysani daaburada Yesussako shiiqqada “Godo ta michchiya ootho ubbaa ta bolla agadda utishin neni co7u gaz? Iza tana maaddana mala izis yoota attin” gadus.
LUK 10:41 Gido attin Goday hizgidi izis zaarides “Martanne Martanne neni daro yoho gish qofa darassa, dirbatasa tugatassa.
LUK 10:42 Koshizay gidikko issi miish xalla, Maaramaka lo7o exa dooradus, hessikka izippe ekettenna.”
LUK 11:1 Issi gallas Yesussay issi son woossides, woossa wursishin iza kaallizaytappe issay Godo xamaqiza Yanisay bena kaallizayta woossa tamaarsidaysatho nekka nuna woossa tamaarsa gides.
LUK 11:2 Izikka istas woosishe hizgidi woosite nu aawo ne sunthi anjjetto ne kawotethi haayo.
LUK 11:3 Hachsi gidiza quma nuus imma.
LUK 11:4 Nuna qohidayta nu maariza mala nuna maara paacenkka nuna gelthofa
LUK 11:5 Qassekka hiz gides “intefe issi uras laggey diikko giidi giddoth he laggezaso biiddi taas issi imathi ogeppe yin muzana kath bayndda gish heezzu buddennay diikko taas tal7arikii?” gides.
LUK 11:7 Laggezikka zaaridi tana waysoppa, kareyykka gordettides, tanikka naytara zin7akichadis ha7i denddada immanas danda7ikke gaandee?
LUK 11:8 Taka intes yootays laggetetha gish dendidi immonta agikkokka izi oychchon salethida gish denddidi koyizaysa wursi immides.
LUK 11:9 Hessa gish tani intes gizay woosite intes imistana, koyite inte demmna, kare qoxxite intes doyettana.
LUK 11:10 Ays giiko woosizay wuri ekkana, koyizayka demmna kare qoxxizadeska doyettana.
LUK 11:11 Intefe aawa gidi uttidi izi yelida nay mole oychchiko shooshu immizay daandee?
LUK 11:12 Woyko phuuphuule oychchiko masmaso immizay daandee?
LUK 11:13 Inte iitata gidishe inte naytas lo7o imota imo erikko salon diza inte aaway bena woosizaytaas Xillo Ayaanaan wosit darisi immennee?
LUK 11:14 Issi gallas Yesussay haasa7isonta mume dayiddanth kessides. dayiddanthazikka kezidappe guye duuna mume addezzi haasa7ides, beydda asatikka darsi malalettida.
LUK 11:15 Gido attin issi issi asati bi7eela zebula geetettiza dayiddanthata halaqan dayiddanthata kesses gida.
LUK 11:16 Issi issi asay iza paacanaas saloppe malaata bessa gidi oychchida.
LUK 11:17 Gido attin Yesussay ista qofa eridi hiz gides “ba garsan shaaketiza kawotethi wuri dhayanan, ba giddon sigay bayndda keethikka kundanna.
LUK 11:18 Inte tana bi7eel zubula dayiddanthata kesses giidi haasi7ista shin xalla7eykka ba giddon issay issafe shaaketikko iza kawotethi waani minnannee?
LUK 11:19 Histtikko tani dayiddanthata bi7eel zubula kessiko inte nayti oonani kesaneeshaa? Hessa gish inte nayti inte bolla firdizayta gidana.
LUK 11:20 Gido attin tani dayiddanthata kessizay Xoossa wolqan gakkides Xoossa kawotethay inteko matidaro erite.
LUK 11:21 Mino uray lo7ethi gixettidi ba keeth naagikko keeththan diza miishshi lo7oon naagetes.
LUK 11:22 Gido attin izappe hara mino uray yiidi xoonikko izi amanettidda ola massara wothi ekkidi izas diza haarozakka wursi haras gishanna.
LUK 11:23 Tanara gidontay tanara eqettes, tanarakka shiishshonta uray laalles,
LUK 11:24 Tuna ayaanaay asappe kezida wode shemppo koyishe haathi bayndda mela son wayetesi, shempo soy dhaykko tani kase kezidaso guye simana gees.
LUK 11:25 Izappe simmidi yishin kase izi aggi bida keethay pitettidinne giigi utidaysa demmes.
LUK 11:26 Hessafe simmidi biiddi izappe iitiza hara laappun dayiddanthata benara ekkidi yes, istikka gelidi heen dana, he uraskka koyroysafe guyyeys keehi iita gidana.”
LUK 11:27 Yesussay hessa haasa7iza wode asa giddofe issi maccash dizara ba qaala dhoqqu oothada nena tookkida qanthinne ne dhammida dhanthati anjjettidayta gadus.
LUK 11:28 Gido attin izi anjjettidayti Xoossa qaala siiyidi azazettizayta gides.
LUK 11:29 Daro derey Yesussako shiiqida wode Yesussay hizgides “haysi ha yellistay iita yellista, gita malaata beyana koyees. Gido attin Yoonassa malaatappe hara dumma malaatay imetenna.
LUK 11:30 Gaassoyka Yoonassay Nanawe asas malaata gidida mala asa nay tani ha yellistaas malaata gidana.
LUK 11:31 Duge baga dere macca kawoya Solomone erateth beyanas biitta gaxappe denddada yida gish pirda wode iza ha yellistara denddada pirdana heko Solomoneppe aadhdhizaddey han dees.
LUK 11:32 Yoonassay sabbakishin siiyidi Nanawe asay ba naggarappe maaretethan gelida gish ha yellistara issife dendidi pirdana.
LUK 11:33 Xomppe oythidi kareppe geliza asas poo7ana mala qoncceson wothetes attin geemason wothiza asi deenna.
LUK 11:34 Ne asatetha poo7oy ne ayfe ne ayfey paxa gidiko ne kumetha asatethay poo7o gidana ne ayfey sakettikko ne kumetha asatethay dhuma gidana.
LUK 11:35 Hessa gish nenan diza poo7oy dhumonta mala naageista.
LUK 11:36 Histikko ne asatethay poo7o gidikko dhumida asatethi deenna agikko ne kumetha asatethay xomppe lo7ethi po7iza mala lo7i beettanna.
LUK 11:37 Yesussay haasa7a wursida mala issi parsawey benara quma maanaas Yesussa xeygides.
LUK 11:38 Yesussay quma maana kushe mecetonta agiddayssa beyidi malalettida.
LUK 11:39 Goday izas hizgides ha7i inte parsaweti xu7asinne keres bollabbagga meeci geeshista inte garssa bagaz uuzetethaninne iitatethan kumides.
LUK 11:40 Inteno eeyato kare baga medhdhiday garssa baga medhibeynee?
LUK 11:41 Yohon gidiko giddon dizaysa muxaata immite he wode wurikka intes geesh gidana.
LUK 11:42 Inteno Farsaweto intes ayye anugappenne xalotappe qassekka dumma dumma kaththafe tamappe isino kessista. Gido attin tuma firdane Xoossa dosanaysa aggi aadhdheetta. Yohon gidiko inte aggi aadhdhannas beesena. Hankoysa aggonta inte oothanna bessizayttikka haayta.
LUK 11:43 Inteno Farsaweto intes ayye mukuraben uttana boncho oydde koyyista giya giddonka asay inte sinthan hokana mala doseista.
LUK 11:44 Asi eronta iza bollara biza qoteti diza duufo inte milatiza gish intena ayye.
LUK 11:45 Muse woga erizaytappe issay zaaridi tamarisizayso ne hessaththo haasa7iza wode nunaka cayaassa gides.
LUK 11:46 Yesussaykka zaaridi inteno Muse woga erizayto inteskka ayye asi tookanaas dandda7onta deexo toho asa toosista inte gidikko intes biradhdhe xeeranika bochchekkista.
LUK 11:47 Inte aawati wodhida nabeta duufo inte lo7ethiza gish intes ayye.
LUK 11:48 Histtikko inte inte aawata ootho minnithiza markata istinabista wodhida intekka ista duufo lo7etheista.
LUK 11:49 Hessa gish Xoossa erateth hizgadus nabetanne hawarista ta istas yeddana isttikka istafe issa issa wodhana haratakka gooddanna.
LUK 11:50 Hessa gish ha yellistay biittay medhetosooppe ha7i gakkanaas gukida nabeta wurso suutha gish oychistana.
LUK 11:51 Aabelle suuthafe oykkidi yarshiza sooppene Xoossa keeththa giddon gukida Zakarasa suutha gakkanaas koyetes Ee ta intes gizay ha yellistay hayssas oychchistana.
LUK 11:52 Inteno woga erizayto intena ayye eratetha qulfe wolqara wothi ekkidi inteskka gelibeykista gelanaytaka digeista.
LUK 11:53 Yesussay heeppe kezidappe guye Xafetinne Farsaweti eqettishe oychchan shemppo diggida.
LUK 11:54 Iza duunappe keziza qaalan iza qaxi oykkanas naagettida.
LUK 12:1 He wode daro derey ba giddon issay issara yedhistana gakanas shiiqi uttidashe Yesussay bena kaallizayta “Farsawista irshofe naagettite, hessikka lo7o qoodheppe qommo hano” gides.
LUK 12:2 Qoncconta kamettidi attizaynne erettonta qotan attannay baa.
LUK 12:3 Hessa gish inte geeman haasa7idazi wuri qoncce kezena, qassekka inte qol7an haythan sasukketi haasa7idazi wuri dere sinthan yootettana.
LUK 12:4 Ta laggeto ta intes gizay asho xalla wodhanappe attin hara aykkokka oothanas dandda7ontaytas babbofite.
LUK 12:5 Gido attin inte babbaanas bessizay oonakkoone ta intes bessana asho wodhidape guye ashonne shemponne issife gathi gaanname taman yegganas danda7izaysa babitte. Ee izas babbite gays.
LUK 12:6 Gaashe kafo ichachchati nam77u santes bayzettettees, gido attin istafe issiniyokka Xoossi dogenna.
LUK 12:7 Inte hu7e ithikey kumeth taybboon dees. hessa gish babbofite, daro gaashe kafotappe inte aadhdhista.
LUK 12:8 T intes yooays “ta gish asa sinthan markatiza asa wursos asa nay qassekka Xoossa kiitancha sinthan iza gish markkttana.
LUK 12:9 Gido attin asa sinthan tana kadida uray Xoossa kiitancha sinthan izi kaddistana.
LUK 12:10 Asa na bolla kawisha qaala haasa7iza uras naggaray wuri maaristana shin xillo ayanan cayiza uray maaretenna.
LUK 12:11 Asay intena oykkidi dere haarizaytakkonne Godatizaytako mukurabe oykki efikko ay zarino ay giino gidi hirgofite.
LUK 12:12 Ays giiko inte haasa7ana koshizaysa xillo ayaanaay he wode intena tamaarsana.”
LUK 12:13 Daro asa garsafe issi uray “tamaarisizayso ta ishay nu aawa lata miishshafe tana gakkizaysa taas immana mala izas yoota” gides.
LUK 12:14 Yesussaykka “hayso tana inte bolla pirdiza daanna oothiday oonee?” gides.
LUK 12:15 Qassekka istas “asas daro miish deyikkokka shemppoy he duretethan deyonta gish naagetite, yiiqqetethafe intena keehi naagite” gides.
LUK 12:16 Zarethidikka qasse istas leemuso hiz gidi yottidees “lo7ethi kath immiza gade Goda gidida issi dure asi dees.
LUK 12:17 He addezzika ba wozinan <ta kaththa shishshada wothizassoy bayndda gish ay oothoo?> gidi qoppides.
LUK 12:18 Addezzika <taas diza gootarata lalada hara aakkizaaz keexada kaththanne taas dizaz ubbaa izan shishshanna.
LUK 12:19 Ta shempiyokka ta shemppoye daro wodes gidiza kath shiishshida gish shemppa uttada ma, uya ufa7ista> gaana gides.
LUK 12:20 Gido attin <Xoossi haysso eeyazo ne shemppiyo hach omars neppe ekkana koyetes, hessa gish ne nees shiishshidays oonas gidanee?> gides.
LUK 12:21 Hessa gish Xoossa achchan dure gidonta bees miishshe shiishshiza asa wursethikka hessa mala.”
LUK 12:22 Hessafe guye Yesussay bena kaallizaytas “intes ta yootays inte duusas ay maanakkonne, woykko inte bollas ay mayanaakkonne daro qoppofite.
LUK 12:23 Ays giiko shemppoy kaththafe asatethi qasse mayoppe aadhdhees.
LUK 12:24 Quurota xellite zeretenna maaxetenna, kath shiishshiza gootaray istas baa shin Xoossi ista muzees. histtikko inte istafe keehi adhdheketii?
LUK 12:25 Gido attin intefe darsi qoppidi ba laytha bolla issi gallas gujjana dandda7izay oonee?
LUK 12:26 Histtikko guutha miish oothooy intes dandda7etontashshe ays hara miishshas keehi qoppetii?
LUK 12:27 Ciishshati waanidi diccizaakkonne ane xellite, waayyettenna, suqettenna gido attin ta intes yootays Solomoneykka giita asa shin istafe issineytho maybeynna.
LUK 12:28 Histtikko Xoossi hach beettiddi wonto taman wodhana maata hayssatho mayziza gidikko inteno amannoy paccidayto intena wosit aathi mayizanee?
LUK 12:29 Hessa gish ay minoo ay maynoo giidi inte wozinay darsi qoppofo.
LUK 12:30 Biitta bollan diza asi wuri hayssa koyees, gido attin hayssi wuri intes koshizayyssa inte salo aaway eres.
LUK 12:31 Wursofekka koyrothidi Xoossa kawotethi koyite hayssi wuri intes gujjeti imettanna.
LUK 12:32 Inteno guutha mehe wude mala gididayto kawotethi intes immanas inte aawa lo7o qofa gidida gish babbofite.
LUK 12:33 Intes dizayssa bayziddi manqotas immite, kaysoy ekkonta son, bil77ay montason, cimonta korojjon wuronta miish salon shiishshite.
LUK 12:34 Inte wozinay inte miish dizason daana.
LUK 12:35 qaqnthan gixxidi giigetite, inte poo7oykka poo77o,
LUK 12:36 Ista Goday bulachcha diggisappe simmidi yaanashe naagetizaytanne izi yiidi pengge qoxishin elle doyanas giigi uttida asata milatite.
LUK 12:37 Ista Goday yiza wode dhiskonta naagidi uttida ashshkarati isti anjjettidayta, ta intes tumu gays ista Goday bees qaanthan gixxi eqqidi ista maaddan utisidi muzana.
LUK 12:38 Omars woykko gidi giddoth yiidi isti dhiskkonta dishin demmikko he ashshkarati anjjettidayta.
LUK 12:39 Kaysoy ay wode yaanakkon eriza gididakko keeththa Goday kaysoy bookkishin co7u giidi besoonttayssa erite.
LUK 12:40 Asa nay inte qopponta woden yanayisa eridi intekka giigetidi naagite.”
LUK 12:41 Phexirosaykka “Godo hayssa leemuso ne yootizay nuus xallaye wurso asasara yootizayii?” gides.
LUK 12:42 Godaykka “histtikko beso asas koshshiza woden quma immana mala keethaddey keeththa asa bolla wothiza amanettidda wozinama asi oonee?” giidi zaarides.
LUK 12:43 Goday simmiishni hessaththo oothishe beettizaddey izi anjjettidadde.
LUK 12:44 Ta intes tumu gays bees diza miish wurso bolla he ura goddasna.
LUK 12:45 Gido attin he uray ta Goday elle yeena gam7ana giidi qoppidi addenne macca ashshkarata bukkikko, qassekka koyida mala miidi uyidi mathotikko
LUK 12:46 he ura Goday izi qopponta gallassan yaana giidi sidhonta saatten yana. yiidikka iza qanxerethidi iza exa amanonttaytara issife oothanna.
LUK 12:47 Be Goda qofa eridi giigetontaynne Goda shene oothonta ashshkaray iita shoch shocettana.
LUK 12:48 Gido attin eronta dishe shochas bessiza mooro oothida ashshkaray guuthara shocistana. Daro imetida asa wursofe daroy koyetes, daro haddara ekkida urappe daroy koyetes.
LUK 12:49 Tani yiday biitta bollan tama eethanassa. He tamay ha7i eexxi kezidakko tana daro ufaysanashin.
LUK 12:50 Gido attin tani xamaqistana xinqatay dees, he xinqatay polistanashe tani keeha metotettadis.
LUK 12:51 Intes tani biitta bolla saro ehanna yida milatizee? Gideenna, ta intes yootays tani yiday issa issafe shaakanassa.
LUK 12:52 Haysafe sinthan issi keeththan ba giddon shaakettida ichachu asati daana. Nam77ati heezata bolla heezati nam77ata bolla denddidi ba garssan shaakistanna.
LUK 12:53 Aaway ba attumma na bolla, attumma naykka ba aawa bolla, aaya ba macca nay bolla maca nayakka ba aayeyi bolla, bolota ba na machchey bolla, na machaka ba boloti bolla denddidi ba garsan shaakistana.
LUK 12:54 Qassekka derezas “inte awa arshey mokiza bagara shaaray kezishin beyidi elleraka iray yana gees geista inte gida malaka hanes.
LUK 12:55 Duge baggara pude carkishshin gallassay ho7o gidana geista, inte gida malaka hanes.
LUK 12:56 Inteno lo7o milatiza iitato saloysanne sa7a medha beyidi hananayisa ereista shin histini ha wodeza eroy intena waani xoonizee?
LUK 12:57 Histikko inte ays tuma firdeketii?
LUK 12:58 Ne morkera daana sinthan eqqana bishin buro oge bollan dashe izara giigana oge maqqa, ne histonta agikko nena gochchidi daana sinth efana, daannaykka nena aathiddi halaqas immana, halaqaykka nena woynen yeggana.
LUK 12:59 Ta nees yootays daannay firdida wursetha santime qanxa wursana gakanas heepe kezaka.”
LUK 13:1 He wode Philaxoossay ista suuthi ista yarshora gathi walakida Galila asata gish Yesussas yoottida asati heen iza ollan deetes.
LUK 13:2 Izikka zaaridi histtini hessamala waayey ista bolla gakkida asati hankko waayey gakkonta attida Galila asa wursotappe aadhdhida nagarancha gidida gish giidi qoppetii? gides.
LUK 13:3 Gideena ta intes yootays inte maaretonta ixxikko inte wurikka he asata mala dhayana.
LUK 13:4 Woykko Salhomen gimbey ista bolla wodhdhin hayqqida, tammanne osppun asati Yerusalemen diza asa wursofe nagarancha gididagish giidi qoppetii?
LUK 13:5 Gideenna ta intes yootays inte maaretonta ixxikko inte wurikka he asata mala dhayanan.
LUK 13:6 Qassekka istas issi uray woyne tookkizasson tokkettida issi balase giza mith daysu, he balase miththaykko ayfe koshshu yiidi issi ayfekka demmibeynna.
LUK 13:7 Woyne akakkiltte oothizaysas “hekko tani ayfe demmna gaada hachchra heezzu layth ha balaseykko simerista yaada issi ayfekka demabeykke, hessa gish izo qanxxa diga, aazas coo biitta xunxazee?” giidi leemuso yootides.
LUK 13:8 Izika zaaridi Godo tani izi xaphon osha yeggada oothetha xeellana mala halaythas agaggarkkii.
LUK 13:9 Yiza laythas iza ayfikko lo7o, ayfonta ixxikko qanxxanddasa gides.
LUK 13:10 Yesussay sanbbata gallas issi mukuraben tamaarisishin
LUK 13:11 tammanne osppun layth kumeth iita ayaanaay oykkidi asatetha pacisida issi maccashya heen daysu, izakka zokkoy kuunnida gish mulekka dhoqqu gaanas dandda7ukku
LUK 13:12 Yesussay izo beyidinne xeeygidi hanne maccashaye neni nena sakkiza hargezappe paxaddasakko gides.
LUK 13:13 Izi ba kushe izi bolla wothini iza heeraka sit gaada eqqadus, Xoossakka galatadus.
LUK 13:14 Mukurabe halaqqazikka sanbbata gallas pathidaysas Yesussa bolla hanqqettidi izakko yiza dereza “oothos bessiza usuppun gallasati diza gish he ootho galassatan yiidi paxite attin sanbbata gallas yooppite” gides.
LUK 13:15 Godaykka zaaridi inteno qoodheppe qommon haasa7izayto inte garsafe issi uray ba boora woykko ba hare sanbbata gallas beson qachchettidasooppe birshiddi haathe ushanaas efi erennee?
LUK 13:16 Histtin hanna maccashiya Abrame na gidada tammanne osppun layth kumeth xalla7ey qachchin diza sooppe sanbbata gallas birshettanas izis besennee? gides
LUK 13:17 Yesussay hizgi oychchida wode izara eqqettizayti wurikka yelattida, gido attin derey wurikka izi oychchida malalisiza oychcho wurson ufa7ettides.
LUK 13:18 Qassekka Yesussay zaaridi Xoossa kawotethi ay milatizee? Izo aazara leemusoo?
LUK 13:19 Issi uray etha ayfe ba gadeni tookkini mokada diccada gita gidiin kafoti izi hangge giddon duusasso giigissana gakanas dicida etha mith milataysu gides.
LUK 13:20 Qassekka Xoossa kawotethi aazara leemusoo?
LUK 13:21 Issi maccash munuqa caallisanas daro dhiillera walakkida guutha irsho malaataysu gides.
LUK 13:22 Hessafe guye Yesussay Yerusaleme bishe kanthi biza katamanne gutatan asa tamaarisishe aadhdhishin,
LUK 13:23 issi uray izakko shiiqidi “Godo firdappe guutha asati xalla atannee?” giidi oychchides. Izikka zaaridi xuntha pengeyra gelanaas baxxettite, daroti gelanaas koyetes shin istas hanena.
LUK 13:25 Keetha Goday denddidi ba kare gordi gidiin inte karen eqqidi Godo kare doyarkki giidi pengge qoxana shin izi zaaridi inte oonakkone awappe yidakkone ta intena erikke gaana gides.
LUK 13:26 Intenikka izas zaaridi nuni nenara issife midosinne issife uydos nu dubbushan nuna ne tamaarsadasa gaana.
LUK 13:27 Izika zaaridi intena inte oonakkone inte awappe yidakko ta intena erikke inte makkal7ati wurikka tappe haakkite gaana gides.
LUK 13:28 Inte Abramenne Yisaqqane Yaqobe nabeta wursota Xoossa kawotethan beyiza wode inte karen yegetti attizza wode he wode intes yeehonne achche garcethi gidana.
LUK 13:29 Asay away mokiza baggafenne wiliza baggafe pude baggafenne duge baggafe yiidi Xoossa kawotetha maaddan uttana.
LUK 13:30 Hekko guyyen dizaytappe bagaz sinthe aadhdhanna sinthan dizaytappe baggati guye aadhdhannayti deetes.
LUK 13:31 He wode Farsawistappe issi issi assi yiidi “Herdoossay nena wodhanas koyiza gish hayssafe dendda kichcha” gida.
LUK 13:32 Yesussay istas “tani buro hachchine wontoone dayiddanthata asappe kessana harggizaytakka pathana heezantho gallas ta ammoso ta gathanna gides gidi he worikkenas yootite” gides.
LUK 13:33 Gido attin nabey Yerusalemeppe karen hayqqanas besontta gish hachchine wonto wontofeinikka ta hamuth sinth gujjana gides.
LUK 13:34 Hanne Yerusaleme nabeta wodhizare neekko kitettiddayta shuuchchara caddizare kuttoy ba ciyista ba qefe gars shiishiza mala ne nayta shishanas aappun wode koyadinashin inte gakkides akkay gidista.
LUK 13:35 Hekko inte keethay kayzides ta intes yootays Goda sunthan yiza uray anjjettides inte gaana wodey gakanashe nam77antho tana beyekista.
LUK 14:1 Issi gallas Yesussay quma maanaas Farsawista halaqatape issa so gelida wode asay wuri Yesussa ay oothanakonne gidi ayfe iza bolla tooki xellides.
LUK 14:2 Heenka asatethay izas purin wayetiza issi assi iza sinthan dees.
LUK 14:3 Yesussaykka Muse woga erizaytanne Farsawista saketizadde sanbbata gallas pathanaas koshize koshennee? gidi oychchides.
LUK 14:4 Istika co7u gida izikka addezza bochchiddi pathi yeddides.
LUK 14:5 Qassekka intefe issi asas sanbbata wode nay woykko booray kundidi olan geliko eeson heeraka kesonta uray oone? gides.
LUK 14:6 Istika oychas aykko zaroka demmnaas dand7ibeyitenna
LUK 14:7 Xeygetida asati uttanaas boncho so koyishin Yesussay beyidi leemuso istas hiz gidi yoottides.
LUK 14:8 Issi assi nena sarges xeysiko boncho son utofa, nepe bollara bonchetizaddey xeysetiko
LUK 14:9 Intena nam77antaka xeysidaddey yiidi ne utidasoza hayssaddes yeda gaana, nenika yelatashe ziqaso banddassa.
LUK 14:10 Gido attin xeysetida wode ziqaso xellada utta, nena xegidaddey yiidi ta lagge haaya dhoqason utta gaandes, nenika he wode nenara maaddan utida asa wurso sinthan bonchetana.
LUK 14:11 Ays giiko bena dhoqqu histizaddey wuri ziq gaana bena ziq histizaddey wuri dhoqqu gaana.
LUK 14:12 Yesussaykka xeygidaddeza hiz gides quma woykko ka7o muzanas xeysiko neysatho nena xeysidi muzonta mala ne laggeta woykko ne ishata, ne dabota, woykko durista woykko dure guttata xegopa
LUK 14:13 Gido attin asa xeysada muzana koyko manqota, kushey toy bayndda wobistane qooqeta xeysa neni anjetana.
LUK 14:14 Xeysetidayti kushe zaranaas danda7onta gish xillota dentha wode nees kushey zaretana.
LUK 14:15 Maaddan Yesussara issife utidaytape issay hayssa siyidi Xoossa kawotethan shiiqidi maaddafe miza uray anjetidadde gides.
LUK 14:16 Yesussaykka hizgides issi assi wolqama diggisa giigisidi daro assi xeygides.
LUK 14:17 Diggissa maana wodeyka gakin xeygetida imathata wurikka giigida gish ha yite gidi xegana mala ba ashkkara yeddides.
LUK 14:18 Gido attin wurikka beso hara gaaso shiishidi isoy ha7i gade shamadis baada beyanas besses hachsi tana lancofa gides.
LUK 14:19 Hankoysika tani ichachu waxa boora shamadis izista paaca xellana gish hach tana lancofa gides.
LUK 14:20 Qasse hara asaykka tani buro miishratethan days baannaas danda7ikke gides.
LUK 14:21 Oothanchayka kitetida soope simmidi hezati gidayssa ba Godas yoottides. he wodeka diggisa giigisidays hanqetidi oothancha hizgides, elella oydu oge kezada manqota, kusheynne toy bayndda wobista qomaxatanne ayfey bayndda qooqeta ha geltha gides.
LUK 14:22 Oothanchayka zaaridi ta Godo ne tana azazidaysa wursa poladis burokka utetha soy dees gides.
LUK 14:23 Godazikka oothanchaza gede oydu oge keza ta keeth kumana mala pudene dugenne aadhdhizaytta wolqara geltha.
LUK 14:24 Tani tuma gays diggisa maana xeysetidaytape issi urayka duunan gelthenna gides.
LUK 14:25 Daro derey izara issife bizayssa beyidi guye simmida Yesussay hizgides.
LUK 14:26 Taako yizay wuri ba aawanne ba, ba machchonne nayta, ba ishatanne michchista ba duus gidiin ixonta agikko tana kaallizadde gidanas danda7enna.
LUK 14:27 Be masqale tookidi tana kaalontay tana kaallizadde gidanas danda7enna.
LUK 14:28 Inte issi assi keethe keexanas koyko polanaas danda7anakkonne danda7ontako koyrotidi ba bira qopontay oone?
LUK 14:29 Keetha keexana doomidi wursanaas hanonta ixxiko beydda assi wuri iza bolla miicana.
LUK 14:30 Istika hizgana haysi addezzi keeth oykides shin polibeyna.
LUK 14:31 Woykko issi kawoy hara kawora olistana giigiidi nam77u tamu shi asa assi ekki yiza kawo zaranaas tamu shi ola asara zaranakonne uttidi qopontay oone?
LUK 14:32 Ola zaranaas danda7ettontta milatida bettikko buro hahon dishin maqaynanas gaana yedes.
LUK 14:33 Izaka mala inte oonikka gidiin bees dizaysa aggontay oonikka tana kaallizadde gidanas danda7enna.
LUK 14:34 Maxiney lo7oshin maxiney mal7onta ixxiko go7ena,
LUK 14:35 Gadeni yegin gidonta gish co kare wora yegetes siyiza haythi diza assi siyo.
LUK 15:1 Issi gallas qaraxa shiishizaytine nagaranchati wuri Yesussappe siyanas iza achch shiiqqida.
LUK 15:2 Farsawetinne Xaafeti “ha addey nagaranchata ixxenna, istarakka mees” giidi ba garssan zigiretida.
LUK 15:3 Yesussaykka istas leemuso hiz gi yoottides
LUK 15:4 “Inte giddofe issi uras xeetu dorssi diikko he xeetu dorssatape issina dhaykko atidda uddufun tammanne uddufunata denbban yeggidi dhayidayssa demmna gakanas koyana bonttay oonee?
LUK 15:5 Demmida wode ufaysara hashen tookki ekkidi
LUK 15:6 beso simmes, ba laggetanne guta asata issi bolla xeeyggidi <dhayida ta dorssiyo demmadis tanara issife ufa7etite> gandes.
LUK 15:7 Ta intes yootays <hessathokka maaroteth koshonta uddufun tammanne uddufun xillotappe maaretethan geliza issi nagaranchan salon ufayssa gidana.” >
LUK 15:8 Woyko issi tamu bira santimey diza maccashiya he tamappe issiniyadhaykko xomppe oythada demmna gakanas keeththa gars pitada lo7etha koyonta maccash oonee?
LUK 15:9 Izakka demmida wode ba laggetanne ba gutata issife xeeyggada “tappe dhayida bira santimeyo demmida gish tanara issife ufa7etite” gandus.
LUK 15:10 Ta intes yootays “hessathokka maarotan geliza issi nagarancha uran Xoossa kiitanchata achchan ufays gidana”
LUK 15:11 Qassekka Yesussay asatas hizgides “issi uras nam77u nayti deetes.
LUK 15:12 Istappekka kaalo naazi ba aawa <aabo! nees diza miishshafe ta gish taas imma> gides. Aawaykka bees diza miishsha ba naytas gishides.”
LUK 15:13 Daro wode gam7onta dishe kaalo naazi ba miishsha wursi shiishshi ekkidi haho biitta biddes. Heenka bees diza miishsha go7ay bayndda coo mela dhaysides.
LUK 15:14 Izikka bees dizaysa wursi wursidappe guyyen he biittan iita koshay denddini daro waaydes.
LUK 15:15 Hessa gish he dereni diza asappe issaadekko shiiqidees. He uraykka ba guddunth heemana mala gudduntha heemizasso yeddides.
LUK 15:16 Naazikka guddunthati miza harqqo maanaas amottides, shin hessakka immizaddey baa.
LUK 15:17 Gido attin iza wozinay simmida wode “ta aawa ashkkaratappe aappunappe kath tirpize shin tani hayssan gafan hayqqana matadinaa?
LUK 15:18 Denddada ta aawa so baada <aabo! salon Xoossa: biittan nena ta qohadis.”>
LUK 15:19 Haysappe guye “ta nena geetistada xeeyggistanas taas beesena: ne ashkkaratappe issa mala tana taybba” gides.
LUK 15:20 Hessa gish dendidi ba aawakko biddes. gido attin buroo izi hahora yishin aaway beyidi michchettidinne izakko woxxi biiddi idimi oykkidi yerides.
LUK 15:21 Naazikka “aabo salon Xoossa, biittan nena ta qohadis, hayssafe guyyen ta ne na geetistada xeeyggistanas taas beesena” gides.
LUK 15:22 Gido attin aaway ashkkaratas eesottidi wursofe doorettida mayo ehidi mayzite iza biradhdhen yiichi, iza tohonkka caamma aathite.
LUK 15:23 Modhdho mirgo ehidi shukkite, miidi ufa7etos.
LUK 15:24 Haysi ta nay hayqqides shin paxides dhaydes shin beettides gides, hessafe guyyen ufa7eteth oykkida.
LUK 15:25 Haysi hanniza wode bayra naazi goshsha son dees, heepekka simmidi so matida wode diitha durus siyides.
LUK 15:26 Izika ashkkaratappe issa xeeyggidi “hessi aazzee?” gi oychchides.
LUK 15:27 Ashkaarazikka “ne ishay yides, izi saronne lo7ooni simmida gish ne aaway handadho mirgo shukides” gides.
LUK 15:28 Bayra ishazikka hanqqettidi so gelanaskka koybeynna. Aawaykka kare kezidi izi so gelana mala woosides.
LUK 15:29 Gido attin izikka zaaridi aawas “hekko tani hayssa gakanas nees aylle mala oothadis, azazoppe isinokka pacisabeyke, gido attin ne ta laggetara ufa7istana mala issi deyshsha laaqqakka imabeyka,
LUK 15:30 Gido attin haysi ne naazi nees dizaysa wursi laymatizaytara wursidi yishin handadho mirgo izas shukkadasa” gides
LUK 15:31 Awaykka “ta nazo ne wurso wode tanara daassa, taas gididay wurikka neessa.
LUK 15:32 Haysi ne ishay hayqqides shin paxides dhaydes shin beettides, hessa gish nuni ufa7istanas besses” gides.
LUK 16:1 Yesussay bena kaallizaytas hiz gides “issi dure adde daysas iza keeththa ayssiza issi assi dees, izi he dure addezza miishsha ogey bayndda lalizayssa worey ha dure addezza haythan wodhides.
LUK 16:2 Dure addezzi uraa xeeygidi <hayso ta siyizaysi aazzee? Haysafe doomada ne ta keethas ayssizadde gidanas dandda7ontagish ne alafetetha garsan diza miishsha oykkida mazgaba zaara>” gides.
LUK 16:3 Keetha ayssizaddezzi ba wozinara ta Goday tana ta alafetethafe goodana gees goya maanas taas wolqay baa, woossanas yeelatays, hessa gididagish ay ootho gides.
LUK 16:4 Tani alafetethafe kezikko asay tana mokki ekkana mala oothanna oge ta erays.
LUK 16:5 Hessa gish iza Goda acoy ista bolla diza asata issi issi ura xeeygides. Koyro yidaysa ne bolla Goda acoy aapunee? gides.
LUK 16:6 Issi xeetu xaaro kumetha zayitey ta bolla dees gides. Alafezi zaaridi kase ne faramida woraqqata hey ekka uttada elle ichachu tamu xaaro gaada xaafa gides.
LUK 16:7 Kaalidi hankkoysa nech ne bolla aappun dizee? gides. Ichachu tamu il7o gisttey dees gides. Alafezi zaaridi kase ne tal7ashe faramida waraqqata hey oyddu tamu il7o gaada xaafa gides.
LUK 16:8 Godazikka shocechiza alafezi oothida cincatetha gish nashides. Ha alame nayti bena milatizaytara diza gaagotethan poo7o naytappe aadhdhidi cincca.
LUK 16:9 Hessa gish tani intena gizay ha biitta miishshay wurida wode medhina keeththan inte ekettana mala ha7i intes diza miishshaara intes lagge medhdhite gays gides.
LUK 16:10 Guutha miishshan amanetizza uray daro miishshan amanettanna, guutha miishshan amanettonttaddey daro miishshan amanettenna.
LUK 16:11 Histikko inte ha biitta miishshan amanettenna ixxikko tuma miishsha hadara oykkite giidi ooni intes immanee?
LUK 16:12 Asa miishshan inte amanettontta ixxikko intes buzu7a gidana miish ooni immanee?
LUK 16:13 Nam77u Godas issi to issi bolla azazettana dandda7iza uray oonikka deenna woy issa dosidi issa ixxees woykko issakko shiiqidi hankkoysa leqqes. Xoossasine miishasinne haaristanas dandda7ekkista.
LUK 16:14 Miishsha darisi siiqiza Farsaweti hessa wursi siyidi Yesussa qidhida.
LUK 16:15 Yesussaykka istas inte intena asa achchan xilisista gido attin Xoossi inte wozina erees. Asa achchan bonchettidda uray Xoossa sinthan tuna giidi istas yoottides.
LUK 16:16 Muse wogayne nabeti Yanisay yaana gakanas haasa7ishe gam77ida. Hessa kaallidi qasse Xoossa kawotethas miishrachchoy sabbakketides, asi wurikka hee gelanaas wadhetes.
LUK 16:17 Gido attin Muse wogappe issi qeerina kundda atanaysafe saloynne biittaynne aadhanaysi kawisha gidana.
LUK 16:18 Be machcho anjji yedidi hara machcho ekkiza assi wurikka laymates ba addefe anjetta bidaro ekkidayskka laymatees.
LUK 16:19 Qassekka Yesussay istas lo7o mayo mayidi gallas gallas lo7o duussa ufayssan diza issi dure assi dees gides.
LUK 16:20 He addezza pengeni kumetha bollay madunth xalla gidida issi Alaazaaree geetettiza manqo adde dizaysi zin7idi dees.
LUK 16:21 Izikka he dure addezza keeththan asay kath miishni maaddafe hugen wodhiza duuxxeth maxi maanaas amotees. Kanatikka iza maduntha laacetees.
LUK 16:22 Ha manqo addezzikka hayqqin salo kiitanchati Abrame ki7o ekki bida dure addezzikka hayqqidi moogetides.
LUK 16:23 Si77olen wayetishe dhoqqu giidi haahon Abrame xellides, Alaazaareekka ba ki77n oykk dishin be7ides.
LUK 16:24 Dre addezzi aawa Abrame hayssan wayetiza taas michcharki Alaazaarey ba biradhdhe xeera irxx haathan bochchidi ta inxxrs irxisana mala yedarki giii wassides.
LUK 16:25 Gdo attin Abramey ta nazo neni biitta bolla dashe lo7o duus deyida mala Alaazaarey kase waye beydyss ne qopp gido attin ha7i izi ufa7etishn neni waaistassa gides.
LUK 16:26 Hessi wuri hanshin haan diza assi haappe hee intekko aadhdhontta mala qassekka intekkon dizay haa nukko aadhdhana koyiza uray haa aadhdhontta mala intesine nuus giddon gita aafoy giiggetides gides.
LUK 16:27 Dure addezzi qasse aabo hessi hessagidikko neni Alaazaare duge ta aawasso yedanamala nena woossays, taas ichachu ishati deetes, hayti hayssa waayeso yontamala biidi istas lo7ethi yootana mala Alaazaare yedarkki gides.
LUK 16:29 Abramey izas zaaridi Museynne nabeti heen ista achchan diza gish istafe siyeto gides.
LUK 16:30 Izika zaaridi aawa Abrame hessamala gidenna hayqqida asappe issi uray hayqoppe dendi biikko isti Xoossa maaretethan gelana gides.
LUK 16:31 Abrameykka zaaridi Museynne nabeti gizayssa siyonta ixxikko hayqqida asappe issi uray dendidakkokka isti amanettenna gides.
LUK 17:1 Yesussay bena kaallizayta hizgides “asa dhuphidi nagaran yeggiza miish yoontta aggenna, gido attin yaana dhuphezas gaaso gidizaddes ayye!
LUK 17:2 He uray ha guuthatappe issas dhuphe gidanappe woxa shuchi iza qoodhen qachetin abba gido izi yeggetizakko izas lo7o gidana.
LUK 17:3 Hessa gish inte hu7es naagetitte. Ne ishay nena qohikko hanqqista, izi ba mooro eridi simmikko maara.
LUK 17:4 Issi gallassan laappun to zaari zaari qohidi laappun toka zari zari maara giiko maara.
LUK 17:5 Hawaretikka Godo nuus amano gujja gida.
LUK 17:6 Godaykka gaashe ayfe lagge amanoy intes diikko hayssa etha dhoqqalista baada abban gela tokkista inte giikko izi intes azazettana” gides.
LUK 17:7 Qassekka Yesussay hizgides “inte giddofe issi asas goshshanchay woykko dorss heemiza ashkkaray diikko, izi goyidi simmiishni taas maana ka7o giigissa, ta maadda uyana gakanas gixistada taas ootha hessafe guye baggan maasa uyasa gees attin ha7i quma maana aadhdha gizee?
LUK 17:9 Histtikko he ashkkara Goday izi iza azazo polida gish iza galati erizee?
LUK 17:10 Hessa gish intenikka inte azazettidayssa wursi polida wode, nuni go7ay bayndda oothanchata nuus oothanas bessizaysa poli oothidos gite.”
LUK 17:11 Hessafe guye Yesussay Yerusaleme bishe Samaryarane Galila achchara aadhdhidees.
LUK 17:12 Issi mannidara gelida wode inchiracha hargiza tamu asati iza demmida. Istika haahon eqqidi
LUK 17:13 ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi “Yesussa! Godo! nuus michchistarkki” gida.
LUK 17:14 Izika ista beydda wode “biite intena qeesetas beesitte” gides. istikka buro bishe oge bolla paxida.
LUK 17:15 Istappe issay ba paxidayssa beyidi ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi Xoossa bonchishe simmides.
LUK 17:16 Izika Yesussa toho bolla kunddidi galattides, izikka Samariya biitta asa.
LUK 17:17 Yesussaykka addeza “paxidayti tamu assi detenne histini uddufunati awa bidoo?” giidi oychchides.
LUK 17:18 Haysa dumma dere asappe attin Xoossa galatizay baawa gusee?
LUK 17:19 Addezakka zaaridi denddada ba nena ne amanoy pathides gides.
LUK 17:20 Xoossa kawotethi aydde yaanakko Farsaweti Yesussa oychchida wode Yesussay “Xoossa kawotethi beettiza malaatatan yuukku” giidi zaaridees.
LUK 17:21 Asay Xoossa kawotethi haan daysu woykko heen daysu gaanas daandda7etenna, Xoossa ka7otethi inte giddon daysu.
LUK 17:22 Bena kaallizaytaskka “asa na gallassatappe issi gallasyo beyanas inte amotana wodey yaana, gido attin inte beyekkista” gides.
LUK 17:23 Asay intes haan daysu woykko heen daysu gaana shin inte ista kaallidi booppitte.
LUK 17:24 Gaasoykka wolqanthi wolqamidi salo gaxappe salo gaxa gakanas po7isiza mala asa nay yiza gallas iza mala hanana.
LUK 17:25 Gido attin haysi wuri hananappe koyro asa nay daro meto ekkanasne hayssa ha yelletethan kadhistanas besses.
LUK 17:26 Nohe wode handaysa mala asa na wodenka hessaththo hanana.
LUK 17:27 Nohey markabben gelana gallas gakanas asay miishnine uyishin ekishine gelishin dhaysiza haathi yiidi wursika dhaysides.
LUK 17:28 Looxe wodekka iza mala handees, asay meesinne uyes bayzesinne shammees tookizaz tokees keethekka keexxetes.
LUK 17:29 Shin Looxey Soddomeppe kezida gallas shuch mithi qoronta tamay diinney saloppe bukkidi wursi dhaysides.
LUK 17:30 Asa nay qonciza gallas hessaththo hanana.
LUK 17:31 He wode ba keeththa bolla diza uray oonikka keeththa giddon diza miish ekkana giidi wodhoppo, hessathokka goshsha son diza asi guye simmofo.
LUK 17:32 Looxe machcho qoppite.
LUK 17:33 Be deyo gam7isana koyizay wuri dhaysana ba shemppo aathi immiza uray gam7isana.
LUK 17:34 Ta intes gays he wode omars nam77u assi issi hiixxan zin7ana, isoy ekettana isoy attanna.
LUK 17:35 Nam77u maccashati issife gaaccishin isiniya ekettana hankora attanna.
LUK 17:36 Nam77u assi issife goshsha son daana issay ekettana issay attanna.
LUK 17:37 Istika zaaridi Godo isti awa ekettanee? gida. izikka anhay diza son ankotti shiiqqana gides.
LUK 18:1 Bena kaallizayti azalontta wurso wode woossanas bessizaysa erisanas Yesussay ha leemusoza istas yoottides.
LUK 18:2 “Issi kataman Xoossine babbontta asenne bonchontta issi daannay dees.
LUK 18:3 He katamankka issi am77i maccash daysu, izakka ta balggarara taas moottoy diza gish firdarikki gashe izakko simeristadus.
LUK 18:4 Daannazikka daro wode gakanas izis firdibeynna, gido attin guyyeppe ba wozinan Xoossi babbontta assekka bonchontta agikko,
LUK 18:5 hanna am77e maccashiya tana wayssiza gish ta izis pirdana, hessa histonta agikko wurso wode simeristada tana daabbursana.” gides.
LUK 18:6 Godaykka hizgides “makkal7ancha daannay gidayssa siyite,
LUK 18:7 Xoossi gallassinne omars izakko wassiza doorettidaytas fiiddenneyee? Tana ay metide giidi ba maado gam7issandee?
LUK 18:8 Ta intes gays istas elle firdana, gido attin asa nay yiza wode biitta bolla amano demandeeshsha?”
LUK 18:9 Bena xillo asa mala qoodidi ceqettizaytasnne harata leqo ayfen xeelizaytas leemusora hizgides.
LUK 18:10 Nam77u asati woossanas maqddase bida, issay Farsawe hinkkoysi qaraxa shiishizadde.
LUK 18:11 Farsawezikka eqqidi ba gish hizgi woossides, Xoosso! tani hara asa mala bonqqizadde, makkal7izadde, laymatizadde harapekka hayssa qaraxa shiishshizadde mala gidonta aggida gish ta nena galatays.
LUK 18:12 Samintan nam77a xoomays, taas dizaysafe tamappe issa immays.
LUK 18:13 Gido attin qaraxa shiishshizaddezi haahon eqqidi pude salo dhoqqu giidi xeellanas koybeynna, gido attin ba tira icishe “Xoosso! tana nagaranchaza maara gides.”
LUK 18:14 Ta intes yootays Xoossa sinthan Farsawezi xillotethi demibeyna shin haysi qaraxizaysi xilidi ba so simmides. Bena dhoqqusizay wuri ziq gaana, bena ziqsizay gidikko dhoqqu gaana.
LUK 18:15 Yesussay bochcherethanna mala asay guutha nayta izakko ehides. Iza kaallizaytikka hessa beydda wode hanqettida.
LUK 18:16 Gido attin Yesussay guutha nayta beekko xeeygidi hiz gides “guutha nayti taakko yanayisa diggoppite, Xoossa kawotethi haytanta malaatasa.
LUK 18:17 Ta intes tumu gays, Xoossa kawotethi guutha na mala ekkontay wuri izin gelenna.”
LUK 18:18 Ayhuddista halaqqatappe issay kiya astaamarezo medhina deyo lattanas ay ootho giidi oychchides.
LUK 18:19 Yesussaykka hizgidi zarides, “aazas tana kiya gazii? Issi Xoossafe attin hara kiyay deenna.
LUK 18:20 Laymatoppa, wodhoppa, kaysotoppa, wordo markkattofa, ne aawanne ne boncha giza azazoza eraasa.
LUK 18:21 Addezzikka hayta gidikko guutha natetethafe doomada naagadis gides.
LUK 18:22 Yesussaykka hessa siyida wode histtikko nees issi miish paces, nees dizaz wursa bayizadda manqotas imma, salo mazgaban demandasa, izape guye yaada tana kaalla gides.
LUK 18:23 Gido attin addezzi hessa siyida wode daro haaroy izas diza gish keehi michetides.
LUK 18:24 Yesussaykka addezza xeellidi daro miishi diza asati Xoossa kawotethi gelanays aymala meto” gides.
LUK 18:25 Durey Xoossa kawotethi gelanaysafe gaammelay narppe lukkora gelanaysi matana.
LUK 18:26 Hessa siyida asay histin oonii attanna dandda7izee? gides.
LUK 18:27 Yesussaykka asa achchan dandda7etontay Xoossa achchan dandda7etees gides.
LUK 18:28 Phexirosaykka hekko nuni nuus dizaz wursi aggiddi nena kaallidos gides.
LUK 18:29 Yesussaykka istas ta intes tumu gays Xoossa kawotethas giidi ba keeth, ba machcho, ba ishanta woykko bena yeliddayta woykko ba nayta aggida uray
LUK 18:30 Ha7i wode daro diikko kushe ekkontaynne yiza wode qasse medhina deyo ekkontay oonikka deenna gides.
LUK 18:31 Yesussaykka bena kaalliza tammanne nam77anta dumma efidi ha7i nuni Yerusaleme kezana goos, nabeti asa na gish xaafidaysi wuri polistana.
LUK 18:32 Dere asas aathi immana, istikka iza qidhi ka77ananne waysana, iza bolla cuttana
LUK 18:33 garafana hessafekka zaaridi wodhana. Izikka heezzantho gallas hayqqoppe dendana gides.
LUK 18:34 Iza kaallizayti gidikko hessa wursofe isinoka eribeyttenna. Iza guussaykka istafe gemettides. Izi aaza gish hasa7idaakkonne eribeyttenna.
LUK 18:35 Yesussay Yarko gizaso matida wode issi qooqe addey oge duunan uttidi woossishe dees.
LUK 18:36 Qooqe addezzikka daro asay ogera aadhdhizaysa siyidi hessi aazzee? gi oychchides.
LUK 18:37 Isttikka izas Naazirete Yesussay hayssara aadhdhes giidi yootida.
LUK 18:38 Izikka Dawite na Yesussa taas qadhetta gi wassides.
LUK 18:39 Yesussappe sintheti bizaytti c7o7uga giidi hanqqettida. gido attin izi Dawite no taas qadhetta giidi darisi waassidees.
LUK 18:40 Yesussaykka eqqidi addezza izakko ehanna mala azaziddes, izikka izakko shiiqida wode
LUK 18:41 ta nees ay oothanna mala koyay giidi oychchides. Qooqezikka Godo xeellanaas koyays gides.
LUK 18:42 Yesussaykka nena ne amanoy pathides xeella gides.
LUK 18:43 Addezzikka heerakka xeellidees. Xoossakka bonchishshe Yesussa kaallidees. Hessa beydda derey wuri Xoossa galattides.
LUK 19:1 Yesussay Iyarko giza sora aadhdhi bishin
LUK 19:2 Zakosa geetettiza issi assi he Yesussay biza oge bolla dees. Izikka dere qaraxa qanxisizaytas halaqqanne keehi dure asa.
LUK 19:3 Izikka Yesussa geetettizaysi awayssakkonne beyanas koyishin qaantha asa gidida gishinne daro derey Yesussa kaalliza gish Yesussa beyanas dandd7ibeynna.
LUK 19:4 Yesussay he ogera aadhdhishin sinthe qaxidi oge bolla diza issi etha miththa bolla kezides.
LUK 19:5 Yesussay etha gars gakidi dhoqqu histi xeellidi Zakosa hach ta ne keeththan pe7anaas besses elella wodha gides.
LUK 19:6 Izikka elle wodhidi ufaysan mokki ekkidees.
LUK 19:7 He wode heen izara diza asay hessa beyidi nagarancha asa keeththan imatistana gees giidi wurikka garsara zuzumettida.
LUK 19:8 Gido attin Zakosay eqqidi Godo tani taas diza miishshe wursofe baga shaakkada manqqotas immana tani oonappekka wordora bonqqa ekkidaazzi diikko oyddu kushe gujjada izades immanna gides.
LUK 19:9 Yesussaykka ha uraykka Abrame na gidida gish hach ha keethas paxatethi yides gides.
LUK 19:10 Haysas gaassoykka asa nay haa yidaysi dhayidayssa koyanasinne ashanassa.
LUK 19:11 Asay hayssa siyishin leemusora haasa7a oykkides gaassoykka izi Yerusaleme gakkanaas matida gishine asatas Xoossa kawotethi qonccanna hanza milattida gishassa.
LUK 19:12 Hessa gish issi kawo nay ba kawotetha shuumeteth ekki yanas haaho biitta biddes.
LUK 19:13 Be ashkarata giddofe tammata xeeygidi tamu minnane istas immidi, ta simadda yaana gakanas hayssa miishshan zal7ite gides.
LUK 19:14 He dere asati qasse iza ixxida gish haysi addezzi nu bolla kawotana mala koyokko giidi iza geedora aathi yedida.
LUK 19:15 Gido attin ha kawo naazi kawo gididi guye ba dere simmides. Kase bishe tamu minnane immida tamu ashkkarati izi immida biran zal7idi woysa tirfisidakkonne eranas ista xeeygidees.
LUK 19:16 Istafe koyroy shiiqidi Godo ne taas immida tamu minnaney hara tamu yelides gides.
LUK 19:17 Godazikka iza ne amanettida ashkkara, lo7o oothadassa, ne guutha miishshan amanettida gish tamu katamata ne haarana mala nees immadis gides.
LUK 19:18 Nam77anthozika izakko shiiqqidi Godo ne taas immida minnaneppe hara ichachu minnaney wodhides gides.
LUK 19:19 Iza Godazi izas zaaridi neni aysana mala tamu katamati nees imettida gides.
LUK 19:20 Qassekka hara oothanchay shiiqqidi Godo neni wothontasoppe ekkizadde zerontasoppe maxizaddenne menxxe iita asa gidida gish ta nees babbada curqan xaaxxa wothida ne minnaneyo hey ekka gides.
LUK 19:22 Iza Godazi zaaridi izas hayso iita oothanchazo ta ne qaalan nena zaara pirdays. Tani wothontasoppe ekkizaddenne zerontasoppe maxxiiza menxe iita asa gididaysa erasashin tani ta miishsha yelora ekkana mala he miishshan oothanna asatas aazas immabeyki gides.
LUK 19:24 Iza Godazikka heen eqqida asata iza kusheppe minnaneza ekkidine tamu minnaney dizaysas immite gides.
LUK 19:25 Istika zaaridi Godo izas tamu minnaney deesko gida.
LUK 19:26 Izikka zaaridi diza uras wursos haray gujjistana, bayndda uras kase dizaysi izappe eketti gidanna gido attin tani ista bolla kawotonta mala koyidayta hayta ta morketa taakko haa ehidi ta sinthan shukkite gides.
LUK 19:28 Hessa haasa7i simmidi Yesussay Yerusaleme kezanas istafe sintheti biddes.
LUK 19:29 Dabre zayite geetettiza zuma bolla diza Beettefaggenne Bittaanya geetettiza katamatakko matida wode bena kaallizaytappe nam77anta kiittishe heen inte sinthan diza qeeri katama biitte biiddi katama inte gelishin oonikka toggi eronta issi qachcheti diza hare gutte inte demmna iza birshidi haa taas ekki yite, intena oonikka aazas birsheti giidi oychchikko Godas koshes gite gides.
LUK 19:32 kiitetidaytikka biidi izi istas yoottida mala hare gutteza demmida.
LUK 19:33 Isti gutteza birshin gutteza Godati beyidi aazas birshetti giidi oychchida.
LUK 19:34 Istika Godas koshshees gida.
LUK 19:35 Hare gutteza Yesussako ehidi ba mayo wurissi gutteza bolla yegidi Yesussa hare gutteza togisida.
LUK 19:36 Asay wurikka ba afala Yesussay biza oge bolla miccidees.
LUK 19:37 Dabre zayite zuma bollara dugeth wothiza ogezakko matida wode qooday bayndda derey ba beydda malaata gish wurikka ufaysara ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi Goda sunthan yiza kawoy anjjettidaysa, saroy salon bonchoy saloppe bolla salon gido gides.
LUK 19:39 Deretappe issi issi Farsaweti Yesussa tamaarsizayso ha nena kaalliza asay gizaysa gonta mala hanqqa gides.
LUK 19:40 Izikka istas zaaridi hayti co7u gidakkonne shuuchchatikka waassana gides.
LUK 19:41 Yesussay Yerusaleme matishe katama beyidi izis yekides. nees saro gidizaz hach ne eridakko aazze dizayishin ha7i ne ayfeppe qotettida gish ne morkketi heera haara nena giddoothidi kun7isana wodey yaana gides.
LUK 19:44 Nenanne ne gibbe garsan nenara diza ne nayta wurssi biittara walakkana. Shuuchcha bolla shuuchchikka aggettenna. Hessi wurikka Xoossi nena koyishin neni eronta aggida gishassa.
LUK 19:45 Hessafe kaallidi Yesussay maqddase gelidi maqddase giddon zal7izayta kessides.
LUK 19:46 Qassekka ta keethay woossa keeththa gidanna geetettidi xaafettidees, inteni gidiko pangazi diza gonggollo histiddista gides.
LUK 19:47 Wontin wontin maqddasen izi tamaarishin Xaafetinne dere halaqqati iza wodhanaas koyida.
LUK 19:48 Gido attin derey wurikka izara oykettidi izi tamarsizaysa kaalliza gish oothanaazi istas kirq gides.
LUK 20:1 Issi gallas Yesussay dere asa maqddasen tamaarsishinne miishrachcho qaala sabbakishin qeese halaqqati Xaafetine dere cimati shiiqqettidi izakko yida.
LUK 20:2 Haysa ne oothizay oona shenenee? Nees shene immiday oonee? giidi iza oychchida.
LUK 20:3 Izikka istas hizgides taka intena issi oychcho oychchays, ane taas zaarite.
LUK 20:4 Yanisa xinqatay saloppeeye asappee?
LUK 20:5 Istika ba garsan hizgidi issay issara zorettida “nu Yanisa xinqatay salope giikko nuna histini aazas amanibbeykkettii? gaana.
LUK 20:6 Asappe giiko asay wuri Yanisay nabe gididaysa amanizza gish nuna shuuchchara caddana.
LUK 20:7 Hessa gish izi awappekkonne nu erokko giidi zaarida.”
LUK 20:8 Yesussaykka histtikko taka aaza wolqan oothizakonne intes yotikke gides.
LUK 20:9 Qassekka Yesussay asas leemusora hizgidi yoottidees. Issi uray woyne mith tokides, biitta goyizaytas kira immidinne hara dere biiddi heen gam7ides.
LUK 20:10 Kaxxiza bone wode kaththafe ekki yaana mala ba ashkkaratappe issi ura gadezza goyida asatakko yediin gada goyizayti kiita bida ashkkara qoxxidi mela kushe yedida.
LUK 20:11 Kaalethidi hara ashkkara yedin goshshanchati ha7ikka oykki qoxxidinne kawishidi mela yedida.
LUK 20:12 Ha7ikka kaalethidi heezantho ashkkara yedin goshshanchati izakka qoxxethi madunthidi gede kare olida.
LUK 20:13 Woyne miththa Goday ha7i ay oothoo? Oone erizayta keeha siiqiza ta naaza yedidakko iza bonchandettoshshaa? gides.
LUK 20:14 Gido attin biitta goyizayti naza beyddamala ba garsan haysi iza laatana naaza gidennee? Haa yite iza wodhidi biitta laattos giidi zorettida.
LUK 20:15 Woyne miththa tookkida sooppe gede kare kessidi naaza wodhida. Histtikko ha7i woyne miththa Goday ha asata wostanee?
LUK 20:16 Yiidine he goshshanchata dhaysana woyne miththa tookkizassoza haratas immana. Dereykka hessa izi gidayssa siyidi hayssa malay hanoppo gides.
LUK 20:17 Yesussaykka istakko xeellidi “histini shuuchchan keeth keexiza asati leqqi aggida shuuchchay keethas waana hu7e gidees geetetidi Xaafettida leemusozas birshethay aazzee?” gides.
LUK 20:18 Ha shuchcha bolla kundiday wuri shuuchchan qoxxettana shuuchchaykka iza bolla wedhida uray wurikka liiqqana.
LUK 20:19 Xaafetine qeese halaqqati hessi leemusozi ista bolla haasa7ettidaysa eridi heerakka iza oykkanas koyida shin derezas babida.
LUK 20:20 Yesussa wolqara haarizaytas aathi immanas iza duunappe keziza bala qaala demmida oykanas kaalli kaalli naagidanne xillo asa milattida iza kaallidi iza duunappe yo naagiza asata izakko yedida.
LUK 20:21 Iza duunappe yo koyiza asati Yesussa astamaare neni tuma haasa7izaysanne tamaarsizaysa qassekka Xoossa oge ne tumu tamaarsizaysane oonakka shaakka maadontaysa nu eroos.
LUK 20:22 Gido attin qeesares giira giiranas bessize bessenne?
LUK 20:23 Izikka ista gene qofa eridi hizgides,
LUK 20:24 ane issi dinnare tana beessite, haysi iza bolla diza medhaynne Xaafezi oonayisee? Istika qeesareysa gida.
LUK 20:25 Izikka zaaridi istas qeesareysa qeesares Xoossisa Xoossassi immite gides.
LUK 20:26 Hessa gish iza haasa7ida qaalappe ekkidi asa sinthan iza qaxanas dand7ibeyitenna izi immida qaalan malaletidi co7u gida.
LUK 20:27 Hayqqidayta denthi baawa giza Saduqawistappe issi issi asati Yesussako yiidi oychcho shiishshida.
LUK 20:28 Godo issi uray machcho ekkidi na yelontta hayqqikko he hayqqidaysa machchiyo iza ishay ekkidi ba isha laatana na izas yelo giidi Musey nuus xaafidees
LUK 20:29 Histini laappun ishati deetes shin istafe bayray machchidi na yelonta hayqqides.
LUK 20:30 Iza kaalozikka izatho hayqqides,
LUK 20:31 Heezanthozikka izo ekkidees, laappunati wurikka he maccashiyo ekkidi wurikka na yelonta hayqqida.
LUK 20:32 Wursethan maccashiya hayqqadus.
LUK 20:33 Laappunatikka ha maccashiyo ekkida shin ha maccashiya wursethan hayqqidayti dendiza wode iza awayssa machcho gidanee?
LUK 20:34 Yesussay istas ha dere nayti geleetesinne eekketees.
LUK 20:35 Buro yaana alamen hayqqidayta dentha demmnas bessizayti gidikko gelettenanne ekettena.
LUK 20:36 Isti kiitanchata mala gidana gish hessafe guye hayqqetenanne hayqoppe dentha nayta gidida gish isti Xoossa nayta.
LUK 20:37 Musey qeeri wora gish xaafettida tarikezan Goda “Abrame Xoossa Yisaqa Xoossa Yaqobe Xoossa” gussan hayqqidayti denddanaysa besses.
LUK 20:38 Wurikka izas deyo gidida gish izi paxxata Xoossafe attin hayqqethata xoossu gidenna.
LUK 20:39 Issi issi Xaafeti astamaare lo7o gadasa gida.
LUK 20:40 Hessafe guye ay assikka iza oychchanas xaalibeynna.
LUK 20:41 Hessafe guye Yesussay hizgides asay Yesussa waanidi izi Dawite na gizee?
LUK 20:42 Gaasoykka Dawitey ba xaafida mazmure maxaafatan “ta ne morketa ne tohos yedheth kessana gakkanaas Goday ta Goda ta oshachchan utta” waanidi gidee?
LUK 20:44 Histtikko Dawitey iza Goda gi xeygishe waani izas na gidanee?
LUK 20:45 Derey wuri siyishin bena kaallizaytas
LUK 20:46 goochchetiza adusa qamse mayidi yuushe dosizaytappene giyay dizason sarokketteth koyizaytapenne mukuraben dhoqqa oydenne, diggisa son boncho so koyizaytappe Xaafistappe naagetite.
LUK 20:47 Haytanti am7ista keeth kalosizayta. assi beyana mala woosa adusetes hayta iita firday naages. gides.
LUK 21:1 Yesussay dhoqqu gi xeellishin dure asati maqddasen muxaata shiishshizaysa giddon muxaata yeggishni beydees.
LUK 21:2 Qassekka issi am77i maccash dizara nam77u sikkina gidiza nam77u xarqqimala he muxaata shiishshizaysani yegishni xeellides.
LUK 21:3 Ta intes tumu gays hanna am7eya wurso asappe bollara aadhdheth immadus gides.
LUK 21:4 Hayti asati immiday bees diza tirpafe gidishin iza gidikko bees bayndda woliqqafe bees dizaznne ba duusas koshiza ubbaa yeggadus
LUK 21:5 Iza kaallizaytappe issi issi asati maqddasey lo7o shuuchchanne asay shiiqidi shiishshida miishshan aymala lo7i keexettidakkonne ba garsan haasa7etishn Yesussay haysi inte beyizzays wuri laletonta shuuchchi shuuchcha bolla keelettidamala attontta wodey yaana gides.
LUK 21:7 Istika iza tamaarsizayso haysi wuri aydde hanannee? Qasse haysi hananayisas malaatay aazze? gidi oychchida.
LUK 21:8 Izikka istas inte balettontta mala naagetite daroti bena ta kirstossakko, wodeykka matides gishe ta sunthara yaana shin inte ista kaalopite gides.
LUK 21:9 Ola gishinne dere makal7atetha gish siyiza wode daggamoppite. Hessi wuri kasetidi hananas besses, wursethi gakides heerakka hanena.
LUK 21:10 Qassekka hizgides derey dere bolla kawoy kawo bolla dendana
LUK 21:11 Biittay wolqama qaath qaaxana koshayne bochay dumma dumma son hanana daro babissizazne saloppe giita malaatay beettanna.
LUK 21:12 Hessi wuri hananappe kassetidi asay intena oykananne goodana mukurabene woyne keeth gelthana kawota sinthene daannata sinthe shishshanna. Hessi wuri ta suntha gish inte bolla gakana.
LUK 21:13 Hessi wurikka markkattanna lo7o qaada gidana.
LUK 21:14 Hessa gish nuna oychizaytas ay zaarinoo? giidi kassetidi hirggonta mala hayssa wozinan wothite,
LUK 21:15 Iintenara eqettizayti wuri izara eqistanasinne balethannas dandda7onta qaalane cincateth ta intes immana.
LUK 21:16 Intena yelidaytine inte ishati inte dabbotine inte laggeti wuri intena aathi immana, intefe baggatta wodhana.
LUK 21:17 Ta suntha gish wurso asa achchan inte ixistana.
LUK 21:18 Gido attin inte hu7e ithikistappe issinaka dhayuku.
LUK 21:19 Inte minni eqqikko inte shemppo inte ashsha na.
LUK 21:20 Ola asay Yerusaleme giddothishin beyikko izis dhayiza wodey matidaysa erite.
LUK 21:21 He wode Yihudani dizayti pude zuma bolla ganggetto kataman dizaytikka katamappe kezite, dere garssan dizaytikka heen ne katama gelopetto.
LUK 21:22 xaafettidays wuri polistanas hanna halo kessiza wode.
LUK 21:23 Biitta bolla gita metoy hanana hayssa dereza bolla hanqoy yaana hessa gish hessa wode qanthara diza maccashshiyo taasne dhanthiza aayetas hirchchi.
LUK 21:24 Mashsha hayqana ba dereppe hara dere di7istana Yerusalemeykka Xoossi eronta dereta wodey polistana gakkanaas Xoossi eronta asatan yedhettidaro gidana.
LUK 21:25 Awa arshe bolla aginna bollanne xollinte bolla malaatay beettanna. Abbafenne abba danbala giirethafe denddidaysani biitta bolla diza derey hirgananne metotistana.
LUK 21:26 Salo wolqamati qaxxiza gish asay biitta bolla aazze hanannesha gussaninne naagon xalla daabburana.
LUK 21:27 Hessa wode asa nay wolqarane gita bonchoranne shaarara yishin beyana.
LUK 21:28 Intekka hayti ha ta gidayti poletethi oykishn intes attotethay matida gish sit gi eqqite inte ayfe pude dhoqqu histite.
LUK 21:29 Kaallethidi ethinne hara miththata wurissi xeellite he miththati haythe kesishin inte beyizza wode bone matidaysa inte ereista.
LUK 21:31 Neysathokka haytanti geetettidayti poletishn inte beyizza wode Xoossa kawotethi inteko matidaysa erite.
LUK 21:32 Ta intes tumu gays haysi wuri polistana gakanas ha yellistay aadhdhenna.
LUK 21:33 Saloynne sa7ay aadhdhanna shin ta qaalay aadhdhenna.
LUK 21:34 Histtikko woggay bayndda duusan daro ushanne duusas hirgan inte wozinay daaburonta mala he gallasay inte qopponta narxamala inte bolla gakonta mala naagetite.
LUK 21:35 Haysi biitta bollan diza asa wurso bolla gakana.
LUK 21:36 Hessa gish buro yaanayisafe inte kessi ekkanamalane asa na sinthan eqqanas dandda7ana mala wurso gallas minnidi woosite.
LUK 21:37 Yesussay gallas gallas maqddassen tamaarsi tamaarsidi omars omars Dabre zayite geetettiza zuma bolla kezi kezi aqees.
LUK 21:38 Asay wurikka izappe siyanaas maalado wonttara Yesussako maqddase yetees.
LUK 22:1 Hessa wode paaziga geetettiza ukeethara bonchiza baaley mati uttides.
LUK 22:2 Qeeseta halaqqattinne Xaafeti hankko dere asa babbiza gish Yesussa dhaysana oge koyida.
LUK 22:3 Yesussa kaalliza tammanne nam77antappe asqqoroto biitta asa Yihuda geetettizaysan xalla7ey gelidees.
LUK 22:4 Yihudaykka qeeseta halaqqatakkonne maqddase alafistakko biiddi istas Yesussa wosit aathi immanakkonne istara haasa7ettidees.
LUK 22:5 Istika hessani ufa7ettidi miishshe immana mala izara giigida.
LUK 22:6 Yihudaykka ista qofa dossidees, Yesussa istas assi beyontta aathi immanas giiga wode naagishn faaziga dorssa shukkiza ukeethara bonchiza baale gallas gakkides.
LUK 22:8 Yesussaykka bena kaallizayta faaziga ka7o maanas biiddi nuus giigissite giidi Phexirosane Yanisa kiittidees.
LUK 22:9 Istika nu awan giigissana mala koyay gida.
LUK 22:10 Izikka zaaridi inte gede Yerusalemenne katama gelishin haatha oto tookkida assi intena demmna, intekka izi biiddi geliza keeth gakanas iza kaalite.
LUK 22:11 Keethadezas astamaarey tana kaallizaytara faaziga ka7o maanas imatha keethi awan dizee? gees gite.
LUK 22:12 Izikka imathas giigettida aaho so bessana izi bessiza son giigissite gides.
LUK 22:13 Istika biiddi Yesussay gida mala keeththa demmida faaziga heen giigissida.
LUK 22:14 Wodey gakida mala Yesussay hawaristara quma maaddan uttidi ta waaye beyanappe kasettada hayssa faaziga intenara issife maanas keeththa amotadis gides.
LUK 22:16 Ta intes tumu gays Xoossa kawotethan hayssa birshethi polistana gakanas hayssa faaziga nam77antho intenara miikke.
LUK 22:17 Woyneppe oothettida ushsha xu7ara ekkidine Xoossa galati simmidi heyite wurikka izappe uyite giidi istas immidees.
LUK 22:18 Ta intes tumu gays hayssappe guye Xoossa kawotethi yaana gakanas nam77antho ha woyne ushshafe uyikke gides.
LUK 22:19 Ukeetha ekkidi Xoossa galattides. Izappe istas menthi immidi haysi inte gish imistana ta asho leemuso gidiza gish hayssa wurso wode tana qoppanas oothite gides.
LUK 22:20 Izathokka ka7oppe guye ushsha xu7a denthidi haysi ushshay inte gish ta suthan wodhdhana oorath caaqqo woga gides.
LUK 22:21 Gido attin tana aathi immana ura kushey ta kushera issife maaddan dees.
LUK 22:22 Asa nay kasettidi iza gish wuri uttida mala izi baana gido attin iza aathi immiza uras ayye.
LUK 22:23 Istika hessa oothannay oonee? giidi ba garsan issay issa oycherethida.
LUK 22:24 Qassekka ooni oonappe aadhdhizakkonne gidi ba garsan issay issara palamettida.
LUK 22:25 Yesussaykka ista dere haariza kawoti ba dere asa wolqara haaretesinne istikka lo7o kawota geettetidi xeygettetees.
LUK 22:26 Inte gidikko hessaththo hanoppite intefe gita gidida uray woykko ta ooppeka aadhdhays giza uray wursofe qeeri na mala haarizaddey haarettizade mala hano.
LUK 22:27 Quma eqqidi muzizaddefene uttidi mizaddefe ooni aadhdhizzee? Uttidi mizaadde gidennee? Tani qasse inte garsan issi ashkkara mala days.
LUK 22:28 inteni gidikko tappe shaaketonta ta wayishin ta matan eqqidayta.
LUK 22:29 Ta aaway tana kawothidaysa mala tanikka ta kawotethan intena kawothana.
LUK 22:30 Hessika ta kawotethan ta maaddafe inte maana malane uyana mala qassekka ta kawotetha algan uttidi tammanne nam77u Isra7ele nayta bolla firdanassa.
LUK 22:31 Qassekka Yesussay Simona xeeygidi Simona xalla7ey intena gistte mala suraggaanas woossidees gides.
LUK 22:32 Gido attin tani neppe amanoy dhayontta mala ne gish Xoossa woossadissi nekka simmida wode ne ishata minnithetha.
LUK 22:33 Simonaykka zaaridi Godo ta nenara woyne wodhanasinne hayqqanas giiga uttadis gides.
LUK 22:34 Yesussaykka zaaridi Phixirosa hach kuttoy issi to wassa naas ta iza erikke gaada heezu to ne tana kaddana gides.
LUK 22:35 Qassekka Yesussay ista ta intena kase caammayne korojoynne qaraxite bayndda kititida wode intes aazzee pacidee? giidi oychchidees. Istika aykkoykka pacibeyna gida.
LUK 22:36 Izikka zaaridi ha7i gidikko korojokka qaraxiteykka diza uray oykko githa mashshay baynddaddey ba mayo bayziddi shammo gides.
LUK 22:37 Ta intes tuma gays makal7atara izi issife paydettides geetetti kase xaafetida qaalay ta bolla polistana besses, ta gish xaafettiddaysas poloy tumappe gakides gides.
LUK 22:38 Iza kaallizayti qasse Godo hekko nam77u githa mashshati hayssan deetes gida. Izikka iza gish haasa7ay gidana.
LUK 22:39 Kase izas dose gidida mala pude Dabrezayite giza zuma bolla kezi biddes. Iza kaallizaytikka iza kaalli bida.
LUK 22:40 Hee gakida mala inte paacen gelonta mala woossite gides.
LUK 22:41 Yesussay bena kaallizaytappe assi shuchch halidi gathanaso mala haakkibiidi gulbati woossides.
LUK 22:42 Aabo ne shene gidikko hano metiyo tappe digga gido attin ne sheney hanoppe attin ta sheney hanoppo giidi wossidees.
LUK 22:43 Saloppe kiitanchay qonccidi Yesussa minnithethidees.
LUK 22:44 Izikka keehi xugetidi woossishin iza asatethafe caway sutha mala gukkides.
LUK 22:45 Woossappe dendidi iza kaallizaytakko biddes. Istika izas michchetidi qoppishin dhiskkoy efidashe Yesussay istakko yiidi,
LUK 22:46 ays dhiskketi? inte paacen gelonta mala ha7i denddidi woossite gides.
LUK 22:47 Izi buro haasa7ani dishin Yesussa kaallizaytappe issay Yihuda geetettizays benara daro asa kaalethi ekki yiidi Yesussa yeranas izakko shiiqqidees.
LUK 22:48 Gido attin Yesussay iza Yihuda tana asa na yeron aatha imaaz gides.
LUK 22:49 Yesussa yuuyi aadhdhi diza asay hanoza lo7ethi xeellidi Godo haytanta mashara buthinnoo? gida.
LUK 22:50 Istafe issay qeeseta alafe ashkkara oshachcha haythe mashara qanxxides.
LUK 22:51 Yesussay ista inte ha7i taas aggitte gidi ashkkara haytha bochchiddi pathides.
LUK 22:52 Qassekka iza oykkana yida qeeseta halaqqata maqddase alafettanne cimata “pangga oykiza asa mala githa masha ne durqqa ekkidi yidetii?
LUK 22:53 Gallas gallas ta intenara maqddasen dishin ta bolla kushe wothibeykkista, haysi dhumay kawottida inte wode” gides.
LUK 22:54 Hessafe guye Yesussa oykki ekkida qeeseta halaqqa gaath gelida, Phexirosaykka Yesussa hahora kaallidees.
LUK 22:55 Asay qeeseta halaqqa gaathan tama eethidi ho7ishe issi bolla uttidashe Phexirosaykka istara issife uttidees.
LUK 22:56 Issi garadeya Phexirosay tama ho7izaytara uttidaysa beyadane tishsh ootha xeellada haysi addezzikka Yesussara diza asa gadus.
LUK 22:57 Phexirosaykka hanne maccashaye ta iza erikke giidi kadidees.
LUK 22:58 Guuthu gam7ishin hara issi uray iza beyidi nekka izara dizaytappe issa gidikii gides. Phexirosaykka hayso tani istara diikke gides.
LUK 22:59 Issi sate mala gam7ishin hara uray qassekka Galila asa gidiza gish sidhey bayndda haysi izara dees gides.
LUK 22:60 Phexirosayka qasse hayso ne gizadde ta erikke gides. Hinno gi kesonta dishin kuttoy u7udees.
LUK 22:61 Godayka Phixirosakko yishe xeellin Phexirosay hach kuttoy u7anas ne tana heezu to kadana giidi Goday kase yooto qaalay iza wozinan karp gides.
LUK 22:62 Phexirosaykka kare kezidi hiqumidi yekides.
LUK 22:63 Yesussa qachidi naagiza asatikka iza bolla qidhdhi qidhdhi ka7ishe shocerethida.
LUK 22:64 Iza ayfe goozidi ane ne nabe gidikkii nena shociday oonakoonee? Ane era gidi oychchida.
LUK 22:65 Hara daro cashsha qaalara kawishida.
LUK 22:66 Gadey wonttin dere cimati qeeseta halaqqattinne Muse woga tamaarsizayti duullata shiiqidi Yesussa duullatakko shiishida.
LUK 22:67 Istika Yesussa ne kirstossaa? Ane nuus yoota gida. Yesussaykka ta intes yoottiddakkokka tana amanekketta gides.
LUK 22:68 Ta intena oychchidakko taas zarekkista.
LUK 22:69 Gido attin ha7ippe oykkidi asa nay wolqama Xoossa oshachchan uttana gides.
LUK 22:70 He wode wurikka histini ne Xoossa naa? gidi oychchida. Izikka ta Xoossa na gididaysa intekka geista gides.
LUK 22:71 Istika hekko izi ba duunara markkatishn nu haythara siyidos hayssafe hara markka aazas koshize gida.
LUK 23:1 Heen shiiqida asay wuri denddidi Yesussa Philaxoossakko ekki bides.
LUK 23:2 Ays nu asay qeesares giira giironta mala balethishsheenne bena kirstossa giidi balethishin hayssa addezza demmidos giidi mootida.
LUK 23:3 Philaxoossaykka Yesussa neni Ayhuddista kawoo? giidi oychchides. Yesussaykka zaaridi ne gida mala gides.
LUK 23:4 Philaxoossaykka qeese halaqatasinne shiiqida asas hayssa addezza bolla iza mootisiza iita yoho demabeykke gides.
LUK 23:5 Isti zaaridi haysi addezzi Galilappe hayssa gakanas kumetha Yuda waayso bolla dees giidi minnithi yootida.
LUK 23:6 Philaxoossay asay gizaysa siyidi Yesussay Galila asakonne lo7ethi eranas oychchides.
