LUK 23:7 Yesussay Herdoossa kawotetha garsan dizayssa shaakki eridi he wode Herdoossay Yerusalemeni diza gish izakko Yesussa yeddides.
LUK 23:8 Herdoossayka kase Yesussa beyanas daro koyishe dizagish Yesussa beyidi keehi ufa7ides. Iza gish kase siyidi izi malaata oothishin beyanas koyidi ufa7ettides.
LUK 23:9 Daro oychchatakka iza oycherechchides shin Yesussay iza oychcha zaaribeyna.
LUK 23:10 Qeese halaqqattinne Xaafeti heen iza matan eqqidi keehi wordo mooto mootida.
LUK 23:11 Herdoossayka ba wotadaratara wuri iza kadhida, kawo mayo mayzidi gede Philaaxoossakko zaari yeddides.
LUK 23:12 Herdoossayne Philaxoossay kase ba garsan issay issara oosha shin he gallas giigida.
LUK 23:13 Philaxoossay qeese halaqqatara dere daannataranne dere asa shiishidi,
LUK 23:14 hayssa addezzi asa wurssi makkali7ana mala denthethes giidi inte taakko ehin ta qorin iza oythiza issi iita miish demabeykke gides.
LUK 23:15 Qassekka Herdoossay issi iita miish iza bolla demmonta aggida gish ha nuukko zaari yeddides. Ha7i inte beyizza mala iza hayqqos gathiza issi iita miish oothibeyna.
LUK 23:16 Hessa gish qaxayada ta iza yedana gides.
LUK 23:17 Izi hessa giday ista baale gallas qachettida asappe issi ura birshizza wogay diza gish.
LUK 23:18 Derey wurikka issi bolla Barbaanne birshadda hayssa addezza digga giidi wassides.
LUK 23:19 Barbaanney katama garssa asa makali7a yohon denthethidi asa wodhi qachettida asa.
LUK 23:20 Philaxoossaykka Yesussa birshanas koyida gish qassekka zaaridi oychchides.
LUK 23:21 Asay zeridi kaqqa kaqqa giidi wassides.
LUK 23:22 Philaxoossay heezantho aazas kaqqoo? Haysi addezzi ay iita oothidee? Tani iza hayqqos gathiza iita ootho iza bolla beyabeykke hessa gish qaxayada ta birsha yedana gides.
LUK 23:23 Asaykka qaala dhoqqu histtidi Yesussay kaqqistana mala Philaxoossa keehi woossishe wassida.
LUK 23:24 Hessa gish Philaxoossay ista oychchoy polistanamala azazides.
LUK 23:25 Asa makal7isidi shemppo wodhdhida gish qachchetidayssa birshanna mala isti woossida ura birshidi Yesussa isti dossida mala ootheto giidi deras aathi immides.
LUK 23:26 Istika Yesussa oykki ekki birshin Qarena geetettiza katamappe issi Simoona geetettiza addey hahoppe yizaysa demmida Yesussay kaqqistana masqale koca izi tookkidi Yesussa kaallana mala woliqqathida.
LUK 23:27 Daro dereynne ba tira ici ici yekkiza maccati
LUK 23:28 Yesussappe guyyera iza kaalida. Yesussay istakko simmi xeellidi inte Yerusaleme maccasay intesne inte naytas yekkite attin taas yekofite gides.
LUK 23:29 Sinthefe inte hekko makkarattine yelonta ulotine nay dhammonta dhanthati anjettidayta gaana wodey sinthara yees.
LUK 23:30 He wode zumato nu bolla wodite qeeri zumatikka nuna qottite gaana.
LUK 23:31 Histini qaye miththa bolla hayssatho oothidayti mela miththa bolla wostaneshaa?
LUK 23:32 Izara issife hayqqana mala hara nam77u iita oothida asata izara efida.
LUK 23:33 Qaraniyo geetettiza so gathidi kaqqida. Iita oothidaytappe issa oshacha baggara issa hadirissa baggara kaqqida.
LUK 23:34 Yesussaykka aabo hayti ba oothizaysa eridi ooothonta gish istas atto ga gides. Istika iza mayoza saama yegidi ba garssan gishetti ekkida.
LUK 23:35 Hessi hanshin asay wuri eqqidi xeellidees, daannatikka “izi hara asa ashshides shin Xoossafe dorettida kirstossay iza gidikko ane ha7i bena asho” giidi qidhida.
LUK 23:36 Wotadaratikka shiiqidi woyneppe aggettidda caalla usha ushidi qidhida.
LUK 23:37 Neni Ayhudde kawo gidikki ane ha7i nena ashsha gida.
LUK 23:38 Iza hu7e bolla baggara masqale koca bolla “haysi Ayhuddista kawo” giza qaala xaafi qaaphida.
LUK 23:39 Iita oothidi kaqqetida asatappe issay cashsha qaala Yesussa bolla qoqqofides. “ne kirstossa gidikii? ane nenaka nunakka ashsha” gides.
LUK 23:40 Iita oothidaytappe issay nees bessiza firda ekkashe Xoossassi babbikkii?
LUK 23:41 Nuni nu oothida iita oothos bessizaysa ekkos haysi addezzi gidikko issi iita oothibeyna.
LUK 23:42 Yesussa ne kawotethara ne yiza wode tana qoppa gides.
LUK 23:43 Yesussaykka zaaridi ta nees tumu gays hach ne tanara gannaten daana gides.
LUK 23:44 Hessa wode gadey seeta gallas shin biiddi udufun saate gakanas wurso biitta bolla dhummidees.
LUK 23:45 Awa arshe poo7oy digettides. Maqddase maggarajaykka daajkketidi nam77u kezides.
LUK 23:46 Yesussaykka keehi wassidi aabo ta shemppo ne kushen immays gida mala shemppo kezides.
LUK 23:47 Xeetu wotadarata halaqqay hessa beyidi “haysi addezzi tumappe xillo asakoshin” giidi Xoossa galatides.
LUK 23:48 Hessa beyanas heen shiiqidi derey wuri he hanidaysa beyidi tira ici icidi simmida.
LUK 23:49 Gido attin Yesussa kase lo7ethi erizayti wuri qassekka Galilappera iza kaalliza maccashati hessa xellishe haakki eqqida.
LUK 23:50 Ayhuddista duulata asappe issay izikka Yosefo geetettiza issi daro keehanne xillo asa.
LUK 23:51 Izikka kase asay Yesussa bolla duulatishn he duulatan deenna. Izikka issi Armattiyaasa geetettiza Ayhuddista katama asa shin Xoossa kawotethi yanayisa naagishe gam7ides.
LUK 23:52 Izikka Philaaxoossakko biiddi Yesussa anha immana mala Philaxosa woossidees.
LUK 23:53 Philaxoossay izas ero gin Yosefoy anha masqale kocappe wothida mala xaaxxidi shuchchafe woocettida kase haray moogetonta duufon efidi wothides.
LUK 23:54 He gallassay asay sanbbatas giigettiza gallas sanbbatay gelana hanes.
LUK 23:55 Galilappe dendidi Yesussara yida maccashatikka Yosefo kaalli biiddi duufoza beydda. Yesussa anha wosit wothidakoone xellida.
LUK 23:56 Heepe simmidi shittoone tiyiza miish giiggissida. Woggay giza mala sanbbata gallas shemppida.
LUK 24:1 Wogga wonta maaladora maccashati ba giigissida shitto ekkidi Yesussa wothida duufokko bida.
LUK 24:2 Shuchchaykka duufoza duunappe genderidi dizaysa beydda.
LUK 24:3 Gido attin giddo gelidi Yesussa anha demmonta aggida gish
LUK 24:4 istas hanzaazi dhayn jalidashe isti qopponta xoliqqettiza mayo mayida nam77u asati ista achchan eqqida.
LUK 24:5 Maccashatikka keehi babbidi duge biitta xeellishin he asati paxxidi dendidaysa hayqqethata garsan ays koyetii gida.
LUK 24:6 Izi dendidees! haan baawa, qassekka izi Galilan dishe intes kase ay gidakonne haasa7ite.
LUK 24:7 Asa nay nagaranchata kushen aadhdhi imistanasinne kaqqistanas, hayqoppekka heezantho gallas dendanas besses giidi yooti wothides.
LUK 24:8 Macasatikka hessa wode kase izi gida qaala haasa7ida.
LUK 24:9 macasati duufosoppe simmidi hessa wurssi Yesussa kaalliza tammanne issinistasnne haratas yoottida.
LUK 24:10 Hessaka hawaristas yoottiday Magidele gizasooppe yida Maaramoone Yohaano geetettizarira Yaqoobe Maaramoone istara issife diza hara maccashista.
LUK 24:11 Gido attin isti macasati yootidays agumo milatin amanibeyitenna.
LUK 24:12 Gido attin Phixiroossay wothan Yesussa duufokko gakkidinne hokkidi duufo giddo xeellishin iza anha xaaxxida mayoy xalla dizaysa beyidi keehi malaletishe beso simmides.
LUK 24:13 He gallas iza kaallizaytappe nam77ati Yerusalemeppe tammanne issi kilomitire hamuthiza Emmahose giza katama beettes.
LUK 24:14 Bishe isti he wode hanida Yesussa hayqqo gish ba garsan haasa7eteettees.
LUK 24:15 Isti haasa7etishin Yesussay istakko shiiqidi istara issife bishin,
LUK 24:16 isti iza erontamala ista ayfey oykettidees.
LUK 24:17 Yesussay ista haysi oge hamutishe inte inte garsan haasa7etizaysi aazze gides. Istika dagamaara muzotishe sit gi eqqaggida.
LUK 24:18 Ista garsafe issay Qaliyopha geetettizaysi zaaridi ha mata galassatan Yerusalemeni handaysa erontta imatha assi nena xallaa? gides.
LUK 24:19 Izikka istas zaaridi aazzi handee? gin isti qasse zaaridi Xoossa sinthanne wurso asa sinthan oothoonine qaalan minno nabe gidida Naazirete Yesussa gish gida.
LUK 24:20 Izaka qeeseta halaqqattinne daannati hayqqo firdassi aathi immidane kaqqida.
LUK 24:21 Nuni gidikko Isra7ele wozinay iza giidi ufa7ettidos shin harappe hessi hanin qasse hach heezantho gallasa.
LUK 24:22 Qasse nu giddofe issi issi maccashati nuna keehi malalisida istikka maalado wontara gede iza duufokko biiddi,
LUK 24:23 iza anhay beettontta ixxin yiidi izi paxxa dizaysa istas yootin kiitanchata beyddaysa nuus yoottida.
LUK 24:24 Nuppekka issi issi assi iza duufokko biidi maccashati gida mala beydda attin Yesussa demmibeyitenna.
LUK 24:25 Izikka istas inte wozinan wothontayto inte wozinay kase nabeti yootidaysa amananappe takkidayto.
LUK 24:26 Xoossafe kitettidays ha metoza ekkanasnne gede ba bonchoso gelanas besenne gides.
LUK 24:27 Museppene nabetappe doomidi xillo maxaafatan iza gish xaafetidayssa istas yooti gelthides.
LUK 24:28 Isti ba bizaso matida wode Yesussay aadhdhi biza milatides.
LUK 24:29 Istika qasse gadey qammiza gish nunara aqa giidi iza keehi woossin istara aqanas gelides.
LUK 24:30 Istara issife maaddan uttidi ukeeth ba kushen oykkidi istas menthi menthi immides.
LUK 24:31 Hessa wode ista ayfey qaaretin iza gididaysa erida, izikka ista ayfeppe geemides.
LUK 24:32 Istika nu yishe oge bolla dishin nuna haasa7isidi xillo maxaafatakka qoncisidi nuus gelanashe yootin nu wozinay tama mala xuugettibeynee? giidi issay issara haasa7ida.
LUK 24:33 Heeraka denddidi Yerusaleme simmi bida. Tammanne issinetinne istara issife dizaytikka issi bolla shiiqi dizayta demmida.
LUK 24:34 Istika ba garsan issay issas “Goday tumu denddidees! Simoonaskka beettidees” gida.
LUK 24:35 iza kaallizaytappe nam77ati oge bolla hanidayssane Yesussay ukeetha menthi menthi immidawode isti wosit eridakko istas yootida.
LUK 24:36 Hessa gish isti ba garsan haasa7etishin Yesussay ista giddon eqqidi saroy intes gido gides.
LUK 24:37 Gido attin isti moytil7e beydda milatin keehi dagammida.
LUK 24:38 Izikka istas aazas daro qoppetii? aazass inte wozinara sidheeti? gides.
LUK 24:39 Ta kushistanne ta tota haa xeellite tanakko, qassekka tana oyki beyite tana inte beyizzaysa mala moytil7es ashoynne meqethi deenna.
LUK 24:40 Iza gi simmidi ba tohotanne ba kushista ista beesides.
LUK 24:41 Istika ufaysa daroppenne malalletethafe denddidaysani buro amanontta dishin Yesussay hessani aykko mizaz dizee? giidi ista oychchides.
LUK 24:42 Istika mole xiixa issi bars izas immida.
LUK 24:43 Izikka ekkidi ista sinthan mides.
LUK 24:44 Izikka intenara ta diza wode Muse wogan nabetaninne mazmure maxaafatan ta gish xaafettidays wurikka polistanas besses gaada ta intes yoottida ta qaalay hayssakko gides.
LUK 24:45 He wode geeshsha maxaafata isti erana mala wozina istas doyidees.
LUK 24:46 Istaskka kirstossay waaye beyana heezantho gallas hayqqoppe denddana geetettidi xaafetidees gides.
LUK 24:47 Yerusalemeppe doomidi wurso deres naggarappe simoynne maarotethi iza sunthan yootettana.
LUK 24:48 Intekka hayssas markkata gides.
LUK 24:49 Taka ta aaway immida ufaysa intes yeddana, inte qasse woliqqa bollafe mayana gakanas Yerusaleme kataman takkite.
LUK 24:50 Hessafe guye ista ekkidi Biittanya giza so kezides. Be kushistaka denthidi ista anjjides.
LUK 24:51 ista anjishshe istafe shaakettidi pude salo biddes.
LUK 24:52 Istika izas hokki goynnida, keehi ufa7etishe Yerusaleme simmida.
LUK 24:53 Wurso wode maqddasen Xoossa galatishe gam7ida.
JOH 1:1 Qaalay kasse koyro dees. Qallakka Xoossa achan dees. He qalaaykka Xoossa.
JOH 1:2 Izee koyro Xoossa achchan dees.
JOH 1:3 Medheteththi wurii izann medhetdes. Medhettdazan izi baynda medhetiday isiinaka dukku.
JOH 1:4 Deyooy ezann deyssu. hana deyooya asas poo7.
JOH 1:5 Poo77y dhumaan poo7ses. dhumayy poo7 muleeka xonena.
JOH 1:6 Xoossafe kiitetda Yanissa getettiza isadeey dess.
JOH 1:7 Iza markkatithaan asi wurii amanna malla Po77s markka giddii yidess.
JOH 1:8 Izi poo7o gish markatana yides atiin izi ba hues po7o gidena.
JOH 1:9 Asa wursoos po7o imiiza tumu poo7oy hayssa ha alamezan yusan dess.
JOH 1:10 Qaalayka kase alamen dess. almeykka medhetdday izana. Gido atin alameey iza erribeeyna.
JOH 1:11 Izi ba bagtako yiin iza bagaty iza ekiibetena.
JOH 1:12 Gido attin iza ekdaytii iza sunesaa amaniddayta isti xossa naytia gidana maata isstass iimdess.
JOH 1:13 Isttikka xossa nayta gididay xoossafe yelettida gish attin asa zeerethafe heskka asa wogan woykko asho shenen gidena.
JOH 1:14 Qaallayka ass giddies, Xossa kiyatethinne tumann kumidii nunaan aqqides, Isi nass awa matan diza bonchoo milatza iza booncho nu beydos.
JOH 1:15 Yanssaykka “tappe guyera yizaysi tafe adhees, gasooyka izi tape kaseka dess gada ta intees yotidaysi hekoo haysi izako” gii matatidess.
JOH 1:16 Iza kumetha kiyatethan nu wuri keyatetha bolla kiyateth ekkidos.
JOH 1:17 Wogay musse baggara immetidas, kiyatethine tumay gidiikoo Yesuss Kirsitosa baggara nusii yidess.
JOH 1:18 Xooss beyedaye oonnkka bawa, gido attin Xossa aawa matan diza xoossa na xoossay issay xalala iza qonccissidess.
JOH 1:19 Ayhudata dannatii Yerusalamappe qeessistane Lewe nayetta Yanssakoo kitidii “ne oonee?” gidi oychchishin,
JOH 1:20 Yanssay “tani Kiristtosa gidikee” gidi geshshi markkatides attin markkatanas ixxibeyna.
JOH 1:21 Isttika “histtine ne oonne? ne Elassa? gidi oychchida, izki gidike” gidi isttas zaaridess, Isttika “izi yana kittetida nabey nene?” gida. izika “akaye tana gidke” gidas.
JOH 1:22 Istii qaas “histin ne onee? nuna kitda asas nu yotanamalla ne nena ona gay?” gida.
JOH 1:23 Izika “nabe Isayasay yootidaysa mala tani xoossa ogge suriistte gishe bazoo biitann wasiizade qalla girethth” gidess.
JOH 1:24 parssawistappe kittettda issi issi asati
JOH 1:25 Hesa gish “ne Xoossi kittidade woykko buroo yana getetida nabaye nene gidontta gidikoo hstiin azaas nuna xmaqqazi?” gidii iza oychchida.
JOH 1:26 Yanssaykka istasi hzgidass “ta haththn xamaqqays gido atiin inte eroontadey inte giddon eqqides.
JOH 1:27 Tappe guyera yanaysi iza, ta iza ccama qachcho birshanass besizade gidikke.
JOH 1:28 Haysi wuri haniday Yanssay xamiqqiza Yordanosse shshafappe he pinththan diza Biitaniyaa getetiza katamana. Biitaniyay
JOH 1:29 “Wonteththa glass Yanissay Yasussay beeko yishshin beydi <deree nagara biitappe digana Xoossa doorssay hekko hysichchi!
JOH 1:30 Tapee guyerra yanayysi izi tappe kassekka diza gish tappe adhdhess> gada ta intess yotizzay haysichch!
JOH 1:31 Takaa ta bagaraa iza eraabeyke shin gidikooka izi Isra7ele deress qonchnamala ta haththan xxamaqashshe yadiss.”
JOH 1:32 Kaleththidika Yanissayy hizgi markatidess. “Xiiloo Ayanay woole kafoo milattdii salopee woodhishshinne iza bolla uttshin beyadiss.
JOH 1:33 Ta tabagara iza eriike shin ta haththan xmaqqanamalla tana kiitidadey <Xiilloo Ayanay iza bola wodhidi shempishshin nee beyanadey Xiiloo Ayanan meccnay izakko> gidii tas yoottidess.
JOH 1:34 Taka hessa beyadiss. Hessa gish izi Xoossa na gididaysa ta markatays.”
JOH 1:35 Wontetha galass Yanissay bena kaliza nam7atara heen eqqides.
JOH 1:36 Yesussay iza achchara adhdhishshn Yanissay beydii “Xoossa dorssay hekkoo haysichch!” gides.
JOH 1:37 Yanssa kalliza nam7ati hessa siiydii Yesussa kallida.
JOH 1:38 Istii iza kaliishshn yesussa guye yuuy xellidii “ayy kooyetii?” gidees. Istkka “asstamaare ne dussasoy awaa?” gida.
JOH 1:39 Izikka ista “ha ydii beyte” gidess. Hessa gish bidii izii awan dizakko be7idane he gllass izara isppe pe7ida. Wodeykka gedee tamuu sateso bidess.
JOH 1:40 Yanissay yotida qaala siydii Yesussa kallida nam7atappe issay Simoona Phixiroossa ishsha Indirassa.
JOH 1:41 Indirassay koyroo ba ishsha simoonakko bidinne “Xoossi kitida kirstossa nu demidos!.” gidess.
JOH 1:42 Hesafe guye Indirassay Simoona Yesussakko ekii yides. Yesussaykka iza tishsh hisiti xelidii. “hayso ne Yoonna na Simoonakko, hayssafe guye ne Keehaaththaa geetistana.” Kehaaththaa gusi Phixrossa gusa wyykoo zlaa shuchu gusa.
JOH 1:43 Wonteththa gallas Yesusay Galilla banass koydees. Piliphoosska demiidi “tana kalla” gidess.
JOH 1:44 Pilphoossaykka Indirasamalane Phixiroossamala Batesaydda kattama asa.
JOH 1:45 Piphoossay natina7ele demiidi “Mussey woga maxxafan qase nabetiikka burope hanana yotiza bee maxxafatann iza gish xafida adeza nuu demidos, izikka Yosefo na Nazirete Yesussakko” gides.
JOH 1:46 Natina7eley qass “Nazireteppe lo7o miishi beti erizee?” gi oychin Pilphossay iza “ha yada beya” gides.
JOH 1:47 Natina7eley Yesussa beyana yishin yesussay beydi iza “hekko geney bayndda tumu Isra77ele ass!” giidi iza gish yotidess.
JOH 1:48 Natina77eleykka zaridi “tana woosta eradii?” gi oychin Yesussaykka “Pilipoossay nena xeyiganappe kase Balasse miththa garsan ne dishshin ta nena beyaddis” gi zarin.
JOH 1:49 Natina77eleay “asstammarea! ne Xoossa na ne Israe77ele kawo” gides.
JOH 1:50 Yesussaykka izas “ne amaniiday ta neena baallass miththa garsan beyadis” gidagsshe? ne buro hessafe adhdhiza daro miish beyana.
JOH 1:51 Gujidikka ta intes tumu gays buro sallooy dooyetin Xoossa kiitanchati asa na bolla wdhishininne kezishin inte beyana.
JOH 2:1 Hedzdzantho galas Galillan garsan diza Qaana gettetizza Kataman sargey dees. Yesussa Ayeeyakka hen dawus.
JOH 2:2 Yesussayne iza kalizaytikka sargezaso xxeygetida.
JOH 2:3 Sargezason woynefe agida ushshayi wuriini Yesussa ayaa Yesussa “woyiine ushshayi wurdeskko” gaduss.
JOH 2:4 Yesussaykka izo “Ayye tass nenara azi dizze, ta woddeye gakiibeynakko gides”
JOH 2:5 He wode Yesussa ayeya Marama hen gadeezzan diza oothanchata “izi initena gizaaysa oththite” gadus.
JOH 2:6 Ayhudatas geshshoo wogayi diza gish usupuuni shuchchafe medhdhetiida gaanetti heen iza ollan dettes, isittikka issay issay nam77u otto wayeko hedzdzuu otto hathth oyikkes.
JOH 2:7 Yesussay oththanichchata “ganeetta heththe kuniithitte” gin isstikka ganetta duunna gakanas cip hisitti kunnththida.
JOH 2:8 Hassafe qassekka oththanichchate “anne ha7i duqqidi sargeza allafezas izappe duqqii imiite” gidesi. Istika duuqqi imiida.
JOH 2:9 Alaafeziikka wooynne ushchan lamettada haththa ganxxi xallidiine izi awappe yidakkonne eribeyna. Haththa duqqidayti gidikko erettes. Hessa gish sargeza allahaaththaey mishiraza xegiidi hizgiidesi.
JOH 2:10 “Assi wuri sargeesoon koyyro lo7o usshshi shishshees, asay maththotidappe guye iitta ehes shini ne qass lo7o ushshu hano gakanas woththagadasa.”
JOH 2:11 Yesussay hessa mallalisiza malata wursofe koyro Galila getetiza deren Qana katamane othides. Be bonchoka hessamalan xoncisides. Iza kalizaytka izan amanida.
JOH 2:12 Hesafe guye Yesussay ba Ayera ba ishatarane bena kalizaytara duge Qifirnahome wodhidi hen gutha wode deyida.
JOH 2:13 Ayhudata paziga ba7aaleye matida gish Yesussay Yarussalame bidess.
JOH 2:14 Maqqidase gibbe gidon borata doresatanne wolista bayzizayta qassekka mishe lamizayti mishe lamishin demidess.
JOH 2:15 Hesa beydi wodoro durqafe doqqi ekidi asanne boratakka maqidqse gibefe kesidese, mishsh lamizyta mishaka dharcidi ista xraphezatakka shiri yagidass.
JOH 2:16 Woole bayziza asakka “hayssa wursi gede digitte ta Awa ketha zale7a keeth histofitte” gidess.
JOH 2:17 He wode iza kalizayti “ne ketha michay tana tamamala xugess” geteti xafetida qaalla hasa7ida.
JOH 2:18 Hesafe guye Ayhude asa halaqati Yesussa “Ne haysssa wurssa oothanas sheney ness dizaysa qoncisanas ne nuna ay malalthiza malata besanee?” gi oychida.
JOH 2:19 Yesussaykka istas “anne hayssa maqidaseza lalite ta iza heedzdzu galasara zara kexxana” gi zaridess.
JOH 2:20 Istika iza “hayssa maqidaseza kexxanas kasa ooydu tammane usupun layth ekidess histin neni hezu glasara kexxa kunthanee?” gi oychida.
JOH 2:21 Gido atin Yesussay “maqqidase” giday ba asatetha gishasa.
JOH 2:22 Hessa gish Yesussay hayqi dendin iza kalizayti he yozza yushi qopidi eridanne hayssa kasse maxafan xafetidaysanne Yesussay istas kaseti yotida qaalla amanida.
JOH 2:23 Fazigaa ba7ale galas Yesussay Yerusalamen diishe oothida malatataa beydi daro asay iza amanidess.
JOH 2:24 Qasse Yesussay asa wursi eriza gish onakka amanibeyna.
JOH 2:25 Izi aussa wozzinan diza wursi eriza gish onikka izas asa gish yotanas koshibeyna.
JOH 3:1 Parsawista baga ass gidida ayhudata hllaqappe issi Niqodimossa getetizaday assi dess.
JOH 3:2 Izi qamara Yesussakko yidi “astamare Xoossi izara dzade gidikofe atin hayta ne oothiza malalsiza malatata oothanas danda7izadeye dena. Hessa gish ne Xoossa achafe yida astamare gdidayysa nuu erosu” gidass.
JOH 3:3 Yesussaykka izas zaridi “ta nes tumu gays assi namantho yeletoonta agikko Xoossa kawoteth beynanas danda7ena” gidess.
JOH 3:4 Niqodimosaykka zaridi “histin assi cimidappe guye wandi namaantho yeletan danda7izee? Qassekka gede bee aye ul7on simi gelidi yeletanee?” gidi oychides.
JOH 3:5 Yesussyka izas hizggidi zarides “ta nes tumu gays assi hathafenne Xillo Anappe yeletontaa dishe Xoossa kawoteth gelanass danda7ena.
JOH 3:6 Asappe yelettida asa. Ayanappe yeletdeye ayana.
JOH 3:7 Hessa gish <inte nmma7antho yeletanas kooshes> ta nena gida gish malaletofa.
JOH 3:8 Carkkoy ba koyida baga carkess, ne carkoss gireth siyasa atin izi awappe yizakkonne awa bizakko erakka, ayanafe yelettidaykka hessa malla.”
JOH 3:9 Niqodimossay “haysi wani hnana danda7ize?” gidi oychdess.
JOH 3:10 Yesussaykka izas “Isra7ele Astemare gidautada hessa ne eriki?
JOH 3:11 Ta nes tumu gays nuni nu erazaysa yotoss, nu be7idaysa markatos gido attin inte nu markateth ekekketta.
JOH 3:12 Ta intess hayssa ha biitta yo yotin amanonta ixikko sallo miish yotikko wosti inte wosti ammanane?
JOH 3:13 Saloppe dugge wopdhia asa naape attin pude saloo keziday haray onikka denna.
JOH 3:14 Bazoo biittan Musey shoshu dhoqqu histi kaqqidaysatho heesathokka asa nayy dhoqqan kaqistanas beses.
JOH 3:15 Hessikka izan ammanizadeye wurikka medhina deyo demanasa gsaasa.
JOH 3:16 Xoossa na ammanizay wuri medhina deyo demanappe attin dhayonta mala Xoossi hayssa alameza daro siqida gish ba mixi issi na immides.
JOH 3:17 Xoassay ba naza ha dugge alame kittday alame asay izan amanidi atinn izi alamme asa bolla firdanas gidena.
JOH 3:18 Iza amanizade bola pirdetena, iza amanonntadey gdikko Xoossa na isinezan amanonta gish benipekka pirdeti utides.
JOH 3:19 Pirdayyka hysamala po77oy ha alame yides shin asas oothoy iitta gdidagish asay po7oppe daro dumma doosides.
JOH 3:20 Iita o7htzadeye wurikka poo7 dosena. izi o7thazza ita o7thooy pooncci kkazontamala izi ba huees poo77y dzzasa kezena.
JOH 3:21 Tuumu o7thzadey gdiiko po77y dizasa yees. izi po77y dizzasa yeza gasoy Xoossa azazzomalla izi o7thdda o7thooy qonncana maalla.”
JOH 3:22 Hessafe kallidi Yesussy bena kallizaytara Yhuudaa dere bedess. heniikka Asaa xxamaqqshe istarra guusa woode gmmidess.
JOH 3:23 Hee wode salleme achaan Henoone gistattzasann daroo haathia dizza gsaa Yaansay asa xaamakchhn asayyka izzko biidi xmaqettdess.
JOH 3:24 Hesa woode Yannsaay buro qaacho kketha gelii beyyna.
JOH 3:25 Hee wode Yaansassne isi isi ayyhudea asat. garrsane Ayyhudata gessa wooga gesii gtta polamaay denndidess.
JOH 3:26 Yannssa kallisayta izakoo shiqqdie “asstamare nenara Yorrdanose shaafa pinnthane neenrra issifa dishhn ne iza gess marrkatoo adezikaa heko xaamaqess asaayka izika bess gdda.”
JOH 3:27 Yannsaayka isstas hzzgdess. “o7nnsika Xoossafe imetonta dishnn ayykoykka dana dandaeena.
JOH 3:28 <Tani izafe snthataa kitadiis atin yana Krrstossay tana gdikke> gada ta intees yotooysas inte inte huerra taa marrkataa.
JOH 3:29 Machii msshray dzadey izika msshra msshra lageey gdikko msshraza achaan ekkdi Msshrazzi gzazz siyees. msshrraza xxalla siiydi ufaeetess hessa gssha ta uhaaththaaysi hii polltdess.
JOH 3:30 Izi xooqu xooqu ganamala taaka zqqi ganamalla koshees.
JOH 3:31 Puudape yezadey wursofe boola. garrsa biitafe gedidaay izi bitazanne biitaaz yootees (hasaees) saloope yesadeey izi wursofe bola.
JOH 3:32 Izi ba beeydazine ba siiydazz markariis gdoo atiin zia marrsatiths ekkzadeey deena.
JOH 3:33 Iza marrkethe ekkzadeey gddko Xoossa tumanncha gdidaaysa qonncsees (besees)
JOH 3:34 Xoossa kittdadeey Xoossa Qalla yotiss Xssika izades ba ayana kunnthie imess.
JOH 3:35 Awaay ba na dosees haanizza yoo wurrsi iza kuseen yeegdees.
JOH 3:36 Nazaan amanizades medaana deyooy dees. nazaan aamanontaay gediiko Xoossa hankooy iza bola dees attin deyoo demena.”
JOH 4:1 He woode Yesussay Yanssapa bollara daaro asa bena kalizadey othizayssane xammaqzayssa Paarssaweti siyyda.
JOH 4:2 Gido attn xmmaqizayti iza kalizzytape atin izi xmmaxxbeyna.
JOH 4:3 Iza gish hasettizaysa Paarsaweti siyydayssa Yesussay eerdi Yihhudda derre aggdi Gaalia dere simmi bidees.
JOH 4:4 Izi he bishshin Sammaryara adhi busi izas dosa gidoonta maane gidides.
JOH 4:5 Heesa gissh Sikkaro getettizzaso Smmarya Katamma bidees. Sikkara Yaqoobeey ba naa Yoosehaaththaos imida bita achan daysu.
JOH 4:6 Henika Yaaqobbe hatha olay dees. Yesussay o7gge haamutti dabburidi gish he o7llay achchan uttidees. Wodeykka gllassape usuppune Ssaate mala.
JOH 4:7 Hesaa woode isi Saammarya dere Mccash dizaara haathe tikkanas he hatha tikanas he hatha olakko yaddus. Yesussyka izo “tana haath ushsha” gides.
JOH 4:8 Hessi hanishin Yesusaa kallizzayta qumma shshamana kattamma bida.
JOH 4:9 Hinna sammarrya Maacashaya Yesussa “ne Ayyhhuda Assi gida utada waanaada tana saammariyya machchas <hathe ushsha> ga o7ychazii?” gadus. Iza hessa gidaay Ayyhhudda Assasinne Sammarriya asa gagoteththi donnta gishasa.
JOH 4:10 Yesussayka Izis “Xoossa iimotaayne nena <tana hathe uusha> gizzadey izi o7naakone ne eeriazzko ne iza woosana beses. Izika ness deeyo hath nees immanakoshin” gides.
JOH 4:11 Izaka Izas hizgadus. “Goodo nees hath duqqza miishi deena haththa olaykka darro cimma, histin ne deeyo hatha Awaappe demmane?
JOH 4:12 Ne haayssa haththa o7llazza nuus immida nu Aawwa Yiqqoobeppe Addazzi Izzine iza nayti iza mmhhetikka haaysa ha o7llape haath uyydaa.”
JOH 4:13 Yesussay izis hizgidees “hayyssa ha haththafe uyzzaye wuri namma7nthoo ssamottidi zari hara uyaanashshn.
JOH 4:14 Ta imizza hath uyzzadey medhinas mulleka samoottena. Gssoykka ta immiza hath uyizzades medhina deyoos ppulttiza puullto hath gidana.”
JOH 4:15 Maccashshayaka “Goodo heeyssafe guye tanna heththi saammonta mallane qaseesaka ta heththi tikkana ha yonnta mmalla hessa ne giza haththa malla hathth tass imaarrkii!” gadus.
JOH 4:16 Yesussayka izo “baadane ne azzinna xega ekkada ya” gides.
JOH 4:17 Maaccashayakka zaradaa “tas azinnay deena” hizgiin Yesussay hizgidees “ <ne tas azzinay deena> guussay tumukko.”
JOH 4:18 Gasooykka kase nes iichachuu azznati detes, qasse ha7i nenara dizzayyssi ne azzina giddenaa, hessa gish ne tummu gaddasa.”
JOH 4:19 Maccashaya izas hizgadus “Goodo neni nabe gdisayssa ta ha7i erraddis.”
JOH 4:20 Kasse nu awwatti haayssa zumaa bolla gooynidaa. Innte qasse “Assaye gooynnanass besizzasay Yerrussallamekko geista.”
JOH 4:21 Yesussaykka izzis hizgides “hanne maaccashshaye Xoossa aawas haayysa zuma boolla woykko Yerrussallamen inte gooynnota wodey yanaysa amaana”
JOH 4:22 Intene inte eroonta Xoossas goyynetta. Nu gidikko asas atootethi Ayyhudeppe giddida gishsha nuni nu erriza Xoossas goyynos.
JOH 4:23 Gido atin tuumu goynnizzayti Xoossa aawas Ayyananinne tumatethan goynizza woddey buuro yaanna. Haray atoshshn haiikka yiddes. Xoossa aawaykka kooyzay heesa malla gooyniizaytta.
JOH 4:24 “Xossi ba hu7es a7yanna. Iza goynizayti aynaninne tumatethan gooynanass beesees.”
JOH 4:25 Macashayakka “Xossay tiyidade Kirstosay yanaassa ta errayys, izi yiidi haniizzaz wurrsi nuus yoottana” gaddus.
JOH 4:26 Yesussayka izis “hii neenara hssaizzay ta izzakko.” giddes.
JOH 4:27 Hessi haniishshin izza kallizzayta ba biddassoppe simmida. Yesussay Maaccashshara hassa7izaysa maallalletida. Giddo atiin “hane a77y kooyazi? wykko haniira a7zzas hassazz?” giiddi o77nikka oychchana.
JOH 4:28 Hessafe guuyye Mccashshaya otooza hen agagada geede kattama bada, asas.
JOH 4:29 “Ta oththidaz wurrssi tass yottdadey ha yiddi beeyte, oone erazzy yanna Xossay tiyida Kirstosay izakkonne!” gadus.
JOH 4:30 Assayka kattamape kezzidi Yessusako bides.
JOH 4:31 He wode Yesussa kalizzyti Yesussa “Asstamarre qumma ma” gdii wossida.
JOH 4:32 Izi qaas “inte eronttay ta mizza qummay tas dees.” gidees.
JOH 4:33 Hssa gsha iza kalizayti “aykko miza kathth asii izas ehideshsh” giidi ba grrssan hasaeetda.
JOH 4:34 “Yesussayka istas zaridi ta quumay tana kiitda ta aawa shene o7thone iza ootho polo” gides.
JOH 4:35 Inte qaas “kaththa mxxay gkkans buro o7yddu agnna a7tddes gista gideketi? Qaas ta gidikko intena <doqu giidi kaththay maxaa gakiidaysa xeelitee.> gays.
JOH 4:36 Maxxizadey ba damussa ekaana, medhianas gidizza ayfe shishana, hessagish zerizzadeynne maxizadeey isfe ufe7istana.
JOH 4:37 Hesa gsha isadey zerana hara uray maxxana getettiza lemusooy tuuma.
JOH 4:38 Ta intena inte daburontayssa maxnamalla yedadis. Harati oothon daburida gido attin inte ista dabursan go7etidista.”
JOH 4:39 Mcashaya “ta oothidazi wurrsi tas izi yootides” gada asas marrkatida malla katamape daroo Samariya asay izan amanides.
JOH 4:40 Hesagisha Samarriya asay Yesussako yidine istakoon gmaa7nmalla wosiida. Izikka nma7u gallas hen gamides.
JOH 4:41 Iza Qalla siydi daroo asay Iza amaanides.
JOH 4:42 Macashayokka “ha7i nu iza amanizzay ne yootida qalla gish xalla gidonta nuuka nu baggra izape siyyda gishane tumaappe izi derre ashshizade gididaysa erida gishasa” gida.
JOH 4:43 Yesusay Samariyan nm77u gallasa gam7idappe guye Galillaa bidess.
JOH 4:44 Izi ba baggra “nabey ba derren boonchistan” gi yootides.
JOH 4:45 Gido atn izi Gallila bin Gallia asay Iza loo7ethi mooki ekkides. Gasoykka pazziga Ba7ale boonchana Yerusalame bidason hen dishshin izi oothidaysa wurrsi deyyda gishshasa.
JOH 4:46 Hessafe guye yesussay hathe Wayyne cajje oothida Gllilla derre garrsan dzza Qanna getittza ktama namantho bidees. He wode Qifrnahomen izas nay sakettida isi kawo shuumey dees.
JOH 4:47 Izika Yesussay Yihudda dereppe gede Galilla yidayysa siydi Yesussako bidees. Yesussay dugge Qifrnahoome wodhanmallane daroo saketdii haykqqana gizza naaza pathanamalla Yesussa woossidees.
JOH 4:48 Yesussaka izas “inte gita malatatanne malallsizaaz beyoonta aykokka amanekkta” gidees.
JOH 4:49 Shumezikka zaridi “Godoo ta naazi hayyqoonta elela woodharkki?” gides.
JOH 4:50 Yesussaka iza “neni ne soo ba nazi paxideess.” gidess. Adezikka Yesussay izas yootida Qalla amaniidi soo smmi bides.
JOH 4:51 Izi soo bishshn iza ahskkarati izara ogen gagidi “ne nazi paxideskoo.” gidi izas yootida.
JOH 4:52 Shumezika nazi ay saten paxxidakoone issta zari oychchides. isstikka izazs “qama gllasappe Lapuun Saten iza michchizayssi agides” gida.
JOH 4:53 Naza awaykka Yesussay “ne naazi paxidees” giday he issti izass yotizza woode gidaysa eriddess. Hessa gshsha he galassfe oykkdi izine iza so asay wuri Yesussa ammidda.
JOH 4:54 Hayssi malattay Yesussay Yihudappe Galila yiidi oothida nma77antho malata.
JOH 5:1 Hesafe kalidi Ayhudista Ba7lley dizza gish Yesussay Yerussallame bideess.
JOH 5:2 Yerusalamen doorsi gelizza pennge achchan iibrawista qalara Betesayda getettza issi pulltoofe shiqqida eloo hathey dees. Bollara kamay diza ichachu o7geti dettes.
JOH 5:3 Daro hargganchatti, ayyfe qooqeti, to woobetinne to silati ogge bolla zinniidi hathay qaxistana gakanas nagetees.
JOH 5:4 Isi isi woode Goda kiitanchay hathan woodhidi hatha qaththes. haththa qathafe kaldi koyrottdi hathan gelizza hargganchay bena sakiza ay hrggefekka paxes.
JOH 5:5 Hen gadaan heedzdzu tammane oosppun laythth kumeth sakketida isadeey dess.
JOH 5:6 Yessusay Adezza hen zin7idayssa beyddine izi daro laythth saketdayssa eridi “ne paxxana kooyaz?” gidess.
JOH 5:7 Hargganchazika zaridi “Godo haththay qaxxetiza woode tana hathan gelththiza assi dena, ta buroo bana gishshin harray tape kaseti hathan gelles.” gidess
JOH 5:8 Yesussayka Iza “dendda ne zin7ida algga tookada ba” gidess.
JOH 5:9 Adezzikka herakka paxxides. Be algga tooki ekidii bidess. Hessi hanidayy Ayhudista sambbata galassa.
JOH 5:10 Hesa gish Ayhudista hallaqat paxxida Adezza “hach Sambbattara ne algga tokkana mala Musse wogay azazena” gida.
JOH 5:11 Izikka Isttas “ne zini7ida algga tookkda ba gi yotides” gides.
JOH 5:12 Isttikka “nena algga tookkada ba giday oonne?” gi oychchida.
JOH 5:13 Deerey darida gishinne Yesussay hepee hakki bida gish iza oonni paththidakonne adezzi eribeyna.
JOH 5:14 Hesafe guye Yesussay Adeza Xoossa keeththan demmidi “hekoo ha7i ne paxadasa kaseysafe Adhizza iita miishi ne bolla gakontta mala nam77anththo nagara othofa” gides
JOH 5:15 Adezikka bidinne iza pathiday Yesussa gididaysa Ayhudista dannatas yotides.
JOH 5:16 Adezza sambbata gallas pathida gish Ayhudista dannat Yesussa oykkana yedi godida.
JOH 5:17 Yesussayka isstas “ta aaway wurso wode oothes, takka othana” gides
JOH 5:18 Hesa gason ayhudista dannat Yesussa wodhana malla kaseppe aththi denththethida, qase izi sammbatta morida gish xalla gidontta “Xoossi ta aawa” gida gishshinne bena Xoossara ginssida gishasa.
JOH 5:19 Yesussay isttsa hizgi zarrides “ta intes tummu gays aaway oothishin be7idaysa othoppe attin nazi ba shenen ayne otheena. Aaway othizaysa iza nay hessathoka oothes.
JOH 5:20 Gasoyka Aaway naaza doses ba othzaysakka wursi iza besees, inte malaletontta mala hayssafeka adhiza ootho buro bessana.
JOH 5:21 Aaway haqqidayta denththizaythone deyoo imizaysatho nazika hessathoo ba koydades deyoo immana.
JOH 5:22 Aaway oonna bollaka pirdeena gido attin pirda maata wuris ba nazas imiddes.
JOH 5:23 Izi hessaththo oththiday asay wuri aawa bonchana malane qaaseka nazaka bonchana malasa. Naza bonchonttay naza kitida aawakka boncheen.
JOH 5:24 Ta intes tumma gays ta qaalla siyzadeesine tana kitidaden amanizades medhina deyooy dees, izadeey hayqoope gede deyoon pinnidees atin iza bolla pirdetena.
JOH 5:25 Ta intes tummu gays kase hayqqida asat Xoossa na qaala siyza woodey yaana, he woodiyakka haano, siyzatii wuri deyoon deyaana.
JOH 5:26 Gasoykka aaway ba bagra deyooy diza mala nazikka ba baggara deyooy dana mala oothides
JOH 5:27 Izi asa na gidida gish pirdana mala Godatethth izas imiddes.
JOH 5:28 Haysan aykokka malaletoppite, Gasoykka buro kase hyqdii dufoon dizaayti wuri Iza qaala giireth siyizza woodey yana.
JOH 5:29 Lo7o oothdayt hayqqope denddid paxxna, Iita othidaayti gidikko hayqoope denddidi pirdistana.”
JOH 5:30 “Ta ta sheenen ayne oththanas danddaike, gido attin ta ta aawape siyda mala pirdays, tana kiitidaysa sheene oththaysi attin ta sheenen ta oththontta gish ta pirdan balay bawwa.
JOH 5:31 Tan ta gish tarkka markkatiko ta markkay tummu gidena.
JOH 5:32 Gido attin ta gish markkatizzadey haraay dees, izika ta gish markkatizzade, markkatethay tummu gididdaysa ta eraays.
JOH 5:33 Inteni Yanssako asse kitideistashin izika tummu markkatidees.
JOH 5:34 Ta hayssa gizay inte attana mala attin tas haara ass markkateth koshshida gish gideena.
JOH 5:35 Yanssay exidii pooizaa poo7 mala, intekka gutha wode iza poo7in uhaaththaaettana kooydista.
JOH 5:36 Tas gidikoo Yanssa markkatethape adhiza markkaay dees, ta markkayka ta aaway tas immida oothok, hesika ta oothiza othooy ta aaway tana kitidaysa tas markkates.
JOH 5:37 Tana kitida ta Aawayka ba huera tas markkatidees, inte gidiko iza qaala giireth mulekka siybeykkista, izas medhoka mulera beybeeykkista.
JOH 5:38 Izi kitidadden inte ammanontta gish iza qaalay inte achchan deyeena.
JOH 5:39 Intes geesha Maxxaafatape medhina deyoo demanas milatin maxaxafata piqqilista, maxxaafatikka ta gish markkatetes.
JOH 5:40 gido attin inte deyoo demaanas tako ha yana kooyekkista.
JOH 5:41 Ta asappe boncho kooykke.
JOH 5:42 ta intena errays, xoossa siqqoy intenan baynddaysa errays.
JOH 5:43 Tan ta aawa sunththan yadiis shin inte tana mooki ekiibeykeista hara uray qase ba sunththan yikoo inte iza mokii ekista.
JOH 5:44 Inte inte garssan isay isape boncho koyzzaytoo issi Xoossafe betizza boncho koyonttaytoo inte waanidi tana amaanana danddaeti,?
JOH 5:45 Ta aawa sinththan intena moottanay intes tana misatoopo intena moottanay inte iza uhaaththaaysi oothiza Musekko,
JOH 5:46 Museey ta gish xaafidaysa ammanidako inte tana ammanana.
JOH 5:47 Izi xaafidaysa inte ammanontta agikoo qase ta qaala inte woostti ammanane?”
JOH 6:1 Hesafe guye Yesussay xiibradoose geetettizaso gaalila abbafee he pinthth pinnidees.
JOH 6:2 Yesussay hargganchata paththida malata beydda gish daroo asay iza kaaliides.
JOH 6:3 Yesussay bena kaalizaytara pude zumma bolla kezii uttddes.
JOH 6:4 He woode Ayhudaata paziiga ba77eley matii utdees.
JOH 6:5 He woode daroo derey Izakoo yizayssa Yesussay dhoqu gi xeeliidi pilphphossa “hayssa deeras gidana quuma awapee shammana danddaiizoon?” gidess.
JOH 6:6 Yesussay Pilphphoossa hessathoo oychchiday iza paccanako, gido attin izi ba ooththanaysa erress.
JOH 6:7 pilphphossayka izas “issi issi urras issi bars gidza kath shamizakooka numm7u xeetu dinaren shaammida kathka hayssas gidena” gidees.
JOH 6:8 Yesussa kalizaytape isay siimoona Phxroossa isha Indryaassa,
JOH 6:9 “Ichchachu bangga ukethine namm7u mole oykkida issi nay hayssan dees, gidoo attin hana hayssa ha derezaas awa gakane?” gidees.
JOH 6:10 Yesussayka zardii “asa wuris utssite” gides, hen gadan daroo maatay diza gish asayka uttides, asa qoodayka ichchachu shi gidizaytako.
JOH 6:11 Hesafe guyee Yesussay uketha ekidi galata wossa wosidi uttdaa asas gishshides, molezaka hessathokaa gishshechides asay wurkka bes gidiza demiides.
JOH 6:12 Asay wurikka kaalli miin Yesussay bena kallizayta “maaddan attidaa kaththa isinooka ashoontta shishshite” gidees.
JOH 6:13 Isttika asay mishshin ichchachu ukethafe attida tammane namm7u leemate kumeth shishshida.
JOH 6:14 Asayka Yesussay ooththida malata beyydi “hayssaadey tummape ha allame yana nabezakko” gidess.
JOH 6:15 Asay qase wolqara Yesussa kawothana qopidaysa a erridi Yesussay qaseka isttafe haki bidi zumma bolla kezzdes.
JOH 6:16 Gadey qaammishshin Yesussa kalizayt duge abbakoo woodhida.
JOH 6:17 Wogolon geliddi qifiranaahone bana kezzda. istti kezshshn gadeey dhumiidees, Yesussay hessa gakanaskka isttakko yibeyyna.
JOH 6:18 wolqama carkkooy carkkiiza gish abbay keez qaaxides.
JOH 6:19 Iza kallzayt baga saate ogge mala wogoloza lagidape guyee Yesussay abba balara toora hamutti wogolozakoo mattishin demmidi baabbida.
JOH 6:20 Izika isttas “tankoo! baboopte!” gidees.
JOH 6:21 Isttika iza uhaaththaayysara gede wogoloza gi doo ekkana koyda, heraka wogolozika istt banaso gakides.
JOH 6:22 Abbafe he pinththan attida asay wonttetha gaalas abba bolla issi wogoloy xaala dizarro beyyda, Yesussa kalizayyt kase berkka bidayssane Yesussay isttara wogolon gelonttaaysa erridda.
JOH 6:23 Gido attin hankko wogolot xiibradoosepe denddidi Yesussay galata wosaa woosidi asa kaththa muzooso achchi yida.
JOH 6:24 Asayka Yesussay woykko iza kalizaytti hen baynddaysa beydii he wogolotan gelidi yesussa koshuu Qifranahomee bides.
JOH 6:25 Abbafe he pinththan iza demmidi “asttamare! ne aydee hayssa yadii” gidda.
JOH 6:26 Yesussayka isttas “ta intes tumma gayys inte tana koyzay kath mi kaallida gish attin malata be7ida gish gideena.
JOH 6:27 Dhayaana kaththas oosofite, gido attin hessafe athid xoossa aaway ammaanithza mattame iza bolla shoccida gish asa nay intes immiza medhina deyoos gidiza kaththas ooththite.”
JOH 6:28 isttika iza “histtin Xoossa ooso ooththanas nu azi ooththino?” gida.
JOH 6:29 Yesussayka “Xoossa oosoy Xoossi kiitida iza nazan ammano.” gidii isttas zaardes.
JOH 6:30 Isttika izas “nu beyddi nena ammanana mala ne nuna aaza malata beesane? qaseka azi ooththane? gides.
JOH 6:31 <Istti maana mala isttas qumma salope immides> geeteti xaafetida mala kase nu aawati baazoo bittan maan7e miida.”
JOH 6:32 Yesussay isttas. “ta intes tummu gays salope wodhida qumma intes imiiday musse giddena, tummu qumma salope intess immizaay ta aawakoo.
JOH 6:33 Gasooyka Xoossa qummay salope wodhidi allamees deyoo imiizaysako” gides.
JOH 6:34 Hesa gish asay “Godo hessa mala qumma nuss wuriso wode immarkkii” gides.
JOH 6:35 yesussayka isttas hizigidess “deyoo qummay tana, taakko yiza urray mulleka gafeetena, tana ammaaniizadeey aydeeka samotena.
JOH 6:36 kase ta intes gida mala inte tana beyddistashin ammanibeeykista.
JOH 6:37 Ta aaway tas immizaay wurkka taakko yana, takoo yizade ta gedee kaare goodike.
JOH 6:38 Gasoykka ta salope wodhiday tana kitidaysa sheene ooththanas attin ta sheene ooththanas gideena.
JOH 6:39 Tana kitidadeey sheene tas immidaytape issadeeka dhaysontta wurisetha gaalas ta denththana.
JOH 6:40 Ee ta sheeney naza beydii iza ammanizadeey wuri medhina deyoo demmanasiko, tanikka wuriseththa gaalas iza hayqqope denththana.”
JOH 6:41 Hesa gish Yesussay “salope wodhidda qummay tana” gidda gish ayhudat iza bolla zuzumeetida.
JOH 6:42 “hayisii Yoseefoo na Yesussa gideene? iza aawane iza aayoo nu errokoni? histtin hai izi <salope wodhadis> waani gizze?” gida.
JOH 6:43 Yesussayka isttas hizzgides “inte intee garrisaan gugummista.
JOH 6:44 Tana kittida ta aaway xeeygidape attin takoo yana danddaizadeey oonikka dena, berika takoo yana danddaizay oonikka dena, takoo yizadeka wurisetha gaalas ta iza hayqqope denithana.
JOH 6:45 Nabbista maaxxafatan asay wuri Xoossafe tammardade gidana geetet xaafeetidees, hessa gish aawape siyydi tammarda assi wuri takoo yana.
JOH 6:46 Hesa guus aawa beeyda assi dess guusu gidena. aawa beeyday Xoossa achchafe yidaysa xaala.
JOH 6:47 Ta intees tumma gays tanan ammanida asas medhina deyooy dees.
JOH 6:48 Tan deyoo qumma.
JOH 6:49 kasse inte aawat bazzo biittan man7e midda gido attin wurkka hayqqida.
JOH 6:50 Salope wodhida qummay hayssa, hayssa mizzadey mulleka hayqqena.
JOH 6:51 Salope wodhida deyoo qummay tana, hayssa ha qummape mizzadey wurkka medhinas dana, allames deyoo gidana mala ta immiza qummay ta ashshoko.”
JOH 6:52 Hesa wode Ayhuddat “haysi addeez nu iza ashsho mana mala woostt iimane?” gidi ba garssan palameetida.
JOH 6:53 Hessa gish Yesussay istta hizzigidees “ta intes tummu gays, asa na ashsho inte moontta aggikko iza suththika uyoontta aggikko intes deyooy deena.
JOH 6:54 Ta ashsho mizza urasine ta suththu uyzaa uraas wurisoos medhina deyooy dees, taka izzade wuriththetha gaalas hayqqope denththana.
JOH 6:55 Gasooyka ta ashshoy tummu qumma, ta suththayka tummu ushsha.
JOH 6:56 Ta ashsho mizzayne ta suththu uyzzay wuri tanan deeyana, takka izzaden deeyana.
JOH 6:57 Deyoo aaway tana kiitida malane takka izzan deyoon diza mala hessathoka ta ashsho mizzadey wuri tanan deyoon dana.
JOH 6:58 Hessa gish salope wodhida qummay hayssa, izika kase inte aawat midaaysa mala gidena, gasooykka he qumma midayt hayqqida, ha qumma mizayt gidikoo medhinas dana.”
JOH 6:59 Yesussay hayssa Qihaaththairanahomeen ayhudata woosa keeththan tammirisiza wode yotiddes.
JOH 6:60 Iza kaallizaytape darzzayt hessa siydii “haysi yoozi dexxoko hayssa oonni ekkane danddaize?” gida.
JOH 6:61 Yesussayka iza kaallizayt hessa yooza gish zuzumetidaysa ba wozinan erridi “<haysi intena dexxize?> gidees.
JOH 6:62 Assa nay Kirisitoossay ba dizzaso simm kezshshin beykoo inte ay gane?
JOH 6:63 Assas deyoo immizzay Xoossa ayanakoo, asa wolqay qaasse aynee go77ena, ta intes yootida qaalay deyoo immiza ayanakoo.
JOH 6:64 Gido attin inte garisan issi issi ammanoontta asat detes. Yesussay isttas hessa giday koyroope dommidi istta garisan ammanoonitayti oonanitakoone qaasse iza aththi immanadeeyka oonakoone erriza gishaskko.
JOH 6:65 Kallethidikka Yesussay aawa sheeney bayyndda takoo ha yana danddaizadeey dena gada ta intes yootiday hessassa.” gidees.
JOH 6:66 Hesafe denddidayssan iza kallizaytape daroot guyee simmida, he gaalasafe dommidi Yesussa kaalo aggida.
JOH 6:67 Hessa gish Yesussay bena kalliza tammane namm7ista “inteka bana kooyet?” gides.
JOH 6:68 Hessa wode Simoonna geetettiza phxxirossay “Godo ne medhina deyooy dishin nu oonakoo banee?
JOH 6:69 Ne geshsha Xoossa na gididdayysa erridi nun ammanidos” gidees.
JOH 6:70 Yesussayka istta “ta intena tammane namm7ista doorabeykina? histtin intefe isaay Xallaeko.” gidees.
JOH 6:71 Izi hessa giday Simoona na Asqqoroto Yuddaa gishasiko. ayysi gikko yudday tammane namm7istape iisa gididdakoka Yesussa athth immanay iza gididda gishshasiko.
JOH 7:1 Hesafe guye Yesussay galila garssan yuyettdees, gido attin Yuhudan yuyanas kooybeeyna, gasooykka Ayhudat iza wodhana kooyza gishshasiko.
JOH 7:2 He wode Ayhudata dase Ba77eley matti uttdes.
JOH 7:3 Hesa gish Yesussa ishshati izakoo shiqqidi hizzigida. “nena kallizayt ne ooththiza oosoza beyana mala ne heyssafe denddada Yuhuda dere ba.
JOH 7:4 Gasooykka qooccen erristana koyzadey ba ooso geeman oothena, neka heytantta wursa ooththashe nena allamen qoonccsana koshshes.”
JOH 7:5 Istt hessa gida gasooy iza ishshataka gidin izan ammanonttayta gidida gishshasiko.
JOH 7:6 Yesussayka isttas hizzigides. “ta wodey buroo gakiibeyna, inte wodey gidiko wuriso wode intes gigako.
JOH 7:7 Deerey intena ixxana danddaena, tana gidikoo ixxes, gasooyka ta allame oosoy iita gididdaysa izas markkattza gishshasiko.
JOH 7:8 Hai inte gede ba77elezaso bite, tass wodey gakontta gish hayssa ha Ba77elezaso bikke.”
JOH 7:9 Hesa gidii Yesussay Galilan attdess.
JOH 7:10 Gido attin iza ishshat Ba77elezaso bidappe guye Yesussay qonccera gidontta qotara ba77elezaso bidees.
JOH 7:11 Ayhudat iza “awan diize?” gishe Ba77elezason koydda.
JOH 7:12 Deereyka Iza gish garisara sasuqi hasaettdes. issi issi asat “izi loo7o asakoo” gishin bagay qase “loo7o gidena izi dere baleththes” gides.
JOH 7:13 Gido attin Ayhudata dannatas babiza gish oonnika iza gish qoonccen hasaibeyna.
JOH 7:14 Ba77elezii wurana baaga gakishin Yesussay xoossa keeth bidi tammariso oykkdees.
JOH 7:15 Ayhudat “haysii addezi tammarontta dishshe hayssa wursi woostti erride” gidi malaletidda.
JOH 7:16 Hessa gish Yesussay hizzgdes. “ta tammarithiza timmiritey tana kittda ta Aawape immetides attin tape gidenna.
JOH 7:17 Tana kittdaysa sheene ooththana koyzadeey dikko haysii ha timmiritey Xoossafe beetdaysa woykko ta tape hasaidaysa gidikkoka errana.
JOH 7:18 Bepe hasaizadeey ba boncho koyyes, kittidade boncho koyzadeey gidiko izi tummancha, wordooy iza bolla denna.
JOH 7:19 Mussey intes woga immidess gideene? gidikkoka inte garisan wog nagii poliidadey oonka deena, inte azass tana wodhana koyeti?”
JOH 7:20 Deereyka iza “ne bolla dayydanthth dees! ne wodhana kooyzay oonne?” gidees.
JOH 7:21 Yesussayka isttas hizzgi zarides “ta issi ooso ooththadiss inte wurikka hano ha oosoy malaleteista.
JOH 7:22 Musseey intes qaxxara woga immidees, he wogayyka immeetiday kase aawatape beetidees attin Mussepe gidena. histtin hekko intekka sambbatta gaalasiika asse qaxxarista.
JOH 7:23 Histtiko Musse wogay sharetontta mala assi smbbata gaalas qaxaretiysa gidiko histtin ta sambbata gaalas asas kummetha asateth paththiin azzas ta bolla hanqqetet?
JOH 7:24 Suurre pirda pirdite attin asa ayfeso xeelidi maadoo pirda pirdofite.”
JOH 7:25 Yerusalame asape issi issi asat hizzgda “istt woodhana koyza addezii hayssa gideene?”
JOH 7:26 heko izi qoonccen hasaees shin istt iza aykooka gibeytena, haysii xoossay kittidade giddidaysa dannat tummu eerizoshsha?
JOH 7:27 Histtin haysii addeezi awa asakone nu erroos, xoossay kitiddadey yishshin qaasse izi awapekone errizadey oonnika deena,
JOH 7:28 Hesa gish Yesussay xoossa keeththan tammarththishe ba qaala dhoqu histtdi “inte tana tummu errata, ta awape yidakone inte errata, gido attin tan ta sheenen yabeykke, tana kittdaysi izi tummancha, gidoshin inte qasse iza errekkista.
JOH 7:29 Ta gidikoo iza achchafe yida gishshine izi tana kittda gish ta iza errays” gidees.
JOH 7:30 Hesa woode iza oykanass koydaa, gido attin buroo wodey gakibeyna gish oonnika oykkbeyna.
JOH 7:31 Gido attin derezape darooy izan ammanides, asay hizgidees “xoossay kittiddadey yizza wode haysi addezi ooso malatape bollaara hara ootthhane?”
JOH 7:32 Assay Yesussa gish garssara sasuketi hasaishshin Parssawet siyda, hessa gish qeessista halaqatne parssawet yesussa oykkanas Xoossa keethth pengge naggizayta yediida.
JOH 7:33 He wode Yesussay “ta intenara guuththa wode dashshana, hessafe guye tana kittidaysako simma bana.
JOH 7:34 Inte tana koyana shin demekkista, inte ta dizzaso yanas danddaekeista.”
JOH 7:35 Hesa gish Ayhudata dannat ba garssan issay issara, “haysi addezii nu demmontta mala awa baneshsha? oonne errizzay Girikista giddo laleti diza Ayhuddatakoo bidi Girikista tammarisanesha?
JOH 7:36 Izi <inte tana koyana shin demekkista, ta dizasoo inte yanas danddaekista gishin hes ay gusee?>” gida.
JOH 7:37 Ba77eleeza wurithetha gita gaalas Yesussay dendidii eqqidne ba qaala dhoqu histtdii “hethth sammottda urray dikoo ha taakko yidi uuyoo.
JOH 7:38 Maxxafay gida mala tana ammanizadefe deyoo haththa pullitooy pullitana.” gidees.
JOH 7:39 Izi hessa gidaay izan ammanizayt buropee ekkana xiilo ayana gishshasiko, gasooyka yesussay boonchetza wodey buroo gakontta gish xiilo ayanay buroo qoonccoontta immetibeyna.
JOH 7:40 Hessa gish derezape issi issi asat he qaala siydii “yana giza nabey tummape hayssakoo” gida.
JOH 7:41 “Harati haysii xoossay kittiddadeko” gida. baggayyt qasse “xoossay kittiddadey Gliilape waan yane?
JOH 7:42 xoossay kittiddadey Dawitte zeereththape yeletanaysane dawitte katamma Bettelemepe yanaysii kase geshsha maxxafan xaafetibeyne?” gida.
JOH 7:43 Hessa gish iza gaason derey ba gidoon shaaketi wodhides.
JOH 7:44 Isttafe issi issi asat iza oykkana koyda, gido attin oonikka oykibbeyna.
JOH 7:45 Hessafe guye xoossa keeth naggizayt qeessata hallaqatakone Parisawettako simmid bida, izetika “aazas iza ekontta yidet?” gida.
JOH 7:46 Wootadaretika zaridi “ha addezi hasaizaysa mala ay assika hasai errena” gida.
JOH 7:47 parssaweti istta “intekka baletidet?” gida.
JOH 7:48 dannatape woykoo parssawistape iza ammanidayt dizosha?
JOH 7:49 Haysii mussee woga errontta derey tummape qanggetdaysa.
JOH 7:50 Haysafe kasse Yesussako bida Parssawistape isa gidida niqoodimoosay isttas
JOH 7:51 “Nu wogan issi mottetizadey ba mottos malththe immin siyonttane izi ay ooththidakone erretontta dishshin pirday pirdeet errize?” gides.
JOH 7:52 Isttika “neka galila asse? galilape nabey denddontaysa qoorerethada gakka erraa” gida.
JOH 7:53 hessafe guye isay isay beso bides.
JOH 8:1 Hesafe guye Yesussay debrrezaytte bidees.
JOH 8:2 Wontteththa gaalas malado wonttara xoossa keeth simmii yidess, dereyka wuri izakko yiin izi uttdii istta tammariso oykides.
JOH 8:3 Musse woga tammarisizaytine Parssawet issi laymatethan oyketda maccashsh dizaro eeki yidi dere sinththan eesida.
JOH 8:4 Yesussayka hizzgdes “Asttamare! heko hana maccashshaya laymatashe oykistadus.”
JOH 8:5 Hani mala maccashi shuchchan cadista hayqana mala mussey nu wogan nuna azazides, nech? hani gish ay gay?
JOH 8:6 Istt iza hessa giday iza bolla mottos gidiza gasoo demanasine iza paccana koyda gishshasa, gido attin Yesussay hokkdi biita bolla ba biradhera xaafoo oykdes.
JOH 8:7 Istt iza shir shir oychchin dhoqu gidi “inte giddofe nagaray bayndda urray koyro shuchchu izi bolla halo” gides.
JOH 8:8 hessafe qasseka hokidi biita bolla xaafides.
JOH 8:9 Isttika hessa siydii cmatape oykkdi wurkka isay isay bi kichchida, hessa gish Yesussay hen eqqida maccashshayra xaala attdes.
JOH 8:10 Hesafe Yesussay dhoqu gidi “hane maccashshaye nena mottizayt awan dizo? ne bolla pirdadey oonikka baye?” gides.
JOH 8:11 Izaka “Godo oonikka baawa.” gadus. Yesussayka “taka ne bolla pirdike, ba! Namm7enththo nagara oosofa.” gides.
JOH 8:12 qasse Yesussay “ta derey poo7o, tana kaallizadey wuri deyoo poo7o demmana, dhuman simerettena.” gidi isttas yootdes.
JOH 8:13 Parssawet “nenii ne gish markkatasa, ne markkaay tummu gideena” gida.
JOH 8:14 Yesussayka isttas hizzgi zaarides “ta ta gish ay markkatkoka ta awape ydakoone qasse ta awa banakoone ta erriza gish ta markkateth tummako, inte gidikko ta awape ydakoone qasse awa banakoone inte erreketta.
JOH 8:15 Inte ashsho qoofa mala pirdista, ta gidiiko oonna bollaka pirdike.
JOH 8:16 Ta pirdikkoka ta pirday tummu pirda, gasooyka ta tarkka pirdike, tana kittda ta aawayka tanara dess.
JOH 8:17 Namm7u asatta markkay tummu gididays inte wogan xaafetdes.
JOH 8:18 Hessa gish tan ta gish markkatays, tana kittda ta aawayka tasi markktes.”
JOH 8:19 Isttika “ne aaway awan dizee?” gidi iza oychchida, Yesussayka isttas “tana gidiin ta aawaka gidiin inte errekista, inte tana errizakoo ta aawaka errannakoshin” gidi isttas zardess.
JOH 8:20 Yesussay hessa isttas yootday Xoossa keethth gibben mishshe woththiza saxxine achchan tammarssishshe yootdes, shin izas oykeettza wodey gakontta gish oonnika iza oykiibeyna.
JOH 8:21 Yesussay qasseka “ta bana shin inte tana koyanane inte inte nagarara hayqana attin ta bizaso bana danddaekista” gides.
JOH 8:22 Ayhudatika ba garssan isay isara izi “<ta bizaso inte yana danddaekista> gizay berkka bena woodhanasesha?” geetetda.
JOH 8:23 Izi qasse istta hizzgdes “inte garssa asa, tan bolla asa, inte hayssa allamee asa, tani ha allamepe gidkke.
JOH 8:24 Inte ta oonnakone erridi ammanontta aggiko inte inte nagarara hayqqana gish ta inte! Inte nagarara hayqqana giday hessa gishshaskko.”
JOH 8:25 Isttika iza “ne oonne?” Gida, Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “hai gaakanas ta isttes iza gish yootzadey tanakko.
JOH 8:26 Ta inte bolla hasaizaysine pirdza yooy daroy dees, gido attin tana kittiddadey ammanetdade, taka izape siydaysa ha allamezas yootays.”
JOH 8:27 Izi isttas aawa gish yootzaysa akeki beytena.
JOH 8:28 Hesa gish yesussay “inte asa na dhoqu hisittd kaqqida wode he ta gidaddey tana gididaysa inte errana, aaway tana tammarssidaysa yootads attin tan ta sheene mala aykoka oosonttaysa inte akekana.
JOH 8:29 tana kittdayssi izi tanara dees, ay wodekka ta uhaaththaayzaz ooththiiza gish izi tana xaala yeegi aggibeyna” gidees.
JOH 8:30 Izi hessa yootda mala daroo asay izan ammanidees.
JOH 8:31 Yesussay bena ammanida ayhudata hizzgdes “inte tummu ta qaalan dikko inte tummupe tana kaallizayta gidana.
JOH 8:32 Tummay azakkone inte erranane tummayka intena geshshana.”
JOH 8:33 Isttika izas zaaridi “nuni Abbrame naytako, nu oonasiika aylleet erroko, histtiin ne nuna waanada inte wozistana gazi?” gida.
JOH 8:34 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “ta intes tummu gays nagara ooththizadey wuri nagaras aylle.
JOH 8:35 Ay wodekka aylleey keeththan luxxe deeyena, yeloy gidkko aydeka keeththan deyes.
JOH 8:36 Histtko nazi intena wozikko inte wozettidayta gidana.
JOH 8:37 Inte Abbramee nayta gididdaysa ta errays, gido attin ta qaala inte erroo gi ekkoontta gish tana wodhanas koyista.
JOH 8:38 Tan ta aawa achchan be7idaysa ta intes yootays, inte qasse inte aawape siydaysa ooththista.”
JOH 8:39 Isttikka izas “nu aaway Abbrameeko” gidi zari yootin Yesussay isttas hizzgdes “inte Abbramee na giddiko Abbrameetho ooththana shin.
JOH 8:40 Ta Xoossafe siyda tumma intes yootin tana wodhanas qaachch denddidista, gido attin Abbrameey hessaththo ooththibeyna.
JOH 8:41 “Inte inte aawatho ooththista” isttika zaaridii “nu laymman yeeletida na gidoko, nu aaway issi Xoossa xaala” gidi izas zaarida.
JOH 8:42 Yesussay isttas hizzgdes “inte aaway Xoossa gididakoo taka Xoossafe keza yida gish inte tana dosanakko shin tana izi kittdes attin ta tarkka ta sheenen yabeykke.
JOH 8:43 Ta yootzaysa ays yuushi qoopeket? gasooyka inte ta qaala siyana koyontta gishshaskko.
JOH 8:44 Inteni inte aawa xalae nayta, inte aawa ammo polana koyista, izi kasseka shemppo wodhidadee, iza achchan tummay dena gish izi tumman eqiibeyna, izi ba huess wordanchane wordo aawa gidida gish izi wordo hasa7e beepe medhi ekkidi hasaees.
JOH 8:45 Ta qasse tummu hasaiza gish inte tana ammanekista.
JOH 8:46 Inte garssafe tana ne hano nagara ooththadasa gidi markkara laathanas moottana danddaizadey dizee? ta tummu hasaizade gidiko histtin aazas tana ammaneket?
JOH 8:47 Xoossafe gidida uuray Xoossi giza siyes, inte gidiko Xoossafe gidontta gish xoossa qaala siyekista.”
JOH 8:48 Ayhudatika zaaridi “nu nena ne Sammaryya asa, ne bolla daydanthth dees gooys tummu gideene?” gida.
JOH 8:49 Yesussay isttas hizzg zaarides. “tani ta aawa bonchays attin daydanththi ta bolla baawa, inte gidiko tana kawushshista.
JOH 8:50 Tan tas boncho koyke, ta bonchetena mala koyzadey qasse dees, izika pirda pirdanadeko.
JOH 8:51 Ta intes tummu gays, oonnika ta qaala naggikoo hayqqo muleka hayqqena.
JOH 8:52 Ayhudat iza hizzggda. “ne bolla daydanththii dizayysa hai nuni errdees, Abrrameyy hayqqdees, nabetika izatho hayqqda, ne qasse ooniko muleka hayqqoo beeyena ga yootassa.
JOH 8:53 Ne nu aawa Abrramepe adhaz? izi hayqqdees, nabettka hayqqda histtin ne nena oonna gaana koyadii?
JOH 8:54 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “ta tarkka tana bonchiko ta bonchoy hada, tana bonchizadey gidiko inte “izi nu Xoossa” gizzay ta aawako.
JOH 8:55 inte iza errontta aggikoka ta qasse errays, ta iza errike giikoo, taka inte mala wordancha gidays. ta qasse iza errayss, iza qaalaka naagays.
JOH 8:56 inte aawa Abrramey ta galas beeyanas ammotid beeydeesine uhaaththaaettidees.
JOH 8:57 Ayhudatii qasse “ness buroo ichchachu tammu layth kummontta ne abrrame beeyadi? gida.
JOH 8:58 Yesussayka “ta intes tummu gays, Abrramey yellettanape kase tani tanako.” gides.
JOH 8:59 ayhudat heraka iza caddanas wuri shuchchu denththida. gido attin Yesussay istta matape qotetidii xoossa keethafe kezi bides.
JOH 9:1 yesussay ogera adhii bishe ba aay uloope yelletethape ayfee qooqidade beeydes.
JOH 9:2 Iza kallizayt iza “tammarisizays haysi addezii qooqe gidi yellistana mala nagara oththiday oonne? iza yellidaytii oththidoye? izi oththide?” gidii Yesussa oychchida.
JOH 9:3 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “iza gidinkka iza yellidaytika nagara oththibeytena, izi hessaththo haniday Xoossa oththoy iza bolla qonccanasiko.
JOH 9:4 Gaalasara tana kittdade oththo oththanas tas besses, buroo oonnika othanas danddaontta qammay yaana?
JOH 9:5 Ha bitta bolla diza wode ha bittas poo7oy tana.”
JOH 9:6 Hessa gi simmidi bitta bolla cuchchu cuttdii ba cuchchan urqqa gigsidi addeza ayfeza he urqqa tydii addeza
JOH 9:7 “Baada selihomen asay xammaqetizason meccista” gides, selihome gusi kittetdaysa gusa, addezika bidi maccetdesine xeellishe simmi yides.
JOH 9:8 Iza dosatnne kase izi hen wosishshin be7ida asay “hayssadey kase uttid wosiza addeza gidene? gida.
JOH 9:9 Isttafe issi issi asati “ee izakko” gida, baggaytii “iza gidena” gida, izi qasse “ta izako” gidees.
JOH 9:10 Isttika “histtin ne ayfey wani xeelide? gidi oychchida.
JOH 9:11 Izika zaaridii “Yesussa geetetza assi bitta bolla urqqa urqqasddine ta ayfeza he urqqa tydiine tana baada seliihomen meccista gi yootin ta baada meccistada xeellanas dandda7eds” gidees.
JOH 9:12 Isttaka “histtin he uray hai awan dizee?” gida, izika “ta errke” gides.
JOH 9:13 Isttikka he kasse ayfe qooqe addeza parssawistako ehaaththada.
JOH 9:14 Yesussay urqqa urqqasiidii addeza ayfe paththida gaalasay ayhudata sambbata gaalasiko.
JOH 9:15 Hessa gish parssawetii addeza izii wostt xeeliidakone iza oychchida, addezika zaaridii “izi ta ayfen urqqa tydees, taka meccistadis, heko hai xeellides” gides.
JOH 9:16 parssawistape issi issi asati “hays addezi sambbata bonchonttade gidida gish izi Xoossafe gideena” gida, baaggay qasse “nagaranchay hayssa mala malata wani ooththana danddaize? gida, hessa gish istta gidon pallamay medhetides.
JOH 9:17 Hessa gish kase ayfe qooqe addezzako simmidi “ha ne ayfe paththida addeza gish ne ay gazz? Gida, addezii zaaridi “izi nabeko” gides.
JOH 9:18 Ayhudati addeza yellida ayeyrane aawara xeeygsi eehisana gakanas addezii kase qooqe gididdaysa ammanibeytena.
JOH 9:19 Isttka (yelidayta) “inte nusi qooqe nay yelletdes giza nazi hayse? histtin hai wanidi xeelana danddaide?” gida.
JOH 9:20 Yellidaytka hizzgi zaarida “izi nu na gididaysane qooqe gididi yelletdaysa errosu.
JOH 9:21 Hai qasse izi wani xeelana danddaidakone iza ayfe oonni pogidakone nu erroko, izi bena danddaidade gidida gish izi ba gish yootanas danddaees, iza oychchitee” gida.
JOH 9:22 Iza yellidayt hessaththo giday oonnika Yesussa izi Kristtossa giidi markkatday wuri ayhudata woosafe godistana mala Ayhudati kase seera oththida gish ayhudatas babidi gida.
JOH 9:23 Hesa gish iza yellidayt izi bena danddaidade gidida gish iza ochchte” gida.
JOH 9:24 Kase qooqe addeza qasseka xeeygd “hayso ne tummayo yootada xoossa boncha, haysi addezi nagarancha gididaysa nu errosu” gida.
JOH 9:25 Izika “izi nagarancha gididaysa ta errike, gido attin ta kase qooqe gididarone qasse hai ta xeelizaro hano xaala errays” gides.
JOH 9:26 Istt qasse iza “izi nes ay oththide? Ne ayfeza wostt pogide?” gidi oychchida
JOH 9:27 Izika “ta intes kase yootin wozinan woth siybeykista shin hai qasse aazas zarethi siyana koyetii? inteka iza kalliizayta gidana koyet?” gides.
JOH 9:28 Hesafe guye iza “nu musse kallizadentta, ne iza kallizade gida” gi caydda.
JOH 9:29 Kase Xoossi Mussera hasaetdaysa nu erros, haysi addezi awape yidakone nu erroko.”
JOH 9:30 Addezika isttas hizzgi zaarides “izi awapekone inte erronttays malalththes, gido attin ta ayfe xeelisdadey iza.
JOH 9:31 Xoossi bes babizadene iza sheene oththizades attin nagarancha ura siyonttaysa nu eerros.
JOH 9:32 Ayfe qooqidi yelletdade ayfey xeelides gizaysa allamey medhetdasope oonnika siyy errena.
JOH 9:33 Haysadey xoossafe gidonttako hayssa ooththanas danddaena.
JOH 9:34 Isttika iza “neni ne Mule asattethay nagaran munuqettin yelletdays ne nuna tammarssana wana xaladi?” gidi iza goodida.
JOH 9:35 Addeza goodidaysa Yesussay siydes, iza demmidine “ne asa nan ammanyy?” gides.
JOH 9:36 Addezika “godo ta izan ammanana mala izi oonne?” gidi oychchides.
JOH 9:37 Yesussayka “ne iza beyadasa hai nenara hasaizay izakoo” gides.
JOH 9:38 Addezika “Godoo iza ammanadis” gidi izas hooki goyniides.
JOH 9:39 Yesussayka “qooqeti xeelana malane xeelizayti qooqana mala pirdanas ta hayssa allamezan yadiis” gides.
JOH 9:40 Izara diza parssawistape issi issi asati hessa siydi “hesi ayy guuse? histtin nuka qooqe?” gida.
JOH 9:41 Yesussayka istta inte qooqeta gididdakoo intes nagara gidena shin inte hai nu xiiloosu giza gish inte nagaray diza mala dana” gides.
JOH 10:1 Ta intes tummu gays, doorssata yire penggerape attin hara baggara guupi geliizaay kaysoone bonqqizzade.
JOH 10:2 Penggera geliizadey izi doorssata hemmiizade.
JOH 10:3 Penggee nagzadey izas penggezza doyees, doorssatka iza qaala syeetes, ba doorssata sunththara sunththara xeeygi keesses.
JOH 10:4 Beyta wursi kessidape guyee istta sinthth adhidi kalethees, doorssatika iza qaala erriza gish iza kaletees.
JOH 10:5 Immatha urra iza qaala errontta gish izafe baqatetes, attin muleka iza kaletena.
JOH 10:6 yesussay hessa lemisoza isttas yootdes, shin istt qasse izi isttas yootdaysa aykoka erribeytena.
JOH 10:7 hessa gish yesussay qasseka isttas hizzgdes, “ta isttas tummu gays doorssat penggey tana.
JOH 10:8 Tape kasse ydayt wuri kaysoone bonqqzayta doorssat gidkoo istt giza siybetena
JOH 10:9 Pengeey tana ta, ta bagara gelizadey wuri attana, gelanane kezana hemmetizasoka demmana.
JOH 10:10 Kaysooy kaysootana wodhanasine dhaysanas xaala yees, ta gidiko intes deyooy dana malane intes kehi darana mala yadsi.
JOH 10:11 Ta loo7o hemmizzade, loo7o hemiizzdey ba shmppo ba doorssata gish aththi immees.
JOH 10:12 Mishshera qaxxaretdii himmizadey gidiko doorssat izas gidoontta gish sudhumey yizza woode doorssaatii yegidii bess baqaates, sudhumeyka doorssata daf daf meesene laales.
JOH 10:13 Baqattza mishshan qaxxarettdadee gidida gishine doorssatas michchetonttagishasa gshasa.
JOH 10:14 Loo7o hemmizadeey tana tani ta doorssata errays, isttika tana erretes.
JOH 10:15 Hesika aaway tana errizaysa mala tan ta shemppota doorssata gish aththa immana.
JOH 10:16 Hayssa ha doorssa yren geloonttayt tas hara doorssat deetes, ta isttaskka ha ehanaas tas beeses, isttika ta qaala siyanane issi mehe gidana, hemmiizayskka isadee gidana.
JOH 10:17 Ta zaarada denththanas ta shemppo ta aththa immiza gish ta aaway tana dooses.
JOH 10:18 Tani ta shemppo ta dossara aththa immadsi attin oonnika tape woothii ekkeena, ta aththa immanas gidiin woykoo zaara denththans gidiin sheeney tassa, hessa he azazoza ta ta aawape ekkadis.
JOH 10:19 Hessa he qaalape denddaysan ayhudata garssan qasseka shaketeth medhetdees.
JOH 10:20 Daroo asay “iza bolla daydanthth diza gishine gooshu gidida gish inte izi gizaysa ays syeeti? gida.
JOH 10:21 Baaggayti qasse “haysii daydanththi dizaddey hayssa mala gideena, daydanthth qooqda ayfe paththi errize? gida.
JOH 10:22 Yerusalamen xoossa keehta oratho ba77ele boncho woodey gakkides, woodeyka gaalas.
JOH 10:23 Yesussay Xoossa keethth giibe gidon seloomoney simmeretzaso geetetzasora adhishshin.
JOH 10:24 Ayhudati iza gidoo aththidi “ne aydee gakanas nu wozzna hirggan gammiisanee? ne Xoos kittidade gidikoo nus qoonccsa yoota gida.
JOH 10:25 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdees “ta intes yootadiskkoo shin inte qasse ammanibeykeista, ta aawa sunththan ta oththiza malatatii ta gish yootetes.
JOH 10:26 Inte qasse ta doorssata gidoontta gish tana ammanekista.
JOH 10:27 Ta doorssatii ta qaala siyetes, taka istta errays, isttikka tana kaalletes.
JOH 10:28 Ta isttas medhina deyoo immana, muleeka istti dhayetena, istt ta kushshepe woththii ekkanas danadey oonnika dena.
JOH 10:29 Tas istta immida ta aaway wurisofee adhes, ta aawa kushshepe istta oonnika bonqqanas danddaena.
JOH 10:30 “Tanine ta aaway nu issino.”
JOH 10:31 Ayhudati iza caadanas qasseka shuchchu denththida.
JOH 10:32 Yesussayka “aawape gidida daroo gita malatata ta intena bessads, histtin ha ta besidaytape awari gish tana shuchchara caadeti? gides.
JOH 10:33 Ayudatiika “nu nena shuchchara caadizay ne coo asi gida dashe nena nerkka xoossu kessada caashsha qaala ne hasaida gishshasape attin ne loo7o ooththidaysa gish gideena” gidii izas zaarida.
JOH 10:34 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “inte wooga gidon <ta intena xoossata gadis> geeteti xaafetibeyne?
JOH 10:35 Xoossa qaalay isttas yida asata <xoossu gikoone maxaafay sharistanas danddaontta gidikoo.>
JOH 10:36 Histtin <ta Xoossa na> gida gish aaway ba shaaki dummasidaysane ha duge allame kittidaysa inte ne caayadasa gidi tana wordo aazas mooteti?
JOH 10:37 Ta aaway ooththizaysa ta oosontta aggkoo tanan ammanopite.
JOH 10:38 Ta izaththo ooththiza gidiko inte tana ammanontta aggikoka ta aaway tanan dizaysa taka izan dizaysa inte errana malane yuush qoopana mala izi ooththida malatan ammanite.”
JOH 10:39 Qasseka istti iza oykanas paacciida shin izi istta kushshepe keesi ekii bidees.
JOH 10:40 Hessafe guye Yesussay, Yanssaay kasse xammaqzasoo gede yoridanosepe he pinthth simmid hen gammides.
JOH 10:41 Daroo asay izako yides, istti qasse “Yanssay issi malataka ooththibeyna, gidoo attin hayssa addeza gish izi yootdaysi wurikka tummuko” gida.
JOH 10:42 Henkka daroo asay Yesussan ammanides.
JOH 11:1 Bittaniiya gizasoon Marammane diza manddaran Allazzare geetettizadey saketides.
JOH 11:2 Izi ishsha Allazzarey saketda Maramma kase Yesussa to bolla shiito gusada Yesussa to ba huee iththken quccdaroko.
JOH 11:3 Hayt michchet “Godo ne dosizaysi saketdes” gidi asse yesussako kittida.
JOH 11:4 Yesussay hessa siyd ha sakoy xoossa nay izan bonchetana malane Xoossi bonchetanasafe attin iza hayqqos gaththizaz dena” gides.
JOH 11:5 Yesussay martta izi michchyo marammone Allazare siqqees.
JOH 11:6 Gido attin Allazarey saketdaysa siyy woththdii hen ba dizason namm7u gaalas gammides.
JOH 11:7 Hessafe guye bena kaallizayta “anee Yuhuda bitta simm boosu” gides.
JOH 11:8 Isttika “asttammare! guththa wodepe kasse asay nena shuchchara caadana koyshshina, ne qasse hai hee simma banee? gida.
JOH 11:9 Yesussay isttas “issi gaalasan tammane namm7u sateey dees gidenee? Gaalasara hammutiza urray ha allameza poo7on simmeretontta gish dhubetena.
JOH 11:10 dhubeetzadey gidikoo qamara hammutizadee, gasooyka poo7oy bayndda gishasa.” gides.
JOH 11:11 Hessa isttas yootdape guye “nu lagge Allazarey ziniides, taka iza dhiskkofee denththana bayss” gides.
JOH 11:12 Iza kaallizati iza “godoo! izi dhiskkda gidiko denddana” gida.
JOH 11:13 Yesussay isttas hessa yootday iza hayqqo gishasa shin ia kallizaytas qasse dhiskko gish yootida milatides
JOH 11:14 hasa gish qoonccera isttas “Allazarey hayqqdes
JOH 11:15 Inte ammanana mala ta hen dontta aggdays inte gish tana uhaaththaayses, hai gidiko ane gede izako boos” gides.
JOH 11:16 Qasse Diidmoosa geeetza Toomasay hankoo yesussa kallizayta “ane nuka bidi izara isife hayqqos” gides.
JOH 11:17 Yesussay bi gakishshn Allazarey haqqi moogetin oydu galas gidides
JOH 11:18 Biitanyaay Yerussalamepe baga satee oge hakes.
JOH 11:19 Istta ishsha hayqqo gish Marammone martta minththethanas daroo ayhuda asay isttako shiqides.
JOH 11:20 Yesussay yidaysa Marttay siyada iza mooka ekana badusu, Maramma gidiko soon uttadus.
JOH 11:21 Marttay Yesussa hizzgadusu “godoo! ne han dizakoo ta ishshay hayqqenako shin.
JOH 11:22 Haika gidiko ne woosida wursi xoossi nes immanayssa ta errays.”
JOH 11:23 Yesussayka izis “ne ishshay denddana” gides.
JOH 11:24 Marttay qasse “wurisethan denththa wode izi denddanaysa ta errays” gadus.
JOH 11:25 Yesussayka izis hizzgidess “dethine deyooy tanakoo, tana ammanizadey hayqqikoka paxa dana.
JOH 11:26 Tanan dizadeyne tana ammanizadey muleka hayqqena, hessa ne ammanay?”
JOH 11:27 Izaka zaarada “ee goodo neni duge ha allameza Kitteti Xoossa na gididaysa ta ammanays” gadus.
JOH 11:28 hessa gadane simmada ba michchiyo Marammo dumma xeeyga kessada “Asttammarey nena koyes” gadus.
JOH 11:29 Marammaka hessa siyda mala elela denddada izaka badus.
JOH 11:30 Hessa gakanas Yesussay Marttara gaggdason dees attin gede manddara garss gelbeyana
JOH 11:31 Marammo minththeethishe izira soon diza Ayudatika maramma puthurkku ga eqqada kezdaysa beydii iza allazare duhaaththao achchan yekkana bizza milatin izo kaallida.
JOH 11:32 Maramma Yesussay dizaso gakka iza demmida mala iza too bolla guhaaththaanada “godo ne han dizakoo ta ishshay hayqqenakoo shin” gadus.
JOH 11:33 Izane izo kaali yida Ayhudati yekizaysa Yesussay beydi daroo michcheetdii
JOH 11:34 “Iza awan moggidet?” gidii oychchdes, isttka “godo hayada beeya” gida.
JOH 11:35 Yesussayka ayhaaththaunxxdes.
JOH 11:36 Ayhudatika “izi iza ay mala sqqzakoo beeyti” gida.
JOH 11:37 Istta garssafe issi issi asati haysi qooqe addeza ayfe pogdaysii hayssadey hayqqontta mala oththanas danddaene shin?” gida.
JOH 11:38 Yesussay iza wozanay michchetin gede duhaaththaoko bides, duhaaththaozika shuchchara tuccettda gonggollo.
JOH 11:39 Izika istta “shuchcha denththte” gides, hayqqdaysa michchya Marttay “godo izi hayqqin hach oydu gaalas gidida gish xinqqanako” gadus.
JOH 11:40 Yesussayka “ne ammaniza gidiko Xoossa boncho beyanddasa gada nes ta yootabeykna?” gides.
JOH 11:41 Hessa gish shuchcha denththida, Yesussayka pudee xeellidi hizzgdees. “ta aawawu ne ta giza siydda gish ta nena galatays.
JOH 11:42 Ne wuriso gaalas ta giza siyzaysa ta errays, gido attin ta hessa giday hayssan eqqda asati ne tana kittidaysa ammanana malasa.
JOH 11:43 Yesussay hessa gidape kaallethidii qaala dhoqqu histtdii “Allazare! ha kezza” gidii xeeygdes.
JOH 11:44 Hayqqda Allazareyka kumeththa asatethay moogo mayoon xaxetda mala duhaaththaope kezides, Yesussayka birsh yedite boo gides.
JOH 11:45 Hessa gish Marammo minththethana yida ayhudatape daroo asay yesussay ooththdaysa beeyd izan ammanides.
JOH 11:46 Isttafe baaggat bidi Yesussay ooththdaysa parssawistas yootda.
JOH 11:47 Hessa qeessista halaqqatnee Parssaweti Ayhudata duulata shiqqana mala xeeygd, hizzgda “ha addezii daroo dumma malatata oththdade gidida gish nu ay oththko loo7o?”
JOH 11:48 Nu coou gikko asi wuri iza ammananane oroome asayka yidi nu biittane nu asa nupe ekkana.”
JOH 11:49 Istta garssafe isaddey he laythth qeessistas wana halaqqa qayapaay hizzgdees, “inte aykooka errekkista.
JOH 11:50 Deerey wuri dhayanape dere gish issi urray hayqqkoo loo7o gidanayssa yushsh qoopeeketii.”
JOH 11:51 Izi hessa beepe gidoontta he layth izi qeessistas halaqqa gidida gish Yesussay Ayhuda dere gish sinththafe hayqqanaysa gish yootdes.
JOH 11:52 Izi hayqqanay He dere asas xalala gidoontta kase laleetda Xoossa naytaka isibolla shishshanasko.
JOH 11:53 He gaalasafe ha simmin iza wodhanas maqqetda.
JOH 11:54 Hessa gish Yesussay he gaalasafe ha simmin Ayhudata garssan qoonccera simmeretibeyna, gidoo attin dugge bazoo bitta matan dizza ehaaththareeme geetetza katamay diza poqqethaso bidi bena kaallizaytara hen tkkides.
JOH 11:55 Ayhudati paziga ba77eley matda mala ba77eley gakkanape kase gesho woga ooththanas daroo asay dumma dumma derepe Yerusalame yidees.
JOH 11:56 Asay yesussa koyshshe xoossa keeththan eqqdi ba garssan isay isaa “intes ay milatzee? ba77elezas yeenesha?” gides.
JOH 11:57 Qeessista halaqatine parssawet qasse Yesussa oykanass izi awan dizakoone errizadey isttas mlatana mala kase azazii woththiida.
JOH 12:1 Paziga ba77eles buro usuppun gaalas attishin Yesussay hayqqope denththida Allazarey dizaso biitaniya bides.
JOH 12:2 hen Yesussas kawo kaththida Marttay iza kawo muzishin izara isife maaddan uttdaytape issay Allazareko.
JOH 12:3 Maramma daroo allo7o wagara shameetda liitroo bagga gidiza geshsha nardoosa shittoo ekka yada Yesussa too bolla gussada tooza ba huee ithkera quccadus, keethaka shittoo sawoy kummidees.
JOH 12:4 Yesussa kaalliizaytape issay Yesussa aththi immana Asqqoroto Yudday hessa ixxid
JOH 12:5 “Haysi shittoozi heedzdzu xeetu dinares bayzeetdii miishshay aazas manqqotas immetbeynee?” gides.
JOH 12:6 Izi hessa giday mishsha shishshza karaxxte oykkzadey iza gididda gish shiqqza mishshafe bees shishshdi goetzadee gidida gishasa, attin manqqotas michchetdii gidena.
JOH 12:7 Yesussa qasse hizzgdees “haysi shittoozi tas mooggo gaalasas qoofetdaz gidida gish he woode gakkanaas iza ba achchan nagu bochchofte.
JOH 12:8 Manqqooti ay woodeka intenara detees, gidoo attin inte tana wuriso woode demmekista.”
JOH 12:9 He woode daroo Ayhuda asati Yesussay hen dizaysa erridi izakoo yida, yidaytkka yesussa xalala koyda gidoontta Yesussay hayqqoope denththida Allazareka beyanaskko.
JOH 12:10 Hessa gish qeessata halaqati Yesussara Allazareka gathii wodhanas ba garssan zooretda.
JOH 12:11 Hessika Allazare gedoon daroo Ayhuda asay Yesussako bi bidi iza ammaniiza gishasiko.
JOH 12:12 Wonttetha gaalas ba77eleza bonchana yida derey Yesussay Yerusalame yizaysa siydees.
JOH 12:13 Zammba heyththi ekkdi Yesussa mokkan kezzdes, derey qaala dhoqu histtdi hizzgdes “hosaeena!” goda sunththan yiza isiraele kawooy anjjetdade!”
JOH 12:14 Kase “hane! xiyonee nayee baboofa! hekoo ne kawooy haree gutte toogdii yess” geetetii xaafetda mala Yesussay hare gutte demmidi toogiides.
JOH 12:16 Iza kaallizayti hessa wuris koyyro wozinan woththbeytana, iza gish xaafettdaysane izas ooththetda hanoka wuris Yesussay hayqqope denddidape guye errida.
JOH 12:17 Al77ezare duhaaththaope xeeygidi hayqqope denththida woode ezara isife diza asay iza denththa gish markkattda.
JOH 12:18 Daroo asayka izi hessa mala giita malata ooththidaysa siydi iza mokkana kezides.
JOH 12:19 Hessa gish parssaweti ba garssan isay issa “histtin ay ooththana danddaizoon? Beyte! kummetha derey atoontta iza kaalles” gida.
JOH 12:20 Goynanas ba77elezas shiqqda asa garssan girrike dere asatika dettes.
JOH 12:21 Isttika gaalila garssan diza beete sayda geetettza dere ass pilphphosa geetetzadeko bidi “Goodo nu Yesussa beeyana koyos” gida.
JOH 12:22 pilphphosayka inddirasas yootdes, inddirasayne pilphphosay bidi Yesussas yootda.
JOH 12:23 Yesussayka isttas hizzgdes “heko asa nay bonchetza saatey gakkides.
JOH 12:24 Ta intes tummu gays gistte ayfey biitan wodhada hayqqontta coou ga uttko berkka atawus, iza hayqqza gidiko hara daroo ayfawusu.
JOH 12:25 Be shemhaaththao dosizadey dhaysess, hayssa biita bolla ba shemhaaththao ixxizadey gidiko medhina deyooy nages.
JOH 12:26 Tas ooththana koyzadey tana, tas ooththzadey ta dizason dana, tas ooththzade ta aaway iza bonchana.
JOH 12:27 Qasseka Yesussay hizzgdes “heko ta shemhaaththaoya mettotadus <aabo! ha saateype tana ashsha goosha?> ta hizzgonta mala ta yiday hano ha metto saateysiko.
JOH 12:28 aabo! ne ne sunththa boncha” hessafe kaalid “ta ta sunthth bonchadis, qasseka gujja bonchana” giza qaalay salope yides.
JOH 12:29 Hen gadan eqqda asay hessa siydi “daday dadates” gida, baggayti qasse “kitanchako hasaizadey” gida.
JOH 12:30 Yesussay hizzgdes “haysi giirethay yiday inte gishasa attin ta gish gidena.
JOH 12:31 Haysi allamey pirdistana woodey hayssa, hayssa dereza hariza xalaey hai gede kare yegistana.
JOH 12:32 Tani dhoqqu gada kaqqetza woode asa wursa tako zaarana.”
JOH 12:33 Yesussay hessa yootday izi ay mala hayqqo hayqqanakoo errisanasiko.
JOH 12:34 Asay qasse “nu woogan xaafettday <xoossay kittidadey medhinas dana> ges histtin ne qasse wanada <asa nay dhoqu gi kaqqistana beses> gazz? ne giza asanay awaysee?” gidi oychchida.
JOH 12:35 Yesussay isttas hizzgdes “hai guutha woodes intenara poo7oy des, gadey dhumontta poo7ora hamutite, qamara hamutzadey izi awa bizakonee errena.
JOH 12:36 Inte poo7o nayta gidana mala poo7oy dishin poo7on ammanite” Yesussay hessa gidape guye bidi istta ayfepe gemmides.
JOH 12:37 Yesussay isttas hessa mala malata istta sinththan ooththinkka ayhudat izan ammanbbeytena.
JOH 12:38 Hesi haniday nabe isiyasay “goodo! nu markkatethi ammaniday oonne? Xoossa qaalay ooss qonccide?” gidi
JOH 12:39 Hessa gish ammananas danddaibeytena, gasooyka nabe isiyasay kase hizzgii xaafida gishshasiko.
JOH 12:40 “Isttii ba ayfen beeydi, ba wozinan yushshi qoopidi simmontta malane izi istta paththontta mala Xoossi istta ayfe qooqisides, istta wozinaka mumisides.”
JOH 12:41 Isiyasay hessa giday xoossay kittidade boncho beeyida gishshasa, hessa gish hessa Yesussay geesh yootdes.
JOH 12:42 Gidikoka ayhudista halaqatape daroo asay Yesussa ammanides, gido attin istta ayhudata woosa keethafe godontta mala parssawistas babiidi ba ammano qonccen markkatibeeytena.
JOH 12:43 Istti hessaththo haniday isttas Xoossafe immettza bonchofe aththidi asape immetza boncho dosida gishasa.
JOH 12:44 Yesussay ba qaala dhoqu histtdii hizzgides “tana ammanizadey tanan xalala gidontta tana kittdadenkka ammanes.
JOH 12:45 Tana beeydadey tana kittdadeeka beeyana.
JOH 12:46 Tana ammanizay wuri dhuman dontta mala ta poo7o gidada hayssa ha allameza yadis.
JOH 12:47 Ta qaala siydi oosonttade bolla pirdanay tana gidike, gasooyka ta yiday dere ashshanas attin dere bolla pirdanas gidena.
JOH 12:48 Tana koyonttadene ta qaala ekkonttade bolla pirdanadey dees, ta izas yootda qaalay wuriseththa gaalas iza bolla pirdana.
JOH 12:49 Gasooyka tani coo ta sheeneni yootabeyke, ta gizaysane ta yootza azazo tas immiday tana kittda ta aawako.
JOH 12:50 Iza azazoy medhina deyoo gididaysa ta errays, hessa gish ta yootzay wuri aaway tas yootdaysako.
JOH 13:1 He woodeyka ayhudata paziga ba77elepe kase Yesussay hayssa allameza yedidi aawako bana saatey gakkiidaysa erridees, hayssa allamezan diza ba baggata wuris sqqides, wurisethi gakkanaasika dosides.
JOH 13:2 Yesussayne iza kaallizayt isife kawo mishshin simmona nay Asqqoroto Yuday Yesussa aththi immana mala xalaey iza wozinan iita qoofa gelththides.
JOH 13:3 Yesussay aaway izas godateth wursi immidaysane izi xoossa achchafe kezidi yidaysa, qase simmidi xoossako banaysa erress.
JOH 13:4 Hessa gish maada bollafe denddine mayoo qaari woththdi pooxa ekkdi xeesan gixxides.
JOH 13:5 Too meecciza gonggen hathth gujjidi bena kaallizayta too meeche oykkdes, ba gixxida pooxanika meccida tooza quccides.
JOH 13:6 Yesussay Simmona geetetza phixirosako shiiqn Simmona geetetza phixirosay iza “goodo! ne ta too meccanee?” gides.
JOH 13:7 Yesussayka “tani ooththizaysa ne hai erraka guyepe qass ne erranddasa” gides.
JOH 13:8 Phixirossayka “ne ta too mulleka meeccaka” gides, Yesussay qasse “ta ne too meeccontta aggiko nesnne tas isifetethi dena” gides.
JOH 13:9 Simmona geetettza phixirossayka zaaridi “goodo hessa gidiko tas too xalala gidontta kushshera hueera wursa meecca” gides.
JOH 13:10 Yesussay qasse “ba asatethi meeccetdades kummetha bollay geshshi gidida gish izas too meechafe attin hara koshshena, inte gesha shin wuri gidekista” gides.
JOH 13:11 Yesussay “inte wurikka gesh gidekista” giday iza aththi immanadey oonnakone erriza gishshsiko.
JOH 13:12 Istta too meeccidape guye ba mayoo eeki maydii kase ba uttdasoo simmi uttdes, qasse isttas hizzgides “ta intes ay ooththidakone wozinan woththideti?
JOH 13:13 Inte tana asttammarene goda gista ta qass asttammarene goda gidida gish inte guusay tummuko.
JOH 13:14 Histtkoo ta intes godane asttammare gidashe inte too meeccza gidiko inteka inte garssan isay issa too meeccana beses.
JOH 13:15 Ta intes ooththdaysa mala inteka ooththana mala ta intes lemmuiso besadis.
JOH 13:16 Ta intes tummu gays ashshikaray godape adhena, kittetda urray kittidadepe adhena.
JOH 13:17 Inte hayssa erridi ooson peyshshiko inte anjjetidayta.
JOH 13:18 Ta hayssa gizay inte wurisota gish gidena, tani ta doridayta wursa errays, gido attin ta kaathi midadeey ta morkke gididi ta bolla denddides giza maxaafa qaalay poletenas koshshes.
JOH 13:19 Ta hayssa haira intes yootzay izi poletza woode ta oonnakone inte ammanana malako.
