JOH 13:20 Ta intes tummu gays ta kittdadee ekkizzadey tana ekes, tana ekkizadey tana kittdade ekkes.
JOH 13:21 Yesussay hessa gi simmidi kezi qoofan gelidinee “ta intes tummu gays inte garssafe isadey tana aththi immana” gidi qonccen yootdes.
JOH 13:22 Iza kaallizayt hessa izi oonna gish gidakone errontta gish ba garssan isay isara xeeletdes.
JOH 13:23 Iza kaallizzayta garssafe Yesussay siqqiza isay Yesussa achchan uttides.
JOH 13:24 Simmona geetettza phixirossay Yanssa sommii besidi “izi oonna gish gizakone ane iza oychcha” gides.
JOH 13:25 Hessa gish izi ba qodhe gede Yesussa hayththako shishshidi “godo! izi oonne? gidi oychchdes.
JOH 13:26 Yesussayka zaaridi “izadey ta hai budena woxen dhim77eda barssizade” gides, hessa gi simmid budena woxen dhim77i ekkid asiqorotepe yida simmona na yuda barisides.
JOH 13:27 Yuday iza badhida mala herakka xalaeey izan gelides, Yesussayka Yuda “ne ooththanays qoopidaysa elela ooththa” gides.
JOH 13:28 Yesussay hessa aazas gidakoone maadan uttda asape gelidadey oonnika dena.
JOH 13:29 Yuday mishshe oykizade gidida gish Yesussa kaallizayttape baggat Yesussay yuda ba77elezas koshshizaysa shaama woykoo manqqootas muxata iima” gida milatdes.
JOH 13:30 Yudayka budena badhida mala herakka kezzidi bides, izi bishin gadeey qammako.
JOH 13:31 Yuday kezii bidape guye Yesussay hizzgdes “asa nay hai bonchetdes, iza gaason Xoossika bonchetdes.
JOH 13:32 Xoossi iza gaason bonchetza gidiko Xoossika iza bonchana, heraka gam77ontta bonchana.
JOH 13:33 Ta Naytoo, ta intenara daroo wode gam77ike inte tana koyana ta kase ayhudata halaqattasika “ta bizzaso inte yana danddaekeista gada yootda mala haika intesiika hessaththo yootays.
JOH 13:34 Inte inte garssan isay isara siqqistana mala ta intes oraththa azazo immays” ta intena siqqda mala inte inte garssan isay isara siqqetite.
JOH 13:35 Inte inte garssan siqqetkoo inte tana kaallizayta gididayssa asii wuri errana”
JOH 13:36 Hessafe guye Simmona geetettza phixirossay yesussa “Godo! ne awa bane?” gidii oychchdes, Yesussay qasse “ta bizasoo ne hai tana kaalana dandda7eka shin guyepe ne tana kaalana” gides.
JOH 13:37 Phixirossayka “Godo! ta nena hai kaalanas ays dandda7ikna? haray attoshshin tani ta shemhaaththaoka ne gish aththa immana” gides.
JOH 13:38 Yesussayka zaaridi ne ne shemhaaththao ta gish aththa immanee? ta nes tummu gays hachchi kuttooy wasanape kasistada ne tana hedzdzu to kadana” gidi zaaridees.
JOH 14:1 Kaalleththdka Yesussay hizzgdes “inte wozinay metotetoofo Xoossu ammanitee, tanaka ammanite.
JOH 14:2 Ta aawa achchan daroo dusasooy des, hessa gidonttakko <intes danaso gigisanasa ta bana gana shin.
JOH 14:3 Bada ta intes soo gigisidape guyee inte ta dizason dana mala ta simma yada intena ekkana.
JOH 14:4 Ta biza ogge inte errista.”
JOH 14:5 Tomassay “Godo! ne awa bizakoone nu errokoshin, oggezza nu wostt erranas danddaeizon?” gides.
JOH 14:6 Yesussayka izas hizzgi zaarides “oggeyne, tummay, deyooyka tanakoo, ta baggara gidikofe attin oonnika awako bana urray dena.
JOH 14:7 Inte tana errizako ta aawaka erranakooshin, hia hayssafe guyee inte iza errana iza beeyoka beydista.”
JOH 14:8 Pilphphosayka Godo! Ne nu aawa beesiiko nuss gidana” gides.
JOH 14:9 Yesussayka izas hizzgides “Pilphphosa! hayssa wode gakanas ta intenara deynkka ne tana erriki? tana be7ida urray aawaka be7ides, histtin neni wanada “nuna aawa besa gazi?
JOH 14:10 Tani ta awan, ta aawayka tanan dizaysa ammaniki? ta intes yootza qaala yootzay ta sheene mala gidena, gido attin oosoza wuris ooththizay tana diza aawako.
JOH 14:11 Tan aawan diza mala aawayka tanan dizaysa inte ammanite, akaye gikoo ta ooththiza oththota gishika tana ammanite.
JOH 14:12 Ta intes tummu gays, tana ammanizadey ta ooththiza ooso oththana, hessafeka aththana, gasooyka tani aawako bana.
JOH 14:13 Aaway naza gaason bonchetana mala inte ta sunththan woosidaysa ta intes wursa ooththana.
JOH 14:14 Inte ay mishsheka ta sunththan woosidaysa wursa ta oththana.
JOH 14:15 Inte tana doosiza gidiko ta azazoyo nagite.
JOH 14:16 Tani aawa woosana, izika intenara medhinasa dana mala hara intena menththeththanade intes immana.
JOH 14:17 Haysi minththeththiza ayanay dere asay iza beey errontt gish allamey ekkanas danddaontta tummu ayana gido attin inte iza errata, gasooyka izi intenara diza gishine izi inte gaththan diza gishasa.
JOH 14:18 Aayane aaway bayndda naytta mala ta intena xalala agiike, ta simmada ha inteko yana.
JOH 14:19 Guththa wodepe guye dere asay tana beeyena shin inte gidiko beeyanddista, tani deyoon diza gish inteka deyoon danddeista.
JOH 14:20 Tani ta aawan diza mala inteka tanan dizaysane taka intenan dizaysa inte he wode erranddista.
JOH 14:21 Ta azazoo ekkidi ooththiza urray tana dosees, tana dosiizadeka ta aaway dooses, taka iza dosana, tanaka izades qoonccisana.
JOH 14:22 Asqqoroto Yudda gidontta hankko Yuday “Godo! neni dere asas gidontta nuss wostta qonccisane” gides.
JOH 14:23 Yesussayka izas hizzgdes. “tana siqqizadey ta qaala nagana, ta aawayka iza dosana, nuni izako yana, yidika izadeera isipee deyana.
JOH 14:24 Tana dosonttadey ta qaala nagena, haysi inte siyza qaalay tana kittida ta aawa qaalape attin ta qaala gidena.
JOH 14:25 Tani hai intenara dashe hayssa intes yootdes.
JOH 14:26 Aaway ta sunththan yedana minththethiza xiilo ayanay qass haniza wuris intena tammarssana, ta intes yootoysaka wuris inte wozinan woththana mala maadana
JOH 14:27 Ta intes sarooteth aggada bays, ta sarootethika ta intes immana, ta intes immiza sarootethi derey immiza sarooteththa mala gidena, inte wozinay hirggofoone baboofo.
JOH 14:28 Ta bana, badaka intekoo simma yana gada ta intes kase yootidaysa siydista, inte tana doszzako ta ta aawako bizays intena uhaaththaaysanakoshin gasooyka aaway tape adhdhes.
JOH 14:29 Haysi haniza wode inte ammanana mala hasysa intes kasista yootadays.
JOH 14:30 Hayssa allameza hariza xalaeey yizza wodey gakkiida gish hai ta intenara daroo hasaiike, izi ta bolla aykooka ooththanas izas wolqay deena.
JOH 14:31 Gido attin tanii aawa dosizaysa derey errana mala aaway tana azazidaysa ta wursa polana anee hayssafe boos denddite.
JOH 15:1 Qasseka Yesussay hizzgdes “tummu woyne miththa anoy tana, akakilitteza ooththanchay ta aawa.
JOH 15:2 Ta bolla dishe ayfe immoontta hangge wuris ta aaway qanxxii diigana, ayfiza hangge gujji ayfaana mala qirxxi geshshana.
JOH 15:3 ta intes yootda qaala gaason inte hai geshshata.
JOH 15:4 Tanan diite, taka intenan dana, hanggey woyne ano bolla doontta aggiko berkka ayfe ayfana danddaonttaysa mala inteka tanan doontta dishshe ayfee ayfanas danddaekista.
JOH 15:5 Tane woyne miththa ano, inte qass hanggista, daroo ayfee ayfizadey tanan dizadene taka izan dizade, gasooyka ta bayndda inte aykoka ooththanas danddaekista.
JOH 15:6 Tanan baynddadeey qanxxetidi woora yegetida hangge mala kare yegetidi hen melana, heyta mala hanggista issi bolla shiqqid taman yegistanane exxana.
JOH 15:7 Inte tanan diiko ta qaalayka intenan diiko inte koydaysa oychchiko demmana.
JOH 15:8 Daroo ayfee inte ayfishin ta aaway bonchetes, hessa malan inte tana kaallizayta gididaysi hessan erristana.
JOH 15:9 Aaway tana dosiidaysatho taka intena dosadis, hessa gish inte ta siqqoon diite.
JOH 15:10 Tani ta aawa azazo polada iza siqqoon deyda mala inteka ta azazoo poliko ta siqqoon deyana.
JOH 15:11 Haysa ta intes yootzay ta uhaaththaaysii intenan gidana malane inte uhaaththaaysiika kumethth gidanasiko.
JOH 15:12 Ta intes immiza azazoy ta intena siqqida mala inteka inte garssan isay isara siqqistanasiko.
JOH 15:13 Asi ba lagees ba shemhaaththao aththii immope adhiiza siqqooy deena.
JOH 15:14 Ta Intena ta azazii wursi inte poliko inte ta laggeta.
JOH 15:15 Ashshikaray goday ooththizaysa erroontta gish simma hayssafe guyee ta intena ashshikarata giikee, gido attin tani ta aawape siydaysa wursa intes qonccisiida gish ta intena ta laggeta gadiis.
JOH 15:16 Ta intena doradiis attin inte tana doribeykista, inte bidi daroo ayfee ayfana mala inte ayfeey eeqi dana mala ta intena wothadis, hessa gish inte ta sunththan woosidaysa wursi aaway intes immana.
JOH 15:17 hessa gish inte intee garssan isay isara siqqistana mala ta intena azazays.
JOH 15:18 Kaalethidika Yesussay hizzgdes. “intena derey ixxiko intefee kase tana ixxidaysa errite.
JOH 15:19 Inte ammanoontta dere asa gidikoo dere asay ba bagga gididade doses, gido attin inte dere bagga gidontta gish ta intena derepe shakkada dorida gish derey intena ixxees.
JOH 15:20 Ashshikaray godape adhena gada ta kase intes yootoysa yushsh qoopite, istti tana godizayti intenaka goddana, istt ta qaala naggizako inte qaala naggana.
JOH 15:21 Istti tana kittidade errontta gish ta gaason inte bolla hessa wursi ooththana.
JOH 15:22 Ta yada isttas yootonttako isttas nagara gidenashin, hai qass istta nagaras haano giza gasooy bawa.
JOH 15:23 Tana ixxizadey ta aawaka ixxes.
JOH 15:24 Hara urray oosontta ooso ta istta garssan oosonttako isttas nagara gideenashin hai istt hessa wursi beeydape guyee tanaka ta aawaka ixxida.
JOH 15:25 Hessika handday kase <tana gasooy bayndda dishin ixxida> geetetdi istta wogan xaafetda qaalay polistanasiko.
JOH 15:26 “Gido attin aawape kezidi yanays taka ta aawa achchafe intes yedanays tumma ayanay minththethzays yidi izi ta gish markkatana.
JOH 15:27 Inte koyropeka tanara diza gish tas inteka markkatanddista.”
JOH 16:1 Qasseka yesussay hizzgdes “hekoo hayssa wursa ta intes inte ammanoy yarkketoope gada yootadiis.
JOH 16:2 Isttii intena ba keethape goodana, haray attoshshin intena wodhizadeey wuri xoossas ooththzade milatza wodey yana.
JOH 16:3 Istt hessaththo ooththizaay tanaka ta aawaka errontta gishshasa.
JOH 16:4 Ta hayssa intes hessa gakiza wode inte ta intes gidaysa qoopanasiko.” kaalleththidika yesussa hizzgdes “hayssa wursa ta intes yootontta aggiday ta intenara isife diza gishshasa.
JOH 16:5 Hai qasse tana kittdaysako bana gays gido attin intefe oonnika <awaa ne bane? gidi oychchanay bawa.
JOH 16:6 Gido attin hayssa wursa ta intes yootda gish inte wozinay muzetes.
JOH 16:7 Ta qasse tummu intes gays ta busii intes goo7e gidana, gasooyka ta bontta aggiko minththethiza ayanay intekoo yeena, ta bidappe guye iza intekoo yedana.
JOH 16:8 Izi yidi asa nagara gishine xiilotetha gish qasseka pirda gish errisana.
JOH 16:9 Asa nagara gish izi errisanay asay tana ammanoontta gishshasa
JOH 16:10 Xiiloteththa gish izi asa errisanay tani ta aawako buusa gishshine qasse namm7enththo inte tana beeyontta gishshasa.
JOH 16:11 Pirda gish izi errisanay hayssa dereza aysiza bolla pirdetda gishshasa.
JOH 16:12 Ta intes buuro yootana daroo yoy des gido attin hai intena dexxan.
JOH 16:13 Tumu ayanay yidi intena tumay dizaso kaalleththana, gasooyka izi siiydaysa yotana attin bepee gidontta gish izi sinththafe hanana yoota intes yootana.
JOH 16:14 Tas dizaysape ekkidi izi intes yootza gish tana bonchana.
JOH 16:15 Aawas gididay wurikka taysa <tas gididaysape ekkidi izi intes yootana> ta gidday hessasa.”
JOH 16:16 Yesussay gujjidi hizzgdes “guththa wodepe guye inte tana beeyekista, qasseka guththa wodepe guye inte tana beeyana.”
JOH 16:17 Iza kaallizaytape baggati ba garssan “haysii nus guththa wodeepe guye inte tana beeyekista qasseka guththa wodeepe guye inte tana beeyana, qasse ta aawako bana> gusii ayy guse? gida.
JOH 16:18 “Histtin haysi <guththa wodepe guye> gizaysi izi aze? izi yootzays nus erretena” gidi ba garssan zar zar oychchetida.
JOH 16:19 Istti iza oychchanaysa Yesussay erridi isttas hizzgdess “inte inte garssan isay isara oychchetzay ta intes “guththa wodepe guye inte nana byyekista qadeeka gutha woodepe guye inte tana beyanaa> gida gshshasee?
JOH 16:20 Ta intes tuma gays inte yekanashshb derey gidiko ufaana inte mmchistanashn inte mmchchy ufayydan ufaaysan lamistana.
JOH 16:21 Maccashii yeloo woodey gakiishn mixxasii hrigayysu shn naa yella yegidapee guyee bista boola nay yelletda gish uhaaththaasafe dendayssan kase ba wayedaysa zara qoopuku.
JOH 16:22 Hesatho inteeka hii mchchetista (yekista) qase ta intena beyana inte wozinaykka uhaaththaaeistana inte uhaaththaaysa zarii ekanadeey deena.
JOH 16:23 “Inte he woode tape aykooka wosedeista ta intes tumu gayys ta sunththa ta awa wosiiko intes wursikka iimana.
JOH 16:24 Hano gakanas inte ta sunththa aykooka wosi eerekista wosiite inte eekana inte uhaaththaaysaykka kumeeththa gidana.
JOH 16:25 “Hii gakanas ta intes lemussora yootadis shn hyssafe huye ta lemusoora yotonta wodde yana gidoo atiin awa gish intes wurssa qoonccsa yootana.
JOH 16:26 He wode inte ta nththan wosana taka <awa inte gish wosana> gikke.
JOH 16:27 Gasooyka away ba bagara intena dosiiza gishshasa away intena dosiizay inte tana dosiiza gishshasane ta Xoossa achchafe ydaysa intee amaniida gishshasa.
JOH 16:28 Tani awa achchfe kezzada hausa ha 7llamee yadissne qaseeka h 7llameza agada awako ta sima bana.”
JOH 16:29 Iza kaliizay hzgida “heko ne hii lemuson gidoonta nus qonccer yotadasaa.
JOH 16:30 Ne ubbaa eeriza malane oniika nena oycchcchanas koshontayssa hii nu eridassa hessa gishsha ne Xoossa achchafe kezidayysa nu amanoos.”
JOH 16:31 Yesussayistas hzgides “intee hii amaniidista”
JOH 16:32 Gdoo atiin inte intee bagara laleetda tana xala agana wodeyy gakiides he satiyka hii gakkadus gidoo atiin away tanara gidida gish ta tarka gidiike.
JOH 16:33 Ta hyysa intes yotizzay inte tanan deyyn intees sarotithii dana malla gada yotaays inte h 7llameen dishshn intes wayeyy dees gidoo atiin aykooy ba ta 7llamee xoondees.”
JOH 17:1 Yesussay hessa gidape guye pudee salo dhoqqu gi xeelid hizzgi wossides “aaboo hekoo hai saatey gakkides, ne nay nena bonchana mala neni ne naza boncha.
JOH 17:2 Ne bonchanayka ne izas immidaytas izi medhina deyoo immana mala ne izas asa wuriso bolla godateth immida gishshasa.
JOH 17:3 Medhdhina deyooyka ne xalala tumu xoossu ne kiittda Yesuss Kiristtoosa erro guusa.
JOH 17:4 Ne tas immida ooso tani wursada ha biita bolla nena bonchadis.
JOH 17:5 Ta aawa! allamey medhdhistanape kase tas nenara diza bonchon haika tana ne achchan bonchariki
JOH 17:6 Haysa dere asape ne tas deeran immida asatas ne oonnakone ta isttas nena qonccsadis, istt kaseka neyta shin ne tas immadasa, isttika ne qaala nagida.
JOH 17:7 Ne tas immidaysi wurikka nepe gididaysa hai istti errida.
JOH 17:8 Ne tas immida qaalataka isttas immadis, isttika ekkida, ta ne achchafe yidaysa tumape errida, ne tana kittdaysaka istt ammanida.
JOH 17:9 “Ta isttas wossays heytii ne tas immidayt istt neyta gidida gish ta isttas wossays, gidoshin hinkoo dere asas wossike.
JOH 17:10 Tas gididay wurikka neysa neysika wurikka taysa, taka isttan bonchetana.
JOH 17:11 Hayssafe guye Tani hayssa biita bolla diike, istt gidiko ha biita bolla deetes, hai ta nekoo bays, ta geshshazo! hayta ne tas immidayta istti nu mala ba garssan issino gidana mala ne tas immida ne sunththan istta naga.
JOH 17:12 Ta isttara isipe dashshe ne tas immida ne sunththan ta istta naggadis, ta naggadis, hessa gish kase xaafetda geshsha maxafa qaalay polistana mala izi kaseka dhayos diza nazape attin isttafe oonnika dhaybeyna.
JOH 17:13 Ta qasse hai neko bays, ta ha biita bolla dashshe hayssa yootizay ta uhaaththaaysi isttan polistana mala gada yootays.
JOH 17:14 Tani ne qaala isttas immadis, tani ha biita asa ginddoonttaysa mala isttika ha biita asi gidetena, hessa gish ha biita asay istta ixxides.
JOH 17:15 Ne istta iittape nagana mala ta nena wossays attin ne istta ha biitafe denththa efana mala nena wossike.
JOH 17:16 Tani biita asi gidonttaysa mala isttika ha biita asii gidetena.
JOH 17:17 Ne istta ne tuman nes shaaka, ne qaalayka tumu qaala.
JOH 17:18 Ne tana ha biita kittoysaththo taka istta biita bolla kittadis.
JOH 17:19 Istt tumape nes duma ass gidida mala tanika tana istta gish dummasays.
JOH 17:20 Istta qaala marikatetha tana ammananayta gishshara ta nena wossays attin ta nena istta gish xalala wossike.
JOH 17:21 Ta wossizay istti wurikka issino gidana malasiko, ta aawawu qasseka ne tanan diza mala nunan gidana malane ne tana kittidaysa ha derey ne ammanana mala wossays.
JOH 17:22 Nunii nu garssan issno gidida mala isttika ba garssan issino gidana mala ne tas ida boncho taka isttas immadis.
JOH 17:23 Ta wossizay sttan, neka tanan gidida mala isttika kumethth issino gidana malako, qasseka neni tana kittda mlane tana ne siqqida mala isttaka ne siqqidaysa dere asay erranasiko.
JOH 17:24 “ta aawawu! ne tana haysi biitayne saloy medhdhistanape kase dossida gish ne tas immidaa ta bonchoza istti beeyana mala hayta ne tas immidaytka ta dizasoon anara dana mala dossays.
JOH 17:25 Xiillo gidida ta aawawu! nena derey erribeyna, ta gidiko nena errays, haytka ne ana kittdaysa errida.
JOH 17:26 Ne tana siqqida siqqooy isttan gidana malane taka isttan gidana mala isttine nena errana mala ooththadis, qasseka istti errana malaka oohthana.”
JOH 18:1 Hessa wursi yootidape guye Yesussay bena kaallizaytara Qeedirone geetetza shooba pinidi akakiltte gidoo gelidees.
JOH 18:2 Yesussayne iza kaallizayti kasseka he gadeyin daroo wode isife shiqiza gish Yesussa aththi immida Y uday he gadeyo kasseka erress.
JOH 18:3 Hessa gish Yuday wotadarata, qeessista halaqatane Farssawistape kitteti yida ashshikarata wursi kaalleththi ekkidi he istti shiqizaso yidees. Izara yida asay paanoose, xoomipenee mashsha toora oykkidi yidees.
JOH 18:4 Yesussay ba bolla gakkanaysa wursi erridi yida asako bidi “Oonna koyeti? gides.
JOH 18:5 Istti qasse “Nazireete yesussa koyoos” gida, Izika isttas “Tani izakoo” gidees. Isttas aththi immida yuday isttara isife eqqides.
JOH 18:6 Yesussay “Ta izako” gida mala asati guye ganddigaridi biita bolla kunddida.
JOH 18:7 Yesussay ha7ika “Oonna koyeeti?” gidi oychchin istti zaaridi “Nazireete Yesussa koyoos” gida.
JOH 18:8 Izika zaaridi “Tani izako gadiiskkoo, histtkoo inte koyizay tana gidikoo hayti beto bochchofite” gides.
JOH 18:9 Hesi haniday “Ta aawawu ne tas immidaytape issadeka ta dhaysabeykee” gida qaalay poleistana malako.
JOH 18:10 Simmoona geetetza phixxirossay giththa mashsha oykkda gish mashsha shohope shodidi issi qeessista halaqa ashshikara dizaysa haythe mashshara padhi yegides. He ashshikaraza sunththi “malkosa” geetetes.
JOH 18:11 Yesussay qasse phixxirossa “Ne mashsha gede shohon zara gelththa. Nees ta aaway tas immida metoo ushsha ta uyoontta milatizee?” gidees.
JOH 18:12 Hessafe guye wootadarati, istta azazizaysinne Ayhudata ashshikarati Yesussa oykkidi qachchida.
JOH 18:13 Koyro he laythas qessistas halaqa gidida qayafaa bollo Haannakko ehaaththaida.
JOH 18:14 Qayafaay “Deere gish issadey hayqqiko lo7okko” gidi Ayhudata dulata kase zooridade.
JOH 18:15 Simmona geetettiza phixxirossayne Yesussa kaallizaytape issadey yesussa kaallida. He uray qessista halaqa achchan kehi erretidade. Hessa gish Yesussara isife qessista halaqaza gibbe gelides.
JOH 18:16 Phixxirossay gidikko penggefe kare baggara eqqdees. Qessista halaqa achchan kehi erretdi Yesussa kaallizaysi yidine penggen diza garadeya phixxirossa gibbe giddo gelththana mala yootdi Pixirosa ekki gelides.
JOH 18:17 Pengge naggiza garadeya Phixxirossa “Neka hessa addeza kaalliza asatape issa gidikki?” gadus. Izi qasse “Tani iza kaallizade gidike” gides.
JOH 18:18 Wodey meegiza wode gidida gish ooththanchatnne ashshikarati tama eththidi eqoon ho7etes. Pixxirossaykka isttara eqidii ho7es.
JOH 18:19 He wode qeessista halaqay Yesussa iza kaallizayta gishane izi tammarisida tmmirtte gish oychchides.
JOH 18:20 Yesussayka izas “Ta asa wursos qoonccen yootadas. Ayhudati shiqiza istta wossa keeththan gidinkka Xoossa keeththan tammarisadis; ta qootan haasa7idazii aykoyka deena.
JOH 18:21 Histtin ne tana oychchizay aazee? ta yootshshin siydayta oychcha; ta yootdiysa istti erretes” gides.
JOH 18:22 Yesussay hessa gida mala hen eqida ashshikaratape issay “Qeessista halaqas hayssaththo wosta zaaray” gishe Yesussa shagalan baqqa shayides.
JOH 18:23 Yesussayka zaaridi “Ta iitta hasa7ida gidiko anne ta gooysa ne markkata; ta yootday likee gidiko tana aazas baqqaz?” gides.
JOH 18:24 Hessafe guye Haanay qachchetida mala Yesussa Qeessista halaqa Qayafaakoo yedidees.
JOH 18:25 He wode Simmoona geetetza Phixxrossay eqqidii tama ho7ishin hankko asay iza haysoo, ne Yesussa kaallizaytape issa gidikii?” gida. Izika zaaridi “Ta iza kaallizade gidike” giidi kadides.
JOH 18:26 Kase Pixxrossay iza hayththe qanxxiidayssa dabooy qeessista halaqa ashshikaratape issay “wona ta nena akaakilitesoon isttara dishin beeyabeykkina? gidees.
JOH 18:27 Pixxrossay qassekka kadides, heraka kutooy wasides.
JOH 18:28 Hessafe guye Yesussa Qayahaaththaa keeththafe dere aysiza kawooza gibbe malladoo wonttara ekki bidda. Ayhuda asas pazziga ba77ele dorssa ashsho mizza wode gidida gish bena tunisontta mala giidi malladora dere aysizaysa gibbe gidoo gelibeytena.
JOH 18:29 Hessa gish Philaxoossay gede isttako kezidi “Hayssa addeza inte aazas mootetii?” gidii oychchidees.
JOH 18:30 Istti qasse “Haysi addeezi iita oosonttade gididako nu iza nes aththi immokoko shin” gida
JOH 18:31 Philaxossayka “Inte iza ekki bidi inte woga mala pirditee” gidees. Ayhudata aysizayti qasse zaaridi “Nu ass wodhana mala nuus fiqadey immetibeyna” gides
JOH 18:32 Hessika haniday Yesussay kase isttas izi waani hayqanakoone yoottida qaalay polistana gishshasko.
JOH 18:33 Philaxoosay qasseka guye gibbe gido gelidi Yesussa xeeygisidi “Ne Ayhudata kawoo?” gidii oychchidees.
JOH 18:34 Yesussaykka zaaridi “Ne hessa gizay nepeyee woykoo hara asatii ta gish nes yoottdoo?” gides.
JOH 18:35 Philaxoossayka “Ta Ayhuda asee? Nena tas aththi immidayti ne baggatanne qeessista halaqattako; ne ayy ooththadii?” gides.
JOH 18:36 Yesussaykka “Ta kawootethi hayssa ha biita bolla gideena, ta kawootethi hayssa ha biita bolla gididakoo Ayhudata dannata kushshen ta kunddoontta mala ta ashshikarati ta gish olistanakoshin. Ta kawootethi gidikoo ha biita bolla gideena” gides.
JOH 18:37 Philaxoossayka “Histtin ne kawoo?” gides, Yesussay qasse “Tani ne gidaysa mala ee kawoo, ta yeleetidayne ha biitta yiday tuma gish markkatanasko. Tumape gididay wuri ta qaala siyees” gides.
JOH 18:38 Philaxoossayka “Tumay azee?” gides. Hessafe guye Phiilaxossay namm7enththo Ayhudatako kezzidi “Ta iza bolla ayko bala beyabeyke.
JOH 18:39 Gido attin kasseka ta intes paziga ba77ele gaalas issi qachcho ass birshiza mala hayssa Ayhudata kawoo intes birshana mala koyeetii?” gides.
JOH 18:40 Istti gidiko “nus Barbbanne birsha attin hayssa gideena!” giidi wassida. Barbbanney ba hu7es pangga.
JOH 19:1 Hessafe guye Philaxoossay Yesussa eefidi gaarafisiidees.
JOH 19:2 Wotadaratikka aguunththa zawuude xaxiidi Yesussa hu7en woththida, zo77o kabakka mayzzida.
JOH 19:3 Izako shiqqi shiqqdi “Ayhuda kawoo saaro saaro!” gi gidi iza shagalan baqqida.
JOH 19:4 Philaxxossay qasseka kare kesiidi “Heko ta iza bolla aykoo morooka demoonttaysa inte errana mala ta iza intes haa kare kessana” gides.
JOH 19:5 Hessa gish Yesussay aguunththa zawuude hu7en woththi ekkidine zo77o kaba maydi kare keziides. Philaxxossayka isttas “Hekoo addezi haysichchi!” gides.
JOH 19:6 eQessista halaqatine istta ashshikarat Yesussa beeydi “Ne iza kaqqa! kaqqa!” gishe wasiida, Philaxxossay qasse “Ta ta baggara iza bolla issi moroka demmabeyke, koykoo inte ehaaththaidii kaqqite” gides.
JOH 19:7 Ayhuda asati qasse “Nuus wogay dees haysi addezi beena xoossa na giza gish nu woga mala izas hayqqoy besees” gida.
JOH 19:8 Philaxxossay hessa istti gizaysa siydi daroo babides.
JOH 19:9 Gede gibbe gelidi Yesussa “ne awape yadii?” gidi oychchidees. Yesussay qasse izas ayy malththeka immibeyna.
JOH 19:10 Hessa gish Philaxxossay “ne tas yootiki? ta nena kaqqanas woykko birsha yedanas godatethi tas dizayssa errikii?” gides.
JOH 19:11 Yesussayka izas zaaridi “sheeney ness Xoossafe immetoonttako nes ta bolla ay godatethika deenashin, gido attin tana nes aththi immidade bolla gita nagaray dees” gides.
JOH 19:12 Philaxxossay hessa Yesussa hassa7e siydapee guye iza birshi yedana koyides shin Ayudatas babida gish istti “ne hayssa addeza birshiko Rome kawoo qeessare bagga gidaka, gasooyka bena berkka kawooththizadey wuri Qeessares moorkke” gishe wurikka wasiida.
JOH 19:13 Philaxxossay hessa siyda mala Yesussa gede kare kesisidi “Loochcha shuchchu” geetettiza soon pirda wombbaran uttides. He pirda sooy ayhudata qaalara “Gabata” getetes.
JOH 19:14 He wode gadeey asii paziga ba77eles gigettiza gaalasa. Wodeyka gaalasafe usuupun saate mala gidides. He wode Philaxxosay Ayhudata “Hekoo inte kawoy hayssichii!” gides.
JOH 19:15 Gido attin istti qass “Gede digga, gede digga, kaqqa” gishe wasiida. Philaxxossayka “inte kawoo kaqqoo?” gides. Qeessista halaqati zaaridi “nus Qessarepe hara kawooy deena” gida.
JOH 19:16 Hessafe simmidi Philaxxosay Yesussa kaqqistana mala isttas aththi immides. Isttka Yesussa oykki ekkii ehaaththaida.
JOH 19:17 Hessafe guye Yesussay ba kaqqistana masqqaleza tookidii “Asa hu7ee guuge” geetettizaso kezides. He sooy Ayhudata qaalara “Golggoota” geetetes.
JOH 19:18 Iza heen kaqqiida. Yesussa gidoo gelththidi hara namm7u asata izatho hadirssarane oshshachchara kaqqidda.
JOH 19:19 Philaxxossay “Nazzirete Yesussay Ayhudata kawoo” giza qaala xaafidi iza masqqale bolla izas hu7esora qaphides.
JOH 19:20 Yesussay kaqqetidasooy katamas mata gidida gish daroo Ayhuda asay Philaxxossay xaafidaysa nababidees. Xaafeetidaysika Ayhudata qaalara, Latiine geetettiza qaalarane Girikee qaalarako.
JOH 19:21 Ayhudata qeessata Halaqati Philaxxossa “ne iza Ayhudata kawoo” gada xaafoopa, Gido attin “<haysi addezii bena ta Ayhudata kawoo gidees> gada xaafa” gida.
JOH 19:22 Philaxxossay qass “Ta xaafidaysa xaafadis” gides.
JOH 19:23 Wootadarati Yesussa kaqqidape guye iza mayooza ekkidi wotadarata issa issa gakana mala oydu kessi shakereththida. Garsara mayiza mayozaka hessaththo shakereththida. Ggido attin garsara mayza mayoz siketoontta pudepe duge gakkanaas coo yeda dees.
JOH 19:24 Hessa gish wotadarati ba garssan “Gishan oonna gakkanakoone errana mala iza bolla exxa yeggana attin dakooko” gida. Hessika hanidday kase “Ta mayoo istti gishshetii ekkida, ta bollara mayza mayoza bolla exxa yegiida” getetida geesha maxaafa qaalay poleistana malasa. Wotararatikka heesa oothida.
JOH 19:25 Yesussa masqqalle achchan iza aayiyane aayeeyi michchiya Qeliyyopha machcha Maramane Megidele geetettizasope yida Marama heen eqqida.
JOH 19:26 Yesussay ba ayiyone izi siqqza iza kaallizaysi ba achchan eqqidayta beeydi, ba aayiyo “Aayee ne naza hessa beeya” gides.
JOH 19:27 Hessafe kaalleththidi bena kaallizaysa “Ne ayo hinoo beeya” gides. Hinoo he saateype simmin he iza kaallizaysi Aayiyo besso ehaaththaidees.
JOH 19:28 Hessafe guye Yesussay ha7i wurikka poleettidaysa erridi geesha maxaafan xaafetdaysi poleistana mala “tana samees” gides.
JOH 19:29 Heen gadan caala phanqqida ushshii kumii uttida issi xaarro malay dees. Hessa gish heen gadan dizayti he caala ushsha zanzza milatza sppoonjje gizaysara hisophphe giza miththa xeeran qaphidi iza dunako shishshida.
JOH 19:30 Yesussay he caalla ushsha xunxxi xeellidi “poleetides!” gides. Be hu7e duge ziqisidi shempo kezides.
JOH 19:31 Hessafe guye Ayhudata danati kaqqetida asata meeqqethth wodirape menththidi istt iza masqqsale bollafe woththana mala Philaxxossa wossiida. Istti hessa ooththiday Ayhudati sambbatas gigetiza gaalas gidida gishshine he sambbatayka daroo giita ba77ale gidida gish sambbata gaalas ahay masqqale bolla gami77ontta malla koyida gishasa.
JOH 19:32 Hessa gish wotadarati bidii Yesussara kaqqetiida asata meqqethth wodiirape wodiirape menththida.
JOH 19:33 Istti Yesussako biin izi kasetidinee hayqqdaysa beeydi iza wodiira meqqethth menththibeyteena.
JOH 19:34 Gido attin wotadarata garssafe issadey toorara iza miileen cadiin heeraka suththine haththi gukkidees.
JOH 19:35 Hessa beeydadeyi inte izan ammanana mala markkattdes. Iza markkayka tuma. Izi yootzayka tumu gididaysa izi errees.
JOH 19:36 Hessika haniday “Iza meqqeththafe isinaka meeqquku” geetetida geesha maxaafa qaalay polistanassa.
JOH 19:37 Qasseka geesha maxafa harason “Istti ba caadide beeyana” gees.
JOH 19:38 Ayhudata dannata babidi qotan Yesussa kaalliza Armmatyasa getetizasoppe yida Yossefoy Yesussa aha ekkanas Philaxoossa wossin Philaxoossayka izas eeroo gides. Hessa gish Yossefoy bidi Yesussa aha ekkidees.
JOH 19:39 Kase Yesussakko qamara yida Niqoodimossayka kiilo bagga gidiza karbbeenne ireete geetettiza mishshara walakeetida shiito ekki yidees.
JOH 19:40 He namm7u asati Yesussa aha ekkidi Ayhudatii aha xaxiza mala shiito cacafidii le77e mayora xaxida.
JOH 19:41 Yesussay kaqqetidason issi akakilitesoy dees. He akakilitezason oonnika moggetonttay oraththa dufooy dess.
JOH 19:42 Ayhudata sambbatas gigeteza gaalas gidida gishshinne dufooykka matan diza gish Yesussa aha heen mogiida.
JOH 20:1 Wooga gaalas wontta malado buroo sosey zoishshin Magidale marama Yesussa dufooko badusu. Iza he gakkishin kase Yesussa dufoo izara goordida shuuchay dufooza duunape denddidi gendderidaysa beeyadusu.
JOH 20:2 Hessa gish iza Yesussa kaallizaytape Simmoona geetetiiza Pixirosakko Yesuyssay dosiza hankko iza kaallizaysako woxxa bada “Goda dufooppe keesi ekkidi awan woththidakone nu erroko” gadusu.
JOH 20:3 Heraka Pixxrossayne Yesussa kaalliza hinkko issay kezzidi gede duhaaththaoy dizasoo bida.
JOH 20:4 Namm7eyka ishaaththaee woxxida, gido attin Yesussa kaalliza hinkkoysi Pixxrossape pilatii woxxidi kaseti dufooy dizasoo gakkides.
JOH 20:5 Dufooza hookii xeelidi ahay xaxxetida mayoo xala dizayssa beeydes. Gido attin gede dufoo giido gellibeeyna.
JOH 20:6 Simmoona geetettiza Pixxrossayka iza kaalli gakkidi dufooza giido gellidees, ahay izan xaxxetida cariqqay hen dizayssa beeydes.
JOH 20:7 Yesussa hu77ey xaxxetida carqqay hankko xaththa carqqatara gidoontta duuma harasson xaxxeti dizayssa beeydees.
JOH 20:8 Koyroti gakkida Yesussa kaallizzaysika dufooza giido geli beeydi ammanides.
JOH 20:9 Gasooyka “Izi hayqqope denddana beeses” giza maaxxafe qaala istti buroo hasa7ibeeytena.
JOH 20:10 Hessafe guye namm7etika simmidi besso besso bida.
JOH 20:11 Magidale marama yeekashshe Yesussa dufoope kareera eqqada hokka dufooza giido xeelladus.
JOH 20:12 Yesussa Ahay dizasson boththa mayoo mayda namm7u kitanchatape issay hu7eson issay toson uttidayta beeyadus.
JOH 20:13 Isttika Maramo “Hane maccashshayee azaas yeekazii?” gida, izaka “Istti ta Goda ehaaththaidii awan woththidakoone ta errike gadus.
JOH 20:14 Iza hiino gada guye yuyshshin Yesussay eqqidayssa demaduus shin izi Yesussa gididayssa errabeykku.
JOH 20:15 Yesussay izo “Hanne maccashshayee! azass yeekazzi? Qasse oonna kooyazzi?” > gides, izika iziis akakkiltte nagizzadee millatiin “Godo! ne ekkida gidikoo ne woththidasso tass yootarkki, ta iza tass ekkana” gaduus.
JOH 20:16 Yesussay izo “Marame!” gides, izakka gede izakko simmada ayhudata qaalara “Rebuune!” gaduus, hessa birshechchi “asttamaree” guusa.
JOH 20:17 Yesussay qass “Ta buroo pude ta aawako kezzabeykke tana oykoofa, gido attin ne ha7i ta ishatakko bada “Ta ta aawakone inte aawako, ta xoossakone inte xoossako kezana gides gada isttas yoota” gides.
JOH 20:18 Hessa gish Magidale Marama Yesussa kaallizaytako bada iza Yesussa beeydaysane izi izis yootidaysa isttas yootadusu.
JOH 20:19 He gaalas wooga Omarss Yesussa kaallizayti Ayhudata dannatas babidii kare ba bolla goordidi keeththa giidon shiqoon dishshin karey dooyetoontta Yesussay iza kaallizayti shiqii diza keeththa gellidees. Istta gidoon eqqidii “Saaroy intes giidoo!” gides.
JOH 20:20 Hessa gi smmidi ba kushshistane ba miiye istta beesides. Iza kaallizaytika goda beeydii keezi uhaaththaa7etida.
JOH 20:21 Hessafe guye qasseka Yesussay istta “intes saaroy gido! ta aaway tana kittda mala taka intena kittays” gides.
JOH 20:22 Hessa gi simmidi istta bolla uuhaaththau gidi “inte Xiiloo Ayana ekkite.
JOH 20:23 Inte asa nagara atto gikko isttas atto geteettana, inte asa nagara attoo gontta ixxiko qass isttas attoo geteteena” gides.
JOH 20:24 Yesussay bena kaallizaytako yida wode tammane namm7istape issay Didimossa geteetiiza Toomassy isttara denna.
JOH 20:25 Hessa gish hankko Yseussa kaallizayti Toomassa “Nu Goda beeydooskko” gida. Toomassay qass “Miismmaren cadeetida iza kushshista ta ta ayfeera beeyoontta dahshene qasseka ta birdhdhe miismmarey gelidason gelitha xeelontta dashshene ta kushshe iza miiye maddunththan gelththa xeelontta dashshe ammanikke” gides.
JOH 20:26 Hessafe kaallin osppun gaalasafe guye iza kaallizayti qasseka keeththa gidoon dishshin Tommssayka isttara isife dishshin kareyka goordana dishshin Yesussay yiidi istta gidoon eqqidi “s saarotethth intes gido” gides.
JOH 20:27 Hessafe guye Toomassa “Ne biradhdhe ha ehada ta kushshista beeya. Ne kushshe ha ehada ta miiyeen gelitha ammana attin ammanonttade gidoopa” gides.
JOH 20:28 Toomassay “Ta Godoo! Ta Xoosso!” gides.
JOH 20:29 Yesussayka Toomassa “Neni tana beeyda gish ammanddassa, tana beeyoontta ammanizayti gidiko istti galateetidayta” gides.
JOH 20:30 Hayssa maaxfan xaafetontta daroo malatata bena kaallizayta sinththan Yesussay oththides.
JOH 20:31 Gido attin Yesussay ha yana kittetida Xoossa nay iza gididaysa inte errana malane ammanidi inte iza sunththan deyoo demana mala haysi xaafettdes.
JOH 21:1 Hessafe guye Yesussay Xibiradoose abba achchan bena kaallizaytas qasseka beetdes.
JOH 21:2 Simmoona geetettiza Pixxiroossay Didimoossa geetettiza Toomassay Gallila Qanna ass gidida Natinaelley Zabidossa naytika Yesussa kaallizaytape hara namm7ati wuri isife dishshin
JOH 21:3 Simmoona geetettiza Pixxiroossay isttas “Ta moole oykkana bays” gides, isttika izas “Nukka nenara bana” gida, izara kezzi bidi wogoolon gellida shin he gaalas omarssi issi mooleka oykkibeytena.
JOH 21:4 Gadey wonttishshin Yesussay abba achchan eqqides, iza kaallizaytii qass izi Yesussa gididayssa erribeyteena.
JOH 21:5 Yesussay istta “Naytoo mooley dizze?” gides, isttika “aykooka bawa” gida.
JOH 21:6 Izika “Giteza wogoolozape oshshacha baggara abban yeegite, inte demmana” gida gish giiteza abba giido yeegidane daroo mooley oykeetda gish giiteza molara gochchana danddaebeyitena.
JOH 21:7 Hessa wode Yesussay iza kaallizaytape Yesusa iza siqiza issay Pixxirossa “Hesi Godakko!” gides. Simmoona geetetza Phixxiroossay “hesi Godakko” giza qaala siyda mala kasse ooso diigofo gidi mayoo qaari woththidi kaloo diza gish herakka mayoo ekki mayidi abba giido guuppi gelidees.
JOH 21:8 Yesussa kaalliza hankkoyti qass biitafe xeetu mitire mala hakii diza gish mooley kumi dizza giiteza gochchi ekkidi wogoolora gakkida.
JOH 21:9 Istti wogoolozape wodhdhishin moley iza bolla diza bonqqo tamane ukethth beeyda.
JOH 21:10 Yesussay istta “Ha7i inte oykkida molezape ha ekki yiite” gides.
JOH 21:11 Hessa gish simmoona geetettiza Phixxiroossay wogooloza giido gellidi xeistane ichchachchu taammane hedzdzu woogga giita mooleti kumiida giiteza abbafe gede gade bolla gochchides. Hessa mala daroo molera diinika giitezi daketibeeyna.
JOH 21:12 Hessafe guye Yesussay istta “Ha yidi miite” gides. Izi Goda Yesussa gididaysa wursi errida gish iza kaallizaytape issadeykka “Ne oonne” gi oychchanas xallidadey bawa.
JOH 21:13 Yesussay yidi ukeththane moleza ekkidi isttas immides.
JOH 21:14 Yesussay hayqqope denddin iza kaallizayti iza beeyshshin haysi hedzdzanththo.
JOH 21:15 Istti mii gigishshin Yesussay simmoona Phixxiroossa “Yoona na Simmoona! hayiti tana dosizayssafe aththa tana dossayii?” gides. Izikka “Ee ta Godo! ta nena dosizayssa nekka errasa” gides.
JOH 21:16 Yesussay iza “Ta laqqata hemma” gides, namm7enththoka “Yoona na Simmoona! ne tana dossay?” gides, izika zaarid “Ee Godo! Ta nena dosizaysa neka errasa” gides, Yesussay qass “laqqata naga” gides,
JOH 21:17 Hedzdzanththo “Yoona na Simmoona Ne tana doossay?” gides. Izi hedzdzanththo “Ne tana dossay” gida gish Pixroossay michchetidine “Godo ne ubbaa errasa ta nena dosizayssakka errasa” gides, Yesussayka qasseka “Ta doorisata hemma” gides.
JOH 21:18 Ta nes tumu gays ne naatethan dashshe ne giththe nerkka gixxada ne koydasso baasashin ne ciimmiza wode gidiko ne ne kushshista pidiisin hara urray nena gixxisanane ne dosoonttaso nena ehaaththaana.
JOH 21:19 Izi Iza hessaththo giday Pixxroossay ay mala hayqqon xoossu bonchanakone izas erisanaskko. hessafe guye Phixxiroossa “Ne tana kaalla” gides.
JOH 21:20 Phixxiroossay yushshi xeelidi Yesussay dosizaysi iza kaallishin beeydes. He urray kase istt ka7o mishshin Yesussa hayththako shiqidi “Godo nena aththi immanadey izi oonne?” gii oychchides.
JOH 21:21 Pixxroossay iza beeydi “Godo hayssadeych wanandde?” gidi Yesussa oychchides.
JOH 21:22 Yesussaykka izas “Ta ha yana gakkanaashin ta iza paxxa woththiko nena azi gaththidee? ne tana kaalla” gides.
JOH 21:23 Hessa gaason ishshata garssan “izi hayqqo hayqqena” giza worey lalletides. Gido attin Yesussay “ta yana gakkanaas paxxa dana mala ta koyko nena azze gaththiday?” gidees attin “hayqqakka” giibeyna.
JOH 21:24 He yoota gish markkatidayne xaafiday ha Yesussa kaallizayssa. Iza markkatethika tumu gididayssa nuni erroos.
JOH 21:25 Yesussay oththida hara darooti deetes. Tas milatiza mala izi ooththida miishshata wursi issi bolla xaafizako xaafeetiza maxaafata haysii biitay tokkana dandda7ena.
ACT 1:1 Tofilosa, Yesussay oothanasine tammarissanas oykidayssa wursia ta nes koyro maxaafan xaafadis.
ACT 1:2 Hessika izi pude denththa gaalas gakkanaas ba doorida kitidaytas xiillo ayana baggara izi isttas immida azazoko.
ACT 1:3 Izi daro waye be7idappe guye istakko shiqidi hayqope denddanayssa haytannitas daroo markkara qonccisishe oydu tamu gaalas gakkanaas isttas gaalas galas beetishe Xoossa kawootetha gish yootides.
ACT 1:4 Isttara isife maadan uttidishe istta hizzgi azazides “Yerussalamepe kezoppite, gido attin ta intes yootishin inte siydayssa ta aaway immida uhaaththaayssa naagitte.
ACT 1:5 Yanissay haththan xaamaqqides shin inte qass guuththa wodeppe guye xiillo ayanan xammaqistana.
ACT 1:6 Isttika issibolla shiqetti uttidishe “Godo! isiraelista kawootethi zaarada hai essane?” gi oychchida.
ACT 1:7 Izika isttas “aaway ba sheenen woththida wode errooy intes immetibeeyna.
ACT 1:8 Gido attin xiillo Ayanay inte bolla wodhdhida wode inte wolliiqa ekkana, Yerussalamenika Yudanika Sammariyanika wursoson biita gaxxa gakkanaas inte tas markkata gidana” gides.
ACT 1:9 Hessa gi yootidape guye istti xeellishin pude salo denddides, salo sharayika istta ayfepe iza genththides.
ACT 1:10 Izi biishin istti iza tish histi pude salo xeelishin booththa mayo mayida namm7u asati qoponnita istta achchan eqqidi;
ACT 1:11 “inteno Galila asato! inte pude salo xeellishe hayssan aazas eqqidetii? Haysi inte maatappe pude salo dennidishin inte beeyza Yesussay salo keezishin inte beeyda mala hessaththoka izi simmi yaana” gida.
ACT 1:12 Hessafe guye Dabirezayite giza zumma bollafe wodhdhid Yerusalame simmida, he zummayka yerussalameppe issi killo mittire mala hakkes.
ACT 1:13 Gede kaatamayo gellida wode kase ba diza keeththa fooqe bolla keziida, heyttikka Phixxirossa, Yanissa, Yaqoobe, Inddarassa, Philliphossa, Toomassa, Barttelomossa, Matossa, Illifossa na Yaqoobe, ba bagga maddizade geetettiza Simmonane yaqoobe na Yuuda.
ACT 1:14 Heyti wurikka maccashatappe Yesussa aayoo marammira hessathokka iza ishshatara issi wozinnan issi bolla qanxxontta minni woossida.
ACT 1:15 He gaallasatan Phixxirossay xeistane namm7u tammu ammaniza asa giidon eqqiddi.
ACT 1:16 Hizzgides “ta ishshato! Yesussa oykkida asata kaalleth oyththida, yuda gish xiillo ayanay kassetidi dawute dunnan hasa7iida geesha maxaafa qaalay polistanas koshiza gishiko.
ACT 1:17 Izikka nuuppe issade mala taybeettidi hayssa ha oosozan gellanas exxa demmides.
ACT 1:18 Shin hayssadey ba iitta ooson demmida miishshan gade shammides. Hennikka ba liiphon gufanni kunnidin iza asatathay giidofe phalliqeti wodhdhides; iza maraccey biita bolla zazetides.
ACT 1:19 Hesikka yerussalamen diza asas wursios siyetides. Biitaykka istta qaalara “akeelidama” geetetides; Birishechayika suththa biita gusa.
ACT 1:20 Gujjidikka Phixxirossay “mazzimmure maaxaafan <iza biittay mela atto, iza biittan assi doopo qassekka iza dannatethi hara assi eekko> geeteti xaafetides.
ACT 1:21 Hessa gish Goda Yesusay nunara diza wode wurson nunara isife dizayta gidofe nu issade dorannas koshshes.
ACT 1:22 Hesikka Yanisa xiinqqateppe ha simmin Yesussay nuppe shakeetidi dendi bana gakkanaas nunara dizade gidannas beeses. Gasoykka ha asatappe issadey nunara Yesussa denththas markka gidana koshshes” gides.
ACT 1:23 Hessa gish Barissabasa woykko Yosixxossa geetettiza Yosehaaththaonne Matiyassa namm7ata shishshidi;
ACT 1:24 Hizzgi wossida “Godo! Ne asa wurso wozina errassa, hayta namm7ata giidofe ne oona doridakko issade nuna beessa.
ACT 1:25 Yuuday yeggi bidason ha ooththa ooththanadene haware gidanade ne doora” gida.
ACT 1:26 Hessafe exxa yeggin exxay Maatiyassas keezides. Izikka taammane issi hawaristara isife tayibeetides.
ACT 2:1 Phenxxaqonxxe geetettiza gaalas gakkanaas asay wurikka issi soon shiqii dishin,
ACT 2:2 Qohaaththaay bayinnida daroo miinno gotte caariko mala girethi asay diza keeththa kummides.
ACT 2:3 Tama lacco malay asas betidi shakeeti shakeeti issi issi urra bolla uttides.
ACT 2:4 Amanizayti wuri Xiillo Ayanan kummiidi Ayanay isttas hasa7anas immidayssa keena hara qaalara hasa7a oykkida.
ACT 2:5 He wode salo guhaaththaanththon diza derepe yida Xoossas babiiza ayhudati Yerusalamen deetes.
ACT 2:6 He gireththa siyidi derey shiqides. Issi issi asay ba qaalara hasa7izaysa siyidi malaletides.
ACT 2:7 Malaletidinne gizazi dhayin hizgida “hayti hasa7izayti wurikka Galila asi dettenee?
ACT 2:8 Histtin nuni nu yelletida nu dere qaalara isti hasa7ishin wossti siyizonii?
ACT 2:9 Nuni Pharite asay Meede asay Eelame asay Mesphphoxxomiyan Yudan Qaphedoqqiyan phanxxosan Isiyan,
ACT 2:10 Firgiyan, Phinhaaththailliyan Gibxen, Qaarena achchan diza Liibiyappenne Romeppe yida;
ACT 2:11 Nuni Ayhudatine gede Ayhudatethan gellida Qaarxesa asane Araabe asata gidishin Xoossa wolqama oosoza hayti nu qaalara hasa7ishin nu siyoos.
ACT 2:12 Wurikka kezi malaletidine gizazi dhayin ba giidon “Haysi azesha?” geetetida.
ACT 2:13 Bagga asay “Hayti daro woyne ush uyida” gidi istta qidhida.
ACT 2:14 Hessa wode Phixxirossay taammane issinistara eqqidine ne qaala dhoqqu histtidi deeras hizzgides “Inteno yuda asatto! Yerusalame dizayto inte wurikka hayssa issi mishsh erritenne ta gizaysa siyte.
ACT 2:15 Ha7i gadey wonttin buroo hedzdzu saate gidida gish inte qoppiza mala hayti asati maththotibeytena.
ACT 2:16 Gido attiin haysi kasse nabe yu7ellen hizzgi yootetida qaalay polistanasko,
ACT 2:17 “Xoossi hizzgees <wursetha gaalas ta ayana ashsho mayida wursio bolla ta guussana; inte macca naytine inte atumma nayti buroppe hananaysa beeyana, yelaga nayti ajjutta beeyana, Cimaati agumo agumeistana.
ACT 2:18 Hessa wode ta macca ashkarata bollanne ta atumma ashkarata bolla ta ayanappe ta guussana. Isttika buro hananaysa hassa7na.
ACT 2:19 Bolla salon malalisiza hanota ta beessana, garssa biittan malatata ta immana; suuththi, tammayinne tulaley hanana.
ACT 2:20 Gitanne boncho gidida Goda gaalasay yanappe kassetidi awa ayhaaththaey dhummana, agiinnaykka suuththu milatana.
ACT 2:21 Goda sunththu xeeyigizay wuri attana.
ACT 2:22 Isra7eele nayto hayssa qaala siyte; inte inte baggara errizayssa mala inte garssan malatanne assi siyi erroontta miishshata iza kushshen ooththidi Xoossi naziirete Yesussas markkatides.
ACT 2:23 Xoossi kase ba qachchidayssa izas beni erratetha mala hayssade inte kushshen aaththi immides. Intekka iita asata kushshen kaaqqeti hayqqana mala ooththidista.
ACT 2:24 Gido attin Xoossi iza bollafe hayqqo wolqa diggidi hayqqope denththides. Hayqqoykka iza oykki ashshanas dandda7ibeyna.
ACT 2:25 Dawiteykka iza gish hizzgides “Tanni Goda wurso wode ta sinththan beeyayis, izi ta oshachchan dees, mulekka hirigike.
ACT 2:26 Hessa gish ta wozinay uhaaththaa7etes, ta dunaykka galates, ta ashshoy uhaaththaayssan dees.
ACT 2:27 Ne ta shemmipiyo dufoon agaakka, ne na geshshaza wooqana mala agaagaaka.
ACT 2:28 Ne deyoo ogge ta errana mala ooththadasa, ne tanara diza gish ta uhaaththaayssay kumeth.”
ACT 2:29 Ta ishshato beni aawatappe Dawitey hayqqi moggetiddayssane iza dufooy hach gakkanaas nu achchan dizayssa babontta ta intes yootana dandda7ays.
ACT 2:30 Izi nabe gidida gish Xoossi iza zeerethafe issade iza kawootetha aliigga bolla wothanayssa kase caaqo qaalan yootidayssa errides.
ACT 2:31 Hessa kasetidi errida gishine iza ashshoy wooqqi duufon atoontta doretida kirstosa denththa gish hassa7ides.
ACT 2:32 He Yesussa Xoossi hayqqope denththidees. Nukka wuri hayssas markkata.
ACT 2:33 Hessa gish izi Xoossa ushshachchan dhoqqu dhoqqu giddape guye xiillo Ayana uhaaththaayssa ba aawappe ekkidi ha7i inte beeyzayssane siyzayssa duge guussides.
ACT 2:34 Dawitey pude salo kezibbeyna, izi ba dunnan hizzgides <Goday ta Godas; “ta ne morketa ne to garssan yeedhissana gakkanaas ta oshshachchan utta.” >
ACT 2:36 Hessa gish Xoossi inte kaqqida Yesussa Godane Kiristtossa hisitidayssa Isiraele asay wuri lo7ethi erro.
ACT 2:37 Deerey hessa siyda mala wozinay bochetides, Phixxirossane hanko yesussay kittidayta “nu ishshato histtin nu ay ooththino? gida.
ACT 2:38 Phixxirossayka hizzgides marotethan gellite; inte nagaray maristana mala intefe issi issi urray Yesuss Kiristtossa sunththan xammaqetite, izi immiza Xiillo Ayana inte ekkana.
ACT 2:39 Izi uhaaththaayssa qaalay intesine inte naytasa, qassekka Godaa Xoossay beeko xeeygiza hahon dizaytasara wursosiko.
ACT 2:40 Hara daroo qaalara isttas markkatishe “hayssa geella yeletethafe intena ashshite” gidi istta qofisides.
ACT 2:41 He gaalas qaala ekkidaytine xaammaqetidayti hedzdzu shiya mala asay kaseyta bolla gujjetides.
ACT 2:42 Isttika kittetidayta timmiritenn, isife qumma mussaninne wossan minnida.
ACT 2:43 Kittetidayta kushshen daroo malatati ooththetida gish asi wuri isttas babiides.
ACT 2:44 Ammanidayti wurikka isife deyida; bees dizazkka wursii issi bolla go7etida.
ACT 2:45 Bees diza mishshene mehe bayzi bayzi ba garssan koshshida mala gishechida.
ACT 2:46 Gaalas gaalas xoossa keeththan isife shiiqetes, ba keeththankka qumma isife uhaaththaayssanine suure wozinara meetes.
ACT 2:47 Istti Xoossa galatishe dere sinththan bonchetida, Godaykka istta bolla gaalas gaalas orathth ammanizata gujjidees.
ACT 3:1 Issi wode gallasappe udufun saate bolla Phixxirossayne Yanissay wossa saaten Xoossa keeth bana kezzida.
ACT 3:2 Issi yellet wodhdhosope dommidi toy sillidade Xoossa keeth gelliza asape muxxata wossana mala asay gaalas gaalas tokki ehaaththaidi wothin issi loo7o geetettiza Xoossa keeththa pengen wossizadey dees.
ACT 3:3 Izikka Phixxirossayne Yanissay Xoossa keethe gellishin beeyid isttafe muxxata wossides.
ACT 3:4 Phixxirossayne Yanissay iza tiishi histti xeellida. Phixxirossaykka iza “Ane haa nuna xeella” gides.
ACT 3:5 Addezikka isttafe aykko demmana gidi istta tiishi histti xeellides.
ACT 3:6 Gido attin Phixxirossay izas zaaridi “tas biraynne woorqqay denna gidikokka tas dizaz ta nes immays Nazireete Yesuss Kiristtossa sunththan dendadda ne toora hammuta” gides.
ACT 3:7 Izas oshacha kushshe oykkidi denththides, Herakka addeza tooyne too qirphpheey miniddes.
ACT 3:8 Guuppi denddi eqqidi Hammuththu oykkides. Heene haane hammutishene guuppishe Xoossaka galatishe isttara isife Xoossa keethth gibbe gellides.
ACT 3:9 Izi Xoossa galatishe heene ha simmeeretishin asay beeydi,
ACT 3:10 hayssadey haanife kase “loo7o” geetettiza Xoossa keeththa peengen uttidi muxxata wossizay iza gididayssa errides. Iza bolla hanidayssafe denddidayssan asay keezi malaletides.
ACT 3:11 Ha paxxida wossanchay Phixxirossakonne Yanisako shiphph gidi isttara oyketi dishin derey wuri malaletidi isttako “Sollommone simereetethaso” geetettizaso woththan yides.
ACT 3:12 Phixxirossay he asa beeyidi hizgides “Inteno Isra7eele dereto, hayssan aazas malaleteetii? Qassekka hayssa addeza nuni nu wolqan woykko nu nu xiillotetha paththidi hammutisida mala qodidi nuna aazas tish histi xeelletii?
ACT 3:13 Nu aawantta Abramentta, Yisaqantta, Yaqobentta Xoossi naza Yesussa bonchides, inte qass iza hayqqos aaththi immidista, Philaxossay izi birshana koynkka inte iza Philaxossa sinththan kadidista.
ACT 3:14 Geeshsha na xiilloza inte kadidi shemmppo wodhdhizaysi birshistana mala wossidista.
ACT 3:15 Deyo imizade inte wodhdhidista, gido attin Xoossi iza hayqqope denththides, hessas nuni markkata.
ACT 3:16 Haysi inte beeyizaysine inte errizayssi mini eqqiday Yesussa sunththan ammanida gishiko. Inte wurikka beeyza mala izi kumetha paxxa demiday Yesussa sunthaninne iza sunththan beettiza ammanoniko.
ACT 3:17 “Ha7ikka ta ishshato inte hessa ooththiday inte hallaqata mala errontta gididaysa ta errays.
ACT 3:18 Gidikokka kiristtossay wayye ekkanayssa Xoossi kasse nebista dunnan hasa7idayssa pollides.
ACT 3:19 Hessa gish inte nagaray qucceti dhayana mala marotethan gellite, inte biza oggepe simmite goda matappe inte oraxxana wodey intes yana.
ACT 3:20 Qassekka Xoossi kase intes doori wothida Yesussa Kiristtossa izi intes yeddana.
ACT 3:21 Xoossi kasse geshsha nabeta dunnan hasa7idaysa mala hannizaysa wursii oraxxisana wodey gakkanaas izi salon gamm7anas koshshes.
ACT 3:22 Musseykka <inte goda Xoossi inte giidofe ta mala nabe intes denththana, izi intes yootizaysa siyitte.
ACT 3:23 He nabeza siyontta ixxida shemmppoy wuri dere garssafe shaketi dhayo> gides.
ACT 3:24 Tumappe Samelappe ha simmin denddida nabeti wuri hayta wodeta gish hasa7ida.
ACT 3:25 Intekka nabeta naytakko. Qassekka Xoossi Abrames <ne zeerethan biitta asi wuri anjjistana> giidi izi caqqida caqqoza latannay intenakko.
ACT 3:26 Xoossi naza denththida wode intena issa issa inte iitatethafe zaaridi anjjana mala kassetidi inteko kittides.”
ACT 4:1 Phixxirossayne Yanissay asas hasa7an dishin qeessista hallaqatine Xoossa keethth nagizayta hallaqay qassekka saduqqaweti hasa7ay bayndda isttako yida.
ACT 4:2 Yiidine kittetidayti asa tammarsizaysasiine Yesussa baggara beettida hayqqidayta denththa gish sabakkizaysas keehi hanqqeetida.
ACT 4:3 Phixxirossane Yanissa oykkidi gadey qammishin wonttana gakkanaas qachcho keeththan ayssida.
ACT 4:4 Gido attin qaala siyda asappe dariza baggay ammanides. Ammanzza atuumma asa qooday gede ichchachchu shi gakkanaas dhoqqu gides.
ACT 4:5 Wonttetha gaalas istta halaqatine cimmat qasseka musse woga tammariszzayti yerussalamen shiiqida.
ACT 4:6 Istta qeessista halqqa Hannaynne qayahaaththaay, Yanissay, Iskkindirosaynne qeessista halaqaso asay wuri he gadan beettida.
ACT 4:7 Isttikka Phixxirossane Yanissa ba giidon aththi essiidi “hayssa inte ooththizay aza wolliqane? woykko oonna sunththane? gidi oychchida.
ACT 4:8 He wode Phixxirossay xiillo ayanan kummidi “inteno dere hallaqato! dere cimmato!
ACT 4:9 Inte hach ha too siila addezas ooththetida loo7o oosoy wani izi poxxidako inte nuna oychchiza gidiko,
ACT 4:10 inte kaqqin Xoossi hayqope denththida nazireete Yesuss kiristtossa sunththan izi paxxidaysane inte sinththan izi eqqidayssas intekka Isra7eele dere asay wuri hayssa errite.
ACT 4:11 Izikka inteni keeththa hiillati kadhi aggida shuchchay ginbbe keethas waanna hu7e gidides.
ACT 4:12 Atootethi hara oonnankka baawa, saloppe garssa baggara nu asa naytti atana mala nus immettiday hayssafe hara sunththi deena” gides.
ACT 4:13 Assaykka Phixxirossayne Yanissay hessaththo xali hasa7izayssa beeyddi isti tammarontta asi gididayssa erridi malaletidane istt kasse Yesussara dizadentta gididayssa akekida.
ACT 4:14 He paxxida addezi isttara eqqidishin beeyida gish isttas hara oothanas gaassoy dhayides.
ACT 4:15 Hessa gish istta duulatappe kessana mala azazida. Hessafe qassekka shiqeetidi ba garssan zooretida.
ACT 4:16 Be garssan hizgida “hayta asata wossitino? Yerusalamen diza asay wuri istta kushshen hannida giita malata errides. Hessa gish nu ha yooza asa ballethanas danda7okko.
ACT 4:17 Gido attin hayssi yoozi dere garsan keehi akkonita malane hayti asati namm7anththo hayssa ha sunththan hara onnaskka yootontta mala isttas loo7eththi yootana.”
ACT 4:18 Istta xeeygidinne mulleka Yesuussa sunththan hassa7ontta malane tammarsontta mala azaziida.
ACT 4:19 Phixxirossayne Yanissay qasse zaarid “nuni xoossafe bollara intes azazistanas beesizakonne ane inte Xoossa sinththan pirdite.
ACT 4:20 Nuni nu beeydayssane nu siydayssa hassa7anappe guye gookk” gida.
ACT 4:21 Qassekka istta bolla maanddidi yeedida, gasooykka hankko derey wuri hanida yooza gaason wurkka Xoossu galatiza gish istta qaxxayanas danddaibeyetena.
ACT 4:22 He giita malatan paxxida addezas layththi uyddu taammufe bollako.
ACT 4:23 Phixxirossaynne Yanissay qachchoppe birshetidi gede ba asattako simmidi qeessista halaqatine dere ciimati istta gidaysa wursikka yoottida.
ACT 4:24 Isttikka hessa siyida mala ba qaala dhoqqu histtidi isife Xoossakko hizzgi wassiida “Wooga Godo! neni salone sa7a abbane abba giidon dizayta wurssa medhdhadassa.
ACT 4:25 Ne ashshikkara nus aawa Dawite dunaara Xilo Ayanan “Hankko dere asay aazas hanqqeti denddide? Deerey aazas meella maqqetizee?
ACT 4:26 Biitta kawooti isife gagidi biitta harizayti issi bolla shiqeetida, Goda bollane dooreti tiyetidayssa bolla duullatida”> gides.
ACT 4:27 Tumappe Heridosayne Phanxxossa Philaxossay Isira7elatarane hara dere asaara hanno kaatamayin ne doora tiyida geeshsha naza Yesussa bolla yoo qachchanas shiqetida.
ACT 4:28 Haysnkka ne wolqaninne ne sheenen kasse ne qopidaysa isti polida.
ACT 4:29 Godo ha7ikka istta manddetha ne beeya, nuni ne aylleti ne qaala babontta kummetha xallatethara yootana mala dandda7isa.
ACT 4:30 Paththanas ne kushshe mica, ne na geshshaza sunththan gita malata ooththa.
ACT 4:31 Istti woosidappe guye istti dizasoy qaaxides. wurikka Xiillo Ayanan kummidi Xoossa qaala xallatethan yootida.
ACT 4:32 Ammanizayti wurikka issi wozinaninne issi qoofan gaagi deetes. Istas dizay wursi issi bolla dees attin bess dizaz “haysi tas buzu7a mishsha” gizadey deena.
ACT 4:33 Kittetidaytikka Goda Yesussa denththa giita wolqan markkateth oykkida, Wuriso bolla giita Xoossa kiyatethi dees.
ACT 4:34 Istta giidon meetottanchay issadeykka bawa. Gasooykka gade gidin keethe gidin bees diza wursii bayzzi bayzzi shishshida mishshe
ACT 4:35 kittetidayta kushshen woththidi issi issi urras izas koshshiza mala gisheetes.
ACT 4:36 Qophirose geetettizason diza Yossefo geetettizadey issi Lewe bagga assi dees. Izikka kittetidaytan “Barnnabassa” geeteti sumides. Hessas birshechay “minththetho naa” guussikko.
ACT 4:37 Izikka ba gade bayizida miishsha ehiidi kittetidayta kushshen wooththides.
ACT 5:1 Issi Hannaniya geetettiza asi Saphphira geetettiza ba machchira ba gade bayzides.
ACT 5:2 Machchiya Saphphiray loo7atha errishshin gadeza bayzzida miishshafe bagga shakki ashiidi bagga ehhidi kittetidayta kushshen immides.
ACT 5:3 Qasse Phixxirossay “haysso Hannaniya neni Xiillo Xyana bolla wordotanasine gade miishshafe ashshana mala xalla7ey ayys ne wozinan gellidee? Bayzanappe kasse gadez neeysa gidene? Ne bayzadeppe guye qasse miishshay ne kushshen deenee? Histtin ne hayssa mala wossita ne wozinnan qoppadii? Ne Xoossa bolla wordotadassa attin asa bolla gideena” gides.
ACT 5:5 Hessa siyida mala Hannaniyay kunidi hayqqides. Hessa siyida asay wuri daroo babbides.
ACT 5:6 Atumassay denddidi aha xaaxidine herakka ehaaththaidi mooggides.
ACT 5:7 Hedzdzu saatepe guye machchiya izi wanidakone errontta dashe yadus.
ACT 5:8 Phixxirossaykka “Anne tas yootta, inte gadeza bayzzida wagaay hano xalalaa?” gides, Izakka “Ee haano ha wagaayn bayzzidos” gadus.
ACT 5:9 Phixxirossaykka “inte Xoossa Ayana paccanas ayys issi dunna gidideti? heeko ne aziina moggida asati moggi simmidi karen pengge bolla deetes. Istti nenakka kessi eikki ehaaththaana” gides.
ACT 5:10 Iza siyda mala herakka iza too bolla kunddada hayqqadus. Atumassaykka soo geellida mala hayqqidaro beeyidi kessi ehaaththaidi izi azzina achchan moggides.
ACT 5:11 Kummetha wossa keeththa asayne hessa siydda asay wuri daroo babiides.
ACT 5:12 Kittetidaytikka dere garssan daroo malatanne mallalisiza mishsh ooththida. Amanizayti wuri “Solomonne pengge geetettiza assi simereetizason shiiqetees.
ACT 5:13 Istas babida gish oonnikka isttara wallakistanas koybeyna. Gido attin derey istta keehi bonches.
ACT 5:14 Daroo maccatinne addetti wodeppe woden Godan ammani ammani istta bolla gujjetida.
ACT 5:15 Hessa gaason Phixxirossay adhdhishin haray attin iza eeshshoy hargganchatappe bagga hargganchata bolla wodhdhana mala harggizayti zinniiza algga bollane zaphpha bolla karen zin7isetes.
ACT 5:16 Yerusalame yushon diza kaatamatappe harggizaytane tuna ayanay waysizayta ehin wuri paxxida.
ACT 5:17 Hessa wode qeessista hallaqayne izara diza Saduqaweti wuri qannate kumida.
ACT 5:18 kittetidayta oykkidi qachcho keeth gelthida.
ACT 5:19 Gido attin Goda kittanchay qaamara qachcho keeththa kaare doyydi istta kessidi,
ACT 5:20 “Biidi Xoossa keethth gibbe giidon eqqidi hayssa deyoo qaala wurso deres yoottite” gides.
ACT 5:21 Gadey wonitdda mala isttas yoottidayssa Xoossa keethth gibbe geellidi dereza tamarso oykkida, qeessista hallaqaynne izara dizaytti yidi Ayhudata duullatane Isra7ele dere cimmata kummeth issi bolla shishida. Kittetidayta qachcho keethafe ekki yanamala asse yedida.
ACT 5:22 Kitteeti bida asati bidi istta qachcho keeththan demmibeytena, Simmidine
ACT 5:23 “Qachcho keethay loeththi qulfeti dees, Naggizaytikka peengge bolla eqqidishin beeyidos, gido attoshin nu doyy gellishin qass keeththan oonikka bawa” gida.
ACT 5:24 Xoossa keeth naggizayta hallaqayne qeessista hallaqatikka hessa siyda mala hanozan daro malalettidane isttas hanoy wuri tikk gides.
ACT 5:25 Heerakka issi urray yiiddi “Hekko inte qachcho keeth gellithida asati Xoossa keeththa gibbe giidon eqqidi dere tammarison deettes” gidees.
ACT 5:26 Xoossa keeth naggizayta hallaqay ba oothanchatara bidi ista oykki ekki yidees. Oykki ehidaytti asay bena shuchchara cadontta mala babbidi wolqathontta loodara ehida.
ACT 5:27 Kittetidayta ehidi Ayhuda dulata sinththan essida. Qeessista hallaqaykka istta “Hayssa ha sunththan inte tammarsontta mala intes loo7ethi yootidoskkoshin inte inte timmiritan Yerussallame wursion deista. Qasse nunakka ha addeza suththas oychcheetizatyta histtanas gixxi denddidista” gides.
ACT 5:29 Phixxirossayne hankko kittetidaytika zaaridi hizzgida “Nuni asape aththidi Xoossas azazistanas beeses.
ACT 5:30 Inte iza miitha bolla kaqqi wodhdhida Yesussa nu aawantta Xoossi iza hayqqope denththides.
ACT 5:31 Izikka Isra7eele naytas nagarappe simmidi maristana mala Xoossi iza wursiofe bollanne ashshizade histtidi ba oshshachchan dhoqqu dhoqqu histtides.
ACT 5:32 Nuunkka hayssas markkata. Qassekka Xoossi bees azazetizaytas immida xiillo ayanayka markka.
ACT 5:33 Asati hessa siyddi iita hanqo hanqqetida, wodhdhanakka koyidda.
ACT 5:34 Gido attin dere achchan kehi bonchetida issi woga asttamare, izikka Gemalliyale geetettiza Faarssawista baggay dullata ass gidon denddi eqqidi kittetidayt guuththa wode Karen gamm7ana mala azazides.
ACT 5:35 Dulata asas hizzgides “Isra7eele asato inte hayta asata bolla ooththanayssa daroo akekkara ooththanas beesses.
ACT 5:36 Hessafe kase issi Tewodassa geetettizadey bena giita ass histti qoodi denddin oydu xeetu derey iza kaallides. Ggido attin izi asa kushshen hayqqides. Iza kaallizaytikka coo lallettin iza hanoy coo mela gidides.
ACT 5:37 Izappe guyekka derey tayybetiza wode Galila Yuday denddidi daro dere benara kaallethides. Bena kaallizaytakka demmides shin izikka dhayides. Iza kaallizaytikka wuri dhayda.
ACT 5:38 Hessa gish ta ha7i intena gizay hayta asata aggite, bochchopite. Istta qoofay woykko istta oosoy asappe gidiko dhayana.
ACT 5:39 Xoossafe gidiko qass inte istta teqqanas dandda7ekista. Oonne errizay inte Xoossara oyeetishe beistanakkonne.
ACT 5:40 Isttika iza zooreza ekkidi kittetidayta xeeygidi garafisida. Namm7anththo Yesussa sunththan hasa7onta mala azazidi yedida.
ACT 5:41 Kittetidaytikka iza sunththa gish kawushshateth ekkanas beesiza gish daroo uhaaththaa7etishe dulata asa achchafe kezzi bida.
ACT 5:42 Galas galas xoossa keeththaninne issa issa keeththan Yesussay izi Xoossi doridade gididayssa tammarsofenne sabbakope mullekka guye gibeytena.
ACT 6:1 Ammanizayta qooday dari dari biza wode girkke biittafe yida ayhuda asati yudan diza ayhuda asa bolla garssara zigiretida, gasooykka wursio wode miza kaathi gishishe ammiista wudan yegontta aggida gishasiko.
ACT 6:2 Hessa gish nu taammane namm7u kittetidayti ammaniza harata issi bolla shishshidi “Nuni kaathi gishshetho ooson gellidi Xoossa qaala tammariso agganas beesena” gida.
ACT 6:3 Hessa gish nu ishshato inte garssafe ciniccata, xiillo ayanan kummidaytane loo7o markkateeth dizayta lappun asi doorte, hayssa halafeteth nu isttas immana.
ACT 6:4 Nuni gidiko wossanine qaala yooton minnana.
ACT 6:5 Istti gida yoyi siyidayta uhaaththaayssides, Ammanonine xiillo ayanan kummidayt Isxxifanose, Philliphosa, Phirisqqorossa, Niqqarona, ximmona, Pharmmenane Yudatethan gellida anxxokiya dere asa gidida Niqqolossa doorda.
ACT 6:6 Heyta ehidi kittetidayta sinthth shishshida, istikka ba kushshe istta bolla wothidi isttas wossida.
ACT 6:7 Xoossa qaalay aakki aakki bides, ammannizayta qooday yerussalamen dari dari bides, qeessistape darooti ammanida.
ACT 6:8 He wode isxxifanosey Xoossa immotethanine wolqan kummid dereza garssan giitta malalisiza malatata ooththides.
ACT 6:9 Wozeetida Ayhudata woossa keeth geeteti xeeygetizasope yida asi gidida Qarenappene Iskkinddriyape; qassekka Kilqqiyappene Issiya awurajjatappe yida asatikka wuri Isxxifanosera marshetida.
ACT 6:10 Gido attin cinccatethan izi hasa7iza hasa7ane izan diza Ayana eqqistanas danda7ibeyteena.
ACT 6:11 Hessa gish “Isxxifanosey Musene Xoossu cayishin nu siydos” giza asata guyera gigisida.
ACT 6:12 Hessa wode dereza, dere cimmatane woga tammarisizayta denthethidanne Isxxifanose oyththidi dere duullatako shishshida.
ACT 6:13 Iza bolla “Hayssi addezi Haysa geesha sooza bollane woga bolla cashsha qaala hasa7a mullekka aggibeyna.
ACT 6:14 Gasooykka haysi addezi Nazirete Yesussay hayssa Xoossa keethth dhayssana gishinnine nu mussepe ekkida woga laammana gi hasa7ishin nu siyidos” gi wordora markkatiza asata shishshi markkasida.
ACT 6:15 Duullata uttida asay wuri Isxxifanose tiishi histti xeellishin iza ayfesoy isttas kittancha ayfeso millati beetides.
ACT 7:1 Qeessista halaqay Isxifanose “haysi ne bolla shiqqida yozi tuumee?” gi oychides.
ACT 7:2 Isxxifanoseykka hizigides “Ta ishaato, ta awwato ta giizaysa siyite nu awa Abramey Kaarane yanappe kasse buro Mesophoxomiyan dishin bonncho Goday izas qonccidi
ACT 7:3 <Ne dereppene ne dabbofe shakeistada ta neena bessizaso ba> gides.
ACT 7:4 Izikka Kaldawista biittafe kezidi Karane biittan uttides. Iza away hayqqidappe guye inte ha7i dizaso ha dere iza ehidees.
ACT 7:5 Haray atoshin issi toy eqiza gadey izas hayssafe immetibeyna. Gido attiin he wode izas issi naykka baynnida dishin izzine izappe guyen iza zerethi biittiyo laatana mala Xoossi izas ccaqqides.
ACT 7:6 Qassekka Xoossi izas hizigi yotides <ne zerethi alagga biittan bete ass gidana. Oyddu xeettu layth aylletetha qammibara garsan wayistana.
ACT 7:7 Gido attiin ista aylle mala harza dere ta qaxxayana. Hessafe guye isti he biittafe kezzidi haanno ha soyin tas goynana.>
ACT 7:8 Hesafe guye qaxxara woga ccaqo izas immides. Abrameykka Yisaqa yellidi iza osppuntha gallasa qaxxarides. Yisaqayka Yaqobe yellides. Yaqobeykka tamane namm77u qomota yellides.
ACT 7:9 He qommota awatti yosefo bolla qanattetidi iza aylletethas duge Gibixe bayzzida. Gido attiin Xoossi izara dees;
ACT 7:10 meto wursofe iza ashides. Gibxe kawo Faaronne sinthan bonncho qumma7isides. Faronney iza Gibxe biitaninne ba keeththa asa wurso bolla alafethethan shuumiides.
ACT 7:11 He wode Kanaaneninne Gibixen daro metto ehida gita koshay dennidides. Nu awataskka miza kaathi dhayides.
ACT 7:12 Yaqobey Giibixe deren kaathi dizayssa siyiddi nu aawata koyyro Gibxe yediides.
ACT 7:13 Istti nam77antho biza wode Yosefoy izi oonakkone bena ba ishatas qonccisides. Faroneykka Yosefo ishshata erides.
ACT 7:14 Hessafe guye Yosefoy kiitidi ba aawa Yaqobenne laappuun tamane ichachu gidiza ba dabota kuummeth ehiisides.
ACT 7:15 Yaqobey duge Gibxe woodhdh7ides. Izikka nu aawatikka wuri heen hayqqida.
ACT 7:16 Ista ahaykka Seekkeme gizaso ehaaththain Abramey Eemore nayytappe ba miishan shammida duhaaththaon moggettides.
ACT 7:17 Xoossi Abrames caaqqida qalay polletiza wodey maatishin Gibixen diza nu asa qodday dari dari bides.
ACT 7:18 Hesafe guye Gibixe bitan yoosefo eronta hara kawoy kawotides.
ACT 7:19 Izikka nu asa ba geene oothon metoothides. Buuro yelletida guutha naytti hayqqana malane yelliidayta kare kessi wora yeganamala wolliqathides.
ACT 7:20 He wode Musey yeletides. Izikka Xoossa achan dosetida malla loo7o na gidides. Be aawa keeththan hedzdzu aggina all7isson diccides.
ACT 7:21 Izi gede worra yeegettida wode kawwo Farone macca nayya deemada bees ekkadus. Be na mala oothada dichadus.
ACT 7:22 Museykka Gibxista eraatetha wurssi tammarides. Yoon erra, oothonikka miinno gididees.
ACT 7:23 “Muse laaythi ooydu tamu gida wode Musey ba ishata Isira7elle nayta beyanas ba wozinan qoppides.
ACT 7:24 Izikka isi Giibixe assi Muse baga asappe isi ura bolla qooho gaathishin beyiddi ba bagga adeza madidi he Gibxe adeza wodhidi he qoheetidayssa hallo keesides.
ACT 7:25 Muses Xoossi iza kushshen issta wozanayssa iza asay akekkiza millatides. Gido atiin issti hessa yuushi qoppibeyteena.
ACT 7:26 Wontetha gallas qasekka Isira7elle naytappe nam7ati ba garssan oyeetishin gakkidi oyetizayta iginthanas koyydi <haytto asato inte inte garssan ishantakko, inte wannidi issay issa qoheetii?> gides.
ACT 7:27 Be lageza bolla qoho gathidaysi Muse suggi yeggidi <Nena nu bolla nuna haarizadene nu bolla piridizade oothi shuumiday oonee? woykko qamma Gibxe adeza wodhoyssatho tannaka wodhana koyaazii?> gides.
ACT 7:29 Musey hessa siyidda mala Midiyame biitta beettidi hen bete ass gidi deyyides. Heenkka nam77u atuma na yeellides.
ACT 7:30 Hessafe oydu tammu laythafe guuye Siina zuma achchan diza bazza biittan qerii worra gidon exxiizza taamma laccon kiitannchay izas bettides.
ACT 7:31 Museykka iza beeydamala mallaleetides. Azakone shaki eranas izzi he izako shiqqishin Goda qalay “tanni ne awannta Xoossa abirame Yisaqane Yaqobe Xoossa gishin siydees. Museykka daro dagammides, xeellanaskka xalibeyna.
ACT 7:33 Godaykka izas hayssi ne eqqidasoy geeshaso gidiida gish ne toope ccamma shoda. Gibxen diza ta dereta waye ta tuumappe beyadis. Issti wasiza issta waye waso siiyada ista ashshanas woodhdhadis. Ne ha7ikka haya ta nena duge Giibixe zarada kiitana gides.
ACT 7:35 Histtin heyyti <nu bolla neena haarizadenne piridizade histti ooni shuumedee?> giidi asay kaase kadhdhida Musse Xoossi qeeri woora gidon izas beetida kiitancha bagara issta haarizadenne ashizade hisitidi istaako zarri yeedides.
ACT 7:36 Izikka ista kallethidi Gibxeppe keesides. Gibxen, zo7o abbanine bazo biittan oyydu taammu laythi daro mallalsiza miishatane gita malatata istas oothides.
ACT 7:37 Isrra7elle nayytas ta mala nabe Xoossi inte garsafe dennthana gidaysi hayssa Musekko.
ACT 7:38 Izikka Siina zuma bolla hassa7ida kitancharanne bazo biitan nu awatara dere dullata giidon dees. Deyyo qalakka ha nuus aathanas ekkides.
ACT 7:39 Nu awati gidiko izara eqqetida attiin izas azazistanas koyoonta gish ba wozinara guuye Giibbxe simmida.
ACT 7:40 Aarooneskka <Nu sinnthara biiza eeqqa nus gigisa nuna Giibbixefe kaallethi kessida Musey wanidako nu erroko> giida.
ACT 7:41 He wode mara miisile meedhdhidi eqqas yarsho shishida. Berkka medhida ba kuushe oothon uhaaththaa7ettidane guppiida.
ACT 7:42 Gido attiin Xoossi isttas zokko zarides. Isti sallo xollinntistas goynana mala aththi immides. Hesikka nabbista mxxaafan “inteno Isra7elle nayto inte baazo biittan oyddu tamu layth diza wode intefe yarshone muuna tas shishi ereetii?
ACT 7:43 Harappekka inte goynanaso othiida eeqqa Molookke dunkenane inte eqqa Refanne xollinnte misile dhoqu dhoqu hissti oykkidista. Hessa gisha ta intena inte dizasoppe dennthada Babiloonera aatha yeddana.” geetetidi xaahaaththaetides.
ACT 7:44 Xoossi Muse bessida lemmusoza malane azazzidayssa mala oothetida Xoossi asara gagiza dunkkaneya nu awatara baazzo biittan deyadus.
ACT 7:45 Nu aawati dunkeneyo ekkidayssappe guye Xoossi Iyaaso kallethin kaase ista gooddida dereta lattida wode dunnkaneyo ekki geellida. Dawite wode gakanas dunkaneyaa he biittan deyadus.
ACT 7:46 Dawiteykka Xoossa sinthan boncho demidi Yaqoobe Godas aqqoso gigisanas woossides.
ACT 7:47 Gido attiin Solmoney izas aqoso kexides.
ACT 7:48 Gido attiin woogga Goday asa kushey keexida keeththan deena. Hesikka nabey <salloy ta zuuppane biittaykka tas tos shemmposo, hiistiin inte tas ay mala keeth kexxeti woykko ta shemmppanasoy awaysse? Hayssa wursi ta kuushshey oothibeynnee? gees Goday> getetti xafetida mala.
ACT 7:51 Inteno wozana mumeto, haytha tuleto, intekka inte aawata amala wursio wode Xiillo Ayanara eqateista.
ACT 7:52 Nbistappe inte aawati gooddonnta naabey oonee? Xiillozi yanayssa kasseti yottida nabetakka wodhida intekka ha7i izza aathi immidistane wodhidista.
ACT 7:53 Kitanncha bagara intes immetida woga ekkidista attiin naggibeykista.” Isxxifanosey Shuchchan Cadeti Hayqidess.
ACT 7:54 Duulatan diza asay hessa siydamala daro hanqitidi, iza bolla ba achche gariccides.
ACT 7:55 Gidinkka Isxxifanosey Xiillo Ayanan kummidine puude salo tish histi xeellishin Xoossa bonchon Yesussay Xoossa oshachan eqqidayssa beydi “Heeko ta saaloy doyeetidayssane asa nay Xoossa ushachan eqqiidayssa beyays” gidees.
ACT 7:57 Hesa wode asay qaala dhoqu histi waasishe ba haythe tuucci oykidi izako isppe woxxida.
ACT 7:58 Isxxifanose oykkidi katamappe gede kare hallida. Shuchan cach oykkida. Hesi wuri hannishin marikkatikka ba mayo Sawulle gettetiza pantha achchan wothida.
ACT 7:59 Isti shuchara iza cadishin Isxxifanosey “ta Goda Yesussa ta sehmppiyo neeko eekka” gidi woosides.
ACT 7:60 Qassekka gulbatidi dhoqa qalan “Godo haytananta nagara qodopa” gidi wassides. Hesa gidappe guye hayqqides
ACT 8:1 Sawuleyka isixxipanose hayqon isttara qofan gagidees. He wode Yerusalamen diza ammanizayta bolla gitta goodetethi denddides. Kittetidayti atta ammanizayti wuri yuda awurajjanine saamariya awurajjan wursion lalletida.
ACT 8:2 Ayana ooson miinni eqqida asati Isixxifanose moggidi, izas daroo yeekkida.
ACT 8:3 Sawuley qasse wossa keeththa dhayssanas giixxi denddides. Ammaniza asa issa issa keethi gellidi maccatane addista goochi goochi keesiddi qasho keeththan yeegides.
ACT 8:4 Laalletidayti wuri ba bidason bidason Xoossa qaala yootida.
ACT 8:5 Pilphphossaykka Sammariya geetettiza kaatama wodhdhidi asas kiristtossa sabakkides.
ACT 8:6 Daro derey Pilphphossay ooththiza malata beeydi izzi yootiza qaala wozinappe lo7ethi siyides.
ACT 8:7 Tuuna ayannatikka daroo asappe wassi wassi kezzida. daro too siillattine wobeetiikka paxxida.
ACT 8:8 Hessa gish he kaatamma asay daroo uhaaththaa7etides.
ACT 8:9 Gido attin hessafe kase he kaattamayin maro marotiidi Sammariya asa daroo malalisizaz ooththiza issi Simmona giza maroy dees. Izikka bena giita asa mala qoodizade.
ACT 8:10 Assay wuri guuthatappe gitata gakkanaas wurikka “haysi addezi gitta wolqama geetettiza Xoossa wolqako” gishe izi giza wursi wozinape siyees.
ACT 8:11 Daroo wode ba marrotetha ooson asa malalisida gish asay iza wozinappe kaalishe gam7ides.
ACT 8:12 Gido attin Pilphphossay Xoossa kawootetha gishine Yesuss kiristtossa gish sabbakkiidayssa siyidi ammanniida maccashayne atummassay xammaqetides.
ACT 8:13 Simmonaykka ammaniid xammaqetides. Pilphphossakka kaalli bidi haniza giita mallata beeyidi malaletides.
ACT 8:14 Yerusalamen diza kitetidayti, Sammariya asay Xoossa qaala ekkidi amanidayssa siydi Phixxirossane Yanissa isttakko kittida.
ACT 8:15 Isttikka Sammariya gakkidi ammanida asay Xiillo Ayana ekkana mala asas woossida.
ACT 8:16 Gasoykka he wode istti coo Yesussa sunththan xamaqetida attin buroo Xiillo Ayanay isttafe issade bollakka woodhdhibeyna.
ACT 8:17 Hessa gish Phixxirossayne Yanissay ba kushshe asa bolla woththin asay Xiillo Ayana ekkides.
ACT 8:18 Simonaykka kitetidayti kushshe woththi wossin Xiillo Ayanay imeetizayssa beeydi Phixxirossasine Yanissas miishshe eekki yiddi
ACT 8:19 “Ta iza bolla ta kushshe woththizadey wuri xiillo ayana ekkana mala hayssa mala godateeth taskka immite” giin,
ACT 8:20 Phixxirossay izas zaaridi “Xoossa immotethi ne mishshan shammana qoppiida gish neni ne mishshara isfe dhaya.
ACT 8:21 Ne wozinay Xoossa sinththan suure gidontta gish nes hayssa ha oosozan gishay woykko eexxa deena.
ACT 8:22 Hayssa ne iitatetha gish ha7i elle marotethan gella, nes Goda wossa, hayssa ne wozina qoohaaththaa nes atto ganakone oone errizay.
ACT 8:23 Gasoykka neni iitatethan kummidaysane makal77an qachchista uttidaysi taas bettees” gides.
ACT 8:24 Simmonaykka zaaridi “Inte gida yootappe aykoykka ta bolla gakontta mala tas Goda wossiti” gides.
ACT 8:25 Phixxirossayne Yanissay Goda qaala markkatidayssafene qonccisi yootidayssafe guye daroo Sammariya manddarattan mishshiracho sabbakishe Yerusalame simmida.
ACT 8:26 Goda kitanchay pilphphoossa “dendda! Yerussalameppe duge baggara gede Gaaza ehaaththaiiza baazo oggara ba” gides.
ACT 8:27 Izikka denddi bides. Hinddako geetettiza Tophiya kawooya ba keeththanine ba kawootethan diza wurso mishsha bolla allafetethan woththida issi Tophiya gunddula assi izara gaggides. He addezi Xoossas goynana Yerusalame bides.
ACT 8:28 Izi heppe simmishe paara gaaren uttidi nabe Issayasa maaxxafa nababes.
ACT 8:29 Ayanay pilphphoossa “Ba sekki paara gaarezakko shiiqa” gides.
ACT 8:30 Pilphphoossaykka eesotidi paara garezako biiddi adezi nabe Isayasa maaxxahaaththaa nababishin siyidi “Hessi ne nababizayssi nes gellizee?” gides.
ACT 8:31 Addezika tana erisiza urray bayndda ta wostta ero?” gides, Izikka gede iza gaarezan gellidi iza achchan uttana mala wossides.
ACT 8:32 Izi nababiiza maaxxahaaththaay “Izi dorssa mala shukeistana laagetides, dorssa laaqqay iththike qanxxizade sinththan co7u giza mala hessathokka izi ba duuna poggibeyna.
ACT 8:33 Bena kawushidi pirday bayndadde gidides. Iza shemppoya biitta bollafe diggista gish, iza yelletitha gish hasa7ana danddaizay oonne?” gees.
ACT 8:34 Addezika zaaridi pilphphoossa “Nabezi hayssa oonna gish gize? Be gish gizeye woykko hara urra gish gizee? Hayana tas yootarkkii!” gides.
ACT 8:35 Pilphphosaykka ba duna doyydi he maaxxaahaaththaappe oykkidi Yesussa mishiracho qaala gish markkatides.
ACT 8:36 Istti isfe bishe haaththi dizaso gakkida. Addezika “Heko haththi hayssan dees, Histtin ta xammaqetontta mala digizay aaze? gides
ACT 8:37 Pilphphoossaykka ne kummetha wozanappe ammanikko xammaqistana dandda7asa giides. Addezika “Yesus Kiristtossay Xoossa na gididayssa amanays” gides.
ACT 8:38 Adezi paara gaarezi eqqana mala azazin namm7ay isfe haathan woodhdhin Pilphphoossay addeza xammaqides.
ACT 8:39 Istt haathafe kezishin Xoossa Ayanay Pilphphoossa denththi ehaaththaides. Addez hessafe guye iza beeybeyna. Gido attin uhaaththaaysan ba ogge bides.
ACT 8:40 Hessafe guye Pilphphoossay Azaxxone gizason betides. Qisaariya gizaso gakkanaas izi biza ogge bolla kaataman wurson mishshiracho qaala sabbakides.
ACT 9:1 Sawuley Goda ammaniiza asa wodhannas ceqetishshe qeessista halaqqako bidees.
ACT 9:2 Goda oggee kaallizayta maccatanne addeista demmi qachchidi Yerusalame ekki yannas Damasqqoo gizason diza Ayhudata wossa keethas dabbidabe xaafana mala qeessista halaqa woosides.
ACT 9:3 Damasqqo gakkanna matishshin qoppontta salope po77oy iza yushshon pol7u giides.
ACT 9:4 Izikka herakka biitta bolla kunddidi salope “Sawule Sawule” tana aazas gooddazii? giza qaala siyydes.
ACT 9:5 Sawuleykka Godo ne oonnee? giides. Izikka izas “tanni ne goodeththiza Yesussakko!
ACT 9:6 Ne ha7i denddada gede kaatama gella, ne ooththanas besiizaz nes yootana” gides.
ACT 9:7 Sawulera isippe biza asati qaala gireththi sisafe attin oonnakka beeyonntta gish ba dunna oykki eqqiida.
ACT 9:8 Sawuley ba kunddidasope denddidi ayfee doyi xeellizza wode aykokka demmanas dandda7ibeyna. Hessa gish izara diza asatti iza kushshe oykkiddi kaaleththi ekkidi Dammasqqo ehaaththaida.
ACT 9:9 Hedzdzu gaalas gakkanaas qooqidine kathth hathth beeybeyna.
ACT 9:10 Dammasqqon issi Hananiiya geetetiiza ammannizadey dees. Izas Goday ajjutan “Hananiiya” giddi xeeygides, izikka “yee Godo” gides.
ACT 9:11 Godaykka iza “dendda Surre geetettiza oggeyra Yuda geetettizadeso ba. Heen Sawule geetettiza issi Xarssesse assi wossishshe dess ne iza koya deemma.
ACT 9:12 Gasooykka Hananiya geetetizzadey Sawuley dizaso yiddi izi xeelana mala iza bolla ba kushshe wothishinine ajjutan beyidees.
ACT 9:13 Hananiyaykka zaaridi “Godo” ha urray Yerussalemen diza geshshata bolla aymala qooho gaththidakone ta daroo asape siyadiss.
ACT 9:14 Izi haa yiday ne sunththa xeeygizayta wurssi qachchanas qeessista halaqqatape godateth ekkiddikko.
ACT 9:15 Godaykka izas “Ne ba! haysi addezi Isra7ele gidonta dereta sinththanine kawoota sinththan hessaththokka Isra7eele dere sinththan ta sunththu tookana mala izi tas dooretiddade.
ACT 9:16 Izi ta sunththa gish aymalla waaye beeyanako ta iza beesana” gides.
ACT 9:17 Hananiyaykka bidi izas yoottetidaso gelideess. Sawule bolla ba kushshe woththiddi “Ta ishsha Sawule ne ha yishshin nes ogge bolla qonccida Goda Yesussay ne ayfeey xeelana malane Xiillo Ayanan nenan kumana mala tana neekko kittides” gidees.
ACT 9:18 Herakka Sawule ayfepe poqqo malay poqqeti wodhdhin Izi xeellana dandda7idesine denddi xamaqetides.
ACT 9:19 Kaththika miiddi minnides. Unddena wode ammanizaytara Dammasqqon gammides.
ACT 9:20 Herakka Yesussay Xoossa na gididayssa Ayhudata wossa keethatan tammariso oykkides.
ACT 9:21 Siyida asay wuri “haysii yerussalamen ha sunththa xeeygizayta dhayisiza addeza giidene? Qasse izi ha yiday he asata qachchi ekki qeessista halaqatako ehaaththaanas gideene” gishe malaletida.
ACT 9:22 Sawuley kasepe minni minni bides. Damasqqon diza Ayhudatas Yesussay izi Xoossi kittidade gididaysa ammanthishe asa duuna oyththides.
ACT 9:23 Daroo gaalassatape guye Ayhudatti Sawule wodhdhanas dulatida.
ACT 9:24 Izikka istta qoofa errides. Isttikka iza wodhdhanas kaatama gelthiza ogen gaalassine qama nagiida.
ACT 9:25 Ammaniizayti gidiiko iza gidothth kaatama gimbbe guththa lukoor xaysen duge wooththida.
ACT 9:26 Sawuley Yerusalame yiidi ammanizaytara wallakettana koyin isti izi tumu ammanizade gididayssa ammanetoontta gish izas babbida.
ACT 9:27 Gido attin Barnabassay iza kittetidaytako ehaaththain sawuley izi Damasqqo ogge bolla Goda wostti beeydakoone Godaykka izas ayi yootidakoone qasekka Damasqqon dishshe izi aymala xalateththara Yesusa suntahan sabakidakko isttas yootides.
ACT 9:28 Hessa gish Sawuley isttara deyides. Yerusalamen yuyi yuyidi babontta goda sunththan yootids.
ACT 9:29 Girikke derepe yida Ayhudistara hasa7ishe palameetides, gido attin asaykka iza wodhanas koydes.
ACT 9:30 Ammanizayitti hessa erridi duge Qisariya gizaso woththidi Xarssesse yediida.
ACT 9:31 Hessa wode Yudanine Galilan, Sammariyankka diza ammanizaytti saron deyiddi kasepe minnida. Qasseka Xoossa yashshatethan simeretishshe Xiillo Ayanan minetidane kasepe qoodan dari dari biida.
ACT 9:32 Phixiroossay derepe deren yuyishshe Liida kataman diza ammanizayta beeyanas dugge wodhdhides.
ACT 9:33 Heen Eena geetettizade osppun layththa hixxan qachchetida issi gundda assi demmides.
ACT 9:34 Phixiroossaykka “Hayso Eena Yesuss kiristtossay nena paththana, dendda ne hiixa denththa” giides. Eenay herakka puththurkku gi dendides.
ACT 9:35 Liidanine Saroonan diza asay wuri iza beeyidi Godan ammanides.
ACT 9:36 Yoophe gizason Xabbiita geetettiza issi ammanizara daysu. Izi sunththa birshechchi Girkke qaalara “dorqqa” geetetes. Iza wursio wode loo77o ooso minna ooththashene manqqota maddashe daysu.
ACT 9:37 He wode iza harggada heyqqin asay aha mecci pude fooqqen kesii wothida.
ACT 9:38 Liiday Yophphes maata gidida gish ammanizayti phixiroossay Liidan dizayssa siyddi namm7u asata kittidi “Elle ha yarkki” gi wossida.
ACT 9:39 Phixiroossaykka denddidi kittetida asatara gakkida wode iza pude he fooqqe bolla kessida. Am7etikka wuri iza yuyi aadhi eqqidi dorqqay paxxa dashe isttara ooththida qamisatane mayoota besi besi yeekkida.
ACT 9:40 Phixiroossaykka asa wursi kifilezape keesikinne gulbatidi woossides. Ahakko simmidi “Hane xabbiita dendda!” gidees. Izakka ba ayfe dooyada xeeladdus. Phixiroossaka beeyada dendda utadusu.
