ACT 25:14 Istti hen daroo galas uttida gish Fisxxossay Phawulossa yooza kawoo Agirphphas hizzgi yootides “Filkisey qaachcho kethan yegi agiida issadey haan dees.
ACT 25:15 Ta Yerusalamen bida wode qeessista hallaqatinne Ayhudata ciimmati ha addeza yoo taako ehidi ta iza bolla pirdana mala oychchida.
ACT 25:16 Ta qasse mootetidadey mootizayta sinththan eqqidi bena mootiza yoozas beessiza malththe immontta dishin mootetidade aththi immooy Rome kawootethas woga gidena” gaada zaaradis.
ACT 25:17 Hessa gish iza mootizayti shiiqetidi yida mala herakka wonttetha gallas pirda wombboran uttada Phawulossa ta sinthth shishshana mala azazadis.
ACT 25:18 Iza mootizayti iza achchan eqqida wode istti iza bolla shishshida mootoy ta baggara izi iitta oothontta agena gaada qopida mala gidibeyna.
ACT 25:19 Gido attin istti izara mootetizay ba ammano gishshine Phawulossay issi hayqqidade <Paxa dees> giza Yesussa gish gidides.
ACT 25:20 Takka hessa mala yoo qora xeellanas tana metida gish Phawulossa <Ne Yerusalame baada heyssa yooza hen pirdistana koyyaz?> gadis.
ACT 25:21 Hizzgin izi qasse yoozi Rome kawoo sinththan beyistana mala koyidi <ta yooy Qeessare sinthth shiiqana mala oychchayss> gida gish iza yoo Qeessarekko ta yeeddana gakkanaas izi qachcho keeththan gamm77ana mala azazadis.”
ACT 25:22 Agirphphay Fisxxossa “Takka izi giza siyana koyayss” gides; Fisxxossaykka “Wontto siyanddassa” gides.
ACT 25:23 Hessa gish wonttetha gallas Agirphphayne Barniqey kawooti mayiza mayo maydine daro bonchora ola asa halaqatarane he kaataman diza giita asatan azhabbeti yiidi pirda keeth gellida. Hessafe guye Fisxxossay Phawulossa xeeyigisides.
ACT 25:24 Fisxosay hizzgides “Kawoo Agirphpha! qass nunara diza asato; Ayhuda asati wuri <hayssi addezi hayssafe guye paxxa daana beessena> giidi wassishe Yerussalamenkka haanikka iza bolla pirdistana mala istti tana oychchizay hayssa inte beeyiza addeza gishshaskko.
ACT 25:25 Ta ta boggara iza hayqqos gaaththiza issi balakka iza bolla demmabeyikke. Izi ta yooy Rome kawoo sinthth shiiqi beeyeto gida gish ta iza he yeeddanas qachchadis.
ACT 25:26 Gido attin iza gish ta ta godas xaahaaththaana giza errettida yoy deena; Hessa gish iza issi issi pacce oychchota oychchiko tas xaahaaththaanaysi daanakkone gaada inteko; harapekka kawoo Agirphpha neekko shishshadis.
ACT 25:27 Gasooykka qachcho assi puude bollattiza dhoqqa dannakko bishin izi mootetiza yo qonccisontta aggoy asa eyya kessizayssi tas bettides.”
ACT 26:1 Agirphphay Phawulossa “ne ne gish hasa7anas dandda7assa> gides. Phawulossaykka ba kushe denthidi malththe hizgi immides.
ACT 26:2 “Kawoo Agirphpha! tana Ayhudati moootiza yoo wursisos hach ta ne sinththan tana maadana malththe immiza gish tana daroo ufayses.
ACT 26:3 Gasoyka ne Ayhudata wogane istta palama wursia looetha errasa; Hessa gish ne ta giza wursia dandda7ada siyana mala ta nena wosays.
ACT 26:4 “Tani guuththa nateththa wodeppe oykkada waana deydakko Ayhuda asati erretes. Koyrope ha7i gakkanaas ta ta dere asa gidoonine Yerusalamen ta deyda duussu asay erres.
ACT 26:5 Qassekka istti markkatana koykko nu ammano gish ta keha minththa woga naggiza Parsawe bagga gidada gamm7idade gididayssa istti koyrope denththidi erretes.
ACT 26:6 Ha7i qasse pirdas tana hayssan essiday Xoossi kasse nu aawatas immida caaqqo qaala uhaaththaayssa gishaskko.
ACT 26:7 Ha uhaaththaayssako gakkanaas nu zarkketi taammane namm7ati Xoossa gaallasine qamma goyinnishe naggida. Kawo nees too! takka Ayhudati tana mootizay ha yoza gishaskko.
ACT 26:8 Xoossi hayqqidayta denththanayssi wannidi Ayhuda gidida inte achchan ammanetibeyne?
ACT 26:9 Takka ta baggara Nazirete Yesussa sunththa eqqistanas beses gada qoppadis shin;
ACT 26:10 Tani Yerusalamen ooththidaykka hessakoshin; Qeessista hallaqqatape ta ekkida godateththara ammanizaytape daroota qasho keeththan yegiissadis; istta wodhdhishin wodhdhizaytara isfe days.
ACT 26:11 Daro wode Ayhudata wossa keethati dizason awankka istti qaaxxayistana malanne ba ammano kadana mala ooththadis; Istta bolla daro hanqqistadakka Isra7eleppe karen diza hara kaatamatakka baada ammanizayta goodadis.
ACT 26:12 “Hayssa ha yoozas Qeessista hallaqatappe kummetha godateththine azazo ekkada dammasqqo gizaso ta bishin;
ACT 26:13 Kawoo nes too! Buroo ta ogen dishin gadey seeta gallas gidishin awa arshe poo7oppe adhdhiza poo7o beyadis; He poo7oy tanane tanara biza asata yuuy adhdhidi salope po7ides.
ACT 26:14 Nu wurkka biita bolla kundidishin Ayhudata qaalara <Sawulle! Sawulle! tana aazas goddazi? Neni qara maashsha bolla eqqiikko nerkka nena qohasa> giza qaala siyadis.
ACT 26:15 Takka <Godo! ne oonne?> Gadis; Godaykka <Ta ne Goda Yesussako!
ACT 26:16 Ha7i denddada ne toon eqqa; ta nes qoncciday ne tana ha7i beyidaysanine sinththafe ta nena beessanayssan ne tas markkatizade gidana mala ta nena shuumana koyadis.
ACT 26:17 Isra7ele asa kushepene ta nena isttakko kittiza Ayhuda gidoontta dere asata kusheppekka ashshana.
ACT 26:18 Ne istta ayfe doyana malane dhumape poo7on kessana mala qassekka xalla7es harettizasope Xoossakko ne zaarana mala ooththana; isttikka tana ammanida gish ba nagarappe marettana qasse dorettidayta giddon istti laata gade demana> gidees.
ACT 26:19 “Hessa gish kawoo Agirphpha! Salope tas immetida ajjutas ta azazettadis.
ACT 26:20 Gido attin ta kassistada Dammasqqon diza asa kaaliethada Yerussalamenine Yuhuda deren wursion dizayta qassekka Ayhuda gidoontta deretikka nagare ogeppe Xoossakko simmidi maretna mala erisadis. Istti nagarappe simmidayssa beessizayssa ooththana mala ta isttas yootadis.
ACT 26:21 Hessa gaason Ayhudati ta Xoossa keeththan dishin tana oykkidi wodhdhana koyda.
ACT 26:22 Hachch gakkanaaskka tas Xoossafe maadoy pacci errena. Hesa gish guuththaskka gitaskka markkatashe hayssan eqqadis. Nabetinne Mussey kassetidi hayssa malay hanana gidayssa yootope attin ta hara aykkokka yootabeykke.
ACT 26:23 Isttikka yootidaysi <Xoossi kittidadey meto beeyana, hayqqope denddon koyro gididi, asi attana poo7o Isra7ele deresinne Isra7ele nayta gidontta deretas qonccana> gizayssakko.”
ACT 26:24 Phawulossay hessa yootishin Fisxxossay “Phawulossa! ha7i ne gooyyontta aggakka; ne daro taamaridayssi nena goshshides” gi wassides.
ACT 26:25 Phawulossay gidikko izas hizzgi zaarides “boncho Fisxxossa! ta nes tuma erada yootayss attin goyabeyke.
ACT 26:26 Ta iza sinththan qonccera yootida kawooy hayssa yooza erres; hayssikka qootara ooththetonttayssa gidida gish kawooy erranayssa ta ammanetayss.
ACT 26:27 Kawoo Agirphpha! nabeta ammanasa gidikki? ne ammanizayssa ta errayss.”
ACT 26:28 Agirphphaykka Phawulossa “Hekko ne tana hanno guuththa wode garssan ammanthana koyasa” gides.
ACT 26:29 Phawulossakka izas zaaridi “guuththa woden gidinkka woykko daro woden ne xalla gidontta dishin hach ta yootidayssa siday wuri hanno ta qachcheteththia atta wurikka ta mala gidana mala ta Xoossa wossayss” gides.
ACT 26:30 Hessafe guye kawooy, dere ayssizaysi, Barnqanne isttara uttida asaykka wuri denddides.
ACT 26:31 Istti hepe kezi bishe ba garssan hays addezi hayqqos woykko qachchos gaththiza mishshe aykokka ooththibeyna” gida.
ACT 26:32 Agirphphaykka Fisxxossa “hayssi addezi yooza Qessares shiiqo gonttako aykko woththoy bayndda mela yedistanako shin” gides.
ACT 27:1 Nuni Xaallane dere markkaben baana mala geeteti qachchetida gish Phawulossane hara qachcho asatakka kawoo Awugisxxossa ola wotadarata gidoofe gidida Yulliyossa geetettiza xeetu halaqas aththi immida.
ACT 27:2 Issiya abba achan diza dereta biza markkaben gillidi bidos. Tesellonqqen diza issi Maqidonyya asi Arisxxirokossa geetettizadey nunara dees.
ACT 27:3 Wonttetha gallas sidona gizaso gakkidos; Yulliyossay Phawulossas loo7o gidida gish Phawulossay ba laggetakko biidi asay izas koshshiza maado ooththana mala piqade immides.
ACT 27:4 Heepe danddi nu bishin sinththa baggara carkkoy nu bolla carkkiza gish abba gidoon diza Qophphorosse deren gemmetidi gede sinththe bidos.
ACT 27:5 Killqqiya gizassone Phinhaaththailiya giza dere achchan diza abba pinddi Luqqiya giza deren diza Muura giza kaatama gakkidos.
ACT 27:6 Heen xeistata hallaqay Xallane dere biza iskkinddiriya dere markkabe demmidi nuna izan gellithides.
ACT 27:7 Daroo gallas loddu gi gi biidi daroo wayettidi Qandose geetettiza kaatama achchi gakkidos; Carkkoykka nu sinthth boontta mala diggin Sallimoon achchara adhdhidi Qarxxese geetettiza abba gidoon diza haruro deren gemettidi bidos.
ACT 27:8 Daroo wayettidi dira dira oykki nu adhdhidape guye Lasyya giza kaatama achchan diza “Loo7o” geetettiza markabe getetizaso gakkidos.
ACT 27:9 Nu biza oge bolla daroo dabuuran xooma wodey adhdhida gish ha7i abba bolla baanas daroo meeto gidida gish Phawulossay benara diza asay naggettana mala hizzgides.
ACT 27:10 “Aso! hayssafe nu kaallidi baana buussay daroo meetora dizayssi tas beettes; Markkabezan diza caanaza bollanne markkabeza bolla xalala gidoontta asa shemppo bollaka gita qohooy gakkana.”
ACT 27:11 Xeistata halaqay qass Phawulossa zoreppe bollara markkabeza lagiza wanazinne marakabeza goday gizayssa siyides.
ACT 27:12 He markkabey eqqizasoy ballggoy adhdhana gakkanaas markkabes loo7o shempposo gidoontta gish dariza bagga asay “hammutha sinthth gujjanas dandda7ettiko away wullizasope duge baggarane puude baggara diza Pinqqe gizaso Qarxeese markkabe shempposo nu gakkidi ballggo heen aaththos” giidi ba qoofa shishshida.
ACT 27:13 Duge baggara guuththa carkkooy carkkishin beeyidi istti qoppida mala hanana millattin baana kezida; Markkabey eqqizasope baana denddidi qarxxeese achchara dira dira oykkidi adhdhi bida.
ACT 27:14 Gido attin guuththa wodepe guye “Away mokkizasope puude bagara yiza gote carkko” geetettiza iita wolliqama carkkoy abba gidoon diza dereype denddidi isttakko abba gidoo yides.
ACT 27:15 Markkabeya carkkoy sugin carkkara eqqeettana dandda7ontta ixxin nu coou giidi carkkoy ehaaththaizaso bidos.
ACT 27:16 Qeeda geetettiza abba gidoon diza dere dizarin geemettidi nu bishin daroo wayettidi markkabeza qeeri wogoloyo oykkidi essanas dandda7idos.
ACT 27:17 Markkabeza laaggizayti qeeri wogoloyo markkabezako goochchi keessidi markkabeza woodorora xaxxida. Markkabezikka Surtese geetettiza abba accey dari dizason kunddontta mala babbidi iza bolla diza shaara woththidi carkkon laageti bida.
ACT 27:18 Gote carkkoy miinni bida gish wonttetha gallas markkkabezan caanettida miishshata issa issa abba gidoo yeggeth oykkida.
ACT 27:19 Hedzdzanththo gallas markkabezas koshshiza miishshatakka ba kushera kessi kessi yeggida.
ACT 27:20 Daroo wode gakkanaas awa arsheka xoolintteka beyontta aggida gishinne carkkoyka kasseppe miinni miinni biza gish hayssafe guye nu attana dandda7okko giza qohaaththaan ufays qanxidos.
ACT 27:21 Asay kathth moontta daro gallas uttides. Hessa gish phawulossay asa gidoon eqqidi hizgides “ha asato! Inte ta giza siyidi Qarxxeseppe denddonttako ha qohoyne ha dhayoy inte bolla gakkenakoshin.
ACT 27:22 Ha7ikka markkabezi xalla qohettana attin intefe issade shempoykka dhayenna. Hessa gish aykkoy bawa; babbofite gaada intena zorayssl.
ACT 27:23 Qamma omars ta izas gidida ta goynniza Xoossi kittida kitanchay ta achchan eqqidi
ACT 27:24 <Phawulosa! Babbopa ne Qeessare sinththan eqqana beeses; hekko nenara isfe bizayta wurssi Xoossi ne gish hayqqope ashshana> giidi tas yootides.
ACT 27:25 Hessa gish inteno asato aykkoy bawa; Xoossi tas hayssa yootidayssa polanayssa ta ammanayss.
ACT 27:26 Gidikokka hayssa gote carkkozi gede issi abba gidoon diza dere achchi ehaaththaidi nuna yeggana.”
ACT 27:27 Taammanne oyddanththo qaamma Mediterane abba gidoon carkkoy nuna wayssishin bishe gidi giddothi markkabeza lagaizaytas abbafe biita bolla gakkida millatides.
ACT 27:28 Hessa gish abba ciimmmateth erranas abban yeggi xeelliza wodoro istti yeggi xeellishin; abba ciimmatethi oyddu taamu mitire keena gidi beettides; gammishe haikka yeggin hedzdzu taamu mitire keena ciimma gididayssa demmida.
ACT 27:29 Nu diza markkabey abba gaxxan diza zaalla shuchchara gaccetontta mala babbidi markkabezappe guye baggara markkabey qaxxontta mala nagiza dhishshike duge abba gidoo yeggida. Hessafe guye isttas qamay wonttana mala woossa oykida.
ACT 27:30 Markabeza lagizayti markkabezape kezidi baqqatana koyda gish markkabezappe sinththa baggara markkabe naggiza dhishshke yegiza millatidi markkabeza bolla diza qeeri wogoloyo duge aabba gidoo yeggida.
ACT 27:31 Hessa wode phawulossay xeetu olla asa hallaqane olla asa wotadarata “hayti markkabezan diza asati markkabeza bolla shemppidi uttontta aggiko intekka attana dandda7ekkista” gides.
ACT 27:32 Hessa gish olla asati wogoloyo oykkida wodoroza qanxxi yeggin iza abba bolla tookistana mala yeedi aggida.
ACT 27:33 Gadey wonttana gishin wurikka kathth maana mala phawulossay istta hizzgi wossides “inte aazi hananesha giidi hirgan kathth moontta aaggin hachchi taammane oyddanththo gaallaskko.
ACT 27:34 Hessa gish inte kathth maana mala ta intena wossayss. Inte miikko miinnana; muleka aykko qohoykka inte bolla gakkena.”
ACT 27:35 Izi hessa gidape guye kathth ekkidi xoossu galatidi asa wursso sinththan kaath muussu oykkides.
ACT 27:36 Hessa wode wurikkka minetidi kaththi mida.
ACT 27:37 Markkabeza gidoon diza asay wuri nam77u xeistane laapun taammanne usupuna.
ACT 27:38 Wurikka mi kaallidape guye markkaben caanetida gistteza duge abba gidoo yeggidi markkabeza deexo kawushshida.
ACT 27:39 Gadey wonttin ba dizaso erribeytena. Gido attin accEy dizaso abba kirqqunththu demmida. Isttas dandda7etizako markkabeza he sugi shishshana qoppida.
ACT 27:40 Markkabeza oykkiza dhishike qanxidi aabba gidoo yeggida. He wode markkabe laggiza wodorota birshida. Ha baggara diza shaara carkko bagga dhoqu histtidi kezana abba gaxa bida.
ACT 27:41 Gido attin markkabeza droo accey koreti uttidayssara iccetidi duge gufaniddes.; Siidhe bolla duge dhishshiketidi qaxxonttayssa giddies. Qass abba dambbalay daroope denddidayssan guye baggara meqqereteth oykkides.
ACT 27:42 Qachcho asappe isadeykka abban wodhdhidi kessi ekkontta mala olla asati wodhana qoppida.
ACT 27:43 Xeistata hallaqay qass Phawulossa ashshanas koyda gish istta qohaaththaa ekkana koybeyna. Gido attin haththe waadhi errizayti markkabezape duge abban guppi guppi woodhdhidi gede biita bolla kezana mala azazides.
ACT 27:44 Hinkko attidayti qass sanqqata bollane markkabepe meeqqi wodhdhida sanqqa bolla abba pinnanamala azazides; hessaththo handdi wurikka saaron abba gidoofe biita bolla gakkida.
ACT 28:1 Nu biittay dizaso saarotethan gakkidape guye nu gakkida abba gidoon diza derey malta geetettizaro gididaro erridos.
ACT 28:2 He dereyin diza asay daroo malaliza keyateth nus ooththides. He wode iray bukkida gishine meego gidida gish tama eththidi nuna mokki ekkida.
ACT 28:3 Phawulossay ahaaththaira miithth shishshidi taaman gujin taama seelappe denddidayssan shoshshi kezidi iza kushe bolla xaaxxetides.
ACT 28:4 Malta asay shoshshi Phawulossa kushe bolla xaaxxetidayssa beeyidi “hayssi addezi shemppo wodhdhidade; gasooykka abba bullahepekka izi attidi yikokka pirdiza Xoossafe kessi ekkidi paxxa daana dandda7ebeyna” giidi ba garssan hasa7ettida.
ACT 28:5 Phawulossay qass shoshsha duge taman qooqofi yeegidi aykokka hanibeyna.
ACT 28:6 Asaykka “Aydepe ayde iza asatethay kixxanesha, woykko qoopontta kundidi hayqqana” giidi naggides; Gido attin istti daroo wode naggishin iza bolla aykkoyne hanonttayssa beeyidi ba qoofa lammidi “hayssi addezi Xoossa” gides.
ACT 28:7 He nu dizaso matan abba gidoon diza dereyo ayssiza Puppulyyosa geetettizadees gadey des; he addezi nuna mookki ekkidi besoon hedzdzu gallas gakkanaas loo7ethi imatides.
ACT 28:8 Heeni Puppulyyosa aawa michchayinne guso harrigey sakkin zinniidi des; Phawulossay izakko gellidi izas wossidesinne iza bolla kushe woththidi paththides.
ACT 28:9 Hessi hessaththo hanidape guye he dereyin diza hara harriganchati yiidi paxxida.
ACT 28:10 Asaykka nus daroo mishshe ehidi nuna bonchizayssa nuna bessida; nu markkaben baana denddin nus koshshizayssa markkaben wursi caandda.
ACT 28:11 Nu maltan hedzdzu aggina gammidape guye ballggoy adhdhana gakkanaas abba gidoon diza dereyin gammiidi Iskindiryappe yiza markkaben gellidi baana denddidos; He markkabeza bolla Diyossiqqorossa geetettiza nam77u mentte eqqata mislley dees.
ACT 28:12 Gede Sirakkose geetettiza kaatama gakkidi heen hedzdzu gallas gammidos.
ACT 28:13 Heepe abba bollara biidi Regiyome geetettiza kaatama gakkidos; Heen issi gallas aqidi duge baggara yiza carkkoy carkkida gish nam77anththo gallas Putiyolusa geetettizaso bidos.
ACT 28:14 Heen ammanizayta demmidi isttara nu lappun gallas gakkanaas uttana mala nuna wossida. Heeppe qasse Rome bidos.
ACT 28:15 Romen diza ammaniza asay nu gish siyidi Ahaaththaiyossa geetettiza giyane “hedzdzu aqoso” geetettizaso gakkanaas nuna mookkana yida; phawulossaykka ista beeydi Xoossu galatidesinne minetides.
ACT 28:16 Nuni Rome gelida wode Phawulossa naganas issi wotadaray izas immettin Phawulossay berkka daana mala izas fiiqadey immettides.
ACT 28:17 Hedzdzu gaallassafe guye Phawulossay Romen diza Ayhudatape gita asata beekko xeeyigisides; isttikka izakko shiiqin hizzgides “Ta ishato! tani isiraele dere bollane nu aawata woga bolla ooththida issi qohooykka deena; Gido attin yerussalamen tana qachchidi Rome asatas aththi immida.
ACT 28:18 Rome asati tana qori oychchidappe guye tana hayqos gaththiza mishshe demmontta aggida gish birshi yeedana koyida.
ACT 28:19 Shin Ayhude asay ta issi wothoy bayindda yeedetontta mala eqqettin ta yooy Qeessare sinthth shiiqidi beetto gaanas tas gidde giddies. Gido attin tani ta dereta mootiza gasoy tas deena.
ACT 28:20 Ta qass ha7i intena xeeygisiday intena beeyanasine haanno intes yootanaskko. Hayssa sanssalatan ta qachchetiday isiraele naytas immettida uhaaththaayssa gasoonkko.
ACT 28:21 Isttikka izas hizzgi zaarida “Ne gish Yuhuda derepe xaahaaththaettida debidabey nuna gakkibeyina. Ha yida asatape oonikka ne gish iita hasa7iday baawa.
ACT 28:22 Hayssa ne kaalliza ammanoza gish awankka asay iitta hasa7izaysa nu erros. Hessa gish ne qoohaaththaay azakkone nu siyana koyos” gida.
ACT 28:23 Bare izas immidi hara gallas kushe kumidi izi diza keeth yida. Izikka maladoppe omarss gakkanaas Xoossa kawootetha gish markkatethan ba qohaaththaa isttas qonccisides. Musse wogappene nabeta maaxxahaaththaatape xaqqasi xaqqasi Yesussa gish isttas gellththi yootides.
ACT 28:24 Isttafe issi issi asati izi yootida qaala ammanida; Bagayti qass ammanibeytena.
ACT 28:25 Isttikka ba garssan issay issara qohaaththaan gaggontta shakketida; Phawulossay wurssethan yootishe hizzgides “xiillo ayanay nabe isyyasa baggara kasse inte aawatas yootidayssi tumakko.
ACT 28:26 Izi yootida qaalay hizzges <Hayssa deerakko baada inte sissi siyana shin yushshi qoppekista, ayfera beeyana shin wozinan woththekista gaada yoota.
ACT 28:27 Gasooykka he asata wozinay mumides, istta hayththeykka tuullides; istta ayfey qoqides. Hessaththo hanonttakko istti ba ayfera beeydi ba heyththera siyidi ba wozinan yushshi qoppidi taakko ha simmanane takka istta paththanashin.>
ACT 28:28 Histtikko Xoosi asi ashshiza kittay ayhuda gidoontta deretaskka kitteetdayssa inte errit; Isttikka erro giidi ekkettes.”
ACT 28:29 Phawulossay hessa yootidappe guye Ayhuda asati ba garssan daroo pallametishe kezi bida.
ACT 28:30 Phawulossay kiratida keeththan nam77u laythth kumethth de7ides; Beekko yiza asa wursii mokki ekkides.
ACT 28:31 Xoossa kawooteth sabbakkon Goda Yesuss Kiristtossa gish oonikka iza diggontta xalatethara asa taamarisides.
ROM 1:1 Yesus Kiristoosa ayllene haware gidanasi xeygettida mishiracho qaala yootanaas kiitettida taape Phawulossape kiitettida kiita.
ROM 1:2 He mishshiracho qaala gishshi kase nabeta baggara geesha maxaafatan ufaysi immetides.
ROM 1:3 Mishshiracho qaalaykka ba naza gishshi izi asho baggara Dawite zereththafe gididayssa yootiza gishshikko.
ROM 1:4 Hessaththoka nu Goda Yesusi kirstoosay ba Geeshatetha ayanan hayqope denddidaysi izi Xoossa na gididayssi gita wolqan qonccides.
ROM 1:5 Kirirstoosa sunththa gishshi ammanontta derey ammanana malane azazistana mala iza baggara nuni hawaratethas gathiza kiyateth ekkidos.
ROM 1:6 Inteka Yesus Kirisitoosayta gidana mala xeygetidaytara deista.
ROM 1:7 Xoossan dosetidaytanne geeshata gidanaas xeygetida Orome biittan diza intes wurisos nu Aawa Xoossafene nu Goda Yesus kirstoosape kiyatethine sarotethi intes gido.
ROM 1:8 Inte ammanoy alame kumethan siyettida gishshine inte gishshi ta Godaa Xoossa, Yesus Kiristoosa baggara galatays.
ROM 1:9 Ta inte gishshi wuriso wode ay mala qopizakone Xoossa na mishshiracho sabakoni ta izas oothiza ta Xoossi taasi marika.
ROM 1:10 Tani ta woosan wuriso wode intena qopoysa. Ha7i qasse wurisethan Xoossa shene gidiko ta inteko baana mala Xoossi taas oge doyana mala woossays.
ROM 1:11 Inte minnana mala maadiza ayana imotethi ta intes shakanassine intena ayfera beyanas laamotays.
ROM 1:12 Heskka intenine tan issay issa amnanon ministanaskko.
ROM 1:13 Ta ishato harason ammanontayta matan taas hanida mala inte matanika taas ooso ayfey beettana mala daro wode qopadisi shin haanno gakanaas ta digistada dizaysa inte erana mala koyays.
ROM 1:14 Tamaridaytas gidin tamarontayskka, eratasine eeyatas wurisos ta bolla tamarssana accoy dees.
ROM 1:15 Intes Oromen dizaysatasika ta mishshiracho qaala yootanas ta amotizay hessaskko.
ROM 1:16 Aammanizayti wuri attana mala Xoossa woliqa gidida gishshi ta mishshiracho qaalan yeelattike; Hesika koyro ayhudatas kallidi hanko dere asaskko.
ROM 1:17 “Xilloy Xoossa ammanon deyees” geetetidi kase xaafetida mala Xoossa xiilloteth mishshiracho qaalan qonccina; He xiillotethay koyrope wurisetha gakanaas ammanon hanana.
ROM 1:18 Tuma, ba iittatethaninne makali7an tucii oykizayta iittatetha bollan istta makall7atetha wuriso bolla Xoossa hanqoy sallope qoncana.
ROM 1:19 Istti eranas bessizazi Xooss wursi isttas qoncisida gishshi Istti Xoossu eranaas qoncceko.
ROM 1:20 Alamey medhettosope haa simmini asa ayfen beetti erontta Xoossa hanotethi hesika izas diza medhina woliqayne Xoossatethay izi medhida medhetethan qonicen bettees. Hessa gishshi asay shiishana gaasoy deena.
ROM 1:21 Istti Xoossu erikoka iza, iza Xoossatetha mala bonchibeytenane galatibeyttena. Gido attin istta qofay mela go7ay baynidazi gididesine yuushi qopontta mala istta wozinay dhumides.
ROM 1:22 Istti bena era gizayta gidikkoka eeyata gidida.
ROM 1:23 Medhina Xoossa boncho hayqqiza asanine kafotan, mehistanine biitta bolla goochettiza medhetethatan milatissidi laammida.
ROM 1:24 Hessa gishshi Xoossi istta ba garssan issay issara berkka ba asatethan tuna ootho oothana mala geeshshatethi bayndda laymmatethas aathi immides.
ROM 1:25 Istti Xoossa tumateth wordon laammida; medhdhida Xoossa olla medhdhetethas goynnidanne isttas oothida. Medhdhida Xoossi izi medhdhinas galatettidayssa; amin77i.
ROM 1:26 Hessa geedon Xoossi istta yelachiza amotethas aathi immides. Istti macasati benara zin7anas besontaytara zin7ana mala bena aathi immida.
ROM 1:27 Hessaththoka attuma asay bees bessiza macasatara zin7anaas bessishin addey addera zin7anaas amon xuugetidi macasatara zin7iza mala addery addera zin7idi pala miishshi oothida. Heytanti berka ba oothida iitta oothozas bessiza qixaate ba bolla ehida.
ROM 1:28 Qasseka istti ba qofara Xoossu eroy nuna maaddena gida gishshi istti oothanaas besonttayssa oothana mala Xoossi istta go7ontta qofas aathi immides.
ROM 1:29 Wuriso baggara makali7ane iittateth, yiiqene iitta oothon xalala kumida; qanatetethan, shemmipo wodhon, ooshshan, balethoninne genen kumidayta qasseka zigirizayta gidida.
ROM 1:30 Asa sunthu moorizayta, Xoossu ixxizayta, ase cayzata, otoronchatanne ceeqettizayta gidida, wuriso wode iitta oothanas oge koyzayta, bena yelidaytas azazetontayta,
ROM 1:31 Yuushshi qopontayata, gida qaala zaari lallizayata, asas michchetontayta menxxe iittata.
ROM 1:32 Hessa oothizayti wurikka hayqqanaas besses giza Xoossa woga istti erishe heytantta bees ootho xalala gidontta hessathoka oothizaytakka minithetheetes.
ROM 2:1 Hessa gishshi neno hara bolla piridizayso neni ta hanni geedon oothadisi gaada gaasoy neesi deena. Ne hara ura bolla piiridizayssan nerika nees kunane ekkaasa. Gaasoykka hara ura bolla ne piridizaysa neka zaarada iza oothiza gishaskko.
ROM 2:2 Hayta malata oothiza asata bolla Xoossa piriday liike gididayssa nu erossi
ROM 2:3 Hesa gishshi ne asa bolla piridashe he ne piiridizasa zaara oothizade gidiko ne Xoossa piiridafe kessa eka attana nees millatizee?
ROM 2:4 woykko Xoossa kiiyatethi nena marotethako kallithizaysa shaaka erontta dashe iza gita kiiyatethane iza danida7a duretetha ne liiqazii?
ROM 2:5 Gido attin neni ne wozina mumetethanine marotethi koyontta ne wozina geedon tuma Xoossa piiriday qoniciza wode Xoossa hanqo gallasa ne daro hanqqo shiishshasa.
ROM 2:6 Xoossi isi isi uras iza ootho mala immana.
ROM 2:7 Lo7o ootho aggontta oothidi boncho sabane medhina dusi koyzaytas miidhina deyo immana.
ROM 2:8 Gido attin berika bena dosizaytasine tuma agagidi iitta kallizayta bolla piiridayne hanqoy gakana.
ROM 2:9 Itita oothiza ay asa bolla koyro Ayhude asa bolla kaallid hanko hara dere asa bolla wayeyne metoy gakana.
ROM 2:10 Gidikkoka lo7o oothizades oonasika Ayhuda asas gidin hankko dere asas sabay, sarotethinne bonchoy gidana.
ROM 2:11 Xoossi oonaka shaakk maaddena.
ROM 2:12 Kase wogay eqontta wode nagara oothida asay wurikka wogay bayinida dhayana. Wogay eqi simmini nagara oothidayti wogan oyketidi piiridistana.
ROM 2:13 Aysi gikko Xoossa achan xiillo geetettizayti eqida wogaas azazetizaytape attin woga sisi siyzayta gidetena.
ROM 2:14 Wogay baynida dere asati wogay yootizaysa coo mela hanotethafe eridi oothishin isttas wogay baynida agikokka isttas medhetetha wogay diza gishshi istti ba oothanayssa ereetes.
ROM 2:15 Istta wozinay isttas marikatiza gishine istta qofay istta mootiza gishshi qasseka istta maaddiza gishshi wogay yootizay istta wozinan xaafetidayssa ereetes.
ROM 2:16 Hesikka ta mishshiracho qaalan tamarssiza mala Xoossi asa wizinan qotetidayssa Kirisitoosa baggara piiridiza gallasan qoniccana.
ROM 2:17 Ne nena Ayhuda asi gikko wogan ammanetasane neesi Xoossara diza issipetethan ceeqetaasa.
ROM 2:18 Woga kaalliza gishshi Xoossa shene erada kumethi gidizazi shaakka erida gidiko
ROM 2:19 Ne qoqista kallethizade dhuman dizaytas poo7o gididaysa ne amanetidade gidiko
ROM 2:20 Wogape ne demida eratethaninne tumatethan hankko eronitayta zorizade, guutha nayitta tamarisizade gidikko
ROM 2:21 Histiko neni harata tamariso agada ne hu7es aazas tamarikii? Ne hara ura kaysottopa ga sabakashe neesi kaysotazii?
ROM 2:22 Ne hara asay laymatontta mala yootashe nees laymaytazii? Nees Eeqa ixxasashin Xoossa keeththa miisha bonqqazii?
ROM 2:23 Neesi wogan ceeqetasa shin woga ne baggara oothontta aggada Xoossa kawushizii?
ROM 2:24 Hesikka “Inte geedon Xoossa sunthi hanko dere asa achan cayetesi” geetetti xaafetida mala hanides.
ROM 2:25 Ne woga naaga pollizade gidiko qaxaras goo7ay dees. Ne wogaa oothonttade gidiko qasse ne qaxaray coo melakko.
ROM 2:26 Qaxaretontta dishe wogaa gizaysa polliko qaxaretidadera gina qodetenee?
ROM 2:27 Nees xaafeti wogayne qaxaray nees diikko diza woga ne nagonttade gidikko hanko qaxaretontta wogas azazetiday ne bolla piridana.
ROM 2:28 Issade coo mela sunthas asa ayfen ta Ayhuda asi gidana gikko izi Ayhuda asi gidena. Tumape qaxeretethi coo karera asho ayfeni bettiza qaxxara gidena.
ROM 2:29 Gidikkokka issi uray Ayuda asa gidanaas danda7izay izas gaatha baggara Ayude asa gidishinkko. Qaxarayka qaxara gidizay xaafetida wogaa xalala gidontta ayanan wozinape gidida qaxxara gidikokka hessa mala assi galata asape gidontta Xoossafe demmees.
ROM 3:1 Histinko Ayude asa gidethasi aaza go7ay dizee? Qaxaray ay go7izee?
ROM 3:2 Awaraka gidin go7ay daro. Harape koyro Xoossa qaalay hadara Ayudatasi immetides.
ROM 3:3 Isttafe issi issi uras ammanoy baynida aggiko Xoossa ammanotethi diigizee?
ROM 3:4 Mulekka diggena! Asi wurikka woridancha “Neni ne qaalape denidayssan tumanicha; Piridanika xonizade gidaasa” hessaththo geeteti xaafettida mala Xoossi qasse tumanicha.
ROM 3:5 Nu makali7a oothoy Xoossa xiillotethi qonccen besiizayssa gidikko hisitini nu ay ganee? Coo asa woga mala palamistanas Xoossi ba hanqqo nu bolla ehizaysi nuusu bessena ganeyee? Hesaka ta giizay asatho qofankko.
ROM 3:6 Tumape hessaththo hanena. Hesatho haniza gidiko Xoossi alame bolla wostti piiridanidee?
ROM 3:7 Ta woridotethi Xoossa tumatethi qonccisizayssan iza bonicho gede gujiizassa gidikko hisitin ha7i gakanas wostti ta bolla nagarancha mala piiridetize?” giidi pallamistana assi daana danda7ees.
ROM 3:8 Hessa gussi “Lo7oy yaana mala ane iitta oothosu” geetesi gidi issi issi asati nu bolla woresizayssa malakko. Hayta asata bolla gakkiza piiriday tumu piiridako.
ROM 3:9 Histinni nu aazi ginoo? Nuni isttafe adhizonii? Mulekka adhoko. Ayhudata gidikkoka hanikko dere asa gidikokka wurikka nagarape garisa baggara diza gish ta wursikka kassistada isttas yootadis.
ROM 3:10 “Xiilloy oonikka deena issi uraykka deena.
ROM 3:11 Yuushi qopiizadey bawa; Xoossu koyzay issadeyka bawa.
ROM 3:12 Wurikka balletidane issi bolla go7onttayta gidida. Loo7o oothizay oonikka bawa; issadeykka deena”
ROM 3:13 Istta duunay doya diza duufo mala istta duunay wuriso wode hasa7ees. Istta meterishay shoosha marzzera dees.”
ROM 3:14 “Istta duunan qanigethin cammo miish kumides.”
ROM 3:15 “Istta tooy suuthu gussanasi eesotees.
ROM 3:16 Istta ogen dhayosoyne mulera dipp gi dhayoy dees.
ROM 3:17 Istti Sarotetha oge eri eretena
ROM 3:18 Istta ayfesonni Xoossas baboy bawa” geeteti xaafettida malakko.
ROM 3:19 Hessa gishshi duunay wurikka goridistana mala derey kumetha Xoossas mallithe immana mala wogay gizay wurikka wogape garsara dizaytas gididaysa nu eroosu.
ROM 3:20 Hessa gishshi wogay nagaray aazakone erisees attiin wogaa nagon oonikka iza achani xiillo geetistanas danida7ena.
ROM 3:21 Ha7i qasse wogaa kasse nabeti izas marikatidaysi wogape karera gidida Xoossa xiilloteth qonicides.
ROM 3:22 Hessi Xoossa xiillotethi Yesus Kirisitoosa amanon dummatethi bayndda bettiza xiillotethikko.
ROM 3:23 Gaasoykka asi wurikka nagara oothides. Xoossa bonichoykka asa naas paciides.
ROM 3:24 Asay Yesus Kirisitoosay, asa na gishshi oothida kiyatethafe denididayssan coo mela xiillides.
ROM 3:25 Iza suuthan gidida ammanon naagarape maristana yarsho histtid Xoossi Yesusa shishides. Izi hessa oothiday kassetidi polletida nagara qaxayonta danida7a adhida ba xiillotethi bessaanaskko.
ROM 3:26 Izi hessa ha wodezan oothiday ba xiillotetha heskka ba baggara xiillo gidi Yesus Kirisitoosan ammanizade xiilisizaysa bessanaskko.
ROM 3:27 Histinni nuni izan ceeqettiza miishshi aazi dizee? aykko miishshankka ceeqetokko. Nu ceeqistana gaasoy aazee? woga naagiza gishshee? gidenna ammanonkko.
ROM 3:28 Ay asikka ammanon attin woga naagon atonttaysa nu geeshshi yoottos.
ROM 3:29 Xoossi Ayhudata Xoossu xalalaa? Haniko dere asaskka Xoossu gidenee? Ee hanko dere asaskka izi Xoossa.
ROM 3:30 Qaxaretidayssa ammanon qasse qaxaretonitaysakka he ammanonikka xiillisizayka izi isi Xoossa xalalakko.
ROM 3:31 Histin hessi hessa gidikko ammano geedon woga go7ay bayndazi oothinoo? Muleka hessaththo hanena. woga nu minthana attin.
ROM 4:1 Hessa gish kasse nu Abiramey hayssafe ay go7a demide ginoo?
ROM 4:2 Abiramey ba oothon xiilidako izi ceeqistanayssi deesiko shin; izi Xoossa siinithan ceeqetenas danida7ena.
ROM 4:3 Geeshsha Maxaafay “Abiramey Xoossu ammanidesine iza ammanoy izas xiillotethan qoodetides” gees.
ROM 4:4 Issi uray ootho oothiko izi ekiza miishay izas coo kiyatethi immetizayssa gidontta izades ootho waga gides.
ROM 4:5 Gido attin ootho oothontta nagarancha ura xiillo kessiza Xoossan ammanizaades iza ammanoy izas xiillotethen taybetteyes.
ROM 4:6 Dawiteykka xiillotethi izas qoodettizay loo7o oothon gidontta asa gishshi hiziges,
ROM 4:7 Isttas istta bolla oothoy atto geetetidaytine istta nagaray maretidayt anijjetidayta.
ROM 4:8 Iza nagara Goday muleka qoodontadey izi anijjtidade”
ROM 4:9 Ha anijjozi qaxarretidaytas xalalayee? woykko qaxaretontaytasaraa? kase koyro nu Aawa Abirame ammanoy izas xiillotethan paydetides gidos.
ROM 4:10 Histin wani izas hessaththo paydetide? Izi qaxaretidape guye? woykko qaxaristanape kassee? Izas xiillotethan paydetiday izi qaxaristanape sinithana.
ROM 4:11 Izi kasse qaxaristanape kasse demmida xiillotethay qaxarisi malata gidida heskka xiillotethas matame ekides. Hessa gish qaxaretontta ammanizaytas xiillotethi paydistana mala wurisotasi izi Aawa.
ROM 4:12 Izi qaxaretidaytaskka Aawa qaxaretidaytas xalala gidontta nu Aawa Abiramey kasse qaxaristanape sinithe izas diza ammano geedo kallizaytas wurisossa.
ROM 4:13 Izi alame latizade gidana mala Abirimeynne iza zereththati ufaysa qaala ekiday waga baggara gidontta ammanon gidida xiillotethankko.
ROM 4:14 Woga nagizayti lattizayta gidiko ammanos go7ay deenna; ufaysikka coo mela gidana shin.
ROM 4:15 Wogay hanqqo kalethes. wogay baynidason wogappe adhethi deenna.
ROM 4:16 Hessa gishshi ufaysi ammanon yides. Hessikka iza ufaysay iza kiiyatethan gidanadanine Abirame zerethasi wurisosi ammanetizayssa gidana mala hanides. Hesikka wogan izayta gididaytas xalala gidontta ammanon Abirame nayta gididaytas wurisotaskko. Izikka nuus wurisoskka Aawako.
ROM 4:17 Hesikka “Ta nena daro dere Aawa oothidis” geeteti xaafetida mala hanides. Izikka hayqidaytas deyo immizaden baynidayssa qasse diza mala oothizaden ammanida Xoossa sinithan izi nuusu Aawakko.
ROM 4:18 Kasse izas “Ne zerethi hessaththo hanana” geetetida mala ayko ufaysikka baynida dishin Abiramey Xoossi hanana gidaysa ammanidi daro dere Aawa gidides.
ROM 4:19 Abiramesi yelettini xeetu layith gidi kichin Abiramey ba asatethay hayqetha mala gididaysanne sarasi yello wodey aadhi bidaysa erisheka ammanon lepibeyna.
ROM 4:20 Gede gujjid ammanon minidi Xoossas boncho immides attin Xoossi gida qaala sidhibeyna.
ROM 4:21 Xoossi izas immida ufaysay polistanaysa kumetha wozinape ammanides.
ROM 4:22 Hessa gishshi izasi xiillotethan qodetides.
ROM 4:23 “Izas xiillotethan paydetides” giza qaala xaafettiday izas xalala gidena.
ROM 4:24 Gido attin Xoossi nu xiillotetha iza baggara paydiza nu Goda Yesusa hayqope denithidaysan ammaniza nusarakko.
ROM 4:25 Izi nu nagara gishshi hayqanasi aadhi immetides. Izi nuna xiillota hisitina hayqope denidides.
ROM 5:1 Histiko nuni xiillida gishshi nu Goda Yesus Kirisitoosa baggara nuusu Xoossara sarotethi dees.
ROM 5:2 Hayssa ha ammanozan miinid diza kiyatethan nuni geliday iza baggara gidida gishshi ufayssan Xoossa boncho gishetti ekizayta gidida gishshi nu ufa7etosu.
ROM 5:3 Hayssan xalala gidontta nuna gakiza waayenkka ufa7eetoos. Gaasoyka waayey danda7an gathizaysa nu erosu.
ROM 5:4 Danida7ay paaccen minoteth immes; paaccen minoteth ufaysi immees.
ROM 5:5 He ufaysay nuna qasse nuna yellachena. Xoossi nuusu immida xiillo ayanan ba siqqo nu wozinan gusiida gishshi he ufayssay nuna yellan gathena.
ROM 5:6 Nu daburanchata gidi dishin Xoossa wodey gakida mala Kirisitoosay nu nagara gishshi hayqides.
ROM 5:7 Xiillo asa gishshi hayqana asi bistanays daro metees. Loo7o asa gishshi hayqanas xalana asi oonee erizay bettana dandda7ees.
ROM 5:8 Gido attin nu buro nagaranicha gidi uttidishin Kiristoosay nu gishshi hayqides. Hesikka Xoossi nuna siqiza ba siiqo heysan besses.
ROM 5:9 Nuni iza suuthan geyidayta gidikko harappeka iza baggara Xoossa hanqqofe attana.
ROM 5:10 Nu Xoossas morketa gidi dishe iza naaza hayqon izara giigidayta gidikko nu izara giigdappe guye iza shemppo baggara nuni keehi attana.
ROM 5:11 Hessa xalala gidenna; qassekka nuni ha7i izara giiga demmida nu Goda Yesusi kiristoosa baggara Xoossankka ufays oothos.
ROM 5:12 Hessa gishshi nagaray issade geedon duge ha alameza yida mala hayqoykka nagara geedon yides. Hayqoykka hessa baggara asa wurisoko yides. hessas gaasoy asi wurikka iza baggara nagara oothida gishshikko.
ROM 5:13 Wogay immettanape kase nagaray biitta bolla deesishin wogay baynddason nagaray nagara gidena.
ROM 5:14 Shin Addameppe ha simmin Muse wode gakkanaas diza woden Addame mala woga menththid nagara oothontayta bollaka hayqoy kawotides. Addamey buro yaana kiristoosas lemisokko.
ROM 5:15 Gidikokka iza kiyatetha immotay asa qoho mala gidena. Issadey mooridayssan daro asay hayqqikokka Xoossa kiyatethanine issi asi Yesusi kiristoosa kiyatethan yida immotay darotas keehi dari immetides.
ROM 5:16 Qasseka Xoossa immotay issade baggara yida nagarappe beettida ayife mala gidenna. Gaasoykka iza piriday issade nagara kaallid pirida ekki yides. Iza immotay qase daro qoho geedon xiilloteth ehides. Hayqoy hayssade baggara kawotidayssa gidikko daro tiripa gidida Xoossa kiyatethinne xiillotetha immota ekkidayti issade baggara hessika Yesusi kiristoosa baggara xoonidi deyon daana.
ROM 5:18 Hisitko issade qoho geedon piriday asa wuriso bolla gakkida mala hessathokka issade xiillotetha oothon asi wurisos deyo immiza xiillotethi beettides.
ROM 5:19 Issadey azazetontta ixxida gishshi daro asay nagarancha gidida mala issade azazetethan qase daroti xiillana.
ROM 5:20 Wogay yiin mooroy darides. Gido attin nagaray daroyssafe bollara Xoossa kiyatethi keehi darides.
ROM 5:21 Hesska handay nagaray hayqo bolla kawotidayssa mala Yesus kiristoosa baggara qasse medhina deyoy bettana mala iza kiyatethan kawotanaskko.
ROM 6:1 Histin nu ay giinoo? Xoossa kiyatethi darana mala nagara gujji othinoo?
ROM 6:2 Mulekka gidenna. Nuni nagaras hayqidosu. Histin hayssafe guye nu waani nagaran daanee?
ROM 6:3 Nuni Yesusi Kiristoosara issino gidana mala xamaqetidayti iza hayqon nu issife gidanas xamaqetidayssa hayssa inte ereketii?
ROM 6:4 Hessa gishshi Kiristoosay ba Aawa bonchon hayqoppe denddida mala nunikka hessaththo ooratha deyon daanas xinqqaten hayqqidi izara moogetidosd.
ROM 6:5 Nuni hessa mala hayqon izara isife gidikko qasse denithanka izara isife gidosu.
ROM 6:6 Hayssafe guye nu nagarasi aylle gidontta mala nagara asatethay kiichana mala kase nu ceea asatethay izara isife kaqetidayssa nu erosu.
ROM 6:7 Gaasoykka hayqida asi nagarape shemipidis.
ROM 6:8 Nuni Kiristoosara hayqidayti gidikko nu izara isife danaysa ammanosu.
ROM 6:9 Kiristoosay hayqope denidida gishshi nam7antho izi hayqonitaysanne iza bolla hayqossa wolqay bayndayssa nu erosu.
ROM 6:10 Izi hayqida wode isito wursi nagara gishshi hayqides. Gida attin Xoossas paaxa dusu dees.
ROM 6:11 Hessaththoka inte nagaras hayqidi Xoossas Yesus Kiristoosa baggara paxxa dizaysa erite.
ROM 6:12 Hessa gishshi iitta oothana koyza iitta asho qofa koydi hayqida inte asatetha bolla nagaray kawotana mala oothofite.
ROM 6:13 Inte asatetha iitta ootho oothiza mishi oothi nagaras harisopite. Hessa mala oothanape hayqope gede deyon pinida asata mala intena Xoossa harisite. Inte asatetha xiillotetha miishsha mala Xoossas harisite.
ROM 6:14 Inte Xoossa kiiyatetha garisan deista attiin woga garisan dontta gishshi intena nagaray haarena.
ROM 6:15 Histin aazi oothinoo? wogaa garisan gidontta nuni Xoossa kiyatetha garisan diza gishshi nagara oothonoo? mule oothanaas bessena.
ROM 6:16 Inte intena aylle mala shiishshiza wode inte azazetizades aylle gididayssa ereista. Hessaththoka gede hayqokko efiza nagaras woykko xiilotethako gathiza azazetethas inte aylle gididayssa ereketii?
ROM 6:17 Inte kasse nagaras ayllista gidikko intes imettida timiritezas inte wozanappe azazetida gishshi Xoossi galateto.
ROM 6:18 Inte nagarape wozetidi xiillotethas aylle gididista.
ROM 6:19 Hayssa ta asa qaalan intes qonccen yootizay inte Yeletethan daburanicha gidida gishshikko. Inte kase wode inte asatetha aylletethasine kassepe adhi iittana mala oothi immista shin ha7i qasse gede geeshatethako efiza xiillotethes aylle hisiti haarisite.
ROM 6:20 Inte kasse nagarasi aylletidi diza wode inte xiillotethafe mella atidista shin.
ROM 6:21 Ha7i qasse inte yelatiza miishshatape he wode ay go7a demmidetii? Hessa he hanoza go7ay hayqoko.
ROM 6:22 Ha7i qasse inte nagarape wozetidi Xoossa ayllista gididista. Hessikka Intena gede geeshatethako kallethes. wurisethaykka medhina deyoko.
ROM 6:23 Nagara waagay hayqokko. Xoossa immotay gidiko Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara medhiina deyoko.
ROM 7:1 Ta ishato tani wogaa eriza asatas yootays. Wogaa shemipora paxxa diza asa xalala harizayssa inte ereketii?
ROM 7:2 Issi macashi azina geliko ba azinara wogan iza qachetizay azinay paxxa diza wode gakanaskko. Azinay hayqiko iza machcho gidiza wogape anjjistaysu.
ROM 7:3 Gido attin azinay paxxa dishin iza hara azina gelliko laymatasusu geetistaysu. Azinay hayqiko qase hara ura iza gelliko kase azina wogape anjjistadus attin layma getetuku.
ROM 7:4 Hessa gishshi ta ishato inteka Yesus Kiristoosa asho baggara wogas hayqidista. Inte hayqope denidida kiristoosa bagga gidin nuni Xoossas ayfe ayfanaskko.
ROM 7:5 Nagarancha medhetetha shenen nu diza wode hayqo ayfe nu ayfana mala wogay denththethida nagara amoy nu bolla oothides.
ROM 7:6 Ha7i gidiko kasse nuna waaxi qachida hayqida gishshi wogape wozetidosu. Hesikka kase cega wogan xaafetidayssan gidontta dishe ooratha ayana ogen nuni oothanaskko.
ROM 7:7 Histin nu ay ginoo? Be hu7es wogay naragaa? muleka gidena. wogaa bagara gidonttako nagaray azakone nu erokoko shin. wogay “amotofa” gonttako amoy azakone tumupe ta erikke.
ROM 7:8 Nagaray qasse wogape kezida azazoy bessida ogen go7ettidi ta gidon dumma dumma iitta amo denithethides. wogay yanappe kasse nagaray hayqithiko.
ROM 7:9 wogay baynida kase tani paxxa dayisse shin wogay yiini qase nagaray paxxa gidides. ta gidikko hayqadis.
ROM 7:10 He asi ashana qofetida azazoyka hayqo ekii yidaysa eradis.
ROM 7:11 Nagaray woga baggara bettida gaason go7ettidi tana balethidesine azazon wodhides.
ROM 7:12 Hessa gishshi wogay ba baggara geeshshikko. azazoyka geesh, xiilone loo7okko.
ROM 7:13 Gido attin loo7osu hanidaysi taas hayqos gididee? Mulekka gidena. Gido attin nagaray ba nagaratethan eretana mala loo7o gidida hano bagara ta bolla hayqo ehides. Hesikka nagaray azazo baggara kassepe aathi nagara darisides.
ROM 7:14 Wogay ayana yo gididaysa nu erosu. Ta qasse nagaras aylle mala bayzetida asikko.
ROM 7:15 Tani ta oothizayssa erike. Ta oothana koyzayssa ootha erike shin ta ixxiza miishsh oothays.
ROM 7:16 Ta oothana koyontta miish oothiza gidikko wogay loo7o gididaysa ta marikatays.
ROM 7:17 Hessa oothizay tana gidontta ta gaathan diza nagaray oothees.
ROM 7:18 Tanan hesikka nagarancha gidida ta madhetetha gidon ayko loo7o miishshi baynidayssa ta erays. Loo7o oothanasi taas amotethi dees shin polla ootha erikke.
ROM 7:19 Ta oothizay oothana gaada koyza loo7o ootho giden. Gido attin ta oothana koyontta iitta ootho oothays.
ROM 7:20 Tani oothanas koyonttayssa oothiza gidiko hessa oothizay tana gidontta ta gidon diza nagarakko.
ROM 7:21 Hessa gishshi haysi wogay oothon dizaysi taas gellides. Hessikka tani loo7o oothana koyaysishin tani iitta oothays.
ROM 7:22 Tani ta gaathara Xoossa wogan ufa7istays.
ROM 7:23 Gido attin ta asatetha gidon oothiza nagara wogay tana qachi oykidi ta qofa wogara oletiza hara wogay ta asatetha gidon oothishin beyays.
ROM 7:24 Ta aymala laafa asee! Hayssa hayqosi imettida asatethafe tana ashanay oonee?
ROM 7:25 Nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara galatay Xoossas gido. Histinkko tani ta baggara ta qofan Xoossa wogasi aylle gidashe tani Ta medhetetha wogan nagara wogas aylleko.
ROM 8:1 Hessa gishshi Yesus Kiristoosa ammanizayta bolla piriday deena.
ROM 8:2 Gaasoykka deyo ayana wogay Yesus Kiristoosa baggara nagarape istta geeshida gishikko.
ROM 8:3 Nagarancha ashoppe dendidayssan wogay polanaas danida7ontaysa Xoossi ba naaza nagarancha asa lemusson nagaras yarishistana mala yedidi pollides. Hsitidi nagara iza ashon piridides.
ROM 8:4 Hessikka nuni ashon gidontta ayanan simeretiza nupe wogay koyza xiillotetha pollanaskko.
ROM 8:5 Asho shene mala daana koyza asata wozinay ashoy koyza mishan shemipees. Ayana shene mala dizayti qasse ba wizinaa, ayanay koyza miishsh bolla wothetes.
ROM 8:6 Ashos xalala qofay hayqo gidishin ayana yoosi qofay gidiko deyone sarotethikko.
ROM 8:7 Nagaras haretiza wozinay Xoossara ooshshakko. Gaasoykka izi Xoossa wogasi haretennane haristanas danida7ena.
ROM 8:8 Asho shene mala diza asatikka Xoossu ufaysanasi danida7etena.
ROM 8:9 Inte qasse Xoossa ayanay intenan diza gidiko ashon gidontta ayanan deista. Kiristoosa ayanay iza bolla deennadey he uray Kiristoosas gidena.
ROM 8:10 Kiristoosay inte gidon dikko qasse inte asatethay naagara geedon hayqethi gidikokka inte ayanay qase xiillotetha gaason deyon dees.
ROM 8:11 Yesusa hayqope dinthida iza ayanay inte bolla diza gidiko Kiristoosa hayqope denthidaysa inte gidon diza iza ayanay hayqanas diza inte asatethas deyo immana.
ROM 8:12 Hessa gishshi ta ishato! hesikka wolliqara hanana shin nu asho shene mala daanas ashosi gidokko.
ROM 8:13 Asho shene mala deyzayssa gidiko inte hayqanane asho ootho iittaza inte ayanan wodhi gidiko inte deyon daana.
ROM 8:14 Xoossa ayanan kallizadenti heytantti istti Xoossa naytakko.
ROM 8:15 Inte ekida ayanay zaaridi intena ayletethan hariiza ayana gidontta “nu Aawa abbo” gi xeygisiza naatetha ayana ekidista.
ROM 8:16 Nuni Xoossa nayta gididaysa he ayanay ba baggara nu ayanara issife nuusu marikatees.
ROM 8:17 Nuni iza nayti gidikko nu iza latizaytako. Nu iza bonchoza latizayta gidana mala adafeka izara iza metoza gishetezayta gidikko nu Xoossu latizadeko; Kirisitossara issife latizayitakko.
ROM 8:18 Ha7i nu ekiza waayey buro nuusu sinithan giigi uttida bonchozara gathi xellishin aykokka gidena gays.
ROM 8:19 Medhetethay wurikka Xoossa nayti qonccanaysa lamotethan naagon dees.
ROM 8:20 Medhetethi wurikka mela hada gidana mala piridettides. Hesikka ba doron gidontta sinithafes haristana mala izi ba shene mala harisida gishaskko.
ROM 8:21 Hesikka medhetethi wurikka dhayssa aylletethafe wozitidi Xoossa naytasi gidida gede bonichitida shene mala dizaso gakanaskko.
ROM 8:22 Ha7i gakanas medhetethi wurikka mixxa mala waayen shenotishe dizaysa nu erosu.
ROM 8:23 Iza xalala gidontta koyro ayana ayfe demmida nunikka nu asatethay attana nu iza na gidanaysaka lamotishene wozinara mixxatishe dosu.
ROM 8:24 Hayssa ha ufaysan xalala attidosu. Ufaysi qasse ayfen betiza miishsh gidiko burope naagiza miishsh gidena; Ha7i ba ayfen beyza miishshi buropes nagiizadey oonee?
ROM 8:25 Gido attin nuni buro nu ayfen beyontta miish ufaysan naagiza gidikko salistay baynida naagosu.
ROM 8:26 Hesathokka qasse nu daburishin ayanay nuna maades. Wossa nu wositi wossanakone nu erontta gishshi ayanay nuni qaalan qonccisanas danida7etontta qaalara nusu wosses.
ROM 8:27 Nu wozina paacci eriza ayanay izi ayana qofa eres. Gaasoykka ayanay Xoossa shene mala ammaniza asasi nuusu wosses.
ROM 8:28 Xoossi bena dosizaytasine iza shene mala xeeygetidaytasi wurisos oothiza miishshi wursikka lo7os oothizaysa nu erosu.
ROM 8:29 Xoossi kasseepe ba erizazayta istti iza naaza milatana mala kasseka doori wothides. hesikka daro ba ishata gidofe izi bayra gidanasa.
ROM 8:30 Kasse koyrope ba dooridayta istta xeeygides. Qassekka xeygidata xiilisides. Be xiilisidaytaka bonchides.
ROM 8:31 Histinni hessa nu ay ginoo? Xoossi nunara gidikko nunara eqistana danida7izay oonee?
ROM 8:32 Be yellos michetontta nu gishshi oothi immiday izako. Hesitin wuriso miishsh nuusu izara kiyatetha aazas immenee?
ROM 8:33 Xoossi dooridayta motiza oonee? Xillisizay Xoossa.
ROM 8:34 Hisittini piridizay oonee? Hayqidi hayqope denididi Xoossa oshachan uttida Yesus Kiristoosay nu gishshi ganates.
ROM 8:35 Nuna Kiristoosa siqope shakanay oonee? Metoye, waaye, woykko godetethee, woykko gafa, woykko kallotethee woykko qopontta gakiiza metoyee, mashaa?
ROM 8:36 Hesikka kasse “Ne gishshi nu shuketiza dorisa mala qoodettidosu. gallasi kumethi ne gish nuni hayqora baxistana” geeteti xaafetidayssa malako?
ROM 8:37 Nuna aazika shakena. Haysa wurison nuna siqidaysan xoonizaytapekka nu aadhosu.
ROM 8:38 Hessa gishshi hayqo gidin deyo gidin kiitanchata gidin woykko ha7i diza miishsh gidin buro yaana miishsha gidin woykko ay wolliqama gidin
ROM 8:39 Dhoqqa gidin woykko ziqa gidin woykko ay medheteth gidin Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara nuusi diza Xoossa siqope nuna shaakana danda7iza miishshi bayndayssa ta shaaka eradis.
ROM 9:1 Ta Yesusa sunthan tumu gays; woridotikke; ta wozinaykka xiillo ayana baggara taas marikatees.
ROM 9:2 Taas wozinape kiichontta iitta qofay michay ta wozinan dees.
ROM 9:3 Ta baggara asa gishshi ta qanigetidane Kiristoosape shakistada wora wodhidako dosays.
ROM 9:4 Isttikka Isiraa7eele naytako. Istti Xoossa na gidana mala Xoossa bonchoyne caaqo qaalay ne wogayne Xoossa keeththa woga ufaysi isttasi imetides.
ROM 9:5 Kase Aawatikka istta bagga Kiristoosa asho baggara istta zeretha zariken qoodetes. Izikka wurisofe bolla gidida medhinas galatetida Xoossa; amin7i.
ROM 9:6 Gido attin hessa guussi Xoossa qaalay attides guussu gidena. Isiraa7eelepe yelettiday wuri Isiraa7eele gidenna.
ROM 9:7 Abiramepe yelettidayti izape yelletida gishshi wurikka iza yellista gidetena shin “Ne zerethi Yisaqa bagara xeygistana” geetetida mala hanides.
ROM 9:8 Hessa guussikka Xoossa na geetetidayti istti ashon yellidayta gidetena shin Abirame nayta geetettizayti burope yellistanaytakko.
ROM 9:9 “Yiza Layth hani wode ta ha simmana; Sarayka nees attuma na yellana” geetetidi izas ufaysa qaalay imettides.
ROM 9:10 Hessa xalalaka gidena. Iribiqa nayti issade nakko. Izikka nu Aawa Yisaqakko.
ROM 9:11 Meniteti yelletidi buro iitta woykko kiya oothontta dishin Xoossa qofay miinana mala
ROM 9:12 Oothon gidontta xeeygidayssafe gidida gishshi “Bayray kaallozas haaristana” geetetidi Iribiqas yootides.
ROM 9:13 Hessikka “Ta Yaqobe dosadis; Eessa ixxadis” geeteti kasse xaafetida mala hanides.
ROM 9:14 Histin nu ha7i ay ginoo? Xoossi besontta ogera maadi erizee? Muleka maadi erena.
ROM 9:15 Xooss Muses “Ta marana koydade marana; Ta Michistana koyza urasikka michistana” gees.
ROM 9:16 Hessa gish hesikka assi koyda mala gidontta woykko asa daburan gidontta Xoossa maarida mala hanees.
ROM 9:17 Geesha maxaafey Farone “Ta woliqay ne bolla bistana malane ta sunthi biitta wurisoson yootistana mala ta nena hayssasi denithadis” gees.
ROM 9:18 Hessa gish Xooss marana koyzade maares. Iza wozina muumisana koyzade wozana muumises.
ROM 9:19 Intefe isadey “Histin hanoy heyssa mala gidiko nuna hano gakanasi aazas waayisizee? Gaasoykka iza shene digana danida7izay oonee?” gaada oychchontta agaka.
ROM 9:20 Shin Xoossas mallithe zaara immizay ne oonee? “Oothetida miishshi, zaaridi oothidayssa ne tana aazas hayssatho oothadii?” gi erizee?
ROM 9:21 Uriqqa medhizadey he uriqafe bagga bonichos bagga qasse coo hiriyso oothosi medhanas iza shene gidenee?
ROM 9:22 Xoossikka ba hanqqo besanasine ba wolliqa erisanasi koydi iza hanqqo qoniccisizayta dhayanasi giigetidayta dhayssontta agagikkochii!
ROM 9:23 Koyro bonichos gigisida iza marotetha besizaytas iza bonicho duretethay eretana mala izi oothanaskko.
ROM 9:24 Xeygidadey Ayhudata baggafe xalala gidontta hanko dereza baggafe gidida nunakka ashontta xeygides.
ROM 9:25 Hose7e maxaafan “Ta dere gidontayta tani ta dereta” ga xeygana; “dosetonttayta iistta ta dosetidayta” gada xeygana.
ROM 9:26 Qasseka “Inte ta dere dekista geeteti yootteidason henka <Isiti deyo Xoossa nayta> geteti xeygistana.”
ROM 9:27 Isayasaykka Isra7eele nayta gish hizigi yootides “Isra7eele nayta qoday abba acce mala darikokka guuthati xalala attana.
ROM 9:28 Goday ba pirida biitta bolla elle piridana.
ROM 9:29 Hessikka kase Isiyasay “Woga Goday nusu zerethi ashonitako nu sodoma katama malane gamira katama mala nukka dhayanashin” geetetidi kasse Isayasa dunani yootidaysa mala hanides.
ROM 9:30 Histin nu ay giinoo? Amanon bettida xiilloteth demanas hanko dere asay daburontta demides.
ROM 9:31 Gido attin xiillotetha wogaa kaalliza Isiraa7eele nayti demibeytena.
ROM 9:32 Hessi aazas hessaththo hanidee? Istti ammanon gidonta oothon demana kallida gishshikko. Isttikka dhuphe shuchan dhuphetida.
ROM 9:33 Hessikka “Hekko asa dhuphiza shuchu Istta kunidisiza zala xiyone bolla ta wothana, Iazn ammanizadey yelletena” geetetidi kasse geeshsha maxaafan xaafetidayssa mala hanides.
ROM 10:1 Ta ishato Isra7eele nayta gishshi ta amaone ta Xoossu wossizay istti dhayonta attanaskko.
ROM 10:2 Istti Xoossa yoosi michetizayta gididaysa ta istta gishshi marikatana danida7ays; Istta michetethi gidiiko eratethan gidena.
ROM 10:3 Xooss asi xiillisiza oge erontta aggidi ba xiillotethas oge kaallida attin Xoossa xiillotetha oge kaallibeyttena.
ROM 10:4 Amaniza asa wursi xillisanas Kiristoosay woga wuris polides.
ROM 10:5 Musey Woga baggara bettiza xiilotetha gish erisishe “Hayta wogata polli oothizadey ha wogatan daana” gizayssakko.
ROM 10:6 Ammanon bettiza xillotethi qase hiziges “Ne wozinara pud sallo oonee baanayii? gopa” hesstho gussi Kiristoosa sallope duge ha wothana gussukko.
ROM 10:7 “Woykko <Duge cimman oonee wodhanayii? goppa” hesikka Kiristoosa hayqope buro denithana guussukko.
ROM 10:8 Gido attin qaalay ay gize “Qaalay ne achan dees; ne dunanine ne wozinan dees. Nuni ammano gishshi sabakiiza qaalay hayssakko.
ROM 10:9 Neni ne dunara “Yesusay Goda” gaada marikatiko Xoossi iza hayqope denithidayssa ne wozinan ne ammanikko attana.
ROM 10:10 Neni xiillanay wozinan ammanikoko shin ne atanay ne dunara marikatikoko.
ROM 10:11 Geesha maxaafay giza mala “Izan ammanizay wurikka yellatena.”
ROM 10:12 Ayhudata gidonine hiniko dere asa gidon dumatethi dena. Issi Goday wurisosikka Godakko. Iza wossizayta gujj anjes.
ROM 10:13 “Goda sunithu xeygizayti wurikka atana” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetides.
ROM 10:14 Histin iza ammanonttayti iza wozigi xeyganee? Qasse iza gishshi siyontta dishe wossiti ammananee? Sabakey baynida dishin wossiti siyanee?
ROM 10:15 Kitetonita wositi sabakanideto? Hesikka “mishiracho qaala ekkii yizayta yuus ay mala loo7o” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetida mala hanides.
ROM 10:16 Gido attin siydayti wurikka Mishiracho qaala ekibeyttena; Isayasay “Godo nu yootidaysa ooni ammanidee?” gida mala hanides.
ROM 10:17 Hessa gishshi ammanoy bettizay yootiza qaala siyethankko. yootetiza qaalaykka Kiristoosa gishshi yootiza qaalapekko.
ROM 10:18 Gido attin asay siybeyneshaa? aada ta oychays; tumape asay siydes; Geesha maxaafan xaafettida mala “Ista qaalay biitta wurisonine alame gaxxa gakanasi siyetides.”
ROM 10:19 Ta qasseka oychays; Isra7eele nayti qaalaa eribeyteneshaa? Koyiro Musey isttas “Ta dere gidonttaytan ta istta mindasana; yuushi qopontta deretan ta istta yilochana” gides.
ROM 10:20 Isayasaykka xalatethan “Tana koyonttaytas ta bettadis; tana oychonttaytas tana qonicisadis” gides.
ROM 10:21 Isiraa7eele gishshi qase “Taas azazetontta derekone taas eeno gontta dereko kumetha gallas ta kushe miccadis” gees.
ROM 11:1 Histin Xoossi dereta yegi agidee? Gaada ta oychays; Muleka agibeyna; takka ta baggara Biniyame zarike, Abirame zereth gidida Isiraa7eele asakko.
ROM 11:2 Xoossi koyrope ba erida dereza yegibeyna. Elasay Isiraa7eele nayta bolla motoy Xoossakko wozigi shishshidakone geesha maxaafay iza gishshi ay gizakone inte eriketii?
ROM 11:3 “Godo! istti ne nabeta wodhida. nees yarishizasoka lallida. Qasse tani tarka atadis. Tanaka wodhana geetes.
ROM 11:4 Xoossi isttas hizgi zaarides “Ba7alle geeteiza Eeqas goynonttayta laapun shihi asi taas ashshadis.”
ROM 11:5 Hessa malaka ha7i ha wodezanika Xoossa kiyatethan Isiraa7eele asape dooreti attida guuthati deetes.
ROM 11:6 Histtin hessi Xoossa kiyatethan gidiko asa oothon gidena. Asa oothon gididaakko Xoossa kiyateth, kiyateh gidena.
ROM 11:7 Histin ay gaanee? Isiraa7eele nayti loo7ethi koydayssa demmibeyttena. Xoossan dooretidayti gidiko demmida. Haniko attidayta wozinay muumides.
ROM 11:8 Kase “Istta ayfey xeelontta mala, istta hayitheyka siyontta mala Xoossi hanno ha gallasiyo gakanaas isttas doccisiza ayana immides” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetida malakko.
ROM 11:9 Dawiteykka “Istta maaday istta oykiza narixa gido; Istta dhuphizazine qixate gido.
ROM 11:10 Istta ayfey xeellofo goozzeto; Istta zokkoy medhinas kuuno” gides.
ROM 11:11 Aner qasse ta zaara oychays, Isiraa7eele asay nam77antho kunddethafe dendanee? dendana. harappeka Isiraa7eele nayta qanatisana gishshi istta mooro gaason atotethi hankko deretas gakkides.
ROM 11:12 Gido attin qasse istta hanko dere asas anjjo gidides. Istta kunidethika qasse hanko deretas anjjo gidiko istti simmi attidakko ay mala gita anjjo gidandeeshin!
ROM 11:13 Hankko Dere asazo, ta intes yootays, ta hanko dere asas kiittetidade gidida gishshi ta oothoza ta minnada polana.
ROM 11:14 Hessikka ta bagga asati minidatana mala denithethada isttafe guutha asata ashshanaas ufaysan oothays.
ROM 11:15 Xoossi istta aggida hanko dere asay Xoossara giigikko Xoossi Isiraa7eele nayta zaaridi ekkiza wode intes aazi hanazi milattizee? Hessa guusi “hayqqope dendides” guusa malakko.
ROM 11:16 Koyro bukasoy loo7o gidikko hanko izappe oothetizaas wurikka loo7okko. Hessaththoka issi miththa xaphphoy loo7o gidikko hanmkko iza bolla diza hanigetikka loo7o gideetes.
ROM 11:17 Keththa dan77on diza miththa hangista malati inte meqqi wodhdhin hankko woran diza miththata milatiza hankko dere asati inte olla gididi inte haaronne inte anjjo shaaki ekkizadentta gidikko;
ROM 11:18 Heyta he meqqi wodhdhida hangista bolla othoretofa. inte istta bolla otoretiko qasse hanno wozinan wothite. He miththaa tookiday nena gidaka. miththay nena tookides attin.
ROM 11:19 Histinko “He hanigeti meqqi wodhdhiday nuni istta olla gelana malakko” gontta agekista.
ROM 11:20 Tumu gidista shin istti meqiday ammano paceppe denididayssankko. Inteka ammanon eqidista. Babbite attin otoretofite.
ROM 11:21 Xoossi koyrope diza hanigistas michetonttade gidiko inteskka michetena.
ROM 11:22 Hessa gishshi Xoossa kiyatethine iza menxxe iittatetha ane xeella. Iza menxxe iittethay kunididayta bollakko. Iza kiyatethay qasse inte iza qadhetetha garisan diza wode gakanaas xalalakko. Hessi baynida aggiko intekka qanixistana.
ROM 11:23 Istti ammanontta minni eqidasope simmiko kase beso simmi gelana. Xoossika istta zarisi gelithana danida7ees.
ROM 11:24 Inte bazo miththafe qanixettida kase inte medhetethafe gidontta loo7o miththan inte gelana danida7iko koyrope ba medhetetha hanigista gididayti heyti kase iza bolla diza miththan simmi geloy isttas waani hanenee?
ROM 11:25 Ta ishato, inte ciincca asi gididayssa intes milatontta mala hayssa gido xuura yooza inte erontta attana mala ta koyke. Hesikka hiniko dere asape xeygetidayti wuri ammanana gakanaas Isiraa7eele nayta wozinay muumides.
ROM 11:26 Hessa gishshi Isiraa7eele nayti wurikka attana. “Ashshizadey Xiyonepe yaana; Yaqobepeka iittateth digana.
ROM 11:27 Tni istta nagara wursa dhayssidape guye ta isttara caaqon geliza qaalay hessako. geetetidi kase geesha maxaafan xaafettida mala handes.
ROM 11:28 Intes hanko deretas Mishiracho qaalay gakana mala Isiraa7eele nayti Xoossan ixettida asi gidida. Gidikokka kase dooro mala gidiko ba Aawata baggara istti dosettidaytakko.
ROM 11:29 Xoossi dooridappene ba kiyateth immmidape guye ba oothida miishan simmidi handattena.
ROM 11:30 Inteka kase azazetonttaytako. Istti azazetontta ixxin ha7i intena maaridayssatho
ROM 11:31 Xoossi Intena maarida geedon isttika maaristana mala ha7i azazetonttayta gidida.
ROM 11:32 Xoossi wursika maaranas asi wuriska azazetontta mala goridides.
ROM 11:33 Xoossa cinccatethine iza erateth ay mala ciimma! Iza priday ay malakone paacetena. Izi adhida geedoyka eretena.
ROM 11:34 “Goda wozina eriday oonee? Izas zore immiday oonee?”
ROM 11:35 Xoossi zaari immana mala izas tal77e immiday oonee?
ROM 11:36 Wurikka izape, izain, izasko. Izas bonichoy medhinape medhinas gido. Amini7i.
ROM 12:1 Hesa gishshi ta ishato inte asatetha geeshine Xoossu ufaysiza paxa yarsho oothidi inte shiishshana mala ta intena Xoossa qadhetan woossays. Hesikka wozinamma asa mala inte Xoossas oothiza oothokko.
ROM 12:2 Loo7o ufaysizazine kumeth gididazi Xoossa sheney azakone inte paaci erana mala inte qofan oraxidi lamettite attin hayssa alame asa milatopite.
ROM 12:3 Intes Xoossi immida ammano mala interika intena paaci xeellite attin ha7i dizaysafe bolara intena dhoqisi xeellontta mala tani taas imettida Xoossa kiyatethan intena issa issa zorays.
ROM 12:4 Nupe issi issi uras issi asatetha bolla daro biliteti diza mala heytikka he biliteti issi mala ootho oothonttaysatho
ROM 12:5 Hessaththoka nuni darota gidi uttidi Kiristoosan issi ashoko. Nuni issay issas ashokko.
ROM 12:6 Nuusi immetida imota mala dumma dumma imotethi dees. Isades burope hananazi yooto gidiko izades immetida ammano mala yooto.
ROM 12:7 Oothi maadizadey oothi maado. Tamarisizadeyka tamariso.
ROM 12:8 Zorizade gidiko zoro. Baynidaytas immizadey gujji immo. Aysizadey minni aysso. maarizadeyka ufaysan maaro.
ROM 12:9 Inte siqotethi qoodhepe qomo gidopo. Iitta gididayssa wursikka ixxite. Loo7o gididayssara issife oykettite.
ROM 12:10 Inte inte garisan issay issara ishata mala loo7ethi siqetite. Issay issa beppe aathi bonichizayta gidite.
ROM 12:11 Godas oothana ayanan xugetizayta gidite attin hessa he minotethafe guye gooppite.
ROM 12:12 Ufayssan ufa7etizayta gidite; meto danida7ite; woossan minnite.
ROM 12:13 Ammanishe waayetizaytas intes dizayssafe shaaki immite. Imath mokite.
ROM 12:14 Intena qanigizayta anjjite attin qanigofite.
ROM 12:15 Ufa7etizaytara ufa7etite; muzotizaytara muzotite.
ROM 12:16 Inte inte garisan dosetethan diite. Maniqotara isopetethan daanas koyte attin otoropitene ceeqetopite.
ROM 12:17 Oonasikka iitta gishshi iitta zaaropite. Asi wuriso achan loo7o miishshi oothanas minnite.
ROM 12:18 Intes danida7etiko inte inte baggara asi wurisora saron diite.
ROM 12:19 Ta siiqoto, inte halo Xoossi kesso attin interika halo kesopite “Halo kesanay tanakko” gees Goday geeteti geeshsha maxaafan xaafetides.
ROM 12:20 Halo kessanape “Neni ne morikey gafiko muza; izi saamotiko usha; ne hessaththo oothiko tama boniqo iza bolla korasa” geetetidi geeshsha maxaafan xaafetides.
ROM 12:21 Iitta loo7o oothon xoono attin iittan xonettofa.
ROM 13:1 Ay asikka bena aysiza daanatas haaristana bessis. Xoossafe imetontta dishin daanatethi deena. Ha7i diza daanati Xoossafe daanatidaytakko.
ROM 13:2 Hessa gishshi daana bolla makali7idey Xoossa woga bolla makali7ees. He makali7izaytika ba bolla pirida eheetes.
ROM 13:3 Dere aysizati iitta oothizayta babiseetes attin loo7o oothizayta babisetena. Ne dere aysizades babbontta agana koyazii? Histinko loo7o ootha; izikka nena galatana.
ROM 13:4 Izi nees loo7o oothanas Xoossa oothanichako. Gido attin ne iitta oothida gidiko izas babba. Gaasoyka izi masha coo mela gixxiibeyna; Izi iitta oothizade qaxayanas Xoossa oothanichako.
ROM 13:5 Hessa gishshi iza qixxetes babo xalala gidontta ne qofapankka daanatizades azazistanas besses.
ROM 13:6 Inte giira immizay hessaskko. Aysizayti hessa he oothoza bolla Xoossi istta wothides.
ROM 13:7 Isttafe issas issas bessizayssa immite. Giira immana besizaytas giira immite; qaraxa qanxxanaas bessizaytas qaraxa qanxxite; Babanas bessizaytas babbite; bonichanas bessizata bonichite.
ROM 13:8 Inte garisan issay issara siiqetethafe attin oona bollaka accoy doopo. Ase siiqiza uray izi wogaa pollides.
ROM 13:9 “Laymatopa”, “Wodhopa”, “amotofa” gizaytane hara azazoti diikokka “Asi wursaka ne mala siiqa” giza hanno issi wogayn wurikka kuyettides.
ROM 13:10 siiqoy asa bolla iitta oothena; Hessa gishshi siiqoy woga wurisos kuusha.
ROM 13:11 Hayssa wodaa cadi xeellidi hessa oothite. Ha7i hana inte dhisikofe denidiza wodeko. Nu kase ammanosope haa simmin ha7i nuus attiza wodey matides.
ROM 13:12 Qamay aadhin wonttana gees. Hessa gishshi ane nu dhuma ootho wora yeggidi poo7o olla miishshe mayosu.
ROM 13:13 Gallasara hamutiza mala ane wogara hamutosu. magulithanine matho gidon; laymma amonine laymman gidopo; qanatetethanine palaman gidopo.
ROM 13:14 Hessa aggidi Yesus Kiristoosa mayte. Asho amo polanaas qopofite.
ROM 14:1 Inte garisan ammanon buro minnonttade shiishi ekkite attin iza qofa bolla piridofite.
ROM 14:2 Issi issi asi bettidayssa wursi maanas ammanoy dees. Qase ammanon minonta uray akakilate xalala mees.
ROM 14:3 Bettidayssa wursi mizadey wursi monttade kadhopa. Monitadey qasse mizade bolla piridofo. Xoossi wursaka ekides.
ROM 14:4 Haniko oothizade bolla piridizadey ne oonee? Izadey kunidiko woykko eqikoka iza Godas. Goday iza esanas danidaeza gishshi izi eqandes.
ROM 14:5 Issadey gallasatape issi gallas hara gallasafe aathidi bessi dumma gallasi gi qopees. Hara uray qasse gallasati wurikka issi gina gi qopees. Issi issi uray ootho.
ROM 14:6 Issi gallas hara galasafe dummasi qopizadey izi hessa oothizay Goda bonchos gidiko mizadeyka Goda bonchos giidi meesi. Miidi Xoossu galates. Monttadeykka Goda bonchos giidi muusu aggesine Xoossas galata immees.
ROM 14:7 Nupe oonikka bessi dizadeyne beppe bessi hayqizadey deena.
ROM 14:8 Nu diikoka Godas dosi. Hayqikoka Godas hanqosu. Hessa gishshi diikoka woykko hayqiko nu Godaskko.
ROM 14:9 Hessa gishshi hayqidaytasine paxxa dizatas Goda gidanasi Kirisitoosay hayqidi Hayqoppe paxxi denidides.
ROM 14:10 Histin ne aazas ne isha bolla piridazii? Aazasi ne isha leqazii? Nu wurikka Xoossa pirida womibara sinith shiqos doosu.
ROM 14:11 “Ta paxxa days. Gulibatey wurikka taasi gulibatana. Inxarisi wuri Xoossas marikatana” geeteti kase geesha maxaafan xaafetides.
ROM 14:12 Hesa gishshi nuni issi issi uray Xoossas Xoossa sinthi shiiqidi nu ootho gishshi izas zaaro immana.
ROM 14:13 Hessa gish nuni nu garisan isay isa bolla piridanape ane naagetos. Hesa aggidi nu ishas dhuphe gidizayssa woykko iza oykiza narxxa wothontta mala ane nu naagetos.
ROM 14:14 Tani Goda Yessusan amanida miza kaththan tunay baynidaysa eradis. Gido attin isadey isi miish tuna gi qopiko he mishay izadesi tunako.
ROM 14:15 Neni ne isha miza kaththa geedon dhuphe gidiko siiqoni simeristabeyka. Kirisitoosay iza gish haniqida ne isha ne miza kaththa gaason wodhopa.
ROM 14:16 Inte loo7o giidi popiza mishi iitta getistana mala oothofite.
ROM 14:17 Xoossa kawotethi xiilo ayanani bettida xilloteth sarotethine ufaysafe attin Muusa yoone usha yoo gidena.
ROM 14:18 Haysatho Krisitosas oothizadey Xoossu ufaysesinne asa achanika galatetes.
ROM 14:19 Hessa gish sarotethi betiza ogene nuni nu garisani loo7onas besiza oge ane koyosu.
ROM 14:20 Nuni Miza kaththa gish giidi Xoossa ootho ane laaloko. kathi wurikka geeshkko. Gido attiin hara urasi dhuphe gidiza kaath muusi qass balla oothoko.
ROM 14:21 Ne ishasi dhuphe gidizazi gidiko ashoka manapene woyne ush uyanape woykko ay mishika ne oothontta aggiko lo7oko.
ROM 14:22 Hessa gish haytantta milatiza mishatasi neesi diza ammanoy ne gidonine Xoossa gidon deyo. Haysi likeko giidi ammanon ekida mishan berika ba bolla piridonttadey izadey anijjetidadeko.
ROM 14:23 Gido attin wozinara sidhishe miiko izi ammanon moontta gish iza bolla piridetides. Ammanoni oothonttazi wurikka nagara.
ROM 15:1 Nuni amanoni minidayti hanko amanoni minotayi meto tokanasi besisi attiin nu Xoossa ufaetizayta gidanaso nusu besena.
ROM 15:2 Nuni wurikka nu lageista gusasine ista ufaysizazi othanasi beses.
ROM 15:3 Kirisitossa bena ufaysiza oothonita “Isiti nena cayda caashay ta bolla gakiides” geteti kase xafetidaysi hanides.
ROM 15:4 Neni gesha maxapistape demiza danida7ane minotethi nusi dana mala korope xafetidaysi wurikka nu izpe nuusi timirite demanamala xafetides.
ROM 15:5 Minotethine danida7a immiza Xoossi inte Yessus Kirisitosa kallishin intesi inte gidon ayana isipetetha iimo.
ROM 15:6 Hesika inte isi wozinane isi dona gididi nu Goda Yessus Krisitossa Godan ayana bonichanasa.
ROM 15:7 Hessa gish Xoosu galatanasi inte Kiristossa ekidamala isi isaka ekite.
ROM 15:8 Kasse awatas imetida ufaysa qaala polanaso Xoossa tumatetha gish gidi Krisitossa Ayhudatasi othizade gididaysa ta intesi yotanas.
ROM 15:9 hessathoka dere asati iza marotetha gish Xoossu galatanamala geteti kasse xafetida mala “Hesa gish ta nena dere gidoni galatana ne sunithaka ta yessana.”
ROM 15:10 Qasse “Haniko dere asato inteka iza deretara ufa7etite” ges
ROM 15:11 Nam7nithoka Zaniko derey inte wurikka Goda galatite derey wuri iza sabiite” ges.
ROM 15:12 Hesatho Isiayasan “Be dere asa bolla kawotiza iseyo nay yana. Yana Derey iza ufaysani nagana” ges.
ROM 15:13 Inite izan amaniza gish ufaysa Xoossi intesi ufaysine sarotethi kunitho. Hesikka xiillo ayana woliqa ufaysany intesi wogape adhi gukanasa. Haniko deretas othanicha gidida Phawulossa.
ROM 15:14 Ta ishato inte loo7ethan kumidayta erateth wurisoni kumidaytane harata zorinas eray dizayta gididaysa ta adafe shaka eradis.
ROM 15:15 Ta Xoossafe ekida imotetha gina qaseka intena qofisanasi isi isi yota bolla xalatethan intesi xafadis.
ROM 15:16 Xoossa wonigilan qasetetha oothoy hanko deretasi Yessusi Krisitossa oothanicha gidanasa. Hesikka hiniko derey xillo ayanan Xoossasi dumatidi Xoossi ekiza yarsho gidanasa.
ROM 15:17 Hesa gish tani Xoossas oothiza gish Yessusa Krisitossan ceeqetays.
ROM 15:18 Ta yotidaysanine ta oothidaysani hanko dere asay Xoossi azaistana mala Kirisitosa azazistana mala Kirisitossay tana gididi oothidazape attin hara hasa7ana xalike.
ROM 15:19 Hesikka haniday xillo ayana woliqani malatata bera hanides. Hesa malanika Yerusalame iliwaqore yehsi gakanasi ta Kirisitossa wonigila polla sabaladisi.
ROM 15:20 Hara uray kasse oothidasoni ta gelonitamala gada kasse Krisitossa sunitha xeygeti eronitason wonigila sabakanaysi tasi ommo.
ROM 15:21 Harapeka “Iza gish istasi yotitonitati iza beyana.
ROM 15:22 Hesa gidoni ta intiko bonitamala daro wode digistadis. Oerome beyanasi Phawulossa gegetethi
ROM 15:23 Hi7 qasi tasi hani oothoy baynida gish daro laythape ha sinini intena beyanasi ta daro lamotaadis.
ROM 15:24 Haysa ta qofa tani isidhaniya biiza polanasi qopaysi. Hara adhashe intena beyanasine intenara gutha wode gami7ada lamota othadamala inte tana ta banasa madanamala ufaysi othoyso.
ROM 15:25 Isi qasse hani diza amanizayta athi madana hai Yerusalame baysa.
ROM 15:26 Gasoykka Maqidoniyayne akayay Yerusalameni diza maiqota madana denidida.
ROM 15:27 Adaka ista madanasi dosida adafe” Isita ocoraa detes. Haniko dere asay Ayhudata ayana anijjo gishetidayta gidida gish biitafe dumida anjo Ayhuda asara gishatasi ista bolla accoy des.
ROM 15:28 Hesa ghsi ta oothoza wursida hayssa isti ekanakone eridape guye isidhiniya bana ta hera adhashe initena beyana.
ROM 15:29 Ta ha inteka bashe intesi Kirisitossa anijo kunitha eka banaysa ta erays.
ROM 15:30 Ta ishato tani Xoossa wosan baxetizamala inteka tanara baaxistanamala diza ta oothoykka hani amanizayta achan ekistanamala tasi wosite.
ROM 15:31 Nuni Yhudan diza manonita asa kushepe nu atanamalane Yerusalame diza ta oothoyka heni amanizayta achan ekistanamalatas wosite.
ROM 15:32 Hesikka Xoossa shenemala he inteko ta ufaysara banamalane intenara isipe oraxanasa.
ROM 15:33 Saroteha Goday intenara wurisotara gido amn7i.
ROM 16:1 Kinkira7ose woossa keeththan oothiza ammanetida michchiyo pebeno intes hadara gays.
ROM 16:2 Ammaniza asas bessiza mokko inte izo Goda sunththan mikki ekkana malane iza intefe koyza ay mishshanka inte izo maaddana mala ta intena qofisays.
ROM 16:3 Kase tanara Goda Yesus kiristoosas issife oothida Pirisiqilasine Aqilas ta saroka gathite.
ROM 16:4 Istti ta gishshi hayqqana gakanas bena aathi immida tana xalala gidontta hanko deretape ammandaytape istta galatetes.
ROM 16:5 Istta keeththan diza ammaniza asaka saro giite. Isiyape koyro kiristoosa n ammanida ta siiqoza Ephenexose saro giite.
ROM 16:6 Intes daro daaburidaro maaramo saro giite.
ROM 16:7 Tnara issife qachchetida Anddiraqoonene Yuliyane saro giite. Heytanti hawarista garisan lo7o sunththara dizaytane kiristoosa taape kase ammanidaytako.
ROM 16:8 Tani Goda baggara daro siiqiza Philyaxone saro giite.
ROM 16:9 Kiristoosa ootho tanara issife oothiza Irobanene ta siiqiza Senxxkeka saro giite.
ROM 16:10 Kiristoosan iza ammanoy paacetidi galatetida Aphilises ta saroka gathite. Arisxabalo so asasikka ta sarota gathite.
ROM 16:11 Ta dabbo Herodiyona saro giite. Godan diza Niriqqaso so asa saro giite.
ROM 16:12 Godan gididi minotethan oothiza macashata Tirifimonone Xirofimono saro giite. Godas oothon daro daaburidaaris tani izo siiqiza Xarsidis ta saroka gathite.
ROM 16:13 Godan doorettida Rufonoosone taas Aayo gididaris iza Aayeys ta saroka yootite.
ROM 16:14 Asqqerinene Afilesonpha, Herimene, Phaxirobane, Herimanene isttara diza ishata wurisotas ta saroka gathite.
ROM 16:15 Filegones, Yuliyas, Neriyasone iza micheyis hessathoka Alixones isttara diza ammanizaytaskka ta saroka gathite.
ROM 16:16 Issay issa yeer yeer ekkidi sarothetite. Kiristoosan ammaniza woossa keeththa asay wurikka intena saro gees.
ROM 16:17 Ta ishato asa garisan shaaketeth medhizaytape inte tamarida timirtta ekkontta ixxon intes dhuphe gidiza asatape inte naagetite.
ROM 16:18 Heytantta mala asati Yesus kiristoosas oothizayta gidontta ba qanththa kaththa gishshi oothizaytakko. Shugo qaalara haasa7anine wozina kiya asata balethetes.
ROM 16:19 Inte mishshiracho qaalas azazetizayta gididayssa asi wuri siyides. Hessika tana daro ufayssides. Gidikkoka inte lo7o hanos cinccata qasse iitta oothos eeyata gidana mala ta koyays.
ROM 16:20 Sarotetha Goday xala7e eeson inte too garisa aathi dinccerethana. Goda Yesus kiristoosa kiyatethi intenara gido.
ROM 16:21 Tanara issife oothiza Xintoosay qasseka ta dabbo Luqiyesay, Iyaasoneyne Susiphixirosay intena saro saro geetes.
ROM 16:22 Hayssa kiitaa xaafiday tani Xerixiyosay intena Goda sunththan saro gays.
ROM 16:23 Tanine hayssan diza kumetha woossa keeththa asa mokki ekkiza Gayiyosayka intena saro gees.
ROM 16:24 Goda Yesus kiristoosa kiyateth intenara wurisotara gido. Amin7i.
ROM 16:25 Tani yootiza michchiracho qaalay Yesus kiristoosa gishshi yootetiza kiitayne beni wodepe dommidi qotan gam7idi ha7i qasse qonccida tuma xuura baggara izi intena ammanon essanaas danda7es.
ROM 16:26 Ha7i qasse hayssi tumay qonccides. Medhina Xoossa azazon wurikka ammanidi azazistana mala nabeta maxaafa baggara dereti wurikka iza erana mala handes.
ROM 16:27 Izi xalala era gidida Godas Yesus kiristoosa baggara medhina bonchoy izas gido. Amin7i.
1CO 1:1 Xoossa shenen Yesus Kiristoosas kiitistanas xeygetida Phawulosapene nu isha Sostinosape,
1CO 1:2 Qoronttosan diza Xoossa woossa keethas, Goda Yesus Kiristoosas duma keezidaytasine isttasara nuusara Goda gidida Goda Yesus Kiristoosa suntha awan awanka xeygiza ammanizaytara gidanas xeygetida asa wursos.
1CO 1:3 Nu Aawa Xoossafe Goda Yesus Kiristoosape kiyatethine saroy intes gido.
1CO 1:4 Goda Yesus Kiristoosa baggara intes imetida Xoossa kiyatetha gishshi wurso wode inte gishshika ta Xoossu galatays.
1CO 1:5 Gaasoyka ay yoonka, hessikka hasa7an gidin eratetha wurson inte duretidista.
1CO 1:6 Kiristoosa gishshi nu intes markattidayssi inte achchan minnides.
1CO 1:7 Hessa gishshi inte Yessus Kiristoosay qonccana gallas naagishin ayana imotethatape aykoka intes paccena.
1CO 1:8 Goda Yesus Kiristoosa nam7antho yaana gallasan inte inte bolla boroy bayinda beettana mala wursethi gakanas izi intena lo7ethi naagana.
1CO 1:9 Izi ba naaza nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosa issipetethako intena xeygida Xoossi izi ammanetida Xoossukko.
1CO 1:10 Ta ishato! inte garisan shaaketethi doontta mala intes issi wozinayne issi qofay daana mala inte inte garisan issino gidana mala Goda Yesus Kiristoosa sunthan ta intena woossays.
1CO 1:11 Ta ishato inte garisan palamay dizayssa ta Qalo7i so asape siyadis.
1CO 1:12 Yoozika hayssa malakko; Inte garisan issi issi asati ta Phawulosa baggakko gees; baggay qasse ta Aphilosa baggakko gees; baggay qasse ta keefa baggakko gishin haray qasse ta Kiristoosa baggaakko gees.
1CO 1:13 Histiko Kiristoosay shaaketi wodhidee? Inte gishshi Phawulosay kaqettidee? Woyko Phawulosa sunthan xamaqetidetii?
1CO 1:14 Inte giddofe Qarsoxxosapene Gayiyosape attin hara oonaka ta xamaqontta gishshi Xoossa galatays.
1CO 1:15 Hessa gishshi oonikka “Ta Phawulosa sunthan xamaqistadis” gaana asi deena.
1CO 1:16 Tumuka Isxxifanose so asa xamaqadis. Heytape hara ta xamaqidakone ta eriza uray deena.
1CO 1:17 Kiristoosay tana kiitiday mishiracho qaala yootanas attin xamaqanas gidena. Kiristoosa masiqaley hada gidontta mala ta asape gidida cinccatethan sabakikke.
1CO 1:18 Masiqaleza kiitay dhayana dizaytas eeyatethikko. Gido attin attana diza nuusu gidiko Xoossa wolqakko.
1CO 1:19 “Cinccata cinccateth ta issitafe dhaysana; eranchata eratetha ta hada oothana” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafettides.
1CO 1:20 Cinccay awan dizee? Tamarida eray awan dizee? Hayssa wodeza piligi erizay awan dizee? Xoossi ha alameza erateth eeyatethan kessibeynee?
1CO 1:21 Xoossa eratethafe dendidayssan alamey ba eratetha giddon Xoossu eroy xoonin sabako eeyatethan ammanizayta ashshanas Xoossa shene gidides.
1CO 1:22 Ay wodeka Ayhudati duma malata koyettes. Girike asati qasse erateth koyettes.
1CO 1:23 Nuna gidiko kaqetida Kiristoosa sabakosu. Hessika Ayhudatas dhuphekko. Hanko ammanontta deretas qasse eeyatethikko.
1CO 1:24 Xoossi xeygidaytas istti Ayhudista gidin woykko Girike dere asa gidikkoka Kiristoosay Xoossa wolqane Xoossa eratethikko.
1CO 1:25 Gaasoyka asa erape Xoossa eeyatethi aadhida eratethikko. Asa minotethafe Xoossa laafatethi aadhes.
1CO 1:26 Ta ishato kase inte xeygetiza wode inte ay mala asakkone ane qopite. Asa qofa mala gidiko intefe darizayti erata gidekista. Intefe daroti waolqqay bayindaytakko. Darotikka gita keeththa asape yeletibeykkista.
1CO 1:27 Gido attin Xoossi erata yeelachanas derape eeyata doorides. Xoossi minota yeelachanas alamezape daburanchata doorides.
1CO 1:28 Xoossi hanko ammanontta asa achan deettes geeteti erettiza miishata bayinda miisha mala oothana hayssa alamezan leqettidaytane kawuyidayta hada milatizayta doorides.
1CO 1:29 Hessika izi oothiday oonkka iza sinthan ceeqetontta malakko.
1CO 1:30 Intena qasse Xoossi Yesus Kiristoosara issifetethi deyana mala oothides. Hessa gishshi Xooss Yesus Kiristoosa nu erateth, nu xiilloteth, nu geeshatethine nuna ashshizade gidana mala oothides.
1CO 1:31 Hesa gishshi kase “Ceeqiza uray Godan ceeqo” geeteti geesha maxaafan xaafetida malakko.
1CO 2:1 Ta ishato ta inteko Xoossa xuura qonccisana biday taas duuna qaratethi woykko era daroy diza gishshi gidena.
1CO 2:2 Ta inte giddon diza wode kaqettida Yesus Kiristoosape attin hara erontta mala ta baggara muritadis.
1CO 2:3 Ta inteko daro daaburan, yashatethanine qassekka daro kokorashe badis.
1CO 2:4 Ta qaalayne sabakoyka ayana wolqa qonccisethanpe attin cimonine era daron gidena.
1CO 2:5 Hessika inte ammanoy Xoossa wolqanpe attin asa cinccatetha bolla xaphontta mala hanides.
1CO 2:6 Nu kaha kunthida asata achchan era hasa7a hasa7osu. Gido attin hayssa ha alameza erateth gidena. Woyko dhayana diza ha alameza haarizayta erateth gidena.
1CO 2:7 Gido attin nu hasa7izay kase qoteti diza Xoossa xuura eratethikko. He eratethay Xoossi daro wodepe kase nuna bonchos kasetid wursi wothidayssakko.
1CO 2:8 Ha alameza haarizaytape oonka ha eratetha eribeyna. Eridako istti boncho Goda kaqettena.
1CO 2:9 Gido attin geesha maxaafan “Asa ayfey beyonttazi, asa haythi siyonttazi, asa wozinayka qoponttazi Xoossi ba dosizaytas giigisides” gees.
1CO 2:10 Xoossi gidiko hessa ba ayana baggara nuusu qonccisides. Ayanayka Xoossas ciima yoo ashontta wursi piligi xeeles.
1CO 2:11 Asa garisan izades diza ayanape attin izade wozina erizay oonee? Hessaththoka Xoossa ayanape attin Xoossa qofa erizay oonka deena.
1CO 2:12 Xoossafe nuusu imettidayssa nuni erana mala Xoossa ayanay nuusu imettides attin nuni hayssa ha alameza ayana ekibeykko.
1CO 2:13 Nu yootizay hayssako. Nu asape tamarda qaala gidontta ayanape tamarda qaala hasa7osu. Ayana tumatethaka nu qonccisizay ayana qaalankko.
1CO 2:14 Xoossa ayanay izan bayinda asi Xoossa ayanape gididazi ekkanas danda7ena. Gaasoyka hessa mala yooy izas eeyatethakko. Izi bess ayanan paacetizade gidida gishshi izi eranas danda7ena.
1CO 2:15 Xoossa ayanay izan diza uray qass wursika paaces attin bess oonankka paacetena.
1CO 2:16 Hessikka “Goda qofa eranas danda7izay oonee? Iza zoranas danda7izay oonee?” geeteti kase geesha maxaafan xaafettida malakko. Nuusu gidiko Kiristoosa wozinay dees.
1CO 3:1 Ta ishato ta intena inte Kiristoosan buro guutha nayta malane buro ammanoy gelontta asa malape attin ayanan kumida asa mala gaada intes hasa7anas danda7abeyke.
1CO 3:2 Inte buro minnontta gishshi ta intena maathi paahadis attin buro mino kathi muzabeykke. Ha7ika gidiko inte burokko.
