2TH 2:16 Izi nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossay qasse nuna siiqqidayne ba kiyateththan medhdhina minththethone loo7o ufayss izi nuus immida Xoossa nu Aaway
2TH 2:17 Izi inte wozina loo7o oothonine qaalan minsso.
2TH 3:1 Wurththethan ta ishato qassekka Goda qaalay inte achchan hanoyssathoka eleeli wurssoso gakkana malane bonchetana mala nuus woosite.
2TH 3:2 Qasseka asi wuri ammanizayssa gidontta gish makkalanchatapene iita asatape nu attana mala nuus woosite.
2TH 3:3 Goday gidiko ammanetidayssa. Izikka intena minnisana; xalaepaka intena naagana.
2TH 3:4 Nu intena azazidayssa inte hai oothidista shin sinththefekka inte oothanayssa nuni Godan ammanetosu.
2TH 3:5 Goday inte wozina Xoossa siiqqookone Kiristtoossa dandda7ako kaaletho.
2TH 3:6 Ta ishato ootho othantta asapene inte nuupe ekkida timirtteza mala doontta ammanizaytape inte haakkana mala Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa sunththan intena nu azazoos.
2TH 3:7 Inte nu lemuso wostti kaalanakone inte inte baggara ereista. nu intenara diza wode ootho oothontta coo deybeykko.
2TH 3:8 Qassekka oona soopekka kaththi coo mela mibeykko. Gido attin intefe oonaskka nu tooho gidontta mala qamane gallas daaburan oothi midos.
2TH 3:9 Nu hessa oothiday inte nuna kaalana mala intes loo7o lemuso gidana giidipe attin nuus kooshshizayssa intefe ekkana nuns woqay dhayin gidena.
2TH 3:10 Nu intenara diza wode “ootho oothanas dosontta asi kaathth moopo giza azazo intes immidos.
2TH 3:11 Inte garssan issi issi asati ootho oothonttayssa nu siydosu. Heytantti ootho oothontta mela bena gaathontta asa yooni gelizaytako.
2TH 3:12 Heyta mala asati ba ootho co7u gi oothana malane ba kath maana mala Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa sunththan nu istta azazoosine zoroos.
2TH 3:13 Inte gidikko ta ishato loo7o ootho oothanape mulekka azaallofite.
2TH 3:14 Hayssa nu kiittida qaalas azazetoonttay oonkka diikko hessa milatizade lo7ethi kaalitene izi ba oothon yeelatana mala izara gaggofite.
2TH 3:15 Gido attin iza inte isha mala hanqqite attin morkke mala xeellofite.
2TH 3:16 Sarotetha Goday izi ba baggara yoo wursson intes saroteth immo. Goday intenara wurssara gido.
2TH 3:17 Hayssa sarota ta ta kushera intes xaafiday tana phawuloossa. Ta kiittas dumma malatay hayssa ta xaafiza xaafoy hayssa milates.
2TH 3:18 Nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa aadho kiyateththi intenara wuryyssara gido.
1TI 1:1 Nuus ufayss gidida yesus kiristtoossaninne nuna ashshida Xoossa azazon, Yesuss kiristtoossay kiittida Phawuloossape.
1TI 1:2 Ammanon taas tumu naa gidida Ximttoossas Xoossa nu Aawape nu Goda Yesus kiristtoossape kiyateth, maarotethine saroy nees gido.
1TI 1:3 Tani Maqqidonyya bashe nena hadara gida mala hayssafe sinththan issi issi asati wordo timirtte tamarssontta mala ne azazana mala Efesoonen daasha.
1TI 1:4 Qassekka asay yootin wurontta beni wode hayssu7en ba wode wurssontta mala azaza. Heyta mala yooy palama denthethes atin ammanon oothetiza xoossa oothos aykkoka go7ena.
1TI 1:5 Ha azazoozas waana ayfe yooy gidikko geeshsha wozinape loo7o qofara hessathoka tumu ammanope beettiza siiqo.
1TI 1:6 Issi issi asay haytape pooqqeti eqqidi go7ay bayndda yootakko simmides.
1TI 1:7 Woga tamarssizayta gidana mala koyetes. Gidikkoka istti ba yootizayssa woykko keehi moottetiza yooza lo7ethi ereetena.
1TI 1:8 Gido attin asi maaran goetizakko wogay lo7o gididayssa nu eroos.
1TI 1:9 Qassekka wogay immetiday xiillo asas gidontta woga yedhdhi aadhdhizaytas, azazetonttaytas, Xoossas babbonttaytass, nagaranchatas, geeshshateth bayinddaytas, Xoossu leeqqizaytas, ba Aayone ba Aawa wodhdhizaytasine shemppo wodhdhizaytas gididayssa nu eroos.
1TI 1:10 Hessathokka laymmatizaytas, addera aqqiza addistas, ase bayzizaytasine shaammizaytas, wordanchatas, asatas wordora caaqqizaytas, loo7o timirttera eqqettiza wurssootaskko.
1TI 1:11 He loo7o timirttey anjjetida Xoossi taas hadara immida boncho miishshirachcho qaalara gaaggizayssako.
1TI 1:12 Tana ba oothos shuumidine ammanetizade oothi ekkidine taas miinoteth immida nu Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa ta galatayss.
1TI 1:13 Hayssafe kase ta ay mala ase cayizzadene goodeththizade, qasse makkali7a as gidikkoka hessa ta eroonttane ammanontta dashe oothida gish Xoossi tana maarides.
1TI 1:14 Yesuss Kiristtoossape gidida ammanorane siiqora nu Goda kiyatethi taas keezi darides.
1TI 1:15 Yesuss Kiristtossay nagaranchata ashshanaas duge hayssa ha alame yides giza qaalay tumane asi wurkka ekkanas bessizayssako. Nagaranchatapekka aadhdhiza nagaranchay tanako.
1TI 1:16 Gido attin ta maaretidaykka Yesuss Kiristtoossay zaway bayindda ba dandda7a, wurssofe aadhdhida nagarancha gidida ta bolla beessiday izan ammananaytasine medhina deyo deemmanaytas leemuso gidana malako.
1TI 1:17 Hessa gish medhinas hayqqi eroontta, ayhaaththaen beeti eroontta berkka xaalla Xoossu gidida kawoos medhdhinape medhdhina gakkanaas izas bonchoyine galatay gido. Ammiinn77i.
1TI 1:18 Ta naa Ximttosa ne gish kasetidi yootettida mala hayssa azazoza ta nees immadis. Hessikka ne he qaala kaalashe loo7o baaxe baaxistanasskko.
1TI 1:19 Ammanoyine loo7o qofay nees deyo. Issi issi asati ba loo7o qofa yeedhdhi adhdhidi abba bolla metoy iza bolla gakkin waayetiza markkabe mala ba ammano dhayiissida.
1TI 1:20 Istta giidon xoossa caashsh aggidi tamarana mala tani xalaes aatha immidayti Nemenewoossayine Iskkinddirossay deetes.
1TI 2:1 Hessa gish wurssofe koyro hara asas shoobetha woosa, gaanatetha woosane galata woosa asa wurssos kawootasine dere ayssizaytas wurssos woosssana mala qopisays.
1TI 2:2 Hessikka tumu ayyana duussanine geeshshateth wursson nuni sarotethanine wogan daana malassiko.
1TI 2:3 Hayssi nuna ashshiza Xoossa achchan loonne ufayssizazikko.
1TI 2:4 Izi asi wuri attana malane tuma erana mala koyees.
1TI 2:5 Issi Xoossi xaala dees. Qassekka Xoossasine asas giidon issi giggisizza gaanay dees. Izikka asi gidida Yesuss Kiristtoossako.
1TI 2:6 Izi bena asa wurssos aathi immides. Hessikka heeraka wodey adhdhontta izas markkatides.
1TI 2:7 Takka hayssas miishshirachcho yootanas kiittetidade. Qasseka deretas tumu ammano assitamare gidada shuumistadis. Hessakka ta wordotontta tumu yootanassikko.
1TI 2:8 Hessa gish attuma asay wursso soon hanqqoy bayinddane palammay bayindda ba geeshsha kushista pude dhuuqqu histtidi woosana mala ta koyayis.
1TI 2:9 Hessathokka maccashshati bonchora bena shiishshi ekkidi beessiza mayo mayeto, attin ba hu7e daadi ekkidi woykko alli7o mayo, worqqanne inqufe aathidi walq walq guuppetto.
1TI 2:10 Gido attin Xoossu woosos giza maccashshati isttas oothana beessiza loo7o oothon lo7etto.
1TI 2:11 Maccashshi coou gaada kumeththara azazeteth tamaru.
1TI 2:12 Maccashshi coou gaanape attin iza tamarssana mala woykko adde bolla godatana mala koykke.
1TI 2:13 Gasooykka koyro addamey medhdhettides; kaalada hewana medhdhettadus.
1TI 2:14 Qassekka koyro ballettiday addamme gidena. Ballettada xoossa wogappe adhdhiday maccashshayoko.
1TI 2:15 Gidikkoka maccashshi ammanonine siiqqon geeshshatethan berkka bena haaron miinnikko naa yelon attana.
1TI 3:1 “Oonikka woosa keeththa cima gidana koykko loo7o ootho amootees” giza qaalay tuma.
1TI 3:2 Hessa gidikko woosa keeth kaalethizadey borey baynddade; issi machchade; ginara dizade; bena haarizade; wogara aqqizade; imaththi mokkizade; tamarththanas danddaizade;
1TI 3:3 Maathotonttade; ooshshu oyetonttade; qass maarage as; asara pallametonttade; miishshe goodonttade; godanas beesses.
1TI 3:4 Be nayta bees azazetizaytane asi bonchizayta histti dichchidi ba keeththa asa wogara ayssizzade gidanas beesses.
1TI 3:5 Issadey ba keeththa asa wogara ayso eroontta agiikko Xoossa woosa keeth wostti naggana danddaize?
1TI 3:6 Otoretethan puuridi Xala7ey kunddida pirdan izi kunddontta mala oorath ammanizade gidoopo.
1TI 3:7 Qassekka iza sunththi boretontta malanne xala7e yarden izi gelontta mala ammanontta asa achchan loo7o markkateth daanas koshshes.
1TI 3:8 Daaqonetikka hessaththo bonichchetidaytane ba gida qaala laammi laammi yeggonttayta; daro woyine ushshas amotonttayta; ogey bayindda goo7a goodonttayta gidanas beesses.
1TI 3:9 Ammanos xuura, loo7o qofara naaganas beesses.
1TI 3:10 Haytanttikka koyroti paaccetteto. Issi iitay istta bolla beetontta aggikko hessafe guye daaqonetethan ootheto.
1TI 3:11 Macca daaqonetikka bonchetidayta; zigironttayta; qass wogara dizayta; hano wursson ammanetidayta gidanas beesses.
1TI 3:12 Daaqoneti issi machchadista gidanas beesses. Qassekka ba naytane ba keeththa asa wogara ayssizayta gidanas beesses.
1TI 3:13 Wogara oothidayti beess gita bonchone Yesuss Kiristtoossan isttas diza ammanon daro xalateth deemmana.
1TI 3:14 Ta neekko elle baana koykkoka hayta azazota nees xaafayss.
1TI 3:15 Ta hanno nees xaafizay ta gamm7iza gidikkoka asay Xoossa keeththan waani daanakkone ne erana mala gaadakko. Keethay deyo Xoossa wossa keethako; hessikka tumu tuussune xaphoko.
1TI 3:16 Tumu ayana duussa xuuray sidhey bayindda gita; izikka “ase gidides; iza xilotethi Xillo ayanan qoncides; kiittanchatas beettides; ammanontta deres yootetides; alamen dizaytan ammanettides; bonchora pude denddi bides” gizayssako.
1TI 4:1 Wode wurssetha bolla issi issi asay ammano aggidi baalethiza ayanatane iita ayana timirtte kaallanayssa xiillo ayanay qonccera yootes.
1TI 4:2 Hessa mala timirttey istta qofay bonqqo biratan xuugettida mala geellatethan dooccida qoodhepe qoommon haniza wordancha asatape yaana.
1TI 4:3 He asati asay ekkontta malane gelontta mala diiggana. Ammanizaytine tuma shaakki eriza asay xoossay medhdhida kath galatarakka ekkizayti moontta mala digganane azazana.
1TI 4:4 Xoossi medhdhiday wurikka lo7o. Asi galatara ekkiko wora wodhdhizay issinakka baawa.
1TI 4:5 Wurikka Xoossa qaalanine woosan geeyana.
1TI 4:6 Hayssa ha azazooza ammaniza asa ne qoofisikko, ammano qaalanine ne ekkiida loo7o timirttezan miinada Yesuss Kiristtoossa loo7o oothancha gidanddassa.
1TI 4:7 Xoossu bonchisontta go7ay bayindda hayssu7eppene cima maaccashshata hayssu7eppe haakkada tuma ayana oothos ne asatetha giiggissa.
1TI 4:8 Asatetha asho ogen dosiisoy guutha wodes go7es shin tumu ayana duussas bena tamarssoy gidikko hayssa ha alamezassine buro yaana duussas ufayssi diza gish wurssos go7es.
1TI 4:9 Hayssi ha qaalay ammanettidayssane wurssi ekkanas beessiza qaalakko.
1TI 4:10 Nu hessas giidi dafettoossine daabuross. Hessikka asa wurssos harapekka ammanizaytas ashiza deyo Xoossan nu ufayss oothiza gishshaskko.
1TI 4:11 Hayta yoota azazanne tamarsa.
1TI 4:12 Ne yelagatetha oonikka kadhdhopo; gido attin ne hasa7an, ne duussan, siiqoon, ammanon, geeshshatethanine ammanizaytas loo7o leemuso gida.
1TI 4:13 Ta he baana gakkanaas qaal nabbabanas, zoranasine tamarsanas miinna.
1TI 4:14 Cimati ne bolla ba kushe woththi woosishin, sinththafe hananayssi nees immettida imotetha lep histta aggoofa.
1TI 4:15 Asi wuri ne diichcha beeyana mala ha yoota lo7etha miinthada dandda7an pola.
1TI 4:16 Ne duussa giishshine ne tamarsiza timirtezas naagetta, haytan miinna. Ne hessa oothiko nenane ne gizayssa siyizayta ashshana.
1TI 5:1 Cima asa ne Aawa mala bonchora zora attin doomm7ofa; naatetha attuma nayta ne ishata mala xeella.
1TI 5:2 Hessathokka cima maaccashshata Aayista mala, naatetha maaccata qasse ne michista mala geeshsha wozinan xeella.
1TI 5:3 Aadafe metottettida amm7ista looeththa naaga.
1TI 5:4 Issi amm7eys nay woykko na nay diza gidikko, he nayti ba soo asata maaddanasine bena yeliddaytas kase istti oothida kushshe zaaron haraape kasetidi ba ammano oothon beessanasinne tamaranas beesses. Hessikka Xoossa ufayssizayssa.
1TI 5:5 Qasse tumape maadoy bayindda, berkka diza amm7eya Xoossu xaalla xeellawusu. Woosasine Xoossafe maado deemmanas gaallasine qaama miinistawusu.
1TI 5:6 Ha biitta loo7o duussu xaalla koyiza amm7eya gidikko iza paxa dashe hayiqqidarokko.
1TI 5:7 Oona bollakka woththoy doontta mala hayssa azazooza asas aatha.
1TI 5:8 Issi asi ba daabbota haraappekka ba soo asa maaddonttade gidikko izi ammano kaadiddadene ammanontta asapekka adhdhida iita asakko.
1TI 5:9 Izisi layththay usuppun tammu layththafe garsara diza amm7ey sunththu amm7ista mazgaban xaapopa. Qasseka iza kase issade xaalla gellidaro gidanas beesses.
1TI 5:10 Nayta dichoninne immatha mokon, ammanizayta too meechchan, metootidayta maadonine loo7o oothon wursson bena aatha immada loo7o oothonkka keeza erettidaro gidanas beesses.
1TI 5:11 Azinay bayindda naatetha amm7ista gidikko hessa mala mazzigaban xaafopa. Gasooykka isttas diza azinara daana amoy istti Kiristtoossas oothana gi gellida qaalape bollara adhdhiza wode adde gellana koyeetes.
1TI 5:12 Istti kase caaqqida qaala miza gish he yoozan ba bolla pirda ehettes.
1TI 5:13 Hessafekka ootho oothanape yuuyi yuuyi asa keeth gelana dosettes. Ootho ixxo xaalla gidontta hasa7anas beessonttayssa hasa7ishe zigirizaytane kooshshontta asa yoo giido coo wooxi gelizayta gidettes.
1TI 5:14 Hessa gish azinati hayqqida naatetha maaccashshati adde gelana mala, nayta yelana malane ba soo as ayssana mala, morkeykka istta bolla wooththiza miishshe demmontta mala ta zorayss.
1TI 5:15 Addaaka hayssafe kase issi issi asati xala7e kaalana guye sherr7i gida.
1TI 5:16 Ammaniza maaccashi oonikka ba soo asa giiddon amm7eti diza gidikko woosa keethi tumu amm7ista xaalla maaddana mala izakka ba baggara ba amm7ista maaddu attin woosa keethas tooho gidana mala aaggaguupu.
1TI 5:17 Woosa keeththa lo7ethi ayssizayti haraapekka saabakonine tamarson miinniza cimati gidikko dikko mado madistanas beesses.
1TI 5:18 Maxxafan “kath buukiza boora duuna qaachchofa” qassekka “ootho oothizadey damussa ekkana beesses” gees.
1TI 5:19 Namm77u markkay woykko hedzdzu markkay markkatontta dishin cima bolla shiiqqiza mooto ekkofa.
1TI 5:20 Harati beeydi naagistana mala nagara oothizayta asa wursso sinththan hanqqa.
1TI 5:21 Xoossanine Yesuss Kiristtoossan doorettida kiittanchata sinththan hayta azazota oonakka maaddontta ne naaggana malane issi miishshikka ta gooripe ziq dhooqu histtontta mala nena hadara gays.
1TI 5:22 Xoossa oothos doranas, oona bollakka ne kushe wootha woosanas eesotopa. Qasse haratara nagara oothanas zuupetopa. nagarape nena xiillotethan naaga.
1TI 5:23 Nena qanththan saakkizaysasinne deenththa saakkoza gish guuthu woyine caajjefe guujjada uya attin hayssafe guye haathe xaalla uyoopa.
1TI 5:24 Issi issi asa nagaray pirday yanafe kasetidi qonces, baggayta nagaray qass pirdafe guye qonces.
1TI 5:25 Loo7o oothoykka hessa mala pirdafe sibthati qoncana, qonconta agikkokka piradafe guye qoncana.
1TI 6:1 Xoossa sunththine iza timirttey cayetontta mala aylletetha qambbara garssan dizayti wuri ba godas kumetha bonchoy beessizayssa ereetto.
1TI 6:2 Ammaniza godati diza ammaniza ashshikarati godati istta ishatas gidida gish godatas beessiza boncho immetto. Harapekka istta oothon maadetiza ammaniza godati isttas dosettidayta gidida gish nekka haytantta mala yoota tamarththanasine zoranas beesses.
1TI 6:3 Oonikka wordo timirtte tamarsikko Goda Yesuss kiristtoosa loo7o qaalane ayana tumatetha minssiza timirttera gaaggonttayssa gidikko
1TI 6:4 He uray otoroteththan kumidesinne aykkoka yuushi qoopena. Issi issi qaalata gish paalamistanassine, ooyistanas iita amoy izan dees. Heyitikka qanateteth, ooshshu, caashshe, iita sidhdhe kaallethettes.
1TI 6:5 Tumay isttafe ekketi gidin beess ayyana oothon wodhdhe deemmana milatiza asatane qofa pacce asata giiddon goochchettidi duuxxontta ooshshu eheettes.
1TI 6:6 Gido attin tumu ayyana asi gideth nuus dizayssan woppu giidi duussara gita wodheko.
1TI 6:7 Gasooykka nu hayssa ha alameza yishe aykkoka ekki yibeyikko; bisheka qasse ayikkoka ekki booko.
1TI 6:8 Gido attin nuus maanayssine nu mayanayss diiko gidana.
1TI 6:9 Dure gidanas koyizayti gidikko gede paacceninne narxxan gelidi oykettizayssa mala daro hadanine iita amon un7etetes.
1TI 6:10 Gasooykka miishsha siiqqoy iitateth wurssos xapho. Issi issi asati dure gidana giidi amope denddidayssan ammano ogeppe ballettidi haraso bidane berkka bena daro meto giido gelththida.
1TI 6:11 Neno Xoossa aso! ne hessa wurssofe baqata. Xiilloteth, tumu ayyanan duussu, ammano, siiqqo, dandda7ane ashshiketeth kaalla.
1TI 6:12 Ammano baaxe lo7otha baaxista. Daro markkata sinththan loo7o ammanetethan ne markkatidayssane ne izas xeeyigetida medhdhina deyoza lo7etha oykka.
1TI 6:13 Wurssoskka deyo immiza Xoossa achchan hessathokka Phanxxoossa Philaxxoossa sinththan tuma markkattida Yesuss Kiristtoossa sinththan ta nena hadara gizay
1TI 6:14 Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossay qonccana gakkanaas nees imetida oothoza wothoy bayinda ne polana malakko.
1TI 6:15 He qonccethay anjjettidayssi berkka wurssi harizaysinne kawoota kawooy, Godatas Goday izi ba woden beessana.
1TI 6:16 Izi xaalla hayqqonttayssa. Oonikka shiiqanas dandda7ontta po7o giidon dees. Iza beeyida asi oonikka baawa, beeyana dandda7izadeyka deena. Izas wollqqayine bonchoy medhdhinape medhdhinas gido; amminnii.
1TI 6:17 Hayssa ha alamezan duretidayti otorettontta mala; gido attin nu ufa7ettana mala wurssikka darssi tirhaaththaisidi nuus immiza Xoossan attin ammanththontta miishshan ammanetontta mala asas yoota.
1TI 6:18 Lo7o oothana malanne lo7o oothon durista gidana mala, keyatane shaakki immanas dosizayta gidana mala asa azaza.
1TI 6:19 Hessathokka tumu gidida deyo deemmana mala buroppe yaana wodes asay mino xapho gidiza haaro bees shiishshana.
1TI 6:20 Ximttossa, ne hadara ekkidayssa wurssa naaga. Xoossa bonchisontta hada duuna loommiu loommiupene wordo erateth geetettiza asi beepe medhdhi kessida timirttefe haakka.
1TI 6:21 Nuus hessa mala eratteth dees giza, issi issi asati hessaththo oothon ammano ogepe balettida. Xoossa kiyatethi intenara gido.
2TI 1:1 Yesuss kiristtoossara isipetethan diza deyo ufaysa qaala gish yotana mala Xoossa sheenen Yesuss Kiristtoossan kiittetida phawulossape,
2TI 1:2 Dosetida ta na Ximttoossa kiyateth, maarotethine sarotethi Xoossa Aawape Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossape nees gido.
2TI 1:3 Paccey bayindda gaallasine qama ne gish woosan qofisashe kase Aawati oothida mala geeshsha wozinara ta gooyinniza Xoossa ta galatayss.
2TI 1:4 Kase ne afunththa qooppa ekkada ta nena beya ekkada ufa7istana laamootayss.
2TI 1:5 Qoodhdhepe qoommo gidontta ne ammanoza qooppayss. He ammanoykka koyro ne Aayey Aayin Loyidinine qassekka ne Aayeyin Ewunqqen dees. Ha7i qass ne bolla dizayssakka ta eradis.
2TI 1:6 Hessa gish ta ta kushe ne bolla wothin ne ekkidayssa ne bolla diza xoossa imota ne denththethana mala ta nena qoofissayss.
2TI 1:7 Xoossi nuus nu nu hu7e haranass Xoossa wollqqa eranasinne siiqistana ayyana immides attin babo ayana immibeyina.
2TI 1:8 Hessa gish Goda gish markkateth woykko Goda gish qachchetida tanan yeellattopa. Gido attin Xoossa wollqqara miishshiracho qaala gish tanara meto ekka.
2TI 1:9 Nu aykkoka oothida gish gidontta dishin ba qofa malane ba kiyatetha mala nuna ashshidayine nuna bees duummathidi izi xeeyigides. He iza kiyatethay medhdhina wodepe kase Yesuss Kiristtoossa baggara nuus immettides.
2TI 1:10 Ha7i qass izi hayqqo wurssi dhaysidi miishshiracho qaala baggara nuna po7on keessida nu dhale Yesuss Kiristtoossa yuussan qonccides.
2TI 1:11 Takka hayssa ha miishshiracho qaala yoottizade, kiittetidadene asttamare gidada shuumettadis.
2TI 1:12 Ta meto beeyizaykka hessa gishiikko. Gidikkokka ta oona ammanizakkone tani ta ammanizade shaakka eriza gish izan yeellatikke. Ta izas immida hadara he gaallasiya gakkanaas izi naaganas danddaizayssa ta shaakka eradis.
2TI 1:13 Ne taape siyida timirtteza Yesuss Kiristtoosara issipetethan diza ammanonine siiqqon lemuso histtada oyykka.
2TI 1:14 Nees immettida lo7o hadara nunan diza xiillo ayyanan naaga.
2TI 1:15 Iisyya awurrajja garssan dizayti wurikka tana aggidayssa ne eraasa. Filggoossayine hermmogeneessay tana aggida asa garssan deettes.
2TI 1:16 Heneessifore soo asa Goday maaro, ayss giikko izi taana daro wode minthethidesinne; ta sanththalatan qachchista dishin tana beeyidi yeellatibeyina.
2TI 1:17 Harappekka izi Oroome yida wode tana kooy kooydi demmides.
2TI 1:18 Wurssetha pirda gallas Goday iza pirdafe ashsho. Izi tana Ehaaththaesoonen ay mala maaddidakkone ne lo7etha eraasa.
2TI 2:1 Hessa gish, ta naazo neni Goda Yesuss Kiristtoossa kiyatethan miinna.
2TI 2:2 Daro markkata sinththan ne taappe siyidayssa harata tamarssanas danddaizaytassine imettida asatas hadara imma.
2TI 2:3 Yesuss Kiristtoossas ammanettida loo7o woottadara mala tanara meto eekka.
2TI 2:4 Woottadaratethan oothizadey ba hallaqqa uhaaththaayssanas dafettes attin hara bena qaxethiza oothon gelli erena.
2TI 2:5 Hessathokka gaade wooxxizadey wooththa wooga naagontta wooxxiko xoono akiillile ekkena.
2TI 2:6 Gooba gooshshanchay ba goyi keessida kaatha xeera mizade gidanas beesses.
2TI 2:7 Ta nees gizayssa ne wozinan wootha siyiko Goday nees yoo wursson akekka immana.
2TI 2:8 Hayqqope denddida dawute zerethth gidida Yesuss Kiristtoossa qopa; ta yootiza miishshiracho qaalaykka hessakko.
2TI 2:9 Hessa geedon iita oothida asa mala qachchettana gakkanaas waaye beeyayss. Gido atin Xoossa qaalay qachchettena.
2TI 2:10 Hessa gish kiristtoossa baggara diza atottethinne medhdhina boncho deemmana doorettidayta gish gaada wurssakka dandda7adis.
2TI 2:11 Nu izara isfe hayqqikko qasse nu izara deyoon daana.
2TI 2:12 Dandda7an miinniko nu izara kawootana. nu iza kaadikko izikka nuna kaadana.
2TI 2:13 Nu izas ammanetonttayta giidikko izi medhdhinas ammanettida mala daana. izi berkka bena kaadana dandda7ena geetettida qaalay ammanettidayssa.
2TI 2:14 Hayta ha yoota gish asa qofisiso aggopa. asay ba garssan issay issara qaala geedon paalametontta mala Xoossa sunththan zora. Hessa mala yooy siyizayta moores.
2TI 2:15 Tumu Xoossa qaala yootizadene yeellachontta oothanchane asi ne gish loo7o markkattizade gidada nenateth wurssa Xoossa sinthth shiishshanas minna.
2TI 2:16 Coo mela duuna lalabetteththafe haakka. Hessa mala yoon waaxxettida asati Xoossafe haakki haakki beettes.
2TI 2:17 Istta timirttey sakkidi paxxontta gede gujji gujji daakketi biza madunththa malako. Heemenewoossane filxxoossa geetettizayti hessa mala timirtte tamarizayta garssan deettes.
2TI 2:18 Heyti tumateththape haakkidi coo mela waayetes. isttikka hayqqope denththi hayssafe kase hani adhdhides giidi issi issi asa ammano guye shiri yeeggettes.
2TI 2:19 Gido attin “Goday bees gidizayta erees” qassekka “Goda sunththu xeeyigizay wuri iitape haakko” giza maatamey iza bolla diza laamettontta Xoossa koyro qofay laametibeyina.
2TI 2:20 Issi gita keeththan worqqafene birape xaalla oothetidayti doontta miiththafene urqqafe oothetidayti dizayssatho heytanttafekka baggayti boncho oothos baggayti qass hiraaysso oothos ekkettettes.
2TI 2:21 Hessa gish oonkka hayta ta gida iita yootape bena geeshshiko he asi boncho oothosu gidizaadene anjjettidade, Goda goizaddene loo7o oothos giigettidade gidana.
2TI 2:22 Paanththatetha iita amotethafe baqqata. Geeshsha wozinara Goda xeeyigiza asatara xiilloteth, ammano, siiqqone saroteth kaalla.
2TI 2:23 Go7ayine birshechi bayindda paalammape haakka. Ayss giikko hessantta malay ooshshu kaalleththizayssa ne eraassa.
2TI 2:24 Goda oothanchay asara oyeettanas beessena. Hessafe asa wursso achchan kiya, asi tamarsanas dandda7izadene miino as gidanas beesses.
2TI 2:25 Izi benara eqqetiza asata ashshsiketethara oykkizade gidsanas beesses. Oonne erizay istti tuma erna mala xoossay isttas maarettanas wode immana danddaes.
2TI 2:26 Hesskka istti yuushi qoopi siimmidi iza shene kunththana mala istta di7i efida xaalae narqqafe istti keessi ekkana.
2TI 3:1 Gido attin wode wurssethan asi mettiza wodey yaanayssa ne erra.
2TI 3:2 Asay bena dosizade gidana, miishshe siiqqizayta, ceeqqettizayta, benan otoranchata, caashshanchata, nena yelidayttas azazetonttayta, galatoonttaytane geeshshateth bayinddayta,
2TI 3:3 Siiqqoy bayinddayta, atto gi maaronttayta, asa sunth morizayta, berkka bena naagonttayta, manxxa iita, loo7o miishshe dosonttayta,
2TI 3:4 Kaadizayta, nagetontayta, coo mela otorettethan puurdayta, Xoossafe aaththidi loo7o deeth dosizayta gidana.
2TI 3:5 Ammaniza asi milatanaashin ammanos diza wollqqa kaadana. Heyta malatappe ne haakka.
2TI 3:6 Heytantti issi issi keeth kolxx gelidi daro deexxo nagaranine duumma duumma iita ammotetha garss gelidi heene ha qaaxxiza ammano laafa maaccashshata qaxxi oykkettes.
2TI 3:7 Heyta mala maaccashshati wursso wode tamareetese shin tuma eri erettena.
2TI 3:8 Iyaneeseyine Iyanbbaaresey Muse bolla denddida mala haytikka istta qofay mooretin bees ammanope kunddida gish tumateth ixxettes.
2TI 3:9 Gido attin istta qofay kuumena. Gasooykka Iyaneessane Iyambbarasse eeyateth asas qoonccida malakka hayta hanoykka wurssos qonccana.
2TI 3:10 Ne gidikko ta timirtteza, ta duussa, ta waana qofa, ta ammanoza, ta dandda7a, ta siiqqozane ta miinnotetha wurssa ne eraassa.
2TI 3:11 Ta goodetethane ta waayeza anxxokiyan, iqoonyyonine lisxxirankka ta bolla gakkidayssa wurssa ta danddaidayssa ta goodetetha ne eraassa. Gidikkoka Goday hessa wurssofe tana ashshides.
2TI 3:12 Tumappe Yesuss Kiristtoossa geeshsha wozinape ammani daana gizayti wurkka goodetizayta gidana.
2TI 3:13 Iita baleththiza asati bees balettidi asa baleththishe iitatetha bolla iitateth gujji gujji baana.
2TI 3:14 Ne gidikko kase ne tamarada erida ogen miinna. Hessa oonappe tamardakkone ne eraassa.
2TI 3:15 Ne guutha naatethape ha7i gakkanaas Yesuss Kiristtoossa ammanon attottethi beettizayssane ciinccateth immiza geeshsha maxaafata lo7etha eraadasa.
2TI 3:16 Geeshsha maxaafati wurikka Xoossa ayyanay kalethin xafetidaytanne as tamarssanas, hanqqanassine suurssanas qassekka xiillotetha ogen kaallethanas go7ettes.
2TI 3:17 Hessikka Xoossa asi lo7o ootho wurssos beessizade gidana malakko.
2TI 4:1 Xoossa sinththanine hessathokka paxxa dizayta bollane hayqqidayta bolla pirdanas diza Yesuss Kiristtoossa sinththan iza qoonccethane iza kawootetha qofara hayssa nees hadara gaayss.
2TI 4:2 Qaala yoota; nees giigi woykko giigontta aggin ne ne baggara giiga utta. daro dandda7ara tamarththon asa suurssa; hanqqane miinisa.
2TI 4:3 Gasooykika asay wuri suure gidida timirtte ekkontta ixxana wodey yaana. Hessafe bollara asay ba amora gaaggizayssa istta hayththey siyana koyzayssa xaalla isttas yootana mala bena tamarththana daro asttamarista ba achchi shiishshana.
2TI 4:4 Tuma siyanape ba haythe haraso zaaradi haysu7e bagga simmana.
2TI 4:5 Ne gidikko haniza yoon wursson loodu ga; meto dandda7a; miishshiracho qaala yooto nees ootho histta; ne oothozakka poola.
2TI 4:6 Ta qass yarshistanas mata uttadis hayssa ha alamezape shaakkista buusa wodey taas gakkides.
2TI 4:7 Loo7o baaxxe ta baaxxistadis. Ta wooxxana woothe wurssadis. Ammanokka naagadis.
2TI 4:8 Akililey taas gigi utides, hessikka xillotetha. hessakka tumu pirdiza Goday he gallas taas immana. Hessikka taas xaalla gidontta iza yuussa laamotizaytas wurssotaskka immana.
2TI 4:9 Takko ellela yaanas nees danddaettida mala ootha.
2TI 4:10 Deemmassay hayssa alameza siiqqidi tana yeggi aggidi Tesolonqqe bides. Qerqqissay galatiya bides. Titoy gede Dalmmaxiya bides.
2TI 4:11 Luqaassay xaalla tanara dees. Marqqoossay tana oothon maadiza gish iza nenara ekka ya.
2TI 4:12 Tikiqosa Efesoone yeedadis.
2TI 4:13 Ne ha yashe ta Xiro7adan Akirphpha achchan woththida ta Maaqane xaaxetha maaxxafata harapekka galban xaafetida maaxxafata taas ekka ya.
2TI 4:14 Xarqimala qooxxiza Iskindiroossay ta bolla daro qoho gaathides shin goday izas iza ootho mala immana.
2TI 4:15 Izi nu yootiza qaala keezi ixxides. Nekka izappe naagista.
2TI 4:16 Tana mootiza yoozas koyro tana ashshana markka ta shiishshin oonkka tana maadana yibeyina. Gido attin wurkka tana yeeggidi bida. Hessakka istta bolla qoho ootha qoodopa.
2TI 4:17 Gido attin qaala kiittay ta baggara kumeth yootettana malane dere asay wuri siyana mala Goda ta achchan eqqidi tana miinssides. gaammo duunapekka ashshides.
2TI 4:18 Goday iita yoo wurssofe tana ashshana. Gede ba salo kawootethas tana sarora gaathana. izas medhdhinape medhdhina gakkanaas bonchoy gido; amminni7i.
2TI 4:19 Phirisqqilass, Aqqilas, Heneshaaththaore soo asasika ta sorokka gaatha.
2TI 4:20 Erisxxossay qooronttoossen attides. Xirofomoossay sakettida gish iza ta miliixen aggadis.
2TI 4:21 Balggoy gakkanape sinththistada taakko ha gakkanaas nees danddaettida mala ootha. Ewuguloos, phuudes, qassekka sinosay, qilawudiyayine ammanizayti wurkka nena saro saro gida.
2TI 4:22 Goday nenara gido. Goda kiyatteth intenara gido.
TIT 1:1 Xoossas doretidayta amanoninne tumu ayanan kallethiza tumma eratethan dichanamala Xoossa aylene Yesus Kirstosape kitetida Phawulosape.
TIT 1:2 Iza amanoyinne eratethay kaasepe ooykidi wordotonta Goday daro wodeppe kasse ba imida medhina deyo ufaysa malakko.
TIT 1:3 Izi kasse gidamala nuna ashida Xoossa azazon hadara imetida sabakon ba qaala qonccisides.
TIT 1:4 Nus kothe gidida tumu amanon ta na Titosas “Xoossa aawape nuna ashida Yesus Kiristossape kiiyatethane sarotethi nes giido.
TIT 1:5 Ta nena qarxxesen agiday burope giigana bessiza daro mishi diza gish ne gigsanamalane ta nena azazidamala katamay dizason wossa keeththa ciimata ne doranasa.
TIT 1:6 Cmatethan doristanayti ista bolla boroy bayndayta, isi machi azinata, nayti amanizaytane waysontayta woykko azazetiza nayta awata gideto.
TIT 1:7 Wossa keeththa ciimay Xoossas oothana hadara ekidade gididamala iza bolla wothay bayndade gidanas beses. Hesiikka ceqetizade, gutha miishan ylotizadene mathotizade, ushanchanne izas besonta ogera go7a gididaz godi eki bizade gidanas besena.
TIT 1:8 Hesafe bollara izi imath makiizade loo7o ootho dosizade berka bena hariizade sure as xiilone bes nagetizade gidanas beses.
TIT 1:9 Hara asata loo7o timrten miithethzadenne he loo7o timirteza ixizayta hanqanas ba tamaridamala qalan minizade gidanas beses.
TIT 1:10 Waysizaytine dunan xalala balethzayti daroti detes; harapekka heyti qaxaretida Ayhuda asatape ammanida asata bagatakko.
TIT 1:11 Heytanta co77u histethi beses. Gaasoyka isti besonta oogera bes go7a demanas besonta timrte tamarson keeththa asa wursi moron detes.
TIT 1:12 Ista Nabistappe isadey ista gish hasa7ishe “Qarxesa asay wuriso wode wordanchatane ita do7ota ganjjemane azalata” giides. f/ nabeza sunthi Epimenidese.
TIT 1:13 He markatethay tumu hessa gish ne ista loo7etha hanqista. Hesikka ista tumma amanoy danamalasa.
TIT 1:14 Ayhuddata haysu7e woykko tumu yooppe hakida asata azazo isti siyopetto.
TIT 1:15 Geshatas mishi wurikka geshsha shin tuatasinne amnontaytas gidikko wurikka tunakko. Harapekka ista qohaaththaaykka wurikka tunides.
TIT 1:16 Isti bena nu Xoosu eros getes shin ba hanotethan dikokka gidiko kadetes. Isti shunizayta, azazetontaytanne loo7o oothos besontaytakko.
TIT 2:1 Ne gidikko asa tumu gididaz tamarsa.
TIT 2:2 Cimma asay wozinama bonchetidayta bena berkka harizayta amanoninne siiqon danda7anka loo7o gidanamala ista zora.
TIT 2:3 Hesathoka cima maccashati bee diza dussan bonchora dizaytanne loo7o hanoteth asa tamarisizayta gideto attiin asa sunthu isizayta woykko woyne ush ussa suken waxetidayta gidonta mala ista tamarsa.
TIT 2:4 Hesatho oothikko natetha maccashati ba azinatane ba nayta dosanamala tamarsanas dandadha7etes.
TIT 2:5 Xoossa qalay oona achanka cayetontamala isti berikka bena harizaytane geshata keeththa gidon ista oothoy ooykidaytanne asas kiiyata ba azinatas azazetizayta giidanamala ciima maccashati ista tamariseto.
TIT 2:6 Hesathokka yalaga atumasay berka bena haranamala ne ista zaro.
TIT 2:7 Ay hanonkka ne asas loo7o lemuso gida. Ne asa tamarsiza timirteza nekka wozinape tamarisizadene nagizade gida.
TIT 2:8 Nu gish ita has7iza asay hasa7anas iita demonta agidi yelatanamala ne has7iiza hasa7a garsan borso yoy doppo.
TIT 2:9 Ayleti azanka ba Godatas haristanamalanne ufaysanamala qasekka awute zarontamala tamarisa.
TIT 2:10 Hanizazan wurison nuna ashida Xoossa timirtey dosistanamala isti loo7o markateth besanamala ba godata mishe kaysotopeto.
TIT 2:11 Asas izape maroy betiza Xoossa kiiyatethi asa wursos qonccides.
TIT 2:12 He kiiyatethaykka nuni nagaran dusune ha alame amotetha kadidi hayssa ha wodezan nurkka nuna haridine xiilotethan tumu ayana dus danaysa nuna tamarises.
TIT 2:13 Hesikka nus anjjetida ufays gidida woga Xoossane nuna ashida Yesus Korstosa bonchoy qooncanaysa naganasa.
TIT 2:14 Izikka nuna itetethafe wozanasinne loo7o oothanas miiniza ba dere bees doranas bena nus aathi iimides.
TIT 2:15 Hessa gish ne tamarsanayti heytanta. Hessakka ne kumetha Godatethara zoranne hanqqa nena oonikka kadhoppo.
TIT 3:1 Assay dere aysizaytas haristanamalane loo7o gidida miish wursi oothanas giga gidanamala asa qofissa.
TIT 3:2 Qasekka oonikka asa bollla iita hasa7ontamalane loo7o asa gidanamala asa wursos kumetha wozinappe ba ashketeth besanamala wuisa qofissa.
TIT 3:3 Nukka kasse qofay bayndaytane azazetontayta ne balletizayta duma duma amoninne loo7o dusas ayletethan haretizaytakko. Asarane nurka nu gasanka oyetishe itatethaninne miqaynetethan doos.
TIT 3:4 Gido attiin nuna ashida Xoossa kiiyatethinne iza siqqoy qonccida wode nu oothida xiilotethan gidonta dishin iza marotetha daron atidos, izi nuna ashiday nam7antho yeleteth gidida mechaninne Xiillo Ayanan ooraxetethankko.
TIT 3:6 Hesaka Xiillo Ayanay nu bolla nu Gooda Xoossi nuna ashida Yesus Kirstosa bagara keezi darsi gusides.
TIT 3:7 Hesikka nu iza kiiyatethan xillidi medhiina deyo ufays ooyki layzayta gdanasa.
TIT 3:8 Hesikka amanetida qaala. Xoossa amanizayti loo7o oothos bena aathi imanamala hayssa ubbaa ne lo7etha yotanamala ta koyays. Hesikka loo7one ay asika koyizaza.
TIT 3:9 Qassekka coo hada palamapenne asay ba qomo qodizazape, lalefenne woga gish dendiza ooshafe ne hakka. Heytanti go7oy baynda pathonta yokko.
TIT 3:10 Asa garsan shakoteth medhiza asa isi to nam7u to ne zorin ekonta ixxiko izadera nes ispetethi doppo.
TIT 3:11 Hesa mala asi baletida nagarancha asa izadey berkka ba bolla piirdidaysa ne era.
TIT 3:12 Arxximone woykko Tikiqosa ta neekko kiitikko ne tako Niqqoliyonne yanas nes danda7etizaz ubbaa ootha. Tani halaytha ballgo hen athana gada qachadis.
TIT 3:13 Woga eriza Zemasayne Aphillossay biishin istas koshzaz ubbaa kuntha mada.
TIT 3:14 Nu bagatas hachis hachis ista koshizaz isti demanamalane ista dethay goo7oy bayndaz gidontamala isti loo7o ootho oothi minanamala tamaranas koshes.
TIT 3:15 Tanara dizayti intena saro getes. Amano gedon nuna siiqqizayta wursi saro giite. Xoossa kiyatethi intenara gido.
PHM 1:1 Yesusi Kirstossa gish qachettida tappe Phawulossapenne nu isha Xiintossape nu siqqo isha gididi nunara issife oothiza Pllimonas.
PHM 1:2 Ne keeththan shiiqqiza ammaniza asasinne nu michchiyo Ampibyas qassekka nunara issife Kirstossa wotadara gidida Arkiiphasses;
PHM 1:3 Nu Aawa Xoossafe nu Goda YesusiKiristossape keeyatethinne sarotethi intes gido.
PHM 1:4 Ta ta wossan nena qopashe wuriso wode Xoossa galatayss.
PHM 1:5 Gaasoykka ne Xoossa asa siiqizaysanne Goda Yesusi Kiristossan ne ammanizaysa ta siyadis.
PHM 1:6 Nuni Kiristossas gididaysanne nuus diza loo7o yoy wuri qonccen eretana mala nekka ne ammano hara asas bessana mala ta nees miina wossayss.
PHM 1:7 Ta ishazo! ne hanon Xoossa asa wozinay ooraxxida gish ne siiqqoy ta wozina keehi miinisides.
PHM 1:8 Hessa gish ne oothanas besizayssa oothana mala nena azazanas taas Kirstosan xalateth deesikkoshin.
PHM 1:9 Gido attin ta nena azazanape siiqora wossayss. Gaasoykka tani Yesusii Kiristosa gish qachistada qasho keeththan diza phawulosakko.
PHM 1:10 Ta nena wossizay ta qasho keeththan dashe Yesusi Kirstosan yeellida na Anasimossa gishaskko.
PHM 1:11 Anasmossay hayssafe kasse nena go7iibeyna shin ha7i gidiko nenakka tanakka go7izadekko.
PHM 1:12 Ta ha7i iza neekko zara yedadis. Ta neekko yedizay iza gidontta ta wozina neekko zara yediza mala qoodayss.
PHM 1:13 Mishiracho qaala gaasotetha ta haan qachista dishin ne tana ootha maadana exxa izi tanara deyidakko tana ufaysses shin.
PHM 1:14 Gido attin ne loo7o oothoy ne dosanipe attin wolliqara gidonta mala gaada nena ooychonta aykokka oothana koyabeykke.
PHM 1:15 Anasmosay hano gakanaas neppe gutha wode shaketikokka oone erizay hayssafe guye wuriso wode nenara daana dandda7ees.
PHM 1:16 Hayssafe guye izi nenara daanay aylle mala gidontta ayllefe adhidi nees asho isha mala gidana. Izi taas dosetida ishakko. Gido attin izi nena oothi go7ana asi gidida gishinne izi nees Kirstossa baggara isha gidida gish nees keehi dosetidade gidana.
PHM 1:17 Nuus diza isipetetha gaason ne tana nees isha mala qoodiza giidikko tana ne mokka ekiiza mala izakka mokka ekka.
PHM 1:18 Izi ne bolla gathida qohoy dikko woykko ne accoy iza bolla dikko iza accoza ta bolla tayba.
PHM 1:19 Heko ta Pawulossay “Iza accoza ta nees qanxana” gaada ta kushera xafadis. Gidikokka ne Kiristossa ammaniday ta baggara gidida gish haray attoshin nekka taas qanxana accoy dizade gididayssa ta nena erissanas koshena.
PHM 1:20 Hi7a ta ishazo heesa loo7o ootho ne taas oothana mala Goda sunthan Kirstossa gish gaada ne ta wozina shempisana mala nena wossayss.
PHM 1:21 Ta nees hayssa xahaaththaiday ne taas azazistanaysa ammanadako. Ta nena ooychidayssafe ne aatha oothonayssa ta erayss.
PHM 1:22 Xoossi inte wossa siydi ta inteko yanadan oothana mala taas ufayssi diza gish ta baada intekon shempanaso taas hayana giigissa.
PHM 1:23 Yesusi Kiristossa gaason tanara qachettida Ephafiray nena saro gees.
PHM 1:24 Hesathokka tanara oothizayti Marqqosay Aristirokosay Demassaynne Luqassay nena saro geettes.
PHM 1:25 Goda Yesusi Kistossa kiiyatethi intenara gido.
HEB 1:1 Beni wodepe oykidi Xoossi dumma dumma ogera nabeta baggara kase nu Aawatas daro wode yootides.
HEB 1:2 Qasse hayssa wurisetha wode bolla wursi latisidane ha alameza midhida ba naaza baggara nuusu yootides.
HEB 1:3 Izika Xoossa boncho po7osine Xoossa xoossatethas lo7o lemuso gididi ba wolliqama qaalan wursika shiishi oykides. Izi asa nagarape geeshidape guye salon boncho Xoossa oshachan uttides.
HEB 1:4 Hessa gishshi laattida sunthay kiitanchata sunthafe adhdhizayssa mala izika kiitanchatape keehi adhdhees.
HEB 1:5 Xoossi kiitanchape “Neni ta nako, Ta nena hachchi yeladis.” Woyko qasseka Ta izas Aawa gidana; Izika ta ta gidana” Oonas gidee?
HEB 1:6 Qasseka Xooss ba bayra naaza duge ha biitta yeddishe “Xoossa kiitanchati wurikka izas goyneto” gides.
HEB 1:7 Kiitanchata gishshi hasa7ishe qasse “Kiitanchata ayanata; Be oothanchataka tama laco kesses” gees.
HEB 1:8 Nza gishshi qasse “Godo ne zupaney medhinape medhina gakanas minni deyana. Neni ne kawotetha like kaalethasa.
HEB 1:9 Neni xiillotehta dosadasa. Makal7aka ixxasa. Hessa gishshi Xoossi ne Goday nena ne lagistape bolla kessides. Nena ufayssa zayte tiyides.
HEB 1:10 Qasse hizgees “Godo neni koyro biitta medhadasa. Salo tika ne kushen oothetida.
HEB 1:11 Istti dhayana, neni gidiko minna deyana. Istti wurikka mayo mala gal7ana.
HEB 1:12 Neni istta mayo mala qalam77ana. Isttika mayo mala laamistana. Ne gidiko aydeka neni nena. Ne duusas wurisethi deena” gees.
HEB 1:13 Xoossi kiitanchatape “Tani ne morketa ne too garisan nena yedhisana gakanas ne ta oshachan utta” Oona gidee?
HEB 1:14 Kiitanchati wurikka atotetha laatana asatas oothanas Xoossafe kiitetiza oothancha ayana gidetenee?
HEB 2:1 Hessa gishshi nuni siyda qaalape balettidi kundontta mala nu siyida qaala lo7ethi naagans besses.
HEB 2:2 Azas gikko kase kitanchata bagara yotetida qalay tumu gidida he qaala yedhi adhiday bees bessiza qixate ekees.
HEB 2:3 Nu qase hessa mala gita maaroteth coo leppi hisitko waani attanee? Hayssi maarotethay koyro Goda baggara nuusu yootetides. Izape siyidaytika nuusu geeshi yootida.
HEB 2:4 Xoossi qasseka malatata, malalithiza miishata, dumma dumma malatata oothonine ba shene mala immida xiillo ayana imotata baggara istta markatethaa minithides.
HEB 2:5 Xoossi hayssa nu iza gishshi hasa7iza buro yaana alameza kiitanchas harisibeyna.
HEB 2:6 Gido attin geisha maxaafay harason hizigdes “Ne izas yuusha qopanas asi aazee? Izas ne qopanas asanay izi aazee?
HEB 2:7 Ne iza kiitanchatape guuth wodes guuthadasa. Boncho zawudene galata iza hu7en wothadas.
HEB 2:8 Ne wursaka iza too garisan haarisadasa. Xoossi wursika izape garisara izas harisishin attiday ay miishika deena. Gido attin ha7i qasse wurikka izas haretishin nu beyok.
HEB 2:9 Gido attin Xoossa kiyatethan asa wuriso gishshi hayqanas kiitanchatape guutha wode guuxida Yesusay waaye hayqo hayqidi ha7i bonchone galata zawude ba hu7en wothidayssa beyosu.
HEB 2:10 Hanzay wurikka izape izas medhetida Xoossi daro nayta bonchoso efanas istta marotethas hu7e gidida Yesusay waayen polanas koshizazi giddies.
HEB 2:11 As geeshizayinne izan geeyiza asay heyti issi keeththa aseko. Hessa gishshi Yesusay istta ba ishata gi xeyganas yellatena.
HEB 2:12 “Tani ne sunththan ta ishatas yootana shiiqida dere sinthan nena galatiza yethi ta yexana.”
HEB 2:13 Hessaththoka “Ta izan ammanetana” qasseka “Tanane taas Xoossi immida nayti nu handes” gees geesha maxaafay.
HEB 2:14 Nytas ashoyne suthi diza mala izika istta mala aseko. Hessika hayqo bolla izas wolqay diza dabulosa izi ba hayqo wolqan zaaranas.
HEB 2:15 Hessaththoka ba diza wode wurison hayqos babon hareti qachetidayta hayqope wozanaskko.
HEB 2:16 Izi ha yiday kiitanchata maadanas gidonta Abirame zerethista maadanas yides.
HEB 2:17 Hesa gishshi wuriso baggara izi ba ishata milatanas besizade gidides. Izi hessa oothiday maarizadene ammanetida waana qesse halaqa gididi Xoossas oothanasine dereza nagarape maaranaskko.
HEB 2:18 Izi ba hu7en pacetidi meto ekkida gishshi paccetizayta maadanas danda7es.
HEB 3:1 Hessa gishshi salope xeyisi intena gakin ammaniza nu ishato nu ammanos hawarene qessista halaqa Yesusa qopite.
HEB 3:2 Musey Xoossa keethe wuriso bolla ammanetidade gidida mala Yesusaykka bena shuumidades ammanetidadeko.
HEB 3:3 Keethe kexxidades keethefe bollara bonchoy diza mala Yesusaska Musepe adhdhiza bonchoy besizade gidanas besses.
HEB 3:4 Keethe wurisoska kexxidadey dees. Gido attin wuriska oothidadey Xoossaa.
HEB 3:5 Musey buro hananayssa markatishe Xoossa keeththa wuriso bolla issi ammanetida oothancha mala gidi de7ides.
HEB 3:6 Kiristoosay gidiko Xoossa keeththa bolla ammanetida na malako. Nunika iza bolla ammanetiza ufayssayne ceeqetiza ufaysi lo7ethi oykiko nu izaso duusa keeth gidos.
HEB 3:7 Hessa gishshi xiillo ayanay giza mala “Inte hachchi iza qaala siyiko
HEB 3:8 Bazzo biittan inte tana paacida wode makalidayssatho inte wozina muumisopite.
HEB 3:9 Inte Aawati kase heen tana paccidane tanara eqetida. Ta oothidayssa wuris oyddu tammu laytha gakanas be7ida” gees Xooss.
HEB 3:10 “He wode yeletethata bolla ta hanqistada <Istta wozinay wuriso wode baletes; Istti ta oge eribeytena> gadis”
HEB 3:11 Qasse “<Ta isttas immiza shemposo istti muleka geletena!> gaada tan ta hanqon caaqadis.
HEB 3:12 Ta ishato intefe oonikka deyo Xoossafe haraso intena haasiza iittane ammanontta wozinay dontta mala naagetite.
HEB 3:13 Harapeka inte garisafe oonikka nagaran baletidi ba wozina muumisontta mala “Hachchi” geetetishin hachchi hachchi inte inte garisan minetite.
HEB 3:14 Nuusi kase koyrope diza ammano nuni wuriseth gakanas lo7ethi minthi oykiko nuni kiristoosara issife laatana.
HEB 3:15 Hessika “Inte hachchi iza qaala siyiko kase makal7idaysssa mala ha7ika inte wozina inte minthontta mala” geeteti geisha maxaafan xaafetidayssatho hanana.
HEB 3:16 Siyidi makal7idayti istti oonanitee? Musey Gibixefe kaaleth kessidayta wurisota gidetee?
HEB 3:17 Xoossi istta bolla oyddu tammu laytha hanqettidayti istti oonanitee? Nagara oothin istta ahay bazzo biittan kundi attidayta gidetenee?
HEB 3:18 Izas azazetontta ixxidaytape attin iza shemposo gelontta mala izi caaqi digiday haray oonanitee?
HEB 3:19 Hessa gishshi istti gelontta attiday ammanoy baynda gishshi gididayssa nu erosu.
HEB 4:1 Gede shemposo gelanas immetida ufaysay ha7ika naageti diza gishshi inte gidofe oonikka hessas besonttade gidontta mala ane naagetos.
HEB 4:2 Heytanttas sabaketid mala nuusika mishshiracho qaalay sabakettides. Gidikoka siyida asatas siyida qaalay ammanon walaketontta aggida gishshi istta maadibeyna.
HEB 4:3 Nu qasse ammanizayti he shempo sooza gelana. Xoossi “Hessa gishshi tani ta hanqon <Istti ta shemposo muleka geletena> gaada ta caaqadis” gides. Gido attin hayssi alamey medhetosope ha simmin iza oothoy poletides.
HEB 4:4 Issi son lapunththo gallas agishshi “Lapunththo galasi Xoossi ootho wurisofe shempides” geeteti geisha maxaafan xaafetides.
HEB 4:5 Qasseka he sozan “tumappe istti ta shemposo muleka geletena” gees.
HEB 4:6 Iza shemposo buro gelana issi issi asati deetes. Kase isttas mishshiracho qaalay sabaketidayti azazetontta ixxida gishshi iza shemposo istti gelibeytena.
HEB 4:7 Hessa gishshi Xoossi “Hachchi” giidi qasseka hara gallas wothides. Hessika aro laythatape guye Dawite baggara “Hachchi inte iza qaala siyiko inte wozina muumisopite” geeteti kase yootetida mala hanides.
HEB 4:8 Iyaasoy isttas shempo immidako Xoossi hara gallas giidi yootenakoshin.
HEB 4:9 Hessa gishshi sambata gallas shempoy Xoossa deres ha7ika dees.
HEB 4:10 Gaasoyka Xoossa shemposo gelizay wuri Xoossi oothi shempida mala izika ba oothope shempana.
HEB 4:11 Hessa gishshi oonikka heytantta mala azazetontta ixxidayssa lemuso kaallidi kundontta mala he shemposoyo gelanas ane minos.
HEB 4:12 Xoossa qaalay paxxa dizayssane oothiza qaalako. Nam77u bagga qara mashafeka adhdhi qara; Shempone ayana; shayane qinccifileka shaakana gakanas caades. Wozina qofane amotethaka paaci xeeles.
HEB 4:13 Xoossa ayfefe geemetida medhetay muleka deena. Nu izas nu gishshi malithe immanas bessiza iza sinthan hanoy wurikka qonccen kallo dees.
HEB 4:14 Hessa gishshi pude salo bida qessista halaqa Xoossa na Yesusay nuus diza gishshi ane nuni nu ammano minthi oykosu.
HEB 4:15 Nu daburishin nuus qadhetana danda7iza qessista halaqay nuusu dees. Izi nu mala wuriso mishshan paaacetides. Gidikoka izi ayko nagaraka oothibena.
HEB 4:16 Hessa gishshi nuni maarotethi ekanasine nuna koshiza wode nuna maadiza iza kiyateth nu demmana mala gede iza maarotetha aliggako ane ammanon shiiqos.
HEB 5:1 Qessata halaqa gidi shuumetiza uray daro asa gidofe dooretesine asa gishshi gididi imotanne nagara gishshi yarsho shiishanas dooretes.
HEB 5:2 Izika ba baggara daburachcha gidida gishshi erontta asatasine oge balidaytas qadhetana danda7es.
HEB 5:3 Izi ba nagara gissine hara asata nagara gishshi yarsho shiishanas izas bessizay hessa gishshiko.
HEB 5:4 Aroney xeyigetidayssatho izi Xoossi xeyigidade gidanas besses attin hessa he bonchoza berika bess ekiza uray deena.
HEB 5:5 Hessaththoka kiristoosay qessista halaqa gidana boncho berika bees ekibeyna. Gido attin “Ne ta naako; Ta nees hachchi Aawa gidadis” gida Xoossafe ekides.
HEB 5:6 Hessaththoka haraso “Malke-xedeqe shuumista mala neni medhinas qessista halaqako” gees.
HEB 5:7 Yesusay hayssa biitta bolla diza wode iza hayqope ashana danda7izayssako ayfunxishe gita qaalara woossa woossides. Addafe ashiketethara izi azazetida gishshi iza woossay izas siyettides.
HEB 5:8 Izi Xoossa na gidikkoka ba ekida waayezape azazeteth tamarides.
HEB 5:9 Hessa baggara pacey bayndade gidi beetidayssafe guye bena azazetizaytas wurisos medhina atotethas gaaso gidides.
HEB 5:10 Malke-xadiqe shuumetetha mala qessista halaqa geeteti Xoossan shuumetides.
HEB 5:11 Hessa gishshi nu hasa7ana miishey buro daroy dees. Gido attin inte dota7ata gidida gishshi intena erisoy metoko.
HEB 5:12 Inte hanni wode asitamare gidanas bessishin Xoossa qaala buro koyrope denthi intena tamarisiza asi intes koshshena. Intes koshizay mino kathi gidontta maathiko.
HEB 5:13 Maathi pahetizay qii guutha na gidiza gishshi lo7one iitta shaakiza timirtte shaaki erena.
HEB 5:14 Mino kathi gidiko lo7one iitta shaakanas benatetha dosisida wozina kunththida asatasiko
HEB 6:1 Hessa gishshi koyrope kiristoosa gishshi immetida timirtteza aggidi ane gede mino timirtteko boosu. Hayqida oothope maarotethan gelo gishshine Xoossan ammano gishshi buro ane izan wodhdhi maadhokko.
HEB 6:2 Hessaththoka xinqqate gishshine kushe asa bolla wotho gishshi qasseka hayqidayata dentha gishshine medhina pirida gishshi buro wothi demoko.
HEB 6:3 Xoossa shene gidiko nu hessaththo oothana.
HEB 6:4 Be ammano kaddida asata istta maarotethan wositti zoranee? Po7oy isttas issi to po7idayta salo imotetha ekki be7idayta xiillo ayana ekki be7idayta;
HEB 6:5 Lo7o Xoossa qaalane buro yaana alameza woliqa ekki be7idayta;
HEB 6:6 Zaaridi kadidayti istta nam77antho zaaridi maarotethin ekoy danda7etena. Gaasoy istti ba mooros Xoossa na zaari kaqetesine kawushetes.
HEB 6:7 Wuriso wode ba bolla ira uyza biittay qesseka iza goyzadey ayfe immiza biittayaka Xoossa achchan anjjistadus.
HEB 6:8 Gido attin agunthune caca mokisiza biittay go7ay baydaro gidana. He biittays qangetethi matan dees. Izi wurisethi taman xuugeteth gidana.
HEB 6:9 Ta ishato nuni hessaththo hassa7ikoka intes inte atotethara oyketida lo7o miishey dizayssa nu sidhoko.
HEB 6:10 Kase gidin woykko ha7i gidinka inte ammanizayta maadidayssane iza suntha gishshi inte bessida siiqotetha balanas Xoossi makal7ancha gidena.
HEB 6:11 Immetida ufayssay polistana gakanas intefe issi issi uray hessa mala ootho wuriseth gakanas genccidi oothana mala nu amotoos.
HEB 6:12 Ammanonine danda7an inte iza ufayssa qaala laatizayta milatanape attin dota7ata gidanayssa nu koyoko.
HEB 6:13 Xoossi Abirames ufayssi immida wode caaqishe hara izape adhiza uray baynda gishshi berika benan hizgiza caaqides. “Ta nena tumape anjjana; tan e zeres darisana.”
HEB 6:15 Abirameyka gencci naagidape kaalidi izas immetida ufayssa demmides.
HEB 6:16 Asay caaqo caaqishe beepe dhoqan caaqees. Caaqozika geetetidayssi poletena mala minthiza gishshi caaqidayta gidon palamay dendiko kase caaqo qaalay digees.
HEB 6:17 Xoossi laametontta ba qofa ufayssa qaala laatanaytas qonccisana mala koyda gishshi caaqo qaalan minthides.
HEB 6:18 Xoossi ay wodeka woridotena; danda7ena. Izi laametontta nam77u miishatan nu sinththan diza ufayssa oykanas izako shiiqida nuusu gita minoteth nu demmana mala oothides.
HEB 6:19 Nuka shempo teqe gidida minone ammanithiza ufayss demmides. He ufayssayka magalashazape guye baggara gede Xoossa keeththa gido gelees.
HEB 6:20 He sozika nu gishshi Yesusay kaseti gelida sooko. Izika Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha mala medhinas qessista halaqa gidides.
HEB 7:1 Hessi malke-xedeqey saleme kawone Xoossa qesseko; Izika Abiramey kawota oli xoonidi simmishin demmidi Abirame anjjides.
HEB 7:2 Abirameykabess diza wurisofe tammu kushepe issi kushe izas immides. Koyro iza sunthas birshechi “Xiillo kawo” guusako. Kaallidi qasse “Saleme kawo” guusi “sarotetha kawo” guusuko.
HEB 7:3 Izas Ayaka Aawayka woykko iza yeletethas zarikeyka baawa. Izi ayde yeletidi, ayde hayqidakone eretibynna. Izas doomethine wurisethi baawa. Gido attin Xoossa na mala medhinas izi qesse gididi dess.
HEB 7:4 Ane inte izi aymala gitakone qopite. Haray attoshin Aawatas wurisos koyroy Abiramey ba di7i ekkidayssa wurisofe tammafe issa kessi immides.
HEB 7:5 Isttas qessetethi immetida Lewe nayti istta ishati Abirame zerethata gidikkoka derape hessika ba ishatape tammafe issa ekkana mala isttas wogan azazetides.
HEB 7:6 Hayssa ha addeza zerethi Lewe zereth gidena. Gido attin izi Abiramepe tammafe issa ekkides. Kase izas ufayssa qaalay immetida Abirame anjjides.
HEB 7:7 Bayray kaallo anjjizayss wogako.
HEB 7:8 Issi baggara tammafe issa ekkizayti hayqizaytako. Hara baggara qasse tammafe issa ekkizadey hayqontta paxa diza mala izas marikatidadey malke-xedeqeko.
HEB 7:9 Haray attoshin Leweyka Abirame baggara tammafe issa kessides gaanas danda7etes.
HEB 7:10 Gaasoyka malke-xedeqey Abirame gaagiza wode Lewey buro ba Aawa Abiramepe yeletibeyna.
HEB 7:11 Paacey baynda poloy bettidayne wogay derezas immetiday Lewe qesetetha mala gididako Aaroone mala gidontta Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha malay hara qessey yaanas aazas koshidee?
HEB 7:12 Qessetetha zarikey laametiza wode wogayka laamistanasi attontta miisheko.
HEB 7:13 Hessi wurikka izas yootetida qessey izi hara zerethiko. Iza zereththafe ooinka yarshoson oothi erizadey baawa.
HEB 7:14 Ne Goday Yuda baggafe yidayssi tumoko. Musey qessista gishshi yootishe ha zeretha gishshi yootidayssi issi mishshika baawa.
HEB 7:15 Malke-xedeqe malay hara qessey dendiko nu kase yootida yoy daro qoncce gidena.
HEB 7:16 Izi qesse gididay dhayontta deyo wolqan attin zereththafe yida wogafe gidena.
HEB 7:17 Izas hizgi markatides “Ne Malke-xedeqe shuumetetha mala medhinas qesseko”
HEB 7:18 Kase azazoy laafane go7ontayssa gidida gishshi attides.
HEB 7:19 Wogay oonaka geeshanas danda7ontta gishshi nu Xoossa achchi shiiqanas izape adhdhiza hara ufayssi nuusu yides.
HEB 7:20 Hessika caaqoy baynda hanbeyna. Hanko Qesse gididayti caaqoy bayndaytako.
HEB 7:21 Izi gidiko qessetetha caaqon ekkides. Gaasoyka Xoossi iza gishshi hizigides “Goday caaqides, ba qofa izi laamena, <Ne medhinas qesse.”>
HEB 7:22 Hessa mala caaqope dendidayssan Yesusay hessafe adhdhiza caaqo qaalas waase giddies.
HEB 7:23 Kase qesseti ba oothon sinthe gujjontta mala hayqoy istta digida gishshi qooday isttas darooko.
HEB 7:24 Yesusay gidiko medhinas dizade gidida gishshi iza qessetethi shaaretontta qessetethiko.
HEB 7:25 Hessa gishshi izi istta gigissana cimatishe wuriso wode hayqontta paxa eqqi diza gishshi iza baggara Xoossako yizayta wursi ashanas danda7es.
HEB 7:26 Hessa gishshi nuusi koshshsiza qeessista halaqay hessa mala geeshine wothoy iza bolla baynda xiillone nagaranchatape shaaketidi salotape bollara bonchetida qessata halaqako.
HEB 7:27 Izi hanko qessata halaqata mala koyro ba nagara gishshi qasseka kaalethidi hanko dereza nagara gishshi gallas gallas yarsho shiishanas iza koshshena. Izi bena aathi immida wode asa nagara gishshi issi too sinththa baggassara yarsho wu wursi polides.
HEB 7:28 Wogay daburancha asata qessatas waana halaqa hisiti shuumes. Wogape kaallidi yida caaqo qaalay gidiko medhinas iza bolla wothoy baynda naaza shuumides.
HEB 8:1 Hessa gishshi nu ha7i oothana waana yoy hayssako. Hayssa mala salo bolla Xoossa boncho aliga oshachan uttida qessista halaqay nuus dess.
HEB 8:2 Izi asi tokkida dunkkane gidon oothizade gidontta Godaa Xoossay tokkida tumu dunkanen geeshason oothizadeko.
HEB 8:3 Qessista halaqay shuumetizay asay Xoossas immizayssasa Xoossas shiishanasine yarsho yarshanasko. Hessa gishshi hayssi ha qessata halaqayka Xoossas shiishanas issi shiishiza miishi izas koshees.
HEB 8:4 Izi biitta bolla dizako qesse gidena. Aazas giiko wogay giza mala yarsho shiishiza hara qesseti dettes.
HEB 8:5 Istti kase salon diza Xoossa keethays lemusone eeshoko. Musey Dunkaaneza oothana gishshin “Nees zuma bolla qonccidayssatho wursa oothanas naagista” giza azazoy hessa gishshi izas immetides.
HEB 8:6 Gido attin Yesusay gido geli cimatiza caaqo qaalay kaseyssafe adhizayssa mala izi ekkida oothoyka kaseyta oothope aadhes. Hesssika kaseyssafe lo7iza ufayssa qaalanko.
HEB 8:7 Kase caaqo qaalan paacey bayndako nam77anththo hara caaqanas koshenashin.
HEB 8:8 Gido atin Xoossi dereza bolla paacey dizayssa demmida gishshi hizges “Isiraa7eele asarane Yuda asara tani oratha caaqo caaqetana wodey yaana” gees Goday.
HEB 8:9 “Hessika ta istta Gibixepe kesanas istta kushe oykkada kase istta Aawatara paaceti qaala mala gidena. Gaasoyka istti kase ta caaqo qaalan eqqibeytena. Taka istta yeda bessadis” gees Goday.
HEB 8:10 “Hessafe guye Isiraa7eele asara ta caaqetana qaaalay hayssa malako gees Goday. tani ta woga istta wozinan wothana. Istta wozina bollaka xaafana. Ta istta Xoossu gidana. Isttika tad ere gidana.
HEB 8:11 Hayssafe guye asi ba guta asa woykko ba isha <Ne Goda era> gi tamarsena. Gaasoyka asi guuthatethafe gitata gakanas wurikka tana erana.
HEB 8:12 Istta qohoza ta maarana. Hayssafe sinththan ta asa nagara nam77antho zaara qopike.”
HEB 8:13 Hayssa ha caaqoza izi “Orath” giidi kase caaqoza gali7a kessides. Hessa gishshi gali7idi wuridayssi dhayana wodey matides.
HEB 9:1 Koyro caaqo qaalazan Xoossas goyniza wogayne biitta bolla diza Xoossa keethey dees.
HEB 9:2 Kse nam77u kifilera diza dunikaney giigeti dees. Koyro kifilezan xomippe wothosoyne xaraphezay qasse ukethi dees. Hessa he kifilezi dumma kifile geetets.
HEB 9:3 Nam77antho kifiley nam77antho magalashape guye baggara diza kifiley wurisofe dumma geetetes.
HEB 9:4 Hessa gidon worqqafe oothetida exane cu7asiza pili7o malayne worqqan meeshettida caaqo Taabootay dees. He tabotayka iza gidon man7ay diza worqqa leematey, cililida Aaroone gufeyne caaqo qaalati iza bolla xaafetida shuchcha masethi dees.
HEB 9:5 He tabotaza bolla diza nagarape maarotetha kamaza bolla ba qefera kammiza boncho Kurubeti detes. Ha7i qasse nu heytantta issa issa gishshi shaaki shaaki hasa7anas danda7oko.
HEB 9:6 Wurika hessaththo giigetidape guye qesseti ba ootho polanas dunkanas koyro kifile geletes.
HEB 9:7 Gidikoka wurisofe gidotiza kifile qessista halaqay xalala gelees. Hessika layththan issi to xalala gidishin izi ba nagara gishine derey erontta oothida nagara gishshi shiishiza yarsho suuthu oykontta muleka galena.
HEB 9:8 Koyro dunkanezi kase diza wode gede wurisofe dumma geetettizaso efiza ogey he wode qoncce gidonttayssa xiillo ayanay besses.
HEB 9:9 Hessika hayssa ha wodezas lemuso gidishin kase shiqiza yarshotine coo immetiza imotati immizayta wozina shempisanasine mule geeshanas danda7ibeytena.
HEB 9:10 Heytanti wurikka oratha wogay yaana gakanas coo mela duuna hasa7a malako. Qasseka istti muusa gishshine usha gishshi qasseka dumma dumma geesho wogata xalalako.
HEB 9:11 Gidikoka Kiristoosay burope yaanas diza lo7o miishshatas qessista halaqa gididi qonccides. Izi izan gelida dunikanazi gitane geeshiko. He dunkanazi asa kushen oothetonttayssane hayssa ha medhetethafe gidena.
HEB 9:12 Izi he dunikanezan gelishe deyshata suuthune mirgo boorata suuthu ekki gelibeyna. Gido attin ase ashanas medhinas ba suuthu ekkidi wurisofe dumma geetettiza kifile hara wode nam77antho elontta mala wurisetha gelo gelides.
HEB 9:13 Isttas kare bagga asatethay tunida asata bolla araciza deysha suuthune mirgo boorata suuthu hessathoka yarshos xugettida ussa bidinththi istta geeshizayssa gidiko
HEB 9:14 Medhina ayanan bena wothoy baynda yarsho oothi Xoossas shiishida kiristoosa suuthi nuni deyo Xoossas goynanas hayqetha oothope nuna ay mala aaththi geeshandee?
HEB 9:15 Hessa gishshi xeygetidayti isttas immana geetetida medhina biitta ekkana mala kiristoosay oratha caaqo cimattizade gidides. Koyro caaqoza garisan diza wode istti oothida nagarape geeyana mala istta gishshi izi hayqides.
HEB 9:16 Bazay bazetizayssa gidiko bazidade hayqo shaaki eranas besses.
HEB 9:17 Gaasoyka bazay minnizay bazidadey haqinko. Bazidadey paxa dishin bazay aykoka oothena.
HEB 9:18 Hessa gishshi koyro caaqo qaalay suuthi baynda minnibeyna.
HEB 9:19 Musey ba azazo woga deras yooti simmidi deyshata suuthu mirgo boorata suuthu haathara ekkidi zo7o ithiken ecere wurice mala hesophe geetettiza miththara ekkidi ba xaafida woga maxaafa bollane dereza bolla wuuxides.
HEB 9:20 “Inte naagana mala inten Xoossi azazida caaqo qaala suuthay hayssako” gides.
HEB 9:21 Hessaththoka dunikanezane iza gidon diza ootho miisha wursi suuthu iza bolla wuuxides.
HEB 9:22 Addafeka guutha mishshati attishin hankko daro miishay suuthan geeyanas bessizayssa wogay azazes. Suuthi gukontte dishin maaroy baawa.
HEB 9:23 Hessa gishshi salo miishshatas lemuso gididayti haytanttan geeyanays attenashin. Salon diza mishshati gidiko hayssafeka adhiza yarshon geeyanas besse.
HEB 9:24 Kiristoosay tumu dunikaneyss lemusone asa kushen oothetida Xoossa keeth gelibeyna. Gido attin ha7i nu gishshi Xoossa sinththan bettanas pude salo gelides.
HEB 9:25 Qessista halaqay ba suuthu gidontta suuthu ekkidi laythan laythan wurisofe dumma kifile gelizayssatho kiristoosay bena yarshanas pude salo shiretti shiretti gelibeyna.
HEB 9:26 Hessa mala gidizako kiristoosay alamey medhetosope haa simmin daro wode meto ekkanas besses. Ha7 qasse wode wurisethan bena yarshidi nagara diganas wurisethas issi to qonccides.
HEB 9:27 Hessathokka asi issi to hayqees. Hessafe kaallidi pirida sinththan eqanas giigi uttides.
HEB 9:28 Kiristoosay daro asa nagara diganas issi to yarshetides. Nam77anthoka izi qonccana. Hessi iza naagizaytas atotethi ekki yaanas attin nam77antho zaari nagara tookanas gidena.
HEB 10:1 Muse wogay buro sinththara yaana lo7o hanotas Eshoope attin tumu adda medhay izas deena. Hessa gishshi laythan laythan paacey baynda shiri shiri shiishiza yarshoy Xoossu goynanas shiqiza asa geeshanas muleka danda7ibeyna
HEB 10:2 Asa mulera geeshana danda7izayssa gididako istti yarsho yarshanayssa aggagetenee? Qasseka Xoossu goynana shiiqiza asay issito geyizako ba wozinara nagarancha gididayssa sidhanakoshin.
HEB 10:3 Gido attin heyti yarshoti layhtan laythan nagara zaari zaari qofisitees.
HEB 10:4 Gaasoyka mirgotane deyshata suuthu asape nagara diganas danda7ena.
HEB 10:5 Hessa gishshi kiristoosay hayssa ha alameza yidi hizgides “Neni imotane yarsho koyabeyke shin ne taas nena giigisadasa.
HEB 10:6 Taman xuugettiza yarshone nagara gishshi shiiqiza yarshon ufa7istabeyka.
HEB 10:7 He wode tani hizgadis “Ta gishshi geisha maxaafan xaafetida mala <Xoosso hekko ta ne shene oothanas yadis” > gadis.
HEB 10:8 Muse wogay hessi hessaththo hanana mala azazikoka izi qasse koyro “Yarsho, imota, xuugettiza yarshone nagara gishshi shiiqiza yarsho ne koyabeykane izan ufa7istabeyka” gees.
HEB 10:9 Kaallethidika “Hekko ta ne shene oothana yadis” gides. Nam77anthoza esanas koyroyssa diggides.
HEB 10:10 Hayssa ha “iza shene” giza qaala mala hara yarsho zaarethi shiishanas koshontta mala Yesus kiristoosa baggara issi to shiiqida yarshon geeydosu.
HEB 10:11 Qessey hachchi hachchi eqqidi ba ootho polees. Ase nagarape geeshanas danda7onttayata wonttin wonttin shiishes.
HEB 10:12 Kiristoosay gidiko yarsho issito medhinas gidanayssa shiishidi Aawa oshachan uttides.
HEB 10:13 He gallasafe simmin iza morketi iza to garisan yedhistana gakanas naagon dees.
HEB 10:14 Gaasoyka issi to shiishida yarshon geyana asata medhinas geeshides.
HEB 10:15 Hessa he hanoza gishshi xiillo ayanayka nuusi marikatees. Koyro hizgees
HEB 10:16 “Hessafe guye ta isttara gelana caaqo qaalay hayssako gees Goday Ta woga ta istta wozinan wothana. Istta Wozinan ta xaafana.
HEB 10:17 Qasseka “Ta istta nagarane makal7a nam77antho qopike” gees Goday.
HEB 10:18 Heytantti wurikka atto geetetidape guye nam77antho nagara nagara hara shiiqana yarshoy deena.
HEB 10:19 Hessa gishshi ta ishato nuni Yesus kiristoosa suutha baggara gede wurisofe dumma geeshi geetettizasoyo gelanas xalateth demmidosu.
HEB 10:20 Hessika magalasha baggara; hessika izi ba asho baggara nuusu doyida orathine deyo gidida ogenkko.
HEB 10:21 Xoossa keeththa bolla shuumetida qessista halaqay nuusu diza gishshi
HEB 10:22 nuni nu iitta qofape geeyanas nu wozina aracetidi nu asatethaka xiillo haathan meecetidi tumu wozinapene kumetha ammanon Xoossako ane shiiqo
HEB 10:23 Nuusu ufayssa qaala immidadey ammanetizade gidida gishshi nuni ammanidi iza gishshi marikatiza ufayssafe hee haa goontta ane lo7ethi oykkos.
HEB 10:24 Siiqonine lo7o oothon nu minni daana mala ane issay issa qofisos.
HEB 10:25 Ane nu wuriso gallas issay issara gakki gakki issay issa minthethos attin issi issi asati shiiqo aggida mala ane nuni shiiqoza aggokko. Harapeka Goda Yussay matatidaysa qopishe kasep minni shiqite.
HEB 10:26 Nuni tuma shaaki eridi ekkidayssafe erishe nagara oothiko hayssafe guye nagaras shiiqanas hara yarshoy deena.
HEB 10:27 Hara buro hananay daro babisiza piriday Xoossa morketa xuugana naagiza mino tamay xalala dees.
HEB 10:28 Muse woga kadhida uray nam77u woykko hedzdzu markkati markkatiko maaroy baynda hayqon qaxxayetes.
HEB 10:29 Histin Xoossa na kadhida uray izan geeyida caaqo suutha hiraysso miisha mala qoodidadesine iza kiyatetha ayana isethidades ay mala hessafe adhiza piriday izas ba ssiza intes milatizee?
HEB 10:30 Tani izas halo kessan. Izade ootho mala izades ta zaarana” gidayssa nu erosu. Qasseka “Goday ba dereza bolla piridana” gees Goday.
HEB 10:31 Deyo Xoossa kushen kundethi daro babises.
HEB 10:32 Intes issi to po7oy po7idape guye meto wode daro baxen inte kase minni eqqida beni wodeza yuushi qopite.
HEB 10:33 Issi issi wode inte duulata dere sinththan cashasine goodetethas aadhi imettidista. Qasse hara wodeka hessa mala waayey istta bolla gakida asatara inteka issife waaye beyidista.
HEB 10:34 Inte intes harape aadhiza medhinas daana haaroy dizayssa eriza gishshi qachchetidaytas michetidistane inte haaroy bonqetishin ufayssan danda7idista.
HEB 10:35 Hessagishshi gita waggay diza kase inte ammanotethiyo agopite.
HEB 10:36 Inte Xoossa dhene polidi izi intes immida ufayssa qaala ekanas minni eqanas intena koshes.
HEB 10:37 Gaasoyka guutha wodepe kaallidi “Yanadey izi yana; gammi7ena”
HEB 10:38 Xiillo uray gidiko ammanon deyo demmana. Guye shiriqaqizadey diiko ta shempoy izade. bolla ufa7etuku
HEB 10:39 Nuni gidiko ammanidi attidayta baggako attin gede guye unddudi dhayzayta bagga gidoko.
HEB 11:1 Ammano geethi issi miishe hanana giidi nu sidhontta dishe beyontta miisheka beyida mal aero gi ekkoko.
HEB 11:2 Kase Aawati galatetiday hessa mala ammanonkko.
HEB 11:3 Hayssi ha alamey Xoossa qaalan medhetidayssa nu ammanon erosu. Hessaththoka ayfen beettizayssi medhettiday beetiza miishafe gidonttayssa nuni erosu.
HEB 11:4 Abeeley Xoossas, Qayele yarshofe adhiza yarsho ammanon shiishides. Xoossi iza yarshoza gishshi hasa7ishe izi ammanon geeshi gididayssa marikattides. Izi hayqqinkka iza ammanoy ha7i gakanas hasa7etes.
HEB 11:5 Henokey hayqo beyontta mala hayssa alamezape ammanon eketides. Xoossi iza ekkida gishshi izi bettibeyna. Ekistanape kasettidi izi Xoossa ufayssidaysi yootetida gishshi izi eketides.
HEB 11:6 Qasseka ammanoy bayndda dishin Xoossa ufayssanas muleka danda7etena. Gaasoyka Xoossako shiiqiza uray wurikka Xoossi gizayssane wozinape iza koyzaytas izi waaga immanayssa ammananas besses.
HEB 11:7 Nohes Xoossi buro Nohey ba ayfen beyontta miisha gishshi naagettana mala yootin Nohey Xoossa babbidi ba so asa ashanas ammanon marikabe kexxidi alame asa piridisides. Ammanon bettiza xiillotethi laatizade giddies.
HEB 11:8 Abiramey bees laata biitta ekkanas xeyigettida wode ammanon azazetides. Awa bizakone erontta aggikoka ero gi bides.
HEB 11:9 Alaga biittan bete asa mala buro nees immistana geetetida biittan ammanon uttides. Izas immetida ufayssa qaala izara issife laatana Yisaqa malane Yaqobem mala dunikanen deyides.
HEB 11:10 Gaasoyka minna dizaaro Xoossi izo qopi medhida katamayo ekkana naagides.
HEB 11:11 Abirames wode gede bidade gidikkoka Saarayka yelontta makara gidikkoka ufayss isttas immidadey ammanettidade hisiti xellida ammanon na Aawa gidanas gakides.
HEB 11:12 Hessa gishshi hayssa hayqqida asa mala qoodetida issi Abiramepe salo xoolintte malane abba ace mala qooday bayndda daro zerethay beettides.
HEB 11:13 Heyti wurikka isttas immetida ufayssa qaala demmontta ba ammanon naagida mala hayqida. Gidikoka istti hayssa biitta bolla immathene bete asi gididayssa erida gishshi haahon dishe beyidi kushen aathida mala ufayssan ekkida.
HEB 11:14 Hessa mala giza asati istta derey awakone ba dere naagizayssa qonccen bessetes.
HEB 11:15 Istti ba yeggi kezida dere zaari qopizako guye simmi baana danda7etesshin.
HEB 11:16 Ha7i hessafe aadhiza pude salon diza dere laamotetes. Hessa gishshi Xoossi isttas salon katama giigisida gishshi istta xalala Xoossa geeteti xeygistanas yelatibeyna.
HEB 11:17 Xoossi Abiramey ba naaza Yisaqa shukana mala paacin Abiramey Yisaqa yarshana ammanon shiishides. Xoossi izas immana gidayssa izika ba na issineza shukanas giigetides.
HEB 11:18 Hessika Xoossi izas “Ne zerethi Yisaqa baggara xeyigistana” gidaysa malakko.
HEB 11:19 Xoossi hayqidade denthanas danda7izaysssa Abiramey ammanida gishshi Yisaqaka hayqope denidida asa mala nam77antho demmides.
HEB 11:20 Yisaqay burope hananayssa qopi ekkidi Yayiqobene eesa mamanon anjjides.
HEB 11:21 Yaqobey hayqana gishshi Yosefo nayta issa issa ammanon anjjidayne ba guufe bolla dariti eqidi goyniday ammanoniko.
HEB 11:22 Yosefoy hayqana gishshi Isiraa7eele asay Gibixepe kezanayssa izi yootidayne ba meqetha gishshi istti ay oothanakone izi istta azaziday ammanonkko.
HEB 11:23 Musey yelettin izas malay lo7o gididayssa beyidi iza yelidayti iza hedzdzu agina gakanas kawoza azazzo babbontta qottiday ammanonkko.
HEB 11:24 Musey dicci gakida parinose nay na geetistanas ammanon ixxides.
HEB 11:25 Guutha wodes nagaran bettiza ufayssafe aathidi Xoossa asara meto beyanas doorides.
HEB 11:26 Gibixe deren diza haarope bollara kiristoosa gishshi waaye ekoy daro aadhiza haaro gididayssa yuushi qopides. Gaasoyka izi sinththafe ekanayssa buro haahon beyida gishshiko.
HEB 11:27 Kawo hanqqos babbontta ammanon Gibixe yeggi kezides. Buro betonttayssa beyza mala qopidi he qofan minni eqqides.
HEB 11:28 Bayrata urisi wodhizayssi Isiraa7eelista bayra nayta wodhontta mala ammanon paazigane suutha wuxxesa woga wothides.
HEB 11:29 Isiraa7eele asay mela biitta bolla hamuttiza mala Eritera abba gidora ammanon pinides. Gibixe asay qasse issitatho hanana gishshi abban mitettides.
HEB 11:30 Isiraa7eele asay Eyariko gimbeza laapun qamma yuuy yuuy aadhidape guye gimbeza ammanon laalides.
HEB 11:31 Layiman aqiza Raba7a dere xomosana yidayta saron mokki ekkida gishshi hanko azazetontta asara dhayontta ammanon attadus.
HEB 11:32 Hayssafe aadhethi ay gaanee? Geedne gishshi, Baaraqe gishshi, Somsone gishshi, Yofitahe gishshi, Dawite gishshi, Samela gishshi qasse nabeta gishshi ta yootontta mala taas wodey deena.
HEB 11:33 Heytantti ammanon kawota xonnida suure pirida piridida bees imettida ufayssa qaala ekida gaamota duuna goridida.
HEB 11:34 Tama woliqa toyssida qaara maccashafe kessi ekki attida. Daaburape minnida. Olason goobata gidida allaga asa ola goodida.
HEB 11:35 Macashatas hayqidayti paxida baggayti qasse hessafe aadhiza hayqope denthi demmanas giidi hayqope atethi leqidi hayqos bena aathi immida waayepe atanas koybeyttena.
HEB 11:36 Issi issi asati asan kaa7ettida. Garafettida. Bagayti qasse qachcho keethi gelida.
HEB 11:37 Shuchan cadettida magazenka nam77u kezi phaliqetida. Mashan shuketi hayqida waayetishe, Goodetishene daaburshe dorisa ittene deyshe itte mayidi waayetida.
HEB 11:38 Ha alamey isttas besontta gidida gishshi bazzonine gezen gongolon ne holla gidon waayetida.
HEB 11:39 Heytantta wurisota ammano gishshi marikatikoka isttafe oonikka imistana geetetida ufayssa qaala gakkidi ekkidadey deena.
HEB 11:40 Xoossi nuusu hessafe aadhzazi giigisida gishshi nu baynda istti xalala kumethi gidana danda7ibeyttena.
HEB 12:1 Hessa gishshi shaara mala nuni yuuy aadhida daro marikati nuusi dishin nuna deexiza toohone qasse nuni qachchi oykiza nagara wursi nuupe wora yeggidi nu sinththan diza wotha genccanine dandan7an ane wothos.
HEB 12:2 Nu ammaniza ammanozas koyrone polo gidida Yesusa ane xeellos. Izi ba sinththan diza ufayssa gishshi masiqale bolla hayqo danda7idi masiqale bolla bena gakana kawushatetha leqqidi Xoossa aligas oshachchan uttides.
HEB 12:3 Histinko inte daaburidi ufayssi qanxxontta mala hessathoka nagaranchatape kase iza bolla gakida hessa mala eqetethi danda7ida Yesusa qopite.
HEB 12:4 Suuthu gukana gakanas nagarara inte buro eqettibeykista.
HEB 12:5 Inte Xoossa nayta gidi uttidi qaalay gizayssa balidista. “Ta naazo Xoossa seera kawushan xeelofa, Nena izi seeriza wode ufayssi qanxxofa.
HEB 12:6 Gaasoyka Goday ba dosizade hanqees. Izi ba dosizade seeres. Izi ba na mala xeellizade qaxayees.
HEB 12:7 Xoossi intena ba na mala qoodiza gishshi hanqo danda7ite. Aaway hanqontta nay oonee?
HEB 12:8 Nay wuri seeran diccizatho inte diccontta aggiko inte Karen yelettida na attin so na gidekista.
HEB 12:9 Hessa wurisofe bollara hayssa biitta nuna hanqqi dichchida asho Aawati deetes. Nuka istta bonchos. Histin deyon deyanas nuus ayana Aawa gididayssatho aazas hessafe aathi azazetokonii?
HEB 12:10 Nu Aawati nuna bees lo7o milati bettida mala guutha wodes qaxayeetes. Xoossi gidiko nuni izan geeshatetha izape demmana mala nuna go7anas qaxayees.
HEB 12:11 Qixatey wurikka ha7is ufayssontta iitta milatees shin guyepe qase dosi ekkida asatas sarotethi izan kumida xiillotetha ayfen gaathes.
HEB 12:12 Hessa gishshsi daaburida inte qesene inte gulibate minisite.
HEB 12:13 Wobey paxana attin kasepe aathi wobontta mala “Inte toos lo7o oge giigisite”
HEB 12:14 Asi wurisora saro daana mala intes danda7etizayssa wursi oothite. Geeyena mala koyite. Geeshatethi baynda Goda beyanas danda7etena.
HEB 12:15 Intefe issadeskka Xoossa kiyatethi paccontta mala qasseka camo ayfe ayfiza mithi mokkidi meto medhontta malane darota moorontta mala naagetite.
HEB 12:16 Issito maana kaathas ba bayrateth bayzida Eesa mala intefe oonikka laaymattizade woykko Xoossu bonchontade gidi beetontta mala naagetite.
HEB 12:17 Eesay guyepe kase ba anjjoza laatanas zaari koyin izas imetontta digettidayssa inte ereista. Izi bena gakiza anjjozaskka daro yekkishe koyidika zaari demmanas danda7ibeyna.
HEB 12:18 Kushen bochchiko bochchetiza tamay iza bolla exxiza Siina zumako he dhumako, he tulalezaakone he gote carikozako inte gakibeykista.
HEB 12:19 Inte zaye giirethako woykko haythan siyetiza qaala giirethako gakkibeykista. Hessa siyida asatika hara qaala gujjontta mala woosssida.
HEB 12:20 Hessas gaaasoyka “Haray attoshin meheyka zuma bochchiza gidiko shuchan cadeti hayqo” giza azazoza asay naaganas danda7ibeyna.
HEB 12:21 He wode heeni hanizayssi wurikka daro babisizayssa gidida gishshsi Museykka “Ta babbada kokoradis” gides.
HEB 12:22 Inte qasse ha Xiyone zuma bolla pude salo Yerusalame ha deyo Xoossa kataman ufayssan shiiqida qooday baynda kiitanchatako yidista.
HEB 12:23 Istta suunthi salon xaafetida bayrata maabarako wurisos daana gidida Xoossako istta bolla wothoy baynda xiillo asata shempoy dizaso matidista.
HEB 12:24 Oaratha caaqon iginththiza Yesusako hessathoka Aabeley shiishida suuthafe aadhiza caaqo qaala yootiza aracetida suuthako gakidista.
HEB 12:25 Intes yootizayssa inte akkaye goontta mala naagetite. Heytantti Xoossi biitta bolla diza asa baggara isttas yootizayssa ekontta ixxidi izape attanas danda7ontta aggiko nuni salzope yidayssi nuusi yootishin nu ekkontta ixxiko izape waanidi attanee?
HEB 12:26 He wode qaala giirethan biitta qaathides. Ha7i qasse biitta xalala gidontta ta saloka qasseka ta zaarada issito qaathana” giza qaala yooti wothides.
HEB 12:27 Hayssi “Qasseka ta zaarada issito” giza qaalay nuna bessizay qaxxonttayti minni daana malane qaxxizayti heytika medhetidayti kichchanas besses.
HEB 12:28 Hessa gishshi nuni muleka qanxxonttayta kawoteth laatanayssa gishshi ane Xoossu galatosu. Qasseka iza ufayssiza ogera bonchosine yashatethan ane izas goynoos.
HEB 12:29 Nu Xoossi xuugiza tama malako
HEB 13:1 Inte inte gidon ishata mala dosetite.
HEB 13:2 Imatha mokko balopite; Issi issi asati hessaththo oothishe erontta kiitanchata imathateth mokki ekkida.
HEB 13:3 Qachcho keeththan dizaytara inteka qachettida mala isttas qopite. Hessaththoka asa kushen waayetizaytara inteka waayetiza mala isttas qopite.
HEB 13:4 Ekoy geloy wuriso asa achchan boncheto. Inte hithey geesh gido. Gaasoyka layma amoy dizaytane laymatizayta bolla Xoossi piridana.
HEB 13:5 Miisha siiqope naagetite. Intes dizaysi gidana. Hessas gaasoy Xoossi “Ta intena muleka aggikene yegike” gides.
HEB 13:6 Hessa gishshi kumetha wozinape nuni “Goday taas maado; ta babbike. Tana asi ay oothana danda7izee? goosu.
HEB 13:7 Intes Xoossa qaala koyrope yooti kaallethizayta balopite. Istta duusan beettiza lo7o ayfey dizayssa yuushi qopite. Inteka ammanon istta milatite.
HEB 13:8 Yesus kiristoosay hachchika wonttoka medhinaskka izi izako.
HEB 13:9 Dumma dumma imatha timirtte ekopite. Nu wozinay minni eqqizay Xoossa kiyatesan attin kaththa woga naagon gidena. Hessa he woga naagizaytaka izan go7etbeytena.
HEB 13:10 Nuusi yarsho soy dees. Gidikoka Dunkaaneza gidon oothiza qesseti he yarsho sooza bolla diza kaththafe ekki montta mala digetida.
HEB 13:11 Qessista halaqay nagara teqqiza mehe suuthu ekkidi wurisofe dumma geetettiza kifile geeles. Mehista ashoy gidiko katamape Karen xuugetes.
HEB 13:12 Hessaththoka Yesusay ba suutha baggara asa geeshanas katama pengefe Karen meto be7ides.
HEB 13:13 Hessa gishshi nuka izi tokkida kawushatetha tokkida nu dizasope gede izako kare ane kezoosu.
HEB 13:14 Gaasoyka hayssan eqqi daana. Katamay nuusi deena. Gido attin buro sinthafe yaana katamayo naagosu.
HEB 13:15 Hessa gishshi wuriso wode galata yarsho hessika iza sunthas marikatiza nu dunape bettiza ayfe gididazi Yesusa baggara Xoossas ane shiishos.
HEB 13:16 Qasseka lo7o oothone intes dizayssafe haratas imo balopite. Xoossi heytantta mala yarshon ufa7etes.
HEB 13:17 Intena kaallethizaytas azazetitene haaretite. Hessas gaasoyka inte gishshi istta alafetethan daro oychiza guday diza gishshi inte shempo gishshi daro baxetetes. Hessa gishshi istti ba oothiza oothoza lanccetishe gidontta ufayssan oothana mala inte isttas azazetite. Inte hessaththo hisitontta aggiko intes lo7ena.
HEB 13:18 Nuusika woossite. Wuriso sooraka lo7o duusu daanas laamotiza lo7o qofay nuusi dizayssa nu sidhoko.
HEB 13:19 Harapeka ta inteko ellen simma baana mala ta as inte woossan mala hadara gayssi.
HEB 13:20 Dorthata hethanchay wogga Goda Yesus kiristoosa ba medhina caaqo qaala suuthan iza hayqope denthida sarotetha Xoossi,
HEB 13:21 Inte iza shene polana mala lo7etethan intena gixiso. Xoossa ufayssizayssa Yesus kiristoosa baggara nunan ootho. Izas medhinape medhinas bonchoy gido. Amin7i.
HEB 13:22 Ta ishato, intes xaafida zore qaalay guuthu gidida gishshi inte hanqetontta mala ta intena hadara gayss.
HEB 13:23 Nu isha Ximotosay irishetidayssa inte erana mala ta koyayss. izi eeson taako yiiko ta izara hee baada intena heen beyana.
HEB 13:24 Inttena kaalethizayta wurisosine ammaniza asa wurisos ta saroka yootite. Xaalanen diza ammaniza asayka intena saro gees.
HEB 13:25 Xoossa kiyatethi intenara gido. Amin7i.
JAM 1:1 Xoossa Goda Yesusi Kiristossa oothancha gidida Yaqobeppe biitta bolla laletida tammane nam77u kochatas sarotethi intes gido.
JAM 1:2 Ta ishato inte bolla duma duma wayey gakkiiko hessa wursi ufaysan qoodite.
JAM 1:3 Gaasoykka inte amano paccetithi intes danda7a immizayssa inte ereetta.
JAM 1:4 Inte danda7an mini eqanaysi intes issi miishshikka pacconta kumetha assine wothoy bayndayta gidana mala ootho.
JAM 1:5 Inte garssafe oonasikka eratethi pacciko oonakka kadhontta ba kiiyatethara wurisos immiza Xoossa wosso; izadeskka imettana.
JAM 1:6 Gido attin sidhey baynda amanon wosso. Gaasoykka sidhiiza uray abba qathiza bullahe cariko malakko.
JAM 1:7 Hessadey Godape aykokk demana giidi issinokka qoppofo.
JAM 1:8 He uray nam77u qohaaththaan ooyketidi ba bizza oge bolla hene haane giza asa malakko.
JAM 1:9 Kase ziiqan diza ura Xoossi dhoqqu histiza gish ufa7etto.
JAM 1:10 Asa haroy maata cisha mala qoqofettiza gish dure ura Xoossi ziq histikko ufa7etto.
JAM 1:11 Away xugidi maata shullisees; maata ciishayka shullees; iza loo7etethikka dhayees; hessathokka durey hachchi hachchi dabursan diishin iza duretethi dhayees.
JAM 1:12 Paccen miinni eqidadey izi anjjetidade. Gaasoyka izi paccera eqitishin Xoossi bena dosizaytas immida ufaysa deyo zawude izi ekkana.
JAM 1:13 Oonikka paccetiza gidikko tana Xoossi paccees goppo, gaasoykka Xoossi ase iittan paccena, izi oonakka pacci erena.
JAM 1:14 Gido attin issi issi uray paccetizay berika ba iitta amo kalishene baletishekko.
JAM 1:15 Amoy qanthetetidape guye nagara yellees. Nagaraykka dicciidape guye hayqo yellees.
JAM 1:16 Ta siiqo ishato inte ballettopite.
JAM 1:17 Loo7o imotethine kumetha anjjoy wuri bolla Salo poo7ota Aawape wodhetes. Iza achan gede ha yuyiza kuwayka (eshoykka) dena.
JAM 1:18 Nu iza medhetethas koyro bayrata gidana mala ba sheninne ba tuma qaalan nuna yellides.
JAM 1:19 Dosetida ta ishato hayssa yuushi qoppite. Asi wurikka siyanas esoto, hasa7asinne hanqqos esotopo.
JAM 1:20 Asa hanqqoy Xoossa xiiloteth oothena.
JAM 1:21 Hessa gish tunatethinne dalggida iittatethi intefe kessi yegidi inte shemppo ashanaas danda7iza inte gidon toketida qaala ashketethara ekkite.
JAM 1:22 Qaalay gizayssa oothite; attin mela siisi xalala siyzadista gididi interkka intena balethofite.
JAM 1:23 Qaala siyishe siyida qaalay gizayssa oothontadey ba ayfeso mastotera xelliza asa malakko.
JAM 1:24 Bena xeelli beydi bees; izi ay milatizakone heraka baletti gides.
JAM 1:25 Gido attin bena geshiza loo7o woga xeelli beydi izan minizadey ba siydayssa oothizadeynne balonttadey izi ba oothon anjjetidade gidana.
