JAM 1:26 Be duuna nagontta berikka ba wozina baleththishe ta ammanayss gizadey berikka bena baleththees. Iza ammanoykka mella hada ammanokko.
JAM 1:27 Xoossa Aawa sinthan iittatethi baynda loo7o ammanoy; “Aayanne Aaway hayqqida nayta, istta azinati hayqqida maccashata metotetishin maadonne hayssa alameza tunatethafe bena nagokko.
JAM 2:1 Ta ishato inte bonchettida Goda Yesussa Kiristosa ammanizayta gidida mala asse besontta ogera maadofiite.
JAM 2:2 Worqqa yiich biradhen aaththdi loo7o mayo mayida asi inte shiqqizaso yiikko hessathokka qiita mayo mayidadey he shiqqizaso yiko qaseka hara qiita mayo mayda manqqo uray gelliko loo7o maydaysa duma boncho bonchidi “nees besiiza loo7o utizaso hessa beya” giidi hayinko manqqoza qasse “Ne hen hessan eqa, woykko haa ya ta garisan hugen uta” inte gikko;
JAM 2:4 Inte inte garsan besontta maado oothista gideketi? Qasseka inte iitta qofan ooykittida iitta pirda piirdizayta gideketi?
JAM 2:5 Ta siiqo ishato ane siyte; isti ammanon durista gidana mala Xoossi bena dosizaytas ufayssan isttas immida kawotetha istti laattana mala hayssa ha alamezan diza manqota dooribeynee?
JAM 2:6 Inte qase manqota kawusheista. Intena waysiza durista gidetene? Intena piirdeso gochizay istta gidetenee?
JAM 2:7 Intenan xeygetida boncho Xoossa sunththa zigirizayti ista gidetenee?
JAM 2:8 Maxaafan “Ne lagge ne hu7e mala siiqa” geeteti xaafettida kawo woga inte polikko loo7o oothista.
JAM 2:9 Inte besonta maado madikko nagara oothista. woga sinthanka inte woga yedhidade gidi qodistana.
JAM 2:10 Gaasoykka woga wursi pollizadey qasekka wogape issineyin dhuphetiza uray wursikka moridade mala qoodettees.
JAM 2:11 “Laymatopa” gidadey izikka zaaridi “wodhopa” gides. Ne laymatontta agikokka ne asa wodhikko wogape adhiidade gidaassa.
JAM 2:12 Inte hasa7a hasa7ishe woykko issi miishshi oothishe intena xiillisiza asa mala gidite.
JAM 2:13 Gaasoykka marontay wurikka maroy baynda pirdistana. Maroy pirda Xoonees.
JAM 2:14 Ta ishato issi uray taas ammanoy dees gikko qasse oothon besontade gidikko iza ay maadanee? Hesamala amanoy iza ashane?
JAM 2:15 Ane qoppite, issi ishay woykko issi michiya mayoy woykko mizayssi baynda aggiko intefe isadey “Inte saron biite, intena megopo, kallite” giiko istta ashos koshizayssa immontta aggikko ay maadanee?
JAM 2:17 Hesathokka oothoy baynda ammanoykka bees hayidayssa.
JAM 2:18 Gido attin isadey “Taas oothoy dees nees ammanoy dees. Neni ne ammano oothope shaakada tana bessa, ta qasse ta ammano oothon nena bessana gikko;
JAM 2:19 Ne “issi Xoossi dizaysa ammanayss” loo7oko; daydanthatikka hessa mala ammanettesinne kehi kokoreetes.
JAM 2:20 Neno eeyazo! oothoy baynda ammanos go7ay bayndayssa eranas marikka koyazii?
JAM 2:21 Nu Aawa Abramey ba na Yisaqa yarshizasoza bolla shiishshida wode oothon xilli beynee?
JAM 2:22 Hessan ammanoy iza oothora isife dizaysanne amanoy ooothon poletidayssa beyazii?
JAM 2:23 “Abramey Xoossu ammanides; He amanoy izas xiillotethan qoodetides” giza maxaafa qaalay poletides; izikka Xoossi dosidade geetettides.
JAM 2:24 Hessa gish asi ammanon xalala gidontta oothonkka xiillizaysa inte beyeista.
JAM 2:25 Hesathokka laymman diza Era7aba kiiteti bida asata mokka ekada hara ogera moyza yedida gish ba oothon xiillabeykee?
JAM 2:26 Shemppofe shaakettida ashoy hayqeeth gidida mala oothopekka shaakettida ammanoy hayqethikko.
JAM 3:1 Ta ishato intefe daroti astamarista gidopeto, gaasoykka nu astamare gididayti aadhetha pirda ekanaysa inte ereista.
JAM 3:2 Nu wurikka daro miishan dhuphetoos. Hasa7an dhuphetontadey dikko izi ba asateth loo7athi naganaas danda7iza kumetha asakko.
JAM 3:3 Nuni parazota azazanaas bixxala barsidi nu koyda mala istta azazoos.
JAM 3:4 Woykko ane markabista xeelite. Ay gitatanne carikon lagetizayta gidikokka marikabe lagiizadey qeeri laafa laagiza misheyira ba koyizaso efees.
JAM 3:5 Hessathokka asatetha garisan inxxarisi guuthu gida utada giita wollqama oothoro oothoristaysu, qeeri tamay gita wora wostti xuuggi dhaysiizakonne ane yuushi qoppiite.
JAM 3:6 Inxxarasikka ba bagara tama malakko. Nu asatetha gidon diza iitta alamekko. Asatetha wursa tuniisaysunne asatetha bolla tama gujawusu, besiika gaaname taman xugistana.
JAM 3:7 Mehey do7ayka kafoti hayssathokka biita bolla gochetizaytinne abba gidon diza medhetethata wursi asi harana danda7esinne istikka haraettida.
JAM 3:8 Gido attin inxxars haranaas danda7ida uray oonikka dena. Wodhiiza maridzdzey izin kumidaronne iza shemppa ekontta iitta mishshikko.
JAM 3:9 Nuni nu inxxarasayra Godanne Aawa anjjoos. Izinkka Xoossa lemison medhetida asa nayta zaaridi qangoos.
JAM 3:10 Anjjoynne qangethi issi duunara keezes. Ta ishato hessi hessaththo hananaas bessena.
JAM 3:11 Issi pullto ollafe mal7o haththinne camo haththi pullti erizee?
JAM 3:12 Ta ishato Balase geetettiza miiththi woyra ayfe woykko woyine miiththi Balase miiththa ayfe ayfanaas danda7ize? Hesathokka camiza hathefe mall7iza haththi bistana danda7ena.
JAM 3:13 Inte garathafe akekara diza ciincca uray oone? cinccay diza gidiko ane ba ootho ashketethan cinccatethara ba loo7o dussan besso.
JAM 3:14 Qasse camonne qaanatey intena xalala dosiza hanoy inte wozinan diza giikko ootoroteth intes siyetofo. Tumaka kadopiite.
JAM 3:15 Hiini mala eratethiya salloppe gidiku. Hina qasse biittafe; ashopene xala7eppekko.
JAM 3:16 qanateyinne berika bena siqqoy dizason wasoynne iitta oothoy wuri dees.
JAM 3:17 Sallope gidida eratethiya gidikko koyro geshshikko, guyepekka saroteth dosizaro, danda7izaaro, ero gizaro, marotethinne loo7o ayfey kumidarokko. Qasse worodo madontaronne ulon geney bayndaro.
JAM 3:18 Saroteth dosiza asati sarotethan zeridi xillotetha ayfe maxeettes.
JAM 4:1 Inte garsan diza oolaynne ooshay awape yidee? Inte wozinan diza amotethafe dendida oola gidenee?
JAM 4:2 Inte amottista shin demekista. Inte asi wodhistanne kehi amotista shin demana danda7ekista. Inte inte garisan ooyetiza gishanne ooletiza gish qasse wosontta gish intes imettena.
JAM 4:3 Inte inte asho ufaysanaas iitta qofan wosiza gish wosidaysa inte ekekista.
JAM 4:4 Inteno laymatizayto alamera siiqetethi Xoossara morketeth gididaysa ereketii? Hessa gish hayssa alamezara siiqitethi koyzay wurikka Xoossas morke.
JAM 4:5 Woykko gesha maxaafa gidon “nunan izi ayssiida ayanay nu ziaysa gidana mala daro amottees” gizaysi intes coo mela gidayssa milatize?
JAM 4:6 Gido attin izi ba kiiyateth nuus gujji immees. Maxafaykka “Xoossi ootoranchatara eqettees, ashikistas qase ba kiiyateth immees” giday hessasikko.
JAM 4:7 Hessa gish intena Xoossas harisiite. Dabuloosara eqitite, izi intefe baqatana.
JAM 4:8 Xoossako shiiqqite izikka intekko shiiqqana. Inteno nagaranchato! inte inte kushe geeshshite, inte nam77u qofan qaxiizayto, inte inte wozina geeshshite.
JAM 4:9 Darsi qoppite; muyagiite; yekiite. Inte michay yehon; ufaysay qasse qadhetethan siimo.
JAM 4:10 Goda sinththan inte intena kawushite qasse izi intena dhooqu dhooqu histtana.
JAM 4:11 Ta ishato inte inte garisan issay issay motoopite ba isha motizadeynne ba isha bolla piridizadey woga bolla iitta hasa7esinne woga bolla piridees. Ne woga bolla pirdizade attin woga naagizade gidakka.
JAM 4:12 Woga wothidadeynne pirdizadey issade xalalakko. Izikka dhaysanaasinne ashanaas danda7izadekko. Gido attin neni ne lagge bolla pirdizadey oone?
JAM 4:13 Inte hachchchi woykko wontto hano ha katamayo woykko hiino he katamayo nu baana, biidi hen izin issi laythth utananne zal77i wodhisana gizayto ane haa siyte.
JAM 4:14 Wonto hananayssa inte erekista. Inte shemppoy iza azee? Inteni guutha wode ayfes bettidi dhayiza haththa penta malakko.
JAM 4:15 Hassa gaanappe “Goda shene gidikonne nu paxxa dikko, hessakka hayssaka oothana” gaanas intes bessees.
JAM 4:16 Ha7i gidiko inte otoretethan ceqetista. Hessa mala oothoretethi wurikka iitta.
JAM 4:17 Hessa gish loo7o gidizayssa oothanas besizaysa erishe oothonttades nagara gidana.
JAM 5:1 Histikko inteno dure asato, ane siiyte. Buro inte bolla gakkana metoza gish yekiite, wu! wu! gi wasiite.
JAM 5:2 Inte haaroy buqqides, inte mayoykka bil7ay/baday/ mides.
JAM 5:3 Inte worqayinne inte biiray shiyides. He shiydaysikka inte bolla marikatesinne inte ashoy tama mala xuugees. Inte wode wurisethas miishshe shiishshidista.
JAM 5:4 Inte inte wozinan wothite inte kaththi maxishe pe7idaytas istta wollqa waaga inte qanxxontta aggida gish inte bolla wasishe inte achchan deettes. Kaththi maxizayta wassoy wursi danda7iza Goda haythan gakides.
JAM 5:5 Inte biitta bolla ishallonne aloo7etethan deyidista, inte wozina shuka galasas dhiikki handadhathidista.
JAM 5:6 Inte intenara eqetontta xiillo asata bolla worido wothidi wodhiidista.
JAM 5:7 Hessa gish ta ishato Goday ha yaana gakanas danda7ite. Goshshe goyizadey biittay loo7o kathth kaxxana gakanaas wani danda7izakone balgo/asura/ irane ofintha ira izi wostti naagizako ane akekkite.
JAM 5:8 Inteka hessaththo danda7ite. Inte wozina miinthite. Gaasoykka Goda yussa gallas matides.
JAM 5:9 Ta ishato inte inte garsan zigretopite, inte zigretiko inte bolla piridistana. Piridanadey heko inte penge bolla eqqides.
JAM 5:10 Ta ishato Goda sunththan intes yootida nabeta wayetethinne istta danda7a intes lemuso histti xeellite.
JAM 5:11 Danda7an genccida asata nu istta “IstTi anjjetidayta” gi qoodizayssa inte ereista. Iyobey wanii danda7idakonne inte iza gish siyidista. Goday iza wurisethan ay oothidakone inte beyidista. Goday asas keehi michetizadenne marizadekko.
JAM 5:12 Harapeka ta ishato sallon gidin woykko biitta bolla gidin woykko ay mishanka caqqofite; “Ee” gaanas bessiza miishsha gidikko “Ee” giite; “Akaye” gaanas gidiko “Akaye” giite hessafe hara giiko inte bolla pirdistana.
JAM 5:13 Inte garisan metotiza uray dizee? Diza gidiko izi wosso. Ufa7etizadey dizee? diza gidiko ufayssa yeethi yeexxo.
JAM 5:14 Inte gidon saketiza assi dizee? diiko wossa keeththa ciimata xeyigo. Isttikka Goda sunththan zayte iza bolla tiyidi izas wosseto.
JAM 5:15 Ammanon wossida wossay hargidade pathana. Godaykka iza denthana. Izi nagara oothidade gidikokka Xoossi iza maarana.
JAM 5:16 Hessa gish intekka inte garisan issay issara inte nagara paxxetite; paxana mala issay issas wossite. Xiillo asa wossay wolliqara dees. Wollqama oothokka ooththees.
JAM 5:17 Elasay nu malaka asekko. Izi iray bukontta mala minthi wossin biitta bolla hezdzdu laythanne bagga gakanaas iray bukiibeyna.
JAM 5:18 Qasseka zaari wossin iray sallope biitta bolla bukides. Biittayka kaath immides.
JAM 5:19 Ta ishato intefe issadey tumape baletin hara uray iza zaariko hessa wozinan wothiite. Nagarancha izi balletida ogepe iza zaaridadey he uray shempo hayqope ashesinne izaade nagara darozaka kammees.
1PE 1:1 Yesus Kiristoosan kiitetida pixxirosape, Asa biittan beten dizaytas Phanxoosen, Galatiyan, Qepedooqiyan, Isiyanine Bitaniya biittan laaleti diza intes,
1PE 1:2 Aaway Xoossi kase intena erida mala dooretidaytas, Yesus Kiristoosas azazistanasine inte iza suuthan aracetidi geeyana mala xiillo ayanan dumattida intes kiyatethine sarotethi daro.
1PE 1:3 Yesus Kiristoosay hayqope dendida gishshi nuusu deyo gidida ufayssi immidayssi ba gita maarotethan nuna bees ooratha nayta histidayss nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosa Aaway Xoossi galateto.
1PE 1:4 Izi dhayontta, mooretonttane ceegontta laataso intes salon giigisi wothides.
1PE 1:5 Inteka wursetha gallasan buro qonccana atotethas ammano geedon Xoossa wolqan naagetidista.
1PE 1:6 Ha7i guutha wodes duma duma paaceti intena waayssikoka inte hessan ufa7ettite.
1PE 1:7 Hessi he paacezi inte bolla gakizay inte ammanozi tumu gididayssa qonccisanaskko. Dhayana worqayka taman paacettes. Worqape aadhi boncho gidida inte ammanoyka hessaththo paacistanas besses. Hessi he paacetida inte ammanoy Yesus Kiristoosay qoncciza gallas galatas, bonchosine sabas intena gaathana.
1PE 1:8 Inte Yesus Kiristoosa ayfera beyontta aggikoka inte iza doosista. Ha7ika inte iza beyontta aggikoka iza ammaneta; Coo qaalan qonccisana danda7ontta gita boncho ufayss inte ufa7etista.
1PE 1:9 Inte naagiza inte shempoyss atoteth inte ammanon demmidista.
1PE 1:10 He atotethaza gishshi intes imistana kiyatethas kase nabeti lo7ethi wozinape pilig xeellida.
1PE 1:11 Kase isttan diza Kiristoosa ayanay Xoossafe tiyettidayssa bolla gakana waayezane he waayezape guye izi demmana bonchoza gishshi kase bessi wothides. Istti qass hessi wurikka ayide waani hananakone yuushi qopida.
1PE 1:12 He kase nabeti intes oothida attin istti bees oothonttayssi isttas qonccen erettides. Istti intes oothiday bolla salope kiitetida xiillo ayana baggara ha7i intes miishiracho qaala yootida asati intes yootidayssa qonccisanasikko. Hessa qaala kiitanchatika beyanas amottida.
1PE 1:13 Hessa gishshi inte inte wozina suurisidi oothos giigetite. Wogara deyite. Yesus Kiristoosay qoncciza wode inte iza kiyatetha demmanas intes kumetha ufayssi deyo.
1PE 1:14 Inte azazetiza nayta gididi erontta dishe inte kase intes diza iitta qofa kaallopite.
1PE 1:15 Intena xeeygida Xoossi duuma gidida mala inteka inte duussan wurson duumatite.
1PE 1:16 Gaasoyka “Tani duuma gidida gishshi inteka duuma gidite” geeteti geesha maxaafan kase xaafetides.
1PE 1:17 Oonaka duuma shaaki maadontta issa issas izade ootho mala piridiza Xoossa “Izi nu Aawakko” giidi inte xeeygizazi gidiko hayssa alamezan inte imathene bete asi gidi diza wode wurson izas babbite.
1PE 1:18 Inte kase inte Aawatape laatida coo mela hada duusafe wozettiday dhayiza biran woykko worqan gidonttayssa inte ereista.
1PE 1:19 Gido attin inte wozetiday iittayne wothoy iza bolla bayinda geesha dorisa mala gidida Kiristoosa boncho suuthankko.
1PE 1:20 Izi erettiday hayssi alamezi medhetanape kase gidishin ha7i qass wursetha woden intes qoncides.
1PE 1:21 Intes ammanoyne inte hidotay Xoossan gidana mala Yesus Kiristoosa baggara he iza hayqope denthidi izas booncho immida Xoossan inte ammanettista.
1PE 1:22 Inte ammanizayta suure wozinape siiqana mala tumas azazetethan inte inte asatetha geeshidista. Hessa gishshi inte inte giddon issay issara lo7ethi siiqettite.
1PE 1:23 Inte nam7antho yeelettiday medhinas minni diza dhayontta deyo Xoossa qaalan dhayontta zereththafe attin dhayiza zereththafe gidena.
1PE 1:24 Geesha maxaafay giza mala “Asho mayday wurikka maata malakko, Iza bonchoyka wurikka wora ciisha malako, Maatayka meles, ciishayka qoqopettes.
1PE 1:25 Goda qaalay gidiko medhinas eqqi dees” Intes sabakettida miishiracho qaalayka hessakko.
1PE 2:1 Hessa gishshi iittateth wursi, baletho wursi, qoodhepe qommon hano, qaanateteth ayko qoommo zigiris intefe digite.
1PE 2:2 Ha7i yelettida guutha nayti maath amotizayssa mala inteka attanas izan dicci dicci baanas geeshi gidida ayana timirtte laamotite.
1PE 2:3 Inte laamotanas bessizay Goday kiya gididayssa shaki erikokko.
1PE 2:4 Hessa gishshi gede deyo shuchu gidida Yesusako shiiqite. He shuchay asay leqqi aggidayssa shin Xoossa achchan qass doorettidayssane boncho waagay dizaddekko.
1PE 2:5 Inte gede Goda Yesusako shiiqanayka deyo shucha mala Xiillo ayana duussaso gidana mala oothetista. Hessaththoka inte Yesus Kiristoosa baggara ufayssiza ayana yarsho Xoossas shiishanas geesha qeeseta gidandista.
1PE 2:6 Geesha maxaafan “Heko dooretida boncho gidida keethas kuriqunthan uttiza shuchu tani Xiyonen woththana. Izan ammanizadey yeelatena” giza qaalay xaafeti uttides.
1PE 2:7 Hessa gishshi intes ammanizaytas he shuchay boncho shuchukko shin hinko izan ammanontaytas qass “Shuchan keexxiza keeththa hiillati leqqi wora yegidayss izi keeththa kurqunthas hu7e gidides”
1PE 2:8 Qasseka “Heko ase dhupiza shuchay hayssich! asa dhuphi kundisiza zaala shuchay hayssakko” gess. Istti qaala ammanontta ixxida gishshi dhuphetettes. kaseka istti hessas dizaytakko.
1PE 2:9 Inte qass dhumape gede daro malalsiza iza po7oko xeeygida Xoossa malalsiza oothoza awajanas dooretida yeleteth, Kawo qeeseta Xoossi intena bees histida inte dumma derekko.
1PE 2:10 Inte kase Xoossa dere gidekista shin ha7i gidikko inte Xoossa derekko. Inte kase intes Xooss qadhetontta derekko shin ha7i gidikko qadhetides.
1PE 2:11 Ta siiqoto! inte hayssa alameza bolla imathene bete asi gidida gishshi shempora olettiza asho amotethatape haakana mala ta intena hadara gayss.
1PE 2:12 Oone erizay “Intena istti iittaa oothetes” giidi asay intena zigirikoka Xoossi nuna beyanas yiza gallas hanko dere asay inte oothoy lo7o gididayssa beyidi Xoossu galatana mala inte isttara diza wode inte amaley lo7o gido.
1PE 2:13 Inte Goda Yesusa gishshi giidi dere ayssizaytas azazetite. Kawoy qass wursofe bollara diza gishshi Kawosika azazetite.
1PE 2:14 Dere ayssizaytas azazetite. Istti iitta oothizayta qaxxayanassine lo7o oothizadayta galatanas Kawope kiitettizaytakko.
1PE 2:15 Inte lo7o oothon hanko eray bayinda eyatethan hasa7izayta co7u histana mala hessika Xoossa shenekko.
1PE 2:16 Inte Xoossas oothiza asata mala gididi hirgay bayinda deyte attin inte inte shene mala diza duussa iittatetha kammiza miishe histopite.
1PE 2:17 Ase wursika bonchite. Ammanizayta siiqite. Xoossas babbite. Kawo bonchite.
1PE 2:18 Inteno Asas oothi aqqizayto! intena oothisiza godatas bonchon azazetite. Inte azazistanay lo7otasine ashikistas xalala gidontta hanko iittatassarakko.
1PE 2:19 Asi galatettizay coo mela qohetishe hessika Xoossa gishshi giidi danda7ikokko.
1PE 2:20 Inte iitta oothida gishshi qaxayettishe danda7iko intes aaza galatay deyanee? Inte lo7o oothidi waaye ekkishe danda7iko inte Xoossafe galata ekkandista.
1PE 2:21 Inte xeeygettidayka hessaskko. Inte iza lemuso kaallana mala Kiristoosay inte gishshi waaye ekkidi intes lemuso gidides.
1PE 2:22 Izi aykko nagarakka oothibeyna. Iza duunan geney beettibeyna.
1PE 2:23 Asay iza cayshin izi zaari cayibeyna. Waayetishe bena tumu piridiza Godas hadara aathi immides attin halo kessana manddibeyna.
1PE 2:24 Nuni nagarape shaakettidi xiillotethan daana mala izi berka ba ashon nu nagara masiqqale bolla tookides. Inte iza madunthan paxidista.
1PE 2:25 Inte dhayida dorisata mala coo mela tuuyru gidistako shin ha7i qass inte shempo heemmizayssakone naagizayssako simmidista.
1PE 3:1 Hessaththoka macheto! inte inte azinatas azazetite. Hessatho issi issi azinati Xoossa qaala ammanonttayta gidikkoka coo mela ba machcheta lo7etethan xalala simmontta agettena.
1PE 3:2 Istti simmana danda7izay inte geeshatethane inte ase bonchiza duusu dizayssa beydikko.
1PE 3:3 Inte lo7etethi coo mela hu7e dathanine worqan gexxetethan, al7o mayo mayon, coo mela ayfen beettiza geexen gidopo.
1PE 3:4 Inte lo7oy Xoossa sinthan wagara diza keehi bonchetidazine dhayontta gexxen, ashiketethan, addatethanine ayanan gexxettida wozina garisan qoteti diza giddo wozina lo7eteth gido.
1PE 3:5 Beni wode ba ufayss Xoossan oothida geesha macashati gexxettiday hayssa malankko. Istti ba azinatas azazettida.
1PE 3:6 Istti azazetidaykka Saaray Abirame “Ta godo!” gaada azazettidayssa malakko. Inteka lo7o miishi oothikone issi iitta miishey intena daganthontta aggiko inte Saara naytakko.
1PE 3:7 Azinato! inte inte machchetara akekan issife deyte. Istti intefe daburancha medheteth gidida gishshine qasseka Xoossi coo mela kiyatethan immiza deyo istti intenara issife laatanayssa gishshi inte istta bonchite. Inte heyssatho oothiko inte woossa dhuphiza miishey deena.
1PE 3:8 Hessafe hara baggara qass inte issay issara siiqon diite. Hara ura bolla gakkiza meto inte meto mala xeellite. Inte inte garisan ishantta mala siiqettite. Ashikistane kiyata gidite.
1PE 3:9 Anjjite attin isttas iitta cashes, cashshe zaaropite. Inte xeeygetiday hessaththo oothid anjjo laatanaskko.
1PE 3:10 Geesha maxaafay giza mala “Deyon daana koyzayine lo7o gallasata beyanas koyiza uray ba duunape iitta hasa7ontta malane ba meterishatika gene hasa7ontta mala naageto.
1PE 3:11 Iitta yoope hakkone lo7o ootho; saroteth koyone kaallo.
1PE 3:12 Goda ayfeti xiillota bagga xeelletes. Iza haythetika istta woossa siyanas doya deetes. Hinko iitta oothizayta qass Goday ba hanqo ayfeso bessana”
1PE 3:13 Inte lo7o oothanas miinetiko inte bolla iitta miishe gaathanay oonee?
1PE 3:14 Inte lo7o oothida gishshi waaye beykoka inte anjjo ekkana. Asay inte bolla iitta oothanas mandetizayssas babbofitene daro qopofite.
1PE 3:15 Goda Kiristoosa inte wozinan bonchitene iza inte deyos Goda histtite. Intes diza ufayssa gishshi intena oychizaytas wurisos malthe immanas wurso wode giigeti uttite.
1PE 3:16 Inte isttas immana malthey qass ashiketethanine bonchon gido. Inte Kiristoosayta gidida gishshi intes diza lo7o amaleza gishshi iitta hasa7iza asay ba iitta hasa7an yeellatana mala intes lo7o qopay deyo.
1PE 3:17 Xoossa shene gidiko inte iitta ootho oothidi waayetanayssyafe lo7o ootho oothidi waayetiko lo7okko.
1PE 3:18 Kiristoosayka nuna Xoossako shiishanas izi ba hu7es xiillokko shin hanko xiillo gidontta nu nagara gishshi nam7anthettontta mala issi to waayettidi hayqides. Izi ashon hayqides shin ayanan qass paxides.
1PE 3:19 Hessa he ayanan qasho keeththan diza shempotako biidi isttas miishiracho qaala yootides.
1PE 3:20 Heyti heen woyne keeththan diza shempoti kase Nohe wode markabezi ootheti giigishin istti simmana mala Xoossi danda7an naagishin nuni nessi azazettokko gidaytakko. He markabezan gellin haathey istta ashidayta qooday osppun gidida guuthata asata xalalakko.
1PE 3:21 Hessi he haathezi ha7i qass inte izan attiza xinqatte lemusokko. Hayssi xinqattey qita bolla geeyanas meccetethi gidontta geesha qopa ekanas Xoossako shiishiza woossakko. Izi intena ashanayka Yesus Kiristoosa dentha baggarakko.
1PE 3:22 Izi pude salo biidi ha7i Xoossa achchan dees. kiitanchatine godatethi isttas dizayti wolqamataka izas haarettida.
1PE 4:1 Kiristoosay ba ashon waaye ekkida gishshi inteka ola olettiza miishe gixxidade asa mala hayssa ha qofan minnidi giigettite. Be ashon waaye beyida uray nagara ootho aggides.
1PE 4:2 Hessafe guye ba diza wode wurson izi daanay iitta asho amotethi oothon gidontta dishe Xoossa shene polonkko.
1PE 4:3 Hinko dere asati oothizayssa mala inte coo mela yeda duussan asho amon, mathon, wogape ogey bayinda kaassan, wogape aathi uyidi durusanine harassiza eeqa goynon kase inte athida wodezi intes gidana.
1PE 4:4 Ha7i qass inte ha yoozan isttara wogay bayinda qixxi qixxontta gishshi istti malaletetesine intena cayettes.
1PE 4:5 Gido attin hayqidaytta bollane paxxa dizayta bolla pirdanas giigi uttidayssas istti malthe immana.
1PE 4:6 Hayqidaytassara miishiracho qaalay yootetiday hessa gishikko. Hessaththoka ay asa bollaka piridiza mala istta asho bolla piridana. Istta shempoy qass Xooss diza mala deyon deyana.
1PE 4:7 Hessa gishshi wode wursethi mattides. Inte minni woossanas danda7ana mala wogara diitene wopu gida qofay intes deyo.
1PE 4:8 Siiqoy daro nagara kammiza gishshi harape bollara inte inte garisan lo7ethi siiqettite.
1PE 4:9 Zuzunthi bayinda issay issa imathatethi mooki ekkite.
1PE 4:10 Duma duma gidida Xoossa kiyatetha imotata ammanetethan ayson intefe issi issi uray bees imettida Xoossa kiyatetha imotan hara ura maado.
1PE 4:11 Tamarisizadey Xoossa qaala tamarisiza mala tamariso. Hagazizadey Xoossi izas immiza wolqan hagazo. Hessa malan Xooss Yesus Kiristoosa baggara haniza wurson galattistana. Bonchoyne godateth medhinape medhina gakkanaas izas gido. Amin7i.
1PE 4:12 Ta siiqoto! inte tama mala paaciza meto giddon gelliza wode hessa malay kase bayinda ooratha miishey gakidazi intes milatin malalettopite.
1PE 4:13 Hessafe bollara Kiristoosa bonchoy qoncciza wode inte keehi ufa7istana mala inte izara iza waayeza ekkizayta gidida mala ufa7etite.
1PE 4:14 Inte Kiristoosa suntha gishshi cayettiko boncho ayanay hessika Xoossa ayanay inte bolla shempiza gishshi ufa7ettite.
1PE 4:15 Intefe oona bollaka metoy gakiko he uray shempo wodhida asa mala, kayso mala, iitta oothida asa mala, asa yoo giddo coo woxxi gelidada mala gidopo.
1PE 4:16 Izi ammanizade gidida gishshi iza bolla gakiza metoy diiko qass Kirstoosa sunthan izi xoossu galato attin yeellatopo.
1PE 4:17 Piriday doomistanas wodey matides. He piriday doomistanay koyro Xoossa asa bollakko. Histtin piriday nunan doommiko Xoossa mishiracho qaalas azazetontta ixxida asa wursethi aazi gidanee?
1PE 4:18 Geesha maxaafay giza mala “xiilloyka waaydi attanas gidiko, hanko Xoossas goynota asayine nagaranchati waanandetoo?”
1PE 4:19 Hessa gishshi Xoossa shene mala waayetiza asati benatetha wurs ammanetida bena medhidayssas hadara immidi lo7o ootho oothontta aggofeto.
1PE 5:1 Hessa gishshi taka isttara issife woossa keethas cimane kirstoosa waayezas marka gidida tani qasseka burope qonccana bonchoza gishettanas diza tani intenara diza woossa keeththa cimata zorays.
1PE 5:2 Intes hadara immetida Xoossa wude naagite. He iza wudeza wolqara gidontta Xoossi koyiza ogera dosara heemmitte. Miishes yiqetethan gidontta haggazanas wozinape koshan gido.
1PE 5:3 Hesathoka inte hallafetetha garisan dizayta yeedhi haaron gidonta wudezas loo7o emuuso beson gido.
1PE 5:4 Inte hessaththo oothikko hanikko wanna heemmizayss qooncciza wode inte mooretontta boncho akilile ekkanayysako.
1PE 5:5 Hessaththoka inteno yeelagato! inte cimmatas azazetite. Inte wurikka ashiketethi afila mala maydi issay issas oothite. “Xooss otorizayta ixxes. Ashikkistass qasse ba kiyatethi immes” geeteti kasse geesha maxaafan xaafetides.
1PE 5:6 Hessa gishshi Xooss ba woden dhoqu hisitana mala minno Xoossa kuushepe garssara intena ziqq histite.
1PE 5:7 Izi intes qopiza gishshi intena metiza qofa wurs iza bolla yeggite.
1PE 5:8 Wogara deyte! beegite! inte morke Daabulosay bess mittana miishe koyshe xaagiza gaamo mala inte yuushon gaarmmames.
1PE 5:9 Alame kuumethan diza inte ishati hessa mala meto ekkana dizayssa inte eridi amanon minni eqqidi izara eqetite.
1PE 5:10 Inte guutha wodes waayetidayssafe guye intena Kiristosa baggara gede medhina bonchos xeeygida kiyatethi wursos Goday izi berka intena gakkida waayezape ashshana, maadanane minthethana qasseka dazigisana.
1PE 5:11 Bonchoyne wolqay medhinape medhina gakkanaas izas gido. Amin7i.
1PE 5:12 Tani iza ammanetida ishakko ga qopizza Silase baggara hayssa kiittaza qanxxara intes xaafadis. Ta hessa xaafiday intena zooranasine hayssi tumu Xoossa kiyatethi gididaysa intes qonncissanas gaadakko. Hessa gishshi inte hayssan Xoossa kiyatethan miinni eqqite.
1PE 5:13 Inte mala dooretidara Babiloonen diza michcho gidida woossa keethaya intes saroka shiishawusu. Ta na Marqosayka intena sarokes.
1PE 5:14 Ammano siiqotethan inte issay issa yeeri ekkidi saroketite. Intes kiristoosaytas wursos saroy gido.
2PE 1:1 Yesus Kiristoosa oothanchane izan kiitetida Simona Pixirosape, nu Godapene nu dhale Yesus Kiristoosape bettida xiillotetha baggara nu demmida ammano mala bonchettida ammano demmidayto;
2PE 1:2 Xoossane nu Goda Yesusa eron kiyatetine saroy intes gido.
2PE 1:3 Be bonchonine ba kiyatethan nuna xeyigidayssa nuni iza erida gishshi iza xoossatetha wolqay deyossine xoossu goynanas nuus koshizazi wursika immides.
2PE 1:4 Be bonchonine ba kiyatethan boncho wogay dizayssane keehi gita gidida iza hidota nuni demidos. Heytantta baggara inte iitta amo gaason hayssa ha alamezan diza dhayope keesi ekkidi Xoossatetha hanozape izara gishetizadentta gididista.
2PE 1:5 Hessa geedon hayssafe kaalliza miishati intes gujistana mala ane minnite. Ammano bolla kiyateth; kiyatetha bolla erateth;
2PE 1:6 Eratetha bolla bena haaro; bena haaro bolla danda7an mineteth; danda7an minetetha bolla xoossu goyno;
2PE 1:7 Xoossu goyno bolla ishantta doseteth; ishantta dosetetha bolla siiqo gugite.
2PE 1:8 Hayti intes dari dizazi gidiko heytii intena inte Goda Yesus Kiristoosa eron go7ayne ayfey bayindaytta gidontta mala naagana
2PE 1:9 Hayti ha miishati bayinda uray gidiko hahon diza miishe demmontta qooqe asa malakko. He uray kase adhdhida ba nagarape geeyidayssaka balettides.
2PE 1:10 Ta ishato! hessa gishshi inte xeeygettidayssane doorettidayssa shaakki eranas keehi ammottizayta gidite. Inte hessaththo oothiko mulekka dhuphetekista.
2PE 1:11 Inte hessaththo hanko medhinape medhinas diza nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosa kawotethan gelanas intes kumetha maatay imettana.
2PE 1:12 Inte hayta ha yoota eridine he inte erida tuman minni deyikkoka heyta tani intena qopisanape guye giike.
2PE 1:13 Tani paxa diza wode wurson intena wurso wode denthethanayssi bessizazi milatidi taas beettes.
2PE 1:14 Nu Goda Yesus Kiristoosay taas qonccisida mala tani hayssa alammezape elelada hayqqanayssa ta erayss.
2PE 1:15 Tani ha7i minettizay ta hayqqada intefe shaakettidape guye inte hayta ha yoota wurso wode qopana mala gaadako.
2PE 1:16 Goda Yesus Kiristoosa wolqape izas yuusa gishshi nu intes yootida wode nuni nu ayfera iza bonchoza beydi marikatoos attin asi coo mela medhi ekkidi gene hasa7iza haysu7e mala gidena.
2PE 1:17 “Tani izan ufa7ettizadey ta dosiza ta naazi hayssakko” giza qaala giireth gita bonchora izas yida wode izi xoossa Aawape bonchone gitatethi ekides.
2PE 1:18 Nuni izara anjjettida zuma bolla dishe hayssa ha salope yida giiretha nuni nu haythan siydosu.
2PE 1:19 Hessi wurikka kase nabeti yootidayssi tumu gididayssa lo7eth qonccises. Hessa gishshi inte dhumason xompes lo7eth naagettizayssa mala kase nabeti yootidayssa lo7ethi naagettite. Inte hessaththo oothanay gadey wonttanas, sosey zo7ana gakkanaasine woontt maatha xoolintezi inte wozinan poo7ana gakkanaassiko.
2PE 1:20 Inte harape aathi qopanas besizay geesha maxaafan diza tinbite qaala yootetida ay miisheka oonikka bess milatida mela birshanas besonttayssako.
2PE 1:21 Ay tinbiteyka asa shene mala muleka yibeyna. Gido attin tinbitey wurikka xiillo ayanay kaallethin iza kaallida asati Xoossafe ekkidi yootidazikko.
2PE 2:1 Gido attin beni wode wordo nabeti dereza giddon dizayssa mala hessathoka ha7i inte giddon wordo asttamareti deyandettes. Heytantti asa dhayssiza wordo timirtte qottara diccana mala oothetes. Bena ashshida Godaka kaddidi bena eesson dhayssizazi ba bolla eheetes.
2PE 2:2 Hessa geedon daro asay yeelachiza istta ogeza kaalles. He istta oothoza geedon tuma ogey cayettes.
2PE 2:3 Heyti wordo asttamareti miishas gaphigaphiza gishshi berka medhi ekkida yoo, yooti yootidi intes dizazi bees bonqqi ekkettes. Beni beni wodesope pirday isttas giigeti uttides. Addafe istta dhayoy naages.
2PE 2:4 Haray atto shin nagara oothida kiitanchatas Xoossi michetontta istta ciimma gidida dhuma olla giddon de7idi pirda gallas gakkans naagistana mala gede gaannamen yegides.
2PE 2:5 Hessaththoka xiillotetha gishshi saabake gidida Nohe hanko laapun asatara ashshidi Xoossas goynontta asati diza alameza bolla dhayssiza haathe ehishe qadhettidi kase he wode alameza maaribeyna.
2PE 2:6 Qassekka Xoossu goynnotayta qaxxaynass wursos lemuso gidana mala Sodomayne Gamora katamati bidinththe gidana gakkanaasine xuugeti dhayana gakkanaas istta bolla pirdides.
2PE 2:7 Wogay bayinda yeellachiza ootho oothiza asata oothon wurso wode so7u gishe diza xiillo Looxe gidiko ashshi ekkides.
2PE 2:8 He xiillo addezi istta giddon diishin gallas gallas izi beyzayssanine siyizzayssan he wogay bayinda asata oothozan iza shemppiya waayettadusu.
2PE 2:9 Histin hessi wurikka hessa mala gidiko Goday bess goynnishe diza asata paacepe ashshanayssane nagaranchattaka wostti qaxxayanakoneka pirda gallassas wostti istta naagidi gathanakone hessa izi eress guusuko.
2PE 2:10 Harapeka heyti tuna gidida ba asho amo kaallizaytane Xoossa godateth kadhizaytta pirda gallassas naagi wothides. Heyti wordo asttamareti istti xalatane otoranchata gidida gishshi salo bolla isttas godatethi dizayta cayshe babbettena.
2PE 2:11 Kiitanchati isttafe bollara wolqayne godatethi dizayta gidikkoka Goda sinthan istta bolla kadhe qaala kessi mootetenna.
2PE 2:12 Heyti wordo asttamareti qass bess erettontta ixida miishe wursi cashe chayettes. Heytanttii woxumayden oykettanasine hayqqanas yellettida. Coo mela ba shenen dizaytane qofay bayinda do7ata malakko. Do7ati coo mela dhayzayssatho isttika mulera dhayana.
2PE 2:13 Qoho ootho oothida gishshi istti mulera ba ootho waaga ekkana. Istta ufayssi seeta gallas mathotethine wogay bayinda buraqokko. Istti hessa mala waagay bayinda gupan intenara issife xeeygettiza wode ase ballethiza ba asho oothozan istti iittane yeellachizaytakko.
2PE 2:14 Isttas nagara oothope naagetontta amottiza ayfey dess. Isttas nagara ootho siiqiza amotethi ay wodeka simmena. Ammanon buro minni eqqontta asata ballethettes. Miishas gaphigaphetes. Istti qanggettidaytakko.
2PE 2:15 Istti suure ogeza aggagidi dhayida. Iitta ootho ootthidi demmiz miish siiqqida Bi7ore naa Bala7ame oge biidi balettida.
2PE 2:16 Bala7amey gidiko ba oothida nagara gishshi seeretides shin hassa7a erontta hareya asa qaalan izas hasa7ada he nabeza balape seera zaaradus.
2PE 2:17 Heyti he asati haathi bayinda pulttotako. Gote carkkon biza shaara malakko. Istta sakkana dhumay naages.
2PE 2:18 Kase bala garisan diza asata giddofe kessi ekki yiidi daro gam7ontta asata, coo mela hada gidida otoro qaala yooton, asho amonine laymman baletheettes.
2PE 2:19 “Inte wozettana” gishe intes ufayss immettes. Xoonettida uray bena xoonidades aylle gidi haarettizayssatho isttika bess nagaras ayllekko.
2PE 2:20 Nu Godane nuna ashshida Yesus Kiristoosa eridi ha alameza tunatethafe kessi ekkidape guye qaseka guye simmidi he kase tunatethan xoonettidi geliko isttas kaseyssafe guyeyssi adhdhida iitta gidana.
2PE 2:21 Istti xiillotetha oge shaaki eridape guye isttas imettida geesha azazozape guye simmanape istti kase he xiillotetha ogeza erontta aggidakko isttas lo7oko shin.
2PE 2:22 “Kanay ba cooyida coosha manas guye simmees” hessathoka “Gudunthi meecettidi guye simmi urqan gendderetess” geetettiza tumu lemusoy istta bolla gakkides.
2PE 3:1 Ta siiqoto! tani intes xaafishin hayssi nam7antho kittakko. Tani intes nam7u kiittataka xaafiday hayta ha yoota akeki ekkidi inte suure qofa qofana mala intena beegothana gaadako.
2PE 3:2 Hayssafe kase geesha nabeti yootida qaalane qass inte hawarista baggara inte demmida nu Godane nuna ashshidayssa azazo inte yuushi qofana mala ta koyayss.
2PE 3:3 Hara wursofe kasetidi hayssa yuushi qopite. wursetha gallasatan qidhizaytine ba iitta amo kaallishe asa kadhizayti yaana.
2PE 3:4 Issti qass “Goda Yesusay yaana giza ufayssi yootetibeynee? Histin izi awan dizee? Beni nu Aawati hayqossope ha simmin, haniza miishey wurikka medhettosope ha simmin hekko kase ba diza mala dees” geetes.
2PE 3:5 Heyti he asati kase daro wodepe kase saloy Xoossa qaalan medhetoyssane biittayka haathafene haathan dizayssa erishe kaadetes.
2PE 3:6 He wode diza alamezi haathan miteti dhayides.
2PE 3:7 Hessaththoka ha7i diza saloyne biittay nagaranchati dhayana diza pirida gallasi gakanas tamas giig uttida.
2PE 3:8 Ta siiqoto! inte gidiko Goda achchan issi gallas shi laytha mala, qasseka shi laythi issi gallas mala gididayssa hessa he hanoza balopite.
2PE 3:9 Issi issi asatas milatizayssa mala Goday ba yootida ufayssa qaala polanas gam7enako shiin asi wurikka maaristana malane ay asika dhayontta mala koyidi izi inte gishshi takkes.
2PE 3:10 Goda gallassay qasse kayiso yeetha mala qopontta dishin gakki wodhana. He gallas saloti gita girethan adhdhana. Medhetethi wurikka taman xuugeti dhayana, biittayine iza bolla dizazi wurikka xuugettana.
2PE 3:11 Hessa gishshi heyti wurikka hessaththo dhayanaz gidiko histin inte geeshatethan Xoossas goynishe daanas intes waani bessenee?
2PE 3:12 Hessa gishshi Xoossa gallasay yanayssa inte lammotizaytinne izi elelli yaana mala oothizayta giditte. He gallas saloy taman xuugeti dhayana. medhetethatika tama seelan seerana.
2PE 3:13 Gido attin nuni izi nuusu immida ufayssa mala xiillotetha oothoy oothetizasso oratha salone oratha biitta naagoosu.
2PE 3:14 Hessa gishshi ta siiqoto! hessi wurikka hanana gallas inte naagishe diiko Goday intena inte bolla boroy bayinda dishin sarotethan demmana mala minni ditte.
2PE 3:15 Nu Goda danda7ay intena ashshanas gididayssa inte erite. Nu siiqo isha Phawulosay bess imettida eratetha mala izi intes xaafidayssi hayssako.
2PE 3:16 Izi hayssa ha hanoza gishshi ba kiittattan wurson hayssathoka xaafides. Iza kiittata giddon eranas waayssiza issi issi hanoti deettes. Eratethi isttas paccidayitine nam7u qofan yooqu gizayti hara geesha maxaafata mirqqizayssathoka haytaka issti mirqqana. Istti hessaththo oothizay bess dhayanaskko.
2PE 3:17 Ta ishato! inte qass hessa kasetidi erida gishshi hanko makal7ata bala geedon goocheti biid kase inte minni dizasope kundontta mala naagettite.
2PE 3:18 Hessape bollara nu Godane nu dhale Yesus Kiristoosa kiyatethanine iza shaaki eron pude diccite. Izas ha7ika medhinasikka bonchoy gido. Amin7i.
1JO 1:1 Dey qaala gish koyrope dizayssa nu nu haythan siydaysane nu ayfera be7idaysa loo7ethi xellidays nu kushera ooyki be7idassa gish hsa7os.
1JO 1:2 Deyoykka qoncides, nukka nu ayfera beydi markatos. Izas iza aawa achan dizasane nuskka qoncida medhiina deyo gish nu intes Yootos.
1JO 1:3 Inteskka nunara isipetethi dana mala nuni be7idaysanne siydaysa intes yootos. Nu isipetethayka aawarane iza na Yesus Kiristossarako.
1JO 1:4 Nu ufaysay kumetha gidanamala nu hayssa intes xafosu.
1JO 1:5 Nu izape siydi intes yootiza kiitay Xoossi poo7o iza acahan mulekka dhumay dena gizaysako.
1JO 1:6 Nu dhuman simeretishe izara nuusu isipetethi dees; Nu giiko wordotosu attin tuman dokko.
1JO 1:7 Gido attin izi poo7on diza mala nukka poo7on simeretiko nu garisan nuus isipetethi dees; iza na Yesuss Kirstosa suthi nuna Nagara wurisofe geshees.
1JO 1:8 Nu nunan nagaray bawaa gikko nurka nuna balethos; Tumaykka nunan deena.
1JO 1:9 Nuni nu nagara paaxiiko izi nu nagara atto ganasinne nu marika7atethafe nuna wursi geshanas izi amanetidadene xiiloko.
1JO 1:10 Nu nagara oothi beyko giikko iza nu woradancha kesosne iza qalayka nunan dena.
1JO 2:1 Ta nayto ta intes hayssa xafizay inte nagara oothonta malako gido attin oonikka nagara oothiko Aawa achan nus xabaqay dees. izika xiilloza Yesuss Kirstossako.
1JO 2:2 Izi nu nagaray atto geetetena mala oge gigisizade. Hesikka nuna xalala gidontta kumetha alame asasara attin nuus xalla gidena.
1JO 2:3 Nu iza azazota polliko nu iza eridaysa hessan amanetos.
1JO 2:4 “Ta iza erays” Gishe iza azazo polontade gidiko he uray wordo asa attiin tumay he uran dena.
1JO 2:5 Qase oonikka iza qaala nagiko tumu Xoossa siqqoy he 7uran polletides. Nuni izan dizaysa erizay hessankko.
1JO 2:6 Ta izan days giza uray oonikka Yesuss simeretida mala simeristanas beeses.
1JO 2:7 Ta siqoto! ta intes xahaaththaizaysi kasse intes dizaro intekon gam77ida azazoyo attin hara ooratha azazo gidena. Gam77ida azazoya kasse inte siyda qaalako.
1JO 2:8 Hara bagara ta intes xahaaththaizay dhumay adhi bishin tumu poo7on gish iza achanka inte achan tumu gidida ooratha azazoko.
1JO 2:9 Poo7on daysi gishe ba isha ixiizadey ha7ikka dhuma gidon dees.
1JO 2:10 Be isha siqqizadey poo7on dees; he uras dhuphe gidiza mishi denna.
1JO 2:11 Gido attin ba isha ixxizadey gidiko dhuma gidon dees; dhuman simeretes. Dhumay iza qoqisida gish izi awa biizakkone ba bizaso erena.
1JO 2:12 Ta nayto inte nagaray Yesus kiristoosape denddidayssan atto geetetida gish ta intes xafays.
1JO 2:13 Aawato! kasse koyrope dizaysa iza inte eriza gish ta intes xafays; Natethato inte iitta uraa Xala7e xoonida gish ta intes xahaaththaays.
1JO 2:14 Natetha nayto! inte Aawa erida gish ta intes xafays. Aawato! koyrope dizaysa iza inte erida gish ta intes xafays. Natethato! inte miinota gidida gishinne Xoossa qaalay intenan diza gish inte iitta ura Xala7e xoonida gish ta intes xafays.
1JO 2:15 Haysa alameza woykko ha alamezan diza ay mishekka dosopite; Oonika ha alameza dosiiko Aawa siqoy izade achchan deena.
1JO 2:16 Gasoykka ha alamezan dizay wuri asho amoteth ayfes loo7one dusan ceqeteth hayti alamepe attin Xoossa Aawape yizayta gidetenna.
1JO 2:17 Alameynne alamen diza amotethi adhana shin Xoossa shene pollizayti gidikko medhinaas daana.
1JO 2:18 Nayto haysi wurisetha sate. Inte siyda mala Kirstosa eqetizadey yaana. Ha7ikka Kirstosara eqetiza daroti yida. Haysi wurisetha sate gididaysa nu hayssan eros.
1JO 2:19 Isti nu gidofe kezida. Gido attin isti kasseka bagga gidettena. Istti nu bagga gididakko nunara miinni eqqanakoshin; Gido attin istti wuri nu bagga gidontaysi eretana mala nuupe shaaketida
1JO 2:20 Intena qasse Kirstossay xiillo ayanan tiyides; Hessa gish inte wurikka tuma ereista.
1JO 2:21 Ta intes xafizay inte tuma eronta gish gidena. Gido attin inte tuma eriza gishinne tuma garisafe ayko wordoyka betonttaysa inte eriza gishasa.
1JO 2:22 Yesussa izi Kirstossa gidena gi kadizadefe hara wordanchay oone? He uray Aawanne naaza kadiiza Kirstossara eqetizadeko.
1JO 2:23 Naaza kadizades oonasika Aaway deena; Naaza ekizades wurisos izas Aawayka dees.
1JO 2:24 Inte koyro siyda qalaya intenan du; inte koyro siydara intenan diko intekka nazanne aawan daana.
1JO 2:25 Medhina deyoyi izi nuus immana gida ufaysa qaalako.
1JO 2:26 Intena balethiza asata gish hayssa intes xafadis.
1JO 2:27 Inte qase izape ekida xiillo ayanay intenan diza gish haray oonikka intena tamarisanas bessena. Izi intena tamarisanays tumu attin worido gidena; Hessa gish xiillo ayanay intena tamarisida mala kirstoosana deyite.
1JO 2:28 Hesa gish nayto izi qonciza wode nusu xalatethi danamala izi yiza wodeka nu iza sinthan yeletonta mala inte izan deyte.
1JO 2:29 Izi xiillo gididaysa inte eriza gidiko xiillo oothizay wuri izape yelletidaysa inte ereta.
1JO 3:1 Nuni Xoossa nayta getistana mala aaway darisi siqqida iza siqqoy nus aymla giitakko ane beyitte! Tumukka nu iza naytako. Alamey nuna eronta agiday iza eronta agida gishiko.
1JO 3:2 Ta ishato nuni ha7i Xoossa naytako buro nu ay hananakone haii qonccibeyna Kirstosa qoncciza wode nu iza beyanane nuka iza milatanaysa nu eros.
1JO 3:3 Haysa izan ufaysa oothizay wuri izi gesh gidida mala bena geshes.
1JO 3:4 Nagara oothzay wurikka makal7a nagarayka makal7ako.
1JO 3:5 Izi nagara dhaysanas qonccidaysa inte ereta. Izanka nagaray ba.
1JO 3:6 Izan diza uray oonikka nagara oothena. Nagara oothiza uray oonikka gidko iza beyibeyana woykko eribeyna.
1JO 3:7 Ta nayto Intena oonikka balethontamala nagetite. Izi xiillo gidida mala xiilo oothizadeyka xiilokko.
1JO 3:8 Nagara oothizay xala7epeko gasoyka xala7ey koyropeka nagara oothizadeko. Xoossa nay qoncidayka xala7e ootho lalanasa.
1JO 3:9 Xoossafe yelettiday wurii nagara oothena. Xoossa zerethi izan diza gishine izi Xoossafe yelettida gish nagara oothana danda7ena.
1JO 3:10 Xoossa naytinne xala7e nayti shaketi eretizay hessankko. Xillo oothontayinne ba isha siqqontay wuri Xoossafe gidena.
1JO 3:11 Inte koyro siydara nu nu garisan siiqistana beses getetida kiitaya hanoko.
1JO 3:12 Iita baga gididi ba isha isethi wodhiida Qayele mala gidopite. izi aazas wodhiide? Gasoykka iza oothoy ita isha oothoy loo7o gididasa.
1JO 3:13 Ta ishato intena 7lame 7assay ixiko malaletopite.
1JO 3:14 Nuni nu ishata dosiza gish hayqope gede deyon piinidaysa nu eros. Siqoy baynda uray wuri hayqo garsan dees.
1JO 3:15 Be isha ixiza uray shempo wodhida asa. Shempo wodhidades medhina deyoy bayndaysa inte ereta.
1JO 3:16 Yesuss Kirstosay ba shempo nu gish aathi imida gish siqqoy azakone nu hessan eros. Nukka nu shempo nu ishata gish aathi imanas nus beses.
1JO 3:17 Mishey diza uray oonikka ba ishay wayetishin beydi izas michetonta agiko Xoossa siiqqoy izan wani danee?
1JO 3:18 Ta nayto tumu oothonippe attiin co dunaninne qalan xala siiqeteth ane agos.
1JO 3:19 Nunii tumu baga gididaysa hayssan erosinne nu woznaka iza sinththan shempsos.
1JO 3:20 Hesikka nu woznay nu bolla pirdiza mishan wurisonkko. Xoossi nu wozina qofape bolara gidida gisha izi wursi eres.
1JO 3:21 Ta ishato nu wozzinay nu bolla pirdonta agikko nus Xoossa sinthan babiza mishi deena.
1JO 3:22 Nu azazota nagiza gishine iza ufaysizazi oothiza gish nu iza wosizaz wursi nu izape ekana.
1JO 3:23 Iza azazoykka nu iza naza Yesus Kirstosa amananasinne izi nuna azazidamala nuni nu garsan dosistana malako.
1JO 3:24 Iza azazota nagizayti wurii izan detes, izikka istan des. Izi nunan dizaysa nu izi nus imida ayanan eros.
1JO 4:1 Ta ishato ayana wursi amanopite. Gido attiin ayanati Xoossapekonne pacci beyte. Gasoykka daro wordo nabeti biitta bolla laletida.
1JO 4:2 Inte Xoossa ayana erana ogey; “Yesuss Kirstossay asa asho maydi yides” giza ayanay wuri Xoossafeko.
1JO 4:3 “Yesuss Kirstosay asa asho mayidi yides” gonta ayanay Xoossafe gidena. Kase izi yana gishin inte siyda Kirstossara eqetizaysa ayanay hessakko. Ha7ikka izi alame bolla dees.
1JO 4:4 Ta nayto inte Xoossita. Inte ista Xonidista gasoykka intenan dizay alamen dizaysafe adhees.
1JO 4:5 Isti alame bagakko, hessa gish isti hasa7izay wuri alampe kezizaysakko. alame asay isti gizaysa siiyes.
1JO 4:6 Nu qasse Xoossa bagakko, Xoosu erizay nu gizaz siyana shin Xoossa baga gidontadey gidiko nu gizaz siyena. Tumma ayananne wordo ayana nu shakki erizay hayssankko.
1JO 4:7 Ta ishato, siqoy Xoossafe gidida gish nu nu garisa ane siqetos. Asa siqqiza asi wuri Xoossafe yelettidanne Xoosu erizadekko.
1JO 4:8 Ase siqonta assi Xoosu erena. Azas giko Xoosi siqoko.
1JO 4:9 Xossay nu garsan ba siqqo qonccsiday nu iza bagara deyo demanamala ba na isneza ha dugge ha alamezan yedidaysankko.
1JO 4:10 Nuni Xoossu siqqibeykko shin izi nuna siqides. Nu nagara dhaysana mala ba naza yeddides. Siqo gusikka hessakko.
1JO 4:11 Ta ishato, Xoosi nuna hayssatho siqqiko nukka nu garsan siqistanas beses.
1JO 4:12 Xoosu be7ida uray oonikka deena. Nu nu garsan siqetiza gidiko Xoosi nunan dana. Iza siqoyka nuna pollistana.
1JO 4:13 Izi nus ba ayana imida gish nu izan dizaysanne izikka nunan dizaysa nu hessan eros.
1JO 4:14 Away ba naza hayssa ha alame asa ashanas yedidaysa nu beydosinne iza giish maarkatos.
1JO 4:15 Yesussay Xoossa na gididaysa amanidi marikatiza wurson Xoossi deesinne, izadeykka Xoossan dees.
1JO 4:16 Hesa gish, Xoossi nuna siqiza siqo nu eros. Nu iza siqqon amanetos. Xossi siqqo. Siqon diza uray Xoossan dees. Xoosikka he uran dees.
1JO 4:17 Nuni hayssa biitta bolla deyzay Kirstosay deydamala gidida gish nuus piirda galas baboy deena. Hesankka siqqoy nunan kumeth gides.
1JO 4:18 Siiqo garsan baboy ba, tumu siqqoy gidiko babo kesi wora yeges. Baboy qixxatera isfe ooyketi des. Babiza ura siqqoy kumeth gidena.
1JO 4:19 Izi kassetidi nuna siqqda gish nukka iza siiqos.
1JO 4:20 Oonikka Xoosu siqays giishe ba isha ixxiko he uray wordo. Be ayfera beyza ba isha siqonta uray ba ayfen beyonta Xoossa siqanas danda7ena.
1JO 4:21 “Xoossu siqiza assi wurikka ba isha siqanas beses” Giiza ha azazoza izi nuus imides.
1JO 5:1 Yesussay izi Kirstossa gididaysa amanizay wuri Xoossafe yelettidas. Aawa dosizay wuri nazaka izatho doses.
1JO 5:2 Nuni Xoosu dosikone iza azazo nagiko nu Xoossa nayta siqizaysa hessan eros.
1JO 5:3 Xoosu doso gusi iza azazo nagoko. Iza azazoti dexxo gidetena.
1JO 5:4 Gasoykka Xoossafe yelettiday wurii alame xones. lame xonizaykka nu amanoko.
1JO 5:5 Yesussay Xoossa na gididaysa amanizadefe attiin alame xonizay haray oone?
1JO 5:6 Hathanine suththan yiday hayssa Yesus Kiristosako. Izi hathaninne suththan yides attiin hathan xala yibeyna. Hessakka iza gish markatizay ayanakko. He ayanay tumu ayanako.
1JO 5:7 Hessa gish izas heedzdzu markati dettes.
1JO 5:8 Heytika; ayana, hathenne suththukko. Heedzdzata qalayka isinoko.
1JO 5:9 Nu asa marikatet ammanikko Xoossa markatethi hessafe adhees. Hesikka izi ba naza gish immida Xoossa markatethakko.
1JO 5:10 Xoossa naan amanizade wurisso wozinan iza gish markay dees. Xoosu amanontay wurikka Xoossi benaza gish immida markatetha amanonta gish iza wordoses.
1JO 5:11 Iza marikatethaykka Xoossi medhina deyo nus imides, he deyoyka iza nazan dees, gizaysakko.
1JO 5:12 Nazi dizades deyoy dees; Xoossa nay bayndades deyoy baawa.
1JO 5:13 Intes Xoossa nan amanizaytas medhina deyoy dizaysa inte erana mala ta hayssa intes xahaaththaays.
1JO 5:14 Nu Xoossa sinth shiqqanas nus diza xalatethi hayssakko. Nu ay mishekka iza shene mala wosiko izi nu wossa siiyana.
1JO 5:15 Nu iza wosiza miish izi wursi siyzaysa nu eriza gidiko nu wosida misha wursi ekanaysa nu eros.
1JO 5:16 Oonikka ba ishay bena hayqqos gathonta nagara oothishin beyikko izas woosso. Xoossikka hayqos gathonta nagara oothidaytas deyo imana. Hayqos gathiza nagaraykka dees. Hayqos gaathiza nagara gish woso giike.
2JO 1:1 Tape ciimazappe; tumappe ta dosiza doretida godateysinne izi naytas, tana xala gidonta tumu erizayti wuri dosizaris, kitetida kita;
2JO 1:2 Gasoykka haysi tummay ha7ikka nu giddon dizaysanne sinthafekka medhinas danaysakko.
2JO 1:3 Xoossa awappenne iza na Yesuss Kirstosappe Kiyatethi, marotethiine saroy tumanine siqqon nunara giido.
2JO 1:4 Ne naytape bagati aawape nus imetida azazoza mala tuman miini dizayta ta beyida gish daro ufa7istadis.
2JO 1:5 Ha7ikka Godateye, kassepeka dizaro attiin ta nes hara ooratha azazo xafikke; hesiikka nu nu garsan siqistanaysakko.
2JO 1:6 He siqoykka nu iza azazoza mala danaysako. Azazozikka inte koyro siyda mala siqqon deyana malako.
2JO 1:7 Yesus Kirstossay asa asho maydi yibeyna giza amanonta daro balethizayti alame bolla laletida. Heyta malay ay assikka as ballethizadene Kirstosara eqetizadeko.
2JO 1:8 Inte gidikko inte dabura wagape mella atontamalanne kumetha woyytto ekana mala inte hu7es nagetite.
2JO 1:9 Kirstossa timrte mala donta urayinne iza tmirteppe baletidi kare keziza ura oonanikka Xoossi deena. Kirstosa timrten dizadey gidiko izas aawayne aawa nay deetes.
2JO 1:10 Oonikka intekko yishe hessa he timrteza ekii yonta ura mokkii ekofiitene saro gopiite.
2JO 1:11 Moki ekiddii ba so gelthizadey he ura oothon izara isino gidees.
2JO 1:12 Ta intes xafanas koyza daro miish des shin waraqataninne qalamen xafana mala koyke. Gidiikokka nu ufaysay kumeth gidana mala ta inteko bada inte sinthan intenara hasa7anas ufays oothays.
2JO 1:13 Doretidari naytii ne miicheyi nayti nena saro geetes.
3JO 1:1 Taape ciimazape, tumape ta siiqiza ta siiqqo laagge gayyosas.
3JO 1:2 Ta ishazo, ne shempoy loo7on dizamala ne asatethay loo7o dana malane ne oothizazi wurikka nees giiga gidanamala ta nees wossays.
3JO 1:3 Ne tumas amanetidade gidida mala qassekka ne hanoy wuri tumu gididaysa isi isi amaniza asati taakko yidi ne gish yotiin siyada ta daro ufa7istadis.
3JO 1:4 Gasoykka ta nayti loo7onne tuman smeretishin siisafe adhiza hara ufaysi tas deena.
3JO 1:5 Ta ishazo issti nes imath gidikokka nenii ne ishatas oothida mishe wurson amanistadasa.
3JO 1:6 Ne bolla ay mala siiqqoy dizakone isti ne gish wosa keeththa asa sinthan marikatida. Isti biiza oogen Xooss ufaysiza hanon ne ista madikko loo7o oothassa.
3JO 1:7 Ays gikko isti Xoossa amanontaytape aykokka ekonta Kirstossa suntha gish mela kezida.
3JO 1:8 Hesa giish nu isippe tumas oothan mala heytanta malata mokkii ekana beses.
3JO 1:9 Ta Wossa keethas hayssafe kase xafadis. Gido attiin kallethizade gidana koyiza Diyoxraxossay nu gizaz ekena.
3JO 1:10 Hesa gish, ta he bikko izi ba ita qalan nu sunthu moranas oothidaysa ta intes qonccisana. Hesikka izas gidonta ixin amaniza asa mokki ekena; Mokkii ekana koyzaytakka digesinne wossa keethafe kesi godes.
3JO 1:11 Ta ishazo, loo7ota milata attiin ita asata milatopa. Loo7o oothizadey wurikka Xoossa asa. Ita oothizadey qasse Xooss beybeyna.
3JO 1:12 Dimexrosas asi wuri loo7o markates. Tumaykka izas markataysu. Nukka izas markatos, intekka nu markkay tumu gididaysa ereta.
3JO 1:13 Ta nees xahaaththaana buro daro yoy dees shin ta nes waraqatan xahaaththaanas koyikke.
3JO 1:14 Ta nena mata wode beyanas ufays oothays, he wode nu isife uti hasa7ana.
3JO 1:15 Ane saron da; ne lageti nena saro saro getes, ta lagista sunthu sunthu xeygada saro ga.
JUD 1:1 Yesus kiristoosas othiza Yaqobe isha Yudape, Intes xeyigetidaytas Xoossi Aaway siiqizaytas Yesus kiristoosay naagidaytas wurisotas;
JUD 1:2 Maarotethi sarotethine siiqoy intes daro.
JUD 1:3 Ta siiqoto nu issife attida atotetha gishshi ta intes xaafanas daro koyadisishin ha7i qasse nam77anthontta issito Xoossi asas immida ammano gishshi inte daro baaxxistana mala ta intena zorays. Ta intes xaafanas taas tooho gidides.
JUD 1:4 Istta bolla piridistanayssi daro wodepe kase istta gish xafetida asati inteko kolixxi gelida. Heytantti xoossu eronttayta, nu Goda kiyatetha coo mela laammizaytane Xoossa goynotaytako. Izi berika nuna haarizayssane nuusi Goda gidida Yesus kiristoosaka kadettes.
JUD 1:5 Inte hessa wurisoka kaseti erikoka Goday ba dereza Gibixefe kessidi ashidayssane hankko ammanonttayta guyepe dhayssidayssa ta intena akekissana koyayss.
JUD 1:6 Hessaththoka ba boncho naagonta ixxidi ba dizaso yeddida kiitanchata inte yuushi qopana mala Xoossi istta gita pirida gallas gakanas medhina qashos giridi gida dhuman naagi wothides.
JUD 1:7 Hessaththoka Sodomene Gamooray qasseka istta heeran diza katamatika laymatidanne salo medhetethatara laymatanas amottida. Hesa gishshi istti medhina taman xuugistanaytas lemiso gidida. f/ Haysi qofazi eketiday Medhetistaha maxafa 19.5-11 gidishin Sodeme asay Loxxekko, yida immathatara laymatana koydayssa beses.
JUD 1:8 Hessaththoka heyti he asati berika ba agumo kaallidi berika ba asho tunathetes. Beepe bollara dizaytas azazetetena. Istti salon bonchora dizaytaka cayettes.
JUD 1:9 Haray attoshin salo kiitanchata halaqay Mikka7eley Muse asho gishshi izara palamettishe “Nena Goday hanqeto!” gides attin izas casha qaala zaaribeyna.
JUD 1:10 Hayti asati qasse isttas eretontta ixxida mishsha wursi cashe cayetes. Aykoka erontta mehista mala coo ba qopi ekkida miishi isttas diiko istti hessan dhayana.
JUD 1:11 Istti Qayele ogen bida gishshi miishas giidi Bala7ame mala balan kunidida. Qasse Qoorey eqettida mala isttika eqettidi dhayida gish istas aye.
JUD 1:12 Hayti ha asati yeellay bayinda laymma hanora issi bolla inte digiseson bettiza wode intes dhuphe gidetes. Istti bessi xalala qopeetes. Istti carikon biza iray baynda shaara malako. Ayfey ayifiza woden ayfey baynda xaphope dhoqalletidi nam77uto melida miththa malako.
JUD 1:13 Istti yeelachiza ba oothoza wolqama abba dambala gopontto mala copu hisitizaytako. Gird gida dhumay istta merinas naagizayssane coo mela waayetiza xoolinteta malako.
JUD 1:14 Adamepe ha simmin lapuntho yeletethi gidida Henokey hizgides “Heko Xoossi qooday baynda geesha kiitanchatara asa wuriso bolla piridanas yaana.
JUD 1:15 Heyta Xoossas goynontta asati oothida iitti ootho geedon istta izi qaxxayana. Addafeka Xooss heyta bees goynontta nagaranchata bolla istti hasa7ida iitta miishata gishshi izi istta bolla piridana.”
JUD 1:16 Heyti he asati wuriso wode zuzumettizaytane ay miishanka ufa7etti eronttaytako. Istti ba iitta amo kaallizaytako. Istta duunan otoretetha qaalay kumides. Bessi ba go7a koyishe ase aadasheetes.
JUD 1:17 Inte ta siiqoto nu Goda Yesus kiristoosay kiitti yeddidayti hayssafe kase yootida qaala akekite.
JUD 1:18 Istti “Wode wurisethan Xoossa shenepe haakidayti berika ba iitta amo kaallishe ase qidhizayti yaana” giidi intes kase yooti wothida.
JUD 1:19 Heyti asa issa issafe shaakizayta; asho amotethi kaalizaytane isttan xiillo ayanay bayindaytakko.
JUD 1:20 Ta ishato, inte qasse wurisofe bollara inte geesha ammanon minni eqqite. Xiillo ayananka minni woossite.
JUD 1:21 Nu Goda Yesus kiristoosay ba maarotethan intena medhina deyon gathanayssa naagetishe intenateha Xoossa siiqon naagite.
JUD 1:22 Sidhishe diza asatas mishetite;
JUD 1:23 Issi issi asata tamape kesi ashite haratas yashatethan michettite shin nagaran tunida istta asatetha bochchida mayoka wuris ixxite.
JUD 1:24 Intena kundethafe ashanasine intena wothoy bayindayta hisitidi ufayssan ba boncho sinththi shiishanas danda7izayssas;
JUD 1:25 Izi xalala Xoossu gididanne nuusi dhale gidida Goda Yesus kiristoosa baggara benipe doomidi ha7i gakanasine medhinasika bonchoyne gitateth, wolqayne Godateth izas gido. Amin7i.
REV 1:1 Hayssi ajjutazi mata wode biitta bolla hananayssa bass oothizayta bessana mala Xoossi Yesus kiristoosas immidayssakko. Yesus kiristoosayka ba kiittancha kiittidi ba oothanchaza Yanisas hayssa ajjutaza qonccisides.
REV 1:2 Yanisayka Xoossa qaala gishshine Yasus Kirstoosay tamarsida tuma gishshi qasseka Yanisay ba ayfen beyidayssaka wursi marikattides.
REV 1:3 Hayssi wurikka hananay mata woden gidida gishshi hayssa tinbite qaala nababbiza uray anjettidadeko. Hessaththoka tinbite qaala siyizayttine ha tinbite qaala xaafettidayssa poli oothizayti istti anjettidaytakko.
REV 1:4 Isiyan diza laapun woossa keethatas, Kaseka dizayssafe, ha7ika dizayssapene, buroka yaana Xoossafe iza aliga sinthan diza laapun ayanatape hessathoka hayqofe denthan bayra gididayssafe, ha biitta kawotas kawone ammanettida marika gididayssafe, nuna siiqizayssafene ba suunthan nuna nu nagarape geeshida Yesus kiristoosape kiyatethine, saroteth, intes gido.
REV 1:6 Nuni Yesus kiristoosa Aawa Xoossas oothana mala nuna izi kawotane qessista kessida Yesus kiristoosas bonchoyne wolqay medhinape medhina gakanas izas gido! Amin7i.
REV 1:7 Heko izi salope shaarara yaana. Kase iza cadi wodhidaytika attontta asi wurikka iza beyana. Biittan diza dereyka eureka iza gishshi yeekana. Hayssi ha yoozi tumukko. Amin7i.
REV 1:8 Kasekane ha7ika dizayssi buropeka yaanayssi wuris danda7iza Godaa Xoossay “Alipayne omegay, koyroyne wurisethi tanakko” gees.
REV 1:9 Tani Yesus Kiristoosa waayeza iza kawotetha qasseka iza danda7an intenara issife gidida ta inte ishay Yanisay Xoossa qaalanine Yesus Kiristoosas marikattida gishshi qachettada Fixximo geetettiza abba gidon diza dere daarin dayss.
REV 1:10 Tani Goda gallas ayanan coo liphiphi gishin dinkke giiretha malay gita giireth taape guyera hizgishin siyadis,
REV 1:11 “Neni beyzayssa waraqatan xaafida laapun woossa keethatas heytika Efesones, Sarimones, Phergamones, Tiyaxirones, Sardeses, Piladelpiyasine Lodoqiyas yedda”
REV 1:12 Hessa taas ooni yootidakone erana gaada ta guye yuuya xeelliza wode woriqafe oothetida istta billa wothiza laapun balata beyadis.
REV 1:13 He xompe wothiza balata gidon asa na milatizade demmadis. Izika hiriki too gakkiza adusa mayo mayidi tira bolla worqa mayo mayides.
REV 1:14 Iza hu7eyne iza hu7e binanay qass boothu shachi milatiza bootha suufe malakko. Iza ayfetika tama laco milatetes.
REV 1:15 Iza tooti tama bonqqon qoxetti kezida qariqimala milatetes. Qaalayka wolqama piissa haathey giiriza mala giires.
REV 1:16 Izi ba oshacha kushen laapun xoolinttista oykkidi uttides. Iza duunape nam7u baggara qara mashay kezes. Iza ayfesoy awa arishe mala xolqqettes.
REV 1:17 Tani hessa beyada hayqqida asa milatada iza too garisan kunidadis. Izi qass ta bolla ba oshacha kushe wothidi hizgides “Ne babbofa! Koyroyne wurisethi tanakko.
REV 1:18 Tani paxa dayss. Kase hayqadissikoshin heko tani hayssafe medhinas paxa deyana. Hayqo bollane Si7ole bolla tani Godakko.
REV 1:19 Hessa gishshi neni be7idayssa ha7i dizayssane guyepe hananayssa xaafa.
REV 1:20 Neni ta oshacha kushen beyida laapun xoolinttistane xompe, istta bola wothiza laapun worqqafe oothetida balata xuuray heko hayssakko. Laapun xoolintteti laapun woossa keethata kiittanchatakko. Xompe wothiza laapun worqqa ballati laapun woossa keethatakko.
REV 2:1 Eefesonen woossa keeththa kiitanchas hizga xaafa “Hayssi laapun xoolinttista ba oshacha kushen oykidadefene xompe wothiza laapun worqqa ballata giddon simerettizadefe yootettides”
REV 2:2 Tani ne oothozane ne dafetetha, ne danda7aka erayss. Neni qass iittata yega adhdhanas danda7onttayssa hawarista dishe bena hawarista gizaytaka shaakada istta wordanchata gidoyssa ne gakka demmidayssa ta erayss.
REV 2:3 Neni danda7an minna eqqidayssane ta suntha gishshi saletontta ne waaye beyindayssa ta erayss.
REV 2:4 Gidikoka ta nena kadhiza issi miishi dess. Hessika beni kase ne siiqoza aggadasa.
REV 2:5 Neni kase ay mala dhoqason dashe ha7i qass ne waana kundidakone ane yuusha qofane maarotethan simma gela. Ne kase oothiza beni ne oothoza zaara otha. Ne hessa wursa zaara oothontta ixxiko ta neeko yaana. Neni maarotethan gelontta ixxiko ne xompe iza bolla wothiza balla he izi dizasope ta dentha gidana.
REV 2:6 Gido attin ta nena galatiza issi miishi dess. Hessika tani ixxiza niqola bagga asa ootho neka ixxadasa.
REV 2:7 “Ayanay woossa keethatas gido” geetettizayssa haythey diza urey wurikka siyo. Xoonida uray Xoossa ganate giddon diza deyo miththa ayfe maana mala ta oothana.
REV 2:8 Sarminese woossa keethas kiitanchas hizga xaafa, “Hayssi koyrone wuriseth gididape kase hayqidadefene ha7i qass paxa dizadefe yootetidazikko.
REV 2:9 Tani ne waayezane ne manqotetha erayss. Gidikoka neni dureko. Ayhude gidontta dashe bena nuni Ayhudeko giza xala7e maabara gididayti heyti ne sunthu mooroyssa ta erayss.
REV 2:10 Buro sinthafe ne bolla gakkana metos babbofa. Inte paacettana mala intefe issi issi ura dabulosay qasho keeththa gelithana. Tamu gallas gakkanaas inte waaye beyanashin ne hayqqana gakkanaas ammanetidade gida. Tani ness deyo akilile immana.
REV 2:11 “Ayanay woossa keethatas gizayssa haythey diza uray siyo! xoonida uray nam7antho hayqon qohettena.
REV 2:12 Pherigamone woossa keeththa kiitanchas hizga xaafa, “Hayss nam7u baggara qare mashsha oykidadefe yootettidazikko.
REV 2:13 Neni xala7e aligay dizason dizayssa tani erayss. Gido attin neni ta suntha lo7etha oykadasa. Ne tana ammanizayssa agabeyka. Taas amanetida marika gidida Anttiphasey xala7ey diza inte kataman asa kushen hayqida wodeka ne tana ammano agabeyka.
REV 2:14 Gidikoka ta nena kadhiza issi miishey ne bolla dess. Hessika Bala7ame timirtte oykida issi issi asati inte giddon dettes. Hessi bala7amey Isiraa7eele asay eeqas yarshettida kathi miidine laymma laymmatidi dhuphistana mala Baalaqe zoridadekko.
REV 2:15 Hessaththoka niqola bagga asata tmirtte oykida asatika inte gidon dettes.
REV 2:16 Hessa gishshi maarotethan gela, akkaye giiko tani ellesada neeko baada nena ta duunape keziza masha milatiza qaalara olana.
REV 2:17 Ayanay woossa keethatas gizayssa haythey diza uray siyo! xoonida uras ta qotan diza man7afe immana. Iza bolla oratha sunthi xaafettida bootha shuchuka izas ta immana. Hessaka ekkidadefe attin hara uray oonka erenna.
REV 2:18 “Tiyaxirone woossa keeth kiitanchas hizga xaafa “Hayssi tama lacho milatiza ayfeti dizadefene bonqqida taman geli qoxetti kezida xariqimala milatiza tooti dizaddefe Xoossa naape kiitettidazikko.
REV 2:19 Tani ne oothone ne siiqo, ne ammanone ne hagazo, ne denda7an minnoyssaka erayss. Kase oothozape guyeyssi adhdhizayssaka ta erayss.
REV 2:20 Gido attin ta nena kadhiza miishi dess. Hessika bena “Ta nabekko” giza maccashayo Elizabelo neni bessa aggida gishshi iza taas oothizayti laymma laymmatana malane eeqas yarishetida kathi maana mala iza tamarisada balethadus.
REV 2:21 Iza maarotethan gelana mala ta izis wode immadis shin iza qass ba laymmatethaf simmanas koyabeyku.
REV 2:22 Hessa gishshi ta izo waaye aliga bolla yeggana. Izira oothida asati ba iitta oothope maarotethan simontta ixiko izira issife laymmatida wurisota bolla gita meto ta ehana.
REV 2:23 Tani izi nayta hayqon qaxxayana. woossa keethati wurikka asa qofane asa amo shaaka erizay tana gididayssa erana. Tani intes issas issas izade ootho mala immana.
REV 2:24 “Tiyaxironen dizaytas intesine hayssa iitta timirtte tamaronttaytas wurisos hessathoka issi issi <xala7es hayssi ciimma xuurako> gtetetizayssa kaallonttayta intena tani hara tooho toossike.
REV 2:25 Gidikoka ta hee baana gakkanaas intes dizazi wuris minthi oykkite.
REV 2:26 xoonida urasine ta oothon wuriseth gakkanaas minnizades hanko dereta bolla ta godateth immana.
REV 2:27 Izi istta birata guufera haarana. Uriqafe medhettida miisha mala izi bukkidi liiqisana. Hessi he godatethayka tani ta Aawape ekoo godatetha malakko.
REV 2:28 Ta izas wontta bolla keziza xoolintta immana.
REV 2:29 Ayanay woossa keethatas gizayssa haythey dizay wuri siyo.
REV 3:1 Saridese woossa keeththa kiitanchas hizga xaafa “Hayssi laapun Xoossa ayanatane laapun xoolinttista oykidadefe yootetidazikko. Ta ne ootho erayss. Neni sunthan paxa daasa shin qass hayqqadasa.
REV 3:2 Beega! hayqqana matidayssane nees wurishe guuthu attida wolqayo zaara mintha. Tani ta Goda sinthan ne oothoy kumeth gidin beyabeyke.
REV 3:3 Hessa gishshi neni ay mala timirtte ekkidakone ne siyosayssa yuusha qopane naaga. maarotethanka gela; Neni beegontta aggiko qass ta kayso mala ne qopotta duxu gaana. Ta ay saaten neeko yanakone ne eraka.
REV 3:4 Gido attin ba mayo tunsontayti Sardesen guutha asati nenara dettes. Heyti bootha mayo mayanayssi isttas bessiza gishshi istti bootha mayo maydi tanara baana.
REV 3:5 xoonidadey isttathoka bootha mayo mayana. Izade sunthu tani ta Aawa sinthanine kiitanchata sinthan erisana. Deyon dizayta sunthi xaafettida deyo mazgabape quccike.
REV 3:6 “Ayanay woossa keethatas gizayssa haythey dizadey siyo.
REV 3:7 Fildilfiya woossa keeththa kiitanchas hizga xaafa “Hayssi geeshine tumancha gididayssafe Dawite keeththa qulife oykidadefe yootettidazikko. Izi doyidazi oonikka gordena. Izi gordidaz oonikka doyena.
REV 3:8 Tani ne ootho erayssi. Heko oonikka gordanas danda7ontta doya penge ne sinthan woththadis. Ne wolqay guuthu gididayssa ta erayss. Gidikoka ne ta qaala naagadasa. Ta sunthaka ne kadabeyka.
REV 3:9 Hessa gishshi bess Ayhude gidontta dishe bena Ayhude gizayti heyti xala7e maabarape gididayti wordoti yiidi ne too garisan kundana mala ta oothana. Tani nena siiqdayssa istti erana mala ta oothana.
REV 3:10 Neni danda7izade gida gaada ta nees yooto qaala ne naagida gishshi taka buro biitta bolla diza asa paacanas kumetha alame bolla yaana. Waayeza galas ta nena naagana.
REV 3:11 Heko ta eeson yaana. Ne aklile oonikka ekkontta mala ness dizazi lo7etha oyikka.
REV 3:12 Xoonida ura tani ta Godaa Xoossa keeththan tuussu histana. Izi heepe muleka kezena. Ta Goda sunthune ta Goda katamaza sunthuka ta iza bolla xaafana. Hana katamaya salope ta Goda achchafe wodhdhana ooratha Yerusalamekko. Taka ta ooratha suntha he izade bolla xaafana.
REV 3:13 Ayanay woossa keethatas yootizayssa haythey dizadey siyo.
REV 3:14 Lodoqiya woossa keeththa kiitanchas hizga xaafa “Hayssi <amin7i> gidadefe tumu ammanettida marka gididadefe Xoossa medhetethi wuri izape beettidadefe yootetidazikko.
REV 3:15 Tani ne ootho erays. Neni mooce woykko micha gidaka. Neni mooce woykko micha gididako lo7okoshin.
REV 3:16 Mooce woykko micha gidontta ne coo donbole gido gishshi ta nena ta duunape cutta kessana gayss.
REV 3:17 Ta dureko, taas daro haaroy dees, taas aykoyka paccibeyna” gaasa shin ne qass poynako aykoy bayinda maniqokko, qooqene ne kallo dizade gididayssa erabeykka.
REV 3:18 Ne dure gidana koyko taape taman paacettida worqa shammana mala neni ne kallotetha yeellatetha kamanas bootha mayo mayana malane xelanaska danda7ana mala ayife dhale shammada ne tiyettana mala ta nena zorayss.
REV 3:19 Tani ta dosizayta wursa hanqayssine qaxxayayis. Hessa gishshi neni minna, maarotethanka gela.
REV 3:20 Heko! tani pengen eqqada xeygayss, oonikka ta qaala siydi ba pengeza taas doyko ta izako gelada izadera maana. Izadeyka tanara maana.
REV 3:21 Tani xoonada ta Aawra iza algan uttidayssatho xoondadey hessathoka tanara issife ta alga bolla ta uttissana.
REV 3:22 Ayanay woossa keethatas gizayssa haythey dizay siyo.
REV 4:1 Hessaf guye tani salon doya diza penge beyadis. Tani koyro siyday dinka giiretha mala giireth hizgides “Haa pude keza, burope hanana miishata ta nena bessana”
REV 4:2 Ta heraka ayanan liphiphi gaada salan diza alga beyadis. He algaza bollaka issadey uttides.
REV 4:3 He alga bolla uttidayssa medhoy iyasphidene serdinone inqqu milayiza algaza yuuyi adhdhidi margide geetettiza inqqu milatiza zuulay dees.
REV 4:4 Hessaththoka he algaza yuuyi adhdhida nam7u tammane oyddu algati dettes. He algata bolla qass bootha mayo mayidi ba hu7e bolla worqa akilile woththida nam7u tammane oyddu cimati utti dettes.
REV 4:5 He algafe qass woliqanthine dada giirethi kezess. He alga sinthan poo7iza laapun xompeti dettes. Heytika Xoossa ayana laapunatakko.
REV 4:6 He alga sithan geesh milxi gida xolliqettiza masttoteda giza abbay dess. Iza gidon alga yushon guye baggara daro ayfera diza oyddu do7ati dettes.
REV 4:7 Koyro do7azi gaamo milatess. Nam7anthozi qass boora milatess. Hedzdzanthoza ayfesoy asa ayfeso milatess. oydanthozi qass piradhdhiza golle kafo milatess.
REV 4:8 He oyddu do7ati issay issay usupun qefera dettes. Qefista yushonine qefeta gidon ayfey kumides. Istti qamane gallasine “Geeshazo! Geeshazo! Geeshazo! wursa danda7iza Godo, kaseka, ha7ika dizayssi, buroka yaanayssi guussafe shempi erettena.
REV 4:9 He do7ati he alga bolla uttidayssasine medhinape medhina gakkanaas dizayssas gitateth, bonchone galataka shiishiza wode wurison,
REV 4:10 Nam7u tammane oyddu cimati medhinape medhina gakkanaas diza ba alga bolla uttidayssa sinthan gufannidi izas goynettes. Bee aklilistaka he alga sinthan woththidi hizgida,
REV 4:11 “Nu Goda Xoosso, Neni wursa medhdhida gishshi, Medhetethi wurikka medhettidayne shempora dizay ne shene gidida gishshi gitatethi, bonchoyne wolqayka ness besses” gida.
REV 5:1 He alga bolla uttidayssa oshacha kushen qaa7a garisanine bolla baggara xaafeti uttida laapun matafan gordettida issi xaaxeti uttida maxaafa beyadis.
REV 5:2 Issi mino kiitancha dayssi gita qaalara “Hayssa matamista birshidi ha Xoossa maxaafa doyanas bessiza uray onee?” gi hasa7ishin beyadis.
REV 5:3 Gido attini salonika gidin woykko biitta bolla woykko biittafe garisa bagganka he Xoossa maxaafa doydi iza gido gelanas xeellanas danda7ida uray oonikka bettibeyna.
REV 5:4 Taka he Xoossa maxaafa birishidi iza giddo xeellanas bessizadey bettontta aggida gishshi daro yekadis.
REV 5:5 Hessa wode chimatape issadey taas “Ne yeekopa! heko Ayhudata bagga gidida Dawite zarkefe dendida gaamoy izi kase xoonides. Izi he Xoossa maxaafazane laapun matameza doyanas danda7es” gides.
REV 5:6 Hessafe guye alga bollane oyddu do7ata gidon he cimata gidonka shukettida dorisa milatizayssi eqqidayssa beyadis. He dorisazas laapun kaceyne laapun ayfey dess. He ayfetika kumetha alame kiitettida Xoossa ayana laapunatakko.
REV 5:7 He dorisay yiidine alga bolla uttidayssa, oshacha kushen diza Xoossa maxaafa ekides.
REV 5:8 He Xoossa maxaafaza ekkida mala oyddu do7atine nam7u tammane oyddu cimati he dorisa sinthan ba liiphon gufannida. Isttika issadey ba kushen diitha mala miishi oykidida. Hessaththoka geeshata woossa gidida izan exaney kumida worqa xaaro ba kushen oykki dettes.
REV 5:9 Ooratha yeth hizgi yexxida “Neni asa duma duma kochafe, duma duma qaalan hasa7izaytape, duma duma qommofene duma duma derepe Xoossas wozanas ne shukettida gishshi he Xoossa maxaafaza ekkanasine matamistaka doyanas bessizade gidadasa.
REV 5:10 Ne istta nu Godaa Xoossaas qessistane kawota histadasa. Isttika biitta bolla kawotana.
REV 5:11 Tani gede zaara xeellishin he alganza, do7atane cimata yuuyi adhdhida daro kiitanchata qaala giireth siyadis. Isttas darotethay daro shiyanine daro miliyonen qoodettes.
REV 5:12 Istti daro gita qaalan “Ha shukettida dorisay wolqa, dureteth, erateth, minoteth, gitateth, bonchone galata ekkanas besses” gida.
REV 5:13 Salonka biitta bollaka, biittafe garisanka, abba giddon diza medhetetha wurison “Alga bolla uttidayssasine dorisas galatayne dhoqateth, bonchoyne wolqay medhinape medhina gakkanaas izas gido!” gishin ta siyadis.
REV 5:14 Oyddu do7atika “Aamin7i” gida. Cimatika ba liipphon gufannidi izas goynida.
REV 6:1 Hessafe guyeka he dorisay laapun matamistape koyro matameza doyishin ta beyadis. He oyddu do7atape issay dada gugumtha mala qaalara “Ha ya!” gishin siyadis.
REV 6:2 Qasseka bootha para beyadis. He parazoza bolla ba kushen wondafe oykidadey dess. He izas qass aklileyka imettides. Izika xoonizade gididi xoonope gede xoonos baanas kezides.
REV 6:3 He dorisay nam7antho matamaza doyda mala nam7antho do7azi “Ha ya!” gishin ta siyadis.
REV 6:4 Qasseka hara xeeq zo7o paray kazides. He parazoza toggidadey biitta bollafe sarotethi dhayssana malane asay ba. e garisan issay issa wursana mala oothisanas izas Godatethine wogga gita mashshay imettides.
REV 6:5 Dorisazi hedzdzantho matameza doyin hedzdzantho do7azi “Ne haya!” gishin siyadis. Qasse para beyadis. Parazoza bolla uttidadezi ba kushen maka miishi oykides.
REV 6:6 Oyddu do7ata giddofe yida milatiza qaala siyadis; he giirethayka “kilos bagga gidizan gisttey issas issi gallasa damusakko. Qasse issi kilone bagga gidiza bangay issi gallasa damusa gido. zaytene woyne mith qohopa” gishin ta siyadis.
REV 6:7 He dorisay oydantho matameza doyin oydantho do7aza qaalay “Ne ha ya!” gishin siyadis.
REV 6:8 Qasseka Cololo parazo beyadis. Parazoza togidayssa sunthi hayqo geetetes. Iza qass dufoy kaalles. Hayqoyne dufoy biittafe sayso olan, gafun, bochanine bazzo do7an wodhana mala godatethi isttas imettides.
REV 6:9 Ichachantho matameza izi doyin xoossa qaala gishshine ba markattida markatetha gishshi hayqidayta shempota yarsho yarshizasoza garisan beyadis.
REV 6:10 Istti qass qaala dhoqu histid “Geeshine tumancha Goda Xooss, Neni biitta bolla diza asa bolla piridonttane nu suutha gishshi ne halo kesonttay ayde gakanasee?” giidi woossida.
REV 6:11 Isttas issas issas bootha mayoy imettides. Isttaka mala buro hayqana. Istta mala oothancha gidida istta lagettine istta ishata qooday kumana gakanas istti guutha wodes shempid takkana mala isttas yootettides.
REV 6:12 Hessafe guye he dorisay usupuntho matameza doyin tani gede izako xeelladis. Heko biittay wolqama qaath qaxxides. Aawa arishey asi kayos mayiza karetha mayo mala karexides. Aginayka kumethara suutha mala zo7adus.
REV 6:13 Wolqqa assura carkoy carkidi miththa ayfe qoqofiza mala salope xoolintey qoqofettides.
REV 6:14 Saloyka waraqata mala xaaxettidi kichides. Zumatine abba giddon diza gadeti wurikka ba dizasope dhay gidida.
REV 6:15 Biitta bolla diza kawoti, biitta haarizayti, ola halaqati, dureti, wolqamati, ashikaratine Godati wurikka gongolo giddonine zumata garisan zaalata garisan qotettida.
REV 6:16 Zumatane zaalataka “Nuna kammite! alga bolla uttidayssa sinthafe, he dorisaza hanqofe nuna qottite.
REV 6:17 wolqama hanqo gallasay gakkides. Iza oone danda7anayii?” gida.
REV 7:1 Hessafe guye oyddu kiitanchata biitta bolla oyddu baggara eqidayta beyadis. Isttika biitta bolla gidin woykko abba bolla woykko miththa bolla ay carkoyka carkontta mala oyddu baggara yiza bocha carko wursi oykida.
REV 7:2 Deyo Xoossa matama oykida hara kiitanchay awa arishey mokiza baggara ha yishiin ta beyadis. Biittane abba qohanas isttas godatethi imettida oyddu kiitachatako ba qaala dhoqu histid,
REV 7:3 Nuni nu goda oothanchata liipho bolla matame wothana gakanas biitta gidin woykko miththata gidiinka heytantta bolla qohopite gi wothides.
REV 7:4 Taka matamay istta bolla wodhidayta qooda siyadis. Isiraa7eele asa kochafe wurisofe matamay istta bolla shocettidayta qooday xeistane oyddu tammane oyddu shiiiko.
REV 7:5 Yuda qommofe matamay istta bolla shocettidayti tammane nam7u shiii, Gaade qommotape tammane nam7u shiii,
REV 7:6 Asere qommofe tammane nam7u shi, Nifitale qommofe tammane nam7u shi, Minase qommofe tammane nam7u shi,
REV 7:7 Simona qommofe tammane nam7u shi, Lewe qommofe tammane nam7u shi, Yisakore qommofe tammane nam7u shi,
REV 7:8 Zabilone qommofe tammane nam7u shi, Yosefo qommofe tammane anmu shi, Biniyame qommofe tammane nam7u shi.
REV 7:9 Hessafe guye ta xeellishin wagay bayinda daro dere beyadis. Heytantika derefe, duma duma qommofe, duma duma zarkefene duma duma qaala hasa7izayt wurisofe shiiqetidaytakko. Heyt wuri bootha mayo mayidi zamba haythe ba kushen oykkid alga sinthanine dorisaza sinthan eqqida.
REV 7:10 Qaala dhoqu histid “Atotethi alga bolla uttidayssafekko!” gida.
REV 7:11 Iza kiitanchati wurikka iza algas, cimatasine oyddu do7ata yuuy adhdhi eqqida algaza sinthan gufanid Xoossas goynida.
REV 7:12 Hizgida “Amin7i! sabay, gitatethi, erateth, galatay, bonchoy, wolqayne minotethi nu Godas Xoossas medhinape medhinas gido amin7i”
REV 7:13 Cimata giddofe issadey taako simmidi tana “Hayti bootha mayo maydayti oonantee? Istti awape yidaytee?” gides.
REV 7:14 Taka “Goda, ne erasa” gadis. Izika taas hizgides “Hayti wolqama waayeza kanthid yidaytakko. Istti ne mayoka dorisa suuthan meeci geeshida.
REV 7:15 Hessa gishshi Xoossa alga sinthan de7idi qamane gallas iza keeththan izas oothettes. Alga bolla uttidayssika isttas dussasokk.
REV 7:16 Hayssafe guye istti gafettana, saamotettena, awa seelayka istta bochchena, hombeyka istta hombena.
REV 7:17 Algaza gidon diza dorisay istta heemizade gidana. Isttaka gede deyo hatha pulitoy dizaso kaalethana. Xoossi istta ayfepe ayfentha quccana.”
REV 8:1 Dorisay laapuntho matameza doyin bagga saate gidizayssa mala saloy co7u gides.
REV 8:2 Xoossa sinthan eqqiza laapun kiitanchata tani beyadis. He asttasika laapun dinkey imettides.
REV 8:3 Exane izan cu7isiza worqafe oothetidayssa oykida kiitanchay yiidi yarsho iza yarshiza soza achchan eqqides. Alga sinthan diza worqafe oothetida yarsho iza bolla yarshizayssa bolla geeshata woossara issife shiishiza daro exaney izas imettides.
REV 8:4 He exaneza cuway geeshata woossara he kiitancha kushepe pude Xoossa sinthe kezides.
REV 8:5 Hessafe guye kiitanchazi exane izan cuwasizayssa oykkidi yarsho yarshiza sozape tama ekkidi izan kunthidi duge biitta bolla yeggides. Daday, giirethi, wolqanthine biittayka qaaxxides.
REV 8:6 Laapun zaye oykida laapun kiitanchati ba zaye punanas giigettida.
REV 8:7 Koyro kiitanchazi ba zayeza punides. Shachine suuthi walakettida tamay medhetides. Duge biitta bolla yegettides. Biittafe cigoy xuugettides. Mithafeka cigoyka xuugetides. Cilila matayka wuri xuugetides.
REV 8:8 Nam7antho kiitanchayka ba zayeza punnides. Issi gita zuma milatiza miishi exishe duge abba giddo yegettides. Abbas cigoy suuthu giddies.
REV 8:9 Abba gidon shempora diza medhetethape cigoy wuri hayqides. Markabistapeka cigoy kumeth dhaydes.
REV 8:10 Hedzdzantho kiitanchazi ba zayeza punnides. Xompe mala eexiza issi gita xoolinttey salope duge kundides. Izi kundiday shaafata cigo bollane haatha pulittota cigo bollakko.
REV 8:11 He xoolintteza sunthay Ereto geetettes. Haathas cigoy camo giddies. He camo haatha geedon daro derey hayqides.
REV 8:12 Oydantho kiitanchay ba zayeza punnides. Awa arishes cigoy, aginas cigoy, xoolinttistas cigoy shocettides. Hessa gishshi heytantta po7ope cigoy dhumides. Hessa malanka gallasafe cigoy omaris giddies. Hessaththoka omarissafe cigoy po7oy bayinda dhuma giddies.
REV 8:13 Ta qass zaara xeellishin issi golle kafoy salo bolla piradhishe gita qaalan “Hanko attida hedzdzu kiitanchati ba dinkista giireth sissiza wode biitta bolla diza asas wo! Wo! isttas wo! Wo! gi waassishin siyadis.
REV 9:1 Ichachantha kiitanchay ba zayeza punnidees. Ta qass salope kase duge biitta bolla kundida xoolintteza beyadis. He izas qass ciimma olla doyiza qulfey imettidees.
REV 9:2 Izika he ciimma ollaza doyidees. He ciimma ollafe wolqama tama cuwa mala cuway kezidees. He ollafe kezida cuwaza geedon awa arisheyne saloy dhumida.
REV 9:3 He cuwape biitta bolla booley kezidees. Biitta bolla diza masmasotas diza wolqa mala wolqay isttas imettidees.
REV 9:4 Biitta bolla diza maata gidin woykko ay miisheka hara cilila miishe montta mala woykko ay miththaka qohontta mala isttas yootetidees. Istti qohana bessizay qass liipho bolla Xoossa matamay bayinda asata xalala gidana malakko.
REV 9:5 He isttaka ichachu agina gakana waaye xalala waayisana attin wodho wodhana mala fiqadey isttas imettibeyna. He booleti asa bolla gaththiza waayezi masimasoy ase dukiko ase seelliza seela malakko.
REV 9:6 He gallasatan asay hayqana koyana shin hayqo demmetena. Hayqanas amottana shin hayqoy isttafe bistana.
REV 9:7 Booleti qass olas giigettida parazota milatettes. Isttas hu7e bolla worqa aklile milatiza miishey dees. Istta ayfesoy asa ayfeso milates.
REV 9:8 Istta hu7e ithikey macasha hu7e ithike milates. Istta achchey qass gaamo achche milates.
REV 9:9 Biratape oothetida xurure geetettiza mayo mala tira bolla mayiza mayoy isttas dees. Istta qefey giiriza giirethay olas togettiza daro parane para gaareta giiretha mala giires.
REV 9:10 Isttas masimaso goyna malayne dukizasoy dees. Isttas goyna gidon ichachu gakanas ase qohiza wolqay dees.
REV 9:11 Kawoyka isttas dees. He izika ciimma olla kiitanchazakko. Iza sunthayka Ibirawista qaalara “Abadone” geetettes. Qasse Giriko qaalara “Aphiliyone” geetettes.
REV 9:12 Koyro waasoy aadhides. Hessafe qass hara nam7u waasoy buro yaana.
REV 9:13 Usupuntho kiitanchayka ba dinkeza punnides. Heko! Xoossa sinthan diza worqafe oothetida yarsho yarishiza sozan diza kacista giddofe giirethi siyadis.
